ABiDarma samuccaya BAzyam / I lakzaNasamuccayaH nAma praTamaH samuccayaH / om namaH ratnatrayAya
# # / / rgya gar skad du / / aa bhi dha rmma sarba du tstsha ya bh'a shum / / bod skad du / / chos-mngon-pa #  kun las btus pa'i bshad-pa #  / / bam po dang-po #  / / 'jam dpal gzhon-nu # r gyur [dd] pa la phyag 'tshal lo /
kimarTam idam SAstram ArabDam
# ci'i-phyir #  bstan-bcos #  'di brtsams she na /
skanDa AdIn AraBya kati kasmAt iti evamAdizu cintA sTAnezu kOSalyakaraNa arTam
# phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  las brtsams te / / du dang ci'i-phyir #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bsam-pa # 'i gnas rnams la mkhas-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir brtsams so /
taTA hi anena kOSalyena dviviDaH anuSaMsaH laByate manaskAra anuSaMsaMH sAMkaTyaviniScaya anuSaMsaH ca
# 'di-ltar #  mkhas-pa #  'dis ni phan yon rnam-pa-gnyis #  thob ste / / yid-la-byed-pa # 'i phan yon dang 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  gtan-la-'bebs-pa # 'i phan yon no /
tatra manaskAra anuSaMsaH SamaTa AnukUlyAt vipaSyanA vRdDayA anukUlyAt ca veditavyaH
# de-la #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'i phan yon ni zhi-gnas #  kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa #  dang lhag-mthong #  'phel-ba # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
SamaTAnu kUlyam punar ezu sTAnezu kRta kOSalasya niHsaMdehatayA yaTezwam AlaMbane EkAgraya yogena suKam citta samADAnataH
# zhi-gnas #  kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa #  ni gnas 'di dag la mkhas-pa # r byas-pa # s the-tshom-med-pa # s / / ji-ltar #  rang-gi #  dmigs-pa #  la rtse gcig pa'i tshul-gyis #  bde-ba # r sems-mnyam-par-'jog-pa # 'i phyir zhi-gnas #  kyi rjes su mthun no /
vipaSyanO= RdDayA anu kUlyam bahuBiH prakArEH jQeya parIkzayA prajQA prakarza gamanataH
# lhag-mthong #  'phel-ba # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  ni rnam-pa #  mang-po # r shes-bya #  yongs su brtags-pa # s shes-rab #  khyad zhugs-pa # r 'gro-ba # 'i phyir /
sAMkaTya viniScaya anuSaMsa ezu sTAnezu kuSalasya sarva praSna vyAkaraNa Sakti yogAt vESSAradya pratilambataH drazwavyaH
# lhag-mthong #  gi rjes su mthun no / / 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  gtan-la-'bebs-pa # 'i phan yon ni gnas 'di dag la mkhas-pa # s 'dri-ba #  thams-cad #  lung-ston-pa # 'i mthu-dang-ldan-pa # s mi-'jigs-pa #  thob-pa # r blta'o /
paQcAkAra AtmavaH tu udBAvanatAm upAdAya iti atra caturAkAram AtmanaH vastu iti AtmavaH tu
# bdag-gi #  gzhi rnam-pa-lnga #  brjod-pa # 'i phyir te / / zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  ni bdag-gi #  gzhi-yin-pa # s bdag-gi #  gzhi'o /
paQcamam tu Atma lakzaNam eva vastu iti AtmavaH tu iti veditavyam
# lnga pa ni bdag-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kho-na #  ste / / gzhi-yin-pa # s bdag-gi #  gzhir rig-par-bya # 'o /
sa parigraha deha grahaNena bAhyasya ADyAtmikasya ca rUpa skanDasya grahaNam veditavyam / vedanA AdInAm upaBogAt tvam tad lakzaNa nirdeSe jQApayizyate
# lus yongs-su-gzung-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  smos-pa # s ni phyi dang nang gi gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  bsdus so / / tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni longs-spyod #  la-sogs-pa #  nyid de / / de-dag #  gi mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # 'i skabs su 'chad do /
tad ASraya Atma svavastu vijQAnam tezAm sa parigraha deha AdInAm ASrayam Atma lakzaNam vastu iti arTaH
# de-dag #  gi gnas ni bdag-gi #  gzhi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / lus yongs-su-gzung-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  gi gnas ni bdag-gi-mtshan-nyid #  de / / gzhi zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
taTA hi loke prAyeNa vijQAne Atma grAhaH Sezezu AtmIya grAhaH iti
# 'di-ltar #  'jig-rten #  na phal-cher #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i phung-po #  la bdag tu 'dzin lhag-ma #  rnams la ni bdag-gi # r 'dzin to /
deha parigrahAByAm iti cakzuH AdI ndriya zawkena rUpa Adi vizaya zawkena ca
# lus yongs-su-gzung-ba #  nyid kyis zhes-bya-ba #  la / / mig la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po #  drug dang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yul drug gis so /
zaXa AkAraH atItaH vartamAnaH ca upaBogaH vijQAna zawkam tasya DAraNam ASraya alaMbana BAvataH / iti evam tadDA raNa tvena dvAdaSAnAm indriya vizayANAm DAtu tvam
# 'das-pa #  dang da-ltar #  gyi nye-bar-spyod-pa #  rnam-pa-drug #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug ste / / de 'dzin-pa #  ni gnas dang dmigs-pa # 'i dang-po # s 'dzin to / / dbang-po #  dang yul bcu gnyis ni de-ltar #  de 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir khams so /
vijQAnAnAm punar upaBoga lakzaNa DAraNa tvena DAtu tvam veditavyam / yaTA atIta pratyutpannAH cakzuH AdayaH upaBoga lakzaNa DArakAH na evam anAgatAH / Aya dvAra mAtra tva Adi indriya arTa mAtra grahaNena dvAdaSa eva AyatanAni vyavasTA pitAni na tu upaBoga lakzaNam vijQAna zawkam iti
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams ni nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  'dzin-pa # s khams nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / skye-ba # 'i sgo tsam yin pa'i phyir dbang-po #  dang don tsam smos-pa # s skye-mched #  bcu gnyis kho-nar #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  yin te / / nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug ni rnam-pa # r ma gzhag go /
upAdAnam CandaH rAgaH ca
# nye-bar-len-pa #  ni 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  te /
tatra CandaH aBilAzaH rAgaH aDyavasAnam / Candena anAgatam Atma BAvam aBilAza muKena upAdatte yena anAgatAn skanDAn aBinirvarttayati
# de-la #  'dun-pa #  ni 'dod-pa # 'o / / 'dod-chags #  ni lhag-pa #  chags-pa # 'o / / 'dun-pa # s ni ma-'ongs-pa # 'i lus 'dod-pa # 'i sgo nas len te / / des ma-'ongs-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams 'grub po /
rAgena vartamAnam Atma BAva maDya vasAna muKena upAdatte yena vartamAnAn skanDAn na parityajati
# 'dod-chags #  kyis ni da-ltar #  gyi lus la lhag-par-chags-pa # 'i sgo nas len te / / des da-ltar #  gyi phung-po #  rnams yongs su mi gtong ngo /
tasmAt etat eva dvayam upAdAnam iti ucyate / tatra skanDa vat nirdeSaH iti
# de-bas-na #  'di gnyi-ga #  yang nye-bar-len-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-la #  phung-po #  bzhin-du #  bshad do zhes-bya-ba #  ni nye-bar-len-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  ste /
upAdAnena yuktAH tasmAt sa upAdAna DarmAH iti veditavyam
# de'i-phyir #  nye-bar-len-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  su rig-par-bya # 'o /
sparSena rUpANAm anyaTA BAvaH veditavyaH
# reg-pa # s gzugs su yod-pa # s ni gzhan-du-'gyur-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
yA deSe iti aBi muKa pradeSe
# gang yul la zhes-bya-ba #  ni mngon du gyur ba'i phyogs la'o /
idam ca idam ca iti asTi SaMkalA Adikam jQeya vastu sa BAgam pratibimbam
# 'di dang 'di'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni keng-rus #  la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  dang 'dra-ba # 'i gzugs-brnyan #  no /
evam ca evam ca iti varNa saMsTAna BedEH citrIkAra tA iti taTAsaMjQA / SuBAnAm karmaNAm suKaH anuBavaH Pala vipAkaH / aSuBAnAm duHKaH / uBayezAm aduHKa asuKaH / taTA hi SuBAnAm aSuBAnAm vA vipAkaH AlayavijQAnam nityam upekzayA eva saMprayuktam Bavati / sA eva ca atra upekzA vipAkaH / suKa duHKayoH tu vipAka ja tvAt vipAka upacAraH / dRzwa Srutatama vijQAta anarTAn iti dRzwam yat ca kzuzA anuBUtam Srutam yat SrotreNa anuBUtam matam yat svayam aByuhitam evam ca evam ca Bavitavyam iti vijQAtam yat pratyAtmam anuBUtam iti / vyavaharati iti aBilApEH prApayati iti arTaH / nAnA avasTAsu ca iti suKa duHKa AdyAsu
# 'di-lta-bu #  dang 'di-lta-bu #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni kha-dog #  dang dbyibs kyi bye-brag #  go / / bkra-ba # r 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-ltar #  'du-shes #  pa'o / / las dge-ba #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni bde-ba-myong-ba # 'o / / las mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi 'bras-bu #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  myong-ba # 'o / / gnyi-ga # 'i 'bras-bu #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa #  myong-ba #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  rnams kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  kun-gzhi # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni rtag-tu #  btang-snyoms #  nyid dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  yin te / / btang-snyoms #  de nyid rnam-par-smin-pa # 'o / / bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  de ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir rnam-par-smin-pa #  zhes nye-bar #  gdags so / / mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang bye-brag-phyed-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i don rnams la zhes-bya-ba #  la / / mthong-ba #  ni gang mig gis myong-ba # 'o / / thos-pa #  ni gang rna-ba # s myong-ba # 'o / / bye-brag-phyed-pa #  ni gang 'di-dang-'di-lta-bur #  'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-nyid-kyis #  mngon-pa # r brtags-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni gang so-so #  rang-gis #  myong-ba # 'o / / tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mngon-par-brjod-pa #  rnams kyis go-ba # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / gnas-skabs #  sna-tshogs #  rnams su zhes-bya-ba #  ni bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams su'o /
yena cakzuzA rUpANi dRzwavAn iti atIta vijQAna upaBoga DAraka tvena DAtu tva darSayati / paSyati iti vartamAna vijQAna upaBoga DAraka tvena
# mig gang-gis #  gzugs rnams mthong-ba # r gyur ba zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'das-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  'dzin-pa #  nyid kyis khams nyid-du #  ston to / / lta-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni da-ltar #  gyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  nye-bar-spyod-pa #  'dzin-pa #  nyid kyis khams nyid-du #  ston to /
yat ca tasya cakzuzaH bIjam upacitam Alaya vijQAnam yatas AyatyAm cakzu nirvartizyate vEpAkyam ca yatas nirvRttam tat api dviviDam bIjam cakzuH DAtuH iti ucyate cakzuzaH hetu tvAt
# mig de'i sa-bon #  bsags-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  yang khams te / / gang-la # s phyi-ma-la #  mig 'grub-par-'gyur-ba # 'o / / rnam-par-smin-pa # 'ang khams te gang-la # s grub zin-pa # 'o / / sa-bon #  rnam-pa #  de-gnyi-ga #  yang mig gi rgyu yin-pas #  mig gi khams zhes-bya'o #  /
yat cakzuH DAtoH rUpe ADipatyam iti rUpi indriya ADipatyena bAhya vizaya nirvartanAt
# mig gi khams ni gzugs la dbang-byed-pa #  ste / / dbang-po # 'i dbang gis phyi-rol #  gyi yul 'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat DAtu vat drazwavyam tat ca yaTAyogam iti yena cakzuzA rUpANi drakzyati yat ca tat bIjam iti evamAdi yojayitavyam / catvAri ca mahABUtAni upAdAya iti
# rang-gi #  rten dang dmigs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  can no / / de ni khams bzhin-du #  blta ste ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyor ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig gang-gis #  gzugs rnams mthong-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  dang de'i sa-bon #  bsags-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / gang-la # s phyi-ma-la #  mig 'grub-pa # r 'gyur zhes-bya-ba #  dang sbyar ro / / 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag rgyur-byas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
kaTam upAdAya rUpam / catvAri mahABUtAni upAdAya janana saMniSraya pratizWopa staMBa upabRMhaNa hetutvena
# 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  dag rgyur-byas-pa #  ni skyed-pa #  dang rten-pa #  dang gnas-pa #  dang ston-pa #  dang 'phel-bar-byed-pa # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
janana Adi hetu tvam punar BUtAnAm upAdAya rUpe paQcaviDam hetu tvam aDikRtya
# 'byung-ba #  dag rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  la rgyu rnam-pa-lnga # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  skyed-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu nyid yin te /
utpatti hetu tvam tEH vinA tat anutpatteH / vRtti hetu tvam BUtAni pratyAKyAya upAdAya rUpasya pRTak deSa avazwamBa sAmarTya aBAvAt
# 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu nyid ni 'di dag med na de mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / 'dug-pa # 'i rgyu nyid ni 'byung-ba #  rnams bsal na rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  la sogs shig tu yul gnod-pa # 'i mthu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anuvRtti hetu tvam BUta vikAreNa tad pratizWita upAdAya rUpa vikriya AgamanAt
# rjes su 'gyur-ba'i-rgyu #  nyid ni 'byung-ba #  gyur na de-la #  gnas-pa # 'i rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  kyang 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sTiti hetu tvam sadRSa utpatti kAle BUtEH upAdAya rUpa saMtAnasya anupacCeda yogena saMDAraNAt
# gnas-par-byed-pa # 'i rgyu nyid ni mtshungs-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i dus na 'byung-ba #  rnams kyi rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  kyi rgyud rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i tshul du 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upacaya hetu tvam vRtti kAle BUtEH UpAt AyarUpa ApyAyanAt iti
# 'phel-bar-byed-pa # 'i rgyu nyid ni 'phel-ba # 'i dus na 'byung-ba #  rnams kyis rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  yongs-su-rgyas-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nIla AdInAm paQcaviMSati enAm rUpANAm vyavasTAnam zaXBiH AkArEH veditavyam / lakzaNataH saMniveSataH anugraha upaGAtataH kriyA saMniSrayataH kriyA lakzaNataH maNXanataH ca caturNA daSAnAm azwAnAm ekEkasya ca yaTAkramam
# sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa #  gzugs rnam-pa #  nyi shu rtsa lnga ni mtshan-nyid #  dang gnas-pa #  dang phan gnod dang byed-pa # 'i rten dang byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang rgyan dang rnam-pa-drug #  gis rnam-pa #  gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / bzhi dang bcu dang brgyad dang gcig dang gcig go-rims #  bzhin no /
tatra aByavakASaH tad anya prativArakaH prazwavya rahitaH yaH deSaH
# de-la #  mngon-par-skabs-yod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa #  zlog-par-byed-pa # 'i reg-bya #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyogs gang-yin-pa # 'o /
naBaH yat uparizwAt nIlam dRSyate
# nam-mkha' #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / gang steng na sngon-po # r snang-ba # 'o /
Sabda vyavasTAnam lakzaNataH anugraha upaGAtataH hetu praBedataH deSanA praBedataH vyavahAra praBedataH ca
# sgra ni mtshan-nyid #  dang phan gnod dang rgyus rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang bshad-pa # s rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang tha-snyad #  kyis rab-tu-dbye-ba # s rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
lakzaNataH Srotra indriya grAhyaH yaH arTaH iti
# mtshan-nyid #  ni rna-ba # 'i dbang-po # s ga zung ba'i don gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
deSanA praBedataH loka prasidDa AdayaH trayaH
# bstan-pa # s rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni 'jig-rten #  gyi grags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gsum mo /
Sezam yaTAyogam veditavyam
# lhag-ma #  ni ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra upAtta mahABUta hetukaH tat yaTA vAc SabdaH
# de-la #  zin-pa # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / ngag gi sgra'o /
anupAtta mahABUta hetukaH tat yaTA vRkza SabdaH
# zin-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / shing la-sogs-pa # 'i sgra'o /
tad uBayaH tat yaTA hasta mRdaFga SabdaH
# de-gnyi-ga #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / lag-pa #  dang rdza-rnga #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgra'o /
loka prasidDaH lOkika BAzA saMgRhItaH / sidDa upanItaH AryeH deSitaH / parikalpitaH tIrTyeH deSitaH
# 'jig-rten #  gyi grag-pa #  ni / / 'jig-rten-pa # 'i skad kyis bsdus-pa # 'o / / grub-pa # s bstan-pa #  ni 'phags-pa #  rnams kyis bstan-pa # 'o / / kun-tu #  brtags-pa #  ni mu stegs pa can rnams kyis bstan-pa # 'o /
AryAna Arya vyAvahArikO tudRzwa AdIn azwO vyavahArAn aDikRtya veditavyO
# 'phags-pa # s tha-snyad #  btags-pa #  dang 'phags-pa-ma-yin-pa # s tha-snyad #  btags-pa #  ni / / mthong-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  tha-snyad #  brgyad kyi dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
ganDa vyavasTAnam sva lakzaNataH anugraha upaGAtataH praBedataH ca / rasa vyavasTAnam api evam eva veditavyam
# dri ni rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  dang phan gnod dang gnas-skabs #  kyi sgo nas rab-tu-dbye-ba # s rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / ro yang de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i dri ni / / tsan dan la-sogs-pa # 'i dri'o /
tatra sahajaH ganDaH candana AdinAm sAMyogikaH DUpa yukti AdInAm pAriNAmikaH pakvaPala AdInAm iti
# sbyar-ba #  las byung-ba #  ni bdug spos sbyar-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dri'o /
sprazwavya eka deSa vyavasTAnam AmarSanataH AtulanataH sparSanataH ApIXanataH saMsargataH DAtu vEzamya sAmyataH ca / ap vAyu saMsargAt SItam / ap pRTavI saMsargAt picCalam
# gyur-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i dri ni shing-tog #  smin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dri'o / / reg-bya # 'i phyogs-gcig #  ni kun-tu #  mnabs pa dang kun-tu #  gzhal-ba #  dang reg-pa #  dang kun-tu #  btsir ba dang 'dus-pa #  dang khams snyoms ma snyoms kyi rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / chu dang rlung 'dus na grang ngo / / chu dang sa 'dus na 'dred do /
viSrAmaH bala mUrjA ca DAtu sAmyAt
# khams snyoms na ngal-sos-pa #  dang nyams yod-pa #  dang spungs che-ba # r 'gyur te /
UrjA punar vESAradyam veditavyam
# sbungs che-ba #  ni mi-'jigs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tRptiH uBayaTA
# tshim pa ni gnyi-ga # 'o /
SezAH jiGatsa AdayaH DAtu vEzamyAt veditavyAH
# bkres-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  lhag-ma #  rnam ni khams-ma-snyoms-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
ABisAMkzepikam paramANu rUpam / AByavakASikam tat eva yaToktam tad anya prativArakaH prazwavya rahitam
# bsdus-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni rdul-phra-rab #  kyi gzugs so / / mngon-par-skabs-yod-pa #  ni de nyid de / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  thogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i reg-bya #  dang bral-ba # 'o /
sAma AdAnikam avijQapti rUpam / parikalpitam pratibimba rUpam
# yang-dag-par-blangs-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-byed #  ma-yin-pa # 'i gzugs so / / kun-brtags-pa #  ni gzugs-brnyan #  gyi gzugs so /

# gcig ni phal-cher #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni log-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni gdon-mi-za-bar #  skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
lakzaNataH dvAByAm anta grAha miTyA dRzwiByAm sa parivArataH sarvAByaH / rUpa AdayaH na AtmA tad vilakzaNa tvAt na hi te Atma lakzaNAH iti / na tezu AtmA anitya tA dozAt / na hi ASraya aBAve ASritam Bavati iti / na rUpavAn AtmA asvAtantrya doza prasaFgAt / na teByaH anyatra AtmA nirdeha tA dozAt / na hi vinA dehena Atma parikalpaH upalaByate iti / asvAtantrya tA dozaH tezu avaSartanAt / aTa evaMviDam AtmAnam kaScid parikalpayet taTA api na upapadyate rUpa AdikaH AtmA ayatnatas mokza dozAt / deha Adi banDana aBAve hi sva rasena eva mokzaH syAt iti / rUpAm AtmA iti samanupaSyati vedanAm saMjQAm saMskArAn vijQAnam AtmA iti samanupaSyati iti etAH paQca Atma dRzwayaH / SezAH paQcadaSa AtmIya dRzwayaH / rUpavAn yAvat vijQAnavAn iti saMbanDena AtmIya tA sA hi tad saMvanDAt tat vAn Bavati iti
# mtshan-nyid #  la brtags na ni mthar 'dzin-pa #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba #  gnyis las 'byung ngo / / 'khor dang bcas-pa #  la brtags na ni lnga po thams-cad-la # s 'byung ngo / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni bdag ma yin te / / mtshan-nyid #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir de-dag #  ni bdag-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ma-yin-pa # 'o / / de-dag #  la bdag med de / / gnas med na gnas-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba # s mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  kyi nyes-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs ni bdag-gi #  ba ma yin te / / de-dag #  la dbang-byed-pa #  med-pa # s rang-dbang-med-pa # 'i nyes-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-dag #  la gzhan na yang bdag med de lus med na bdag kun-tu #  brtags-pa # r mi dmigs-pa # s lus med-pa # 'i nyes-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / ci ste la-la-zhig #  bdag rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # r yongs su rtog na / / de-lta-na-yang #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # 'i bdag mi 'thad de / / lus la-sogs-pa # 'i 'ching-ba #  med na / / rang-gi-ngang-gis #  grol bar 'gyur-ba # s sgrim mi-dgos-pa # r thar-par-'gyur-ba # 'i nyes-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs bdag yin par lta-ba #  dang tshor-ba #  dang 'du-shes #  dang 'du-byed-rnams #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  bdag yin par lta-ba #  de-dag #  lnga ni bdag-tu-lta-ba # 'o / / bdag gzugs-dang-ldan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas bdag rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  lhag-ma #  bco lnga ni bdag-gi # r lta-ba # 'o / / 'brel-ba # s bdag-gi # r gyur ba ni 'di-ltar #  de de dang 'brel-ba # s de dang ldan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / gzugs bdag-gi #  yin pa zhes-bya-ba #  yin pa nas /
AtmIyam rUpam yAvat vijQAnam iti vaSa vartti AtmIyatAm upAdAya yasya hi yat vaSena vartate dAne viniyoge vA tasya tadA AtmIyam iti ucyate / rUpe yAvat vijQAne AtmA iti avinirBAga vRtti AtmIya tA ayam AtmA ezu anusRtaH vistRtaH prakziptaH aFga aFga anusAri gataH iti parikalpanAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  bdag-gi #  yin pa zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar ni dbang-sgyur-ba # s bdag-gi # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir te / / gang zhig sbyin-pa # 'am bskob la gang-gi #  dbang-du-'gyur-ba #  de ni de'i bdag-gi #  zhes-bya'o #  / / gzugs la bdag gnas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  la bdag gnas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar ni tha dad du mi-'jug-pa # s bdag-gi # r 'gyur-ba #  ste / / bdag 'di ni 'di dag la rjes su zhugs shing rnam-pa # r zhugs nas bzhag-pa #  ste / / yan-lag #  can yan-lag #  gi rjes-su-song-ba # r kun-brtags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anirUpitaH tuka tvam punar rUpam iti evam Adi lakzaNam nirUpayataH Atma dRzweH anavakASAt
# ma dpyad-pa # 'i gzhi can ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  la kun-tu #  dpyad na bdag-tu-lta-ba # 'i skabs-med-pa # 'i phyir te /
tat yaTA rajjum sarpataH gRhNAti kaScid sahasA na punA rajjuH iti nirUpayan= tAm sarpataH gRhNIyAt iti
# dper-na #  'ga' zhig gis ma-brtags-pa # r thag-pa #  la sprul du 'dzin-pa #  dang 'dra ste / / thag-pa #  yin par dpyad na de-la #  sprul du mi-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# khro-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni btags-pa'i-yod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / khong-khro-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  las gud-na #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-'og-tu #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni khros-pa # 'i 'og-tu # 'o / / mi-bzod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnod-pa-byed-pa #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa # r mi-byed-pa # 'o / / 'di ni chos-nyid #  do /

# kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  dang bcas na 'gyod-pa # r 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  reg-pa # r mi-gnas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / tshig rtsub mo brlang zhing drag-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzhan gyi zher-'debs-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  ngor lhangs [?] zhes zer ba ni /

# tshe-ring-ba # 'i mtshan-ma #  bzung nas de-la #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i phyir te / / mi-'chi-ba # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  sngon-du-btang-nas #  srog la rgyags pa skye'o /
anyatama anyatamA sA AsravA saMpattiH kula vala rUpa meDA budDi Boga ESvarya AdikA veditavyA / rAga aMSikam nAndI sOmanasyam saMklizwaH harza viSezaH / SuBa nimittam anusarataH rAga anukUlam pUrva hasita ramita krIxita anusmaraNAt cittasya anupaSamaH veditavyaH kOsIdya saMniSraya dAnakarmaka tvam aSraddaDAnasya prayoga= Canda aBAvAt
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rigs dang stobs dang gzugs dang yid-gzhungs-pa #  dang blo dang longs-spyod #  dang phyug-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / dga'-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi dga'-ba # 'i bye-brag #  go / / sdug-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  rjes-su-'jug-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-chags #  kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'o / / sngon dgod dgod-pa #  dang rtse rtse ba la-sogs-pa #  rjes su dran nas sems rnam-par-ma-zhi-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / le-lo # 'i rten byed-pa # 'i las can zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma dad na sbyor-ba #  la 'dun-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /

bahirDAvikzepaH Sruta Adi kuSale prayuktasya tad alaMkaMbanAt bahis kAma guNezu citta gamanam veditavyam
# phyi-rol-du #  g-yeng ba zhes-bya-ba #  ni thos-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dge-ba #  la zhugs-pa #  de-la #  dmigs-pa #  la phyi-rol-du #  'dod-pa'i-yon-tan #  lnga po dag la sems 'gro-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

# dus-ma-yin-pa #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa # 'o /

# rigs-pa #  ni dus-su #  ji-ltar #  gnang-ba #  dang dus yin na yang-na #  ba dang las-su-rung-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ro / / mi-rigs-pa #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa # 'o /
kRtya atipatti saMniSraya dAnam upakleSa Atmakasya midDasya veditavyaH / anaBipretam karaNam aBipretapUrvikA su carita duScarita kriyA anaBipretam karaNam parEH balAt avazwaBya kAryamANasya kleSa aBiBavAt vA yaTAyogam veditavyam / moha aMSikaH iti upakleSa saMgRhItaH / kAle yAvat na prativiramati akAle tat UrDvam / yuktam sTAne ayuktam asTAne / cetanAm vA niSritya prajQAm vA iti anaByUha aByuha avasTAyAm yaTAkramam / paryezaNa AkArA manasaH aBijalpanA vitarkaH pratyavekzaNa AkArA manasaH aBijalpanA anuvicAraH iti / tO= eva vitarka vicArO saMvaDyete OdArika sUkzma vyavasTAnAt anayoH / tat yaTA loBasya loBa prahANam SradDAyAH ASradDaya prahANam / rAga pratipakzaH vErAgyam tasya paripanTa karaNam tasya tena tad utpattO= antarAya karaNAt / evam kroDa AdInAm api upakleSAnAm mEtrI Adi AtmIya rati pakza antarAya karaNam veditavyam / citta viprayuktAnAm saMskArANAm aDizWAnataH svaBAvataH prajQaptitaH ca nirdeSaH veditavyaH / asaMjQi samApatti niroDa samApattI BUmitaH api niHsaraNa vihAra saMjQA pUrvakAByAm manaskArAByAm api nirdizwe / AsaMjQikam manaskAra varjyEH eBiH eva / SezAH aDizWAna AdiBiH triBiH eva / tatra kuSala akuSalAnAm DarmANAm iti aDizWAna nirdeSaH / AcayApacayaH iti svaBAva nirdeSaH / taTA hi Acaye aDimAtrEH SradDAdiBiH samanvAgataH iti ucyate / apacaye sati mRduBiH iti / prAptiH pratilamBaH samAgamaH iti prajQaptiH iti prajQapti nirdeSaH
# bya-ba #  shor ba'i rten byed-pa #  ni nye mongs pa'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / bsams-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni legs-par #  nyes-par-spyod-pa # 'i byed-pa #  las mngon-par-dga'-ba #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'o / / ma bsams-pa # 'i bya-ba #  ni gzhan dag gis nan-gyis #  byed du bcug-ste #  byed-pa # 'am / / nyon-mongs-pa # s zil-gyis-mnan-pa #  ste / / ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du rig-par-bya # 'o / / gti-mug #  gi char gtogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # s bsdus-pa # 'o / / dus ni ji-srid #  mi spong gi bar-du # 'o / / dus-ma-yin-pa #  ni de'i-'og-tu # 'o / / rigs-pa #  ni gnas-pa # 'o / / mi-rigs-pa #  ni gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'o / / sems-pa # 'am shes-rab #  la rten zhes-bya-ba #  ni mngon-pa # r mi rtogs-pa #  dang mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no / / kun-tu-tshol-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  yid kyis mngon-par-brjod-pa #  ni rtog-pa # 'o / / so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  ni spyod-pa # 'o / / sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  ni / / gnas dang ngo-bo-nyid #  dang btags-pa # s bshad-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / gnas bstan-pa # 'o / / 'phel-ba #  dang 'grib-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rang-bzhin #  bstan-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  'phel-ba #  yod-na #  dad-pa #  chen-po #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'grib-pa #  yod-na #  chung-ngu #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / thob-pa #  dang rnyed-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes gdags so zhes-bya-ba #  ni btags-pa #  bstan-pa # 'o /
evam anyezu api yaTAyogam yojayitavyam / SuBa kRtsna vIta rAgasya iti tRtIya DyAna vIta rAgasya

asTAvarANAm iti pravRtti vijQAna saFgRhItAnAm

niroDaH iti samApatti cittakRtaH kAla antaram AsTAvara citta cEtta samudAcAra niroDaH ASrayasya avasTA viSezaH niruDyate anena iti kRtvA
# 'gog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  byas-pa #  ste / / dus-gzhan-na #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  brtan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  kun-tu-'byung-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  kyi bye-brag #  go /
niroDa samApattO= upari avIta rAgasya iti avacanEH Bava agravIta rAgasya arhataH api tad saMBavAt / tat ekatyAnAm ca sTAvarANAm iti klizwa manaH saMgRhItAnAm
# 'dis 'gog-par #  'gyur-ba # s na 'gog-pa # 'o / / 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la ni steng ma'i 'dod-chags #  dang ma-bral-ba #  zhes mi brjod de / / de-la #  srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i dgra-bcom-pa #  yang yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / brtan-pa #  de-dag #  las kyang kha-cig #  ces bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid kyis bsdus-pa #  rnams so /
ete ca samApattI BUmitaH manaskArataH aDizWAnataH svaBAvataH prajQaptitaH ca nirdezwe AsaMjQikam manaskAra varjEH eBiH eva / SezAH aDizWAna AdiBiH triBiH eva / nikAya saBAgaH eka janmikaH skanDa saMtAnaH
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  'di gnyis ni sa dang yid-la-byed-pa #  dang gnas dang ngo-bo-nyid #  dang btags-pa # s bsten to / / 'du-shes-med-pa #  ni yid-la-byed-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  gnas la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  gis lhag-ma #  gsum po dag gis bshad do / / ris-mthun-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshe gcig gi phung-po # 'i rgyun no /
sTiti kAla niyamaH iyantam kAlam anena asmin nikAya saBAge avasTAtavyam varza Satam varza sahasram vA iti karma kRtaH sAmarTya viSezaH
# gnas-pa # 'i dus-nges-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni ris-mthun-pa # r 'dis lo brgya'am / / lo stong ngam / / dus ji-srid #  cig tu gnas-par-bya-ba #  ste / / las kyis byas-pa # 'i nus-pa # 'i bye-brag #  go /
tasmin tasmin sattva nikAyaH iti deva manuzya Adizu sattva jAtizu / Atma BAva sadRSa tAyAm iti eka jAtIyatAyAm
# sems-can-gyi-ris #  de-dang-der #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni lha-dang-mi #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems-can #  gyi skye-ba #  rnams su'o / / lus 'dra-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-pa # r gcig pa'o /
bAhyasya api rUpasya jAtimat tve nikAya saBA agamAtra grahaNam sattva saMtAne lakzaNa prajQapti jQApana arTam
# phyir rol gyi gzugs kyang skye-ba #  dang ldan-pa # s ris-mthun-pa #  tsam smos te sems-can #  gyi rgyud la mtshan-nyid #  gdags-pa # r bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bAhyam hi rUpam saMvartta vivartta praBAvitamA DyAtmikAH tu jAti jarA Adi praBAvitAH iti
# phyir rol gyi gzugs ni 'jigs-pa #  dang 'chags-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'o / / nang gi 'du-byed-rnams #  ni skye-ba #  dang rga-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'o /
prabanDa vinASaH maraNam veditavyam
# rgyun 'jig-pa #  ni 'chi-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
ete ca jAti AdayaH na pratikzaNam veditavyAH kiMtarhi prabanDa avasTAsu iti
# skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'di dag ni skad-cig-re-re-la #  rig-par-bya-ba #  ni ma yin gyi / / rgyun gyi gnas-skabs #  la bya'o /
svaBAva aDivacanam cakzuH Srotram devaH manuzyaH iti evamAdi
# ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi tshig bla dags zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang lha-dang-mi #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
viSeza aDivacanam sarva saMskArAH anityAH sarva sattvAH marizyanti iti evamAdi
# khyad-par #  gyi tshig bla dags zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'du-byed-thams-cad #  mi-rtag-pa # 'o / / sems-can-thams-cad #  'chi-ba # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tad uBaya ASrayezu i ti svaBAva viSeza aDivacana ASrayezu akzarezu asi u iti evamAdizu
# de-gnyi-ga # 'i gnas yi-ge #  rnams la zhes-bya-ba #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  gyi tshig bla dags kyi gnas yi-ge #  aa ai au zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
etAvat ca sarvam yat uta svaBAvaH viSezaH tad uBaya vyavahAraH ca tat sarvam eBiH anuvyavahriyate iti
# thams-cad #  ni 'di dag tsam du zad de / / 'di-ltar #  ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  dang de-gnyi-ga # r tha-snyad #  gdags-pa # 'o / / de thams-cad #  ni 'di dag gis tha-snyad #  'dogs te /
atas ete nAmapada vyaQjana kAyAH vyavasTApitAH
# de'i-phyir #  ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs 'di dag rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
paryAya akzaraNa tAm upAdAya iti yaTA cakzuH cakzuH iti etasmAt paryAyAt anyezu api netra akzi nayana locana Adizu paryAya antarezu kzarati tEH api tad saMjQAnAt
# rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  gzhan-du-mi-'gyur-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni dper-na #  mig ni mig ces bya-ba # 'i rnam-grangs #  de-la #  gzhan-pa #  'dren byed dang gsal byed dang khrid byed dang lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  gzhan dag tu'ang 'gyur te / / de-dag #  gis kyang de shes-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
na evam e iti etat akzaram aH iti etam paryAyam mukttvA paryAya antareNa Sakyate jQApayitum atas paryAya akzaraNAt akzaraNi / kzaraNam punar gamanam veditavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  aa a'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i yi-ge #  'di ni aa a'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-grangs #  'di ma-gtogs-par #  rnam-grangs #  gzhan gyis bstan-pa #  mi nus te / / de'i-phyir #  rnam-grangs #  gzhan-du-mi-'gyur-ba # s yi-ge #  rnams so / / 'gyur-ba #  ni 'gro-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
prabanDa anupacCede pravRtti vyavasTAnam ekasmin kzaNe vyavacCinne vA tad upacAra aBAvAt hetu Pala nAnAtvam izwasya Palasya su caritam anizwasya duScaritam iti evamAdi
# rgyun ma chad-pa #  la 'jug-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / skad-cig-gcig #  gam rgyun-chad-pa #  la de nye-bar-'dogs-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  tha-dad-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la 'dod-pa'i-'bras-bu # 'i rgyu ni legs-par-spyod-pa # 'o / / mi-'dod-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i rgyu ni nyes-par-spyod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste /
PalAnAm pRTak pRTak anyonya hetuka tvam
# 'bras-bu #  rnams ni so-so # r rgyu gzhan dang gzhan-las #  'byung-ba # 'o /
hetu Pala sArUpyam anyatve api yat yasya Palam yujyate
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  mthun-pa #  ni gzhan yin-du-zin #  kyang / / gang-gi #  'bras-bu #  gang 'os-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA dAnasya Boga saMpad iti evamAdi
# 'di-ltar #  sbyin-pa'i-'bras-bu #  ni longs-spyod #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
ekEkasya eva pravRttiH ayugapad pravRttiH veditavyA
# re-re-nas #  'byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni cig-car #  mi-'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
hetu Palasya prabanDena pravRttO satyAm yat tatra hetu Palam utpanna nirudDam saH atItaH kAlaH iti prajQapyate yat anutpannam saH anAgataH kAlaH yat utpanna anirudDam sa pratyutpannaH kAlaH iti
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  rgyun tu 'byung-bar-gyur-pa #  de-la #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  byung zin-pa #  dang 'gags zin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni 'das-pa'i-dus #  zhes gdags so / / gang ma-byung-ba #  de ni ma-'ongs-pa # 'i dus zhes gdags so / / gang byung-ba #  la ma 'gags-pa #  de ni da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i dus zhes gdags so /
hetu Palasya diS vyAptO deSa upacAraH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # s phyogs la khyab-pa #  la yul nye-bar #  gdags ste [*te] /
rUpa saMgRhItam ca atra hetu Palam veditavyam arUpiNAm diS vyApana sAmarTya aBAvAt
# gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  ni phyogs la khyab-par-byed-pa # 'i mthu-med-pa # s rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  ni 'dir gzugs su bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
pratyekaSaH Bede saMKyA iti aBinna eka Atmaka tve dvi tri saMKyA Adi anupapatteH
# so-so #  tha-dad-pa #  la grangs shes-bya #  ba ni tha-dad-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  gcig pa la gnyis gsum zhes-bya-ba # 'i grangs la-sogs-pa #  mi 'thad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
hetu Pala pratyayAnAm samavaDAnam tat yaTA vijQAna AKyasya hi hetu Palasya indriya apariBedaH vipaya ABAsa gamanam tat jQAnam manaskAra pratyupasTAnam ca iti / evam anyatra api yojitavyam
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i rkyen rnams 'dus-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i rgyu'i 'bras-bu'i-rkyen #  ni dbang-po #  ma-nyams-pa #  dang yul snang-ba # r gyur ba dang de skyed-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  nye-bar-gnas-pa #  ste / / de-bzhin-du #  gzhan la yang sbyar-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
iti evam ete citta viprayuktAH saMskArANAm DarmANAm avasTAsu prajQapanAt sarve prajQapti santaH veditavyAH
# de-ltar-na #  sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi chos 'di rnams ni gnas-skabs #  dag la gdags-pa # 'i phyir / / thams-cad #  kyang btags-pa'i-yod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra kuSala akuSala Adi AcayApa caya avasTAyAm ekaH
# de-la #  dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'phel-ba #  dang sgrib-pa'i-gnas #  skabs la ni gcig go /
citta cEtasikA pravRtti avasTAyAm trayaH
# sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  mi-'byung-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  la ni gsum mo /
sTiti avasTAyAm ekaH
# gnas-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  la ni gcig go /
sAdRSya avasTAyAm ekaH
# 'dra-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  la ni gcig go /
lakzaNa avasTAyAm catvAraH
# mtshan-nyid #  kyi gnas-skabs #  la ni bzhi'o /
vyavahAra avasTAyAm trayaH
# tha-snyad #  kyi gnas-skabs #  la ni gsum mo /
alABa avasTAyAm ekaH / hetu Pala avasTAyAm SezAH iti
# ma-thob-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  la ni gcig go / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i gnas-skabs #  la ni lhag-ma #  rnams so /
hetu Palam punar atra sarva saMskRtam veditavyam
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  ni 'dus byas thams-cad-du #  rig-par-bya #  ste /
tatas anyasya utpAdAt hetuH
# de-la # s gzhan 'byung-ba # s rgyu'o /
anyatas tad utpAdAt Palam iti
# gzhan-las #  de 'byung-ba # s 'bras-bu # 'o /
skanDa AdInAm samudAcAre tad bIja paripuzwiH vAsanA iti ucyate
# phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  kun-tu-'byung-ba #  la de'i sa-bon #  yongs-su-rgyas-pa #  ni bag-chags #  zhes-bya'o #  /
sarva bIjakam tezAm eva skanDa AdInAm utpatti bIjEH yuktatvAt
# sa-bon #  thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag-nyid #  'byung-ba # 'i sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AlIyante tasmin DarmAH bIjataH sattvAH vA Atma grAheNa iti AlayavijQAnam
# der chos-rnams #  sa-bon #  du 'du-ba # 'am / / bdag-tu-'dzin-pa # s sems-can #  du 'du-ba # 'i phyir kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
pUrva karma nirmita tvAt vipAka vijQAnam
# sngon-gyi-las #  las nges-par #  byung-ba # 'i phyir rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
punar punar pratisaMDi banDe Atma BAva upAdAnAH dAdAna vijQAnam / tat punar etat cittam iti ucyate sarva Darma vAsanA citta tvAt
# yang-dang-yang #  nyid mtshams-sbyor-ba # r byed-pa # s len-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o / / de ni sa zhes kyang bya ste / / chos-rnams #  kyi bdag chags bsags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tat etat Alaya vijQAnam asti iti kaTam vijQAyate
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  de yod-pa # r ji-ltar #  shes she na /
yasmAt tena vinA
# 'di-ltar #  de med na /
upAttamA Adi spazwa tvam bIjam karma na yujyate
# len dang bzod dang gsal-ba #  dang / / sa-bon #  dang ni las rnams dang /
kAyikaH anuBavaH acitte samApattI cyutiH taTA
# lus-kyis #  myong dang sems med-pa # 'i / / snyoms 'jug de-bzhin #  'chi mi rung /
etasyAH ca uddAna gATAyAH viBAgaH tat yaTA viniScaya saMgrahaNIma zwABiH AkArEH AlayavijQAnasya astitA pratyetavyA
# sdom-pa # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa # 'i 'di'i rnam-par-dbye-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  rnam-par-nges-pa # r bsdu-ba # 'i nang-du #  byas so / / rnam-pa-brgyad #  kyis kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-pa-nyid #  du rtogs-pa # r bya ste /
tat yaTA antareNa Alaya vijQAnam ASraya upAdAna asaMBavataH Adi pravRtya saMBavataH spazwa pravRtti asaMBavataH bIja tva asaMBavataH karma asaMBavataH kAyika anuBava asaMBava asaMBavata sama Apatti asaMBavataH vijQAna cyutya saMBavataH ca
# 'di-ltar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  med na lus-nye-ba # r len-pa #  mi srid-pa #  dang gzod-ma-nas #  byung-ba #  mi srid-pa #  dang / / gsal-ba # r byung-ba #  mi srid-pa #  dang sa-bon #  mi srid-pa #  dang las mi srid-pa #  dang lus-kyis #  myong-ba #  mi srid-pa #  dang sems med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  mi srid-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  'chi-'pho-ba #  mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kena kAraNena ASraya upAdAnam na yujyate / Aha paQcaBiH kAraNEH
# ci'i-phyir #  lus-nye-ba # r len-pa #  mi rung zhe na / / smras-pa #  / / rnam-pa-lnga # s ste [*te] /
taTA hi AlayavijQAnam pUrva saMskAra hetukam
# 'di-ltar #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni sngon gyi 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'o /
cakzuH Adi pravRtti vijQAnam punar vartamAna pratyaya hetukam
# mig la-sogs-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni da-ltar-gyi-rkyen #  gyi rgyu-las-byung-ba #  ste /
yaTA uktam indriya vizaya manaskAra vaSAt vijQAnAnAm pravRttiH Bavati iti vistareNa
# ji-skad-du #  / / dbang-po #  dang yul dang yid-la-byed-pa # 'i dbang gis rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams 'byung-ba # r 'gyur ro zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu #  ste /
idam praTamam kAraNam
# 'di ni gtan-tshigs #  dang-po # 'o /
api ca kuSala akuSalAH zaXni vijQAnakAyAH upalaByante
# yang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # r dmigs-pa #  ste /
idam dvitIyam kAraNam
# 'di ni gtan-tshigs #  gnyis-pa # 'o /
api ca zaNNAm vijQAna kAyAnAm sA jAtiH na upalaByate yA avyAkRta vipAka saMgRhItA syAt
# yang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug-po #  dag la lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # r rnam-par-smin-pa # s bsdus-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  mi dmigs-pa #  ste /
idam tRtIyam kAraNam
# 'di ni gtan-tshigs #  gsum-pa # 'o /
api ca pratiniyata ASrayAH zaX vijQAnakAyAH pravartante tatra yena yena ASrayeNa yat vijQAnam pravartate tat eva tena upAttam syAt avaSizwasya anupAtta tA iti na yujyate upAtta tA api na yujyate vijQAna virahita tayA / idam caturTa kAraNam / api ca punar punar ASrayasya upAdAna dozaH prasajyate
# yang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug 'byung-ba #  ni gnas so-sor-nges-pa #  ste / / gnas gang-dang-gang-las #  rnam-par-shes-pa # r gang-dang-gang #  'byung-ba #  de-dang-de #  ni des zin-pa # r 'gyur gyi lhag-ma #  ni ma-zin-pa # r 'gyur te mi rung ngo / / zin-pa # r yang mi rung ste / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'di ni gtan-tshigs #  bzhi-pa # 'o / / yang-dang-yang #  lus 'dzin-pa # 'i nyes-pa # r yang 'gyur te /
taTA hi cakzuH vijQAnam ekadA pravartate ekadA na pravarttate evam avaSizwAni / idam paQcamam kAraNam
# 'di-ltar #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  res-'ga' #  ni 'byung / / res-'ga' #  ni mi 'byung ngo / / lhag-ma #  rnams kyang de-bzhin #  te / / 'di ni gtan-tshigs #  lnga pa'o /
iti pUrva karma pravarttamAna pratyahetutaH api kuSala akuSalataH api tat jAtyanupalaMBataH api pratiniyata ASrayataH api punar punar upAdAna dozataH api na yujyate
# 'di-ltar #  sngon-gyi-las #  dang da-ltar #  gyi 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba #  dang dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  yin pa dang de'i rnam-pa #  mi dmigs-pa #  dang gnas so-sor-nges-pa #  dang yang-dang-yang #  lus-nye-ba # r len-pa # s kyang mi rung ngo /
kena kAraNena Adi pravRtti saMBavaH na yujyate
# ci'i-phyir #  gzod ma'i 'jug-pa #  'byung-ba # r mi 'gyur zha na /
sa ced kaScid vadet yadi Alaya vijQAnam asti tena dvayoH vijQAnayoH yugapad pravRttiH Bavizyati
# gal-te #  la-la-zhig #  'di-skad-du #  / / ci ste kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-na #  de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gnyis cig-car-'byung-ba # r 'gyur ro zhes zer na de-la #  'di-skad-du #  brjod-pa # r bya ste /
saH idam syAt vacanIyaH adozaH eva BavAn doza saMjQI / taTA hi Bavati eva dvayoH vijQAnayoH yugapad pravRttiH / tat kasya hetoH
# nyes-pa-med-pa #  nyid la khyod nyes-pa # r 'du-shes #  par zad kyi / / 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gnyis cig-car-'byung-ba #  nyid do / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  /
taTA hi ekatyasya yugapad radzwu kAmasya yAvat vijQAtu kAmasya Aditas itaretara vijQAna pravRttiH na yujyate
# 'di-ltar #  kha-cig #  cig-car #  mthong-ba #  'dod-pa #  nas / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  'dod-pa #  la / / thog-mar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig 'byung-ba #  mi rung ste /
taTA hi tatra manaskAraH api nirviSizwaH indriyam api vizayaH api
# 'di-ltar #  de na yid-la-byed-pa #  dang dbang-po #  dang yul yang yod-pa # r bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kena kAraNena asatyAm yugapad vijQAna pravRttO manaH vijQAnasya cakzuH Adi vijQAna sahAnucarasya spazwa tvam na saMBavati / taTA hi yasmin samaye atItam anuBUtam vizayam samanusmarati tasmin samaye avispazwaH manaH vijQAna pracAraH Bavati na tu taTA vartamAna vizayaH manaH pracAraH avispazwaH Bavati
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  cig-car-'byung-ba #  med na ci'i-phyir #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang lhan-cig #  rjes-su-'jug-pa #  yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  gsal-ba # r mi 'gyur zhe na / / 'di-ltar #  gang-gi-tshe #  'das-pa # 'i yul myong-ba #  rjes-su-dran-pa #  de'i tshe yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  rgyu-ba #  ni gsal-ba #  ma yin la / / da-ltar #  gyi yul la rgyu-ba # 'i yid ni de-ltar #  mi-gsal-ba #  ma yin te /
atas api yugapad pravRttiH vA yujyate avispazwa tvam vA manaH vijQAnasya / kena kAraNena bIja tvam na saMBavati zaNNAm vijQAna kAyAnAm anyonyam
# de'i-phyir #  yang cig-car-'byung-ba #  dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  mi-gsal-ba # r yang rung ngo / / ci'i-phyir #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug-pa #  dag phan tshun gyi sa-bon #  nyid ma yin zhe na /
taTA hi kuSala anantaram akuSalam utpadyate akuSala anantaram kuSalam tat uBaya anantaram avyAkRtam hIna DAtuka anantaram maDya DAtukam maDya DAtuka anantaram praNIta DAtukam evam praNIta DAtuka anantaram yAvat hIna DAtukam sa Asrava anantaram anAsravam anAsrava anantaram sa Asravam lOkika anantaram loka uttaram loka uttara anantaram lOkikam

saMkleSa apracAra tAm upAdAya iti tena Alabanena saMkleSa vastunaH saMkleSa SUnya karaNAt / yadA api saMklizwA iti ucyate tadA api AgantukaH tatra upakleSaH veditavyaH / katamaH punar AgantukaH tatra upakleSaH / anapodDRta grAhya grAhaka bIjasya paratantra cittasya dvaya AkArA pravRttiH / na Darma tA cittasya / prakRti praBAsvarA hi sarva DarmANAm Darma tA iti / nimittAni rUpam vedanA yAvat boDiH iti prapaQcitAni tezAm tatra upaSamAt animittam / BUtam yat aviparItam tasya kowiH paryantaH nErAtmyAt pareNa tattva aparyepaNAt
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  mi rgyu-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la #  dmigs-pa # s kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dngos-po #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # s stongs par byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang-gi-tshe #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  can zhes-bya-ba #  de'i tshe yang de-la #  glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / chos-rnams #  kyi chos-nyid #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba # 'o / / mtshan-ma #  rnams ni gzugs dang tshor-ba #  nas byang-chub #  ces bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  spros-pa #  rnams te / / de-la #  de-dag #  nye-bar-zhi-ba # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'o / / yang-dag-pa #  ni gang phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'o / / de'i mtha' ni mur thug-pa #  ste / / bdag-med-pa #  las pha rol tu de-kho-na #  btsal du med-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# sgra ni rgyun-chad-pa # 'i phyir yul gzhan dag tu gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud de 'byung-ba # 'i rgyun gyis yul gzhan-du #  'gro-ba #  med kyi 'di-lta-ste #  rang-gi-yul #  na 'dug cing thang-cig #  'byung ste / / mar-me'i-'od #  rgyas-pa #  bzhin-du #  sgra rgyas-pa #  'byung-ba #  yang de-ltar #  blta'o / / nye yang-ba # r du bcad-pa # 'i sgra gsal-ba # r mi thos-pa # 'i sgra de thogs-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir rtsig pa'i gseb nas chung-ngu #  'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  drug-po #  dag las rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  na du zhig /

# rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gsum ni rang-bzhin #  gyi rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang mngon-pa # r spyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
tatra svaBAva vikalpaH pratyutpannezu saMskArezu anuBUyamAnezu yaH sva lakzaNa AkAraH vikalpaH
# de-la #  rang-bzhin #  gyi rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni de-ltar #  'byung-ba # 'i 'du-byed #  myong-ba #  na gang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kyi rnam-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
anusmaraNa vikalpaH yaH anuBUta pUrva saMskAra AkAraH
# rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni / / gang sngon myong-ba # 'i 'du-byed #  kyi rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
aBinirUpaNa avikalpaH yaH atIta anAga taprati utpannezu viparokzezu aByUhana AkAraH vikalpaH
# mngon-pa # r spyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni gang 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar #  gyi lkog-tu-gyur-pa #  rnams la mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
api Kalu sapta vikalpAH AlaMbane svarasa vAhaH vikalpaH sa nimittaH animittaH paryezakaH pratyavekzakaH klizwaH aklizwaH ca vikalpaH
# yang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  bdun te / / dmigs-pa #  la rang-gi-ngang-gis #  'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang mtshan-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang mtshan-ma-med-pa #  dang kun-tu-tshol-ba # r byed-pa #  dang so-so # r rtag-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o /
tatra AdyaH vikalpaH paQca vijQAnakAyAH acitrayitvA AlaMbanam yaTAsvam vizayezu svarasena eva vahanAt
# de-la #  rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang-po #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug ste / / dmigs-pa #  la bkra-ba # r ma-bzung-ba # r rang-gi-yul #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rang-gi #  dang gis 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sa nimittaH svaBAva anusmaraNa vikalpaH vartamAna atIta vizaya citrIkaraNAt
# mtshan-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  ni rang-bzhin #  dang rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ste / / da-ltar #  dang 'das-pa # 'i yul la bkra-ba # r 'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
animittaH anAgata vizayaH manoraTa AkAraH vikalpaH SezAH aBinirUpaNa avikalpa svaBAvAH veditavyAH
# mtshan-ma-med-pa #  ni ma-'ongs-pa # 'i yul yid la brnags pa'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o / / lhag-ma #  rnams ni mngon-pa # r spyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du rig-par-bya #  ste /
taTA hi ekadA aByuhanamAnaH paryezate ekadA pratyavekzate ekadA klizwaH Bavati ekadA aklizwaH iti
# 'di-ltar #  res-'ga' #  ni mngon-pa # r rtog cing kun-tu #  tshol lo / / res-'ga' #  ni so-so # r rtog go / / res-'ga' #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  du 'gyur ro / / res-'ga' #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma yin no /
yadA rUpa Adi prativijQaptikam vijQAnam tat kena kAraNena cakzuH Adi vijQAnam iti ucyate na rUpa Adi aBijQAnam iti
# gang-gi-tshe #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i so-so # r rnam-par-rig-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  de ci'i-phyir #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes bya'i gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes mi bya zhe na /
paQcaviDa vigraha upapatteH rUpa Adi vacana anupapattiH / kaTam iti
# tshig rnam-pa # r sbyar-ba #  rnam-pa-lnga #  'thad-pa #  dang gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i tshig mi 'thad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ji lta zhe na /
cakzuzi vijQAnam cakzuH vijQAnam ASraya deSe vijQAna utpattitaH sati ca tasmin= tad BAvAt / taTA hi sati cakzuzi cakzuH vijQAnam avaSyam utpadyate ananDAnAm anantataH anDakArasya api darSanAt / na rUpe satya vaSyam anDAnAm adarSanAt iti
# mig la rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / gnas kyi yul la rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de yod-na #  de'ang yod-pa # 'i phyir te / / 'di-ltar #  mig yod-na #  long-ba #  ma-yin-pa #  rnams kyi mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ste / / tha-na #  mun-pa #  na yang mthong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs yod-du-zin-kyang #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  'byung-ba #  ma yin te /
cakzuzA vijQAnam cakzu vijQAnam tad vaSena avikRte api rUpe vijQAnasya vikriya Agamana tvAt
# long-ba #  rnams kyis mi mthong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / gzugs ma gyur kyang de'i dbang gis rnam-par-shes-pa #  'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tat yaTA kAma lavya aDi upahatena cakzuzA nIla Adi rUpezu api pIta darSanam eva Bavati iti
# dper-na #  mig ser gyi nad kyis btab na gzugs sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang mig gis ser-po #  nyid-du #  mthong-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
cakzuzaH vijQAnam cakzuH vijQAnam vijQAna bIja anubanDAt cakzuzaH tad nirvRtteH
# mig las rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / mig ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i sa-bon #  dang 'brel-ba #  ste / / de-la # s 'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
cakzuze vijQAnam tasmE hita ahita tvAt
# mig gi phyir rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste de-la #  phan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
taTA hi vijQAna saMprayuktena anuBavena indriyasya anugrahaH upaGAtaH vA Bavati na vizayasya iti
# 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i myong-ba # s dbang-po #  la phan gnod du 'gyur gyi yul la ni ma yin no /
cakzuH vijQAnam cakzuH vijQAnam uBayoH sattva saMKyAta tvAt na tu avaSyam rUpasya iti
# mig dang mtshungs-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / gnyi-ga #  yang sems-can #  gyi grangs-su-gtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs ni gdon-mi-za-bar #  sems-can #  gyi grangs-su-gtogs-pa #  ma yin no /
kim tAvat cakzuH rUpANi paSyati iti veditavyam aTa vijQAnam
# ci mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ngam / / 'on te rnam-par-shes-pa # s mthong zhe na /
na ekam na aparam paSyati iti veditavyam nirvyApAra tvAt DarmANAm
# chos-rnams #  ni byed-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir gcig gis kyang mi mthong la / / cig shos kyis kyang mi mthong-ba # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
sAmagrayAm tu satyAm darSana prajQaptiH
# tshogs-pa # r gyur-pa #  las mthong-ba # r gdags so /
api Kalu zaXBiH AkArEH cakzuzaH rUpa darSane prADAnyam veditavyam na vijQAnasya / katamEH zaXBiH
# yang rnam-pa-drug #  gis ni mig gis gzugs mthong ngo zhes gtso bor rig-par-bya # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa # s ni ma yin no / / rnam-pa-drug #  gang zhe na /
utpatti kAraNaH taH cakzuzaH tad utpatteH
# 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu'i phyir mig las de 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tad pada sTAnataH darSanasya cakzuH ASrayaNAt
# de'i-gnas #  kyi phyir mthong-ba # 'i rten mig yin pa'i phyir ro /
acala vRttitaH cakzuzaH nityam eka jAtIya tvAt
# mi g-yo-ba # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir mig ni rtag-tu #  rigs gcig pa'i phyir ro /
svatantra vRttitaH pratikzaNam utpatti pratyaya sAmagrya napekza tvAt
# rang dbang du 'jug-pa # 'i phyir skad-cig-re-re-la #  'byung-ba #  rkyen-tshogs-pa #  la mi ltos-pa # 'i phyir ro /
SoBA vRttitaH tena ASraya SoBanAt
# mdzes-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir des gnas mdzes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AgamataH cakzuzA rUpANi dRzwve ti vacanAt
# lung gi phyir mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ngo zhes gsungs-pa # 'i phyir te /
etat ca yaToktam sarva vijQAnasya na saMBavati iti
# ji-skad-du #  bshad-pa #  de thams-cad #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  la mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
cala vRtti tvam tu asya bahu prakAra utpatitaH veditavyam
# 'di ni rnam-pa #  mang-po # r 'byung-ba # s g-yo-ba # r 'jug-pa #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
yaTA DAtuzu Ayatanezu ca asaMskRtam vyavasTApitam evam kasmAt na skanDezu api vyavasTApitam
# ji-ltar #  khams rnams dang skye-mched #  rnams la 'dus-ma-byas #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  phung-po #  rnams la ci'i-phyir #  rnam-pa # r ma bzhag ce na /
skanDa arTa asaMBavAt
# phung-po # 'i don-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
rUpa AdInAm atIta Adi prakAra aBisaMkzepeNa rASi arTaH skanDa arTaH nirdizwaH / sa ca nityasya na saMBavati iti na skanDezu asaMskRta vyavasTAnam
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni 'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dag gis bsdus te / / spungs pa'i don ni phung-po # 'i don-du #  bstan la / / de ni rtag-tu #  yod-pa-ma-yin-pa # s phung-po #  rnams la 'dus-ma-byas #  rnam-pa # r mi gzhag go /
kena kAraNena te eva DarmAH skanDa DAtu Ayatana muKEH pRTak deSitAH
# ci'i-phyir #  chos 'di rnams phung-po #  dang khams 'di rnams skye-mched #  kyi sgo nas logs-shig #  tu bshad ce na /
vineyAnAm samAsa vyAsa nirdeSa kOSalya utpAdana arTam
# gdul bya rnams bsdus-pa #  dang rgyas-par-bstan-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  bskyed-pa # 'i phyir te /
taTA hi skanDa nirdeSe ye rUpa vijQAne samAsena nirdizwe te DAtu Ayatanezu ekAdaSaDA / saptaDA ca BittvA vyAsena nirdizwe yaTAyogam
# 'di-ltar #  phung-po #  bstan-pa #  la gzugs dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  gang dag mdor-bstan-pa #  de-dag #  khams dang skye-mched #  rnams la rnam-pa-bcu #  gcig dang rnam-pa #  bdun du phye-nas #  rgyas-pa # r bstan te ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
ye tu tatra vedanA AdayaH vyastAH te DAtu Ayatanezu Darma DAtu Ayatana tvena samastAH iti
# der tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gang dag rgyas-par-bstan-pa #  de-dag #  ni khams dang skye-mched #  rnams su chos-kyi-khams #  dang skye-mched #  du bsdus te bstan to /
api Kalu lakzaNa mAtra vyavasTAnataH skanDa nirdeSaH grAhya grAhaka grahaNa vyavasTAnataH DAtu nirdeSaH grahaNAya dvAra BUtasya grAhya grAhaka mAtrasya vyavasTAnataH Ayatana nirdeSaH veditavyaH / samApta mAnuzaMgikam
# yang mtshan-nyid #  tsam rnam-par-gzhag-pa # s phung-po #  bstan to / / 'dzin-pa #  dang gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r byed-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # s khams bstan to / / 'dzin-par-byed-pa #  skye-ba # 'i sgor gyur-pa #  gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  tsam rnam-par-gzhag-pa # s skye-mched #  bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / zhar-las-byung-ba #  rdzogs s+ho /
atas param mUlagranTasya eva arTa nirdeSaH drazwavyaH
# 'di man-chad-du #  ni rtsa ba'i gzhung nyid kyi don bshad-pa # r blta'o /
arhataH caramam cakzuH parinirvANa kAle paScimam
# dgra-bcom-pa #  tha-ma # 'i mig go zhes-bya-ba #  ni yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dus tha-ma #  ste /
tatra DAtuH cakzuH antarasya ahetutvAt
# de ni mig gzhan gyi rgyu yin-pas #  khams ma yin no /
ArUpya upapannasya pRTagjanasya cakzuH hetuH iti tatas pracyutya rUpiNi DAtO= upapadyamAnasya yasmAt Alaya vijQAna saMnivizwAt cakzuH bIjAt ca kzuH nirvartizyate na tu Aryasya punar anAgamanAt iti
# gzugs-med-par-skyes-pa # 'i so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i mig gi rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de nas shi 'phos te / / gzugs-can #  gyi khams su skye-ba # 'i mig gi sa-bon #  kun-gzhi # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  las 'di-ltar #  yang mig mngon-par-'grub-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  ste / / yang phyir-mi-'ong-ba # s na 'phags-pa #  rnams kyis ni ma yin no /
kAyaDAtuH na kAyaH ArUpya upapannasya pRTagjanasya yaH kAyaDAtuH iti etat atra vaktavyam aNXa gata AdInAm kAya saMBavAt pranazwa kAyasya ca AjIvita svAt iti
# lus kyi khams yin la lus ma-yin-pa #  la yang gzugs-med-par-skyes-pa # 'i so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i rgyu'o zhes-bya-ba #  'dir brjod-pa # r bya ste / / sgo-nga # 'i nang na 'dug-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la ni lus yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / lus-zhig-pa #  ni mi-'tsho-ba # 'i phyir ro /
syAt manoDAtuH na manaH iti atra asaMjQi samApanna sya agrahaNam klizwamanaH sadBAvAt
# yid kyi khams yid la yid ma-yin-pa # 'ang yod ces bya-ba #  la / / 'dir 'du-shes-med-pa #  la snyoms-par-zhugs-pa #  ma smos-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jAtaH BUtaH nirvRtti vRdDi ca aDikRtya yaTAkramam
# byung zhing skyes-pa # r gyur zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'grub-pa #  dang rgyas-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste go-rims #  bzhin no /
ArUpya avacareNa manasA ArUpya avacarAn sva BUmi kAnana AsravAn= ca DarmAn vijAnAti iti Arya SrAvakam aDikRtya
# gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa # 'i yid kyis gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa # r rang-gis #  pa rnams dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyang shes so zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
bAhyakaH pRTagjanaH sva BUmikAn eva vijAnAti iti / iha DArmikaH tu kaScid pUrva Sruta pariBAvana avaSAt UrDvaBUmikAn api AlaMbate tad utpAdana arTam
# phyi-rol #  gyi so-so'i-skye-bo #  ni rang-gi #  sa pa rnams nyid rnam-pa # r shes kyi chos 'di pa ni la-la #  sngon thos-pa # s yongs-su-bsgoms-pa # 'i dbang gis sa-gong-ma #  la yang dmigs te bskyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA rUpam taTA anuBavaH iti suKa Adi vedanIya Adi indriya arTa dvayAt suKa Adi vedanA utpatteH
# gzugs ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  myong ngo zhes-bya-ba #  ni bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i dbang-po #  dang yul gnyis las bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'tshor-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA vedayate taTA saMjAnItaH iti yaTA anuBavam nimitta udgrahaNAt
# tshor-bar-byed-pa #  ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  'du-shes #  su byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  myong-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA saMjAnIte taTA cetayati yaTAsaMjQam karma aBisaMskaraNAt
# ji-ltar #  'du-shes #  su byed-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  sems-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'du-shes #  ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA cetayate taTA vijQAnam tatra tatra upagam Bavati iti yaTA aBisaMskAram vizayezu gati antarezu ca vijQAna pariNAmAt
# sems-par-byed-pa #  ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa # r byed de / / de-dang-der #  nye-bar-'gro-ba # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  mngon-par-'dus-byas-pa # 'i yul rnams la 'gro-ba-gzhan #  rnams su rnam-par-shes-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yatra saMkliSyate vyavadAyate ca iti sa indriye kAye
# gang-ba #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i lus la'o /
yena anuBavena iti sa Amiza nirAmiza Adyena yaTAkramam
# myong-ba #  gang-gis #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni zang-zing-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zang-zing-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
yena nimitta grahaNa aBisaMskAreNa iti ayoniSaH yoniSas ca pravRttena
# mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa #  dang mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  gang-gis #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa #  dang tshul-bzhin-du #  'jug-pa # s so /
yat saMkliSyate vyavadAyate ca iti citta dOzWulyAt OzWulya upapattitaH
# gang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems gnas-ngan-len #  dang bcas-pa #  dang gnas-ngan-len #  med-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
ekAdaSaviDAt tRzNA prakArAt rUpa AdInAm atIta Adi prakAra vyavasTAna veditavyam
# srid-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gcig gi skabs kyi gzugs la-sogs-pa #  'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # s rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sA punar apekzA tRzNA aBinandana atRzNA aDyavasAna tRzNA Ama tRzNA vizaya tRzNA kAma tRzNA samApatti tRzNA duScarita duHKa tRzNA su carita suKa tRzNA viprakRzwa tRzNA sa nikRzwa tRzNA ca
# de-yang #  bltas-pa # 'i srid-pa #  dang mngon-par-dga'-ba # 'i srid-pa #  dang lhag-par-chags-pa # 'i sred-pa #  dang bdag la sred-pa #  dang yul la sred-pa #  dang 'dod-pa #  la sred-pa #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la sred-pa #  dang nyes-par-spyad-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  la sred-pa #  dang lags par spyad-pa # 'i bde-ba #  la sred-pa #  dang ring-ba #  la sred-pa #  dang nye-ba #  la sred-pa #  ste /
asyAH tRzNAyAH AlaMbana tvena yaTAkramam atIta AdayaH prakArAH yojitavyAH / aparaH paryAyaH / utpannAn utpanna BedataH grAhaka grAhya BedataH bahirmuKa antarmuKa BedataH klizwA klizwa BedataH viprakRzwa saMnikRzwa BedataH vAtIta AdIni yaTAyogam veditavyAni / tatra utpannam atItam pratyutpannam ca / anutpannam anAgatam / vahiH muKam asamAhita BUmikam / antarmuKam samAhita BUmikam / SizwaH sugama tvAt na viBaktaH
# sred-pa #  'di dag gi dmigs-pa #  nyid kyis go-rims-bzhin-du #  'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r sbyor-ba # r bya'o / / yang rnam-grangs #  gzhan-du-na #  byung-ba #  dang ma-byung-ba # 'i bye-brag #  dang 'dzin-pa #  dang gzung-ba # 'i bye-brag #  dang phyi-rol-du #  bltas-pa #  dang nang-du #  bltas-pa # 'i bye-brag #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i bye-brag #  dang ring-ba #  dang nye-ba # 'i bye-brag #  dang 'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  byung-ba #  ni 'das-pa #  dang da-ltar #  ro / / ma-byung-ba #  ni ma-'ongs-pa # 'o / / 'dzin-pa #  ni nang gi'o / / gzung-ba #  ni phyi'o / / phyi-rol-du #  bltas-pa #  ni mnyam-pa # r ma bzhag-pa # 'i sa pa'i'o / / nang-du #  bltas-pa #  ni mnyam-par-bzhag-pa # 'i sa pa'i'o / / lhag-ma #  ni go-sla-ba # s ma bshad do /
duHKa vEpulya lakzaNa tAm upAdAya iti rUpa Adi saMniSrayeNa jAtTa Adi duHKa pratAnAt
# sdug-bsngal #  ni shin-tu #  rgyas-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kho-na # 'i phyir te zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la brten-nas #  skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  rgyas-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
saMkleSa BAra udvahanam rUpa Adi ASrita tvAt kleSa Adi saMkleSasya
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  khur khyer-ba #  nyid kyi phyir te zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la brten-pa # 'i phyir te /
tat yaTA loke yena SarIra pradeSena BAraH uhyate tatra skanDa upacAraH dRzwaH skanDena BAram udDahati iti
# dper-na #  'jig-rten #  na phrag-pa # s khur khyer-ba # 'i phyir lus kyi phyogs gang-gis #  khur khyer-ba #  de-la #  phrag-pa #  zhes 'dogs-pa #  mthong-ste #  dang mtshungs so /
sarva Darma bIja arTaH iti hetu arTam aDikRtya Alaya vijQAne / kArya kAraNa BAva DAraNam azwAdaSasu DAtuzu zaNNAm vijQAna DAtUnAm indriya arTa DAtUnAm ca yaTAkramam
# chos-thams-cad #  kyi sa-bon #  gyi don to zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la rgyu'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  dang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  'dzin-pa # 'i don to / / 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i-dngos-po # r 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni khams bco brgyad po dag la rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  drug dang dbang-po #  dang don gyi khams rnam go-rims #  bzhin no /
sarva prakAra Darma saMgrahaNena sUtra antara nirdizwAnAm pRTivI DAtu AdInAm anyezAm api DAtUnAm ezu eva azwAdaSasu yaTAyogam saMgrahaNAt veditavyam
# chos kyi rnam-pa # r thams-cad #  bsdus nas 'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mdo-sde #  gzhan dag las sa'i-khams #  la-sogs-pa #  dang khams gzhan dag bstan-pa #  dag kyang khams bco brgyad po 'di dag gi nang-du #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du bsdu-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
bIja arTaH sarva prakAra Darma saMgraha arTaH ca Ayatana arTaH api veditavyaH
# sa-bon #  gyi don dang chos kyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  bsdus-pa # 'i don ni skye-mched #  kyi don-du #  yang rig-par-bya # 'o /
rUpa AdAnAm Pena piNXaH pama tvam asataH riktatas tucCataH asArataH ca KyAnAt veditavyam
# gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni dbu-ba #  rdos pa la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu #  nyid de / / med-pa #  dang gso-ba #  dang gsog dang snying-po-med-pa # r snang-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
etezAm punar sUtra padAnAm arTaH Atma Suci suKa nitya viparyAsa pratipakzeNa yaTAkramam anAtma tAm upAdAya iti evamAdiBiH padarveditavyaH
# mdo'i-tshig #  'di rnams kyi don ni bdag dang gtsang ba dang bde-ba #  dang rtag-par #  phyin-ci-log-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ste / / bdag-med-pa #  nyid kyi phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshig rnams go-rims-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
kaTam kati kimarTiBiH iti praSna traya vyavasTApanam lakzaNa vastu saMmohayoH samAropasya ca prahANa arTam
# ji-ltar #  du zhig ci'i-phyir #  zhes 'dri-ba #  gsum rnam-par-'jog-pa #  ni mtshan-nyid #  dang dngos-po-la-rmongs-pa #  dang sgro-'dogs-pa #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tatra kaTam dravya sat iti dravya sataH lakzaNa nirdeSena tad saMmohaH prahIyate
# de-la #  ji-ltar #  rdzas su yod ces bya-ba #  ni rdzas-su-yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # s de-la #  rmongs-pa #  spong ngo /
sarvANi dravya santi iti anena vastu saMmohaH prahIyate Atma dravya aBiniveSati Ajana arTam iti anena samAropaH prahIyate
# thams-cad #  kyang rdzas-su-yod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni dngos-po-la-rmongs-pa #  spong-ba #  dag la rdzas su mngon-par-zhen-pa #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sgro-'dogs-pa #  spong ngo /
evam anyatra api yojyam
# de-bzhin-du #  gzhan rnams la'ang sbyor byar bya'o /
aBilApa nirapekzaH indriya gocaraH tat yaTA rUpam vedanA iti evamAdikam nAmnA acintayitvA yasya arTasya grahaNam Bavati
# dbang-po # 'i spyod yul brjod-pa #  la mi ltos-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  gzugs dang tshor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ming bkra-ba # r mi-'dzin-pa # r don gang-yin-pa #  'dzin-pa #  yin no /
tad anya nirapekzaH tat yaTA arTa antaram anapekzya yatra tad budDiH Bavati
# de-las-gzhan-pa #  la mi ltos-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / don gzhan la mi ltos-pa #  de'i blo 'byung-ba #  ste /
na yaTA Gawa Adizu rUpa AdIn apekzya Gawa Adi budDiH iti
# ji-ltar #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la ltos nas bum-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la bum-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i blo 'byung-ba #  lta-bu #  ni ma yin no /
saMkleSa alaMkanam saMvRti sad saMkleSa vRtti arTena / AtmA saMkleSasya nimittam iti aBiniveSa tyAjana arTam
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni kun-rdzob #  tu yod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  'phel-ba # 'i phyir ro / / bdag ni kun nas kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rgyu'o snyam-du #  mngon-par-zhen-pa #  spang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
viSudDaye AlaMbanam parama arTa sat parama jQAna gocara arTena / sarvANi zaramArTa santi iti taTatA vyatirekAt sarva DarmANAm
# rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni don-dam-pa # r yod-pa #  ste / / ye-shes-dam-pa # 'i spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / thams-cad #  kyang don-dam-pa # r yod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos-thams-cad #  kyang de-bzhin-nyid #  las gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yena saMkliSyate vyavadAyate ca iti rAga AdiBiH cetasikEH SradDA AdiBiH ca iti veditavyam
# gang-gis #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-las-byung-ba #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
yA ca tatra avasTA iti rUpa citta cetasika avasTAsu prajQaptAH citta viprayuktAH saMskArAH / yat ca vyavadAnam iti asaMskRtam vyavadAnam veditavyam / tat ca yaTAyogam / punar trayodaSaviDasya vijQAnasya yaH vizayaH tat jQeyam anena pradarSitam
# de'i-gnas #  skabs gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  dag la btags-pa #  sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  so / / rnam-par-byang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dus-ma-byas #  te / / de ni ci-rigs-su #  sbyar ro / / yang shes-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gsum gyi yul gang-yin-pa #  de ni shes-bya #  ste /
tat punar Srutam ayam jQAnam cintA mayam jQAnam lOkika BAvanA mayam jQAnam paramArTa jQAnam para citta jQAnam Darma jQAnam anvayajQAnam duHKa jQAnam samudaya jQAnam niroDa jQAnam mArga jQAnam kzaya anutpAda jQAnam mahAyAna jQAnam ca
# de-dag #  ni thos-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i shes-pa #  dang bsams-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i shes-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pa # 'i bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i shes-pa #  dang don-dam-pa #  shes-pa #  dang gzhan-gyi-sems #  shes-pa #  dang chos-shes-pa #  dang rjes su rtogs-pa # 'i shes-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-shes-pa #  dang kun 'byung shes-pa #  dang 'gog-pa-shes-pa #  dang lam-shes-pa #  dang zad-pa #  dang mi-skye-ba-shes-pa #  dang theg-pa-chen-po #  shes-pa #  ste /
ete anye ca yaTAkramam aDimukti jQAna AdIni veditavyAni
# de-dag #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  mos-pa # 'i shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra para citta jQAnam para Atma jQAnam parAtma citta vizayAt
# de-la #  gzhan-gyi-sems #  shes-pa #  ni gzhan gyi bdag-nyid #  shes-pa #  ste / / gzhan gyi bdag-nyid-kyi #  sems yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
Darma jQAnam aDara jQAnam satyezu Aditas utpAdAt
# chos-shes-pa #  ni 'og ma-shes-pa #  ste / / bden-pa #  rnams la thog-mar #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
anvaya jQAna mUrDva jQAnam Darma jQAnAt UrDvam utpAdAt
# rjes su rtogs-pa # 'i shes-pa #  ni gong-ma #  shes-pa #  ste / / chos-shes-pa # 'i 'og-tu #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
vidUzaNAya asamutTApanAya anutpAde jQAne nizWAyAm mahArTezu jQAnam tad vidUzaNa jQAnam yAvat mahA arTa jQAnam iti yojayitavyam / mahArTa tvam punar sva para arTa tvAt / tatra avikalpanataH paQcaBiH vijQAnakAyEH / vikalpanataH manaH vijQAnena / hetutaH AlayavijQAnam / pravRttitaH tad anyat vijQAnam nimittataH indriya arTAH / nEmittikataH vijQAnAni / vipakza pratipakzataH sa rAgam vigata rAgam sa dvezam vigata dvezam iti evamAdi / sUkzma praBedataH saptaviDa durvijQAna vijQapti BedAt
# rnam-par-sun-'byin-pa # 'i phyir / / kun nas mi ldang-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / mi-skye-ba-shes-pa #  la mthar-thug-pa #  don chen-po #  la shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni rnam-par-sun-'byin-pa # 'i shes-pa #  nas don chen-po # 'i shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / don chen-po #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  gyi phyir ro / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga po dag gis so / / rnam-par-rtog-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # s so / / rgyus zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s so / / 'jug-pa #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o / / rgyu mtshan ni dbang-po #  dang don rnams so / / rgyu mtshan las byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams so / / mi-mthun-pa #  dang gnyen-po #  ni 'dod-chags #  dang bcas-pa #  dang 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang bcas-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang bral-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
saptaviDA durvijQAnAH vijQAptiH tat yaTA asaMvidita vijQaptiH BAjana vijQaptiH sarvakAlam aparicCinna AkAra tvAt citra AkAra vijQaptiH ekasya anekaH AkAraH vicitraH ca iti durvyavasTApanAt asyAH sUkzma tvam / sahaBAva vijQaptiH eka kAla utpannAti vijQAnAni kaTam pRTak yaTAsvam vizayam paricCindanti iti durvyavasTApanAt sUkzma tvam
# phra-ba # 'i rab-tu-phye-ba # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  rnam-pa #  bdun gyi bye-brag #  gis te / / rnam-par-shes-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  bdun ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / ma-rig-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni snod kyi rnam-par-rig-pa #  phra-ba #  ste / / dus-thams-cad-du #  rnam-pa #  yongs su mchad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sna-tshogs #  kyi rnam-pa # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni gcig gi rnam-pa #  ni gcig dang sna-tshogs #  te / / rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i phyir 'di ni phra-ba #  nyid do / / lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni dus-gcig-tu #  'byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams ji-ltar #  so-so # r rang-gi-yul #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yongs su gcod-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sUkzma tvam iti sarvatra aDikRtam veditavyam
# phra-ba #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni thams-cad-du #  sbyar-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
vipakza pratipakza laGu parivRtti vijQaptiH kaTam rAga Adi samasta banDanam cittam tat muhur eva sakRt vIta rAga Adikam Bavati iti
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  las gnyen-po #  myur-du #  'byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni ji-ltar #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'ching-ba #  thams-cad #  dang ldan-pa # 'i sems te / / yud tsam nyid la thang-cig #  tu 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  dang bral-bar-'gyur-ba # 'o /
vAsanA vijQaptiH kaTam karmaBiH samudAcaradBiH cittam vAsyate na ca tasmAt anyA sA vAsanA na api tanmAtram eva Pala dAnam ca prati krameNa vRtti lABaH iti
# bag-chags #  kyi rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni ji-ltar #  las kun-tu-'byung-ba #  rnams kyis sems la bag-chags #  bsgo-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  ste / / de-la # s bag-chags #  gzhan-pa # 'ang ma yin la de tsam nyid kyang ma yin te /
pratisaMDi vijQaptiH kaTam aneka prakAra Atma BAva nirvartaka karma pariBAvitam sat vijQAnam taTA api aparisPuwAyAm maraNa avasTAyAm sahasA prabudDayAni atara karma vAsanAm anyatarasyAm gatO pratisaMDi vaDnAni iti
# 'bras-bu #  'byin-pa # 'ang rim-gyis #  'byung-ba #  rnyed-pa # 'o / / nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni ji-ltar #  lus rnam-pa-du-ma # r 'grub-pa # 'i las kyis yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  yod-pa #  dang de-bzhin-du #  'chi-ba # 'i dus na shin-tu #  mi-gsal-ba # 'i tshe 'phral-la #  las kyi bag-chags #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig sad cing rgyas nas 'gro-ba #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig tu nyid mtshams-sbyor-ba # r 'gyur ro /
mukta vijQaptiH kaTam arhataH cittam paramam nizprapaQcam Darma tA prAptam saMsAra ucita sarva prakAra sASrava caryA samatikrAntam anena AkAreNa vartate iti durvyavasTApanAt asyAH sUkzma tvam veditavyam
# grol ba'i rnam-par-rig-pa #  ni dgra-bcom-pa # 'i sems mchog-tu #  spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  thob-pa #  'khor-ba #  na 'dris-pa #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i spyod-pa # 'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  la yang-dag-par #  shin-tu-'das-pa #  ste / / rnam-pa #  'dis rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i phyir 'di phra-ba #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
drazwA Adi grahaNena drazwA SrotA GrAtA svAdayitA sprazwA vijQAtA ca iti ezAm grahaNam veditavyam
# mthong-ba #  po la-sogs-pa #  smos-pa # s ni mthong-ba #  po dang nyan-pa #  po dang smon-pa #  po dang myong-ba #  po dang reg-pa #  po dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  po zhes-bya-ba #  'di dag bsdu-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

sa rAga Adi nimitta jQAnAt carita praveSAt
# spyod-pa #  la 'jug-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i sems shes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atIta janma paraMpara Agamana jQAnAt AgatitaH
# 'ongs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'das-pa # 'i tshe-rabs #  gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud de 'ongs-pa #  zhes pa'i phyir ro /
anAgata utpatti gamana jQAnAt gatitaH
# 'gro-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-'ongs-pa # 'i skye-ba # r 'gro-ba #  shes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
trEDAtuka nirmokza upAya jQAnAt nisaraNataH
