# thams-cad #  kyang mngon-par-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni thams-cad #  kyang tha-ma #  gsum gyi yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra rUpI iti rUpam tasya Darmasya Atma svaBAvaH tasmAt asO rUpI na tu rUpa antareNa yuktatvAt
# gzugs ni chos de'i-bdag-nyid #  dang ngo-bo-nyid #  yin te / / de'i-phyir #  de gzugs-can #  yin gyi gzugs gzhan dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ni ma yin te /
yAvat uktam syAt rUpasvaBAvaH iti
# gzugs kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  brjod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
BUta ASrayataH api iti rUpa antara yogAt api rUpitvam iti darSayati upAdAya rUpasya BUta rUpeNa yogAt gata rUpANAm ca parasparam iti
# 'byung-ba #  rten-du-gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs gzhan dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  gzugs-can #  nyid-du #  ston te / / rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  ni 'byung-ba # 'i gzugs-dang-ldan-pa #  dang 'byung-ba # 'i gzugs rnams kyang-na # ng phan tshun ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nAndI samudayaH iti nAndI eva yasya samudayaH tad rUpi na tu yaTA vedanA AdInAm pUrvikA ca nAndaH samudayaH pratyutpannaH ca sparSa AdiH iti / sa pradeSataH sAvayavatvAt / deSa vyAptitaH dikzu pratyAsparaNAt
# dga'-ba # 'i kun-'byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dga'-ba-nyid #  gang-gi #  kun-'byung-ba #  yin pa de gzugs-can #  yin gyi / / ji-ltar #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i kun-'byung-ba #  ni sngon gyi dga'-ba #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i reg-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yang yin pa lta-bu #  ni ma yin no / / phyogs-dang-bcas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni cha-shas #  dang bcas-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yul la khyab-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyogs rnams su lus-kyis #  rgyas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
deSa upadeSataH amuzyAm diSi iti vyavadezwum Sakya tvAt deSa gocarataH kasmiH cit pradeSe sTitasya alaMkaMbanI BAvAt
# yul nye-bar #  bstan du rung-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyogs che-ge-mo-zhig #  na'o zhes bstan-pa # r nus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yul spyod yul du gyur-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyogs-'ga' #  zhig na 'dug-pa # r dmigs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
dvaya sama gocarataH sattva dvayasya kasmiH cit pradeSe sTitasya alam vana uBO= / dvaya sama gocarataH sattva dvayasya sama mAlam vanIBAvAt na tu evam arUpiNaH yaTA Atma anuBavam parEH parigrahItum aSakyatvAt iti
# gnyis spyod yul du 'dzin-pa #  mtshungs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-can #  gnyis mtshungs-pa # r dmigs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  ni de lta ma yin te / / ji-ltar #  bdag-gis #  myong-ba #  bzhin-du #  gzhan dag gis shes-pa # r mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMbanDataH cakzuH vijQAnAH dInAm api paryAyeNa rUpitvam rUpi indriya saMbanDAt
# 'brel-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yang brgyud-pa # s gzugs-can #  nyid de / / dbang-po-gzugs-can #  dang 'brel-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anubanDataH ArUpyANAm pRTagjanAnAm rUpa bIja anubanDAt / prarUpaNataH vitarka vicArANAm AlaMbana prarUpaNAt
# rjes su 'brel-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs-med-par-skyes-pa # 'i so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams la gzugs kyi sa-bon #  rjes-su-'brel-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rab-tu-rtogs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni rtogs-pa #  rnams dmigs-pa #  la rab tu rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vyAbADanataH paQcAnAm skanDAnAm pANi Adi saMsparSEH Soka AdiBiH ca yaTAyogam rUpaNAt bADanAt iti arTaH / saMprApaNataH deSanAyAH arTa nirUpaNAt
# gnod-par-bya-ba #  yin pa'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni phung-po #  lnga po dag la-la # g pa la-sogs-pa # s kun-tu #  reg-pa #  dang mya-ngan #  la-sogs-pa # s ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du gnod-pa # r byar rung-ba # 'i phyir te gnod-par-bya-ba #  yin zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / go-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni bstan-pa # s don la rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMcaya vyavasTAnataH paramANoH UrDvarUpasya sAvayava vyavasTAnAt
# bsags-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni rdul-phra-mo #  las gong-ma # 'i gzugs cha-shas #  dang bcas-pa # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bahirmuKataH kAma avacarasya rUpasya kAma guNa tRzNA saMBUta tvAt
# phyi-rol-du #  bltas-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i gzugs 'dod-pa'i-yon-tan #  la sred-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
antar muKataH rUpa avacarasya rUpasya samApatti citta tRzNA saMBUta tvAt atas eva asya manaH maya tvam veditavyam
# nang-du #  bltas-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs-na-spyod-pa # 'i gzugs de snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems la sred-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir te / / de'i-phyir #  'di yid-las-byung-ba #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
AyatataH pRTagjanasya pUrva anta aparAntayoH paryanta vyavasTAna aBAvAt
# yun-ring-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i gzugs sngon-gyi-mtha' #  dang phyi-ma'i-mtha' # i mu rnam-par-gnas-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
paricCinnataH SEkzasya rUpasya paryantIkRta saMsAra tvAt
# yongs su chad-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni slob-pa # 'i gzugs 'khor-ba # 'i mthar-phyin-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tad kAlataH aSrEkza rUpasya pratyuta pannaBava mAtra avaSezAt
# de'i dus kyi phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-slob-pa # 'i gzugs da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i srid-pa #  tsam zhig las pa'i phyir ro /
nidarSanataH budDa Adi rUpasya saMdarSana mAtra tvAt anizpanna tAm upAdAya
# nges-par #  ston-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni sangs-rgyas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gzugs ni kun-tu #  ston-pa #  tsam du zad kyi grub-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra sarvANi rUpINi vyAvADana rUpitvena
# thams-cad #  kyang gzugs-can #  dag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnod-par-bya-ba # 'i gzugs-can #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
yaTAyogam SezEH veditavyam
# lhag-ma #  rnams ni ci-rigs-su #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
bahirmuKa tA AdayaH tu zaX rUpi BedAH vedanA Adi sADAraNAH veditavyAH / Sizwasya rUpi vat praBedaH iti / iti kaTam / yaTA rUvita dAtmataH api iti vistareNa rUpI iti uktam taTA sa nidarSana tad AtmakaH api sa nidarSanam vistareNa yojayitavyam
# phyi-rol-du #  bltas-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gzugs-can #  gyi rab-tu-dbye-ba #  drug ni tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang thun-mong-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / lhag-ma # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni gzugs-can #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs de'i-bdag-nyid #  kyi phyir zhes-bya-ba #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  do /
tatra sarvANi sa nidarSanAni sarva nidarSana saMbanDa AdinA rUpiNAm api sa nidarSana tvAt
# thams-cad #  kyang bstan-du-yod-pa #  dag go zhes-bya-ba #  ni bstan-du-yod-pa #  dang 'brel-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  rnams kyang bstan-du-yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AvRNoti Avri yatas iti gamana pratibanDa arTena / AvRNoti iti etAvati vaktavye Avriyate ca iti vacanam praBA Adi rUpasya sa pratiGa tva vyavasTApana arTam / tat hi AvriyataH eva na avRNoti iti ezA tasya jAtiH eza svaBAvaH iti arTaH
# sgrib-par-byed-pa #  dang bsgrib-pa # r bya-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / 'gro-ba # 'i gegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir sgrib-par-byed-pa #  zhes de tsam du bstan-pa # s bsgrib-pa # r bya-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig gis 'od la-sogs-pa # 'i gzugs thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # r rnam-pa # r 'jog ste / / de ni bsgrib-pa # r bya-ba #  nyid yin gyi / / sgrib-par-byed-pa #  ni ma yin no / / 'di ni de'i rigs te / / 'di ni ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
paramANoH UrDvam iti ekasya paramANoH apratiGa tvAt
# rdul-phra-rab #  las gong-ma #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rdul-phra-rab #  gcig thogs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yat na samADi vaSa varti rUpam iti samADi vaSena vartamAnasya apratiGa tvAt sama cittaka devatAvata
# gang ting-nge-'dzin-gyi-dbang #  gis ma bsgyur-pa # 'i gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  ni ting-nge-'dzin-gyi-dbang #  bsgyur-ba # 'i gzugs ni thogs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir te / / sems-mnyam-pa # 'i lha bzhin no /
prakopa pada sTAnam yatra ASrayaH AlaMbane vA dvezaH utpadyate
# rab-tu-'khrug-pa # 'i gzhi'i-gnas #  ni gnas sam dmigs-pa #  gang-la #  zhe-sdang #  skye-ba #  ste /
anena ca sa pratiGa arTena sarva ANi sapratiGAni / yaTAyogam vA iti SezEH
# thogs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i don 'dis ni thams-cad #  kyang-thog # s pa dang bcas-pa #  dag go / / yang-na #  ci-rigs-su #  sbyar ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni lhag-ma #  rnams so /
Asravat tad AtmataH AsravANAm sa Asrava tvam Asrava svaBAvena yuktatvAt
# zag-pa #  de'i-bdag-nyid #  kyi phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni zag-pa #  rnams zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  nyid de / / zag-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Asrava saMbanDataH tad sahaBuvAm cita cEttAnAm cakzuH AdInAm ca asra saMprayukta tvAt Asrava Sraya tvAt ca yaTAkramam
# zag-pa #  dang 'brel-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni de dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dang mig la-sogs-pa #  zag-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  dang gnas yin pa'i phyir te go-rims #  bzhin no /
Asrava banDataH kuSala sa AsravANAm tad vaSena punar Bava nirvartanAt
# zag-pa # s bcings-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i dbang gis dge-ba #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  rnams kyang yang-srid-pa #  'grub-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Asrava anubanDataH anya BUmikAnAm api anya BUmi kAsrava dOzWulya ASraya tvAt
# zag-pa # 'i rjes-su-'brel-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa pa gzhan rnams kyang sa pa gzhan gyi zag-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Asrava anukUlyate iti kleSa dOzWulya anugata tve api nirvedya BAgIyAnAm anAsrava tva vyavasTApana arTam sarva Bava vEmuKyena tad pratipakza tvAt
# zag-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams nyon-mongs-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len dang ldan du zin-kyang #  zag-pa-med-pa #  nyid-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir te / / srid-pa #  thams-cad-la #  rgyab kyis bltas-pa # 'i phyir dang de'i gnyen-po #  la bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Asrava anvayataH arhatAm skanDAnAm pOrvajAnmika kleSa saMBUta tvAt / paQca skanDAH sa AsravAH / paQcadaSa GAtavaH antyAn= trIn hitvA
# zag-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni dgra-bcom-pa #  rnams kyi phung-po #  rnams tshe-rabs #  snga-ma # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / khams bco lnga ni tha-ma #  gsum ma-gtogs-pa # 'o /
daSa AyatanAni antye dve hitvAH
# skye-mched #  bcu ni tha-ma #  gnyis ma-gtogs-pa # 'o /
trayANAm DAtUnAm dvayoH ca AyatanayoH pradeSaH sa parivAram Arya mArgam asaMskRtam ca hitvA / Sastra AdAna Adi raNa hetavaH rAga AdayaH raNAH
# khams-gsum #  dang skye-mched #  gnyis kyi phyogs ni 'phags-pa'i-lam #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o / / mtshon-cha #  len-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni 'thab-pa #  ste /
yAvanti sa AsravANi tAvanti saraNAni iti evamAdi tadA anubaMDi arTena veditavyam / punar Bava aDyavasAna hetavaH rAga AdayaH Amizam / kaTam dvezasya punarBava aDyavasAna hetu tvam
# 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rgyu yin-pas #  'thab-pa # 'o / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  ji-snyed-pa #  'thab-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'ang de snyed do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni de'i rjes su 'brel-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / yang-srid-pa #  la lhag-par-chags-pa # 'i rgyu nyid de /
vyAvadAnika Darma dvezeNa punarBava aDyavasAnAt
# rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i chos la zhe-sdang-ba # s srid-pa #  la lhag-par-chags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kAma guNa aDyavasAna hetavaH rAga AdayaH greDaH
# 'dod-pa'i-yon-tan #  lnga la lhag-par-chags-pa # 'i rgyu yin-pas #  zhe na pa'o /
kIdRSena dvezeNa tat aDyavasAnam
# zhe-sdang #  ci-'dra-ba #  zhig gis de-la #  lhag-pa # r chags shen /
nEzkramya dvezeNa
# mngon bar 'byung-ba #  la zhe-sdang-ba # s so /
kAmakAreNa saMmuKIBAvaH vimuKIBAvaH ca na asaMskRtasya saMBavati nitya tvAt
# 'dod-pa-bzhin-du #  byed-pa # s mngon-du-phyogs-pa #  dang rgyab-kyis-lta-ba #  ni 'dus-ma-byas #  la mi srid de / / rtag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na eva saMskRta na asaMskRtasya dvaya avyatirekAt yat uktam dvayam idam saMskRtam ca asaMskRtam ca iti / tat kaTam dvayam evam eva Bavati iti
# 'dus byas kyang ma yin 'dus-ma-byas #  kyang ma-yin-pa #  ni 'di gnyis las gud-na #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'dus byas dang 'dus-ma-byas #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di gnyis so zhes gang gsungs-pa #  de ji-ltar #  gnyis kho-nar #  'gyur zhe na /
kAmakAra saMmuKIBAva arTena saMskRtam eva iti vaktavyam
# 'dod-pa-bzhin-du #  byed-pa # s mngon-du-phyogs-pa #  dang rgyab-kyis-lta-ba # 'i phyir 'dus byas zhes-bya'o #  /

# las dang nyon-mongs-pa # s mngon-pa # r 'dus-ma-byas #  pa'i phyir 'dus-ma-byas #  zhes bya ste / / gnyis las gud-na #  med do /

paraMpara utpannam janma prabanDe

avasTA antara utpannam kalala Adi avasTAsu vyADi Adi avasTAsu ca

# ma-phrad-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang yid do /

# phrad-nas #  'dzin-pa #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i dbang-po # 'o / / da-ltar #  gyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  so-so-ba #  yul so-sor-nges-pa #  'dzin-pa #  ni dbang-po-lnga #  las byung-ba # 'o /
sva sAmAnya lakzaNasya sarva kAlasya sarvasya vizayasya grAhakam zazWa indriya jam
# rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  dus-thams-cad-pa # 'i yul-thams-cad #  'dzin-pa #  ni dbang-po #  drug las byung pa'o /
pratyaya sAmagrayA vijQAnasya utpattim aDikRtya prajQaptyAm grAhaka upacAraH veditavyaH na tu BUta arTena vyApAra tvAt DarmANAm iti
# rkyen tshogs nas rnam-par-shes-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-te #  btags-nas #  'dzin-pa # 'i nye-bar-'dogs-pa # r rig-par-bya-ba # 'i yang-dag-pa'i-don #  du na chos-rnams #  byed-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yat tAvat grAhakam grAhyam api tat cakzuH AdInAm api manaH vijQAnena grAhya tvAt
# 'dzin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  gzung-ba #  yang de yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  yang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # s gzung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
grAhaka gocaraH eva iti avaDAraNam cEtasika vyudAsa arTam
# 'dzin-pa # 'i spyod yul nyid ces bsnan pa ni sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir ro /
SrutacintA maya tad anuDarma pratipatti saMgRhItasya ababahirmuKa tvam nizyanda Darma hetuka tvAt tad vaSena nirvANa Adi alaMkaMbanataH drazwavyam
# thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  dang bsam ba las byung-ba #  dang de'i rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa # s yongs-su-bsdus-pa #  ni phyi-rol #  tu bltas-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  nyid de / / rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de'i dbang gis mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la dmigs-pa # r blta'o /
nizyanda DarmaH punar budDa AdInAm aDigama anvayAH deSanA veditavyA
# rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i chos ni sangs-rgyas #  la-sogs-pa # s thugs-su-chud-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i brtan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
catvAraH DAtavaH GrANa vijQAna DAtuH ganDa DAtuH jihvA vijQAna DAtuH rasaDAtuH ca
# khams bzhi ni sna'i rnams par shes-pa # 'i khams dang lce'i-rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i khams dang dri'i khams dang ro'i khams so /

# skye-mched #  gnyis ni dri dang ro'i skye-mched #  do / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  dag gi phyogs-gcig #  ni gang-'dod-pa # 'i khams su bsdus-pa # 'o /
daSAnAm DAtUnAm iti saptAnAm vijQAna DAtUnAm rUpa Sabda Darma DAtUnAm ca

# skye-mched #  bzhi ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  do /
hetu Pala upayogataH iti utpanna tvAt nirudDa tvAt ca yaTAkramam
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  spyad zin dang zhes-bya-ba #  ni skyes zin-pa #  dang 'gags zin-pa # 'i phyir te go-rims #  bzhin no /

# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r byed-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  shin-tu-'das-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  sems kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r byed-pa # 'i mthu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
hetu parigraha vinASataH vAsanAm sTApayitvA vinazwa tvAt
# rgyu yongs-su-bzung-nas #  zhig zhes-bya-ba #  ni bag-chags #  gzhan nas zhig-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# 'bras-bu #  dang rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  yod-pa #  dang med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  na di ltar gyi dus na des bskyed-pa # 'i bag-chags #  yod-pa #  dang de 'jog-par-byed-pa # 'i rdzas-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
smara saMkalpa AdInAm nimitta tvam AlaMbana mAtra BAvAt aveditavyam
# dran-pa # 'i kun-tu-rtog-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  ni mtshan-ma #  ni dmigs-pa #  tsam du yod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sarvezAm eka deSaH anAgata pratyutpannA asaMskRta varjaH / hetO sati anutpannataH iti asaMskRtAt viSezaNa arTam tat haya nud pannam api sanna hetumat iti / labDa sva lakzaNataH anirvRtta svaBAva tvAt
# thams-cad-kyi #  phyogs-gcig #  ces bya-ba #  ni ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o / / rgyu yod kyang ma-byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dus-ma-byas #  las bye-brag #  tu dbye-ba # 'i phyir te / / de ni ma byung la rgyu-dang-ldan-pa #  yang ma yin no / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ma-thob-pa #  ni / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  ma-grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
hetu Pala anupayogataH tad bIjasya akRta kRtya tvAt tasya ca anutpanna tvAt / hetu Pala upayoga anupayogataH punar anivartya tvAt asTita tvAt ca
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  ma-spyad-pa #  ni de'i sa-bon #  gyi bya-ba #  ma-byas-pa #  dang de 'ang ma-skyes-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  spyad-zin-pa #  dang spyad ma-zin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yang mi 'grub-pa #  dang yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atIta anAgata praBAvana nimittataH pratyutpannam aDizWAya atIta anAgata prajQapteH
# 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa # r rab tu gzhag-pa # 'i rgyu zhes-bya-ba #  ni da-ltar-byung-ba #  la brten-te #  / / 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa # r btags-pa # 'i phyir te /
yat tAm avasTAm prApsyati tat anAgatam

# gang thob zin-pa #  de ni 'das-pa # 'o /
kAritra pratyupasTAnataH cakzuH AdInAm vijQAna ASraya Adi BAvAt
# byed-pa #  nye-bar-gnas-pa # s kyang zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i gnas la-sogs-pa # r yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atIta nirdeSa aDikAreNa idam api jQApyate kim arTa BagavatA atIta AdIni eva trINi kaTA vastUni vyavasTApitAni na nirvANam iti / nirvANasya pratyAtma vedanIya tayA niraBilApyatAm upAdAya kaTayitum aSakya tvAt iti arTaH dRzwa Srutam atavijQAta vyavahArANAm BUta Bavya vartamAna aDizWAna tvAt
# 'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i skabs kyis 'di'ang ston te / / ci'i-phyir #  bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis 'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gsum po nyid gtam gyi gzhir gtam gzhir rnam-pa # r gzhag gi mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ni ma yin zhe na / / mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba #  ni so-so #  rang-gi #  rig-par-bya-ba #  dang brjod-du-med-pa #  nyid kyi phyir te / / brjod-pa # r mu nus zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / byung-ba #  dang 'byung-ba #  dang da-ltar #  ni mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang bye-brag-phyed-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tha-snyad #  rnams kyi gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# rang-bzhin-gyis #  so-so # r ma-brtags-pa # r zhes-bya-ba #  ni rang-gi #  dang gis te / / dge-ba'i-bshes-gnyen #  la-sogs-pa # 'i stobs kyis ma yin zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
ruciH saMtizWate iti na kevalam ruciH eva upapatti prAtilamBikA kim tarhi saha tEH SradDA AdiBiH iti
# 'dod-pa #  kun-tu #  gnas-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni skye-ba # s thob-pa # 'i 'dod-pa #  'ba'-zhig #  ma yin gyi / / dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang lhan-cig-tu # 'o /
kuSalasya BAvanA sarve Sruta maya AdayaH kuSalAH Darma AveditavyAH / svarga AXya kula upapatti parigrahAByAm aByudaya hetum darSyati / vyavadAna anukalya parigraheNa prApti hetum iti / vidUzaNa apratipkza AdayaH parastAt nirdekzyante
# dge-ba #  sgom-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  thams-cad #  dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o / / mtho-ris #  dang phyug-po # 'i rigs su skye-ba #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  gnyis kyis ni mngon-par-mtho-ba # 'i rgyu ston to / / rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa # s ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  thob-pa'i-rgyu #  ston to / / rnam-par-sun-'byin-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ni 'og nas 'chad do / / de-dag #  kyang gang zhe na / / de-la #  rnam-par-sun-'byin-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i 'dus byas rnams la nyes-dmigs-su-lta-ba #  ste / / des-na # ng dang 'bras la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # s nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  sun-'byin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / spong-ba'i-gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sbyor-ba #  dang de-ma-thag-pa # 'i lam ste / / de-dag #  gis nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gzhi'i gnyen-po #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba'i-lam #  rnams te / / de-dag #  gis spong-ba # 'i thob-pa #  kun-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / thag bsring-ba # 'i gnyen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i gong-ma # 'i lam ste /
tad anyaH kleSa upakleSaH duScarita samutTApakaH iti sa punar yaH kAmAvacaraH anEH sargikaH nEHsargikaH tu yaH duScarita samutTApakaH saH akuSalaH / tad anyaH nivRta avyAkRtaH veditavyaH
# de sngar spangs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  thag bsring-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nyes-par-spyod-pa #  kun-nas-slong-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i rang-'khrungs #  ma-yin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang rang-'khrungs #  las ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  kun-nas-slong-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de mi-dge-ba # 'o / / de-las-gzhan-pa #  ni bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

# de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  rnams kyi phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o / / khams bzhi dang skye-mched #  gnyis ma-gtogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bshad ma-thag #  pa'o /
tad anyezAm skanDa DAtu AyatanAnAm eka deSaH kAmarUpya avara anAsrava varjyaH
# de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  rnams kyi phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o /
caturNA skanDAnAm vedanA AdInAm
# phung-po #  bzhi zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
trayANAm DAtUnAm manaH Darma manaH vijQAna DAtUnAm
# khams-gsum #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam-pa # r shes ba'i khams so /
dvayoH AyatanayoH manaH Darma AyatanayoH
# skye-mched #  gnyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  de /
pradeSaH kAmarUpA avacarAn Asrava varjyaH
# de-dag #  gi phyogs-gcig #  ni 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs-na-spyod-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o /
eka deSa vErAgyam BUmim aDikRtya yAvat azwamasya kleSa prakArasya prahANAt
# phyogs-gcig #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni sa'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / sa brgyad pa'i bar-du #  nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sakala vErAgyam nava masya prahANAt
# mtha'-dag #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni dgu pa spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
satkAya vErAgyam vA punar aDikRtya SEkzasya eka deSa vErAgyam aSEkzasya sakala vErAgyam veditavyam / prativeDa vErAgyam darSana mArgeNa / upaGAta vErAgyam lOkikena mArgeNa / samudDAtavErAgyam loka uttareNa iti veditavyam
# yang 'jig-tshogs #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  slob-pa #  ni phyogs-gcig #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid do / / mi-slob-pa #  ni mtha'-dag #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / rtog-pa # s 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis so / / gnod-pa # 'i 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  gyis so /
daSa vErAgyANi iti atra prAtikUlya arTaH vErAgya arTaH veditavyaH na avaSyam prahANa arTaH / uccataram sTAnam prAptavataH nihInesTAne iti uccataram nagara SrEzWayAdi sTAnam prAptavataH grAma mahattara Adi sTAne nihIne / bAlAnAm nirvANaH iti tasya SAnta tva ajQAnAt satkAyABiH aFgAt ca / pratilabDa darSana mArgasya trEDAtukaH iti saMskAra duHKa tAm parijQAtavataH sarva sAhasra vastu nirvedAt / prakRtyAH vErAgyam prakRti vErAgyam yAvat prahANena vErAgyam prahANa vErAgyam iti pada vigraha jAtiH veditavyayA
# legs-par #  gnon-pa # 'i 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid ces bya-ba #  ni 'jig-rten #  la 'das-pa # 'i phyir nyid kyis 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i bcu zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  mi-'phrod-pa # r 'dzin-pa # 'i don ni 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid kyi don-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / gdon-mi-za-bar #  spong-ba # 'i don-du #  ni ma yin no / / thabs shin-tu #  chen-po #  thob-pa #  thabs dma'-ba #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni grong-khyer #  gyi gtso bo la-sogs-pa #  dang grong dpon la-sogs-pa #  lta-bu # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / byis-pa #  rnams mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la #  zhi-ba #  nyid-du #  mi-shes-pa #  dang 'jig-tshogs #  la mngon bar chags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  thob-pa # r khams-gsum-pa #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'du-byed #  sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid-du #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  zag-pa #  dang bcas ba'i dngos-po-thams-cad #  la yid 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
mokza prayuktasya kuSalam SEkzam iti saMBRta saMBAra avasTAyAH praBRti mokza arTa prayuktasya veditavyam
# thar-pa #  la brtson pa'i dge-ba #  ni bslab-pa # r blta'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni tshogs-bsags-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / thar-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir brtson par rig-par-bya # 'o /
saMBRta saMBAra avasTA punar ADigAmika mokza BAgIya avasTA veditavyA
# tshogs-bsags-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni mngon bar 'gro-ba #  thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
daSAnAm DAtUnAm vijQAna rUpa Sabda Darma DAtUnAm
# khams bcu zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos-kyi-khams #  rnams so /
caturNAm AyatanAnAm rUpa Sabda manaH Darma AyatanAnAm
# skye-mched #  bzhi zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  rnams so /
SikzAyAm nizWA gatasya iti aDiSIlam aDicittam aDiprajQam ca SikzAyAm nizWA gatasya arhataH iti arTaH
# bslabs-pa # 'i mthar-phyin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni lhag-pa'i-tshul-khrims #  dang lhag-pa'i-sems #  dang lhag-pa'i-shes-rab #  ni bslab-pa # 'o / / mthar-phyin-pa #  ni dgra-bcom-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
pRTagjanasya kuSala Adikam iti mokza prayukta varjasya / sa hi SikzAyAm aBiSikzaNAt SEkzaH ucyate iti
# so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni thar-pa #  la brtson pa ma-gtogs-pa # 'o / / de ni bslab-pa #  la slob-pa # s slob-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
SEkzasya klizwa avyAkRtam iti atra klizwam akuSalam nivRta avyAkRtam ca yaTAsaMBavam / avyAkRtam punar anivRta avyAkRtam veditavyam
# slob-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ni mi-dge-ba # 'o / / lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  ni bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  ste / / ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyor ro / / mi-slob-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
parikalpitA klizwA dRzwiH asat Darma SravaNa pUrvikA paQca dazwayaH
# nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi lta-ba #  kun-tu #  brtags-pa #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni dam-pa'i-chos #  ma-yin-pa #  nyan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i lta-ba #  lnga po dag go /
parikalpita grahaNam sahaja satkaya anta grAha dRzwi vyudAsa arTam / anta grAha dRzwiH kIdRSI sahajA / ucCeda dRzwiH yatas aBisamaya prayuktasya uttrAsaH Bavati aTa kaH tarhi me AtmA iti
# kun-tu #  brtags-pa #  smos-pa # s ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i 'jig-tshogs #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir ro / / mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  la zhugs-pa #  can nga'i bdag gang yin zhes skrag-pa #  gang-la # s byung-ba # 'o /
dRzwi sTAnam dRzwi sahaBuvaH DarmAH tad vIjam ca taTA eva vicikitsA sTAnam api veditavyam
# lta-ba # 'i gnas zhes-bya-ba #  ni lta-ba #  dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i chos-rnams #  dang de'i sa-bon #  no / / the-tshom #  gyi gnas kyang de-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
ye ca dRzwO vipratipannAH kleSa upakleSAH iti ye dRzwi muKena pravRttA tad alaMkaMbanAH ca rAga AdayaH
# lta-ba #  log-par-zhugs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dag ces bya-ba #  ni lta-ba # 'i sgo nas zhugs-pa #  dang de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  pa gang-yin-pa # 'o /
sarvezAm eka deSaH BAvanA prahAta vyAna Asrava varjaH
# thams-cad-kyi #  phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsgoms-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o /
darSana prahAta vyAviparyayeNa sa AsravAH iti parikalpita klizwa dRzwa yAdikAt anye sa AsravAH iti arTaH
# mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  las bzlog-pa #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi lta-ba #  kun-tu #  brtags-pa #  las gzhan-pa # 'i zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
atra punar sa Asrava grahaNena nirveDa BAgIyAnAm api grahaNam veditavyam dOzWulya anubanDa arTena
# 'dir zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  smos-pa # s ni / / des-pa # r 'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams kyang bsdu-ba # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / gnas-ngan-len #  gyi rjes su 'brel-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sarvezAm eka deSaH darSana prahAta vyAna Asrava varjaH
# thams-cad-kyi #  phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  ni zag-pa-med-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'o /
skanDAnAm eka deSaH aprahAtavyaH lokottaraH mArgaH tad pRzwa labDaH ca / daSAnAm DAtUnAm caturNA ca AyatanAnAm ekadeSaH iti sa ca saMskRtam ca / kIdRSaH rUpa Sabda DAtU na prahAtavyO / aSEkzasya kuSala kAya vAc karma svaBAvO
# phung-po #  rnams kyi phyogs-gcig #  spang-bar-bya-ba #  ma-yin-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam dang de'i-rjes-la #  thob-pa # 'o / / khams bcu dang skye-mched #  bzhi zhes-bya-ba #  ni de dang 'dus-ma-byas #  so / / ci-'dra-ba # 'i gzugs dang sgra'i khams spang-bar-bya-ba #  ma yin zhe na / / mi-slob-pa # 'i lus-dang-ngag-gi-las #  kyi rang-bzhin #  no / / chos-kyi-khams #  dang skye-mched #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  ma-gtogs-par #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  do / / bam po gsum-pa #  / / bdag dang chos rgyu-med-pa #  dang dbang-phyug #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # r mngon bar zhen-pa #  spang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  gang gsungs-pa #  ni 'di yod-pa # s / / 'di 'byung / / 'di skyes-pa # 'i phyir 'di skye-ba #  ste /
avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti evamAdi
# 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs so /
tatra asmin sati idam Bavati nirIha pratyaya utpattim upAdAya
# de-la #  'di yod-pa # s 'di 'byung zhes-bya-ba #  ni g-yo-ba #  med-pa # 'i rkyen las byung-ba #  phyir te /
sati kevalam pratyaye Palam Bavati na tu Pala utpAdanam prati pratyayasya kAcid iha iti arTaH
# rkyen yod-na #  'bras-bu #  'byung-ba # r zad kyi 'bras-bu #  'byung-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir rkyen la g-yo-ba #  ni ci-yang #  med ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
asya utpAdAt idam utpadyate anitya pratyaya utpattim upAdAya na hi anutpAdi kAraNAt kiMcid utpadyamAnam kArya sidDam iti kRtvA
# 'di skyes-pa # 'i phyir 'di skye ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-rtag-pa # 'i rkyen las byung-ba # 'i phyir te / / ma-byung-ba # 'i rgyu las 'bras-bu #  'byung-ba #  ma-grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti evamAdi samarTa pratyaya utpattim upAdAya nirIhaka tva anitya tve api sati na yatas kutaScid pratyayAt sarvam eva Palam utpadyate kiMtarhi samarTAt / tat yaTA vidyA atas saMskArAH yAvat jAtitaH jarA maraNam iti
# ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni nus-pa # 'i rkyen las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / g-yo-ba #  med cing mi-rtag-pa #  yin-du-zin #  kyang rkyen gang-yang-rung-ba #  las 'bras-bu #  thams-cad #  mi 'byung gi nus-pa # 'i rkyen las 'byung ste 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  'byung-ba #  nas skye-ba #  las rga shi 'byung-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
yAni avidyA AdIni dvAdaSa aFgAni viBaktAni tAni eva punar samasya catvAri aFgAni Bavanti AkzepAH Fga AdIni
# ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yan-lag-bcu-gnyis #  rnam-par-phye-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni mdor bsdus yan-lag #  bzhir 'gyur te / / 'phen-pa # 'i yan-lag #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
etAvat ca pravRtti nirdeSe nirdezwavyam yat uta hetu kAle yena Akzipyate yat ca Akzipyate Pala kAle yena aBinirvartyate yat ca aBinirvatyate tat etat sarvam eBiH aFga EniH dizwam veditavyam
# 'byung-ba #  bstan-pa #  la ni 'di dag tsam zhig bstan-pa # r bya ste / / 'di-ltar #  rgyu'i-dus #  na gang-gi #  'phen-pa #  dang gang 'phen-pa #  dang 'bras-bu'i-dus #  na gang-gis #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r dang gnang mngon-par-'grub-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  thams-cad #  ni yan-lag #  'di rnams kyis bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra Akzepaka aFgam avidyA saMskArAH vijQAnam ca anAgata janma aBinirvRttaye satyezu ajQAna pUrvakeNa karmaNA citta vAsanA arTena
# de-la #  'phen-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ni ma-rig-pa #  dang 'du-byed #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / ma-'ongs-pa # 'i skye-ba #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r 'gyur-pa # r bden-pa #  rnams mi-shes-pa #  sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i las kyi bag-chags #  sems la bsgo-ba # 'i phyir ro /
Akzipta aFgam nAma rUpam zaXa Ayatanam sparSaH vedanA ca tayA citta vAsanayA nAma rUpa AdInAm mAyatyAm pUrvotara saMniSraya krameNa aBinirvRtaye bIja puzwitaH
# 'phangs-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ni ming-dang-gzugs #  dang skye-mched-drug #  dang reg-pa #  dang tshor-ba #  ste / / sems kyi bag-chags #  kyi ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  snga-ma #  la phyi-ma #  brten-nas #  rim-gyis #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r bya-ba # 'i ched du sems kyi bag-chags #  de-dag #  gi sa-bon #  brtas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aBinirvartaka aFgam tRzNA upAdAnam BavaH ca aprahINakAma Adi tRzNA divasena kAma Adizu su carita duScarita prakAra rati pUrvakeNa Canda rAgeNa sa upAdAne vijQAne sati maraNa avasTAyAm Pala dAnam prati Candara AgAnurUpya antara karma vAsana aBimuKIBAvAt
# mngon-par-'grub-pa # r byed-pa # 'i yan-lag #  gi sred-pa #  dang len-pa #  dang srid-pa #  ste / / 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i srid-pa #  ma-spangs-pa # 'i dbang gis 'dod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r legs-par-spyod-pa #  dang nyes-par-spyod-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  la goms-pa # r dga'-ba #  sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  kyis nye-bar-len-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa # r yod-pa # r gyur ba na 'chi-ba # 'i dus na 'bras-bu #  'byin-pa # r bya-ba #  la 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i las gang-yang-rung-ba # 'i bag-chags #  mngon-du-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aBinirvRtti aFgam jAtiH jarA maNam ca tena prakAreNa karma antara vAsanA aBimuKye sati anyatarasmin gati yoni Adi Beda Binne nikAya saBAge yaTAkzipte nAma rUpa Adi nirvRtteH
# mngon-par-grub-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ni skye-ba #  dang rga shi ste / / rnam-pa #  des de-la # s gzhan gyi bag-chags #  mngon du gyur na ji-ltar #  'phangs-pa #  bzhin-du #  'gro-ba #  dang skye-gnas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  tha-dad-pa # 'i ris-mthun-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba # r ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jAti jarA maraNa vacanam saMskRta lakzaNa traya aDikAreNa udvejana arTam
# skye-ba #  dang rga shi smos-pa #  ni 'dus-byas-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  gsum gyi skabs kyis skyo-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
jarA maraNasya eka aFga karaNam vinA api jarAm maraNa saMBavAt
# rga-ba #  dang 'chi-ba #  yan-lag #  gcig-tu #  bya-ba #  ni rga-ba #  med-pa # r yang 'chi-ba'i-srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na tu evam jarAyu jAyAm yonO vinA nAma rUpa AdiBiH zaXa Ayatana AdInAm saMBavaH iti ezAm pRTak aFgIkaraNam veditavyam / aFga pratyaya tva vyavasTAnam caturaH pratyayAn aDikRtya
# mngal nas skye-ba'i-gnas #  su ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # r skye-mched-drug #  la-sogs-pa #  'byung-ba #  ni de lta ma yin te / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  yan-lag #  so-so # r bya-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / yan-lag #  rkyen nyid-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni rkyen bzhi'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
tatra tAvat avidyA saMskArANAm pUrva utpanna AvAsanataH hetu pratyayaH tad pariBAvita saMtAna utpannAnAm karmaNAm punarBava aBisaMskaraNa sAmarTyAt tad kAla samudAcAriNI
# de-la #  ma-rig-pa #  ni 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rkyen te / / snga logs su byung-ba # 'i bag-chags #  kyis rgyu'i-rkyen #  to / / des yongs-su-bsgos-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i las rnams yang-srid-pa # r mngon bar 'du-byed #  par nus-pa # 'i phyir te / / de'i tshe kun-tu-'byung-ba # 'i tshul can no /
AveDataH samanantara pratyayaH tad Akzepaka viSezeNa saMskAra srota anupravRtteH
# shugs kyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen te / / de'i tshe 'phen-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis 'du-byed #  kyi rgyun gyi rgyun-chags-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
manaskArataH AlaMbana pratyayaH mUXa avasTAyAH agra tA AdiBiH ayoniSoma manaskAra alaMkaMbanI BAvAt
# yid-la-byed-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  te / / rmongs-pa # 'i dus na mchog la-sogs-pa # r tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa # s dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sahaBAvataH aDipati pratyayaH tad ADipatyena tad saMprayuktAyAH cetanAyAH viparIta alaMbana aBisaMskaraNAt
# lhan-cig #  byung-ba # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-po'i-rkyen #  te / / de'i dbang gis de dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dmigs-pa #  la phyin-ci-log #  tu mngon bar 'du-byed #  pa'i phyir ro /
avidyA Bave sattvAn saMmohayati tad AvRtteH pUrva anta aparAnta maDya antAnAm yaTA BUta aparijQAnAt / yatas evam vicikitsati kim nu aham aBUvam atite aDvani Ahosvit na aBUvam iti evamAdi / pratyayaH ca Bavati saMskArANAm tad vaSena punarBavika karma upacayAt
# ma-rig-pa #  ni srid-pa #  la sems-can #  rnams rmongs-pa # r byed ces bya-ba #  ni des bsgribs-pa #  rnams sngon-gyi-mtha' #  dang phyi-ma'i-mtha' #  dang-ba # r gyi mtha' yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yongs su mi-shes-pa # 'i phyir te / / 'di-ltar #  ci bdag 'das-pa'i-dus-na #  byung-ba #  zhig gam / / 'on te ma-byung-ba #  zhig snyam pa la-sogs-pa #  de-ltar #  the-tshom-za-ba # 'o / / 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rkyen kyang yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i dbang gis yang-srid-pa # 'i las la-sogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMskArA gatizu sattvAna viBajanti karma vaSena sattvAnAm gati antara gamana vEcitryAt
# 'du-byed-rnams #  ni yang 'gro-ba #  rnams su sems-can #  dag rnam-pa # r 'byed ces bya-ba #  ni las kyi dbang gis sems-can #  rnams 'gro-ba-gzhan #  du 'gro-ba #  sna-tshogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayAH ca Bavanti vijQAnasya vAsanAyAH AyatyAH nAma rUpa aBinirvRttaye bIja pozaNAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bag-chags #  kyi rkyen kyang yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyi-ma-la #  ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  'grub-par-'gyur-ba # r sa-bon #  gso-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vijQAnam karma banDam DArayati saskArAH hita vAsanA asaha utpatteH
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni sems-can #  rnams kyi las kyi 'ching-ba #  'dzin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'du-byed #  kyis bskyed-pa # 'i bag-chags #  dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayaH ca Bavati nAma rUpasya mAtuH kukzO vijQAna avakrAntyA nAma rUpa vivRdDi gamanAt
# ming-dang-gzugs #  kyi rkyen kyang yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma'i-mngal #  du zhugs na ming-dang-gzugs #  kyi lus 'phel-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
nAma rUpam Atma BAvam sattvAn grAhayati tad nivRttyA sattvAnAm nikAya saBAga antaraBa janAt
# ming-dang-gzugs #  ni sems-can #  rnams lus len du 'jug ces bya-ba #  ni de grub na sems-can #  rnams ris-mthun-pa # r gzhan la brten-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nAma rUpa AdInAm zaXa Ayatana Adi pratyaya BAvaH pUrva aFga saMniSrayeNa uttara aFga nirvRttitaH drazwavyaH
# ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa #  skye-mched-drug #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rkyen du 'gyur-ba #  ni yan-lag #  snga-ma #  la brten-nas #  yang lag phyi-ma #  'grub-pa # r blta'o /
zaXa Ayatanam Atma BAva paripUrim ca sattvAn grAhayati tad nivRttO= indriya antarO= EkalyAt
# skye-mched-drug #  ni sems-can #  rnams lus rdzogs-pa # r len du 'jug-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de 'grub na dbang-po #  gzhan ma-tshang-ba-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayaH ca Bavati sparSasya / sparSaH vizaya upaBoge sattvAn pravartayati tad muKena suKa vedanIya Adi triviDa vizaya upaBogAt
# reg-pa #  ni yul gyi longs-spyod #  la sems-can #  rnams 'dzud-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i sgo nas bde-ba-myong-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yul rnam-pa-gsum #  la longs-spyod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayaH ca Bavati vedanAyAH / vedanA janma upaBoge ca sattvAn pravartayati tad aDizWAnena izwa Adi karma vipAka upaBogAt
# tshor-ba #  ni skye-ba # 'i longs-spyod #  la sems-can #  rnams 'dzud-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la #  brten-nas #  'dod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  la nye-bar-spyod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayaH ca Bavati tRzNAyAH tad saMprayoga Adi aBilAza muKena tRzNA utpatteH
# srid-pa # 'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni de dang phrad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r 'dod-pa # 'i sgo nas sred-pa #  'byung pa'i phyir ro /
tRzNA janmani sattvAn Akarzati tad vaSena janma antara srotaH anupacCedAt
# sred-pa #  ni sems-can #  rnams kyi skye-ba #  'dren-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i dbang gis tshe-gzhan #  du brgyud-pa #  rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayaH ca Bavati upAdAnasya AsvAda prArTanA muKena kAma Adizu Canda rAga pravRtteH
# len-pa # 'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni ro myang-ba # r 'dod-pa # 'i sgo nas 'dod-pa #  la sogs ba la 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
upAdAnam punarBava AdAnAya sa upAdAnam ca sattvAnAm vijQAnam karoti naraka Adi gati viSizwa punarBava pratisaMDaye karma vAsanA niyamAt / pratyayaH ca Bavati Bavasya tad vaSena saMskAra vAsanaya vRtti lABAt
# len-pa #  ni yang-srid-pa #  len-pa # 'i phyir sems-can #  rnams kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  nye-bar-len-pa #  dang bcas-pa # r byed ces bya-ba #  ni sems-can #  dmyal-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'gro-ba #  bye-brag #  can du yang-srid-pa # 'i nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i las kyi bag-chags #  nges-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / srid-pa # 'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i dbang gis 'du-byed #  kyi bag-chags #  'byung-ba #  rnyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
BavaH punarBave sattva anaBimuKIkaroti anantara gati antarA vAhanAt pratyayaH ca Bavati jAteH tatas nikAya saBAga antara nirvRtteH
# srid-pa #  ni yang-srid-pa # r sems-can #  rnams mngon-du-phyogs-pa # r byed ces bya-ba #  ni de ma-thag-tu #  'gro-ba-gzhan #  'dren-pa # 'i phyir ro / / skye-ba'i-rkyen #  kyang yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la # s ris-mthun-pa #  gzhan 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
jAtiH nAma rUpa Adi AnupUrvyA sattva anaBinirvartayati uttarottara avasTA antara AvAhanAt
# skye-ba #  ni ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  sems-can #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r byed-pa #  ni phyi-ma-phyi-ma # 'i gnas-skabs #  gzhan 'dren-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyayaH ca Bavati jarA maraNasya jAtO satyAm tad prabanDasya anyaTA tva vinASa saMBavAt
# rga shi'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni skye-ba #  yod-na #  de'i rgyus gzhan-du-'gyur-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jarA maraNam punar punar vayaH pariNAmena jIvita pariNAmena ca sattvAn yojayati yOvana AyuzA vinASena yojanAt
# rga shi ni yang-dang-yang #  na tshod 'gyur-ba #  dang srog 'gyur-ba #  la sems-can #  rnams sbyor-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni dar la bab-pa #  dang tshe rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa #  la sbyor-ba # 'o /
vijQAnasya karma saMkleSa saMgrahaNam saMskAra vAsanA praBAvita tvAt vijQAna aFgasyaH
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  las kyi kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r bsdu-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yan-lag #  'du-byed #  kyi bag-chags #  kyis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
nizkartRkA arTaH ISvara Adi kartR rahita tvAt
# byed-pa-po #  med-pa # 'i don zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang-phyug #  la spags-pa # 'i byed-pa-po #  dang bral-ba #  phyir ro /
sa hetuka arTaH avidyA Adi hetuka tvAt / niHsatva arTaH svayam anAtma tvAt / paratantra arTaH pratyaya aDIna tvAt / nirIha arTaH pratyayAnAm nirvyApAra tvAt / anitya arTaH aSASvat tvAt / kzaNikA arTaH utpatti kAlAt pareNa anavasTAnAt
# rgyu-dang-bcas-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i don zhes ba ba ni ma-rig-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / sems-can-med-pa'i-don #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  bdag-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzhan-gyi-dbang-gis #  don zhes-bya-ba #  ni skyen la rag-las-pa # 'i phyir ro / / g-yo-ba #  med-pa # 'i don zhes-bya-ba #  ni rkyen rnams byed-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mi-rtag-pa'i-don #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ther zug ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / skad-cig-ma'i-don #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni skyes-pa # 'i dus las pha rol tu mi-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
hetu Pala prabanDa anupacCeda arTaH kAraNa kzaNa niroDa sama kAlam kArya kzaNa utpAdAt
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # 'i rgyud rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i don zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu'i skad-cig #  'gag-pa #  dus mnyam-du #  'bras-bu # 'i skad-cig #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
anurUpa hetu Pala parigraha arTaH sarvatas sarvasya asaMBavAt
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  mthun ba'i don zhes-bya-ba #  ni thams-cad-la # s thams-cad #  mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
vicitra hetu Pala arTaH aneka eka jAtIyAt kAraNAt eka jAtIya kArya utpatteH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  sna-tshogs #  kyi don zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu du-ma #  dang gcig gi rnam-pa #  las 'bras-bu # 'i rnam-pa #  gcig dang du-ma #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pratiniyata hetu Pala arTaH saMtAna antarA PalanAt
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  so-sor-nges-pa # 'i don zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu gzhan-las #  'bras-bu #  gzhan mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
punar eBiH eva arTaH pratItyasamutpAdasya paQcaviDam gAmBIrya veditavyam
# yang don 'di dag gis rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  rnams pa ldas zab-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
hetu gAmBIrya vizama hetu ahetuvAda pratipakzena dvAByAm arTAByAm
# rgyus zab-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu # d dang rgyu-med-par-smra-ba # 'i gnyen-po # r don gnyis kyis zab bo /
lakzaNa gAmBIrya nirAtmaka tayA eka arTena
# mtshan-nyid #  kyis zab-pa #  ni bdag-med-pa #  nyid kyis te don gcig gis so /
utpatti gAmBIrya pratyayeByaH Pala utpattO= api atakRta tayA dvAByAm arTAByAm
# skye pas zab ba ni rkyen rnams las 'bras-bu #  'byung-ba #  yang des ma-byas-pa # 'i phyir te / / don gnyis kyis so /
sTiti gAmBIryam avyavasTAnAm sTiti ABAsanAt dvAByAm arTAByAm
# gnas-pa # s zab-pa #  ni gnas med kyang gnas-pa # r snang-ba # 'i phyir te / / don gnyis kyis so /
pravRtti gAmBIryam hetu Pala pravRtti durvijQAna tvAt caturBiH arTEH iti
# 'byung-ba # s zab-pa #  ni rgyu las 'bras-bu #  'byung-ba #  rnam-par-shes-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i phyir te / / don bzhis zab-pa # 'o /
antareNa eva kartAram karma kriyA ca asti tad Pala upaBogaH ca iti ayam atra karma Pala avivipraNASaH veditavyaH / na svayaMkRtaH DarmaH anutpannasya aBAva Adyena asO kriyeta
# byed-pa-po #  med kyang las-dang-byed-pa #  dang de'i 'bras-bu #  la spyod-pa #  yod de / / 'di ni 'dir las dang 'bras-bu #  chud-mi-za-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / chos ni bdag-nyid-kyis #  ma-byas-pa #  ste / / gang-gis #  byed-pa #  de ma skyes te med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na para kRtaH pratyayAnAm akartR katvAt
# gzhan gyis kyang ma byas te rkyen rnams byed-pa-po #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na uBaya kRtaH etena eva kAraNa dvayena
# gnyis-ka # s kyang ma byas te / / rgyu de gnyis kyis ma-byas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na asvayaMkAra apara kAra hetu samutpannaH hetu pratyayAnAm Pala utpattO sAmarTyAt
# rang-gis #  byed-pa #  dang gzhan gyis byed-pa #  dang rgyu-med-pa #  las byung-ba #  yang ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni rkyen rnams 'bras-bu #  skyed nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aparaH paryAyaH / na svayaMkRtaH pratyaya apekzaNAt
# rnam-grangs #  gzhan-du-na #  bdag-nyid-kyis #  ma-byas-pa #  ni rkyen-la-ltos-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na para kRtaH satsu api pratyayezu nirvIjasya anutpAdAt / na uBaya kRtaH tad uBa yoniH Ihaka tvAt
# gzhan gyis ma-byas-pa #  ni rkyen yod-du-zin-kyang #  sa-bon #  med-pa #  ni mi-skye-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gnyi-ga # s ma-byas-pa #  ni de-gnyi-ga #  la g-yo-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na ahetu samutpannaH bIja pratyayAnAm Sakti sadBAvAt iti / Bavati hi api / sva bIja tvAt na paratas na svayam tad apekzaNAt / niScezwa tvAt na ca dvAByAm tad SakteH na api ahetutaH / iti / na svayam na paratas dviviDa kowi pratikzepe api gamBIraH pratItyasamutpAdaH syAt prAk eva yatra catasraH api kowayaH pratikzipyante tasmAt etasya parama gAmBIrya veditavyam / vijQAna utpatti praBedataH cakzuH pratItya rUpANi ca utpadyate cakzuH vijQAnam iti evamAdi / vyutpatti praBedataH satva lokam aDikRtya avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti evamAdi
# rgyu-med-pa #  las byung-ba #  yang ma yin ba ni sa-bon #  dang rkyen rnams la nus-pa #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzhan-yang #  / / rang-gis #  bon las te gzhan-las #  min / / de-la #  ltos phyir bdag-gis #  byas ma yin / / g-yo-ba #  med phyir gnyis kyis ma byas la / / de ni nus-pa # s rgyu med byung ma yin / / bdag las ma yin gzhan-las #  ma yin zhes-bya-ba # s / / mu rnam-pa-gnyis #  spong yang rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  zab-pa # r 'gyur na / / gang-du #  mu-bzhi #  char spong-ba #  lta-smos #  kyang ci dgos / / de-lta-bas-na #  'di mchog-tu-zab-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig dang gzugs la brten-nas #  mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / 'chi-'pho-ba #  dang skye-ba # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-can-gyi-'jig-rten #  gyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
bAhya vasA utpatti praBedataH bIjam prati iti aFkuraH aFkuram pratItya kANXaH / taTA na apatra puzpa PalAni yojyAni
# phyi'i lo-tog #  'byung-ba # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sa-bon #  la brten-nas #  myu-gu #  / / myu-gu #  la brten-nas #  sdong bu ste / / de-bzhin-du #  sbu gu dang 'dab ma dang / / me-tog #  dang 'bras-bu #  rnams kyang sbyar-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
saMvarta vivarta praBedataH sarva sattva sADAraNa karma ADipatyam pratItya mahA pRTivI AdInAm utpAdAt
# 'jig-pa #  dang chags-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi thun mong gi las kyi dbang la brten-nas #  sa-chen-po #  la-sogs-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
AhAra upastamBa praBedataH caturaH AhArAn pratItya trEDAtuke satvAnAm avasTAnAt
# zas kyis brten-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni zas-bzhi #  la brten-nas #  sems-can #  rnams khams-gsum #  na gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
izwa anizwa gati viBAga praBedataH su carita duScaite pratItya sugati durgati gamanAt / viSudDi praBedataH mokza BAgIyAni pratItya nirveDa BAgIya utpattitaH yAvat darSana BAva nAma argAnu pUrvyA arhat tva prAptitaH paratas vA Gozam prati iti ADyAtmam ca yoniSas manaskAram samyak dRzwiH tatas yAvat sarva Asrava kzayaH iti
# 'dod dang mi-'dod-pa # 'i 'gro-ba #  rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni legs-par-spyad-pa #  dang nyes-par-spyad-pa #  la brten-nas #  bde-'gro #  dang ngan-'gror-'gro-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  la brten-nas #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  'byung-ba #  nas mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyi rim-gyis #  dgra-bcom-pa #  thob-pa # 'i bar dang gzhan gyi sgra la brten-nas #  nang-du #  tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa #  dang yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  dang gang-zag #  pa thams-cad #  zad-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
praBAva praBedataH aDigamam prati iti aBijQA AdayaH vESezikAH guNAH iti / eBiH praBedEvistareNa saMskArANAm pratItyasamutpAdaH anusartavyaH
# mthu stobs kyis rab-tu-dbye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni thob ba la brten-nas #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  rnams 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  'di dag gis 'du-byed-rnams #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  rgya-cher #  rtogs-pa # r bya'o /
saMkleSa anuloma pratilomaH iti pravRtya AnupUrvIm aDikRtya avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti evamAdi anuloma nirdeSaH / jarA maraNaMjarA maraNa samudayaH jarA maraNa niroDa gAminI pratipadi iti satya vyavasTAnam aDikRtya pratiloma nirdeSaH veditavyaH pratiloma nirdeSaH
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i lugs dang mthun-pa #  dang lugs dang mi-mthun-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'byung-ba # 'i rim-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni lugs dang mthun-par #  ston to / / rga shi dang rga shi kun-'byung-ba #  dang rga shi 'gog-pa #  dang rga shi 'gog-par #  'gro-ba # 'i lam zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / bden-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
vyavadAna anuloma pratilomataH iti tat yaTA vidyA niroDAt saMskAra niroDaH iti evamAdi vyavadAna anuloma nirdeSaH
# lugs dang mi-mthun-pa #  bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-bzhin-du #  ma-rig-pa #  'gags-pa # s 'du-byed #  'gag ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i lugs dang mthun-pa #  ston to /
kasmin= asati na jarA maraNam Bavati kasya niroDAt jarA maraNa niroDaH iti pratiloma nirdeSataH
# gang med na rga shi mi-'byung-ba #  dang gang 'gags na rga shi 'gags-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni lugs dang mi-mthun-pa #  ston to /
hetu pratyayaH AlayavijQAnam kuSala vAsanA ca sa Asrava anAsravANAm ca saMskArANAm yaTAkramam
# rgyu'i-rkyen #  gang zhe na / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang dge-ba # 'i bag-chags #  so zhes-bya-ba #  ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
AlayavijQAnam punar dviviDam vEpAkikam ABisaMskArikam ca
# kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / rnam-par-smin-pa #  dang mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  las byung-ba # 'o /
tatra vEpAkikam upapatti prAtilamBikAnAm hetu pratyayaH
# de-la #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni skye-ba # s 'thob-pa #  rnams kyi rgyu'i rkyan to /
ABisaMskArikam prAyogikAnAm AyatyAm cAlaya vijQAna antarasya hetu pratyayaH drazwavyaH
# mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  las byung-ba #  ni sbyor-ba-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi ste / / phyi-ma-la #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  gzhan gyi rgyu'i-rkyen #  du blta-bar-bya # 'o /
ABisaMskArikam punar Alaya vijQAnam tad jAnmika pravRtti vijQAna samudAcAra vAsitam veditavyam
# mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  las byung pa'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni / / tshe de'i 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i bag-chags #  bsgos-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
kuSala vAsanA mokza BAgIyAnAm vAsanA drazwavyA
# dge-ba # 'i bag-chags #  ni thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams kyi bag-chags #  su blta-bar-bya #  ste /
tezAm loka uttara aByupagamanizyanda Darma nEmittikataH tad vAsanAyAH loka uttara Darma hetutvam veditavyam / api Kalu svaBAvataH api iti evamAdinA zaX hetavaH hetu pratyayaH iti darSayati
# de-dag #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  thob-pa'i-rgyu #  mthun-pa'i-chos #  kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir de'i bag-chags #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / yang ngo-bo-nyid #  ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni rgyu drug-po #  dag rgyu'i-rkyen #  du ston to /
tatra svaBAvataH praBedataH ca kAraNa hetoH vyavasTAnam
# de-la #  ngo-bo-nyid #  dang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni byed-pa'i-rgyu # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
SezEH padEH yaTAkramam saha BU saMprayukta saBAga sarvatraga vipAka hetUnAm vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# tshig lhag-ma #  rnams ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  lhan-cig-'byung-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang skal-pa #  mnyam-pa #  dang kun-tu #  'gro-ba #  dang rnam-par-smin-pa'i-rgyu #  rnams su rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
hetu svaBAvam aDikRtya kAraNa hetu vyavasTAnAt sarva hetavaH kAraNa hetO= antarBUtAH veditavyAH
# rgyu'i-ngo-bo #  nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  byed-pa'i-rgyu #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir rgyu thams-cad #  ni byed-pa'i-rgyu # 'i nang-du #  'dus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sahAya Adi viSeza praBAvana arTa tu pRTak vyavasTAnam
# grogs la-sogs-pa #  ni bye-brag #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir so-so # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
kAraNa hetu praBede vijQAna sAmagra yAdikam yat nirdizwam udAharaNa mAtram tat drazwavyam tayA diSAni asya api tad jAtIyasya aByuhana arTam
# byed-pa'i-rgyu # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  la / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs la sogs gang bstan-pa #  de ni dpe tsam du blta-bar-bya # 'o / / phyogs 'dis ni de-lta-bu # 'i rang-bzhin-can #  gzhan la yang mngon bar brtag-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tatra utpatti kAraNam tatas kAryasya aBUtvA prAdurBAvAt
# de-la #  'byung-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni de-la # s 'bras-bu #  ma-byung-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sTiti kAraNam utpannasya prabanDa anupacCedAt
# gnas-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni skyes-pa # 'i rgyud rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
DRti kAraNam pAta pratibanDAt / prakASana kAraNam AvRtasya aBivyaQjanAt / vikAra kAraNam tat saMtAnasya anyaTA tva ApAdanAt
# rten-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni ltung-ba # 'i gegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gsal-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni sgrib-pa #  bsal-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'gyur-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni rgyud gzhan-du-'gyur-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
viyoga kAraNam saMbanDasya dvEDIkaraNAt
# 'bral-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni 'brel-ba #  gnyis su gcod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pariNati kAraNam tat avayavAnAm deSa antara saMcaraNAt
# bsgyur-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni de'i cha-shas #  yul gzhan-du #  'pho-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMprati ayakAraNam tena viparokza anumAnAt
# yid-ches-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni des lkog-tu-gyur-pa #  rjes-su-dpag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMpratyAyana kAraNam tena samyak niScayAt
# yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni des yang-dag-par #  nges-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prApaNa kAraNam tena aDigamAt
# thob-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni des thob-par-byed-pa # 'i rgyu'i phyir ro /
vyavahAra kAraNam yaTA nAmaDeyam nimitta udgrahaNena aBiniviSya anuvyava haraNAt
# tha-snyad #  kyi byed-rgyu #  ni ming ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mtshan-mar-'dzin-pa # s mngon bar zhen nas rjes su tha-snyad-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
apekzA kAraNam anyatra icCA utpatti nimitta tvAt
# ltos-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni gzhan-du #  'dod-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
Akzepa kAraNam tad anvaya avasTA antara parApara BAvinaH AveDaka tvAt
# 'phen-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni de'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  gnas-skabs #  gzhan-du #  gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud de 'byung-ba # s 'phen-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ABinirvRtti kAraNam anantara BAvinaH janaka tvAt
# mngon bar 'grub-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni de ma-thag-tu #  'byung-ba #  bskyed-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
parigraha kAraNam sva bIja utpAdinaH upodvala tvAt / AvAhana kAraNam tadA AnukUlyena AkarzaNAt
# yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni rang-gi-sa-bon #  las byung-ba #  stobs bskyed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / chud-pa # r byed-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni de'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # s 'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratiniyama kAraNam Binna svaBAva tayA anyonya Pala tvAt
# so-sor-nges-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni rang-bzhin #  tha-dad-pa # s 'bras-bu #  gzhan dang gzhan 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sahakAri kAraNam sva kArya nirvartane kAraNa antara apekzaNAt / viroDi kAraNam viDna karaNAt / aviroDi kAraNam tad viparyayeNa veditavyam
# lhan-cig #  byed-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni rang-gi-'bras-bu #  'grub-par-byed-pa #  la rgyu gzhan la ltos-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mi-mthun-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni gegs-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mi-mthun-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  ni de-las-bzlog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tat yaTA BUtAni BOtikam ca iti yaTAsaMBavam na tu avaSyam sarvatra saMGAte catvAri mahABUtAni Bavanti rUpa Adikam vA BOtikam
# 'di-lta-ste #  'byung-ba #  rnams dang 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du snang gyi [*gi] tshogs-pa #  thams-cad #  dang gzugs la-sogs-pa #  'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  la 'byung-ba-chen-po-bzhi #  po dag gdon-mi-za-bar #  'byung-ba #  ni ma yin no /
iti atas yadi atra asti tat tena saha utpadyate na anyonyam vinA iti
# de'i-phyir #  gang na gang yod-pa #  de ni de dang lhan-cig #  'byung ste / / gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig med na ni ma yin no /
sahAya nEyamyena saha BU hetuH vyavasTApitaH
# de-ltar-na #  grogs su nges-pa # s lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i rgyur rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
BUtAni BOtikam ca iti udAharaNa mAtram etat veditavyam citta cEtasikAnAm anyonyam avinABAva niyamAt
# 'byung-ba #  dag dang 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # s de ni dper brjod-pa #  tsam du zad-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams ni gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig med na mi-'byung-ba # r nges-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yadi evam saMprayukta hetoH pRTak vyavasTAnam na prApnoti citta cEtasikAnAm saha BUhetO= antar BAvAt / yadi api etat evam taTA api anyena arTena / ye DarmAH sahaBAvena alaMkanam pratipadyante na anyatama vEkalyena te saMpratipattitaH saMprayuktaka hetuH vyavasTApyate na sahaBAva mAtreNa tat yaTA cittEH cEtasikAH ca / pUrva BAvitAnAm iti pUrvAByaH tAnAm pUrvam samudAcaritAnAm iti arTaH
# gal-te #  de-ltar-na #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i rgyu logs-shig #  tu gzhag tu med-pa # r 'gyur te / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams lhan-cig-'byung-ba # 'i rgyu'i nang-du #  'dus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  yin-du-zin #  kyang don gzhan gyis mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i rgyur 'gyur te / / chos gang dag lhan-cig-'byung-ba # s dmigs-pa #  mthun-par #  rtogs kyi gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig ma tshang na ma-yin-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams so / / sngon dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i chos bsgoms-pa #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni sngon-goms-par-byas-pa #  rnams te / / sngon kun-tu #  spyad ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
yA aparAnte uttarottarA puzwatara tamA pravRttiH iti tEH paripozita bIjAnAm tad anvayAnAm anAgate kAle viSizwa utpattitaH drazwavyA / evam ayam saBAga hetuH sadRSAnAm puzwi nimitta tvena vyavasTApitaH / sarvatraga hetuH na kevalam sadRSasya eva puzwaye kim tarhi yasya kasyacid rAga AdeH kleSasya aByAsena sarvezAm dveza AdInAm prabanDa puzwayA dRXIkAraH Bavati atas vanDana gAXI karaNAt mokza prApti paripanTa arTena asya vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# phyi-ma'i-mtha' #  gong-nas-gong-du #  shin-tu #  rgyas-pa #  dang mchog-tu #  rgyas-pa # r 'byung-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-dag #  gi sa-bon #  yongs su gsos ba rnams te / / de'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  rnams ma-'ongs-pa'i-dus-na #  khyad-par-can #  du 'byung-ba # r blta'o / / de-ltar-na #  skal-ba-mnyam-pa # 'i rgyu 'di ni 'dra-ba #  rnams kyi rgyas-par-byed-pa # 'i rgyur rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / kun-tu #  'gro-ba # 'i rgyu ni 'dra-ba #  rgyas-par-byed-pa #  'ba'-zhig-tu #  ma zad kyi / / 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  goms-par-byas-pa # s zhe-sdang #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyun rgyas-par-bstan-pa # r byed-pa # r 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  dam du 'ching-bar-byed-pa # s na thar-pa #  thob-pa # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
vipAka hetuH punar AyatyAm ekAnta visadRSasya eva anivRtta avyAkRtasya Atma BAva saMgra hItavya vipAkasya Akzepaka tvAt parigraha arTena vyavasTApitaH
# rnam-par-smin-pa'i-rgyu #  ni phyi-ma-la #  gcig-tu #  mi-'dra-ba #  bsgribs la lung du mi ston-pa # 'i lus su bsdus-pa #  ste / / rnam-par-smin-pa #  'phen-pa # 'i phyir yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i don-gyis #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
kuSala sa Asrava grahaNa manAsravANAm janma viroDi tvena anAkzepaka tvAt
# dge-ba #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  smos-pa #  ni zag-pa-med-pa #  rnams kyi skye-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # s 'phen-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nErantaryasam anantarataH api iti na avaSyam kzaNanEH antarya kiMtarhi citta antara nErantam api atra nErantarya drazwavyam / itaraTA hi acittika samApattO vyutTAna cittasya samApatti cittam na samanantara pratyayaH syAt / Bavati ca
# rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  chad-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gdon-mi-za-bar #  skad-cig #  gi bar-chad-med-pa #  ma yin gyi sems gzhan gyi bar-chad-med-pa #  yang 'dir bar-chad #  med bar blta-bar-bya #  ste / / gzhan-du-na #  snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems ni sems med-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  las langs-pa # 'i sems kyi de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen du ni mi-'gyur-ba # 'i rigs na 'gyur-ba # s de'i-phyir #  rgyud gcig la phyi-ma # 'i sems dang snga-ma # 'i sems kyi bar-du #  sems gzhan gyis bar-du-ma-chod-pa #  ni de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen to /
tasmAt ekasmin saMtAne paScimasya cittasya pUrvakam cittam citta antareNa anantaritam samanantara pratyayaH / yaTA cittam evam cEtasikAH api veditavyAH / saBA gavisaBAga citta cEtta utpatti samanantarataH api iti kuSalAH citta cettAH kuSalAnAm saBAgAnAm akuSala avyAkRtAnAm ca visaBAgAnAm anantara utpannAnAm samanantara pratyayaH / evam kuSala avyAkRtAH svAni aprakArANAm yojayitavyAH
# sems la ji-lta-ba # r sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyang de-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / mthun-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa #  las sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i de-ma-thag-pa # s kyang zhes-bya-ba #  la / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i dge-ba #  rnams ni mthun-pa #  dge-ba #  rnams dang mi-mthun-pa #  mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  de ma-thag-tu #  'byung-ba #  rnams kyi de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen to / / de-bzhin #  tu mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  rnams kyang rang dang gzhan gyi rnam-pa #  rnams dang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
tat yaTA kAmAvacarA kAmAvacarANAm rUpa ArUpya avacarAn AsravANAm ca anantara utpannAnAm samanantara pratyayaH
# de-bzhin #  tu 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  rnams ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  rnams dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  de ma-thag-tu #  'byung-ba #  rnams kyi de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen to /
evam rUpAvacara AdayaH api pRTak pRTak rUpa avacarAdonAm kAmAvacara AdInAm ca anantara utpannAnAm iti yojayitavyam / kim Kalu sarvasya cintasi anantaram sarva cittam utpadyate ahosvit asti pratiniyamaH / asti iti ucyate
# de-bzhin #  gzugs-na-spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yang so-so # r gzugs-na-spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  de ma-thag-tu #  'byung-ba #  rnams kyi de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen to zhes sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / ci sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi de ma-thag-tu #  sems thams-cad #  'byung ngam / / 'on te nges-pa #  yod ce na /
avEtasya cittasya anantaram idam ca idam ca cittam utpadyate iti ucyamAne bahu vaktavyam jAyate
# nges-pa #  yod ces bya ste sems 'di'i 'og-tu #  sems 'di dang 'di 'byung ngo zhes brjod na ni brjod-pa #  mang-ba # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt sAmAnyena citta utpattO lakzaNa mAtram vyavasTApyate
# de-lta-bas-na #  spyir sems 'byung-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  tsam rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
tat yaTA daSaBiH balEH cittasya utpAdaH veditavyaH paricaya balena Canda balena prayoga balena samApatti balena samaH veDa balena hetu balena vizaya balena smRti balena manaskAra balena pratisaMDi balena ca
# 'di-ltar #  stobs-bcu # s sems 'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / 'dris-pa # 'i stobs dang 'dun-pa'i-stobs #  dang sbyor-ba'i-stobs #  dang snyom-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i stobs dang 'phen-pa # 'i stobs dang rgyu'i-stobs #  dang yul-gyi-stobs #  dang dran-pa'i-stobs #  dang yid-la-byed-pa # 'i stobs dang nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i stobs kyis so /
paricaya balam punar triviDam mRdu maDyam aDimAtram ca
# 'dris-pa # 'i stobs ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / chung-ngu #  'bring dang chen-po # 'o /
samApatti sTiti vyutTAna nimittAnAm anupalakzita tvAt mRdu / upalakzitAnAm sva paricitta tvAt maDyam / su paricita tA upalakzita tvAt aDimAtram
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang gnas-pa #  dang ldang-ba # 'i rgyu rnams mi mngon-pa # 'i phyir chung ngo / / mngon-pa # r legs-par #  ma-'dris-pa # 'i phyir 'bring ngo / / legs-par #  'dris-pa # 'i phyir chen-po # 'o /
tatra mRdunA paricaya balena DyAna ArUpyANAm AnupUrvya samApattiH veditavyA / maDyena vyutkrAntaka samApattiH ekAntarika yogena
# de-la #  'dris-pa #  chung-ngu # 'i stobs kyis ni bsam-gtan #  dang gzugs-med-pa #  rnams la mthar-gyis #  snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'bring gis ni gcig gis bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  thod rgal du snyoms-pa # r 'jug go /
aDimAtreNa yaTezwam sarvANi vA vyutkrAmya anulomam pratilomam ca samApattiH veditavyA
# chen-po # s ni ji-ltar-'dod-pa # 'am thams-cad-la #  thod rgal du zhugs nas lugs dang mthun-pa #  dang lugs dang mi-mthun-pa # r snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
Candabalena dvitIya DyAna lABI praTamam DyAnam samApannaH yadi AkAMkzati dvitIya DyAna BUmikam vyutTAna cittam AmuKIkaroti aTa nA kAMkzati kAmAvacaram kuSalam anivRta avyAkRtam vA / evam anyatra api vistareNa yojyam / prayoga balena kAma avacarasya kuSalasya vAnantaram tat praTamatas rUpa avacaram cittam utpadyate / anAgamyasya kuSalasya anantaram mOlam / mOlasya kuSalasya anantaram dvitIya DyAna samApannakam iti evamAdi vistareNa yAvat Bava agrAt veditavyam / samApatti balena SudDakam samApannasya kadAcid SudDakam eva utpadyate kadAcid klizwam / AveDa valena samADeH vyutTAya carataH tAvat samAhita BUmikam cittam asamAhita kzaNa anantara vyatiBinnam anuvartate yAvat tad viroDi kleSa samudAcArAt parihINaH iti
# 'dun-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni bsam-gtan-gnyis-pa #  thob-pa #  bsam-gtan-dang-po #  la snyoms-pa # r zhugs la / / gal-te #  'dod na bsam-gtan-gnyis-pa # 'i sa pa las ldang-ba # 'i sems mngon du byed do / / gzhan-du #  'dod na yang 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  dge-ba # 'am ma-bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  mngon du byed do / / de-bzhin-du #  gzhan la'ang rgya-cher-sbyar-bar-bya # 'o / / sbyor-ba'i-stobs #  kyis ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i dge-ba #  nyid kyi mjug-thogs-su #  thog-ma-kho-nar #  gzugs-na-spyod-pa # 'i sems 'byung ngo / / mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i mjug-thogs-su #  dngos-gzhi # 'o / / dngos-gzhi # 'i mjug-thogs-su #  bsam-gtan-gnyis-pa # 'i nyer-bsdogs #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  nas rgya-cher #  srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i bar-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i stobs kyis ni dag-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sems res-'ga' #  ni dag-pa #  pa gnyis skye'o / / res-'ga' #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  no / / 'phen-pa # 'i stobs kyis ni ting-nge-'dzin #  las langs-nas #  rgyu-ba #  na ji-srid #  du de dang mi-mthun-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  kun-tu-'byung-ba # s yongs-su-nyams-pa # r ma gyur ba de srid du mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sa pa'i sems dang mnyam-pa # r ma bzhag-pa # 'i skad-cig #  'dren-ma # r rjes su 'jug go /
tad viroDi kleSa saMprayuktasya punar cittasya hetu AdiBiH ca turBiH balEH samudAcAraH veditavyaH tatra tAvat hetu balena yadi avaSyam BUmi parihANi saMvartanIyam AvaraNam pUrvam upacitam Bavati vizaya balena yadi rAga Adi utpatya anukUlaH SuBa Adi nimittaH praBAva utkawa vizayaH ABAsa samAgataH Bavati smRti valena yadi smaraNa saMkalpEH atItAn vizayAn prapaQcayati manaskAra balena yadi mImAMsAmanaH kAreNa anyatara pracCuBa nimittam manasikaroti iti
# de dang mi-mthun-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i sems ni rgyu la-sogs-pa # 'i stobs-bzhi # s kun-tu-'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-la #  rgyu'i-stobs #  kyis ni gal-te #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  yongs-su-nyams-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  sngon bsags-par-gyur #  pa'o / / yul-gyi-stobs #  kyis ni gal-te #  'dod-chags #  la sos pa 'byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa #  / / sdug-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # 'i stobs shas-che-ba # 'i yul snang-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'o / / dran-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni gal-te #  dran-pa # 'i kun-tu-rtog-pa #  dag gis 'das-pa # 'i yul la 'pho-ba # r byed-pa # 'o / / yid-la-byed-pa # 'i stobs kyis ni gal-te #  spyod-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # s sdug-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'o /
pratisaMDi balena nava maraNa cittAni Atma BAva tRzNA saMprayuktAni trizu DAtuzu pratyekam kAma rUpa ArUpya avacarANi eka
# nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i stobs kyis ni / / 'chi-ba # 'i sems rnam-pa #  dgu ste lus la sred-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  khams-gsum #  du so-so # r 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  dag go /
tatra kAmaDAtoH cyutvA kAmaDAtO= eva pratisaMDi vaDnataH kAmAvacaram Atma BAva tRzNA saMprayuktam maraNa cittam veditavyam / rUpa ArUpya DAtvoH pratisaMDi baDnataH rUpa ArUpya avaram
# de-la #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  nas shi-'phos-nas #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  de nyid-du #  nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i lus la sred-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni 'chi-'pho-ba # 'i sems su rig-par-bya # 'o / / gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  su nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i sems ni gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa # 'i 'chi-ba # 'i sems su rig-par-bya # 'o /
taTA rUpa ArUpya DAtuByAm cyutvA tatra vA anyatra vA utpadyamAnasya zaw cittAni yojayitavyAni
# de-bzhin-du #  gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  nas shi-'phos-nas #  de nyid dang gzhan-du #  skyes-pa # 'i sems kyang drug tu sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
sA punar Atma BAva tRzNA sahaja anirUpita alaMkbana anivRta avyAkRtA ca
# lus la sred-pa #  de ni lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  la mi-spyod-pa #  dang bsgribs-pa # 'i lung du-ma #  bstan ba'o /
Atma BAva jAtiH ca asyAH prakAra aparicCedena alaMbanam veditavyam
# lus dang lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  'di ni dmigs-pa #  ni rnam-pa #  yongs su mi gcod-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
tad vaSena anantaram pRTagjanAnAm antarA aBava pratisaMDiH / AryANAm api avIta rAgANAm maraNa kAle yAvat aspazwa saMjQA avasTAm na gacCati tAvat asO tRzNA samudAcarati / te tu enAm paricCidya pratipakzeNa aBinigRhNanti
# de'i dbang gis de ma-thag-tu #  so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams ni bar-ma-do'i-srid-pa # r nying mtshams sbyor ro / / 'phags-pa #  'dod-chags #  dang ma-bral-ba #  rnams ni 'chi-ba # 'i dus na ji tsam du 'du-shes #  mi-gsal-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  su ma-gyur-pa #  de srid du sred-pa #  de kun-tu #  'byung ngo /
vIta rAgANAm tu AryANAm pratipakzasya valIyaH tvAt na eva asO samudAcarati aprahINA api satI
# de-dag #  ni yongs su rtogs-nas #  gnyen-po # s tshar gcod do / / 'phags-pa #  'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  rnams ni ma spongs su zin-kyang #  gnyen-po # 'i stobs-che-ba # s de kun-tu #  mi 'byung ngo /
tad anuSaya vaSena tu tezAm pratisaMDiH
# de'i bag-la-nyal #  gyi dbang gis ni de-dag #  nying mtshams sbyor ro /
antarABava pratisaMDi kzaNaH punar nityam anivRta avyAkRtaH eva vipAka tvAt
# bar-ma-do'i-srid-pa # 'i nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i skad-cig #  ni rtag-tu #  ma-bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  nyid de / / rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatas UrDva kuSalaH api akuSalaH api avyAkRtaH api yaTAsaMBavam cyuti cittam sTApayitvA
# de'i-'og-tu #  ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar te / / 'chi-'pho-ba # 'i sems ma gtogs so /
antarABava cyuti cittam tu nityam klizwam maraNa Bava vat
# bar mdo'i srid-pa # 'i 'chi-'pho-ba # 'i sems ni rtag-tu #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  te / / 'chi-'pho-ba # 'i srid-pa #  bzhin no /
upapatti pratisaMDiH punar nityam anivRta avyAkRtaH eva iti veditavyam
# skye-ba # 'i nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  ni rtag-tu #  ma-bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
boDisattvAnAm tu praNiDAna balena upapadyamAnAnAm maraNa citta Adikam ekAntena sarva kuSalam veditavyam / samAptaH samanantara pratyaya prasaFgaH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  smon-lam-gyi-stobs #  kyis skye-ba #  rnams kyi 'chi-ba # 'i sems la-sogs-pa #  ni thams-cad #  kyang gcig-tu #  dge-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-ma-thag-pa # 'i rkyen gyi skabs rdzogs so /
paricCinna vizaya alaMbanataH paQcAnAm vijQAna kAyAnAm AlaMbanam pratiniyata vizaya tvAt paQcAnAm vijQAna kAyAnAm
# yul yongs su chad-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  tshogs lnga po dag gi dmigs-pa #  ste / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga po dag gi yul so-sor-nges-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aparicCinna vizaya alaMkabanataH manaH vijQAnasya alaMkaMbanam sarva Darma vizaya tvAt manaH vijQAnasya
# yul yongs su ma chad-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ste / / chos-thams-cad #  yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
acitrIkAra vizaya alaMbanataH avyutpanna saMjQAnAm manaH vijQAnasya alaMbanam nAmataH akzarIkartum aSakya tvAt
# yul la bkra-ba # r 'dzin-pa #  med-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ming lam byang-ba #  rnams kyi yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ste / / ming dang yi-ge # r byed mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
citrIkAra vizaya alaMbanataH tad viparyayAt veditavyam
# yul la bkra-ba # r 'dzin-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / de-las-bzlog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sa vastuka vizaya alaMkbanataH dRzwim asmin tad saMprayuktAn= ca DarmAn sTApayitvA tat anyezAm AlaMbanam
# dngos-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i yul gyi dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni lta-ba #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang de dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ma-gtogs-par #  de-las-gzhan-pa #  dag gi dmigs-pa # 'o /
avastuka vizaya alaMkabanataH sTApitAnAm AlaMbanam Atma aDizWAna tvAt
# dngos-po #  med ba'i yul gyi dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-gtogs-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ste / / bdag gzhi-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vastu AlaMbanataH anAsra vAlaMbanAn visaBAga DAtu BUmi sarvatragAna nivArita vastukAn= ca atIta anAgata aMbanAn sTApayitvA tad anyezAm AlaMbanam
# dngos-po # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / zag-pa-med-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  dang skal-ba #  mi-mnyam-pa # 'i khams dang sa'i kun-tu #  'gro-ba #  rnams dang ma-'ongs-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  gzhi gtan la phebs pa med-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  de-las-gzhan-pa #  dag gi dmigs-pa # 'o /
parikalpa alaMkanataH sTApitAnAm AlaMbanam sva parikalpam AtrAlaMbanAt
# kun-tu #  brtags-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma-gtogs-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ste / / rang-gi #  kun-brtags-pa #  tsam la dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
viparyasta alaMbanam nitya Adi AkArANAm
# phyin-ci-log #  gi dmigs-pa #  zhes bya ni rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r byung-ba #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o /
aviparyasta alaMkbanam anitya Adya AkArANAm / sa vyAGAta alaMkbanam aprahINa jQeya AvaraNAnAm / avyAGAta alaMbanam prahINa jQeya AvaraNAnAm iti
# phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / thogs-pa #  dang bcas ba'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  ma-spangs-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / thogs-pa-med-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sgrib-pa-spong-ba #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o /
AlaMbana pratyaye viniScayaH lakzaNataH api praBedataH api sTititaH api parijQAnataH api prahANataH api Ala vana vyavasTAnam veditavyam / kaTam lakzaNataH
# dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  gyi rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni mtshan-nyid #  dang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang; bzhag-pa #  dang yongs-su-shes-pa #  dang spangs-pa # s kyang dmigs-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / mtshan-nyid #  kyis ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
yaH arTaH tad pratiBAsAnAm citta cEtasikAnAm DarmANAm utpatti nimittama te ca utpannAH tad arTa aBiniveSa vyavahAra pratyAtma avagamAya Bavanti tad alaMkaMbana lakzaNam / kaTam praBedataH
# don gang der-snang-ba # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  rnams 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu dang de-dag #  byung nas kyang don de-la #  mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dang tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  dang so-so #  rang-gis #  rig-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  ni dmigs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / rab-tu-dbye-ba # s ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
asat AlaMbanam tat yaTA viparyastAnAm citta cEtasikAnAm atIta anAgata svapna pratirbiba mAyA Adi AlaMbanam ca / sa dAlaMbanam tad anyezAm
# med-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  phyin-ci-log-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  dang 'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang rmi-lam #  dang gzugs-brnyan #  dang sgyu-ma #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # 'o / / yod-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa #  dag gi dmigs-pa # 'o /
anAlaMbanam AlaMbanam rUpam citta viprayuktAH asaMskRtam ca
# dmigs-pa-med-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni gzugs dang sems dang ldan-pa-ma-yin-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  so /
sAlaMbanam AlaMbanam citta cEtasikAH DarmAH
# dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  rnams so /
samyak tu AlaMbanam tat yaTA kuSalam
# yang-dag-pa-nyid #  kyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  dge-ba # 'o /
miTyA tva AlaMbanam tat yaTA klizwam
# log-pa #  nyid kyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  no /
na eva samakra tvana miTyA tva AlaMbanam tat yaTA anivRta avyAkRtam
# yang-dag-pa-nyid #  kyang ma yin la log-pa #  nyid kyang ma-yin-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  ma-bsgribs-pa # 'i lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'o /
yoniSas AlaMbanam tat yaTA kuSalAnAm citta cEtasikAnAm / ayoniSaH AlaMbanam tat yaTA klizwAnAm / na eva yoni SonAya uniSaH tad vinirmuktAnAm
# tshul-bzhin #  gyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i dge-ba #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / nyon-mongs-pa-can #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / tshul-bzhin #  yang ma yin la tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni de-dag #  ma-gtogs-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o /
saBA gama alaMbanam tat yaTA kuSala AdInAm kuSala AdIni sva BUmikAnAm ca sva BUmikam sa AsravANAm ca sa Asravam anAsravANAm ca anAsravam
# 'dra-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyi dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang rang-gis #  pa rnams kyi rang-gis #  pa dang zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  rnams kyi zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  rnams kyi zag-pa-med-pa # 'o /
visaBAga mAlaMbanam tat yaTA kuSala AdInAm akuSala AdIni anya BUmikAnAm ca anya BUmikam sa Asrava anAsravayoH ca anAsravam / nAnA tvam AlaMbanam tat yaTA sa vitarka vicArANAm citta cEta sikAnAm / ekatvam AlaMbanam tat yaTA vitarka avicArANAm
