# mi-mthun-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams kyi mi-dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang sa gzhan-pa #  rnams kyi sa gzhan-pa #  dang zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  rnams kyi zag-pa-med-pa #  dang zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'o / / sna-tshogs #  kyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rtog-pa #  dang bcas dpyod-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / gcig bu'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  mi rtog mi dpyod-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / 'bral-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
viBUti AlaMbanam tat yaTA saMjQika prAyogikAnAm citta cEtasikAnAm AkASa vijQAna Anantya AyatanikAnAm ca
# 'du-shes-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams dang nam-mkha' #  dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye-mched #  kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / 'bral-ba #  ni med-par-'gyur-ba # 'o /
aBisaMkziptam sUkzmam AlaMbanam tat yaTA kiMcanya AyatanikAnAm
# gzhan-du-na #  'bral-ba #  chen-po #  nyid la bya'o / / bsdus-pa #  phra-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  pa rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o /
paryantikam sUkzmam AlaMbanam tat yaTA na eva saMjQAnA saMjQAyatanikAnAm / kleSaH AlaMbanam tena alaMbyate iti kRtvA / DarmaH AlaMbanam tat yaTA AryANAm nAma kAya pada kAya vyaQjana kAyAH / arTaH AlaMbanam tad ASritaH arTaH / parIttam AlaMbanam tat yaTA SrAvaka yAnam / vipulam AlaMbanam tat yaTA mahAyAnam / nimittam Alavanam tat yaTA SamaTa pragraha upekzA nimittAni / animitta mAlaMbanam tat yaTA nirvANam Bava agrayam ca
# mthar-phyin-pa # 'i phra-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'du-shes #  med 'du-shes #  med min skye-mched #  pa rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni des dmigs-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / mdo-sde # 'i tshig la yod-pa # 'i chos kyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / gtsug lag rnams kyi ming-gi-tshogs #  dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi-ge # 'i tshogs rnams so / / don gyi dmigs-pa #  ni de-la #  brten-pa #  brjod-par-bya-ba # 'i don gang-yin-pa # 'o / / chung-ngu # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'o / / rgya-chen-po # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / theg-pa-chen-po # 'o / / mtshan-ma # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / zhi-gnas #  dang rab-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang btang-snyoms-kyi-mtshan-ma #  rnams so / / mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  dang srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'o / / de-kho-na # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
tattvam AlaMbanam tat yaTA taTatA zoXaSAnAm ca AkArANAm satyAni / vEhArikam AlaMbanam tat yaTA niroDa samApattiH
# de-bzhin-nyid #  dang rnam-pa-bcu #  drug-po #  dag gi dmigs-pa # 'i bden-pa #  rnams so / / gnas-par-bya-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o /
vaSa varti AlaMbanam tat yaTA vimokza AdInAm sarva AkAra jQa tAvasAnAnAm guNAnAm
# dbang bsgyur-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / rnam-par-thar-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  mkhyen-pa #  nyid kyi mthar-thug-pa # 'i yon-tan #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o /
kzaNikam AlaMbanam tat yaTA SEkzANAm tat janmikam eva
# skad-cig-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / mi-slob-pa #  rnams kyi tshe de nyid do /
anuvarti AlaMbanam tat yaTA budDaboDisattvAnAm / kaTam sTititaH
# rjes-su-'brang-ba #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa # 'o / / gzhan-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
AlaMbanasya aparinizpattitaH taTA vyavasTApanAt
# de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # s so /
caturBiH ca kAraNEH aparinizpannam AlaMbanam veditavyam virudDa vijQAna nimitta tayA anAlaMbana vijQAna upalabDyA yatnam antareNa aviparyAsa prasaFgatayA triviDa jQAna anuvartana tayA ca
# rnam-pa-bzhi # s yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ji mthun-pa # 'i rgyu dang dmigs-pa-med-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dmigs-pa #  dang bsgribs-pa #  med-pa # r yang phyin-ci-log #  med-par-'gyur-ba #  dang shes-pa #  gsum gyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # r 'gyur-ba # s so /
tatas ca grAhakasya api aparinizpattiH
# de'i-phyir #  'dzin-pa #  yang yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # 'o /
triviDam jQAnam vaSitA jQAnam vipaSyana ajQAna nirvikalpa jQAnam ca / tatra caturNA kAraNAnAm udAharaNAni
# shes-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni dbang gi shes-pa #  dang lhag-mthong #  gi shes-pa #  dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'o / / de-la #  rnam-pa-bzhi # 'i dper brjod-pa #  ni /
preta tiryak manuzyANAm devAnAm ca yaTArha taH
# yi dgas dud-'gro #  mi rnam dang / / lha rnams ji-ltar #  rigs rigs su /
tulya vastu manaH BedAt arTa anizpattiH izyate
# dngos gcig yid ni tha dad phyir / / don ma-grub-pa # r 'dod-pa #  yin /
atIta AdO taTA svapne pratibiMba dvaye api ca
# 'das sogs de-bzhin #  rmi-lam #  dang / / gzugs-brnyan #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  po yang /
asat nAlaMbana tvAt ca tad alaMkbana yogataH
# med phyir dmigs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir / / de ni dmigs-pa # r rung ma yin /
arTasya arTa tva nizpattO jQAnam na syAt akalpakam / tad aBAvAt ca budDa tva prAptiH na eva upapadyate
# don ni don-du #  grub gyur na / / mi rtog ye shes med-pa # r 'gyur / / shes-pa #  rtog-pa #  med mi 'gyur / / de med-pa # s na sangs-rgyas #  nyid /
boDisattve vaSi prApte aDimukti vaSa AdyataH
# thob-pa # r 'thad-pa #  ma yin no / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dbang thob dang /
taTA BAvaH pRTivI AdO DyAyinAm ca upalaByate
# rnal-'byor-pa #  la 'di-ltar #  yang / / mos-pa # 'i dbang gis sa la sogs / / dngos-po #  de-ltar #  dmigs-pa # r 'gyur /
nizpanna vicayasya iha DImataH samADi lABinaH
# 'di-la #  rnam-pa # r 'byed grub dang / / blo ldan zhi-ba #  thob-pa #  yi /
sarva Darma manaskAre taTA arTaKyAnataH api ca
# chos kun yid-la-byed-pa #  la /
jQAna cAre avikalpe hi sarva arTa AKyAnataH api ca / arTa aBAva upagantavyaH vijQapteH tad aBAvataH / kaTam parijQAnataH / lakzaNa praBeda sTitInAm yaTA BUta jQAnataH / kaTam prahANataH
# de-ltar #  don ni snang-ba # 'i phyir / / mi rtog ye shes rgyu-ba #  la / / don kun snang-ba #  med phyir-yang #  / / don med khong du chud bar bya / / de med-pa # s na rnam rig med / / yongs-su-shes-pa # s ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / mtshan-nyid #  dang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang gzhag-pa #  rnams yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab-tu-shes-pa # 'i phyir ro / / spong-ba # s ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
SrAvaka yAna mahAyAnAByAm ASraya parivRttitaH
# nyan-thos #  dang theg-pa-chen-po # s gnas-gyur-pa #  ste / / nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # s gnas-gyur-pa # s ni /
SrAvaka yAna ASraya parivRttyA skanDa DAtu Ayatana alaMkabaneByaH vimokzaH na tu tezu viBu tva lABaH / mahAyAna ASraya parivRttyA tu uBayam iti
# phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  kyi dmigs-pa #  dag las rnam-pa # r thar gyi / / de-dag #  la dbang 'byor-pa #  thob-pa #  ni ma yin no / / theg-pa-chen-po # s gnas-gyur-pa #  ni gnyis-pa # 'o /
samAptaH AlaMbana pratyaye yaTA granTam viniScayaH / pratizWA aDipatitaH vAyu maNXa lAdIni ammaNXa lAdInAm BAjana lokaH sattva lokasya BUtAni BOtikAnAm indriyANi vijQAnAnAm iti evamAdi
# dmigs-pa'i-rkyen #  gzhung ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  rdzogs so / / rten la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la rlung-gi-dkyil-'khor #  la-sogs-pa #  ni chu'i dkyil 'khor la-sogs-pa #  la rten la dbang-byed-pa # s bdag-po'i-rkyen #  to / / snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  ni sems-can-gyi-'jig-rten #  gyi'o / / 'byung-ba #  rnams ni 'byung-ba-las-gyur-pa #  rnams kyi'o / / dbang-po #  rnams ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  rnams kyi'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
AveDa aDipatitaH sarva sattva sADAraNam karma BAjana lokasya pOrANam sa Asrava karma vipAkasya iti evamAdi sahaBAva aDipatitaH cittam ca etasAnAm manaskAraH cittasya sparSI vedanAyAH iti evamAdi
# 'phen-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi thun mong gi las ni snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  'phen-pa #  la dbang byed bas bdag-po'i-rkyen #  to / / sngon gyi zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i las rnams ni rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / lhan-cig-'byung-ba #  la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / sems ni sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi lhan-cig-'byung-ba #  la dbang-byed-pa # s bdag-po'i-rkyen #  to / / yid-la-byed-pa #  ni sems kyi'o / / reg-pa #  ni tshor-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
atas param dvAviSati mindriyANi aDikRtya aDipati vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# 'di man-chad #  ni dbang-po #  nyi shu rtsa gnyis kyi dbang-du-byas-te #  / / bdag-po # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra vizaya aDipatitaH cakzuH Srotra GrANa jihvA kAyam anEndriyAnAm tadA ADipatyena rUpa Adi aBinirvRtteH
# de-la #  yul la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid-kyi-dbang-po #  rnams te / / de'i dbang gis gzugs la-sogs-pa #  mngon-pa # r 'grub ba'i phyir ro /
prasava aDipatitaH strI puruza indriyayoH tadA ADipatyena garBa avakramaNAt
# skye-ba # r dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni pho dang mo'i dbang-po #  ste / / de'i dbang gis mngal-du-'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sTAna aDipataH jIvita indriyasya tad vaSena nikAya saBAga sTAnAt
# gnas-pa # r dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni srog-gi-dbang-po #  ste / / de'i dbang gis ris-mthun-pa # r gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Pala upaBoga aDipatitaH suKa duHKa sOmanasya upekza indriyANAm tad aDizWAnena izwa anizwa vipAka pratisaMvedanAt
# 'bras-bu #  la nye-bar-spyod-pa # r dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang btang-snyoms #  kyi dbang-po #  rnams te / / de'i dbang gis sdug-pa #  dang mi-sdug-pa'i-rnam-pa # r smin-pa #  so-so # r nyams-su-myong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
lOkika viSuDi aDipatitaH SradDA vIrya smRti samADi prajQA indriyANAm tEH kleSa vizkamBaNAt
# 'jig-rten-pa # 'i rnam-par-dag-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dad-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po #  rnams te / / de-dag #  gis nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa # r gnon-pa # 'i phyir ro /
loka uttara viSuDi aDipatitaH anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriyasya ajQndriyasya ajQAtO= indriyasya ca vyavasTAnam veditavyam tEH anuSaya samudGAtAt iti
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i rnam-par-dag-pa #  la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-shes-pa #  kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  dang kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po #  dang kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  la rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / de-dag #  gis bag-la-nyal #  legs-par-bcom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vijQAna avirahita tad sAdRSya indriya vizaya prabanDa utpatitaH sa BAgam veditavyam vijQAna sahitasya vijQAna sAdRSyena indriyasya vizayezu prabanDena utpatteH vijQAna vRtti sAdRSya arTena tad indriyam sa BAgam iti ucyate
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang ma bral zhing de-dang-'dra-ba # 'i dbang-po #  yul la rgyun-du #  'byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni brten-pa #  mtshungs-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang ldan zhing rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang 'dri-ba # 'i dbang-po #  yul rnams la rgyun-du #  'byung zhing rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung-ba #  dang 'dra-ba # 'i phyir dbang-po #  de ni brten-pa #  dang mtshungs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
vijQAna virahita sva sAdRSya prabanDa utpatitaH tad saBA gam vijQAnena viprayuktasya indriyasya sva Atma sAdRSyena prabanDa utpattiH indriya lakzaNa sAdRSya arTena tad sa BAgam veditavyam
# rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang bral zhing rang dang 'dra-ba #  rgyun-du #  'byung-ba # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-dag #  dang mtshungs-pa #  ste / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang mi-ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  bdag-nyid #  dang 'dra-ba #  ni rgyun-du #  'byung zhing dbang-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang 'dra-ba # 'i phyir de dang mtshungs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
rUpa skanDa eka deSaH cakzuH Adi paQcAndriya lakzaNaH
# gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'i phyogs-gcig #  ces bya-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po-lnga # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
paQca rUpINi DAtu AyatanAni cakzuH AdIni iti eva
# gzugs-can #  gyi khams dang skye-mched #  lnga'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig la sogs ba nyid do /
vedanA utpatti ASraya rUpataH iti yat rUpam ASritya vedanA utpadyate tat upAttam iti ucyate
# tshor-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i gnas kyi gzugs kyi zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs gang-la #  brten-nas #  tshor-ba #  'byung-ba #  de zin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
rUpa skanDa eka deSaH sa aDizWAna indriya saMgahItaH
# gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'i phyogs-gcig #  ces bya-ba #  ni gnas-dang-bcas-pa # 'i dbang-po # s bsdus-pa # 'o /
paQca rUpINi DAtu AyatanAni cakzuH AdIni
# khams dang skye-mched #  gzugs-can #  lnga / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'o /
caturNAm ca eka deSaH rUpa ganDa rasa sprazwavyAnAm indriyA vinirBAgI
# bzhi'i phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  dbang-po #  las gzhan-du #  ma-gyur-pa # 'o /
vizaya grahaNa aDipataH cakzuH AdInAm zaNNAm tad ADipatyena rUpa Adi AlaMbane citta cEta pravRtteH
# yul la 'dzin-pa # r dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  drug ste / / de'i dbang gis gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  la sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kula prabanDa aDipataH strI puruza indriyayoH tatas putra pOtra Adi anvaya pravRtteH
# rigs kyi rgyud la dbang-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni pho dang mo'i dbang-po #  ste / / de-la # s bu dang tsha bo la-sogs-pa # 'i rigs 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
Sezam yaTA aDipati pratyaye nirdizwam taTA anugantavyam
# lhag-ma #  ni bdag-po'i-rkyen #  ji-skad-bstan-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  khong-du-chud-pa # r bya'o /
rUpa skanDa eka deSaH cakzuH Srotra GrANa jihvA kAya strI puruza indriya lakzaNaH
# gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'i phyogs-gcig #  ces bya-ba #  ni / / mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid dang pho dang mo'i dbang-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
saMskAra skanDa eka deSaH jIvita SradDA vIrya smRti samADi prajQA indriya lakzaNaH
# 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # 'i phyogs-gcig #  ces bya-ba #  ni srog dang dad ba dang brtson 'grus dang dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi dbang-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
dvAdaSa DAtavaH indriya vijQAna DAtavaH / zaXa AyatanAni ADyAtmikAni
# khams bcu gnyis zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang-po #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  rnams so / / skye-mched-drug #  ces bya-ba #  ni nang gi rnams so /
Darma DAtu Ayatana eka deSaH ca jIvita indriyam suKa AdIni SradDA dAni paQca
# chos-kyi-khams #  dang skye-mched #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni srog-gi-dbang-po #  dang bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  lnga lnga'o /
duHKA vedanA duHKa AtmikA satI svena eva lakzaNena duHKa duHKa tAH
# sdug-bsngal-gyi-tshor-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bdag-nyid #  yin te / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kho-na # s sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid do /
tad utpatti nimitta BUtAH tu indriya arTAH tad saMprayuktAH ca duHKa vedanIya tvAt duHKa duHKa tA drazwavyA
# de-la # s 'byung-ba # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa #  dbang-po #  dang don rnams dang de dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  rnams ni sdug-bsngal #  myong-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  blta'o /
suKAyAH vedanAyAH tad vedanIyAnAm ca DarmANAm vipariNAmena dOrmanasya utpAdAt tad vipariNatiH vipariNAma duHKa tA
# bde-ba'i-tshor-ba #  dang de myong-bar-byed-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  'gyur-ba # s yid-mi-bde-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir de 'gyur-ba #  ni 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid do /
tatra ca anunayena cittasya vipariNamanam vipariNAma duHKa tA veditavyA
# de-la #  yang rjes-su-chags-pa # s sems 'gyur-ba #  ni 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya #  ste /
yaTA uktam avadIrNaH vipariNatena cittena iti
# ji-skad-du #  zhen nas gyur-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
aduHKa asuKAH vedanA Alaya vijQAna saMprayuktA tad vedanIyAH ca saMskArAH duHKa vipariNAma duHKa tayA udOzWulyena anugata tvAt tena duHKa tA dvayena avinirmukta tvAt ekadA duHKa avasTAm Bajante ekadA suKa avasTAm na nitya kAla maduHKa asuKa avasTAH eva Bavanti
# sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang de myong-bar-byed-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  dang sdug-bsngal #  dang 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyi gnas-ngan-len #  dang ldan-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal #  de gnyis las rnam-par-ma-grol-ba # s res-'ga' #  ni bde-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  la brten / / res-'ga' #  ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi gnas-skabs #  la brten-te #  / / rtag-tu #  khor mor sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  su 'gyur-ba #  ni ma yin no /
tasmAt anitya tA anubanDa arTena ayogakzema tvAt saMskAra duHKa tA veditavyA / skanDAnAm
# de-lta-bas-na #  mi-rtag-pa #  rjes su bcings-pa # s grub-pa-dang-bde-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
trayANAm DAtUnAm manaH Darma manaH vijQAna DAtUnAm / dvayoH ca AyatanayoH manaH Darma AyatanayoH
# phung-po #  rnams dang khams-gsum #  ni yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa'i-khams #  rnams so / / skye-mched #  gnyis ni yid dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  do /
eka deSam sTApayitvA anAsrava lakzaNam tad anyAni sarvANi iti / akuSalasya kuSala sa Asravasya ca AyatyA sa saMprayogam Alaya vijQAnam vipAkaH / atas tena vipAkena tat uBayam sa vipAkam iti ucyate / skanDAnAm
# phyogs-gcig #  ma-gtogs-pa #  ni zag-pa-med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / thams-cad #  do zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-las-gzhan-pa #  dag go / / mi-dge-ba #  dang dge-ba #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ni phyi-ma-la #  yod de / / de'i-phyir #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  des-na #  de gnyis rnam-par-smin-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  las gzhan-pa #  mig la-sogs-pa #  dang bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa #  de-la # s byung-ba #  zhes brjod-pa #  'thob ste / / de-la # s skyes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
daSAnAm DAtUnAm vijQAna rUpa Sabda Darma DAtUnAm / caturNA ca AyatanAnAm rUpa Sabda manaH Darma AyatanAnAm / eka deSaH avyAkRta anAsrava varjaH / AlayavijQAnAt tat anyat tu cakzuH Adikam ca suKa duHKa Adikam ca tat vipAkra jam iti AKyAm laBate tatas jAtam iti kRtvA / pariNatitaH pAriNAmikaH kavaXIkAraH AhAraH pariNAma kAle indriya mahA BUta pozaNAt
# phung-po #  rnams dang khams bcu zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa #  bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos-kyi-khams #  rnams so / / skye-mched #  bzhi zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  rnams so / / phyogs-gcig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  dang zag-pa-med-pa #  ma-rtogs-pa # 'o / / 'ju bas kyang 'ju ba las gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni kham gyi zas 'ju ba'i dus na dbang-po # 'i 'byung-ba-chen-po #  brtas-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vizayataH vEzayikaH sparSa AhAraH izwa vizayA DizWAnena sparSena ASraya anugrahaNAt
# yul gyis kyang yul las gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni reg-pa # 'i zas te / / yid-du-'ong-ba # 'i yul gyi gnas kyis reg-pa # s lus la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ASAtaH ASikaH manaH saMcetana AhAraH aBipreta vastu prativadDa ASA vaSena ASraya anugrahaNAt
# re-ba # s kyang re-ba #  las gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid la sems-pa # 'i zas te / / 'dod-pa # 'i dngos-po #  dang 'brel-ba # 'i re-ba # 'i dbang gis lus la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upAdAnataH OpAdAnikaH vijQAnam AhAraH AlayavijQAna upAdAna vaSena AtmaBA vA upasTAnAt / taTA hi tad viyuktaH ASrayaH pUtIBavati iti
# len-pa # s kyang len-pa #  las gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i zas te / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i dbang gis lus-gnas-pa # 'i phyir te /
punar catvAraH api AhArAH samasya caturBiH praBedEH vyavasTApyante
# 'di-ltar #  de dang bral na lus ru la bar 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / yang zas-rnam-pa-bzhi #  po dag ni bsdus nas rnam-pa-bzhi # s rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA aSudDa ASraya sTitikaH kAma avacarANAm pRTagjanAnAm sakala banDana tvAt
# ma-dag-pa # 'i lus-gnas-pa # r byed-pa #  ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams kyi ste / / mtha'-dag #  ni 'ching-ba #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ma-dag-pa # 'i gnas so /
SudDa aSudDa ASraya sTitikaH SEkzANAm rUpa ArUpya avacarANAm ca pRTagjanAnAm sa avaSeza vanDana tvAt
# dag-pa #  dang ma-dag-pa # 'i lus-gnas-pa # r byed-pa #  ni slob-pa #  rnams dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa # 'i so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams kyi ste / / 'ching-ba # 'i lhag-ma #  las pa'i phyir ro /
SudDa ASraya sTitikaH arhatAm sarva banDana vinirmukta tvAt
# dag-pa # 'i lus-gnas-pa # r byed-pa #  ni dgra-bcom-pa #  rnams kyi ste / / 'ching-ba #  thams-cad-la # s rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sTiti sAMdarSikaH budDAnAm boDisattvAnAm ca mahA praBAva prAptAnAm AhAra vaSena sTitiH iti saMdarSana mAtra tvAt
# gnas-pa # r kun-tu #  ston-pa #  ni sangs-rgyas #  rnams dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mthu chen-po #  thob-pa #  rnams kyi ste / / zas kyi dbang gis gnas-pa # r kun-tu #  ston-pa #  tsam gyi phyir ro /
asaMskRta eka deSaH nizpanna svaBAvaH sottaram iti nirvANam muktvA tasya sarva Darma agra tva Adi SudDAyAH ca taTatAyAH tad lakzaNa tvAt
# 'dus-ma-byas #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  gis kyang gong-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa #  ste / / de'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  yin-pas #  de ni chos-thams-cad #  kyi mchog yin pa'i phyir ro /
samAsatas praBedaH triviDaH triviDam svaBAvam aDikRtya pudgala nErAtmya nayena veditavyaH
# bsdus-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / gang-zag #  la bdag-med-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum gyi dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra parikalpitaH svaBAvaH skanDa AdIni aDizWAya avidyamAnaH Atma Adi svaBAvaH yaH parikalpitaH
# de-la #  kun-tu #  brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la brten-nas #  med-pa # r yang bdag la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  du gang kun-tu-rtog-pa # 'o /

# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  de-dag #  ni gang-du #  yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  bdag la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  de 'byung-ba # 'o /

# yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni dngos-po #  dang dngos-po-med-pa #  dang mi-ldan-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de / / phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la bdag la-sogs-pa #  med-pa #  pa dang bdag-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yod-pa-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  kyi phyir ro /

# mtshan-nyid #  kyis rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni chos-rnams #  kyi rang-bzhin #  gyi dbang-du-byas-te #  / / gzugs dang tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /

# rnam-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni khyad-par #  gyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  rdzas-su-yod-pa #  dang btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /

# rgyun gyis rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni lus gcig la yang phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i skad-cig #  so-so #  gzhan gyi dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o / / phyi-rol #  tu bltas-pa # s rab-tu-dbye-ba #  gang zhe na /
bahirmuKa praBedaH yat BUyasA kAma avacaraH iti BUyograhaNam nizpanda Darma hetuka Sruta cintA Amaya vyudAsa arTam / samAptaH praBedaH
# phal-cher #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  na spyod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  las byung-ba #  ma-rtogs-pa #  ston-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bam po bzhi-pa #  /

# mtshan-nyid-kyis-bsdus-pa #  ni gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  nyid kyis gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  bsdus-pa #  nas / / rgya-cher #  chos-kyi-skye-mched #  kyis chos-kyi-skye-mched #  bsdus-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o / / khams-kyis-bsdus-pa #  gang zhe na /
DAtu saMgraheNa sarvANi skanDa DAtu AyatanAni AlayavijQAnena saMgRhItAni sarvezAm tatra bIjataH asti tvAt
# phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  thams-cad #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # s bsdus-pa #  ste / / de-la #  de-dag #  thams-cad-kyi #  sa-bon #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jAti saMgraheNa skanDEH rASi Adi arTa yuktAH rUpa AdayaH sarve saMgRhItAH vilakzaNAH api anyonyam sva lakzaNena eka jAtIya tvAt
# rigs kyis bsdus-pa #  ni phung-po #  rnams kyis spungs pa la-sogs-pa # 'i don-dang-ldan-pa #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'o / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kyis phan tshun mtshan-nyid #  mi 'dra yang rigs gcig pa'i phyir thams-cad #  bsdus so /
evam DAtuBiH ca AyatanEH ca upaBoga DAraNa arTa yuktAH Aya dvAra arTa yuktAH cakzuH AdayaH saMgRhItAH veditavyAH
# de-bzhin-du #  khams rnams dang skye-mched #  rnams kyis kyang nye-bar-spyod-pa #  'dzin-pa # 'i don-dang-ldan-pa #  dang skye-ba # 'i sgo'i don-dang-ldan-pa #  mig la-sogs-pa #  bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
avasTA saMgraheNa skanDAH eka jAtIyAH api suKa Adi avasTAm niyamayya suKa avasTAH suKa avasTEH eva saMgRhItAH na duHKa Adi avasTEH / evam duHKa avasTA duHKa asuKa avasTAH ca tad avasTEH eva saMgRhItAH / yaTA skanDAH evam DAtavaH AyatanAni ca
# gnas-skabs #  kyis bsdus-pa #  ni phung-po #  rnams rigs gcig-tu #  zin-kyang #  bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  nges-par #  byas-na # s bde-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni bde-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  nyid kyis bsdus kyi / / sdug-bsngal #  gyi gnas-skabs #  kyis ni ma yin no / / de-bzhin-du #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi gnas-skabs #  kyang de nyid kyi gnas-skabs #  kyis bsdus so / / phung-po #  rnams ji-lta-ba # r khams rnams dang skye-mched #  rnams kyang de-bzhin #  no / / grogs kyis bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la /
sahAya saMgraheNa rUpa skanDaH saha tad ASritEH vedanA AdiBiH sahAyEH gRhyamANaH paQcaBiH skanDEH saMgRhItaH
# gzugs-kyi-phung-po #  ni sdud-pa #  na de-la #  brten-pa #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  grogs rnams dang lhan-cig-tu #  phung-po #  lnga po dag gis bsdus so /
evam vedanA AdayA api pratyekam sa parivArAH gRhyamANAH paQcaBiH skanDEH saMgRhItAH Bavanti
# de-bzhin-du #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  rnams kyang sdud-pa #  na so-so # r phung-po #  lnga po dag gis bsdus-pa # r 'gyur ro /
taTA DAtavaH AyatanAni ca sa parivArANi pratyekam sarva arDa atuBiH AyataneH ca saMgRhItAni veditavyAni / eka deSa saMgraheNa SIla skanDaH rUpa skanDa eka deSena saMgRhItaH
# de-bzhin-du #  khams rnams dang skye-mched #  'khor dang bcas-pa #  rnams kyang so-so # r khams dang skye-mched #  thams-cad-kyi # s bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / phyogs-gcig #  gis bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / tshul-khrims-kyi-phung-po #  ni gzugs-kyi-phung-po # 'i phyogs-gcig #  gis bsdus so /
samADi prajQA skanDO saMskAra skanDa eka deSena
# ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi phung-po #  ni 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po # 'i phyogs-gcig #  gis bsdus so /
kAma vyApAda hiMsA DAtavaH Darma DAtu eka deSena saMgRhItAH
# 'dod-pa #  dang gnod-sems #  dang rnam-par-'tshe-ba # 'i khams ni chos-kyi-khams #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  gis bsdus so /

# nam-mkha' #  mtha' yas skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa #  ni yid dang chos-kyi-skye-mched #  kyi phyogs-gcig #  gis bsdus so /
evam kRtvA yAvantaH DarmAH skanDa DAtu AyatanEH saMgRhItAH sUtra antarezu tezAm anyatama saMgrahaH eka deSa saMgrahaH veditavyaH / sakala saMgraheNa duHKa skanDaH paQcaBiH upAdAna skanDEH saMgRhItaH kAmaDAtuH azwAdaSaBiH DAtuBiH asaMjQi sattva Ayatanam daSaBiH AyatanaMganDa rasa Ayatana varjEH saMgRhItam
# de-ltar #  byas-na #  mdo-sde #  gzhan dag tu phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  kyis bsdus-pa # 'i chos ji-snyed-pa #  de-dag #  gang-yang-rung-ba # s bsdus-pa #  ni phyogs-gcig #  gis bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / mtha'-dag-gis #  bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / sdug-bsngal-gyi-phung-po #  lnga po nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po dag gis bsdus so / / 'dod-pa'i-khams #  ni bco brgyad po dag gis bsdus so / / 'du-shes-med-pa # 'i sems-can #  gyi skye-mched #  ni dri dang ro'i skye-mched #  ma-gtogs-pa #  skye-mched #  bcu po dag gis bsdus-pa # 'o /
evam kRtvA yAvantaH DarmAH skanDa DAtu AyatanaMH saMgRhItAH sUtra antarezu tezAm aSezatas saMgrahaH sakala saMgrahaH veditavyaH
# de-ltar #  byas-na #  mdo-sde #  gzhan dag tu phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  rnams kyis bsdus-pa # 'i chos ji-snyed-pa #  de-dag #  ni mtha'-dag-gis #  bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / gcig-gis-gcig #  bsdus-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / phung-po #  rnams ni so-so # r khams dang skye-mched #  rnams kyis bsdus te /
itaretara saMgraheNa skanDAH pratyekam DAtuBiH AyatanEH ca saMgRhItAH yaTAyogam evam DAtavaH skanDAyatana AyatanAni skanDaDAtuBiH saMgRhItAni iti vistareNa avagantavyam
# ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro / / de-bzhin-du #  khams rnams kyang phung-po #  dang skye-mched #  rnams kyis bsdus shing / / skye-mched #  rnams kyang phung-po #  dang khams-kyis-bsdus-pa # r rgya-cher #  khong-du-chud-pa # r bya'o /
saMgraha lakzaNam punar loka prasidDa saMgraha anusAreNa zaXi vaDam drazwavyam / tat punar katamat
# yang bsdus-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'jig-rten #  gyi grags-pa # s bsdus-pa #  dang mthun-par #  rnam-pa-drug #  tu blta ste / / de-yang #  gang zhen /
pada sTAna saMgrahaH yaTA jambUdvIpa saMgRhItAH manuzyAH araNya saMgRhItAH mRgAH iti loke ucyate taTA iha api cakzuH AdiBiH cakzuH vijQAna AdInAm saMgrahaH veditavyaH
# gzhi'i-gnas #  kyis bsdus-pa #  ni dper-na #  mi 'dzam-bu'i-gling #  gis bsdus so / / ri dags rnams ni dgon-pa # s bsdus so zhes 'jig-rten #  na brjod-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  'dir yang mig la-sogs-pa # s mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

# 'ching-ba # s bsdus-pa #  ni dper-na #  thag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s shing khur ba la-sogs-pa #  bcings-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  lus-kyis #  mig la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po #  rnams bcings so /

paramANu deSe sarvezAm deSinAm iti eka paramANu paryApannAnAm rUpa AdInAm avinirBAgaH samAna deSa tvena veditavyaH
# rdul-phra-rab #  kyi phyogs la phyogs can thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni rdul-phra-rab #  gcig-tu #  gtogs-pa # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni phyogs mthun-pa # s tha-dad-pa #  med-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

# rdul-phra-rab #  las gong-ma #  phyogs can rnams 'dres-par-gyur-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / chu rnyog ma can gyi nang na chu dang sa'i rdul-phra-rab #  rnams phan tshun du 'dres-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /

# mthun-par #  rtogs-pa # s mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni gzhan gyi dngos-po #  dang yin gyi rang-gi #  dngos-po #  dang ni ma-yin-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  sems ni sems gzhan dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin zhing tshor-ba #  yang tshor-ba #  gzhan dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
na virudDayoH tat yaTA rAga dvezayoH kuSala akuSalayoH vA iti evamAdi

na visadRSa kAlayoH tat yaTA vartamAna anAgatayoH atIta vartamAnayoH vA
# dus mi-'dra-ba #  gnyis ma-yin-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / da-ltar #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  gnyis dang 'das-pa #  dang da-ltar #  gnyis so /
na visaBAga DAtu BUmikayoH tat yaTA kAma avacara rUpa avacarayoH praTama dvitIya DyAna BUmikayoH vA iti evamAdi
