# mthun-par #  gtogs-pa # s mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  drug-pa #  'di dag ni kun-tu #  'gro-ba #  ste / / gnas-skabs-thams-cad #  du 'di dag las gang-yang-rung-ba #  gcig med na med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ucitaH tad ekatyAnAm ca SEkzA SEkzANAm iti ekAnta lOkikAnAm kuSalAnAm akuSala avyAkRtAnAm ca yaTAsaMBavam / Adya tad uttarANAm iti apUrva jAtIya tvena praTama kzaNa utpannAnAm dvitIya Adi kzaNa utpannAnAm ca loka uttarANAm anucita tva jQApana arTam
# 'dres-pa #  ni slob-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa #  dag las kyang kha-cig #  go zhes-bya-ba #  ni gcig-tu #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i dge-ba #  rnams dang mi-dge-ba #  rnams dang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  rnams kyis te / / ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro / / dang-po #  de-dang-de # 'i 'og ma rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  skad-cig #  dang-po #  las byung-ba #  rnams dang skad-cig-gnyis-pa-la #  sogs-pa #  las byung-ba #  rnams kyang sngon gyi rang-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # s ma-'dris-pa #  nyid-du #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ldan-pa #  gang zhe na /
samanvAgamaH lakzaNataH pUrvavat tat yaTA kuSala AdInAm DarmANAm AcayA pacaye prAptiH pratilamBaH samanvAgamaH iti prajQaptiH
# mtshan-nyid #  kyis ni snga-ma-bzhin #  no zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi 'phel-ba #  dang 'grib-pa #  la 'thob-pa #  dang rnyed-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  gdags so zhes-bya'o #  / / sa-bon-dang-ldan-pa #  gang zhe na /
bIja samanvAgamaH iti kAmaDAtO jAtO BUtaH trEDAtukEH kleSa upakleSEH samanvAgataH iti avIta rAgam pRTagjanam aDikRtya etat vEditavyam / vIta rAgaH tu tatra UrDvam vA jAtaH yatas BUmeH vIta rAgaH tad BUmikEH asamanvAgataH samanvAgataH ca pratipakzeNa upahata tvAt asamudDAtita tvAt ca anuSayataH yaTAkramam
# 'dod-pa'i-khams #  su skyes-pa # r gyur ba ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang ldan te / / de ni so-so'i-skye-bo #  'dod-chags #  dang ma-bral-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  ni de 'am / / gong-ma # r skyes kyang rung ste / / sa gong gis 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # r sa de pa rnams dang de-dag #  dang mi-ldan-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  yang yin te / / gnyen-po # s gnod-par-byas-pa #  dang-ba # g la nyal legs-par #  ma bcom-pa # 'i phyir go-rims #  bzhin no /
upapatti prAtilamBikan= ca kuSalaH iti yatra jAtaH tad BUmikEH eva
# skye-ba # s thob-pa # 'i dge-ba #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni gong-du #  skyes-pa # 'i sa pa de'i sa pa rnams nyid dang ldan no /
trEDAtuka pratipakza lABI iti loka uttara mArga lABI
# khams-gsum-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  thob-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam thob-pa # 'o /
yasya yasya prakArasya pratipakzaH utpannaH iti BAvanA prahAtavyasya aDimAtra AdeH kleSasya
# rnam-pa #  gang-dang-gang #  gi gnyen-po #  byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsgoms-pas-spong-ba # r bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  chen-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tasya tasya bIja samanvAgamena asamanvAgataH anuSayataH samudDAtita tvAt
# de-dang-de # 'i sa-bon #  dang mi-ldan-pa # s ldan-pa #  ma yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / bag-la-nyal #  legs-par-bcom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vaSitA samanvAgamaH prAyogikAnAm kuSalAnAm iti Sruta maya AdInAm sati api bIje tad aByAsa kRtAm tad janmikIm bIja puzwim antareNa saMmuKIkartum aSakya tvAt
# dbang dang ldan-pa #  gang zhe na / / sbyor-ba-las-byung-ba #  dge-ba'i-chos #  'jig-rten-pa #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  ni thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sa-bon #  yod-du-zin-kyang #  de goms-pa # r ma-byas-pa # s tshe de'i sa-bon #  brtas-pa #  med-pa # s mngon du byed mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tad ekatyAnAm ca avyAkRtAnAm SaMlpa sTAnikanEH mANika citta praBRtInAm
# de-dag #  las kyang lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  kha-cig #  ces bya-ba #  ni bzo'i gzas nas sprul pa'i sems la-sogs-pa # 'o /
mokza hetu vEkalyAt AtyantikaH ezAm hetu asamanva AgamaH iti
# thar-pa # 'i rgyu dang mi-ldan-pa # 'i phyir / / de-dag #  gtan-du #  rgyu dang mi ldan te /
mokza prApti hetu asamanva AgamaH iti arTaH
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  rnams dang thar-pa #  thob-pa'i-rgyu #  dang mi-ldan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
kaH punar mokza prApti hetuH
# thar-pa #  thob-pa'i-rgyu #  gang yin zhe na /
yasya evam taTatAyAm kleSa dOzWulyam saMnivizwam Bavati tat kim pratipakzA anukUla pratyaya lABe Sakyate samudDAtayitum sa BavyatA rTena hetuH iti ucyate
# de-bzhin-nyid #  la nyon-mongs-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len gnas-pa #  yin te / / rgyu gang gnyen-po # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i rkyen rnyed na legs-par #  'joms nus-pa #  de skal-ba-dang-ldan-pa # 'i phyir rgya zhes-bya'o #  /
viparyayAt hetu vEkalyam veditavyam / II satyaviniH cayaH nAma dvitIyaH samuccayaH / tad sattva janmataH janma aDizWAnataH ca iti yaH ca jAyate sattva lokaH yatra ca jAyate BAjana loke tat uBayam duHKa iti uktam Bavati uktam
# bzlog-pa #  ni rgyu dang mi-ldan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / de ni sems-can #  gyi skye-ba #  dang skye-ba'i-gnas #  kyis kyang zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-can-gyi-'jig-rten #  gang skye-ba #  dang snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  gang-du #  skye-ba #  de-gnyi-ga #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  zhes bstan-pa #  yin no /
yaH ca sattva lokaH yaH ca BAjana lokaH karma kleSa janitaH karma kleSa aDipateyaH iti AByAm tayoH sattva BAjana lokayoH duHKa tva kAraNam jQApayati
# sems-can-gyi-'jig-rten #  gang-yin-pa #  dang snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  gang yin ba de-la # s dang nyon-mongs-pa # s skyed-pa #  dang las dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dbang gis byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni go-rims #  bzhin te / / de gnyis kyis ni sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyi rgyu ston to /
api Kalu jAtiH duHKam iti evamAdi pUrvam samasya duHKa satya lakzaNam vyutpAdya aDunA duHKa satyam AraBya sUtra uktasya nirdeSasya arTa viBaktum AraBate
# yang skye-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  lo zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni sngar mdor bsdus te sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bstan nas / / da-ni #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  las brtsams te / / mdo-sde #  las byung-ba #  bstan-pa'i-don #  rnam-par-dbye-ba # r brtsams te /
jAtiH duHKam saMvAda duHKa tAm tad anyat uKa sva ASraya tAm ca upAdAya iti mAtuH kukzA vAma pakvASayayoH antarAle AsInasya nizkrAmataH vA kukzeH viviDa aSuci dravya asaMpIXa aFga saMmarda duHKa anuBava pArTena jAtO satyAm jarA Adi duHKa aByanuzaFga arTena ca yaTAkramam
# skye-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  ni dog pa'i sdug-bsngal #  nyid dang de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  gyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni ma'i-mngal #  na zhu-ba #  dang ma-zhu-ba #  gnyis kyi bar na 'dug-pa #  las 'byung-ba #  dang mngal na mi gtsang ba'i rdzas sna-tshogs #  kyis gzir te / / lus kyi yan-lag #  kun-tu #  btsir ba la-sogs-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  myong-ba # 'i phyir ro / / btsas nas kyang rga-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  zhar la 'byung-ba # 'i phyir te /
zax samAnAni azwO Bavanti vipariNati duKam triDA kRtvA
# go-rims #  bzhin no / / brgyad yin yang drug tu 'gyur zhes-bya-ba #  ni gsum-'gyur #  ba'i sdug-bsngal #  du byas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jAti AdiBiH duHKa duHKa tA paridIpana vacanam duHKa vedanIya Darma sva lakzaNa arTena
# skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid yongs su bstan to zhes-bya-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i chos kyi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
priya vinA Ama AdinA vipariNAma duHKa tA paridIpana vacanam prApta aprApta suKa vedanIya Darma vipariNati sva lakzaNa arTena
# sdug-pa-dang-bral-ba # 'i dngos-po #  la-sogs-pa # s 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid yongs su bstan to zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig ni phrad-pa #  dang ma-phrad-pa # s bde pa myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i chos 'gyur-ba # 'i rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  yin ba'i phyir ro /
paQca upAdAna skanDA duHKam iti anena saMskAra duHKa tA paridIpana vacanam dvaya avinirmokzA nitetA nubanDa yoga kzema arTena / jAtiH muKam iti evamAdi saMvRti satyena duKam lOkika jQAna vizaya tvAt
# nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga sdug-bsngal #  lo zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyi yongs su bstan to zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig 'di gnyis las rnam-pa # r ma grol zhing mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  rjes su 'brel te grub-pa-dang-bde-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / skye-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  lo zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa # r sdug-bsngal-ba #  ste / / 'jig-rten-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
paQca upAdAna skanDA duHKam iti paramArTa satyena duKam saMniveSa taTatA muKena lokottara jQAna vizaya tvAt
# nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga sdug-bsngal #  lo zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnas-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  kyi sgo nas don-dam-pa'i-bden-pa # r sdug-bsngal-ba #  ste / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
duHKa sAmAnya lakzaNe yEH AkArEH yogine duHKa satyam vyavacArayanti tat yaTA nityataH duHKataH SUnyataH na Atma tas ca
# sdug-bsngal #  gyi spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni rnal-'byor #  bas rnam-pa #  gang dag gis sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # r spyad-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang sdug-bsngal-ba #  nyid dang stong-pa-nyid #  dang bdag-med-pa #  nyid kyis so /
tatra dvAdaSa viDena lakzaNena anityam duHKa satyam veditavyam
# de-la #  mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis kyis mi-rtag-pa #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
tat punar rasat lakzaNam yaTA na asti sarvadA duHKa satyam Atma Atma uBaya svaBAvam iti yaH arTaH saH arTaH anityam iti satyam iti
# de-yang #  med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / bdag dang bdag-gi #  ba'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi sdug-bsngal #  pa'i bden-pa #  rtag-tu #  med-pa # 'i don gang-yin-pa # 'i don de ni mi-rtag-pa #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'o /
akArasya pratizeDa arTa tvAt nitya Sabdasya ca sarva kAla arTa tvAt iti
# mi zhes-bya-ba #  ni dgag-pa # 'i don yin pa'i phyir ro / / rtag ces bya-ba # 'i sgra ni dus-thams-cad-pa # 'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
vinASa lakzaNam saMskArANAm BUtvA aBAvaH / vipariNa tila kzaNam prabanDa asAdRSyena pravRttiH
# rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'du-byed-rnams #  byung nas med-par-'gyur-ba # 'o / / 'gyur-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rgyu mi-'dra-ba #  nyid-du #  'byung-ba # 'o /
viyoga lakzaNam tad avasTezu eva vastuzu svaBAva vaSi tva BraMSaH kvacid parEH svIkaraNam api veditavyam
# 'bral-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni dngos-po # 'i gnas-skabs #  de-dag-nyid #  la rang-bzhin #  gyi dbang nyams-pa #  dang kha-cig #  tu ni gzhan dag gis bdag-gi # r byas-pa # r yang rig-par-bya # 'o /
saMnihita lakzaNam yat tadAnIm eva anuBUyamAna anitya tA
# nye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi tshe na mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  myong-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
DarmatA lakzaNam yAma vaSyam anuBavizyati
# chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  ni gang gdon-mi-za-bar #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'o /
kzaNa lakzaNam Atma lABa anantaram avaSya vinASitA
# skad-cig #  gi mtshan-nyid #  ni bdag-nyid #  rnyed nas de ma-thag-tu #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa #  nyid do /
prabanDa lakzaNam anAdim ati saMsAre AjavaMja vIBAvena vRttiH
# rgyun gyi mtshan-nyid #  ni thog-ma-med-pa #  can gyi 'khor-ba #  nas 'ong-ba-dang-'gro-ba # r 'gyur-ba # s 'byung-ba # 'o /
vyADi jarA maraNa lakzaNam DAtu vEzamyam Kaliti Adikam sTiti kAla aveDa upayogaH ca
# na-ba #  dang rga-ba #  dang 'chi-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni khams-ma-snyoms-pa #  dang spyi cer du gyur-pa #  dang gnas-pa # 'i dus kyi 'phen-pa #  zad-pa # 'o /
citta citta AkAra vRtti lakzaNam vipakza pratipakza avasTAna avasTita tvam
# sems sna-tshogs #  kyi rnam-par-'gyur-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  dang gnyen-po # 'i gnas la gnas-pa # 'o /
Boga saMpad tila kzaNam sarva lOkika samRdDaH nAma na Atyantika tayA duranta tvam / BAjana saMvarta vivarta lakzaNam mahA pRTivI AdinAm agni AdiBiH punar punar vinASataH utpAdataH ca agni ambu vAyu saMvartanIBiH dahana kledana SozaNa AtmikABiH yaTAkramam
# longs-spyod #  'byor-pa #  rgud-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i 'byor-ba #  thams-cad #  gtan-du #  'dug-pa #  ma-yin-pa # s mthar nyes-pa #  nyid do / / snod 'jig-pa #  dang chags-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni sa-chen-po #  la-sogs-pa #  me la-sogs-pa # s yang-dang-yang #  'jig-pa #  dang 'byung-ba #  ste /
praTama dvitIya tRtIya sTAna avasAne loka saMniveSe saMvRtte tad UrDvam yAni avaSizyante dvitIya tRtIya caturTa DyAnasya anAntarANi tAni tAsAm SIrzANi veditavyAni
# me dang chu dang rlung 'tshig-pa # r byed-pa #  dang rul-ba # r byed-pa #  dang skam par byed-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  'jig-pa #  rnams dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  bsam-gtan-dang-po #  dang gnyis-pa #  dang gsum-pa # 'i gnas kyi mthar-thug-pa # r 'jig-rten-gnas-pa #  'jig go / / de'i gong-ma #  lhag-ma #  lus pa bsam-gtan-gnyis-pa #  dang gsum-pa #  dang bzhi-pa # 'i gnas gzhan gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  ni de-dag #  gis bsdus bar rig-par-bya # 'o /
caturTa DyAna BUmikAnAm tarhi vimAnAnAm kena saMvarta vivartaH
# bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa #  rnams kyi gzhal-med-khang #  rnams gang-gis #  'jig cing chags she na /
na kena cit bAhyena tEH eva tu sarvEH jAyamAnEH saha tAni vimAnAni nirvartante cyavamAnEH saha tAni niruDyante iti
# phyi-rol #  gang-gis #  kyang ma yin gyi gzhal-med-khang #  de-dag #  ni sems-can #  de-dag-nyid #  skye-ba #  dang lhan-cig-tu #  'grub cing 'chi-ba #  dang lhan-cig-tu #  'gag ste /
saH eva tezAm saMvarta vivartaH veditavyaH
# de nyid de-dag #  gi 'jig-pa #  dang chags-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
yEH kalpasya niryANam Bavati iti parisamAptiH Bavati iti arTaH / ekaH antara kalpaH apakarzaH vivarta kAle ekAnna viMSatitamaH / azwAdaSa utkarza apakarzAH / tatas UrDvam ekaH utkarzaH paScimaH
# de-dag #  gis bskal-ba #  tshar-phyin-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r 'gyur zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / chags-pa # 'i dus na mar-'bri-ba #  bar-gyi-bskal-pa #  gcig dang yar-'phel-ba #  dang mar-'bri-ba #  bco brgyad de bcu dgu'o / / de'i-'og-tu #  tha-ma # r yar-skye-ba #  gcig go /
AyukzayAt maraNam kAla cyutim aDikRtya yAvat Akzepam AyuzaH parisamApta tvAt
# tshe zang ces bya-ba #  ni 'chi-ba #  ste / / tshe'i 'phen-pa #  ji tsam yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir dus-su-'chi-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o /
puNya kzayAt akAla cyutim aDikRtya samApatti AsvAdana tayA tad AyuH Akzepaka karma BAvanA upaDAtAt
# bsod nams zad ces bya-ba #  ni dus-ma-yin-pa # r 'chi-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i ro-myong-bar-byed-pa # s de'i tshe 'phen-par-byed-pa'i-las #  bsgos-pa #  las gnod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
karma kzayAt prabanDa cyutim aDikRtya tasmin= Ayatane upapadya apara paryAya vedanIya karmaNaH upayukta tvAt aBAvAt vA tatra BUyas anutpattitaH veditavyam
# las kyang zad nas zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyun chad nas 'chi-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / gnas der skyes nas myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  dang lan-grangs-gzhan-la #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i las spyad-zin-pa # 'i phyir ram / / med-pa # 'i phyir der yang mi-skye-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
azwa AkAram vA duHKam iti saMbADa duHKa tA Adi
# sdug-bsngal-rnam-pa-brgyad #  ces bya-ba #  ni dog pa'i sdug-bsngal #  nyid la-sogs-pa # 'o /
utpAda aMSikI anitya tA aBUtvA BAvaH sa ca duHKa pakzyANAm saMskArANAm bADana AtmakaH
# skye-ba # 'i char gtogs-pa # 'i mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  ni ma-byung-ba #  las 'byung-ba #  ste / / de ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi phyogs kyi 'du-byed-rnams #  la gnod-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  do /
iti tAm anitya tAm pratItya duHKa duHKa tA prajQAyate
# mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  de-la #  brten-nas #  sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid rab tu shes so /
vyayAMSikI BUtvA aBAvaH sa ca suKa pakzyANAm saMskArANAm anaBipretaH
# 'jig-pa # 'i char gtogs-pa #  na byung nas med-par-'gyur-ba #  ste / / de ni bde-ba'i-phyogs #  kyi 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi mi-'dod-pa # 'o /
iti tAm pratItya vipariNAma duHKa tA prajQAyate
# de-la #  brten-nas #  'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid rab tu shes so /
sa dOzWulyAnAm saMskArANAm prabanDena udayaH api anaBipretaH vyayaH api iti tad uBaya aMSikIm anitya tAm pratItya saMskAra duHKa tA prajQAyate
# gnas-ngan-len #  dang bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi rgyun-du #  'byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa #  yang 'dod-pa #  ma yin te / / de-gnyi-ga # 'i char gtogs-pa # 'i mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  la brten-nas #  'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid rab tu shes so /
saMskAra anitya tAm saMskAra vipariNAmatAm ca saMDAya uktam mayA yat kiMcid veditam idam atra duHKasya iti ayam aduHKa suKasya suKasya ca veditasya duHKa vacane aBisaMDiH veditavyaH
# ngas 'du-byed #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  dang 'du-byed #  'gyur-ba #  nyid la dgongs nas gang-ci #  tshor yang rung 'di ni 'dir sdug-bsngal #  du gsungs so zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dir sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  dang bde-ba-myong-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyi tshig tu dgongs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
duHKasya tu veditasya duHKa tvena prasidDa tvAt loke na tatra punar aBisaMDiH ucyate iti
# sdug-bsngal #  myong-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  'jig-rten #  na grags-pa # 'i phyir der yang dgongs-pa #  brjod mi dgos so /
yezu ca anityezu saMskArezu jAti Adikam prajQAyate tezAm anitya tvAt duHKam iti aBisaMDiH veditavyaH
# 'du-byed #  mi-rtag-pa #  gang dag la skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r snang-ba #  de-dag #  ni mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  kyi phyir sdug-bsngal #  du dgongs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
anyaTA mArgaH api anitya tvAt duHKam syAt iti
# gzhan-du-na #  ni lam yang mi-rtag-pa # 'i phyir sdug-bsngal #  du 'gyur ro /
SUnyatA lakzaNam nitya Adi lakzaNasya AtmanaH saMskAreByaH arTa antara BUtasya tezu aBAvaH
# stong ba'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi bdag 'du-byed-rnams #  las don gzhan-du #  gyur ba ste / / de-dag #  la med-pa # 'o /
tezAm ca saMskArANAm nityakAlam tad rahita prakRti kalakzaNasya nErAtmyasya BAvaH tad uBayam SUnyatA iti ucyate
# 'du-byed #  de-dag #  ni rtag-tu #  de dang bral-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  gyi mtshan-nyid #  kyi bdag-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin te / / 'di gnyi-ga #  yang stong-pa-nyid #  ces bya'o /
svaBAva SUnyatA parikalpitam svaBAvam upAdAya tasya sva lakzaNena eva aBAvAt
# ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  nye-bar #  bzung-ba #  ste / / rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kho-na # s med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
taTA BAva SUnyatA paratantram svaBAvam upAdAya tasya yena yena prakAreNa parikalpyate tena tena prakAreNa aBAvAt / prakRti SUnyatA parinizpannam svaBAvam upAdAya tasya SUnyatA prakRtika tvAt / anAtma lakzaNam punar tezAm eva saMskArANAm Atma vAdiBiH parikalpitena Atma lakzaNena anAtma lakzaNa tA
# de-bzhin-du #  yod-pa-ma-yin-pa # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  nye-bar #  bzung-ba #  ste / / de ni rnam-pa #  gang-dang-gang #  kun-tu #  brtag-par-bya-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  de-dang-de #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  stong-pa-nyid #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  nye-bar #  bzung-ba #  ste / / de ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rang-bzhin #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / bdag-med-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'du-byed #  de-dag-nyid #  bdag-tu-smra-ba #  rnams kyis kun-tu #  brtags-pa # 'i bdag-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ma-yin-pa #  nyid do /
vinASa Adi lakzaNa anitya tA prasidDA kzaNi kalakzaNA tu na prasidDA sarva saMskArANAm atas sA prasADayitavyA
# 'du-byed-thams-cad #  'jig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  du ni grags la / / skad-cig-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du ni ma grags te / / de'i-phyir #  de bsgrub-pa # r bya'o /
tatra citta cEtasikAnAm kzaNika tvam loke prasidDam atas tena aprasidDam rUpasya kzaNika tvam prasADyate
# de-la #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams la ni skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  'jig-rten #  du grags te / / de'i-phyir #  des ma-grub-pa # 'i gzugs kyi skad-cig-pa #  nyid bsgrub bo /
kaTam iti / citta upAtta tAm upAdAya kzaNikena hi cittena kAyaH upAtta / kena arTena
# ji-ltar #  zhe na / / sems-kyis #  zin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems skad-cig-pa # s lus zin-pa # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  zhe na /
citta eka yoga kzema tAm upAdAya taTA hi kAyaH sa vijQAnakaH eva samudAgacCati vijQAna apakrAntyA ca pUtIBavati
# grub-pa-dang-bde-ba #  gcig pa'i phyir te / / 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  nyid-kyi-lus #  ni yang-dag-par #  'grub kyi / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang bral-ba #  ni rul-ba # r 'gyur ro /
tasmAt cittena eka yogakzema tvAt tat iva asya kzaNika tvam veditavyam
# de-lta-bas-na #  sems dang grub-pa-dang-bde-ba #  gcig pa'i phyir de-bzhin-du #  'di yang skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
kim ca citta ASraya tAm upAdAya cittasya hi vikAreNa kAyasya vikAraH dRSyate suKa duHKa rAga dveza Adi avasTAsu
# sems gyur na de 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang 'dod-chags #  dang zhe-sdang #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  na sems 'gyur-ba # s lus 'gyur-ba # r snang ste /
atas pratikzaNam vikAriNaH cetasaH anuviDAnAt kAyasya kzaNika tvam sidDam
# de'i-phyir #  skad-cig-re-re-la #  'gyur-ba # 'i sems kyi rjes su 'gyur-ba # s lus skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  grub bo /
citta ADipatya saMBUta tAm upAdAya cittasya hi sa indriyaH kAyaH ASrayaH prasidDaH yasya ca yaH utpatya ASrayaH na asO sva vinASam antareNa tasya ASrayIBavan dRzwaH
# sems kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la / / dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i lus ni sems kyi gnas su rab tu grub-pa #  ste / / gang zhig gang-gi #  skye-ba'i-gnas #  yin pa de bdag 'jig-pa #  med-pa # r de'i-gnas #  su 'gyur-ba # r mi snang ste /
tat yaTA agni aMkura AdInAm inDana bIja AdikaH
# dper-na #  me dang myu-gu #  la-sogs-pa # 'i shing dang sa-bon #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin no /
tasmAt pratikzaNam cittasya ASraya BAvAt pratikzaNam eva vinaSyati iti sidDam
# de-bas-na #  skad-cig-re-re-la #  sems kyi gnas-su-gyur-pa # s skad-cig #  re-re #  kho-na #  la rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa #  grub bo /
cittasya ADipatya saMBUta tAm upAdAya sarvam hi ADyAtmika bAhyam rUpam cittasya ADipatyena saMBavati
# sems kyi dbang gis 'byung-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  la nang dang phyi'i gzugs thams-cad #  ni sems kyi dbang gis byung-ba #  ste /
atas kAraNasya kzaNika tvAt kAryasya kzaNika tvam veditavyam ye hetavaH ye pratyayAH rUpasya utpAdAya te api anityAH anityAn Kalu hetu pratyayAn pratItya utpannam rUpam kutas nityam Bavizyati iti sUtra padAnusAreNa
# de-bas-na #  rgyu skad-cig-pa #  yin pa'i phyir / / 'bras-bu #  yang skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya #  ste / / gzugs 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu gang dag yin pa dang rkyen gang dag yin pa de-dag #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  yin na / / rgyu rkyen mi-rtag-pa #  la brten-nas-'byung-ba # 'i gzugs rtag-par #  ga las 'gyur zhes mdo las byung-ba # 'i tshig gi tshul du rig-par-bya # 'o /
citta vaSa varttitAm ca upAdAya praBAva viSizwasya ca cittasya rUpam vaSe vartate tena yaTezwam pariNAmAt
# sems dbang bsgyur-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni mthu khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i sems gzugs la dbang bsgyur-ba #  ste / / de ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  bsgyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atas pratikzaNam anyaTA aDimokze sati anyaTA utpAdAt kzaNika tva sidDiH
# de'i-phyir #  skad-cig-re-re-la #  rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  mos na rnam-pa #  gzhan 'byung-ba # s skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  grub po /
api Kalu ante vikAra upalabDi tAm upAdAya na hi pratikzaNa prakRti vikAri tAm antareNa AkasmikaH rUpasya ante vikAraH yuktaH sa ca upalaByate
# yang mthar 'gyur-ba # r dmigs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / skad-cig-re-re-la #  rang-bzhin-gyis #  'gyur-ba-med-pa # r glo-bur-du #  gzugs kyi tha-ma # r 'gyur-ba # 'i mi rigs na zhes dpe gzhan-las #  'byung ngo /
tasmAt sva asaMtAnika pratikzaNa vikAra aBivRdDi hetuka tvAt antyasya rUpa vikArasya kzaNikam rUpam iti sidDam
# mtha' mi-'gyur-ba # 'i rigs na / / de-yang #  dmigs-pa #  de-bas-na #  mtha' ma'i gzugs kyi 'gyur-ba # 'i rang-gi-rgyud #  kyi skad-cig #  re-re #  'gyur-ba #  'phel-ba # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir gzugs skad-cig-par #  grub bo /
utpannasya ca anapekzya pratyayam sva rasa vinASitAm upAdAya sarvasya utpannasya vinASaH pratyayam anapekzya svarasena eva Bavati
# skyes nas kyang rkyen la mi ltos-pa # r rang-gi-ngang-gis #  rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni skyes-pa #  thams-cad #  ni rkyen la mi ltos-pa # r rang-gi-ngang-nyid-kyis #  'jig-pa # r 'gyur ro /
atas pratyaya antara nirapekzaH avaSyaMBAvI vinASaH utpanna mAtrasya eva BAvasya na Bavati paScAt Bati iti na kiMcid viSezaNam asti
# de'i-phyir #  rkyen-gzhan #  la mi ltos-pa # r gdon-mi-za-bar #  'jig ste / / dngos-po #  skyes-pa #  tsam nyid kyis 'jig-pa #  ma yin la / / phyis 'jig go zhes-bya-ba # r ni bye-brag #  cung-zad #  kyang med do /
tasmAt sarveza vinASina utpanna mAtreNa vinazwam iti sidDam kzaNika tvam
# de-lta-bas-na #  rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa # 'i tshul can thams-cad #  ni skyes-pa #  tsam gyis 'jig-par-'gyur-ba # s skad-cig-pa #  nyid-du #  grub bo /
eka pradeSa ASrayi BAva arTaH upAdAya arTaH BUta deSa nirapekzasya pRTak svatantra vRtti tA sAma arTi aBAvAt
# phyogs-gcig #  la brten-pa # 'i dngos-po # 'i don ni rgyur-byas-pa # 'i don to zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'byung-ba # 'i phyogs la mi ltos-pa # r 'byung-bar-gyur-pa #  logs-shig #  tu rang dbang du 'byung-ba # 'i mthu-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
asti samudAya eka BOtikaH tat yaTA SuzkaH mRd piNXaH
# 'byung-ba #  gcig las gyur ba'i 'dus-pa #  yang yod de / / 'di-lta-ste #  sa rdog skam-po #  lta-bu # 'o /
asti dvi BUtikaH saH eva ArdraH
# 'byung-ba #  gnyis las gyur-pa #  yang yod de / / de nyid gsher-ba # 'o /
asti triBUtikaH saH eva uzNaH
# 'byung-ba #  gsum las gyur-pa #  yang yod de de nyid dro-ba # 'o /
asti sarva BUtikaH saH eva ArdraH uzNaH ca mRd piNXaH gamana avasTAyAm iti
# 'byung-ba #  thams-cad-la # s gyur-pa #  yang yod de / / sa rdog de nyid gsher-ba #  dang dro-ba #  dang 'dril zhing 'gro-ba # 'i tshe'o /
asti samudAya eka upAdAya rUpikaH tat yaTA praBA / dvi upAdAya rUpikaH tat yaTA Sabda ganDaH vAyuH / tri upAdAya rUpikaH tat yaTA DUmaH tasya rUpa ganDa sprazwavya viSeza praBAvita tvAt / sprazwavya viSezaH punar atra laGu tvam veditavyam
# 'dus-pa #  rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  gcig pa yang yod de / / 'di-lta-ste #  'od lta-bu # 'o / / rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  gnyis dang ldan-pa #  yang yod de 'di-lta-ste #  sgra dang dri dang bcas-pa # 'i rlung lta-bu # 'o / / rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  gsum dang ldan-pa #  yang yod de / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / du-ba #  lta-bu # 'o / / de ni gzugs dang dri dang reg-bya # 'i bye-brag #  gis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir te / / reg-bya # 'i bye-brag #  ni 'dir yang pa nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / yang rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  gsum dang ldan-pa #  yang yod de / / dri rnam-pa #  med-pa # 'i nor-bu # 'i snod kyi nang na yod-pa # 'i chu la gzugs dang ro dang reg-bya #  yod-pa # 'o / / rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  bzhi dang ldan-pa #  yang yod de /
catur upAdAya rUpikaH tat yaTA guXa piNXaH / paQca upAdAya rUpikaH tat yaTA saH eva sa SabdaH
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / bu-ram #  gyi ling lta-bu # 'o / / rgyur-byas-pa'i-gzugs #  lnga dang ldan-pa #  yang yod de / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / de nyid sgra dang bcas-pa # 'o /
iti anyatra api yat yatra upalaByate BUtam BOtikam vA tatra tat asti iti veditavyam na anyatra
# de-ltar #  gzhan la yang-'byung-ba # 'am 'byung-ba #  las gyur ba gang na gang dmigs-pa #  de na yod-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / gzhan-du-na #  ni ma yin no /
niHSarIraH paramANuH iti niHsvaBAvaH vyavasTAna mAtram iti arTaH apakarza maryAdA BAvAt
# rdul-phra-rab #  lus med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rang-gi #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa #  ste / / rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  tsam du zad do zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
budDyA paryanta BedataH tu paramANu vyavasTAnam budDyA yAvAn avapApa karza paryantaH Sakyate praBettum tAvatA paramANu vyavasTAnam kriyate
# bshig na mu thug-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / blos mthar rab tu phye-nas #  rdul-phra-rab #  tu rnam-pa # r gzhag ces bya-ba #  ni blos ji tsam du cha-shas #  kyis bshig pa'i mthar rab-tu-dbye-ba # r nus-pa #  de tsam du rdul-phra-rab #  tu rnam-par-'jog-pa # r byed-pa # 'o /
kim punar kAraNam yat evam niHSarIraH api paramANuH vyavasTApyate
# ci'i-phyir #  de-ltar #  lus med kyang rdul-phra-rab #  tu rnam-pa # r 'jog ce na / / ril-po # 'i 'du-shes #  rnam-par-bshig-pa # 'i phyir te /
piNXa saMjQA viBAvana tAm upAdAya avayavaSas hi budDyA BidyamAne rUpe sarvam etat ekam rUpam iti piNXa saMjQA vigacCati yatas pudgalanEH Atmya praveSyasya anukUlyam Bavati iti
# gzugs la blos cha-shas #  kyis bshig na 'di thams-cad #  ni gzugs gcig go zhes ril-po # r 'du-shes #  pa dang bral-ba # r 'gyur te / / 'di-ltar #  gang-zag #  la bdag-med-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # r 'gyur ro /
rUpa dravya aparinizpatti praveSa tAm ca upAdAya evam hi budDyA BidyamAnam rUpam na kiMcid Bavati iti matvA rUpa dravyasya aparinizpattim praviSati yatas vijQapti mAtra avatAreNa Darma nErAtmya praveSayasya anukUlyam Bavati iti
# gzugs la rdzas su yongs-su-grub-pa #  med-pa # r 'jug-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / de-ltar #  blos rab tu phye na gzugs ci-yang-med-pa # r rtogs-nas #  gzugs la rdzas su yongs-su-grub-pa #  med-pa # r 'jug ste / / 'di-ltar #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  tsam du 'jug-pa # s chos-la-bdag-med-pa #  la 'jug-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # r 'gyur ro / / blo'i dbye-ba #  dang rdzas kyi dbye-ba # s rdul-phra-rab #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r shes-pa # r bya ste / / tshig gnyis dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
vipula duHKam asaMliKitam kAma avacaram anupacita kuSala mUlAnAm sarva duHKa tA gati yoni praBAvita tvAt kAmaDAtoH anupacitta kuSala mUla tvena anAvRtam sarva gati gamana tvAt ca yaTAkramam tad vipulam asaMliKitam ca veditavyam saMliKitam tat eva utpanna mokza BAgIyAnAm avaSyam parinirvANa niyamAt
# sdug-bsngal #  shin-tu #  rgyas la ma bsrabs-pa #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  na spyod-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba ma bsags-pa #  rnams kyi ste / / 'dod-pa'i-khams #  ni sdug-bsngal #  nyid thams-cad #  dang 'gro-ba #  dang skye-gnas #  kyis rab-tu-phye-ba #  dang dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba ma bsags-pa # s na / / thogs-pa-med-pa # r 'gro-ba #  thams-cad-du-'gro-ba # 'i phyir te / / go-rims-bzhin-du #  de ni shin-tu #  rgyas la ma bsrabs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / bsrabs-pa #  ni de nyid thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  skye pa rnams kyi ste / / gdon-mi-za-bar #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r nges-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
saMliKita asaMliKitam tat eva kAma avacaram duHKam lOkika vErAgya avaropita kuSala mUlAnAm duHKa duHKa tA Adi samatikrama niyamita tvAt anAtyantika tvAt ca yaTAkramam
# bsrabs-pa # 'ang ma yin la ma bsrabs-pa # 'ang ma-yin-pa #  ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  de nyid 'jig-rten-pa # s 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed-pa #  rnams kyi ste / / sdug-bsngal-gyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid la-sogs-pa #  las yang-dag-par #  shin-tu #  'da' bar nges-par #  byas-pa #  dang gtan-du #  ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir te /
evam maDya asaMliKita AdIni yaTAyogam yojayitavyAni
# go-rims #  bzhin no / / bar-ma #  bsrabs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yang de-bzhin-du #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
mahA saMdeKa prati upasTAnam aneka sattva saMtAnika duHKa apanayana prati upasTAnAt
# bsrabs-pa #  chen-po # s nye-bar-gnas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-can #  du-ma # 'i rgyud-la-yod-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal-bsal-ba # r nye-bar-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kuSala Adi cittasya maraNam iti Atma sneha samprayuktAt cyuti citta apavarga avasTAm aDikRtya veditavyam
# dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems yod-pa #  la 'chi-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-la-chags-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i 'chi-'pho-ba # 'i sems kyi snga-rol #  gyi gnas-skabs #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
manaH mayaH upapAduka tvena citta mAtra hetuka tvAt
# yid-las-byung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rdzus te skye-ba #  nyid de / / sems tsam gyi rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
ganDarvaH ganDena arvaNAt ganDa anusAreNaH papatti deSa gamanAt iti arTaH
# dri-za #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni dris 'gro-ba # 'i phyir te / / dri dang mthun-par #  skye-ba # 'i yul du 'gro-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
param saptAham tizWati antareNa ca cyavate yadi upapatti pratyayAn laBate
# de-ltar #  thogs na zhag-bdun #  gnas te / / de tshun chad kyis 'chi-'pho # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gal-te #  skye-ba'i-rkyen #  rnyed na'o /
aTa na laBate saptAhAt pareNa cyutvA punar antarA aBave eva nivartate
# ci ste ma rnyed na zhag-bdun #  gyi 'og-tu #  shi-'phos-nas #  yang-ba # r do'i srid-pa #  nyid 'grub bo /
evam yAvat sapta kRtvas tatas pareNa ekadA ca vyAvartate yadi tad avasTA syAt yatra upapatti pratyayaH
# de-ltar #  lan bdun gyi bar-du #  byas-na # s ci ste na ldog go zhes-bya-ba #  ni gal-te #  gnas-skabs #  de na gzhan-du #  skye-ba'i-rkyen #  stobs-dang-ldan-pa #  zhig mngon du gyur na ste /
balavantaH AmuKIBUtAH Bavanti caturTa DyAna lABinaH arhat tva aBimAninaH BikzoH tad BUmi kAntarA Bava aBinirvRttO mokza apavAdi kamiTya adRzwi pratilamBAt nAraka antara ABava aBinirvRtti vat
# bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa #  thob-pa # 'i dge slong dgra-bcom-pa # 'o snyam pa'i mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal-can #  sa de pa'i bar mdo'i srid-pa #  mngon-par-grub-pa #  na thar-pa #  la skur ba 'debs-pa #  log-pa # r lta-ba #  rnyed nas sems-can #  dmyal-ba # 'i bar mdo'i srid-pa #  mngon-par-'grub-pa #  bzhin no /
tatrasTaH ca karma upacinoti pUrva aveDa vaSena kuSala Adi cetanA samudAcArAt
# de na gnas-pa #  yang las bsogs so zhes pa ni sngon-gyi-'phen-pa # 'i dbang gis dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems kun-tu-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
saBAgAn= ca sattvAn paSyati yEH saha pUrva tat kuSalam akuSalam vA caritam Bavati tEH saha vartamAnam AtmAnam svapnaH iva saMjAnIte
# skal-ba-mnyam-pa # 'i sems-can #  rnams kyang mthong zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang dag dang lhan-cig-tu #  sngon dge-ba # 'am / / mi-dge-ba #  kun-tu-spyod-pa # r gyur-pa #  de-dag #  dang bdag lhan-cig-tu #  'dug-pa # r rmi-lam #  tsam gyi tshod du shes so /
yatra ca asO= upapannaH tad pUrva kAla Bava AkRtiH nirvartate
# gang-du #  skye-bar-'gyur-ba #  de'i sngon logs kyi srid-pa # 'i byad-gzugs #  grub bo /
tatas UrDvam indriya aBinirvRttiH yaTA pratItyasamutpAdaH iti nAma rUpa Adi AnupUrvyA / yaTA uktam / kalalam praTamam Bavati kalalAt jAyate arbudam / arbudAt jAyate peSI peSItaH jAyate Danam
# de'i-'og-tu #  dbang-po #  rnams mngon-pa # r 'grub ste / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  las ji-skad-du #  'byung-ba #  de-bzhin #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ming-dang-gzugs #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rim-pa # s so / / ji-skad-du #  / / thog-ma #  nyid-du #  nur nur 'gyur / / nur-nur-po #  las mer mer 'gyur / / mer-mer-po #  las nar nar 'gyur / / nar nar po las gor gor 'gyur /
GanAt praSAKAH jAyante keSa loma naKa AdayaH
# gor gor po las rkang-lag #  'gyus / / skra spu sen-mo #  la sogs 'byung /
indriyANi ca rUpINi vyaQjana Adi anupUrvaSas
# dbang-po-gzugs-can #  rnams dang ni / / mtshan rnams mthar-gyis #  'byung-ba # r 'gyur / / zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
samudaya satyam yatas duHKam samudeti / tat punar katamat
# kun 'byung gi bden-pa #  ni gang-la # s sdug-bsngal #  kun-'byung-ba #  ste / / de-yang #  gang zhe na /
kleSAH kleSa aDipateyam ca karma iti sa Asravam iti arTaH
# nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dbang gis 'byung-ba # 'i las te / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
yadi evam kim arTa BagavatA tRzNA eva samudaya nirdeSe nirdizwA / sarvatra ga tvena prADAnyAt
# gal-te #  de lta ma yin na kun-'byung-ba #  zhes bstan-pa #  la ci'i-phyir #  bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis sred-pa #  nyid bstan ce na / / thams-cad-du-'gro-ba # s gtso bor gyur ba'i phyir te /
tRzNA vastu sarva tragA prApta aprApta sarva Atma BAva vizaya vastu vyApanAt
# ji-ltar #  sred-pa #  dngos-po-thams-cad #  du 'gro-ba #  ni thob-pa #  dang ma-thob-pa # 'i yul dang yul-gyi-dngos-po #  thams-cad-la #  khyab-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prApte AtmaBAve tRzNA aprApte pOnarBavikI
# de-la #  lus thob-pa #  ni sred-pa # 'o / / ma-thob-pa #  ni yang-'byung-ba # 'o /
prAptezu vizayezu nandI rAga saha gatA
# thob-pa # 'i yul rnams ni dga'-ba # 'i 'dod-chags #  dang ldan-pa # 'o /
aprAptezu vizayezu tatra tatra aBinandinI veditavyA
# ma-thob-pa # 'i yul rnams ni / / de-dang-de #  la mngon-par-dga'-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
avasTA sarvatragA duHKa duHKa tA Aditya vasTezu saMskArezu anugata tvAt
# gnas-skabs-thams-cad #  du 'gro-ba #  ni / / 'du-byed-rnams #  kyi sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  gnas-skabs #  gsum po dag dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra duHKa duHKa tA avasTezu prAptezu viyoga tRzNA aprAptezu asaMyoga tRzNA
# de-la #  sdug-bsngal #  nyid yi gnas-skabs #  thob-pa #  la ni 'bral-ba # r srid do / / ma-thob-pa #  la ni mi phrad-pa # r srid do /
vipariNAma duHKa tA avasTezu aviyoga tRzNA saMyoga tRzNA ca prApta aprApta BedAt
# 'gyur-ba # 'i sdig bsngal nyid kyi gnas-skabs #  la ni thob-pa #  dang ma-thob-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis mi-'bral-ba # 'i srid-pa #  dang phrad-pa # 'i sred-pa # 'o /
saMskAra duHKa tA avasTezu saMmoha tRzNA kleSa dOzWulya praBAvita tvAt aduHKa vedanA praBAvita tvAt ca
# 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyi gnas-skabs #  la ni gti-mug #  gi sred-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len gyis rab-tu-phye-ba #  dang / / sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa #  bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i tshor-ba # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
AlayavijQAnam viSezeNa saMskAra duHKa tA avasTam tatra ca Atma saMmoha suKena tRzNA pravRttA veditavyA / aDva sarvatragA trizu api aDvasu anugata tvAt
# bye-brag #  tu ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyi gnas-skabs #  te / / de-la #  bdag tu rmongs-pa # 'i sgo nas srid-pa #  'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / dus-thams-cad-du #  'gro-ba #  ni dus-gsum #  po dag ni rjes-su-'gro-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atIte tAvat aDvani apekzA kAreNa anugatAH anAgate aBinandana AkAreNa pratyutpanne aDyavasAna AkAreNa
# 'das-pa'i-dus #  la ni bltas-pa # 'i rnam-pa # s rjes su 'gro'o / / ma-'ongs-pa #  la ni mngon-par-dga'-ba # 'i rnam-pa # s rjes su 'gro'o / / da-ltar-byung-ba #  la ni lhag-par-chags-pa # s rjes su 'gro'o /
DAtu sarvatrikA trEDAtuka sParaNAt kAma rUpA rUpya tRzNABiH
# khams-thams-cad #  du 'gro-ba #  ni 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  dag gi sred-pa #  dag gis khams-gsum #  khyab-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ezaNA sarvatrikA tayA kAma Bava miTyA brahmacarya ezaNAt
# tshor-ba #  thams-cad-du-'gro-ba #  ni des 'dod-pa #  dang sred-pa #  dang log-pa # s tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  tshol-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kAma ezaNayA kAmaDAtoH aparimucyamAnaH tatra eva duHKam nirvartayati
# 'dod-pa # 'i tshol-ba # s ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  las yongs su ma grol ba de nyid-du #  sdug-bsngal #  'grub-pa # r byed do /
taTA BavEzaNayA rUpa ArUpya DAtvoH duKam nirvartayati
# de-bzhin-du #  srid-pa-tshol-ba # s ni gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  su sdug-bsngal #  'grub-pa # r byed do /
miTyA brahmacarya ezaNayA saMsArAt aparimucyamAnaH tatra saMsarati iti
# log-pa # s tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  tshol-ba # s ni 'khor-ba #  las yongs su ma grol bar der 'khor ro /
prakAra sarvatrikA SASvata ucCeda prakAra anugata tvAt Bava viBava tRzNAByAm
# rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  'gro-ba #  ni 'byung-ba #  dang 'jig-pa # 'i sred-pa # s rtag-pa #  dang chad-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dRzweH praQcAkAraH BedaH satkAya dRzwiH anta grAha dRzwi miTyA dRzwiH dRzwi parAmarSaH SIla vrata parAmarSaH iti
# lta-ba #  rnam-pa-lnga # 'i bye-brag #  ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba #  dang lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'o /
apraSAnta lakzaNa tA kleSAnAm sAmAnya lakzaNam veditavyam
# rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyi spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  du rig-par-bya # 'o /
sA punar zaXa AkArA tat yaTA vikzepa apraSAnta tA viparyAsa apraSAnta tA OdDatyA praSAnta tA styAnam idDa apraSAnta tA pramAda apraSAnta tAla jjA praSAnta tA ca
# de-la #  rnam-pa-drug #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  g-yeng bas rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba #  dang phyin-ci-log #  gis rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba #  dang rgod-pa # s rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba #  dang rmugs pas rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba #  dang-ba # g med-pa # s rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba #  dang 'dzem-pa #  med-pa # s rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba # 'o /
kleSa anuSayaH ca aprahINaH Bavati iti tad pakzasya dOzWulyasya asamudGAti tatvAt
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bag-la-nyal #  ma-spangs-pa # r gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i phyogs dang mthun-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  legs-par #  ma bcom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kleSa sTAnIyaH ca DarmaH ABAsa gataH Bavati raMjanIya AdiH
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-gnas #  kyi chos snang-bar-gyur-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni chags-par-'gyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tatra ca ayaH niSoma nakkAraH pratyavasTitaH Bavati iti tasmin vizaye SuBa nimitta Adi udgrAhakaH rAga Adi utpatti anukUlaH / avidyA dRzwi vicikitsA UrDva BUmi AlaMbanA api santi na punar AsAm sA BUmiH sAkzAt AlaMbanam veditavyam yaTA sva BUmiH tad parikalpa muKa pravRtta tvAt tu tad AlaMbana vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# de-la #  yang tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  nye-bar-gnas-pa #  yin zhes-bya-ba #  ni yul de-la #  sdug-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  'dzin-pa #  ste / / 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  'byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'o / / ma-rig-pa #  dang lta-ba #  dang the-tshom #  sa-gong-ma-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  yang yod mod kyi / / de-dag #  ni ji-ltar #  rang-gi #  sa pa la dmigs-pa #  bzhin-du # s de mngon-sum-du #  dmigs-pa #  ni ma-yin-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / de-la #  kun-tu #  brtags-pa # 'i sgo nas zhugs-pa # 'i phyir / / de-la #  dmigs-pa # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra avidyA UrDvaBUmi AlaMbanA yA dRzwi saMprayuktA
# de-la #  ma-rig-pa # s gong-ma #  pa la dmigs-pa #  ni gang lta-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'o /
dRzwiH satkAya dRzwi sTApayitvA na hi para BUmikAn saMskArAn aham iti aBiniviSamAnaH dRzwaH iti
# lta-ba #  ni 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  ma gtogs te / / gzhan gyi sa pa'i 'du-byed #  la nga'o snyam-du #  mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni ma mthong ngo /
UrDva BUmikasya tu kleSasya aDas BUmiH AlaMbanam na Bavati tatas vIta rAga tvAt
# sa-gong-ma # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  ni sa-'og-ma #  dmigs-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-la # s 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i phyir ro /
niroDa mArga alaMkanasya tO na alaMkabanam loka uttareNa jQAnena tad pRzWa labDena vA pratyAtma vedanIya tvAt
# 'gog-pa #  dang lam la dmigs-pa #  ni de gnyis la dmigs-pa #  ma yin te / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes dang de'i-rjes-la #  thob-pa #  so-so #  rang-rang-gis #  rig-par-bya-ba #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
tat parikalpitam tu asya alaMbanam iti vaktavye tad parikalpaH tu asya alaMbanam iti vacanam tat avyatirekAt parikalpitasya asya
# de'i dmigs-pa #  ni des yongs su rtogs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i dmigs-pa #  ni des yongs su brtags-pa # 'o zhes brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de'i dmigs-pa #  ni des yongs su rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig de-la # s yongs su brtags-pa #  gud-na #  med do /
rAgaH pratiDena na saMprayujyate ekAnta virudDayoH ekatra vRtti ayogAt
# 'dod-chags #  ni khong khro dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni shin-tu #  mi-mthun-pa #  gnyis gcig-tu #  'byung-ba #  mi-rigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vicikitsayA api na saMprayujyate na hi vicikitsO= avasTita budDiH aDyavasyati iti
# the-tshom #  dang yang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ni / / the-tshom #  du gyur na blo gnas-pa #  med-pa # s chags-par-'gyur-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
SizwEH tu asya mAna AdiBiH avirudDa tvAt saMprayogaH veditavyaH
# lhag-ma #  ni de dang zhes-bya-ba #  ni nga-rgyal #  la-sogs-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
pratiGaH mAnena dRzwyA ca na saMprayujyate na hi yaH yatra vastuni pratihataH tena saH unnatim gacCati tat vA saMtIrayitum Saknoti iti evam anyat api yojayitavyam
# khong-khro-ba #  yang nga-rgyal #  dang lta-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni su zhig dngos-po #  gang-la #  zhe-'gras-pa # r gyur-pa #  des de khengs-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / der yang rtog-pa # r mi nus so / / de-bzhin-du #  gzhan la yang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
kroDa AdayaH anyonyam na saMprayujyante iti virudDAH virudDEH na saMprayujyante / tat yaTA rAga aMSikAH pratiGAMsikEH
# khong-khro-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  phan tshun mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mi-mthun-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin te / / dper-na #  'dod-chags #  kyi char gtogs-pa #  rnams zhe-sdang #  gi char gtogs-pa #  dag dang ma-yin-pa #  bzhin no /
avirudDAH tu kleSa vat eva saMprayujyante iti veditavyam
# mi-mthun-pa-med-pa #  dag ni nyon-mongs-pa #  bzhin-du #  mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
AhrIkyAna patra Apyam sarvatra akuSale saMprayujyate sva para nirapekzatAm antareNa akuSala sat samudAcArA saMBavAt
# ngo-tsha-med-pa #  dang khrel-med-pa #  ni mi-dge-ba #  thams-cad #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan #  la mi-lta-ba #  med-pa # r kun-tu-'byung-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam styAna AdayaH sarvatra klizwe yojayitavyAH akarmaNi Adikam antareNa klizwatvA saMBavAt iti
# de-bzhin-du #  rmugs pa la-sogs-pa #  yang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  thams-cad #  dang sbyar-ba # r bya ste / / las-su-mi-rung-ba #  nyid la-sogs-pa #  med-pa # r nyon-mongs-pa-can #  mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yadi ena prakAreNa yasmin vastuni saMprayojayati tad nirdeSena saMyojana nirdeSaH veditavyaH / kim saMyojayati
# gang zhig rnam-pa #  gang-gi #  dngos-po #  gang-la #  kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  de bstan-pa # s kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  ci zhe na /
anunaya saMyojanam tAvat trEDAtuka rAga svaBAvam saMyojayati
# rjes-su-chags-pa # 'i kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  de kun-tu-sbyor-bar #  byed do /
kena prakAreNa saMyojayati / tat vataH trEDAtukAn udvege satya kuSala samudAcarataH kuSalA samudAcarataH ca / kasmin saMyojayati
# rnam-pa #  gang-gis #  kun-tu #  sbyor zhe na / / de dang ldan-pa #  khams-gsum-pa #  la yid mi-'byung-ba #  ni mi-dge-ba #  kun-tu #  spyod cing dge-ba #  mi-spyod-pa # s so / / gang kun-tu #  sbyor zhe na /
AyatyAm duHKa aBinirvRttO
# phyi-ma-la #  sdug-bsngal #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r ro /
evam pratiGa saMyojana Adizu yojayitavyaH
# de-bzhin-du #  khong khro'i kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  la yang sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
avidyA saMyojanena saMprayuktaH duHKa DarmAn samudaya DarmAn na aDyavasyati Pala hetu BUtAn sa AsravAn saMskArAH tad AdIn avApari jQAnAt / dRzwi saMyojanena saMprayuktaH miTyAni saraNam paryezate iti Aha mokzaH mama mokzaH muktaH ca nityaH BavizyAsi ucCetsyAmi vA iti na ca bOdDAnAm asti mokzaH iti
# mi rig-pa # 'i kun-tu-spyod-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi chos-rnams #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i chos-rnams #  la lhag-pa # r chags te 'bras-bu #  dang rgyur-gyur-pa #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  dang de'i nyes-dmigs #  yongs su mi-shes-pa # 'i phyir ro / / lta-ba # 'i kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  dang ldan-pa #  ni log-pa # s nges-par-'byung-ba #  kun-tu #  tshol te bdag grol bar 'gyur ro / / bdag grol lo / / grol nas kyang rtag-par #  'gyur ro snyam pa dang chad-pa # r 'gyur te / / sangs-rgyas #  pa la thar-pa #  med do snyam pa'o /
parAmarSa saMyojanena saMprayuktaH miTyA niHsaraNa upAyam kalpayati aBiniviSate Arya azwAFgam mArgam hitvA satkAyadRzwayA tad pUrvakeNa ca SIla vratena SudDi pratyayanAt
# mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  dang ldan-pa #  ni log-pa # s nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i thabs la rtog ste / / 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yan-lag-brgyad-pa #  por nas 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang de sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  kyis lhag-pa # r yid-ches-pa # 'i phyir ro /
rAga Adi banDana eva pariNAma duHKa tA Adi banDana vacanam suKa Adi vedanA anuSayita tvAt
# 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'ching-ba # s 'gyur-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  nyid la-sogs-pa #  la 'ching-ba # r bstan-pa #  ni 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  ni bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  la phra-rgyas-su-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
bAhyena hi banDanena badDaH dvayam na laBate gantum ca na laBate AsInaH api yaTezwam aBipreta cezwAyAm kAmakAram na laBate
# phyi-rol #  gyi 'ching-ba # s bcings-pa #  ni gnyis mi 'thob ste / / 'gro-ba #  mi-thob-pa #  dang 'dug kyang ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  dang bsam-pa #  dang spyod-pa #  dang 'dod-pa-bzhin-du #  byed-pa #  mi-thob-pa # 'o /
tat sADarmyeNa ADyAtmikam rAga Adi banDanam veditavyam
# nang gi 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'ching-ba #  yang de-dang-'dra-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
kAma ezaNAyAH aviratasya kAma rAga pratiGa anuSayO= anuSayA te tad muKena tayoH puzwi gamanAt
# 'dod-pa #  'tshol-ba #  ma-spangs-pa # 'i 'dod-pa-la-'dod-chags #  dang khong-khro-ba # 'i bag-la-nyal #  phra rgyas su 'gyur te / / de'i sgo nas de gnyis rgyas-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
miTyA mokzam mokza upAyam ca santIrayanti iti yaTAkramam tisRBiH dRzwiBiH dvAByAm ca parAmarSAByAm yaTA saMyojanezu uktam iti
# log-pa # r thar-pa #  dang thar-pa # 'i thabs la rtog-pa # r byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-tu-sbyor-ba # 'i nang-du #  lta-ba #  gsum dang mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  gnyis ji-skad-du #  bshad-pa #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
zaX rAga AdIn kleSAn sTApayitvA tad anyaH klizwaH cEtasikaH saMskAra skanDaH kroDa AdikaH veditavyaH
# gang 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams ma-gtogs-par #  de-las-gzhan-pa #  sems-las-byung-ba # 'i 'du-byed-kyi-phung-po #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  no zhes-bya-ba #  ni khro-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
kuSala pakza antarAyAya yoginAm punar punar udvegena cittam paryavanahyanti iti paryavasTAnAni / kuSala pakzaH punar yaTAkAlam SamaTa pragraha upekzA nimitta BAvanA tad saMniSrayaH ca brahmacarya Adi SudDi saMgRhItam SIlam
# rnal-'byor-pa #  rnams kyi dge-ba'i-phyogs #  kyi bar-chad-bya-ba # 'i phyir-yang #  dang yang shas-cher #  sems la kun nas 'khril bar byed-pa # s kun-nas-dkris-pa #  dag go / / dge-ba'i-phyogs #  ni zhi-gnas #  dang rab-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang btang-snyoms #  kyi rgyu mtshan bsgom-pa #  ste / / dus ji-lta-ba #  bzhin no / / de-dag #  gi gzhi ni tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dag-pa # s bsdus-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  so /
tatra SamaTa kAle styAnam idDam antarAyam karoti ADyAtmam saMkzepa AvAhanAt / pragraha kAle OdDatya kOkRtyam bahirDA vikzepa AvAhanAt
# de-la #  zhi-gnas-kyi-dus #  ni rmugs pa dang gnyid par chad byed de / / nang-du #  zhum-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rab-tu-'dzin-pa'i-dus #  na ni rgod-pa #  dang 'gyod-pa #  ste / / phyi-rol-du #  rnam-pa # r g-yeng bar byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upekzA kAle IrzyA mAtsaryam tad vataH para Atma saMpattyam arSa graha muKena muhur muhur citta kaMpanAt
# btang-snyoms-kyi-dus #  na ni / / phrag-dog-dang-ser-sna #  ste / / de dang ldan na gzhan dang bdag-gi #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  la mi-bzod-pa #  dang kun-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i sgo nas yang-dang-yang #  sems g-yo-ba # 'i phyir ro /
SIla viSudDi kAle AhvIkyAna patra Apyam tat uBayavataH sarvaTA Apatti sTAnezu alajjanAt iti
# tshul-khrims #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dus na ni / / ngo-tsha-med-pa #  dang khrel-med-pa #  ste / / de-gnyi-ga #  dang ldan na rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  ltung-ba # 'i gnas kyis mi 'dzem-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMkleSa vyavadAna guNa vEguNya arTena yaTAkramam oGa yoga vyavasTAnam veditavyam / ASrita ASraya saMbanDa yogena iti dRzwayA oGaH ASritaH avidya oGaH ASrayaH saMmohe sati mokza tad upAya viparItam saMtIraNAt
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir chu-bo #  dang sbyor-ba #  go-rims-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / gnas-pa #  dang gnas 'brel-ba # 'i tshul-gyis #  so zhes-bya-ba #  la / / lta-ba # 'i chu-bo #  ni gnas-pa # 'o / / ma-rig-pa # 'i chu-bo #  ni gnas te / / rmongs-pa # r gyur na thar-pa #  dang de'i thabs la log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dRzwi SIla vrata upAdAnAByAm tIrTyAH anyonyam vivadanti tatra aneka matyAt
# lta-ba #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  kyi nye-bar-len-pa #  gnyis kyis mu-stegs-can #  rnams nang rtsod de / / de-la #  blo du-ma # r gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Atma vAda upAdAnena tu anyonyam na vivadanti AtmanaH asti tvam prati sarvezAm mata sAmyAt / Atma vAda upAdAnena tIrTya ihaDArmikEH sArdDam vivadanti ezAm nErAtmya vAdi tvAt
# bdag-tu-smra-ba # 'i nye-bar-len-pa # s ni nang mi rtsod de; thams-cad #  kyang bdag-yod-pa #  nyid-du #  blo mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro / / chos 'di pa rnams dang ni rtsod de / / bdag-med-pa # r smra-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aBiDi AdayaH kAya granTAH iti na rUpa kAyasya ete granTAH veditavyAH kiMtarhi samAhita citta svaBAvasya kAyasya parigranTa arTena granTAH
# brnab-sems #  la-sogs-pa #  lus kyi mdud-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni de-dag #  gzugs-kyi-lus #  kyi mdud-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sems kyi rang-bzhin #  gyi lus kyi bar-du #  bcod pas mdud-pa #  dag go /
pRTak dRzwi saMniSrayeNa idam eva satyam moGam anyat iti aBiniviSya jQeyam saMtIrayatAm ayoniSaH jQeya saMtIraNa hetoH cittam vikzipyate / kutas vikzipyate
# so-so # 'i lta-ba #  la brten-nas #  'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni don-med-pa # 'o zhes mngon-pa # r zhen nas shes-bya #  la kun-tu-rtog-pa # s tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # r shes-bya #  la log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i rgyus sems rnam-pa # r g-yeng bar byed do / / gang-la # s rnam-pa # r g-yeng bar byed ce na /
samAhita cittasya yaTA BUta jQAna darSanataH
# mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sems yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  shes-pa #  mthong-ba #  la sogs /
kuSala pakzasya asaMsaMKyAnAya cittam nivRNvanti iti nivaraNAni kuSala pravRtteH antarAyam kurvanti iti arTaH
# dge-ba'i-phyogs #  mi rtogs-par-'gyur-ba # r sems la sgrib-par-byed-pa # s sgrib-pa #  rnams te / / dge-ba-la-'jug-pa # 'i bar-chad #  byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
kAmacCandam pravrajyA aBirateH antarAyam karoti vizaya upaBoga aBilAza muKena tatra tatra aBiramaNAt
# de-la #  'dod-pa-la-'dun-pa #  ni rab-tu-'byung-ba #  la mngon-par-dga'-ba # 'i bar-chad #  byed de / / yul la nye-bar-spyod-pa # r 'dod-pa # 'i sgo nas /
vyApAdaH ca udanAyAm samyak pratipatteH sabrahmacAriBiH SikzA sTAnezu codyamAnasya vyApanna citta tayA asamyak SEkzaNAt
# de-la #  mngon-par-mi-dga'-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gnod-sems #  ni bskul-ba # 'i dus na ste / / tshangs-pa #  mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa #  rnams kyis yang-dag-par-bsgrub-pa # 'i bslab-pa # 'i gnas la bskul nas gnod-sems #  kyi sems-kyis #  yang-dag-par #  mi-slob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
styAnam idDam udDatya kOkRtyam ca SamaTa pragrahayoH pUrvavat saMkzepa vikzepa AvAhana AdiBiH
# rmugs pa dang gnyid dang rgod-pa #  dang 'gyod-pa #  ni zhi-gnas #  dang rab-tu-'dzin-pa #  gnyis snga-ma-bzhin-du #  zhum-pa #  dang rnam-pa # r g-yeng bar byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vicikitsA upekzAyAm niScaya mantareNa aByupekzitum aSakya tvAt
# the-tshom #  ni btang-snyoms-kyi-dus #  na ste / / gtan la phebs pa med-pa # r btang-snyoms #  su byed mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratipakza lAMgaH lEduHBeda arTena Kila vyavasTAnam veditavyam janma antara aByAsena KilIBUta tvAt
# gnyen-po #  thong gshol gyis rlog-pa # r dka'-ba # 'i phyir tha bar rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / tshe-rabs-gzhan #  na goms-par-byas-pa # s spyod-pa # s tha bar gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dOHSIlya aSuci saMBAvanA nimitta tvAt malAH
# 'chal pa'i tshul-khrims #  mi gtsang bar yid-ches-pa # 'i rgyu yin-pas #  dri-ma #  rnams so /
punar punar saMsAre jAti jarA maraNa yogena niDnanti iti niGAH
# yang-dang-yang #  'khor-ba # r skye-ba #  dang 'chi-ba # 'i tshul-gyis #  gnod-par-byed-pa # s sdig-pa #  rnams so /
Bava Bogezu ratnezu ca tRzNA vicikatsA muKena anupraviSya todanAt SalyAH
# srid-pa #  dang srid-pa # 'i yo-byad #  rnams dang dkon-mchog #  rnams la sred-pa #  dang the-tshom #  gyi sgo nas zhugs-pa # s gnod-pa # 'i phyir zug rdu rnams so /
bahu upakaraNa parigraheNa sa kiMcanam kRtvA Baya AdiBiH yojanAt kiMcanAH
# yo-byad #  mang-po #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa # s lci-yang #  dang bcas-pa # r byas-na # s 'jig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang sbyor-ba # 'i phyir lci-yang #  rnams so /
prANa atipAta Adi akuSala caryA vAhanAt duScaritAni
# srog-gcod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-dge-ba #  spyod-pa #  'dres-pa # s nyes-par-spyod-pa #  rnams so /
loBa dveza mohAnAm eva akuSala mUla tvena vyavasTAnam eBiH muKEH sattvAnAm duScarita caraNAt
# chags-pa #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang gti-mug #  nyid mi-dge-ba # 'i rtsa bar rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / de-dag #  gi sgo nas sems-can #  rnams nyes-par-spyad-pa #  spyod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra Amiza kiMcid kahetoH Boga arTinaH loBena duScaritam caranti
# de-la #  zang-zing #  cung-zad #  tsam gyi rgyus sems-can #  longs-spyod #  don-du-gnyer-ba #  rnams chags-pa # s nyes-par-spyad-pa #  spyod do /
apakAra nimitta parikalpa hetoH para aparADa AmarziNaH dvezeNa miTyA Darma aBiniveSa hetoH viparIta darSinaH mohena duScaritam caranti yAjQikA AdayaH iti
# gnod-par-byas-pa # 'i rgyu la yongs-su-rtog-pa # 'i rgyus gzhan-gyi-nyes-pa #  mi-bzod-pa #  rnams zhe-sdang #  gis nyes-par-spyad-pa #  spyod do / / chos log-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rgyus phyin-ci-log #  tu lta-ba #  la mchod-sbyin #  la-sogs-pa #  dag gti-mug #  gis nyes-par-spyad-pa #  spyod do /
citta visAram srutam kurvanti iti AsravAH
# sems rnam-pa # r 'phro bar zag-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir zag-pa #  rnams so /
kAyika cEtasika viGAta karatvAt viGAtAH
# lus dang sems la phongs-par-byed-pa # s phongs-pa #  rnams so /
ayoniSA unmittam anuvyaQjanam ca grAhayitvA kAyam cittam ca paridahanti iti paridAhAH
# tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  dang mngon-rtags #  'dzin du bcug-nas #  lus dang sems la yongs-su-gdung-ba # r byed-pa # s yongs-su-gdung-ba #  rnams so /
rUpa Adike vastuni rati aDyavasAnam kArayitvA tad vipariNAme Soka AdiBiH sattvAn AyAsanti iti pAyAsAH
# gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po #  la dga'-ba # 'am lhag-par-chags-pa # r byed du bcug-nas #  de rnam-pa # r gyur na mya-ngan #  la-sogs-pa # s sems-can #  rnams nyon-mongs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir 'khrug ba rnams so /
raNayanti Sastra AdAna AdiBiH iti raNAH
# mtshon-cha #  len-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s 'thab-pa # r byed-pa # s 'thab-pa #  rnams so /
aDarma rAga Adi mahAparidAha kara tvAt jvarAH iva jvarAH veditavyAH
# chos-ma-yin-pa #  la 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  ni yongs-su-gdung-ba #  chen-po #  byed-pa # s rims-nad #  dang 'dra-ba # s na rims-nad #  rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra aDarma rAgaH yaH akuSalezu karma paTeNa anurAgaH
# de-la #  chos-ma-yin-pa #  la 'dod-chags #  ni gang mi-dge-ba'i-las #  kyi lam rnams la rjes-su-chags-pa # 'o /
vizama loBaH anyAyena aDarmeNa vizaya paryazwiH
# mi-mthun-pas-chags-pa #  ni mi-rigs-pa # 'i chos-ma-yin-pas #  yul kun-tu #  'tshol-ba # 'o /
miTyADarmaH durAKyAtaH Darma vinayaH veditavyaH
# chos log-pa #  ni nyes-par-bshad-pa # 'i chos-'dul-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
jAtimUlaka saMskAra taru vanam saMjAnayanti iti vanasAH
# skye-ba # 'i rtsa ba 'du-byed #  kyi shing gi nags-tshal #  la chags-par-byed-pa # s nags-sbyor #  rnams so /
kAya sa apekzAt tayA kuSala prayoga vibanDanAt vibanDAH
# lus la lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang bcas-pa # s dge-ba-la-sbyor-ba # 'i gegs-byed-pa # s gegs rnams so /
kAya sApekzata AdIni punar paQca cetaH vinibanDAn aDikRtya
# lus la lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ni sems kyi-ge # gs lnga'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o /
rAgaH vizaye dRzwO ca vipratipannaH iti BAvanA prahAtavyaH darSana prahAtavyaH ca yaTAkramam
# 'dod-chags #  ni yul dang lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsgoms-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  dang mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  dang go-rims #  bzhin te /
SuBa tA mAtra alaMbana tvAt rAgasya yaH api sattvezu rAgaH saH api vizaya muKena eva vipratipannaH veditavyaH
# 'dod-chags #  ni sdug-pa #  tsam du dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang yang sems-can #  la 'dod-chags #  pa de ni yul gyi sgo nyid nas log-pa # r rtog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
evam pratikUla mAtra alaMkbana tvAt pratiGasya sattvezu api pravartamAnaH vizaya muKena eva vipratipannaH veditavyaH
# de-bzhin-du #  khong-khro-ba #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu #  tsam du dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sems-can #  rnams la 'byung-ba #  ni yul gyi sgo nyid nas log-pa # r rtog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
mAnaH sattvezu dRzwO ca vipratipannaH hInAt asmi SreyAn iti evamAdi AkAra pravRtta tvAt satvezu vipratipannaH veditavyaH
# nga-rgyal #  ni sems-can #  rnams dang lta-ba #  log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni chung du-ba # s bdag che'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir sems-can #  rnams la log-pa # r rtog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
satkAya anta grAha miTyA dRzwayaH jQeye vipratipannAH samAropa apavAda muKena yaTAyogam
# 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  dang mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  dang log-pa # r lta-ba #  ni shes-bya #  la log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sgro-'dogs-pa #  dang skur ba'i sgo nas ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
SIla vrata parAmarSa AdiH dRzwO vipratipannaH dRzwi dozeNa eva SIla vratasya SudDitaH parAmarSanAt
# tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  ni lta-ba #  la log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni lta-ba # 'i nyes-pa #  nyid kyis tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  la lhag-pa # r mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vicikitsA pratipakze vipratipannA satyezu budDiH dIrGa ApAdanAt
# the-tshom #  ni gnyen-po #  la log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni bden-pa #  rnams la blo rnam-pa-gnyis #  su 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
te duHKa samudayayoH daSa api kleSAH nidAnam Bavanti
# nyon-mongs-pa #  bcu char yang sdug-bsngal #  dang kun-'byung-ba # 'i rgyu yin la /
tO ca tezAm pada sTAnam
# de gnyis kyang de-dag #  gi gzhi'i-gnas #  yin no /
atas te tad nidAna pada sTAnataH vipratipannAH iti ucyante
# de'i-phyir #  de'i rgyu dang gzhi'i-gnas #  kyis log-pa # r rtog-pa #  rnams zhes-bya'o #  /
niroDe mArge ca uttrAsa saMjananataH vipratipannAH kleSa vaSAt saMsAre aBiratasya vyavadAnataH prapAta saMjQA trAsAt / viparIta kalpanataH ca niroDe mArge ca vipratipannAH drazwavyAH tIrTyEH anyaTA parikalpya tatra vipratipatteH
# 'gog-pa #  dang lam la yang skrag-pa #  skyes-pa # s log-par-zhugs-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dbang gis 'khor-ba #  la mngon bar dga'-ba #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  la g-yeng bar 'du-shes #  nas skrag-pa #  dang phyin-ci-log #  tu rtog-pa # s 'gog-pa #  dang lam la log-pa # r rtog-pa # r blta-bar-bya # 'o / / mu-stegs-can #  rnams kyis ni rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  kun du brtags-nas #  de-la #  log-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kAma avacaraH rAgaH paQca vijQAna kAyikaH suKena saMprayujyate / manaH vijQAna kAyikaH sOmanasyena
# 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga dang ldan-pa #  ni bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no / / yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs dang ldan-pa #  ni yid-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no /
sarva upekzayA aprabanDa uparati kAle
# 'dod-chags #  thams-cad #  ni rgyun-chad-pa # 'i dus na btang-snyoms #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no /
duHKa dOrmanasyAByAm tu na saMprayujyate harza AkAra pravRtta tvAt
# sdug-bsngal #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  gnyis dang mi mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin te / / dga'-ba # 'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pratiGaH duHKena saMprayujyate paQca vijQAna kAyikaH zazWaH dOrmanasyena sarvaH upekzayA pUrvavat suKa sOmanasyAByAm na saMprayujyate dEnya AkAra pravRtta tvAt
# rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga dang ldan-pa # 'i khong-khro-ba #  ni sdug-bsngal #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no / / drug-pa #  yid-kyi-sa #  pa ni yid-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no / / thams-cad #  ni btang-snyoms #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan te snga-ma-bzhin #  no / / bde-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni ma yin te / / dman-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
mAnaH kAma DatO suKena na saMprayujyate paQca vijQAna kAyika aBAvAt / praTama dvitIyayoH tarhi DyAnayoH kaTam suKena saMprayujyate
# nga-rgyal #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  na bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin te / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs lnga dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bsam-gtan-dang-po #  dang gnyis-pa # r bde-ba #  dang ji-ltar #  ldan zhe na /
manaH BUmikena suKena
# yid-kyi-sa #  pa'i bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no /
kaTam tatra manaH BUmikam suKam
# de ni yid-kyi-sa #  pa'i bde-ba #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
yat tat ucyate prIti suKam iti yaTA uktam prItiH katamA
# dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  zhes gang 'byung-ba #  ste / / ji-skad-du #  dga'-ba #  gang zhe na /
yA parivRtta ASrayasya parivRtti vijQAna ASritA citta tuzwiH citta Odvilyam citta harzaH citta kalpa tA sAtam veditam vedanA gatam / suKam katamat / yat parivRtta ASrayasya Alaya vijQAna ASritaH ASraya anugrahataH ASraya hlAdaH sAtam veditam vedanA gatam iti / tat etat uktam Bavati
# gang gnas-gyur-pa # 'i 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la brten-pa # 'i sems tshim pa dang sems shin-tu #  dga'-ba #  dang sems-rangs-pa #  dang sems-dga'-ba #  dang bde-ba-myong-ba #  ste / / tshor-ba # r gtogs-pa # 'o / / bde-ba #  gang zhe na gang gnas-gyur-pa # 'i kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la brten-pa # 'i gnas la phan-pa #  dang gnas kyi tshim pa dang bde-ba-myong-ba #  ste / / tshor-ba # r gtogs-pa # 'o zhes bshad-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / de ni 'di-skad-du #  bstan to / / 'jug-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  la brten-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la brten-pa #  yin te / / gzhan la mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
suKA vedanA praTama dvitIyayoH DyAnayoH utpadyamAnA yena citta cEta kalApena saMprayujyate tam ca harza AkAreNa prINayati ASrayam cAlaya vijQAna svaBAvam prasrabDi suKena hlAdayati
# bde-ba'i-tshor-ba #  bsam-gtan-dang-po #  dang gnyis-pa #  la 'byung-ba #  na / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i tshogs gang yang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  de dga'-ba # 'i rnam-pa # s tshim-par-byed-pa #  dang gnas kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  shin-tu #  sbyongs pa'i bde-ba # s tshim-par-byed-pa #  ste /
atas tad uBaya kRtya kara tvAt uBayaTA eva asyAH vyavasTAnam veditavyam prItiH suKam ca iti / tasmAt tayA saMprayujyamAnaH mAnaH suKena sOmanasyena ca saMprayujyate iti ucyate
# de-lta-bas-na #  de gnyis-ka # 'i bya-ba-byed-pa # 'i phyir 'di ni dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  rnam-pa #  gnyi-ga # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o zhes bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de-bas-na #  de dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i nga-rgyal #  ni bde-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
miTyAdRzwiH kAmaDAtO dOrmanasyena sOmanasyena ca saMprayujyate sukRta duzkRta kAriNAm tad vEPalya darSanena aDRti harza utpAdAt
# log-pa # r lta-ba #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  na yid-bde-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  zhes bya ste / / legs-par-bya-ba #  dang nyes-par-bya-ba #  byed-pa #  rnams kyi de'i 'bras-bu-med-pa # r mthong-nas #  mi mos-pa #  dang dga'-ba #  skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
suKa duHKAByAm na saMprayujyate manaH BUmika tvAt sarvasyAH dRzweH
# bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  ba dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni ma yin te / / lta-ba #  thams-cad #  ni yid-kyi-sa #  pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
vicikitsA kAmaDAtO sOmanasyena na saMprayujyate aniScita cittasya nErvRttyam antareNa sOmanasya aBAvAt
# the-tshom #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  na yid-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma yin te / / sems gtan la phab pa med-pa #  ni mos-pa-med-pa # s yid-bde-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
rUpaDAtO vicikitsA uttara DyAyinAm api prIti suKam samADi vala ADAnena anuvartate eva iti tatra suKa sOmanasyAByAm api saMprayujyate
# gzugs-kyi-khams #  na ni the-tshom #  gyi shas-che-ba # 'i bsam-gtan-pa #  rnams kyi dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi stobs bskyed-pa # 'i rjes-su-'gro-ba #  nyid de / / de na bde-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang yang mtshungs-pa # r ldan no /
AveNikAyAH api avidyAyAH ezaH eva nayaH drazwavyaH suKa sOmanasyAByAm saMprayoga asaMyogam AraBya
# ma-rig-pa #  ma-'dres-pa #  yang bde-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  las brtsams te tshul 'di-'dra-ba # r blta-bar-bya # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  btang-snyoms #  dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan zhe na /
sarva kleSAH upekzayA saMprayujyante OdAsInyam Agamya asta gamana tAm upAdAya iti kleSa pravanDasya mandatara tamatA gamanena uparata vegasya uparamaNa Adante avaSyam OdAsInya muKena upekzAyAH saMprayogaH veditavyaH
# tha-mal-pa # r 'dug-pa #  la brten-nas #  nub-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rgyun je chung je chung du 'gro-ba # s rgyun-chad-pa # 'i shugs kyis rgyun-chad-pa # 'i phyir tha-ma # r gdon-mi-za-bar #  tha-mal-pa # r 'jug-pa'i-sgo #  nas btang-snyoms #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
rUpaDAtO caturvijQAna kAyikaH tatra GrANa jihvA vijQAna aBAvAt
# gzugs-kyi-khams #  na ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs bzhi dang mtshungs-pa # r ldan te / / de na sna dang lce'i-rnam-par-shes-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
mAna AdayaH manaH vijQAna kAyikAH eva paritulana tA muKa pravRtti tvAt
# nga-rgyal #  la-sogs-pa #  ni yid kyi rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs dang ldan-pa #  nyid de / / yongs su 'jal-ba # 'i sgo nas 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
mAnasya eka deSa pravRtti tvam kenacid eva aMSena unnati gamanAt
# nga-rgyal #  ni phyogs-gcig #  la 'jug-pa #  nyid de / / gang-yang-rung-ba # 'i yan-lag #  gis khengs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /

sahajA satkAya dRzwiH kA BAvanA prahAtavyA

yAma DizWAya utpanna darSana mArgasya api Arya SrAvakasya asmin samudAcarati
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  skyes su zin yang gang-la #  brten-nas #  'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  la nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  kun-tu-'byung-ba # 'o /
yaTA uktam na aham Ayuzmanda AsakemAn paQca upAdAna skanDAn AtmataH AtmIyataH vA samanupaSyAmi api tu asti me ezu paQca sUpa AdAna skanDezu asmi iti mAnaH asmi iti CandaH asmi iti anuSayaH aprahINaH aparijQAtaH aniroDitaH avAntIkRtaH iti / yaTA klizwasya DAtrI cEla vyoza AdiBiH su DOtasya nirmalasya api sataH tad aDivAsana akRtam ganDa mAtram anuvartate yat tat suganDa dravya pariBAvanayA BUyas api apanetavyam Bavati evam eva darSana mArgeNa prahINa parikalpita satkAya dRzwi malasya api Arya SrAvakasya pUrva aBiniveSa aByAsa kRtam aparicCinna vastukam Atma darSanam anuvartate yat tat punar mArga BAvanayA prahAtavyam Bavati iti
# ji-skad-du #  tshe-dang-ldan-pa #  bran can kho bos ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po 'di dag la bdag gam bdag-gi # r rjes su mi mthong mod kyi / / 'on-kyang #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po 'di dag la nga'o-snyam-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  dang nga'o snyam pa'i 'dun-pa #  dang nga'o snyam pa'i bag-la-nyal #  ma-spangs-pa # 'o / / yongs su ma shes so / / ma bkag go / / mtha'-med-pa # r ma byas so zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / dper-na #  ma ma'i gos dri-ma-can #  du gyur-pa #  bul tog la-sogs-pa # s legs-par #  bkrus te dri-ma-med-pa # r gyur kyang de zhen-pa # r gos-pa # s dri-ma #  nam pa'i bag yod de / / de spos dri zhim-po #  bsgo-ba # s yang bsal-ba # r bya-dgos-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  kun-tu #  brtags-pa # 'i dri-ma #  spangs-pa # 'i 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  la yang sngon mngon-pa # r zhen te goms-par-byas-pa #  dngos-po #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'i bdag-tu-lta-ba #  rjes su 'brang ste /
anta grAha dRzwiH sahaja ucCeda dRzwi saMgRhItA veditavyA yayA nirvANAt pratyudAvartate mAnasam paritrasanam upAdAya aTa kaH tarhi me AtmA iti
# de ni lam bsgoms-pa # s spang-ba # r bya-dgos-pa #  yin no / / mthar-'dzin-par-lta-ba #  lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  ni chad-pa # r lta-ba # s bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / des bdag-gi #  bdag gang yin zhes yongs su mi chad-pa # 'i phyir mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la yid phyir-ldog-pa # r byed do /
rAga AdayaH BAvanA prahAtavyAH dRzwi pakzAn muktvA / tad nidAna vastu parijQAnam kleSa anuSayaH ca aprahINaH Bavati evamAdi pUrvavat / svaBAva parijQAnam kleSaH ezaH utpannaH citta saMkleSa AtmakaH iti / avaparijQAnam AtmA avyAvADAya saMvartate para vyAbADAya uBaya vyAbADAya dRzwa DAmikam avadyam prasavati sAMparAyikam dRzwa Darma sAMparAyikam avadyam prasavati tad jam cEtasikam duHKa dOrmanasyam pratisaMvedayate iti evam triBiH prakArEH parijQAya utpannaH kleSaH anaDivAsana yogena parivarjyate
# lta-ba # 'i phyogs dang mthun-pa #  ma-gtogs-par #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  ni bsgoms-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  dag go / / de'i gzhi'i dngos-po #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bag-la-nyal #  ma-spangs-pa #  yin te zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  snga-ma-bzhin #  no / / ngo-bo-nyid #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i bdag-nyid-kyi #  nyon-mongs-pa #  ni 'byung-po #  zhes-bya'o #  / / nyes-dmigs #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-la-gnod-pa #  dang gzhan la gnod-pa #  dang / / gnyi-ga-la-gnod-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  dang / / mthong-ba # 'i chos kyi kha na ma thob ba bskyed-pa #  rnams dang / / tshe phyi'i ma'i kha na ma-thob-pa #  bskyed-pa #  dang de-la # s byung-ba # 'i sems-las-byung-ba #  sdug-bsngal #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  myong-bar-byed-pa # 'o / / de-ltar #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyis yongs su shes-nas #  nyon-mongs-pa #  'byung-bar-'gyur-ba #  dbang du mi len-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  yongs su spang ngo /
anutpannasya tu anutpAdAya mArgaH BAvyate
# ma-skyes-pa #  mi bskyed-pa # 'i phyir lam bsgom mo /

# 'dres-pa #  la dmigs-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni tha-dad-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  ste / / chos-thams-cad #  kyi spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  kyi rnam-pa # r zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

na te kleSa prahANa arTam kiMtarhi anAtma AkAra parikarma arTam / anitya AkAram hi niHsRtyAn Atma AkAraH / yaTA uktam yat anityam tat duKam yat duKam tat anAtmA iti
# de-dag #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba #  ma yin gyi bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa # r yongs-su-sbyang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir te / / mi-rtag-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  la brten-nas #  sdug-bsngal-gyi-rnam-pa #  'thob bo / / sdug-bsngal-gyi-rnam-pa #  la brten-nas #  bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa #  'thob ste / / ji-skad-du #  gang mi-rtag-pa #  de sdug-bsngal-ba # 'o / / de bdag-med-pa # 'o zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
atas eva anAtma AkArasya anuttarya vyavasTAnam
# de-bas-na #  bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa #  ni bla-na-med-pa #  nyid-du #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /

# bla-na-med-pa #  nyid las brtsams nas bla-na-med-pa #  nyid gsum ste / / shes-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid dang / / lam bla-na-med-pa #  nyid dang /
tatra jQAna anuttaryam nErAtmya jQAnam tatas pareNa jQAna antara aparyezaNAt
# rnam-par-grol-ba #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid do / / de-la #  shes-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid ni bdag-med-pa # 'i shes-pa #  nyid de / / de'i-pha-rol-du #  shes-pa #  gzhan btsal du med-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# lam bla-na-med-pa #  nyid ni sla-la #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  myur-ba #  ste / / de ni lam thams-cad-kyi #  mchog yin pa'i phyir ro /

# rnam-par-grol-ba #  bla-na-med-pa #  nyid ni mi-slob-pa #  mi-'khrugs-pa # 'i rnam-par-grol-ba #  ste / / rnam-par-grol-ba #  thams-cad-la # s khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i phyir ro /

upalabDi karma cakzuH AdInAm rUpa darSana Adi

# lus la-sogs-pa # 'i las la-la # s kyi lam zhes-bya-ba #  ni mdo-sde #  dang mthun-par #  ji-ltar #  gtso bo bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / de-la #  sbyor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yang lus la-sogs-pa # 'i las kyi nang-du #  'dus-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# bsam-pa #  ni gzhi de-la #  der 'du-shes #  pa'i bsam-pa #  dang / / las-kyi-lam #  de byed-par-'dod-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o /

# sbyor-ba #  ni de bya-ba # 'i phyir bdag gam gzhan gyi lus dang ngag dang yid kyi rtsom pa'o /

# nyon-mongs-pa #  ni 'dod-chags #  dang zhe-sdang #  dang gti-mug #  'dus-pa #  dang so-so-ba #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni sbyor-ba #  de-dang-de # 'i dus sam / / phyis las de-dang-de # s yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'o / / de-la #  srog-gcod-pa # 'i gzhi ni sems-can #  no /
