kleSaH loBa AdikaH
# nyon-mongs-pa #  ni 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
nizWA Agamanam tasya prANinaH tena prayogeNa anantaram praScAt vA maraNam / adatta AdAna AdAnAm vastu ca nizWA Agamanam ca nirDekzyAmaH / Sezam yaTAyogam yojayitavyam
# zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni sbyor-ba #  des de ma-thag-tu #  'am phyis shi-ba # 'o / / ma-byin-par-len-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gzhi dang zin-pa # r byas-pa #  bshad-par-bya # 'o / / lhag-ma #  ni ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
adattA dAnasya vastu para parigRhItam sattva saMKyAtam asat saMKyAtam vA / nizWA Agamanam tad svIkaraNam
# ma-byin-par-len-pa # 'i gzhi ni gzhan gyis yongs-su-gzung-ba #  sems-can #  gyi grangs-su-gtogs-pa # 'am sems-can #  gyi grangs su ma-gtogs-pa # 'o / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni bdag-gi # r byas-pa # 'o /
kAma miTyA AcArasya vastu agamyA strI gamyA vA anaFga AdeSa akAle vamA trAyuktAByAm ca sarvaH ca pumAn naKakam ca / nizWA Agamanam dvaya dvaya samApattiH / mRzA vAdasya vastu dRzwam Srutam matam vijQAtam adRzwam aSrutam amatam avijQAtam ca
# 'dod-pa # s log-pa # r g-yem ba'i gzhi ni spyod yul-ma-yin-pa # 'i bud-med #  dang spyod yul yin yang yan-lag #  ma-yin-pa #  dang yul-ma-yin-pa #  dang dus-ma-yin-pa #  dang tshod-ma-zin-pa #  dang rigs ma-yin-pa #  dang pho dang ma-ning #  thams-cad #  do / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni gnyis-kyis-gnyis-sprad-pa # 'o / / brdzun-du-smra-ba # 'i gzhi ni mthong-ba #  dang thos-pa #  dang bye-brag-phyed-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang ma-mthong-ba #  dang ma-thos-pa #  dang bye-brag #  mi-phyed-pa #  dang rnam-pa # r ma shes ba'o /
ASayaH anyaTA vat kukAma tA
# bsam-pa #  ni gzhan-du #  'du-shes #  la gzhan-du-smra-ba # r 'dod-pa # 'o /
nizWA Agamanam parzad prativAdi vijQApanam
# zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni 'khor dang phyir-rgol-ba # s go-bar-byed-pa # 'o /
pESunyasya vastu samagra vyagrAH sattvAH
# phra-ma # 'i gzhi ni sems-can #  'dum pa dang mi-'dum-pa #  dag go /
ASayaH tezAm eva Beda apratisaMDAna aBiprAyaH / nizWA Agamanam Bedya vijQApanam
# bsam-pa #  ni dbye-ba #  dang sdum mi-byed-pa # r sems-pa # 'o / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni phye-ba # r shes-par-byed-pa # 'o /
pAruzyasya vastu AGAta nimitta BUtAH sattvAH / nizWA Agamanam pArUzANAm
# ngag rtsub po'i gzhi ni kun-nas-mnar-sems #  kyi gzhir-gyur-pa # 'i sems-can #  rnams so / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni ngag rtsub po smras-pa # 'o /
saMBinna pralApasya vastu anarTa upasaMgRhIta arTaH / nizWA Agamanam tasya BAzaNam
# tshig-kyal-pa # 'i gzhi ni don-med-pa #  dang ldan-pa'i-don #  no / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni de smras-pa # 'o /
aBiDyAyAH vastu parakIyam vitta upakaraNam
# brnab-sems #  kyi gzhi ni gzhan-gyi-nor #  dang yo-byad #  do /
ASayaH tatra tad saMjQinaH taTA aruciH / prayogaH tad svIkaraNa saMpraDAraNam / nizWA Agamanam tad svIkaraNa niScayaH
# bsam-pa #  ni de-la #  der 'du-shes #  shing de-bzhin-du #  'dod-pa # 'o / / sbyor-ba #  ni de bdag-gir-bya-ba # r sems-pa # 'o / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni bdag-gir-bya-ba # r nges-pa # 'o /
vyApAdasya vastu AGAta nimitta BUtAH sattvAH / nizWA Agamanam prahanana niScayaH / miTyAdRzweH vastu sannarTaH
# gnod-sems #  kyi gzhi ni kun-nas-mnar-sems #  kyi rgyur-gyur-pa # 'i sems-can #  rnams so / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni bsad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r nges-pa # 'o / / log-pa # r lta-ba # 'i gzhi ni don-yod-pa # 'o /
ASayaH satya tad saMjQinaH taTA aruciH / nizWA Agamanam apavAda niScayaH
# bsam-pa #  ni yod-pa #  la med-pa # r 'du-shes #  shing de-bzhin-du #  'dod-pa # 'o / / zin-pa # r byas-pa #  ni skur ba 'debs-pa # r nges-pa # 'o /
parAjQapti saMcetanIya tA yaTA kaScid anicCan= api parEH balAt AjQApyamanaH aBisaMGAya akuSalam Acarati
# gzhan gyis bsgo-ba #  sems-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni 'di-la #  ste / / 'ga' zhig mi-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  gzhan dag gis nan-gyis #  bsgos nas bsams te / / mi-dge-ba #  spyod-pa # 'o /
para saMjQapti saMcetanIya tA yaTA kaScid anicCan= iva parEH saMjQApyamAnaH samAdApyamAnaH hitam etat iti grAhyamANaH aBisaMGAyAH kuSalam Acarati
# gzhan gyis gsol-ba-btab-pa #  sems-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'ga' zhig mi-'dod-bzhin-du #  gzhan dag gis gsol-ba-btab-nas #  'di ni phan-pa # 'o zhes yang-dag-pa #  'dzin du bcug cing len du bcu gnas bsams te mi-dge-ba #  spyod-pa # 'o / / mi-shes-pa # 'i sems-pa #  la gyur-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
avijQAya saMcetanIyatA yaTA kaScid guNa doza anaBijQaH anaBinivizwaH yadRcCayA aBisaMDAya AkuSalam Acarati
# kha-cig #  yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  mngon-pa # r mi shes shing / / mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med la / / 'dod dgar bsams nas mi-dge-ba #  spyod-pa # 'o /
mUla aBiniveSa saMceta nIyatA yaTA kaScid kuSala mUlEH loBa AdiBiH aBiBUtaH Avizwa cittaH tIvreNa aBiniveSena aBisaMGAya akuSalam Acarati
# rtsa ba la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i sems las gyur-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'ga' zhig mi-dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba la chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s zil gyis non cing sems non nas mngon-pa # r zhe na pa drag-po # s bsams te mi-dge-ba #  la spyod-pa # 'o /
viparyAsa saMcetanIya tA yaTA kaScid Darma kAmaH vizama hetu dRzwiH AyatyAm izwa Pala arTam aBisaMDAya AkuSalam Acarati
# phyin-ci-log #  gi sems-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'ga' zhig chos 'dod kyang mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu #  la lta ste / / phyi-ma-la #  yid-du-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i don-du #  bsams nas mi-dge-ba #  spyod-pa # 'o /
tatra pUrvikABiH tisRBiH saMcetanIyatABiH kRtam api karma na eva upacIyate yatas asya na avaSyam vipAkaH pratisaMvedanIyaH
# de-la #  sems-pa #  las gyur-pa #  dang-po #  gsum ni las byas su zin-kyang #  stsogs-pa #  nyid-du #  mi 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  'di'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  ma yin no /
paScimAByAm tu saMcetanIyAByAm yadi kRtam Bavati upacitam ca avaSyam eva asya vipAkaH pratisaMvedyate
# sems-pa #  las gyur ba tha-ma #  gnyis ni gal-te #  byas-pa # r gyur na bsags-pa #  yin te / / de'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  gdon-mi-za-bar #  myong-ba # r 'gyur ro /
upacayaH vAsanA vRdDiH iti Alaya vijQAne vipAka bIja paripozaNam veditavyam
# stsogs-pa #  ni bag-chags #  'phel-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i sa-bon #  yongs su gsos par rig-par-bya # 'o /
karma kriyA niyamaH pUrva karmaBiH eva niyamya vipAka saMtatiH AvidDA Bavati
# las-byed-pa # r nges-pa #  ni sngon-gyi-las #  rnams kyis rnam-par-smin-pa'i-rgyu # d nges-par #  byas-na # s 'phangs-pa # r gyur ba ste /
yat asmin janmani anena idam karma karaNIyam iti sa tam avaDim alaMkaGayitvA tat karma karoti yasya akaraNAya pratibanDam budDAH api BagavantaH na samarTAH kartum yaTA hetu niyamanam Pala saMtAna pariNAmAt iti
# gang-gi-tshe #  de-la #  'dis las 'di byed-pa # r nges-par #  de dang mi-'gal-ba # r las de byed / / de'i rgyu'i nges-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  'bras-bu # 'i rgyur gyur ba'i phyir de mi-bya-ba # r bzlog-pa #  ni sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams kyis kyang mdzad mi spyod do /
vipAka pratisaMvedanA niyamaH saMcetanIyasya karmaNaH pUrvavat
# rnam-par-smin-pa #  myong-ba # r nges-pa #  ni / / sems-pa #  las gyur-pa # 'i las kyi ste snga-ma-bzhin #  no /
avasTA niyame dRzwa Darma vedanIya AdiBiH avasTA api niyamitA Bavati iti
# dus-nges-pa #  ni mthong-ba # 'i chos la myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las rnams kyi dus kyang nges-par #  byas-pa #  yin te /
yaTA anena vipAkena dRzwe Darme Bavitavyam anena upapadyAnena aparasmin paryAya iti
# ji-ltar #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  'dis ni mthong-ba # 'i chos la rnam-par-smin-pa # r byed do / / 'dis ni skyes nas so /
akuSalAnAm karma paTAnAm mRdu maDya aDi mAtrANAm vipAka Palam tiryak preta narakezu veditavyam
# 'dis ni lan-grangs-gzhan-la # 'o zhes-bya'o #  / / mi-dge-ba #  bcu'i las-kyi-lam #  rnams kyi rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni dud-'gro #  dang yi dgas dang sems-can #  dmyal-ba #  rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o /
nizyanda Palam apAyeByaH cyutvA manuzyezu upapannAnam pratyekam prANa atipAtAt AttAt anAdi AnurUpyeNa Atma BAva parigrahayoH vipattiH / tat yaTA alpa Ayuzka tA dAridrayam iti evamAdi yaTAyogam / aDipati Palam pratyekam tad AnurUpyeNa eva bAhyAnAm BAvAnAm sasya AdInAm vipattiH / tat yaTA prANa atipAtasya ADipatyena alpa ojasaH Bavanti evamAdi / yaTA sUtram sarvEH daSaBiH akuSalEH karma paTEH AsevitEH BAvitEH bahulIkRtEH narakezu upapadyate / tat ezAm vipAka Palam / sa ced icCatvam AgacCati manuzyANAm saBA gatAm prANa atipAtena alpa AyuH Bavati adattA AdAnena Boga vyasanI Bavati / kAma miTyA AcAreNa sa sapatna dAraH / mRzA vAdena aByAKyAna bahulaH / pESUnyena mitra BedaH asya Bavati / pAruzyeNa amanojQa Sabda SravaNam Bavati / saMBinna pralApena anAdeya vAkyaH / aBiDyayA tIvra rAgaH / vyApAdena tIvra dvezaH / miTyAdRzwyA tIvra mohaH tasyAH moha BUyaH tvAt / idam ezAm nizyanda Palam / prANa atipAtena atyevitena bAhya aBAvAH alpa ojasaH Bavanti / adatta AdAnena aSani rajaH bahulAH / kAma miTyA AcAreNa rajaH avakIrNAH / mRzA vAdena duganDAH / paSUnyena utkUla nikUlAH / pArUzyeNa Uzara jaFgamAH pratikruswAH pApa BUmayaH / saMBinna pralApena viza martya pariNAmAH / aBiDyayA sUkzma PalAH / vyApAdena kawukaPalAH / miTyAdRzwayA alpa PalA aPalA vA / idam ezAm aDipati Palam / daSAnAm kuSalAnAm karma paTAnAm vipAka Palam deva manuzyezu / nizyanda Palam tezu eva pratyekam AnurUpyeNa Atma BAva parigraha saMpattiH / yaTA kuSalAnAm karma paTAnAm vipAka Pala Adi triPalA vasTAnam kRtam evam kuSala AdInAm karma paTAnAm sa AsravANAm deva manuzyezu trINi PalAni yaTAyogam yojayitavyAni / ekena karmaNA ekam Atma BAvam Akzipati ekena karma kzaNena eka janmikasya eva vipAkasya bIja pozaNAt / ekena anekam Akzipati tena eva aneka janmika vipAka bIja pozaNAt / anekena ekam Akzipati bahuBiH karma kzaNEH tasya eva ekasya punar punar bIja pozaNAt / anekena aneka mAkzipati bahuBiH anyonya apekzayA janma paraMparA bIja pozaNAt iti / kena kAraNena rUpa ArUpya pratisaMyuktam kuSalam Anijyam iti ucyate / yaTA kAmAvacaram anya gatikam api paripUrakam kuSala mUlam anyatra vipAkam prayacCati na evam rUpya arUpya avaram BUminA eyena Pala dAnAt / atas vipAka dAnam pratyakampana arTena anijyam uktam samAhita BUmika tvAt ca akampana arTena iti / Pala vipAka saMmUXasya apuNyAH saMskArAH saMBavanti tezAm ekAnta klizwa tvena avidyA sAMniDye sati Pala vipAka aBisaMparaNya AkArAyAH samyak dRzweH anavakASAt / tattva arTa saMmUXasya puNya aniMjyAH tattva arTaH ucyate catvAri Arya satyAni / tatra saMmohaH kuSala cittAnAm api adRzwa satyAnAm anuSayataH anubudDaH Bavati yat vaSena te duHKataH trEDAtukasya yaTABUtam aparijQAnAt punarBava hetu BUtAn puNya anijya saMskArAn utTApayanti / na tu evam dRzwa satyAH tattva arTa saMmoha aBAvAt / atas te tad hetukAH iti ucyante

 mi 'byor-ba #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  tshe-thung-ba #  dang dbul-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro / / bdag-po'i-'bras-bu #  ni so-so #  dang mthun-pa #  nyid-du #  phyi'i dngos-po #  lo-tog #  la-sogs-pa #  mi 'byor-ba #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  srog-gcod-pa # 'i dbang gis ni byin chung-ba # r 'gyur zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-du #  dge-ba #  bcu'i las-kyi-lam #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  bdag-gir-byed-pa # r nges-pa # 'o zhes bstan-pa #  de-la #  gal-te #  gzhan-gyi-nor #  dang yo-byad #  de nyid 'dod-pa # r gyur na / / de bdag-gir-bya-ba # 'i phyir mngon-pa # r 'du-byed #  de /
prANa atipAtasya loBena prayogaH mAMsikA AdInAm / dvezeNa eva vEra niryAtana kAmAnAm / mohena yAjQikA AdInAm / dvezeNa eva nizWA nirGRNatAm antareNa para sattva vipAdana asaMBavAt / evam pAruzya AdInAm yaTAyogam yojayitavyam / aBiDyA AdInAm kaTam loBa AdiBiH prayogaH / tatra aBiDyA karma paTaH para vitta upakaraNa svIkaraNa niScayaH iti uktam / tat yadi tena eva vitta upakaraNena arTI Bavati tat svIkaraNAya aBisaMskaroti atas asya loBena prayogaH vyavasTApyate / aTa mA eva asya BUt iti evam dvezeNa / aTa parasvIkaraNe na kaScid dozaH iti mohena prayogaH veditavyaH / evam anyat api yojayitavyam / anyonya ADipateyam api karma sADAraNam veditavyam yad vaSAt sattvAH anyonyam cita cEtta pariNAma nimittam Bavanti iti / vEpakzikAt karmaNaH prAtipakzikEH karma balavat drazwavyam pratipakza balena Akziptasya api vipakza Palasya anyaTAtva ApAdanAt / sarvam ca kuSalam karma saMcetanIyam pratipakza balikasya AkuSalAt balavat drazwavyam / pratipakza bala durbalasya tu akuSalam kuSalAt balavat
# de'i-phyir #  chags-pa # s sbyor-ba # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go / / ci ste 'di yi ra ma gyur cig ce na / / de-ltar-na #  ni zhe-sdang #  gis sbyor ro / / ci ste gzhan gyis bdag-gi # r byas kyang nyes-pa #  ci-yang #  med do snyam na gti-mug #  gis sbyor-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / gzhan la yang de-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / phan tshun gyi dbang gis byung-ba #  yang thun-mong-ba # 'i las su rig-par-bya #  ste / / de'i dbang gis sems-can #  rnams phan tshun du sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i rgyur 'gyur ro / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi las ni gnyen-po # 'i las stobs-dang-ldan-pa # r blta ste / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyis 'bras-bu #  'phangs su zin-kyang #  gnyen-po # 'i stobs kyis gzhan-du #  bsgyur-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gnyen-po # 'i stobs-can #  gyi dge-ba'i-las #  sems-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni / / mi-dge-ba # s stobs-dang-ldan-pa # r blta'o / / gnyen-po # 'i mthu chung-ba # 'i mi-dge-ba #  ni dge-ba #  bas stobs dang ldan no /
sarvam ca aviSezeNa kuSala akuSalam niyata vipAkam Arya mArgeNa aprahINam balavat iti ucyate / kAma pratisaMyuktam akuSalam prakRtyA balavat kleSa upakleSa Adi bahu parivAra tvAt
# dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  rnam-par-smin-pa # r nges-pa #  'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyis ma spangs ba thams-cad #  ni bye-brag-med-par #  stobs-dang-ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'dod-pa #  dang rab tu ldan-pa # 'i mi-dge-ba #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  stobs-dang-ldan-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i 'khor mang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yadi api pUrva aByastam tat api balavat saMtateH tena BAvita tvAt
# gang sngon gyi goms-pa # r byas ba de-yang #  stobs-dang-ldan-pa #  ste / / des rgyud la bsgos-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yat api pada sTam paripUrNa vayasAm tIvra aBiniveSa prasAda karaNAt / yat api asADyam aparisanirvANa DarmakANAm pratipakzeNa anuhArya tvAt
# gang gnas la gnas-pa #  ni nar son pa rnams kyi ste / / mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dang dad-pa #  drag-po # s byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yongs su mya-ngan #  las mi 'da' ba'i chos-can #  rnams kyi lam sgrub tu med-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni gnyen-po # s byung du med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kzetrataH api mAtR baDAdikam
# zhing ni ma-gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
citta aBisaMskArataH api mahA boDi praNiDAna Adikam balavat karma veditavyam
# sems kyi mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems #  por smon-lam-btab-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / stobs-dang-ldan-pa # 'i las su rig-par-bya # 'o /
punar navaBiH AkArEH balavat karma veditavyam
# yang rnam-pa #  dgus stobs-dang-ldan-pa # 'i las su rig-par-bya #  ste 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA kzetrataH yadi guNavat dakziNIyam kzetram Bavati / vastunaH yadi praNItam praBUtam deya vastu Bavati / svaBAvataH dAnAt SIlam SIlAt BAvanA iti evamAdiH
# zhing ni gal-te #  yon-tan-dang-ldan-pa # 'i sbyin-gnas #  zhing du gyur-pa # 'o / / dngos-po #  ni gal-te #  sbyin-pa # 'i dngos-po #  gya nom zhing mang-po # r gyur-pa # 'o / / ngo-bo-nyid #  ni sbyin ba bas tshul-khrims #  stobs dang ldan no / / tshul-khrims #  pas bsgom-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
ASrayataH puNyAnAm kartA yadi vIta rAgaH Bavati
# gzhi ni bsod nams byed-pa #  gal-te #  'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # r gyur-pa # 'o /
manaskArataH yadi tIvra prasAda sahagataH manaskAraH Bavati
# yid-la-byed-pa #  ni gal-te #  yid-la-byed-pa #  dang-ba #  drag-po #  dang ldan-par-'gyur-ba # 'o /
ASayataH yadi nirvANa ASayaH Bavati
# bsam ba ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  dang ldan-par-gyur-pa # 'o /
sahAyataH yadi tad anya puNya kriyA vastu parigRhItam Bavati
# grogs ni de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i bsod nams bya-ba # 'i dngos-po # s yongs-su-zin-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'o /
bahulIkArataH yadi pOnaH punyena kRtam Bavati anuvitarkitam vA / bAhu janyataH yadi svayam ca kRtam Bavati anyEH ca kAritam iti
# lan-mang-du-byed-pa #  ni yang-dang-yang-du #  byas-pa # r gyur ba'am / / rjes su rnam-par-brtags-pa # 'o / / skye-bo-mang-po # s kyang zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-gis #  kyang byas-pa # r gyur la gzhan dang kyang byed-du-bcug-pa # 'o /
yaH evam vadet yaTA yaTA ayam puruza pudgalaH karma karoti upacinoti taTA taTA vipAkam pratisaMvedayataH iti evam sati brahmacarya vAsaH na Bavati avakASaH ca na prajQAyate samyak duHKa kzayAya duHKasya anta kriyAyE
# su zhig 'di-skad-du #  skyes-bu #  gang-zag #  'di ji-ltar #  las byed cing stsogs-pa #  de-lta-de-ltar #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  myong-ba #  gyur na / / de-ltar-na #  tshangs-par-spyod-pa # s gnas-pa # r mi 'gyur zhing yang-dag-par #  sdug-bsngal #  zad-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal #  mthar dbyung-ba # 'i skabs kyang mi snang ngo zhes zer zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kaTam kRtvA brahmacarya vAsaH na Bavati
# ji-ltar #  byas-na #  tshangs-par-spyod-pa # s gnas-pa # r mi 'gyur zhe na /
tIvra kleSasya pratisaMKyAya saha duHKena saha dOrmanasyena SIla paripAlanAt / yadi tad vipAkaH taTA eva saha duHKena saha dOrmanasyena anuBUyata vRTA tat paripAlanam syAt
# nyon-mongs-pa-drag-po #  dang ldan-pa # s so-so # r brtags na sdug-bsngal-dang-bcas-pa # r tshul-khrims #  yongs su bsrungs ba'i phyir gal-te #  de'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  yang de-bzhin-du #  sdug-bsngal #  dang bcas shing yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  myong na ni de yongs su srung-ba #  don-med-pa # r 'gyur ro /
pAradArika praBRtInAm ca saha suKena saha sOmanasyena dOHSIlya karaNa Adi Adi tad vipAkaH taTA eva anuBUyata vRTA tad viratiH syAt iti evam kRtvA brahmacarya vAsaH na Bavati / kaTam avakASaH ca na prajQAyate samyak duHKa kzayAya duHKasya anta kriyAyE / atas eva tad upanizad gatasya brahmacarya vAsasya duHKa vipAka tvAt iti
# gzhan-gyi-chung-ma #  la-sogs-pa #  la bde-ba #  dang bcas shing yid-bde-ba #  dang bcas-pa # r tshul-khrims-'chal-ba # r byas-pa # 'i phyir gal-te #  de'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  myong na ni de spong-ba #  don-med-pa # r 'gyur te / / de-ltar #  byas-na #  tshangs-par-spyod-pa # s gnas-pa # r mi 'gyur ro / / ji-ltar #  na yang-dag-par #  sdug-bsngal #  zad-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal #  mthar dbyung-ba # 'i skabs kyi kyang mi snang zhe na / / de'i-phyir #  de'i rgyur gyur ba tshangs-pa #  spyod-pa # s gnas-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  sdug-bsngal-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  byas-na #  bde-ba #  dang bcas-pa # 'i las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni bde-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur / / sdug-bsngal-dang-bcas-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  'gyur /
evam ca kRtvA suKa sahagatasya karmaNaH suKa sahagataH eva vipAkaH duHKa saha gatasya duHKa saha gataH aduHsuKa saha gatasya tad sahagataH eva iti niyamaH pratizidDaH
# sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i ni / / sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba # 'i nges-pa #  ni 'dir bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis bkag go /
atra yaH tu evam yaTA vedanIyam yaTA vedanIyam iti evamAdinA suKa saha gatasya kuSala akuSalasya yaTAyogam AyatyAm suKa duHKa asuKa vedanIyasya suKa AdikaH vipAkaH anujQAtaH / evam duHKa aduHKa sahagatasya suKa Adi vedanIyasya suKa AdikaH vipAkaH anujQAyate iti
# yongs su zhig 'di-skad-du #  / / skyes-bu #  gang-zag #  'di ji-ltar #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  ji-ltar #  myang-ba # r 'gyur zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni bde-ba-dang-ldan-pa # 'i dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  phyi-ma-la #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du bde-ba-dang-sdug-bsngal #  dang sdug-bsngal #  yang ma-yin-pa #  bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # r myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni gnang ngo /
pravrajitasya saMvaraH paQcaviDaH Bikzu saMvaraH yAvat SAmaNeH IsaMvaraH iti
# rab-tu-byung-ba # 'i sdom-pa #  ni rnam-pa-lnga #  ste / / dge slong gi sdom-pa #  nas dge-tshul-ma # 'i sdom-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
sa duScarita viveka caritam kAma viveka caritam ca pudgalam aDikRtya vyavasTApitaH
# nyes-par-spyod-pa #  las dben-pa # r spyod-pa #  dang 'dod-pa #  las dben-pa # r spyod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-zag #  gi dbang-du-byas-nas #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ste /
taTA hi sa tAdRSaH Saknoti yAvajjIvam prANa atipAtAda brahmacaryAt ca virantum iti
# 'di-ltar #  de-'dra-ba #  de ni ji-srid-'tsho'i-bar-du #  srog gcad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  nyes-par-spyod-pa #  dang mi-tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  spang-ba # r nus so /
upAsaka upAsikA saMvaraH duScarita viveka caritam aDikRtya no tu kAma viveka caritam
# dge-bsnyen #  dang dge-bsnyen-ma # 'i sdom-pa #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  las dben-pa # r spyod-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / 'dod-pa #  las dben-pa # r spyod-pa #  ni ma yin no /
atas eva asya yAvajjIvam kAma miTyA cAra viratiH vyavasTApyate na abrbrahmacarya viratiH iti
# de-bas-na #  'di'i sdom-pa #  ni ji-srid-'tsho'i-bar-du #  'dod-pa #  la log-pa # r g-yem pa spang-ba # r rnam-pa # r gzhag gi / / mi-tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  spong-ba #  ni ma yin no /
upavAsa saMvaraH na eva duScarita viveka caritam na kAma viveka caritam
# bsnyen-gnas #  pa'i sdom-pa #  ni nyes-par-spyod-pa #  las dben-pa # r spyod-pa #  yang ma yin 'dod-pa #  las dben-pa # r spyod-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ste /
atas eva asya ahorAtrakaH upavAsa saMvaraH prajQaptaH SanEs tad uBaya aByasana arTam iti
# de'i-phyir #  de'i sdom-pa #  na nyin zhag gcig pa la bsnyen-gnas #  pa'i sdom-pa #  brtags te / / rims kyis de-gnyi-ga #  goms-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA paNXa paNXakAnAm BikzuBikzuNI pakza upAsanA yogya tvAt upAsaka tva pratizeDaH evam uBaya vyaQjanAnAm api strI puruza kleSa samudAcAreNa uBaya pakza upAsanAya yogya tA iti na te pRTak uktAH
# ji-ltar #  tha-ma #  dang ma-ning #  rnams la ni dge slong dang dge slong ma'i phyogs gnyis la bsnyen-bkur-bya-ba # 'i 'os ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir dge-bsnyen #  nyid ni bkag-pa #  bzhin-du #  mtshan gnyis-pa #  rnams kyang de-bzhin-du #  ste / / skyes-pa-dang-bud-med #  kyi nyon-mongs-pa #  kun-tu-spyod-pa # s phyogs gnyi-ga #  la bsnyen-bkur-bya-ba # 'i 'os ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir de-dag #  logs-shig #  tu ma bshad do /
DyAna saMvaraH dOHSIlya samutTApakAnAm loBa AdInAm kAma avacarANAm kleSa upakleSAnAm vizkamBaNa pratipakzeNa bIja upaGAte sati pradeSa vErAgyeNa api kAmeByaH vIta rAgasya yA tasmAt OHSIlyAt viratiH
# bsam-gtan #  gyi sdom-pa #  ni 'chal-ba'i-tshul-khrims #  kun-nas-slong-ba #  dag gi chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams rnam-pa # r gnon-pa # 'i gnyen-po # s sa-bon #  bcom-pa # s phyogs-gcig-pa #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid-du #  zad de 'dod-pa #  dag las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i 'chal-ba'i-tshul-khrims #  te / / spong-ba #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
yAvat tRtIya DyAna vIta rAgasya dUrIBAva pratipakzeNa tezAm eva dOHSIlya samutTApakAnAm sutarAm bIja upaGAtaH veditavyaH
# bsam-gtan #  gsum-pa # 'i bar las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # 'i ring du byed-pa # 'i gnyen-po # s 'chal-ba'i-tshul-khrims #  kyi kun-nas-slong-ba #  de-dag-nyid #  kyi sa-bon #  shin-tu #  'joms par rig-par-bya # 'o /
caturTa DyAna vIta rAgasya tvArUpyezu rUpa aBAvAt lola saMvara avyavasTAnam veditavyam
# bsam-gtan-bzhi #  ba la 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  ni gzugs-med-pa #  rnams ni gzugs-med-pa # 'i phyir tshul-khrims-kyi-sdom-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  med-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
OraBrikAH ye paSUn hatvA tad vikrayeNa jIvikAm kalpayanti / evam kOkkuwikA AdayaH yaTAsaMBavam yojayitavyAH
# shan pa ni gang dag phyugs rnams bsad nas de 'tshong-ba # s 'tsho-bar-byed-pa #  rnams so / / bya-gag-gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang de-bzhin-du #  ji-ltar #  mthun-mthun-du-sbyor-ba # r bya'o /
nAga banDakAH araNyAt hastinaH vadDvA damayanti
# glang-po-che-'dzin-pa #  ni gang dag nags nas glang-po-che #  bzung nas 'dul-bar-byed-pa #  rnams so; /
nAga maNXalikAH ye sarpAn AdAya tad krIxanEH jIvanti
# sprul gyis 'tsho-ba #  ni gang dag sprul bzung nas rtse bas 'tsho-bar-byed-pa #  rnams so /
mUtrakAH ye parAn pESunyena upahatva jIvanti
# nyan rna-ba #  ni gang dag gzhan dag la phra-ma # s gnod-pa # r byas-na # s 'tsho-bar-byed-pa #  rnams so /
aBijat mataH vA tad karma samAdAnataH vA iti tad kulInasya anya kulInasya ca yaTAkramam
# de-dag #  gi las skyes-pa # s sam yang-dag-par-blangs-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni de'i rigs sam / / gzhan gyi rigs kyi go-rims #  bzhin no /
kAya vAc prayoga pUrvakaH tad karma aDyAcAra niScayaH asaMvaraH iti ucyate
# de-dag #  gi las spyad-pa # r nges-par #  byas-pa #  ni lus dang dag gi sbyor-ba #  sngon-du #  btang-ba #  ste / / sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
yaTA ukta saMvara asaMvara vinirmuktasya dAna priya vacana Adikam Kawa capewa Adikam ca karma nava saMvarona asaMvaraH iti ucyate
# ji-skad #  bshad-pa # 'i sngom-pa #  dang sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  dang mi-ldan-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  dang ngag snyan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang khu tshur dang thal lcag la-sogs-pa # 'i las ni sdom-pa #  yang ma yin /
dRzwa Darma vedanIyam karma yatra janmani kRtam tatra eva yat vipacyate
# sdom-pa-ma-yin-pa #  yang ma yin ba zhes-bya'o #  / / mthong-ba # 'i chos la myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i las ni tshe gang-la #  byas-pa #  de-nyid-la #  gang rnam-par-smin-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'o /
upapadya vedanIyam yat anantare janmani tat yaTA paQcAnantaryANi karmANi
# skyes nas myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i las ni gang de ma-thag-tu #  'byung-ba # 'i tshe la myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  mtshams-med-pa-lnga'i-las #  rnams so /
yasya tAvat ekam eva anantarya tasya tad vipAkaH anantaram yuktaH yasya idAnIm saMbahulAni tasya kaTam tad vipAka pratisaMvedanA
# gang-gi #  mtshams-med-pa #  gcig nyid ni de'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  de de-ma-thag-pa # r rigs na / / de gang-gi #  mang-po #  gang-yin-pa #  de'i de-dag #  gi rnam-par-smin-pa #  ji-ltar #  myong-ba # r 'gyur zhe na /
sarvezAm yugapad vipAkaH pratisaMvidyate taTA hi aneka anantara kAriNaH ASrayaH sukumArataraH nirvartate kAraNAH ca bahu tIvra vicitrAH yad vaSAt BUyasIm vedanAm pratyanuBavati
# thams-cad-kyi #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  gcig-car #  myong-ba # r 'gyur te / / 'di-ltar #  mtshams-med-pa #  du-ma #  byed-pa # 'i lus shin-tu #  gzhon-pa # r mngon-pa # r 'grub la / / chad-pa #  yang mang zhing mi-zad-pa #  sna-tshogs #  'byung ste / / de'i dbang gis tshor-ba #  shin-tu #  mang-po #  'byung-ba # r 'gyur ro /
AramBam ca pratyetAni dRzwa Darma vedanIya AdIni vyavasTApyante na tad mAtra vedanIya tAm aDikRtya
# rtsom pa'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  mthong-ba # 'i chos la myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'di dag rnam-pa # r gzhag gi / / de tsam la myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ni ma yin no /
yasya tatra eva janmani vipAkaH vipaktum AraBate tad dRzwa Darma vedanIyam
# tshe-de-nyid-la #  gang-gis #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  rnam-par-smin-pa # r rtsom pa de ni mthong-ba # 'i chos la myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'o /
yasya anantare janma nyAraBate tat upapadya vedanIyam
# gang de ma-thag #  ba'i tshe la rtsom pa de ni skyes nas myong-bar-'gyur-ba # 'o /
yasya anantaram janma laGayitvA AraBate tad apara paryAya vedanIyam iti evam ca kRtvA hAcitta avadAne Anantaryasya karmaNaH narake punar punar cyuti upapAdena vipAka pratisaMvedanam anulomitam Bavati iti
# gang de ma-thag-tu #  'byung-ba # 'i tshe thal nas rtsom pa de ni lan-grangs-gzhan-la #  myong-bar-'gyur-ba #  ste / / de-ltar #  byas-na #  kyi hud sems zhes-bya-ba # 'i rtogs-pa #  brjod-pa #  las mtshams-med-pa'i-las #  kyi rnams par smin-pa # s sems-can #  dmyal-ba # r yang-dang-yang #  'chi-'pho-zhing-skye-ba # s rnam-par-smin-pa # s myong ngo zhes 'byung-ba #  dang mthun-par #  byas-pa #  yin no /
kRzNam kRzNa vipAkam karma akuSalam klizwa tvAt anizwa vipAka tvAt ca
# gnag la rnam-par-smin-pa #  gnag-pa # 'i las ni mi-dge-ba #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang rnam-par-smin-pa #  mi-'dod-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
viparyayAt Suklam Sukla vipAkam trEDAtukam kuSalam
# bzlog-pa #  ni dkar la rnam-par-smin-pa #  dkar-ba #  ste / / khams-gsum-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'o /
kRzNa Suklam kRzNa Sukla vipAkam yat kAma pratisaMyuktam vipAkam vyAmiSram kuSala akuSalam iti arTaH / kaTam ekam kuSalam Bavati akuSalam ca / na atra pravRtti kzaNanA eyam yena ucyate tat eva uBayam iti api tu sahASaya prayogeNa ekam karma iti ayam atra aBi saMDiH vedivyaH
# dkar gnag tu gyur la rnam-par-smin-pa #  dkar gnag tu gyur-pa #  ni gang-'dod-pa #  dang rab tu ldan-pa # 'i 'dres ma ste / / dge mi dge zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / gcig na ci ltar dge-ba # r yang 'gyur la mi-dge-ba # r 'gyur zhe na / / di la 'jug-pa'i-skad-cig #  nges-par #  de-gnyi-ga #  brjod-pa #  ni ma yin gyi / / bsam-pa #  dang ldan cig pa'i sbyor-ba #  las gcig ces bya ste /
tayoH ca kRzNa Sukla tAm pratyanyonyAsA dRSye sati ekam karma kRzNa Suklam vyavasTApyate
# 'di ni 'dir dgongs-pa #  yin par rig-par-bya # 'o / / de gnyis nag-po #  dang dkar-po #  nyid-du #  phan tshun 'dra-bar #  gyur-pa # s nag-po #  dang dkar-po #  las gcig-tu #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
tatra ASayataH kRzNam prayogataH Suklam yaTA api kaScid parAn vaQcayitu kAmaH tezAm saMpratyayana nimittam BAvena dAnAni dadAti yAvat pravrajati api api
# de-la #  bsam-pa #  gnag la sbyor-ba #  dkar-ba #  ni dper-na #  'ga' zhig gzhan dag la slu-ba # r 'dod nas de-dag #  yid-ches-pa # r bya-ba # 'i mtshan-ma # r bsam-pa # s sbyin-pa #  rnams sbyin-pa #  nas rab-tu-'byung-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
prayogataH kRzNam ASayataH Suklam yaTA api kaScid putram vA Sizyam vAhitAn nivArayitu kAmaH hite ca niyojayitu kAmaH anukampA cittaH kAyena vAcA vA paruzayA tasmin kAle saMkliSyate / akRzNa Sukla avipAkam karma karma kzayAya saMvartate prayoga Anantarya mArgezu anAsravam karma prayoga mArga anantaram ArgANAm prahANa pratipakza tvAt
# sbyor-ba #  gnag la bsam-pa #  dkar-ba #  ni dper-na #  'ga' zhig bu 'am slob-ma #  la mi-phan-pa #  bzlog-pa # r 'dod cing phan-pa #  la sbyor-ba # r 'dod nas / / snying brtse ba'i sems-kyis #  lus dang ngag gis drag-tu #  byed-pa #  de'i tshe / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur ro / / mi gnag cig dkar la rnam-par-smin-pa # r mi 'gyur zhing-las #  zad-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i las gang zhe na / / sbyor-ba #  dang-ba #  chad-med-pa # 'i lam rnams la zag-pa-med-pa # 'i las zhes-bya-ba #  la / / sbyor-ba #  dang-ba # r chad-med-pa # 'i lam rnams ni spong-ba'i-gnyen-po #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra akRzNam kleSa mala aBAvAt / Suklam ekAnta vyavadAna tvAt / avipAkam saMsAra viroDi tvAt
# de-la #  mi gnag-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i dri-ma-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / dkar-ba #  ni gcig-tu #  rnam-pa #  byang-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-par-smin-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba #  ni / / 'khor-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro /
karma kzayAya saMvartate asya eva kRzNa Adikasya triviDasya sa Asravasya karmaNaH tena anAsraveNa karmaNA vipAka dAnava Asana asamudGAtAt
# las-zad-par-'gyur-ba #  ni nag-po #  la-sogs-pa #  zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i las rnam-pa-gsum #  po 'di nyid zag-pa-med-pa # 'i lam des rnam-par-smin-pa #  'byin-pa # 'i bag-chags #  legs-par-bcom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aviSezeNa ca sarvasya anAsravasya karmaNaH paripanTa mAnukUlyam svaBAvam aDikRtya vaMka doza kazAyANAm SOceyAnAm mOneyAnAm ca yaTAkramam vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# bye-brag-med-par #  zag-pa-med-pa # 'i las 'di thams-cad-kyi #  bar-du-gcod-pa #  dang rjes-su-mthun-pa #  dang ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  yon po dang nyes-pa #  dang rnyog-pa #  dang btsang ba dang thub-pa #  rnams go-rims-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra vaMkamRjuka mArgasya azwa aFgasya utpatti AvaraNa BUtam kAya vAc manaH karma
# de-la #  yon po ni lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  drang-po # 'i lam 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yan-lag-brgyad-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i sgrib-pa # r gyur-pa # 'o /
dozaH yena kAya Adi karmaNA dUzite saMtAne tat tAdRSam AvaraNa BUtam karma utpadyate
# nyes-pa #  ni lus la-sogs-pa # 'i las gang-gis #  rnam-pa # r sun-phyung #  ba'i sems-kyi-rgyud #  la de-dang-'dra-ba # 'i sgrib-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i las 'byung ngo /
kazAyAH tIrTika dRzwi saMniSritam kAya Adi karma budDa SAsana prasAda vipakzeNa aSradDya kAluzya parigRhIta tvAt
# rnyog-pa #  ni mu-stegs-can #  gyi lta-ba #  la brten-pa # 'i lus la-sogs-pa # 'i las gang-yin-pa #  ste / / sangs-rgyas-kyi-bstan-pa #  la dad-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma-dad-pa # 'i rnyog-pa # s yongs-su-zin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aparaH paryAyaH SASvata ucCeda anupatitam maDyamA pratipad viroDa arTena vaMkam
# rnams grangs gzhan-du-na #  / / rtag-pa #  dang chad-pa # 'i mthar lhung-ba #  ste / / dbu-ma'i-lam #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir yon po'o /
apavAda dRzwi parigRhItam vyavadAna vyavasTAna pradveza arTena dozaH
# skur ba'i lta-ba # s yongs su bzung-ste #  rnam-par-byang-ba #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  la rab tu zhe-sdang-ba # 'i phyir nyes-pa # 'o /
satkAya dRzwi parigRhItam nErAtmya tattva darSana prativadDa arTena kazAyaH iti
# 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # s yongs su bzung-ste #  / / bdag-med-pa # 'i de-kho-na #  la lta-ba # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i phyir rnyog-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
SOceyAni su viSudDa SIla saMgRhIta mRju dRzwi saMgRhItam ca yat kAya vAc manaH karma SIla dRzwi vipatti mala varjita tvAt
# gtsang ba ni shin-tu #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  kyis yongs-su-zin-pa #  dang lta-ba-drang-po # s yongs-su-zin-pa # 'i lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / tshul-khrims #  dang lta-ba #  la log-par-zhugs-pa # 'i dri-ma #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
mOneyAni SEkzA SEkzANAm yat anAsravam kAya vAc manaH karma munInAm tad karma iti kRtvA
# thub-pa #  ba ni gang slob-pa #  dang mi-slob-pa #  rnams kyi lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  zag-pa-med-pa #  ste / / de thub-pa #  rnams kyi las yin pa'i phyir ro /
dAna saMpadam aDikRtya dAnam dAtA Bavizyati iti anena aBIkzNa dAna tAm darSayati tad SIla tayA punar punar dAnAt
# sbyin-pa #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  sbyin-pa-po # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni phyir zhing sbyin-pa #  ston te / / de'i dang tshul can du gyur-pa # s yang-dang-yang #  sbyin ba'i phyir ro /
SramaNeByaH brAhmaNeByaH iti evamAdinA akzapAta dAnatAm aviSezeNa sarva arTiByaH dAnAta
# dge-sbyong #  rnams dang bram-ze #  rnams la zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni phyogs mi 'byed-pa # r sbyin-pa #  ston te / / 'dod-pa #  thams-cad-la #  bye-brag-med-par #  sbyin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anna pAnam iti evam AdinA icCA paripUraNa dAna tAm yaTA aBiprAyam sarva upakaraNa vastu parityAgAt
# bza'-ba-dang-btung-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni / / 'dod-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r sbyin-pa #  ston te / / bsam ba ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yo-byad #  kyi dngos-po-thams-cad #  yongs-su-gtong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
muktatyAgaH pratata pANiH vyavasarga rataH yAyajUkaH tyAga saMpannaH dAna saMviBAga rataH iti eBiH padEH yaTAkramam aniSrita dAna tA AdayaH veditavyAH
# lhug par gtong-ba #  dang lag brkyang-ba #  dang gtong-ba #  la dga'-ba #  dang mchod-sbyin-byed-pa # 'i dang tshul can dang gtong-ba #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang sbyin-pa #  legs-par #  'ged pa la dga'-ba #  zhes bya'i tshig 'di dag ni mi-gnas-par-sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
aniSrita dAna tA punarBava Boga apariNAmita tvena veditavyA
# mi-gnas-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  ni srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  kyi phyir yongs su mi bsngo-ba #  nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
deya saMpadam aDikRtya utTAna vIrya aDigatEH iti anena anaBidrugDa deya vastu tAm darSayati
# sbyin-par-bya-ba #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  ldang-ba # 'i brtson 'grus kyis thob-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sbyin-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  gnod-pa # s grub-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ston te /
aBidrugDam hi anutTAna bIrya aDigatam Bavati sva sTAne sTitvA para nikzepa apalapanena pratilabDa tvAt
# gnod-pa # s grub-pa #  ni ldang-ba # 'i brtson 'grus kyis thob-pa #  ma yin te / / rang-gi #  gnas na 'dug cing gzhan gyis bcol-ba #  bsnyon pas thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bAhu bala upArjitEH iti anena aparApahRta deya vastu tAm
# lag dar-ba # 'i mthus bsgrubs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sbyin-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  gzhan-las #  phrogs-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ston to /
pareByaH hi apahRtam na bAhu bala upArjitam Bavati tEH kRcCreNa viviDEH UpAyEH arjitasya apaharaNAt
# gzhan-las #  phrogs-pa #  ni lag dar-ba # 'i mthus bsgrubs-pa #  ma yin te / / de-dag #  gi sha thang bar thabs sna-tshogs #  kyis bsgrubs-pa #  phrogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sveda mala apakzitEH iti anena akuTita vimala deya vastu tAm sveda malAByAm apapakzipta tvAt ujJita tvAt iti arTaH
# rdul dang dri-ma # s ma phog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sbyin-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-pa #  ma rul cing dri-ma-med-pa #  ston te / / rdul dang dri-ma # s mas ma phog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni spangs zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
DArmikEH iti anena kalpika deya vastu tAm Sastra vizama Adya kalpika vastu vivarjita tvAt
# chos-dang-mthun-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sbyin-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  rung-ba #  ston te / / mtshon dang dug dang chang la-sogs-pa #  rung-ba-ma-yin-pa # 'i dngos-po #  yongs su spangs-pa # 'i phyir /
Darma labDEH iti anena Darma arjita deya vastu tAm darSayati tulA kUla Adi miTyAjI iva parivarjanena upArjita tvAt
# chos-kyis #  thob-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni sbyin-par-bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  chos-kyis #  bsgrub-pa #  ston te / / gzhal-ba # l g-yo 'jug-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang log-pa # s 'tsho-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yongs su spangs-nas #  bsgrubs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
SIlam samAdAya AKaNXanena tad yogAt SIlavAn Bavati
# tshul-khrims #  yang-dag-par #  blangs-nas #  ma-nyams-pa # s de dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir tshul-khrims-dang-ldan-pa #  yin no /
mokzam prati yaH saMvaraH sa prAtimokza saMvaraH / sa hi saMsArAt niryANAya Bavati
# thar-pa # 'i phyir sdom-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni so-sor-thar-pa # 'i sdom-pa #  ste / / de ni 'khor-ba #  las 'byung-ba # r 'gyur-pa #  yin no /
AcAra saMpannaH sadBiH agarhiteH yA paTa Adi tvAt / gocara saMpannaH paQcAgocara parivarjanAt
# cho-ga #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  ni spyod-la # m la-sogs-pa #  dam-pa #  rnams kyis ma-smad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / spyod yul phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  ni spyod yul-ma-yin-pa #  lnga spangs-pa # 'i phyir te /
paQca BikzoH agocarAH GozaH veSaH pAna AgAram rAja kulam caNXAla kaWinam eva paQcamam
# dge slong gi spyod yul-ma-yin-pa #  lnga ni gsod-pa # 'i sa dang smad 'tshong gi gnas dang chang 'tshong gi khyim dang rgyal-po'i-pho-brang #  dang gdol ba'i khyim ste lnga pa'o /
prajQapti sAvAdyezu api prakRti sAvadyezu iva tIvreNa gOraveNa SikzaNAt aNu mAtrezu avadyezu Baya darSI Bavati
# bcas-pa # 'i kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  rnams dang rang-bzhin #  gyi kha na mtho-ba #  rnams la yang bsam pha drag-po # s bslab-pa # s kha na ma thob chung du tsam rnams la yang 'jigs-par-lta-ba #  yin no /
samantAt paripUrNa SikzAm AdAya Sikzate SikzA apadeSzu iti ucyate
# kun nas yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bslab-pa #  rnams blangs-nas #  slob-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # r blangs te bslab-pa'i-gzhi #  rnams la slob ces bya'o /
atas param SIlam AraBya yat BagavatA sUtra antarezu nirdizwam kAyena saMvRtaH Bavati iti evamAdi tasya arTaH ucyate
# 'di man-chad-du #  ni tshul-khrims #  las brtsams nas / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis mdo-sde #  gzhan dag las lus dang ngag bsdams-pa #  yin no zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gang bstan ba de'i don brjod-pa # r bya'o /
tatra kAyena vAcA saMvRtaH Bavati saMprajanya parigRhIta tayA yaTA anujQAtam aBikrama pratikrama Adizu budDi pUrvam samyak vartanAt
# de-la #  lus dang ngag gi bsdams-pa #  yin pa ni shes-bzhin #  gyis yongs-su-zin-pa # 'i yin pa'i phyir te / / ji-ltar #  bka'-stsal-pa #  bzhin-du #  'gro-ba-dang-ldog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la blo sngon-du-btang-nas #  legs-par #  bsgrubs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kAya vAc saMpattyA saMpannaH Apatti anaDyApanna tayA SIla avipAdanAt
# lus dang ngag phun-sum-tshogs-pa # s phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  ni ltung-ba #  mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir te / / tshul-khrims #  chud-mi-gson-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pariSudDa kAya vAka samudAcAraH samADi saMniSraya tayA samADi balena dOHSIlya mala dUrIkaraNAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  la gnas-pa # 'i phyir te / / ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi stobs kyis 'tshal-ba # 'i tshul-khrims #  kyi dri-ma #  thag bsring pa'i phyir te /
kuSala kAya vAc samudAcAraH klizwa vitarka avyavakIrNa tayA ekAnta SuBa tvAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  dge-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi rtog-pa #  dang ma-'dres-pa # 'i phyir te / / gcig-tu #  dge-ba # 'i phyir ro /
anavadya kAya vAc samudAcAraH Bava Boga apariNAmita tvena sadBiH praSasta tvAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  med-pa #  ni srid-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  kyi phyir yongs su mi bsngo-ba # s dam-pa #  rnams kyis bsngags-pa # 'i phyir ro /
avyAbaDya kAya vAc samudAcAraH Atma utkarzaNa AdiBiH parezAm avajQA duHKa saMvAsena aGawwanAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  gnod-pa-med-pa #  ni bdag-la-bstod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s gzhan dag khyad du gsod cing 'grogs na mi-bde-ba # s zher-'debs-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Anulomika kAya vAc samudAcAraH nirvANa anuprApti anukUla tayA Arya mArga AvAhanAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  rjes-su-mthun-pa #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  thob-par-byed-pa #  dang mthun-pa # 'i phyir te / / 'phags-pa'i-lam #  'dren-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anucCavika kAya vAc samudAcAraH sva doza guNa AvizkamBaNa CAdana arTam
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  rjes su 'byor-ba #  ni rang-gi #  nyes-pa #  dang yon-tan #  sgrogs-pa #  dang mi-spyoms-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Opayika kAya vAc samudAcAraH sabrahmacArI upagrahaNa SIla tayA upagamana arha tvAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  thabs-dang-ldan-pa #  ni tshangs-pa #  mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa #  nye-bar #  sdud-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  yin pa'i phyir te / / nye-bar-'gro-ba # r bya-ba # 'i 'os yin pa'i phyir ro /
pratirUpa kAya vAc samudAcAraH guruzu guru sTAnIyezu ca nihita mAna tayA yaTArham upacaraNAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  'tsham ba ni bla-ma #  rnams dang bla-ma #  dang 'dra-ba #  rnams la nga-rgyal #  bcag pa'i phyir te / / ci-rigs-su #  bsnyen-bkur-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pradakziNa kAya vAc samudAcAraH avavAde pradakziNa grAhitayA svayaMdRzwi parAmarSa tvAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  mthun-pa #  ni gdams-ngag #  la mthun-par-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir te / / rang-gi #  lta-ba #  la mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atapta kAya vAc samudAcAraH kazwa tapaH lUha aDimukti vivarjita tayA anAtma tapa tvAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  gdung-ba #  med-pa #  ni dka'-thub-drag-po #  dang ngan don la mos-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir te / / bdag la gdung-ba # r mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ananuta api akAya vAc samudAcAraH samutsRzwAn BogAn karmAntAn= ca AraBya avipratisAritayA paScAt tApa aBAvAt
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  phyis 'gyod-pa-med-pa #  ni longs-spyod-pa #  rnams dang las-kyi-mtha' #  rnams spang-pa #  la brtsams nas 'gyod-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir te / / phyis 'gyod-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
avipratisAra kAya vAc samudAcAraH kuSala pakza mAraBya alpa mAtreNa asaMtuzwasyAH vipratisAri tayA yAvat Sakyam saMpAdanAt / karma svakam ezAm te ime karma svakAH / kaTam punar tezAm karma svakam Bavati
# lus dang ngag gi kun-tu-spyod-pa #  yid la gcags pa med-pa #  ni dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la brtsams nas cung-zad #  tsam gyis chog-par-mi-'dzin-pa # 'i yid la gcags pa med ba'i phyir te / / bsgrub nus-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o / / 'di dag gi las ni bdag-gir-bya-ba #  yin-pas #  'di dag ni las-bdag-gir-bya-ba #  dag go / / de-dag #  gi las-bdag-gir-bya-ba #  ji-lta-bu #  yin zhe na /
svayaMkRta karma vipAka pratisaMvedanatAm upAdAya tat hi nAma svakam iti ucyate yat parEH asADAraNam iti
# rang-gis-byas-pa # 'i las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  myong-ba # 'i phyir te / / gang gzhan dag dang thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  de ni bdag-gi #  zhes-bya'o #  /
karmANi dAyAyaH ezAm te ime karma dAyAdAH
# 'di dag ni las kyi bgo-skal-la-spyod-pa #  yin-pas #  'di dag ni las kyi bsgo skal la spyod-pa #  dag go /
kaTam karmaNAm dAyAda tvam
# ji-ltar #  na las kyi bgo-skal-la-spyod-pa #  nyid yin zhe na /
tasyAm svayaMkRta vipAka pratisaMvedanAyAm kuSala akuSalAnAm karmaNAm anyonya dAyAt atAm upAdAya yaTAsvam izwa anizwa Pala saMviBajanAt / te punar sva kRta karma izwa anizwa vipAka pratisaMvedinaH sattvAH kutas Aditas saMBUtAH kim ahetukAH Ahosvit prakRti ISvara Adi hetukAH iti Aha karma yonIyAH
# rang-gis-byas-pa # 'i las kyi rnams par smin-pa #  myong-ba #  de-la #  dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba #  so-so # 'i bgo-skal-la-spyod-pa # 'i phyir te / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / rang-rang-gi #  'bras-bu #  'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa #  'ged pa'i phyir ro / / rang-gis-byas-pa # 'i las la 'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa #  dag gi rnam-par-smin-pa #  myong-ba # 'i sems-can #  de-dag #  thog-ma #  ga las byung / / ci rgyu-med-pa #  las byung-ba #  zhig gam / / 'on te rang-bzhin #  dang dbang-phyug #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  zhig ce na / / smras-pa #  / / las kyi skyes gnas la dgag go /
karmevezAm ahetu vizama hetu varjitaH yoniH sattvAnAm saMBavAya iti arTaH
# 'di dag gi las nyid rgyu-med-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu #  rnams par spangs-pa # 'i skyes gnas te / / sems-can #  rnams 'byung-ba # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
evam tAvat pravRttim AraBya nivRttim api AraBya karma pratisaraNAH sa Asrava karma prahANAya anAsrava karma saMSrayaNAt karma eva ezAm pratisaraNam Bavati iti
# de-ltar #  'jug-pa #  las kyang brtsams ldog-pa #  las kyang brtsams nas las bstan-par-bya-ba #  dag ste / / zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i las spang-ba # 'i phyir zag-pa-med-pa # 'i las rten yin-pas #  / / 'di dag gi brten-par-bya-ba #  ni las nyid yin no /
yat uktam acintyaH sattvAnAm karma vipAkaH iti na sarvEH prakArEH a sAvacintyaH veditavyaH / kaTam tarhi cintyaH kaTam acintyaH
# sems-can #  rnams kyi las kyi rnam-par-smin-pa #  bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa # 'o zhes gang gsungs-pa #  de ni rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  yin par rig-par-bya # 'o / / bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ni ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
kuSala akuSalasya izwa anizwaH vipAkaH sugati durgatyoH iti cintyaH Sakya tvAt samyak dRzwi Adi guNa AvAhanAt ca
# dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  bde-'gro #  dang ngan-'gro # r 'dod-pa #  dang mi-'dod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ste / / nus-pa #  dang yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  'dren-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anena karmaNA sattvAnAm Atma BAvasya varNa saMsTAna Adi prakAra Beda vEcitryam iti acintyaH aSakyatvAt sarvajQAt anyasya unmAda Adi doza bAhanAt ca eva / tat eva karma sTAna AdiBiH acintyam
# las 'dis sems-can-rnams-kyi-lus #  kyi kha-dog #  dang dbyibs la-sogs-pa #  rnams pa tha-dad-pa #  sna-tshogs #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ste / / mi-nus-pa #  dang thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  las gzhan-pa #  mgo rmongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nyes-pa #  'dren-pa # 'i phyir ro / / dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las de nyid gnas la-sogs-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba # s ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo /
tatra sTAnam yatra pradeSe sTitvA yat karma kRtvA grAme vA nagare vA ityAdi
# de-la #  gnas ni grong ngam grong-khyer #  gyi phyogs gang-du #  gnas nas las de byas zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
vastu yat aDizWAnam sattva saMKyAtam asat saMKyAtam vA / hetuH kuSala akuSala AdeH kuSala akuSala mUlAni yaTAyogam / vipAkaH tat eva Atma BAva vEcitryam
# dngos-po #  ni sems-can #  gyi grangs-su-gtogs-pa # 'am / / sems-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i grongs su gtogs-pa #  gang-la #  brten-te #  byas-pa # 'o / / rgyu ni dge-ba #  dang mi-dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba rnams te / / ji-ltar #  mthun mthun sbyar ro / / rnam-par-smin-pa #  ni lus sna-tshogs-pa #  de nyid do /
bAhya BAva vEcitrya aBinirvartakam karma acintyam kIdRSena Kalu karmaNA kaNwaka AdInAm tEkzNa Adikam kRtam iti loka cintA nantarBUta tvAt
# sna-tshogs #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # r byed-pa # 'i las bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ni las ci-'dra-ba # s tsher-ma #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rno-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  byas-pa #  ste / / 'jig-rten #  gyis bsam-par-gtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
maNi mantra ozaDi muzwi yoga pratisaMyuktam karma acintyam / tatra maNi pratisaMyuktam candrakAnta AdInAm udaka kzaraNa Adi
# nor-bu #  dang sngas dang sman dang mkhyud spyod dang ldan-pa # 'i las bsam gyis mi khyab ste / / de-la #  nor-bu #  dang ldan-pa #  ni chu-shel #  la-sogs-pa #  las chu 'byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
mantra pratisaMyuktam tat aBimantritAn Ama dAha Adi
# sngags dang ldan-pa #  ni sngags de-dag #  gis btab-pa #  mi 'tshig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
OzaDi pratisaMyuktam tayA gRhIta yAntuH DAtA Adi
# sman dang ldan-pa #  ni des zin na mi-snang-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
muzwi yoga pratisaMyuktam tena tena muzwi yogena jvara apagama Adi
# mkhyud spyad dang ldan-pa #  ni mkhyud spyad de-dang-de # s rims-nad #  dang 'bral-bar-'gyur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
sarva ca yoginAm praBAva karma acintyam / kaTam
# rnal-'byor-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  mthu'i las bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
te citta praBAvena mahA pRTivI kampayanti AkASena vA utpatanti iti evamAdi
# de-dag #  gi sems kyi mthus sa-chen-po #  g-yo-ba # r byed-pa # 'am / / nam-mkha' #  la 'phur-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
boDisattvAnAm vaSitABiH yat kriyate karma tat acintyam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi dbang gi las la-sogs-pa # s las gang byed-pa #  de bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA AyuH vaSi tayA boDisattvAH AyuH saMskArAn aDizWAH ye yAvat icCanti tizWanti
# tshe la dbang-ba #  sa ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams tshe'i 'du-byed #  byin gyis brlabs nas ji-srid #  'dod-pa #  de srid du gnas so /
citta vaSitayA yaTecCam samADIn samApadyante parizkAra vaSitayA aprameyam anarDeyam upakaraNa varza sattvAnAm varzanti
# sems-la-dbang #  ni ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  ting-nge-'dzin #  la snyoms-pa # r 'jug go / / yo byang la dbang-ba # s ni sems-can-thams-cad #  la yo-byad #  rin che-ba #  dang dpag-tu-med-pa # 'i char 'bebs so /
karma vaSitayAni aDAtu BUmi gati yoni avasTA vedanIyAni karmANi anyaTA pariNAmayanti
# las la dbang-ba # s ni khams dang sa dang 'gro-ba #  dang skye-gnas #  dang gnas-skabs #  gzhan na myang-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'i las rnams gzhan-du #  bsgyur ro /
upapatti vaSi tayA DyAnEH api vihRtya aparihItAH eva kAmaDAtO= upapadyante / aDimukti vaSi tayA pRTak vyAdIna vAdi tvena aDimucyante
# skye-ba #  la dbang-ba # s ni bsam-gtan #  la gnas shing yongs su ma nyams bzhin-du #  'dod-pa'i-khams #  su skye'o / / mos-pa #  la dbang-ba # s ni sa la-sogs-pa # r chu la-sogs-pa # r mos so /
praNiDAna vaSitayA yaTezwam sva para arTa saMpatti karANi asaMKyeyAni mahA praNiDAnAni aBinirharanti
# smon-lam #  la dbang-ba # s ni ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i smon-lam-rgya-chen-po #  grangs-med-pa #  mngon-pa # r sgrub bo /
RdDi vaSi tayA sattvAnAm avaja na arTam aprameyam RdDi pratihArya saMdarSayanti
# rdzu-'phrul #  la dbang-ba # s ni sems-can #  rnams 'dun-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir rdzu-'phrul-gyi-cho-'phrul #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  kun-tu #  ston ston to /
jQAna vaSitayA Darma arTa nirukti pratiBAnAnAm prakarza paryantam gacCanti
# ye shes la dbang-ba # s ni chos-dang-don #  dang nges-pa'i-tshig #  dang spobs-pa #  rnams kyis rab kyi mthar-phyin-pa # r 'gro'o /
Darma vaSitayA yaTArham yAvat sarva satvAnAni anyEH nAma pada vyaMjana kAryaH sUtra AdIn DarmAn vyavasTApya yugapad citta paritozaNe samarTAH Bavanti iti
# chos la dbang-ba # s ni ci-rigs-par #  ji tsam du sems-can-thams-cad #  la ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs gzhan dang gzhan dag gis mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos rnam-pa # r bzhag nas cig-car-du #  sems yongs su tshim par byed-nus-pa # r 'gyur ro /
budDAnAm budDa kRtya anuzWAna karma acintyam / kaTam
# sangs-rgyas-thams-cad #  kyi sangs-rgyas-kyi-mdzad-pa #  bsgrub-pa # 'i 'phrin-las #  bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
anABoga pratigatAH Darma DAtu eka rasa tA sarve budDAH BagavantaH sattvAnAm yaTA yadA yAvat kRtyam anuzWAtavyam tat sarvam anutizWanti evam budDAnAm budDa vizayaH acintyaH
# sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  thams-cad #  lhun-gyis-grub-pa # r gtogs-pa # r thugs su chud cing chos-kyi-dbyings #  rog cig pa nyid-du #  gyur nas sems-can #  rnams la gang-gi-tshe #  dang ji-lta-bu #  dang ji-srid #  du mdzad-pa #  bsgrub-par-bya-ba #  de thams-cad #  rjes su gnas te / / de-ltar #  sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab bo /
punarBavasya vAsanAyAH AhArakam kAraNam iti hetuH
# yang-srid-pa # 'i bag-chags #  'jog-pa # 'i byed-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyu'o /
upacita vAsanAnAm sattvanAm deva Adi satva nikAye tad AkRti prakRti sAdRSyena samasya udayasya kAraNam iti samudayam
# sems-can #  bag-chags #  bsags-pa #  rnam-pa #  lha la-sogs-pa # 'i sems-can-gyi-ris #  su de'i cha byad dang rang-bzhin #  dang 'dra-bar #  mthun-par #  'byung-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni kun-'byung-ba # 'o /
pratyAtmaMsaMtA AnanEyaByena gati yoni Adi sarva prakArEH prakarzeNa yAvat Bava agra gatasya udBavasya kAraNam iti praBavaH
# so-so #  rang-gi-rgyud #  nges-pa #  dang 'gro-ba #  dang skye-gnas #  la-sogs-pa #  rnams dang mchog-tu #  'byung-ba # s srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i 'gro-ba # 'i bar-du #  'byung-ba # 'i byed-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rab-tu-skye-ba # 'o /
apUrvasya anyasya Atma BAvasya prAptO pUrva Atma BAvAtyayena kAraNam iti pratyayaH
# sngon ma-byung-ba # 'i lus gzhan dang gzhan 'thob-pa #  dang sngon 'thob-pa # 'i lus 'da' ba'i byed-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rkyen to /
saMskArANAm uparamAt sa niroDaH anyaH syAt tad asaMvaDyamAnaH arTa antara BUtaH syAt
# 'du-byed #  de-dag #  gi 'jig-pa #  las 'gog-pa #  de-dag #  gzhan zhig yin na ni 'brel-ba #  med de don gzhan-du #  'gyur ro /
aTa ananyaH syAt saMkleSa lakzaNaH syAt / atas eva na uBayaH na anuBayaH ca
# ji ste gzhan ma yin na ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du 'gyur te / / de'i-phyir #  gnyi-ga #  yang ma yin / / gnyi-ga #  yin pa yang ma yin no /
prapaQcaH punar asmin= arTe ayoniSaH cintya iti amArgeNa anyAyena anayena cintya iti arTaH anyaTA cintayitavye anyaTA cintanAt / kaTam punar cintyaH / SAntaH praNItaH iti evamAdiBiH prakArEH
# spros-pa #  ni skabs 'dir tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # r sems-pa #  yin te zhes-bya-ba #  ni lam ma-yin-pa #  dang / / rigs ma-yin-pa #  dang thabs-ma-yin-pa # r sems-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / sems-pa #  yang gzhan-las #  sems-pa # r bya-ba #  yang gzhan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sems-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na / / zhi-ba #  dang gya-nom-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis so; /
niralaMkAraH prajQA viktAnAm vidyA Adi vESezika guNa alaMkAra aBAvAt
# rgyan med-pa #  ni shes-rab #  kyi cha las rnam-par-grol-ba #  rnams kyi yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  rigs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyan med-pa # 'i rgyan med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
paryAyataH aSeza prahANam iti uddeSaH SezaH nirdeSaH / atas eva tad pariSizwAni padAni upAdAya iti ucyate tEH tasya nirdeSAt
# rnam-grangs #  kyi sa ni ma-lus-par-spangs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bstan-pa # 'o / / lhag-ma #  ni bshad-pa # 'o / / de'i-phyir #  de'i tshig lhag-ma #  rnams kyis phyir ro zhes brjod de; de-dag #  gi de bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam kRtvA aSeza prahANam / paryavasTAna anuSaya prahANAt

# de-la #  nges-par #  spangs-pa #  ni kun-nas-dkris-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / 'byung-ba #  yongs su spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vyantIBAvaH anuSaya prahANam mUla aBAve atyantam anutpAdAt
# byang-ba # r gyur-pa #  ni bag-la-nyal #  spangs-pa #  ste / / rtsa ba med na gtan mi-skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tad punar darSana BAvanA mArga pratipakza BedAt dviDA vyavasTApyate kzayaH virAgaH iti
# de ni gnyen-po #  mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyi bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-gnyis #  su rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / zad-pa #  dang 'dod-chags #  dang bral zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
tatra darSana mArgeNa virAgatAm aDikRtya kzayaH alpa mAtra avaSizwa tvAt kleSa rASeH / BAva nAma argeNa virAgaH tasya BUmi vErAgya gamana praviBAvita tvAt
# de-la #  zad-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis bral-ba-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa # 'i tshogs cung-zad #  tsam zhig lus pa'i phyir ro / / 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyis bral-ba-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
tad uBaya visaMyoge punar satyAyatyAm ca duHKam niruDyate anutpatti Darma tA ApAdanAt / dRzwe ca Darme dOrmanasyam vyupaSAmyati asamudA AcArAt
# de ni sa la 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid-du #  'gyur-ba # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de gnyis kyis bral-ba # r gyur na mi-skye-ba'i-chos #  nyid-du #  byas-pa # s phyi-ma-la #  sdug-bsngal #  'gog-pa #  dang kun du mi-'byung-ba # s mthong-ba # 'i chos la yid-mi-bde-ba #  rnam-par-zhi-ba # r 'gyur te /
atas tad Pala BUtasya duHKasya prahANam aDikRtya Aha niroDaH vyupaSamaH iti / pUrva karma kleSa samudAgatAnAm tu sattvAnAm sva rasena eva uparamam aDikRtya Aha astaMgamaH iti
# de'i-phyir #  de'i 'bras-bu # r gyur ba sdug-bsngal #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  spong pa'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  'gog-pa #  dang rnam-pa # r zhi bzhes-bya-ba #  smos so / / sngon-gyi-las #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # s yang-dag-par-bsgrub-pa # 'i phung-po #  rnams ni rang-gi-ngang-gis #  'jig-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  nub-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
evam kRtvA aSeza prahANam nirdizwam veditavyam

durdRSam Aryasya eva ekasya prajQA cakzuzaH gocara tvAt
# blta dka'-ba #  ni 'phags-pa #  gcig-pu # 'i shes-rab #  kyi spyan gyi spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
acalam naraka Adi gati asaMcAreNa sTira tvAt

trANam tad prAptO jAti Adi sarva upadrava apagamanAt
# skyob pa ni de thob na skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnod-pa #  thams-cad-la # s bzlog-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# mgon ni de'i bsam-pa #  dang sbyor-ba-byas-pa #  'bras-bu-yod-pa # 'i gzhi'i-gnas #  yin-pas #  rten yin pa'i phyir ro /
parAyaNam paramasya Arya tvasya AgamanAya pada sTAna tvAt arhati tva prApti upAya alaMkbana tvAt iti arTaH / acyutam ajAta tvena BraMsA saMBavAt / nirjvaram sarva icCA viGAta saMtApa aBAvAt
# dpung gnyen ni 'phags-pa'i-mchog #  nyid-du #  'gro-ba # 'i gzhi'i-gnas #  yin pa'i phyir to / / dgra-bcom-pa-nyid #  'thob-pa'i-thabs #  la dmigs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / 'chi-'pho #  med-pa #  ni ma-skyes-pa # s nyams-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rims-nad #  med-pa #  ni 'dod-pas-phongs-pa # 'i gdung-ba #  thams-cad-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nizparidAham Soka Adi sarva paridAha pratiprasrabDyA SItala tvAt
# yongs-su-gdung-ba #  med-pa #  ni mya-ngan #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yongs-su-gdung-ba #  thams-cad #  rgyun-chad-pa # s bsil ba'i phyir ro /
kzemam vyADi jarA maraNa Baya rahitArya vihAra ASraya tvAt
