Arogyam kleSa Adi AvaraNa roga rahita tvAt
# nad-med-pa #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrib-pa-dang-bral-ba # 'i phyir ro /
AniQjyam sarva vizaya prapaQca vikzepa rahita tvAt
# mi g-yo-ba #  ni yul gyi spros-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba thams-cad #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir ro /
nirvANam rUpa Adi saMjQA apagamasya SAnta suKa vihArasya alaMkbana tvAt / punar niroDa satyam AraBya ajAta AdayaH paryAyAH duHKa lakzaNa viparyaya arTena veditavyAH / duKam hi tatra tatra sattva nikAye pratisaMDi banDena jAyate / tatas uttara kAlam Atma BAva paripUryAH varDate
# mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  thams-cad #  dang bral te zhi zhing bde-bar-gnas-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / yang 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  la brtsams nas / / ma-skyes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  rnams te / / sdug-bsngal-gyi-mtshan-nyid #  las bzlog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / sdug-bsngal #  ni sems-can-gyi-ris #  de-dang-der #  nyid mtshams-sbyor-ba # r byed-pa # s skye-ba # 'o / / de'i-'og-tu #  lus-yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r 'phel lo /
tat ca duHKam pUrva karma kleSa AveDena kRtam / tat ca vartamAnam duHKam karma kleSAnAm ca anya Bava saMskaraNe pada sTAnam Bavati
# sdug-bsngal #  de-yang #  sngon-gyi-las #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # s 'phangs te byas-pa #  ni da-ltar-gyi-las #  dang nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyis srid-pa #  gzhan-du #  byed-pa # 'i gzhi'i-gnas #  yin te /
tatas avyucCeda yogena punarBavasya saMtati utpAdaH Bavati / atas tad viparyayeNa duHKa niroDaH Arya satyam yaTAkramam ajAtam aBUtam akRtam asamutpannam veditavyam / api Kalu niroDa satyam aDikRtya
# de'i rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  yang-srid-pa # 'i rgyun skye-bar-'gyur #  ro / / de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  'gog-pa #  'phags-pa'i-bden-pa #  ste / / ma-skyes-pa #  dang ma-byung-ba #  dang ma-byas-pa #  dang 'dus-ma-byas #  pa dang skyes-pa #  med-pa #  dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / yang 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa-bzhi # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / 'gog-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams dang bral-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o /
SAnta lakzaNam saMskAra duHKa tayA apraSAnta lakzaNAnAm upAdAna skanDAnAm visaMyogam aDikRtya
# zhi-ba'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  nyid kyis ma-zhi-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga rnams dang bral-ba # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o /
praNIta lakzaNam kleSa duHKa visaMyogAt svayam Suci suKa svaBAva tAm aDikRtya
# gya-nom-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir / / bdag-nyid #  gtsang ba dang bde-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa # 'o /
niHsaraNa lakzaNam nitya hita svaBAva tAm aDikRtya apunar AvartanAt kzema tvAt ca yaTAkramam hitam kuSalam iti Sakya tvAt
# nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rtag-pa #  dang phan-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / yang phyir-mi-ldog-pa #  dang bde-ba # 'i phyir phan-pa-dang-bde-ba #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
mArga satyam yena duKam parijAnIta iti evamAdi satyezu asya kRtya aDikAreNa lakzaNa nirdeSaH veditavyaH
# lam gyi bden-pa #  ni gang-gis #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / bden-pa #  rnams la 'di'i bya-ba # 'i skabs kyis mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
paQcaviDaH mArgaH iti praBeda aDikAreNa
# lam rnam-pa-lnga #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rab-tu-dbye-ba #  lnga'i skabs kyi'o /
paQca praBedaH sa parivAra mArga satya aDikArAt veditavyam
# rab-tu-dbye-ba #  'di yang lam gyi bden-pa #  'khor dang bcas-pa # 'i skabs kyis rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra saMBAra mArgaH SIla AdikaH yasya paripUrNa tvAt Uzma gata Adi AnupUrvyA satya darSanAya tad AvaraNa prahANAya ca saMtAnasya yogya tAm pratilaBate iti
# de-la #  tshogs kyi lam ni tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / de yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # s dro-bar-gyur-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i go-rims-kyis #  bden-pa-mthong-ba # r bya-ba #  dang de-la #  sgrib-pa #  spangs bar bya-ba # 'i phyir sems-kyi-rgyud #  'os su gyur-pa #  'thob bo /
yat vA punar anyat Opanizadam kuSalam iti avipratisAra Adikam veditavyam
# gang yang rgyur-gyur-pa # 'i dge-ba #  gzhan zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'gyod-pa-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
uzma gatam pratyAtmam satyezu Aloka labDaH samADiH prajQA sa saMyogaH iti samAhitena cittena satya aDipateyasya sUtra Adikasya Darmasya manaH jalpasya muKEH arTa saMpraKyAne sati SamaTaH ca vipaSyanA ca Uzma gatam iti veditavyam
# dro-bar-gyur-pa #  ni so-so #  rang-gis #  bden-pa #  rnams la snang-ba #  thob-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  shes-rab #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  bden-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'i chos mdo-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  yid kyis brjod-pa # 'i sgo nas don snang-bar-gyur-pa # 'i zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  ni dro-bar-gyur-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tad vRdDiH mUrDAnaH tad upari vyavasTApana arTena
# de 'phel pa ni rtse mo ste / / de'i gang na rnam-par-gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kzAntiH eka deSa pravizwa anusRtaH samADiH iti
# bzod-pa #  ni phyogs-gcig #  la zhugs-pa #  dang rjes-su-song-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  zhes-bya-ba #  la /
kaTam eka deSa pravizwaH Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na phyogs-gcig #  la zhugs-pa #  yin zhe na /
ekAntena grAhya BAva lakzaNAt
# gcig-tu #  gzung-ba #  med-pa # r bzod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam eka deSa anumRtaH grAhaka aBAva prativeDA anukUlya avasTAnAt
# ji-ltar #  na phyogs-gcig #  gi rjes-su-song-ba #  yin zhe na / / 'dzin-pa #  med-pa # r rtog-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # r gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
lOkikaH agraDarmaH yat antaram Aditas lokottaraH mArgaH
# 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog ni gang-gi #  'og-tu #  thog-mar #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam mo /
darSana mArgaH lOkika agra Darma anantaram nirvikalpa SamaTa vipaSyana alakzaNaH veditavyaH
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog gi 'og gi rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  gi mtshan-nyid #  du rig-par-bya # 'o /
sama samAlaMbya alaMbana jQAnam api tat iti tena grAhya grAhaka aBAva taTatA prativeGAt / pratyAtmam apanIta sattva saMketa Darma saMketa sarvatas apanIta uBaya saMketa alaMbana Darma jQAnam api tat iti / kaTam pratyAtmam apanIta sattva saMketa alaMkabana Darma jQAnam
# dmigs-par-bya-ba #  dang dmigs-par-byed-pa #  mnyam-pa # s mnyam-pa # r shes-pa # 'ang de-bzhin #  te zhes-bya-ba #  ni des gzungs ba dang 'dzin-pa #  med-pa # 'i de-bzhin-nyid #  rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / so-so #  rang la sems-can #  gyi brda dang chos kyi brda gsal-ba #  dang thams-cad-du #  gnyi-ga # 'i brda gsal pa dmigs-pa # 'i chos-shes-pa #  'ang de yin no zhes-bya-ba #  la / / sems-can #  gyi brda so-so #  rang-gis #  gsal-ba #  la dmigs-pa # 'i chos-shes-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
tena svasantAne Atma nimitta avikalpanAt
# des rang-gi-rgyud #  la bdag-gi #  mtshan-ma # r rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam pratyAtmam apanIta Darma saMketa alaMbana Darma jQAnam
# so-so #  rang la chos kyi brda gsal-ba #  la dmigs-pa # 'i chos-shes-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
tena sva saMtAnaH eva rUpa Adi Darma nimitta avikalpanAt
# des rang-gi-rgyud #  nyid la gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # r rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam sarvatas apanIta uBaya saMketa alaMbana Darma jQAnam
# thams-cad-du #  gnyi-ga # 'i brda gsal-ba #  la dmigs-pa # 'i chos-shes-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
sarvatra aviSezeNa Atma Darma nimitta avikalpanAt iti / praBedaSas punar darSana mArgaH satyezu zoXa SaDarma anvaya kzAnti jQAnAni
# thams-cad-du #  bye-brag-med-par #  bdag dang chos-kyi-mtshan-ma #  la rnams par mi-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang mthong-ba'i-lam #  la rab-tu-dbye-ba #  na bden-pa #  rnams pa bcu drug ste / / chos dang rjes-su-rtog-pa #  la bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  rnams so /
tatra duHKe Darma jQAna kzAntiH prayoga mArge duHKa satya aDikArika sUtra Adi Darma vicAraNA jQAnam yoniSas manaskAra saMgRhItam aDipati kRtvA sva saMtAnika duHKa satye tad taTatA pratyakza anuBAvinaH loka uttarA prajQA samyak dRzwi svaBAva utpadyate yayA duHKa darSana prahAtavyAn= trEDAtukAnazwAviMSatim anuSayAn prajahAti
# de-la #  sdug-bsngal #  la chos-shes-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  ni sbyor-ba'i-lam #  la / / sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'i mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos la rnam-par-dpyod-pa # 'i shes-pa #  ste / / tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa # s bsdus-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  rang-gi-rgyud #  la yod-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la de'i de-bzhin-nyid #  mngon-sum-du #  'gyur-pa # 'i 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i shes-rab #  yang-dag-par-lta-ba # 'i rang-bzhin #  'byung ste / / des sdug-bsngal #  mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  khams-gsum-pa # 'i bag-la-nyal #  nye shu rtsa brgyad rab tu spang ngo /
tasmAt ucyate duHKe Darma jQAna kzAntiH iti / tayA kzAntyA duHKa darSana prahAtavya kleSa prahANAt parivartitaH ASraye tad anantaram yena jQAnena tAm ASraya parivRtti pratyanuBavati tad duHKe Darma jQAnam iti ucyate
# de-bas-na #  sdug-bsngal #  la chos-shes-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  zhes-bya'o # ; / / bzod-pa #  des sdug-bsngal #  mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  spang-ba # 'i phyir gnas gyur nas de ma-thag-tu #  shes-pa #  gang-gi #  gnas gyur ba de myong-ba #  de ni sdug-bsngal #  la chos-shes-pa #  zhe bya'o /
etat ca uBayam Adyam kzAnti jQAnam anvayaH sarvezAm SEkzA SEkzANAm Arya DarmANAm tatas tezAm samudAgamAt
# dang-po # 'i bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  'di gnyis ni slong-ba #  dang slob-pa # 'i 'phags-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi rgyu yin te / / de-la # s de-dag #  yang-dag-par #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atas tad AlaMbya anvayaH ezaH Arya DarmANAm iti pratyAtmam pratyakza anuBAvinti anAsravAH prajQAH duHKe anvaya jQAna kzAnti
# de'i-phyir #  'di gnyis ni 'phags-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  kyi rgyu'o zhes de-la #  dmigs nas so-so #  rang la mngon-sum-du #  'gyur-ba # 'i zag-pa-med-pa # 'i shes-rab #  ni sdug-bsngal #  la rjes-su-rtog-pa # r shes-pa # 'i bzod-pa # 'o /
tAm anvaya jQAna kzAntim yena jQAnena pratyanuBavati tad anvaya jQAnam iti ucyate
# rjes-su-rtog-pa # r shes-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  dang de shes-pa #  gang-gis #  myong-ba #  de ni rjes-su-rtog-pa # 'i shes-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
lokottarasya hi mArgasya dvayam vizayaH taTatA samyak jQAnam ca
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyi yul ni gnyis te / / de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes so /
tatra Darma jQAna pakzasya mArgasya taTatA vizayaH
# de-la #  chos-shes-pa # 'i phyogs kyi lam gyi yul ni de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
anvaya jQAna pakzasya samyak jQAnam
# rjes-su-rtog-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'i phyogs kyi yul ni yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes so /
atas idam ucyate Darma jQAna kzAnti jQAnEH grAhya avaboDaH anvaya kzAnti jQAnEH grAhaka avaboDaH iti
# de'i-phyir #  'di skad ces bya ste chos-shes-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  rnams kyis ni gzung-ba #  rtogs so / / rjes-su-rtog-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  rnams kyis ni 'dzin so [?] rtogs so zhes-bya'o #  /
yaH BagavatA zazWaH animitta vihArI pudgalaH AKyAtaH saH etezu kzAnti jQAnezu vartamAnaH veditavyaH sarva nimitta anupalamBAt
# bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis gang mtshan-ma-med-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'i gang-zag #  drug bka'-stsal-pa #  / / de ni bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  de-dag #  la gnas-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  mi dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
te ete kzAnti jQAna saMgRhItAH zoXaSa cittakzaNAH darSana mArgaH tEH adRzwa pUrvANAm Aryasa tyAnAm pratyekam caturBiH darSanAt
# bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa # s bsdus-pa #  sems-kyi-skad-cig #  bcu drug-po #  'di dag ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  ste / / de-dag #  gis sngon ma-mthong-ba # 'i 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa #  re-re #  la yang rnam-pa-bzhi #  bzhir mthong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
na ca atra BAvasya aBatvA prAdurBAva mAtram citta kzaNaH veditavyaH
# 'dir dngos-po #  ma-byung-ba #  byung-ba #  tsam la sems-kyi-skad-cig #  tu rig-par-bya-ba #  ni ma yin gyi /
kim tarhi yAvatA jQeye jQAnAt patteH parisamAptiH Bavati
# ji tsam du shes-bya #  la shes-pa #  'byung-ba #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  la bya ste /
tat yaTA duHKam parijQeyam iti ekaH citta lakzaNaH / evam samudayaH prahAtavyaH iti evamAdiH
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / sdug-bsngal #  ni yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems-kyi-skad-cig #  gcig go / / kun 'byung ni spang-ba # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  yang de-bzhin #  no /
yat ca etat darSana mArgam AraBya vistareNa vipaMcittam vyavasTAna mAtram tat sarvam veditavyam pratyAtmam eva vedanIya tvAt lokottarAyAH avasTAyAH
# gang mthong-ba'i-lam #  las brtsams te / / rgya-cher #  rnam-pa # r spros-pa #  de thams-cad #  ni rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  tsam du rig-par-bya #  ste / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  ni so-so #  rang-gis #  rig-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sarvam hi mArga satyam caturBiH prakArEH anugantavyam vyavasTAnataH vikalpanataH anuBavataH paripUritaH ca
# lam gyi bden-pa #  thams-cad #  ni rnam-pa-bzhi # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang myong-ba #  dang yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'o /
tatra vyavasTAnata yaTAsvam aDigamanizWA prAptA SrAvaka AdayaH tad pRzWa labDena jQAnena parezAm prApaNa nimittam nAma pada vyaQjana kAyEH mArga satyam vyavasTApayanti iti api satyezu kzAntayaH jQAnAni iva ityAdi
# de-la #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa # s ji-ltar #  rang-gi #  khong-du-chud-pa #  mthar-phyin #  nas / / de'i-rjes-la #  thob-pa # 'i shes-pa # s gzhan dag la go-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs rnams kyis lam gyi bden-pa #  rnam-pa # r 'jog ste / / bden-pa #  rnams la bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  ni 'di-lta-bu # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
vikalpanataH aBisamaya prayuktAH lOkikena yaTA vyavasTAnam vikalpayataH yat aByasya nti
# rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  la zhugs-pa # 'i 'jig-rten-pa # 'i shes-pa # s ji-ltar #  rnam-pa # r bzhag-pa #  bzhin-du #  rnam-pa # r rtog cing goms-par-byed-pa # 'o /
anuBavataH taTA aByasyantaH yAma Aditas darSana mArga AKyAm loka uttarAm nizprapaQca avasTAm pratyAtmam anuBavanti paripUritaH tad UrDva yAma ASraya parivRttim paripUrya yAvat aDigamanizWAm prApnuvanti
# myong-ba #  ni de-ltar #  goms-par-byed-pa #  na mthong-ba'i-lam #  zhes brjod-pa # 'i 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  gang-yin-pa # s dang-po #  so-so # r rang-gis #  myong-ba # 'o / / yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  ni de'i-'og-tu #  gnas-gyur-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-nas #  thob-pa #  mthar-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  'thob-pa # 'o /
te punar aDigamanizWA prAptAH tat pRzWa labDena jQAnena mArga satyam vyavasTApayanti / iti evamAdi tat caturAkAram mArgacakram punar punar anyonya ASrayeNa pravartate iti veditavyam
# thob-pa #  mthar-phyin-pa #  de-dag #  ni de'i-rjes-la #  thob-pa # 'i shes-pa # s lam gyi bden-pa #  rnam-pa # r 'jog go / / de-ltar-na #  rnam-pa #  'di bzhi ni lam gyi 'khor-lo #  ste / / yang-dang-yang #  gzhan dang gzhan la brten-nas #  'jug-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
yat uktam virajaH vigata malam Darmezu Darma cakzuH utpadyate iti tad darSana mArgam aDikRtya uktam tat praTamatas satyezu Arya prajQA cakzuH svaBAva tvAt
# chos-rnams #  la chos kyi mig rdul-med #  cing dri-ma-dang-bral-ba #  skyes so zhes-bya-ba #  gang gsungs-pa #  de ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi dbang du mdzad nas gsungs-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  de ni thog-ma-kho-nar #  bden-pa #  rnams la 'phags-pa # 'i shes-rab #  kyi spyan gyi rang-bzhin #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra Darma kzAntiBiH virajaH tABiH kleSa rajaH prahANAt
# de-la #  chos la bzod-pa #  rnams kyis ni rdul-med #  de / / de-dag #  gis nyon-mongs-pa'i-rdul #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
Darma jQAnEH vigata malam tezAm prahANa tad AvaraNa mala ASraya utpAdAt
# chos-shes-pa #  rnam ba ni dri-ma #  dang bral ste / / de-dag #  ni de'i sgrib-pa # 'i dri-ma #  spangs-pa # 'i gnas su skyes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar anayoH eva kzAnti jQAna avasTayoH yaTAkramam parijQayA prahANena ca mArgasya viSudDa tAm aDikRtya virajaH vigata malam veditavyam
# yang bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  'di gnyis ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  dang spangs-pa # 'i lam gyi rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas #  ba ste / / rdul-med-pa #  dang dri-ma-dang-bral-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
dRzwA iti evamAdi api darSana mArgam eva aDikRtya veditavyam vineyAnAm satya aBisamaya anantaram vacanAt
# chos mthong-ba #  zhes pa la-sogs-pa #  yang mthong pa'i lam nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / 'dul-ba #  rnams bden-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i 'og-tu #  gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra Darma kzAntiBiH dRzwa DarmAH tABiH tattva prativeDAt
# de-la #  chos la bzod-pa #  rnams kyis ni chos mthong-ste #  de-dag #  gis de-kho-na-rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Darma jQAnEH prApta DarmAH tEH ASraya parivRtti sAkzAt karaNAt
# chos-shes-pa #  rnams kyis chos thob ste / / chos-shes-pa #  rnams kyi gnas-gyur-pa #  mngon-sum-du #  thob-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anvayakza antiBiH vidita DarmAH tABiH Arya Darma anvayaH ezaH iti tad uBaya saMvedanAt / anvaya jQAnEH paryavagAXa DarmAH tEH yAvat jQeyam parisamApanAt
# rjes-su-rtog-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  rnams kyis chos rig ste / / de-dag #  gis 'di ni 'phags-pa # 'i chos kyi rgyu'o zhes de gnyis rig-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rjes-su-rtog-pa # 'i shes-pa #  rnams kyis chos rtogs te / / de-dag #  gis shes-bya #  ji-snyed-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sarvEH tIrNa kAMkzaH sarvEH kzAnti jQAnEH lokottareNa mArgeNa Pala aDigame sati dIrGarAtram aBikAMkzite sva aDigame asaMdehAt
# bzod-pa #  dang shes-pa #  thams-cad-kyi # s som nyi las brgal-te #  / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyi 'bras-bu #  thob-pa # s yun-ring-po-nas #  'dod-pa #  rang-gis #  thob-pa #  la the-tshom-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tIrNa vicikitsaH pariDi game sarvEH iti vartate para aDigame tad avasTasya anyezAm api viSeza aDigamam prati vimatya BAvAt
# thams-cad-kyi #  gzhan gyis thob-pa #  la the-tshom #  las brgal-te #  / / de'i dus na gzhan dag gis kyang khyad-par-thob-pa #  la yid-gnyis-za-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
apara pratyayaH mArga BAvanAyAm para upadeSam antareNa api svayaMkuSala tvAt
# lam bsgom-pa #  la gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog-pa #  ni gzhan la lung-mnos-pa #  med-pa # r yang bdag-nyid-kyis #  mkhas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ananyaneyaH avetya prasAda pratilaBena SAstuH SAsane anya tIrTyEH janma antare api ahArya tvAt / Darmezu vESAradya prAptaH aDigamam AraBya paripraSna Darmezu pApa icCA aBimAnika vat avalIna citta tA BAvAt / BAvanA mArgaH lOkikaH mArgaH
# gzhan gyis mi bkri pa ni shes-nas #  dang pa thob-pa # s gzhan mu-stegs-can #  rnams kyis tshe-rabs-gzhan #  la yang ston-pa # 'i bstan-pa #  las mi-'phrogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / chos-rnams #  la 'jigs-pa #  thob-pa #  ni thob-pa #  las brtsams nas yongs-su-dri-ba # 'i chos-rnams #  dang lung bstan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  la sdig-pa #  'dod-pa #  mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal-can #  bzhin-du #  sems-zhum-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bam po drug-pa #  / / bsgom-pa'i-lam #  ni 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  bden-pa #  rnams mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i'o / / de'i-gong-du #  gyur-pa #  ni kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  lhag-ma #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir zhugs-pa #  ste / / gang 'jig-rten-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i lam mo /
tatra lOkikaH mArgaH DyAnAni ArUpyAH ca
# de-la #  'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  ni bsam-gtan #  rnams dang gzugs-med-pa #  rnams so /
te punar DyAna ArUpyAH saMkleSataH vyavadAnataH vyavasTAnataH viSudDitaH ca veditavyAH / kaTam saMkleSataH
# bsam-gtan #  dang gzugs-med-pa #  de-dag #  kyang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  dang rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  dang rnam-par-dag-pa # s rig-par-bya # 'o / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # s ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
catvAri avyAkRta mUlAni tRzNA dRzwiH mAnaH avidyA ca tEH saMklizwa cittAnAm klizwa DyAna muKena rUpa ArUpya avara sarva nivRta avyAkRta kleSa upakleSa AvartanAt
# lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i rtsa ba bzhi-po #  sred-pa #  dang lta-ba #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang ma-rig-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  gis sems kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  can du gyur ba rnams kyi nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bsam-gtan #  gyi sgo nas gzugs dang gzugs med na spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad #  bsgribs-pa # 'i lung du mi ston-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tatra tRzNayA AsvAda saMkleSena saMkliSyate prasrabDi suKa AsvAdAt
# de-la #  sred-pa # s ni ro myang-ba # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # s kun nas nyon mongs te / / shin-tu #  sbyangs ba'i bde-ba # 'i ro-myong-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dRzwyA dRzwi uttara DyAyitayA saMkliSyate DyAnam niScitya pUrva anta kalpa Adi dRzwi samutTApanAt
# lta-ba # s ni lta-ba #  shas-che-ba # 'i bsam-gtan-pa #  nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs te / / bsam-gtan #  la brten-nas #  sngon-gyi-mtha' #  la rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
mAnena mAna uttara DyAyitayA saMkliSyate tena viSeza aDigamena unnati gamanAt
# nga-rgyal #  gyis ni nga-rgyal #  gyi shas-che-ba # 'i bsam-gtan-pa #  nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs te / / des khyad-par #  du thob na khengs-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
avidyayA vicikitsA uttara DyAyitayA saMkliSyate tat tvA prativeDena mokza kAmasya tasmin viSeza aDigame mokzaH na mokzaH iti vicikitsotpAdanAt
# ma-rig-pa #  ni the-tshom #  gyi shas-che-ba # 'i bsam-gtan-pa #  nyid kyis kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  ste / / de-kho-na #  ma-gtogs-pa # s thar-pa-'dod-pa #  khyad-par #  de thob-pa #  la thar-pa #  yin nam ma yin snyam-du #  the-tshom-skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam vyavadAnataH / SudDakAH DyAna ArUpyAH lOkikAH api kuSala tvAt paryavasTAnam alApa gata tvena vyavadAtA iti ucyante
# rnam-par-byang-ba #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na dag-pa # 'i bsam-gtan #  dang gzugs-med-pa #  'jig-rten-pa #  rnams kyang dge-ba # 'i phyir kun-nas-dkris-pa # 'i dri-ma-dang-bral-ba # s na rnam-par-byang-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
kaTam vyavasTAnataH / DyAnAnAm tAvat caturDA vyavasTAnam aFga samApatti mAtrA saMjQA karaNa BedAt
# rnam-par-gzhag-pa # s ji-lta-bu #  zhe na bsam-gtan #  rnams ni yan-lag #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dang tshad dang ming-du-gdags-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-bzhi # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
ArUpyANAm triDA aFga varjEH
# gzugs-med-pa #  rnams ni yan-lag #  ma-gtogs-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  mo /
kim punar aDikRtya DyAnezu / vitarka AdayaH eva aFga tvena vyavasTApitAH sat svanyezu Darmezu
# gang-gi #  dbang-du-byas-nas #  chos gzhan dag kyang yod-bzhin-du #  rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  kho-na #  bsam-gtan #  rnams la yan-lag #  nyid-du #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na /
tAvadBiH pratipakza anuSaMsa tad uBaya ASraya aFga parisamApteH
# de tsam gyis gnyen-po #  dang phan yon dang de-gnyi-ga # 'i gnas kyi yan-lag #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
praTame tAvat DyAne vitarkaH vicAraH ca pratipakza aFgam tAByAm kAma vyApAda vihiMsA vitarka Adi prahANAt
# bsam-gtan-dang-po #  la rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa #  ni gnyen-po # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / de gnyis kyis 'dod-pa #  dang gnod-sems #  dang 'tshe-ba # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
prItiH suKam ca anuSaMsa aFgam vitarka vicArAByAm pratipakzite vipakze tad viveka ja prIti suKa lABAt
# dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  ni phan yon gyi yan-lag #  ste / / rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa #  gnyis kyis gnyen-po #  byas-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  de-la # s dben-pa-las-skyes-pa # 'i dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
citta ekAgra tA tad uBaya niSraya aFgam samADi saMniSraya balena vitarka Adi pravRtteH iti
# sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni de-gnyi-ga # 'i gnas kyi yan-lag #  ste / / ting-nge-'dzin #  la brten-pa # 'i stobs kyis rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
taTA dvitIye DyAne aDyAtma saMprasAdaH pratipakza aFgam tena vitarka vicAra pratipakzaNAt
# de-bzhin-du #  bsam-gtan-gnyis-pa #  la nang rab tu dang-ba #  ni gnyen-po # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / de rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prIti suKe citta ekAgra tA ca Seze aFge pUrvavat
# dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni yan-lag #  lhag-ma #  gnyis la snga-ma-bzhin #  no /
tRtIye DyAne upekzA smRtiH saMprajanyaH ca pratipakzAFgam tEH prIti pratipakzaNAt
# bsam-gtan #  gsum-pa #  la btang-snyoms #  dang ngan-pa #  dang shes-bzhin #  ni gnyen-po # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / de-dag #  dga'-ba # 'i gnyen-po #  byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
suKam citta ekAgra tA ca Seze aFge yaTAkramam
# bde-ba #  dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni yan-lag #  lhag-ma #  gnyis dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
caturTe DyAne upekzA pariSudDiH smRti pariSudDiH ca pratipakza aFgam tAByAm suKa pratipakzaNAt / aduHKa asuKA vedanA anuSaMsa aFgam
# bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa #  la btang-snyoms #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  dang dran-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  ni gnyen-po # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / de gnyis bde-ba # 'i gnyen-po #  byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa #  ni phan yon gyi yan-lag #  go /
citta ekAgra tA tad uBaya aFgam iti
# sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni de-gnyi-ga # 'i gnas kyi yan-lag #  go; /
kaTam punar praTamam DyAnam samApadyamAnasya sapta manaskArAH Bavanti
# ji-ltar #  na bsam-gtan-dang-po #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  bdun du 'gyur zhe na /
yena samAhita BUmikena manaskAreNa kamezu AdIn avAdi darSanena OdArika lakzaNam pratisavedayate / tad aBAvAt ca praTama DyAne SAnta lakzaNam
# mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sa pa'i yid-la-byed-pa #  gang-gi #  'dod-pa #  rnams la nyes-dmigs #  la-sogs-pa # r lta-ba # s rags-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  rab tu rig-pa #  ste / / de med-pa # 'i phyir bsam-gtan-dang-po #  la zhi-ba'i-mtshan-nyid #  do /
ayam ucyate lakzaNa pratisaMvedanIya manaskAraH sa ca Sruta cintA vyavakIrNaH veditavyaH
# 'di ni mtshan-nyid #  rab tu rig-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes bya ste / / de ni thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  dang 'dres-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tat UrDva Srutam cintAm ca atikramya ekAntena BAvanA kAreNa tat OdArika SAnta lakzaNa nimitta alaMkanAm SamaTa vipaSyanAm BAvayan punar punar yaTAparyezita AmOdArika SAnta tAm aDimucyate iti ayam aDimokzikaH
# de'i-'og-tu #  thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  las 'das nas gcig-tu #  bsgom-pa'i-rnam-pa # s de'i rags-pa #  dang zhi-ba'i-mtshan-nyid #  kyis mtshan-ma #  la dmigs-pa # 'i zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  bsgom zhing yang ji-ltar #  yongs su bsal-ba #  rags-pa #  dang zhi-ba #  nyid-du #  mos te / / 'di ni mos-pa-las-byung-ba #  zhes ba'o /
tad aByAsAt tad praTamatas prahANa mArga sahagataH manaskAraH prAvivekyaH tena aDimAtra kleSa prakAra prahANAt tad pakza dOzWulya apagamAt ca eva
# de goms-pa # s thog-ma-kho-nar #  spong-ba # 'i lam dang ldan-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  ni rab-tu-dben-pa #  las byung-ba #  ste; des nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  chen-po #  spangs-pa #  dang de'i phyogs kyi gnas-ngan-len #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sa yogI tad UrDva prahANArAmaH Bavati prahANe anuSaMsa darSI parItta praviveka prIti suKa saMspRzwaH kAlena kAlam prasadanIyena manaskAreNa saMpraharzayati yAvat eva styAnam idDa OdDatya upaSamAya / ayam rati saMgrAhakaH / tasya evam samyak prayuktasya kuSala pakza prayoga upastabDa tvAt kAma avacara kleSa paryavasTAna asamudAcAre sati tad prahINa prahINa tA avagama arTa tad utpatti anukUla SuBa nimitta manaskAreNa pratyavekzaNam mImAMsAm anaskAraH
# rnal-'byor #  ba de de'i-'og-tu #  spong-ba-la-dga'-ba # r 'gyur zhing / / spong-ba #  la phan yon du lta ste / / rab-tu-dben-pa # 'i dga'-ba-dang-bde-ba #  chung du reg nas dus-dus-su #  dang-bar-'gyur-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  ji tsam du rmugs pa dang gnyid dang rgod-pa #  dang bral-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir rab-tu-dga'-ba # r byed-pa # r 'di ni dga'-ba #  sdud-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / de-ltar #  legs-par-zhugs-pa #  de dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor-ba # s brten-pa # 'i phyir 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i kun-nas-dkris-pa #  kun nas mi-'byung-ba # s / / de spangs sam ma-spangs-pa #  khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir /
tasya evam mImAMsA pratipakzam BAvayataH tAvat kAlika yogena sarva kAma avacara kleSa saMyogAya praTama DyAna prayoga paryavasAna gataH pratipakzam anaskAraH prayoga nizWaH
# de 'byung-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'i sdug-pa # 'i mchan ma yid-la-byed-pa # s so-sor-rtog-pa #  ni dpyod-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # 'o / / des de-ltar #  dpyad nas gnyen-po #  bsgoms-pa # s dus de-srid-cig #  pa'i tshul-gyis #  'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir bsam-gtan-dang-po #  la sbyor-ba # 'i mthar-thug-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni sbyor-ba # 'i mtha'o /
tad anantaram mOla praTama DyAna sahagataH prayoga nizWA PalaH iti
# de'i-'og-tu #  dngos-gzhi # 'i bsam-gtan-dang-po # r gyur ba ni sbyor-ba # 'i mtha'i 'bras-bu #  yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tatra lakzaNa pratisavedinA prahAtavyam prAptavyam ca samyak parijQAya prahANAya prAptaye ca cittam praNiGatte / ADimokzikena tat arTa samyak prayogam AraBate / prAvivekyena aDimAtrAn kleSAn jahAti
# de-la #  mtshan-nyid #  rab tu rig-pa # s ni spang-bar-bya-ba #  dang thob-par-bya-ba #  legs-par #  yongs su shes-nas #  spang-ba #  dang thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir sems 'jog go / / mos-pa-las-byung-ba #  ni de'i-'og-tu #  yang-dag-par-sbyor-ba #  tsam mo / / rab-tu-dben-pa #  las byung-ba # s ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  chen-po #  rnams rab tu spong ngo /
rati saMgrAhakeNa maDyam kleSa prakAram jahAti
# dga'-ba #  sdud-pa # s ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  'bring du spong ngo /
mImAMsakena prApti niraBAna tAyAm cittam avasTApayati
# dpyod-pa # s ni thob-pa # r mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  med-pa #  la sems 'jog-par-byed #  do /
prayoga nizWena mRdum kleSa prakAram jahAti
# sbyor-ba # 'i mthas ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  chung-ngu #  rab tu spong ngo /
prayoga nizWA Palena ezAm manaskArANAm su BAvitAnAm BAvanA Palam pratyanuBavati
# sbyor-ba # 'i mtha'i 'bras-bu # s ni yid-la-byed-pa #  legs-par-bsgoms-pa #  'di dag gis bsgoms-pa'i-'bras-bu #  myong-ba # r byed do /
yaTA praTama DyAna samApattaye sapta manaskArAH evam yAvat na eva saMjQAna asaMjQAyatana samApattaye yaTAyogam yojayitavyAH / OdArika lakzaNam punar sarvAsvaDA BUmizu yAvat AkiMcani AyatanAt samAsena dviviDam veditavyam duHKatara vihArita apraSAnta vihAritayA alpa Ayuskata ratA ca tad viparyayeNa UrDvaBUmeH SAnta lakzaNam veditavyam / mAtrA vyavasTAnam DyAnAnAm tAvat mRdu maDya aDimAtra pariBAvita tvAt
# bsam-gtan-dang-po #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i phyir yid-la-byed-pa #  rnam-pa #  bdun ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  'du-shes #  med 'du-shes #  med min skye-mched #  kyi bar la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / rags-pa'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni sa-'og-ma #  thams-cad #  de / / ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye-mched #  kyi bar-du # 'o / / mdor-bsdu-na #  rnam-pa-gnyis #  su rig-par-bya #  ste / / rab-tu-ma-zhi-ba # r gnas-pa # s shin-tu #  sdug-bsngal-bar-gnas-pa #  dang shin-tu #  tshe-thung-ba # 'o / / de-la # s bzlog-ste #  sa-gong-ma #  ni zhi-ba'i-mtshan-nyid #  du rig-par-bya # 'o / / tshad rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / bsam-gtan #  rnams ni chung-ngu #  dang 'bring dang cher yongs-su-bsgom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratyekam triDA DyAna upapattiH Palam Bavati
# re-re #  la yang bsam-gtan #  gyi skye-ba #  gsum gsum ni 'bras-bu #  yin te /
tat yaTA brahmakAyikA brahma purohitA mahAbrahmANam iti evamAdi yaTApUrvam uktam
# 'di-lta-ste #  tshangs-ris #  dang tshangs-pa-mdun-na-'don #  dang tshangs-pa-chen-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ji-ltar #  gong-du #  bshad-pa # 'o /
ArUpyezu tu vimAna sTAna antara saMniveSa asaMBavAt evam upapatti BedaH na vyavasTApyate
# gzugs-med-pa #  rnams na ni gzhal-med-khang #  gi gnas gzhan gnas-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir de-ltar #  skye-ba # 'i bye-brag #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  med de /
api tu tezAm api asti mRdu Adi pariBAvitAnAm upapattO= ucca nIcatAH AyuH Adi viSezeNa hIna praNIta tA ca klizwa aklizwa tA bAhulya viSezeNa iti
# 'on-kyang #  de-dag #  chung du la-sogs-pa #  yongs-su-bsgoms-pa #  rnams kyis skye-ba #  la tshe la-sogs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyis mthon-po #  dang dma'-ba #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa #  mang-ba # 'i khyad-par #  gyis ngan-pa-dang-bzang-po #  ni yod do /
saMjQA karaNa vyavasTAnam caturTa DyAna praBedAnAm samADInAm asaMKyeyAni acintyAni ca nAmAni
# ming-du-gdags-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni bsam-gtan-bzhi # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams kyi ming grangs-med-pa #  dang bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa #  rnams te /
taTA hi yAvataH praTama DyAna saMgRhItAn samADIn budDAH BagavantaH boDisattvAH ca mahA praBAva prAptAH samApadyante tezAm samADInAm SrAvakAH pratyekabudDAH ca nAmAni api na jAnanti
# 'di-ltar #  bsam-gtan-dang-po # s bsdus-pa #  ji snyed la sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mthu chen-po #  thob-pa #  rnams snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  de-dag #  gi ming yang nyan-thos #  rnams dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams kyis mi shes na /
kutas ca ezAm saMKyAm jQAsyanti samApatsyante vA
# de-dag #  gi grangs shes-par-'gyur-ba # 'am snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r lta-ga-la #  'gyur te /
yaTA nirdizwam prajQApAramitAyAm sADitam samADi Satam / evam anyezu api tezu tezu mahAyAna sUtrezu iti / kaTam viSudDitaH
# ji-ltar #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  las ting-nge-'dzin #  brgya lha gcig bstan-pa #  dang de-bzhin-du #  theg-pa-chen-po # 'i mdo-sde #  gzhan de-dang-de-dag #  nas 'byung-ba # 'o / / rnam-par-dag-pa # s ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
prAnta kowikAH DyAna ArUpyA viSudDiH iti ucyate vESezika guNa aBinirhArAya nikAma lABa AdiBiH karmaNi tA prakarza nayanAt
# rab kyi mtha'i cha las byung-ba # 'i bsam-gtan #  dang gzugs-med-pa #  rnams ni rnam-par-dag-pa #  zhes bya ste / / yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub ba'i phyir 'dod-pa-bzhin-du #  'thob-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s las-su-rung-ba #  mchog-tu #  phyin par khrid pa'i phyir ro /
lokottara mArgaH BAva nAma arge azwO duHKa Adi Darma anvaya jQAnAni yaTA darSana mArge nirdizwAni
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyi bsgom-pa'i-lam #  la brgyad de / / sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa #  la chos dang rjes-su-rtog-pa # 'i shes-pa #  rnams te / / ji-ltar #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  la bstan-pa #  rnams te /
tad saMprayuktaH ca samADiH anAgamya saMgRhItaH praTamam DyAnam yAvat AkiMcanya Ayatanam
# ji-ltar #  mthong-ba'i-lam #  la bstan-pa #  rnams so / / de-dag #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  ni mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa # s bsdus-pa # 'am / / bsam-gtan-dang-po #  nas ci-yang-med-pa # 'i skye mchod kyi bar-du # 'o /
na eva saMjQAnA saMjQA Ayatanam aparisaPuwam saMjQA pracAra tayA parama pawu pracArasya Arya mArgasya asaMniHSraya tvAt ekAntena lOkikam veditavyam
# 'du-shes #  med 'du-shes #  med min skye-mched #  ni 'du-shes #  kyi rgyu-ba #  yongs su mi-gsal-ba # s 'phags-pa'i-lam #  mchog-tu #  gsal-ba # 'i gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir gcig-tu #  'jig-rten-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
atas eva ca tad saMjQA mAndyAt Alambana animittIkaraNa arTena animitm iti ucyate
# de'i-phyir #  de'i 'du-shes #  dman-pa # s dmigs-pa #  la mtshan-ma # r mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir mtshan-ma-med-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
kutas punar etat jQAyate na eva saMjQAnA saMjQA Ayatane Arya mArgaH na asti iti
# 'du-shes #  med 'du-shes #  med min skye-mched #  la 'phags-pa'i-lam #  med-pa #  de ji-ltar #  shes she na /
yasmAt uktam BagavatA yAvat eva saMjQA samApattiH tAvat AjQA prativeDaH iti / niroDa samApattiH lokottarAH Arya mArga pRzWa laBya tvAt / manuzyezu aBinirhriyate utpAdyate Aditas iti arTaH pUrva utpAditAyAH paScAt saMmuKa uBO= manuzyezu vA tasmin= eva janmani rUpaDAtO vA upapadye
# 'di-ltar #  bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis ji tsam du 'du-shes #  kyi snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  de tsam du kun-shes-pa # s rtogs so zhes gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  ste / / 'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyi rjes la thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mi rnams kyi nang-du #  mngon bar sgrub po zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / thog-ma #  nyid-du #  skyed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  ste / / sngar skye na mi rnams kyi nang-du #  tshe de nyid dam gzugs-kyi-khams #  su skyes nas mngon du 'gyur ro /
kaTam ArUpya lABinaH rUpa DAtu vIta rAgasya Arya SrAvakasya rUpaDAtO= upapatiH
# 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  gzugs-kyi-khams #  las 'dod-chags #  dang bral ste / / gzugs-med-pa #  thob-pa #  gzugs-kyi-khams #  su ji-ltar #  skye zhe na /
na avaSyam rUpa DAtu vIta rAgaH eva ArUpyam samApadyate
# gzugs-kyi-khams #  kyi 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  nyid gzugs-med-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  nges-pa #  med do /
atas eva atra catuzkowikam Bavati yaH rUpavIta rAgaH sarvaH saH ArUpya SAnta vimokza samApattAH yaH vE ArUpya SAnta vimokza samApattA sarvaH sa rUpa vIta rAgaH iti
# de'i-phyir #  gang gzugs la 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  de thams-cad #  gzugs-med-pa #  zhi-ba #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r byed la / / gang yang gzugs-med-pa #  zhi-ba #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r byed-pa #  de thams-cad #  gzugs las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  yin nam zhe na /
praTamA kowiH anAgamyam niSritya rUpavIta rAgaH
# mu-bzhi # r 'gyur te mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa #  la brten-nas #  gzugs la 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  ni mu dang-po # 'o /
dvitIyA kowiH caturTa DyAna lABI Arya Arya upapatti anarTI prahANa mArgam nirAkRtya viSeza mArgam niSrityA rUpya SAnta vimokza samApattA
# bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa #  thob-pa # 'i 'phags-pa #  gzugs-med-pa # r skye-ba #  don-du-mi-gnyer-ba #  la spong-ba # 'i lam bsal-nas #  khyad-par-can #  gyi lam la gnas te gzugs-med-pa #  zhi-ba #  rnams par thar-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r byed-pa #  ni mu gnyis-pa # 'o /
tRtIyA kowiH saH eva vErAgya arTI prahANa mArgam niSrityA rUpya SAnta vimokza samApattA / caturTI etAn AkArAn sTApayitvA / ArUpye zu upapannAnAm kasmAt na saMmuKIBavati
# de nyid 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  don-du #  gnyer zhing spong-ba # 'i lam la gnas te gzugs-med-pa #  zhi-ba #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # r byed-pa #  ni mu gsum-pa # 'o / / rnam-pa #  de-dag #  ma-gtogs-pa #  ni mu-bzhi #  pa'o /
SAntena vihAreNa vihartu kAmAH AryAH manuzyezu enAm aBinirhRtya saMmuKIkurvanti
# gzugs-med-par-skyes-pa #  rnams la ci'i-phyir #  mngon-sum-du #  mi 'gyur zhe na / / zhi-ba # r gnas-pa # s gnas-pa # r 'dod-pa # 'i 'phags-pa #  rnams mi'i-nang-du #  de mngon-pa # r bsgrubs-nas #  mngon-sum-du #  byed do /
ArUpyezu tu upapannAH te prayatnena eva vEpAkikEH parama SAntEH vimokza vihArEH viharanti iti atas tad saMmuKIkaraNa arTam na punar prayatnam AraBante iti
# gzugs-med-par-skyes-pa #  de-dag #  ni bsgrim mi-dgos-pa # r rnam-par-smin-pa #  las byung-ba #  mchog-tu #  zhi-ba #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  la gnas-pa # s gnas-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  de mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # 'i don-du #  yang 'bad-pa #  mi rtsom mo /
mRdu maDya aDimAtraH mArgaH pratyekam punar mRdu AdiBiH triBiH prakArEH BittvA nava prakAraH vyavasTApyate BAvanA heyAnAm krameNa prahANa jQApana arTam
# lam chung du dang 'bring dang chen-po #  re-re #  la yang chung du la-sogs-pa # s rnam-pa-gsum #  du phye-nas #  rnam-pa #  dgur rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / bsgoms-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  rnam-pa #  rim-gyis #  spang-ba #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kim punar kAraNam mRdu mRdunA mArgeNa aDimAtraH kleSaH prahIyate
# ci'i-phyir #  lam chung-ngu # 'i chung dus nyon-mongs-pa #  chen-po'i-chen-po #  spang zhe na /
sa hi atyarTaH vipanna hrIvyapanna api AlajjinaH saMtAne samudAcarati sUpa lakzaH ca asO su paricCedaH tasmAt asO sTUla mala vat alpena api pratipakzeNa apanIyate
# de ni ngo-tsha-shes-pa #  dang khrel-yod-pa #  dang shin-tu #  bral zhing 'dzem-pa #  med-pa # 'i sems-kyi-rgyud #  la kun du 'byung-ba # s de rtogs-pa # r sla zhing yongs su gcad-pa # r sla-ba #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  de ni dri-ma #  che long bzhin-du #  gnyen-po #  chung-ngu # s sel to /
yaH tu ayam duzparicCeda samudAcAraH sUkzma lInaH saMtAne mRdu mRdu kleSaH sUkzma mala vat mahatA pratipakza balena apanIyataH iti adaH vipakza prakAra viparyayeNa pratipakza prakAra vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# gang yongs su gcad-pa # r dka'-ba # r kun-tu #  'byung zhing phra la rgyud-la-zhen-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  chung-ngu'i-chung-ngu #  de ni dri-ma #  chung-ngu #  bzhin-du #  gnyen-po #  chen-po # 'i stobs kyis sel te / / de'i-phyir #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi rnam-pa #  las bzlog-nas #  gnyen-po # 'i phyogs kyi rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
prayoga mArgaH yena mArgeNa BAvyamAnena pratyekam aDimAtra aDimAtra Adi kleSa prakAra Adi jAti pakzasya dOzWulya aFgasya apagamAt krameNa ASrayaH parivartate sa BAvanA mArge prayoga mArge iti ucyate
# sbyor-ba'i-lam #  ni lam gang bsgoms-pa # s chen-po # 'i yang chen-po #  la-sogs-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i bye-brag #  dang phyogs kyi gnas-ngan-len #  gyi cha-shas #  re-re #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir rim-gyis #  gnas-gyur-pa #  de ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  la sbyor-ba'i-lam #  zhes-bya'o #  /
yasya tu anantaram tad prakAra kleSa jAti tad pakza dOzWulya avaSeza apagamAt tena dOzWulyena nirdOWulyaH ASrayaH parivartate saH Anantarya mArgaH
# gang-gi #  'og-tu #  de nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gi rnam-pa #  dang phyogs kyi gnas-ngan-len #  ma-lus-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir des gnas-ngan-len #  med-pa # r gnas-gyur-pa #  de ni bar-chad-med-pa'i-lam #  lo /
vimukti mArgaH yena nAma ASraya parivRtti pratyAtmam anuBavati
# rnam-par-grol-ba'i-lam #  ni gang-gis #  gnas-gyur-pa #  de so-so # r rang-gis #  myong-ba # 'o /
viSeza mArgaH tad UrDva avaSeza kleSa prahANam kurvataH ye prayoga anantara vimukti mArgAH
# khyad-par-gyi-lam #  ni de'i-'og-tu #  nyon-mongs-pa #  lhag-ma #  spong par byed-pa # 'i sbyor-ba #  dang-ba # r chad-med-pa #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba'i-lam #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
aparaH paryAyaH aviSeza mArgaH tasya kleSa prahANa prayoga maDya pekzya sUtra AdIn DarmAH cintayataH pUrva cintita aDigata Darma pratyavekzaNA vihAreNa vA viharataH samApatti antaram vA samApadyamAnasya yaH mArgaH
# rnam-grangs #  gzhan-du-na #  khyad-par-gyi-lam #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # r sbyor-ba #  btang-ste #  / / mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos sems-pa # 'am sdar bsam-pa #  dang khong-du-chud-pa # 'i chos la so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i gnas-pa # s gnas-pa # 'am / / snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  gzhan la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  gzhan-pa #  snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i lam gang-yin-pa # 'o /
punar aBijQA AdIn vESezikAn guNa anaBinirharataH tEH vA viharataH yaH mArgaH
# yang mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'am de-dag #  gi gnas-pa # 'i lam gang-yin-pa # 'o /
iti evam BAvanA mArga vistareNa nirdiSya tad anuzaMgeNa mArga BAvanA varNyate
# de-ltar #  bsgom-pa'i-lam #  rgya-cher #  bshad nas de'i zhar la byung-ba # 'i lam bsgom-pa #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
caturviDA mArga BAvanA samyak prahANAn aDikRtya yaTAyogam
# lam bsgom-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  ni yang-dag-par #  spong pa'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
tatra pratilamBAya BAvanA pratilamBa BAvanA tayA AlabDa kuSala Darma pratilamBAt
# de-la #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir bsgom-pa #  ni thob-par-bya-ba'i-don #  du bsgom-pa #  ste / / des dge-ba'i-chos #  ma-thob-pa #  rnams thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nizevaNam eva BAvanAH nizevaNa BAvanAH labDa kuSala Darma aByasanAt
# brten-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ni brten-pa #  nyid bsgom-pa #  ste / / dge-ba'i-chos #  thob-pa #  goms-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nirDAvanAya BAvanA nirDAvana BAvanA samudAcAra avasTA kuSala Darma nirvAsanAt
# bsal-ba # 'i phyir bsgom-pa #  ni bsal-ba # 'i don-du #  bsgom-pa #  ste / / kun-'byung-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  su mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  sel-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pratipakzasya BAvanA pratipakza BAvanA anAgata akuSala Darma anutpatti Darma tA ApAdanAt
# gnyen-po-bsgom-pa #  ni gnyen-po #  la bsgom-pa #  ste / / ma-'ongs-pa # 'i mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  mi-skye-ba'i-chos-can #  du byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aparaH paryAyaH mArgaH utpadyamAnaH svAm vAsanAm sTApayati sADAsanA pratilamBa BAvanA tatas tad anvayAnAm uttaptatara ApatteH / asya eva mArgasya saMmuKIBAvaH aBinizevaNa BAvanA
# rnam grang gzhan-du-na #  'phags-pa'i-lam #  skye-ba #  na rang-gi #  bag-chags #  'jog-pa #  de ni bag-chags #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir bsgom-pa #  ste / / de-la # s de'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  rnams cher 'bar-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / lam de nyid mngon-du-byed-pa #  ni brten-pa # 'i bsgom-pa # 'o /
tena sva vipakza dOzWulya niroDanAt nirDAvana BAvanA / ASrayasya parivRtta tvAt AyatyAm anutpatti Darma tAyAm avasTApanam pratipakza BAvanA
# des rang-gi #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi gnas-ngan-len #  'gog-par-byed-pa #  ni bsal-ba # 'i phyir bsgom-pa # 'o / / gnas-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir phyi-ma-la #  mi-skye-ba'i-chos-can #  du 'jog-pa #  de ni gnyen-po-bsgom-pa # 'o /
punar pratipakzasya vidUzaNa AdikaH caturviDaH praBedaH veditavyaH
# yang gnyen-po #  ni rnam-par-sun-'byin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi # r rab-tu-dbye-ba # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / de-la #  rnam-par-sun-'byin-pa # 'i gnyen-po #  ni /
tatra vidUzaNa apratipakzaH sa Asravezu saMskArezu AdIn avadarSanam tena roga gaNXa AdiBiH AkArEH upAdAna skanDa dUzaNAt
# zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i 'du-byed-rnams #  la nyes-dmigs-su-lta-ba #  ste / / des-na # d dang 'bras la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  sun-'byin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prahANa pratipakzaH prayoga Anantarya mArgAH tEH kleSa prahANAt
# spong-ba'i-gnyen-po #  ni sbyor-ba #  dang-ba # r chad-med-pa # 'i lam rnams te / / de-dag #  gi nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
ADAra pratipakzaH vimukti mArgAH tEH prahANa prApti saMDAraNAt
# rten gnyis po ni rnam-par-grol-ba'i-lam #  rnams te / / de-dag #  gis spong-ba # 'i thob-pa #  kun-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro; /
dUrIBAva pratipakzaH tad upari maH mArgaH tena pUrva prahINa kleSa dUrIkaraNAt
# thag bsring-ba # 'i gnyen-po #  ni de'i gong-ma # 'i lam ste / / des sngon spangs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  thag bsring-ba # 'i phyir ro /
punar boDi pakzi Adi Bedena ekAdaSaviDaH mArgaH vyavasTApyate
# yang byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  la sogs ba'i bye-brag #  gis lam rnam-pa-bcu #  gcig-tu #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA vastu parIkzA mArgaH smRti upasTAnAni Aditas tena aSuBa AdiBiH AkArEH kAya vedanA citta Darma vastu parIkzaNAt
# dngos-po #  la yongs-su-rtog-pa # 'i lam ni dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams te / / des thog-ma #  nyid-du #  mi gtsang ba la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam gyi lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos kyi dngos-po #  la yongs-su-rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vyAvasAyikaH mArgaH samyak prahANAni taTA sarvANi vastUni parIkzyAnena AvaraNa prahANAya vIrya AramBAt
# rtsol ba las byung-ba # 'i lam ni yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  rnams te / / de-ltar #  dngos-po #  rnams la yongs-su-brtags-nas #  des sgrib-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i don-du #  brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i phyir ro /
samADi parikarma mArgaH RdDi pAdAH taTA apariSoDita AvaraNasya anena CandavIrya citta mImAMsA muKEH samADeH karmaNi tA ApAdanAt
# ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # r byed-pa # 'i lam ni rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  rnams te / / de-ltar #  sgrib-pa #  yongs su sbyangs-pa #  ni 'dis 'dun-pa #  dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod-pa # 'i sgo nas ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams kyis las-su-rung-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aBisamaya prayogikaH mArgaH indriyANi taTA kRta samADi parikarmaNaH anena Arya mArga samudAgamAya aDipati BUta Uzma gata UrDva prayogAt
# mngon-par-rtogs-pa # r bya-ba'i-sbyor-ba # 'i lam ni dbang-po #  rnams te / / de-ltar #  ting-nge-'dzin #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  byas-pa #  ni des 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i phyir dbang-byed-pa # r gyur-pa #  dro-bar-gyur-pa #  dang rtse mo la sbyor-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aBisamaya SlizwaH mArgaH balAni taTA ADipatya prAptasya anena anantaram satya prativeDAya aSradDA Adi vipakzAna aBiBUta kzAnti agraDarma prayogAt
# mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  dang 'dres-pa # 'i lam ni stobs rnams te / / de-ltar #  dbang-byed-pa #  thob-pa #  ni lnga po 'dis de ma-thag-tu #  bden-pa #  rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ma dang pa la-sogs-pa #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  zil-gyis-mi-non-pa #  bzod-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog la sbyor-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aBisamaya mArgaH boDyaFgAni tena Aditas pratyAtmam tattva aBisaMboDAt
# mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i lam ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  rnams te / / des thog-ma-kho-nar #  so-so #  rang-gis #  de-kho-na # r mngon du yang-dag-par-rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
viSudDinEH yANikaH mArgaH Arya azwa aFgaH mArgaH tad UrDvam tena BAvanA prahAtavya kleSa prahANAya viSudDaye niryANAt iti
# rnam-par-dag-pa #  nges-par-'byin-pa'i-lam #  ni 'phags-pa'i-lam #  yan-lag-brgyad-pa #  ste / / de'i-'og-tu #  des bsgoms-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams rnam-par-dag-pa # r bya-ba # r nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atas eva ezAm boDi pakzANAm eva AnupUrvI veditavyA / niSraya indriya BinnaH mArgaH catasraH pratipadaH / tatra duHKA pratipada nAga mAyA rUpya miSritAH yaTAkramam SamaTa vipaSya nAmAndyAt / suKA DyAna niSritA yuga nadDa vAhi tvAt / DanDa aBijQA dvayoH api anayoH duHKa suKa niSrayayoH mRdu indriyANAm / kzipra aBijQA tayoH eva tIkzNa indriyANAm iti
# de'i-phyir #  de-ltar #  byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  'di dag gi go-rims #  ni 'di-lta-bu #  yin par rig-par-bya # 'o / / gnas dang dbang-po #  tha-dad-pa # 'i lam ni lam-bzhi #  ste / / de-la #  dka'-ba # 'i lam ni mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa #  dang gzugs-med-pa #  la brten-pa #  ste / / go-rims-bzhin-du #  zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  zhan-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sla-ba #  ni bsam-gtan #  la brten-pa #  ste / / zung ngu 'brel-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro; / / mngon-par-shes-pa #  bul-ba #  ni dka'-ba #  dang sla-ba # 'i gnas 'di gnyis la ste / / dbang-po-rtul-po #  rnams kyi'o / / mngon-par-shes-pa #  myur-ba #  ni 'di gnyis nyid la ste /
SikzA traya pariSoDanaH mArgaH catvAri Darma padAni
# dbang-po-rnon-po #  rnams kyi'o / / bslab-pa-gsum #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # 'i lam ni chos kyi gnas bzhi ste /
tatra anaBiDyA vyApAdam aDiSIlam SikzAyAH pariSoDanam ananunayA pratiGa muKena SikzA pada AKaNXanAt
# de-la #  brnab-sems-med-pa #  dang gnod-sems-med-pa #  gnyis kyis ni lhag-pa'i-tshul-khrims #  kyi bslab-pa #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba #  ste / / rjes-su-chags-pa #  dang khang khro-ba #  spangs-pa # 'i bslab-pa # 'i gnas mi-nyams-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samyak smRti ADi cittam SikzAyAH pariSoDanam AlaMbana asaMmoze sati citta samADAnAt
# yang-dag-pa'i-dran-pa # s ni lhag-pa'i-sems #  kyi bslab-pa #  yongs-su-spyod-pa #  ste / / dmigs-pa #  ma brjed-pa #  ni sems-mnyam-par-'jog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samyak samADinA aDiprajQam SikzAyAH pariSoDanam samAhita cittasya yaTA BUta jQAnAt iti
# yang-dag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gyis ni lhag-pa'i-shes-rab #  kyi bslab-pa #  yongs su sbyong ste / / sems-mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  las yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  shes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sarva guNa aBinirhArakaH yaH mArgaH SamaTa vipaSyanA tatas sarva lOkika lokottara guNa aBinipatteH
# yon-tan-thams-cad #  sgrub-par-byed-pa # 'i rnal-'byor #  gyi lam ni zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  ste / / de-la # s 'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i yon-tan-thams-cad #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
mArga saMgraha mArga strINi indriyANI tatra anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriyeNa prayoga darSana mArgayoH saMgrahaH AjQA indriyeNa BAvanA mArgasya AjQAtA avIndriyeNa nizWA mArgasya iti
# lam sdud-pa # 'i lam ni dbang-po-gsum #  po dag ste / / de-la #  mi-shes-pa #  kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po # s ni sbyor-ba #  dang mthong-ba'i-lam #  sdud do / / kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po # s ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  sdud do / / kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po # s ni mthar-phyin-pa # 'i lam sdud do /
punar boDi pakzyANAm DarmANAm paQcaBiH prakArEH vyavasTAnam veditavyam AlambanataH svaBAvataH sahAyataH BAvanAtaH BAvanA PalataH ca
# yang byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  kyi chos-rnams #  ni rnam-pa # r lngas rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / dmigs-pa #  dang ngo-bo-nyid #  dang grogs dang bsgom-pa #  dang bsgoms-pa'i-'bras-bu # s so /
tatra smRti upasTAnAnAm AlaMbanam yaTAkramam kAyaH vedanA cittam DarmAH
# de-la #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ni lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos-rnams #  te /
kim arTa punar etat evam AlaMbanam vyavasTApyate
# go-rims #  bzhin no / / ci'i-phyir #  'di dag dmigs-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag ce na /
yasmAt viparyasta budDayaH bAlAH prAyeNa sa indriyam kAyam ASritya suKa Adim upaBuQjAnAH upalabDa lakzaNAH Atma rAga AdiBiH SradDA AdiBiH ca saMkliSyante vyavadAyante ca iti vikalpayanti atas Aditas samyak tad vastu lakzaNa parIkzA arTam evam caturDA Alambana vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# 'di-ltar #  byis-pa #  phyin-ci-log-gi-blo #  can rnams ni phal-cher #  dbang-po-dang-bcas-pa # 'i lus la brten-nas #  bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la spyod-pa #  na dmigs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi bdag 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # r 'gyur-ba # r rtogs te / / de'i-phyir #  thog-ma #  nyid-du #  dngos-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  de / / legs-par #  yongs su brtags-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
svaBAvataH prajQA smRtiH ca kAya Adi anupaSyana avacanAt smRti upasTAna vacanAt ca yaTAkramam
# ngo-bo-nyid #  ni shes-rab #  dang dran-pa #  ste / / lus la-sogs-pa #  la rjes su lta-ba #  zhes 'byung-ba #  dang; dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  zhes 'byung-ba # 'i phyir go-rims #  bzhin no /
sahAyataH tAByAm saMprayuktAH cita cEtasikAH / BAvanA aDyAtmam bahirDA aDyAtma bahirDA ca kAya Adizu kAya Adi anupaSyanA / tatra aDyAtmam kAyaH cakzu Srotra GrANa jihvA kAya indriyANi ADyAtmika Ayatana saMgRhIta tvAt sattva saMKyAta tvAt ca
# grogs ni de-gnyi-ga #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams so / / bsgom-pa #  ni nang dang phyi'i lus la-sogs-pa #  la lus la-sogs-pa # 'i rjes su lta-ba # 'o / / de-la #  nang-gi-lus #  ni mig dang rna-ba #  dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi dbang-po #  rnams te / / nang gi skye-mched #  kyis bsdus-pa #  dang sems-can #  gyi grangs-su-gtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
bahirDA kAyaH bahirDA rUpa Sabda ganDa rasa sprazwavyAni bAhya Ayatana saMgRhIta tvAt asattva saMKyAta tvAt ca
# phyi'i lus ni phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg-bya #  rnams te / / phyi'i skye-mched #  kyis bsdus-pa #  dang sems-can #  gyi grangs sum gtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aDyAtma bahirDA kAyaH cakzuH Adya Ayatana saMbadDAni rUpa AdIni AyatanAni indriyADizWAna BUtAni sattva saMKyAta tvAt vAhya Ayatana saMgRhIta tvAt ca
# nang dang phyi'i lus ni mig la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  dang 'brel-ba # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i skye-mched #  dbang-po'i-gnas #  su gyur-pa #  rnams te / / sems-can #  gyi grangs-su-gtogs-pa #  dang phyi'i skye-mched #  kyis sdud-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pAra saMtAnikAni ca ADyAtmikAni rUpINi AyatanAni aDyAtma bahirDA kAyaH Ayatana vyavasTAm saMtAna vyavasTAm ca pramANayitvA
# gzhan-gyi-rgyud #  la yod-pa # 'i nang gi skye-mched #  gzugs-can #  rnams kyang-na # ng dang phyi'i lus te / / skye-mched #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  dang rgyud rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  brtson par byas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kAye kAyasya sAdRSyena paSyanA kAye kAya anupaSyanAH vikalpa pratibimba kAya darSana anusAreNa prakRti bimba kAya avaDAraNAt
# lus la lus kyi rjes su lta-ba #  ni lus la lus dang 'dra-bar #  lta-ba #  ste / / rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gzugs-brnyan #  gyi gzugs mthong-ba #  dang mthun-par #  rang gzhin gyi gzugs-kyi-lus #  nges-par-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aDyAtmam vedanA AdayaH aDyAtmam kAyam upAdAya utpannAH cakzuH Adi AlaMbanatayA sva ASraya utpannana tayA vA
# nang gi tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni nang-gi-lus #  la brten-nas-'byung-ba #  rnams te / / mig la-sogs-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  dang rang-gi #  gnas las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
bahirDA vedanA AdayaH bahirDA kAyam upAdAya utpannAH rUpa Adi Alambana tayA parASraya utpannatayA vA / aDyAtma bahirDA vedanA AdayaH DyAtma bahirDA kAyam upAdAya utpannAH svasantAnika bAhya Ayatana Alambana tayA pArasaMtAnika ADyAtmika Ayatana alaMkbana tayA vA
# phyi'i tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni phyi-rol-gyi-lus #  la brten-nas-'byung-ba #  rnams te / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  dang gzhan gyi gnas las byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / nang dang phyi'i tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ni nang dang phyi'i lus la brten-nas-'byung-ba #  rnams te / / rang-gi-rgyud #  la yod-pa # 'i phyi'i skye-mched #  la dmigs-pa #  dang gzhan-gyi-rgyud #  la yod-pa # 'i nang gi skye-mched #  la dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rjes su lta-ba #  yang de-bzhin #  te / / ci-rigs-su #  sbyar ro zhes ba ni blo la snang-ba #  dang khyad-par-med-pa #  bsgom-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dgu po 'di dag ni dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # 'i yan-lag #  go /
cetasaH lIna tvam viSeza aDigama pratyAtma pariBava muKEH vizAdaH
# sems-zhum-pa #  ni khyad-par-thob-pa # r bya-ba #  la bdag dman-pa # r sems-pa # 'i sgo nas sgyid-lug-pa # 'o /
parisrava pariKedaH daMSa maSaka Adi upadrava utpaIXa nAsa hanam
# gnod-pa # s yongs su skyo-ba #  ni sha-sbrang #  dang sbrang-bu #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnod-pa # s nyen-pa #  mi-bzod-pa # 'o /
alpa mAtra saMtuzwiH alam me tAvatA kuSala pakzeNa iti prativAraNam
# cung-zad #  tsam gyis chog-par-'dzin-pa #  ni dge-ba'i-phyogs #  'di tsam gyis chog go zhes phyir bzlog-pa # 'o /
Apatti vipratisAraH aBikrama pratikrama Adizu asaMprajQAna cAriNaH SikzA vyatikrama pUrvaH paScAttApaH
# ltung-ba # s yid la gcags pas ni 'gro-ba-dang-ldog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la shes-bzhin #  med-pa # r spyod-pa #  ste / / sngar bslab-pa #  dang 'gal nas phyis 'gyod-pa # 'o /
nikzipta DuratA pramAda dozeNa yaTA AramBam kuSala pakza prayoga anta anirvAhaH iti / Palam yaTAkramam smRti upasTAnAnAm Suci suKa nitya Atma viparyAsa praharaNam aSuBa BAvanAtaH yat kiMcid veditam idam atra duHKasya iti jQAnAt ASraya alaMkbana Adi BedEH pratikzaNam vijQAnasya anvagamanAt nirvyApAra saMkleSa bya vadana Darma mAtra parIkzaNAt ca iti
# brtson pa 'dor-ba #  ni bag-med-pa # 'i nyes-pa # s dge-ba'i-phyogs #  ji-ltar #  brtsams pa la sbyor-ba #  mthar mi-'byin-pa # 'o / / 'bras-bu #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams la gtsang ba dang bde-ba #  dang rtag-pa #  dang bdag tu phyin-ci-log #  spang-ba #  ste / / mi-sdug-pa-bsgom-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang-ci #  tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'di-ltar #  sdug-bsngal-bar #  shes-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gnas dang dmigs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-par-shes-pa #  skad-cig-re-re-la #  gzhan-du-'gyur-ba # r rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  chos tsam du zad de byed-pa #  med-pa # r yongs su rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar ezAm yaTAkramam catur satya avatAraH Palam
# yang 'di dag gi 'bras-bu #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  bden-pa #  bzhi la 'jug ste /
kAya smRti upasTAnena duHKa satyam avatarati saMskAra duHKa tAla kzaNena dOzWulyena praBAvita tvAt kAyasya asya
# lus dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s ni sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug ste / / lus ni 'du-byed-kyi-sdug-bsngal #  gyi mtshan-nyid #  gnas-ngan-len #  gyis rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
taTA hi tad pratipakza BUtA prasrabDiH kAyaH eva viSezeNa utpadyate iti
# 'di-ltar #  de'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa #  shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ni lus nyid la khyad-par-can #  du 'byung ngo /
vedanA mRtyu upasTAnena samudaya satyam avatarati suKa Adi vedanA aDizWAna tvAt saMyoga Adi tRzNAyAH
# tshor-ba #  dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s ni kun 'byung gi bden-pa #  la 'jug ste / / phrad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r srid-pa #  ni bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshor-ba # 'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro /
citta smRti upasTAnena niroDa satyam avatarati nirAtmakam vijQAna mAtram na Bavizyati iti paSyataH AtmA ucCeda ASaFkA muKena nirvANa uttrAsa aBAvAt
# sems dran-pa #  nye-bar #  gzhag bas ni 'gog-pa # 'i bden-pa #  la 'jug ste / / bdag med cing rnam-par-shes-pa #  tsam med-par-'gyur-ba #  lta-ba # s na / / bdag chad-pa # r 'dogs-pa # 'i sgo nas mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la skrag-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Darma mRtyu pasTAnena mArga satyam avatarati vipakza Darma prahANAya pratipakza Darma BAvanAt iti
# chos dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa # s ni lam gyi bden-pa #  la 'jug ste / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi chos spong-ba #  dang gnyen-po # 'i chos la brten-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar ezAm kAya vedanA citta Darma visaMyogaH Palam yaTAkramam veditavyam tad BAvanayA kAya Adi pakza dOzWulyA apagamAt iti
# yang 'di dag gi 'bras-bu #  ni lus dang tshor-ba #  dang sems dang chos dang bral-ba # r go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya #  ste / / de-dag #  bsgoms-pa # s lus la-sogs-pa # 'i phyogs kyi gnas-ngan-len #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir ro /
samyak prahANAnAm praTamasya anutpannaH vipakzaH AlaMbanam tena anutpanna pApaka akuSala DarmAn utpAdAya Canda jananAt
# yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  rnams kyi dang-po # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  skyes-pa #  ste / / des sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  rnams spang-ba # 'i phyir 'dun-pa #  skyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dvitIyasya utpannaH vipakzaH / tRtIyasya anutpannaH pratipakzaH / caturTasya utpannaH AlaMbanam iti yaTA sUtram yojayitavyam
# gnyis-pa # 'i dmigs-pa # s ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma-skyes-pa #  dang gsum-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni gnyen-po #  ma-skyes-pa #  dang bzhi-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni gnyen-po #  skyes-pa #  ste / / ji-ltar #  mdo-sde #  las 'byung-ba #  bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
Candam janayati iti evamAdiBiH sa ASrayA vIrya BAvanA paridIpitA
# 'dun-pa #  skyed do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshig rnams kyis ni brtson 'grus bsgom-pa #  gnas-dang-bcas-pa #  yongs su bstan to /
atra ASrayaH CandaH tad pUrvaka tvAt udyogasya / yadA SamaTa Adi nimittam anaskAreNa nirapekzA alaMkabanam kevalam pratipakzam BAvayati tadA vyAyat ca uJataH iti ucyate
# de-la #  gnas ni 'dun-pa #  ste / / de ni brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'i phyir ro / / gang-gi-tshe #  zhi-gnas-kyi-mtshan-ma #  yid-la-byed-pa # s gnyen-po #  skyon-med-pa #  'ba'-zhig #  sgom-pa #  de'i tshe 'bad-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
yadA tulayA upakleSe utpanne tad apakarzaNa arTa prasadanIya Adi manaskArEH cittam unnAmayati OdDatya upakleSe ca utpanne pratyAsaMkzepa muKena cittam DArayati tadA vIryam AraBate iti ucyate
# gang-gi-tshe #  nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  bying-ba #  'byung-ba #  de bsal-ba # 'i phyir dga'-ba # r gyur-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  rnams kyis sems 'bar-ba # r byed-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rgod-pa #  byung-ba #  na nang-du #  sdud-pa # 'i sgo nas sems 'dzin-pa #  de'i tshe brtson 'grus rtsom pa zhes-bya'o #  /
atas eva laya OdDatya apakarzaNa upAya saMdarSana arTam anantaram Aha cittam pragRhNAti pradaDAti iti
# de'i-phyir #  bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i thabs bstan-pa # 'i phyir de'i-'og-tu #  sems-rab-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang rab tu 'jog-pa #  smos so /
Palam praTama dvitIyayoH samyak prahANayoH aSeza vipakzahAniH tAByAm yaTAyogam utpannAn utpanna pApaka akuSala Darma prahANAt
# 'bras-bu #  ni yang-dag-pa # 'i spong-ba #  dang-po #  dang gnyis-pa # 'i ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma-lus-par #  nyams-pa #  ste / / de gnyis kyis ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  nyams-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tRtIyasya pratipakza pratilamBaH tena anutpanna kuSala Darma utpAdanAt
# gsum-pa # 'i ni gnyen-po #  thob-pa #  ste / / des dge-ba'i-chos #  ma-skyes-pa #  skyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
caturTasya pratipakza vRdDiH tena utpanna kuSala Darma vipula tA ApAdanAt iti
# bzhi-pa # 'i ni gnyen-po #  thob bas 'phel-ba #  ste / / des dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  spong-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
RdDi pAda alaMkanam nizpannena samADinA yat karaNIyam RdDayA Adikam kRtyam
# rdzu-'phrul #  gyi rkang ba rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  gyis grub-pa # 'i bya-ba #  rdzu-'phrul #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
Canda samADiH yat satkRtya prayogam Agamya spRSati cittasya ekAgra tAm tIvreNa Candena tIvreNa AdareNa prayogaH satkRtya prayogaH iti kRtvA
# 'dun-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang gus-par-sbyor-ba #  la brten-nas #  sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa #  ste / / gus-par-sbyor-ba #  ni 'dun-pa-drag-po #  dang rim-gro #  cher byas te sbyor-ba # 'o /
vIrya samADiH yat sAtatya prayogam Agamya spRSati cittasya ekAgra tAm
# brtson 'grus kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang rgyun-du-sbyor-ba #  la brten-nas #  sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa #  ste /
tat vIryam iti ucyate yat nityam prayujyate eva na kadAcid na prayujyate
# gang rtag-tu #  sbyor zhing nam yang mi sbyor-ba #  ma-yin-pa #  de ni brtson 'grus zhes-bya'o #  /
citta samADiH yat pUrva janma antare samADi BAvanAm Agamya tad paripuzwa bIja tvAt cittasya sva rasena samADi anukUla pariNAme sati spRSati cittasya ekAgra tAm
# sems-kyi-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni sngon gang-gi-tshe #  rabs gzhan na ting-nge-'dzin #  bsgoms-pa #  la brten-nas #  des sems kyi sa-bon #  yongs su brtas-pa # 'i phyir rang-gi-ngang-gis #  ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # r gyur na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa # 'o /
api Kalu RdDi pAda aBinirhArayoH nidarSana arTam eva samyak prahANa BAvanAyAm Candam janayati iti evamAdi nirdeSaH veditavyaH
# rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i rgyu yang-dag-par-bstan-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  dag-pa # r spong-ba #  bsgom-pa #  la 'dun-pa #  skyed do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
cittam pradaDAti pragRhNAti iti ezA ca atra pAWA AnupUrvI veditavyA
# sems rab tu 'jog-pa #  dang rab tu 'dzin zhes-bya-ba #  de ni 'dir brjod-pa # 'i lugs kyi go-rims #  su rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra citta samADiH yat citam pradaDat spRSati iti pratyAtmam cittam eva cittam DArayan Samayan= aBisaMkzipan= aDigacCati iti arTaH
# de-la #  sems-kyi-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni gang sems rab tu 'jog-pa #  ni sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni sems nyid kyis sems nang-du #  'dzin zhing zhi-ba # r byed / / sdud-pa # r byed /
mImAMsA samADiH yat citam pragRhNan= iti Darma vipaSyanA muKena cittam uttApayati iti arTaH
# 'thob-pa # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / dpyod-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  ni sems-rab-tu-'dzin-pa #  na zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos la lhag-mthong #  gi sgo nas sems 'bar-ba # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
BAvanA Canda AdInAm azwAnAm prahANa saMskArANAm aByAsaH
# bsgom-pa #  ni 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  brgyad goms-par-byed-pa # 'o /
te punar azwO prahANa saMskArAH caturDA kriyante
# spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  brgyad po de-dag #  ni rnam-pa-bzhi # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
tat yaTA vyAvasAyikaH Canda vyAyAma SradDAH / tatra CandaH vyAyAmasya ASrayaH / Candasya punar SradDA nimittam
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'bad-pa #  ni 'dun-pa #  dang rtsol ba dang dad-pa # 'o / / de-la #  'dun-pa #  ni rtsol ba'i gnas so / / 'dun-pa # 'i rgyu ni dad-pa #  ste /
taTA hi yaH yena arTI Bavati tat prApti arTa vyAyacCate / arTi tvam ca na antareNa tat asti tu Adi aBisaMpatyam iti
# 'di-ltar #  gang-zag #  gang zhig don-du-gnyer-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni de thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir rtsol lo / / de yod-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  yid-ches-pa #  med na don-du-gnyer-ba # r mi 'gyur ro /
anugrAhikaH prasrabDiH tayA kAya citta anugraha karaNAt
# phan-'dogs-pa #  ni shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  ste / / des lus dang sems la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
OpanibanDikaH smRti saMprajanye AlaMbana asaMpramozeNa cittasya ekAgra avasTAnAt tad pramAde ca sati paricCedAt yaTAkramam
# nye-bar-'dogs-pa #  ni dran-pa #  dang shes-bzhin #  te / / dmigs-pa #  ma brjed-pa # s sems rtse gcig pa nyid la 'jug-pa #  dang de-la #  bag-med-pa # r gyur na yongs su gcod-pa # 'i phyir te /
prAtipakzikaH cetanA upekze citta pragraha praDAna aBisaMskArAByAm utpanna laya OdDatya parivarjanAt nirupakleSa SamaTa Adi nimitta anukaraNAt ca iti / saMkzepa nidAnam vipaSyana arahitasya kOsIdya muKena layaH
# go-rims #  bzhin no / / gnyen-po #  ni sems-pa #  dang btang-snyoms #  te / / sems-rab-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang rab tu 'jog-pa #  mngon bar 'du-byed #  pas bying-ba #  dang rgod-pa #  'byung-ba #  yongs-su-spong-ba #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa #  ni zhi-gnas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  rjes-su-'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang 'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sdud-pa #  dang g-yeng ba bzhi dang bcas-pa # r yongs su spangs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  sgom-pa #  de-la #  sdud-pa # 'i gzhi ni lhag-mthong #  dang bral-ba #  ste / / le-lo # 'i sgo nas bying-ba # r 'gyur ro /
vikzepa nidAnam aSuBa saMjQA rahitasya OdDatya muKena saMpragrahaH
# g-yeng ba'i gzhi ni mi-sdug-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  dang bral-ba #  ste / / rgod-pa # 'i sgo nas yang-dag-par #  rab tu mi 'dzin to /
saMkzepaH styAna nimitta muKe na antar saMkocaH
# sdud-pa #  ni rmugs pa dang gnyid kyi sgo nas nang-du #  zhum-pa # 'o /
vikzepaH SuBa nimitta anusAra muKena vizayezu visAraH
# g-yeng ba ni sdug-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # 'i rjes-su-'brang-ba # 'i sgo nas yul rnams la rnam-pa # r 'phro ba'o /
AlIna tva anukUlA BAvanA pratyavekzaNA nimittam niSritya Darma vipaSyanA
# zhum-pa-med-pa #  dang mthun-pa # 'i sgom-pa #  ni so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  la brten-nas #  chos la rnam-par-blta-ba # 'o /
avikzepa anukUla aSuBataH keSa Adi dravya pratyavekzA
# g-yeng ba med-pa #  dang mthun-pa #  ni skra la-sogs-pa # 'i rdzas la mi gtsang bar so-sor-rtog-pa # 'o /
tad uBaya anukUla Aloka saMjQA
# de-gnyi-ga #  dang mthun-pa #  ni snang-ba'i-'du-shes #  so /
etat ca yaTA kramam aDikRtya uktam BagavatA na ca me CandaH ati lInaH Bavizyati na ati pragRhItaH na aDyAtmam saMkziptaH na bahirDA vikziptaH paScAt pUrva saMjQI Bavizyati UrDvam aDas saMjQI ca vivRtena cetasA paryavanadDena sa praBAsa sahagatam cittam BAvayizyAmi na ca me anDakAra Ayattatvam Bavizyati cetasaH iti / Palam yaTezwa mRd haya Adi guNa nizpAdanAt
# de-yang #  bdag-gi #  'dun-pa #  ha-cang #  yang zhum-pa # r yang me 'gyur-ba #  dang ha-cang #  rab tu gzung-ba # r yang ma-yin-pa #  dang nang-du #  bsdus-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa #  dang phyi-rol #  tu g-yeng ba yang ma-yin-pa #  dang phyi-ma #  dang snga-ma # 'i 'du-shes #  dang steng dang 'og gi 'du-shes #  su bya'o snyam pa dang de-ltar #  rnam-par-phye-ba # 'i sems-kun-nas-dkris-pa #  med-pa # s snang-ba #  dang ldan-pa # 'i sems bsgom-pa # r bya'i bdag-gi-sems #  mun-pa #  can gyi tshul du ni mi-'gyur-ba # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i dbang du mdzad nas / / bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis go-rims-bzhin-du #  gsungs so / / 'bras-bu #  ni ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  rdzu-'phrul #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  bsgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
indriyANAm catvAri Arya satyAni AlaMbanam satya aBisamaya prayoga saMgRhIta tvena tad AkAra tvAt
# dbang-po #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ni 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa-bzhi #  po rnams te / / bden ba mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  la sbyor-ba # s bsdus-pa # s de'i rnam-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /

# 'bras-bu #  ni de'i dbang gis ring-po # r mi thogs-pa # r mthong-ba'i-lam #  skye-ba #  dang de nyid kyi dus na nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  la brten-pa # 'i sems-kyi-rgyud #  do /
balAnAm alaMkbana Adikam indriyEH samAnam / Pale tu viSezaH
# stobs rnams kyis dmigs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni dbang-po #  rnams dang mthun no / / 'bras-bu #  la ni bye-brag #  yod de / / 'di-ltar #  de-dag #  gi 'bras-bu #  de ni ji-skad-du #  /
taTA hi ezAm tat ca yaToktam ASradvya Adi vipakza nirleKaH ca aDikaH iti atas eva ezAm tulyAnAm AlaMbana svaBAva AdikAnAm api anavamRdyata arTa viSezeNa boDi pakza antara tvam
# ma-dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  bsrabs-pa # s lhag-pa # r bstan-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  'di dag gis dmigs-pa #  dang ngo-bo-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  mthun du zin yang mi-brdzi-ba # 'i don gyi bye-brag #  gis byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  gzhan nyid do /
boDyaFgAnAm AlaMbanam caturNAm Arya satyAnAm yaTABUtata iti paramArTaH viSudDa yAlaMbanam iti arTaH

Darma vicayaH svaBAva aFgam saMboDi lakzaNa tvAt

prasrabDiH samADiH upekzA ca asaMkleSa aFgam
# shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang btang-snyoms #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ste /
tatra prasrabDyA na saMkliSyate tayA dOzWulya srAvaNAt

samADO na saMkliSyate tatra sTitasya ASraya parivartanAt
# ting-nge-'dzin #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / de-la #  gnas-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
upekzA saMkleSaH aBiDyA dOrmanasya apagata aklizwa avasTA svaBAva tvAt
# btang-snyoms #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa #  ste / / brnab-sems #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang bral-ba #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
BAvanA smRti saMboDi aFgam BAvayati viveka miSritam iti evamAdiH eBiH caturBiH padEH yaTAkramam catur satya alaMkaMbanA boDyaFga BAvanA paridIpitA
# bsgom-pa #  ni dran-pa #  yang dag byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  dben-pa #  la gnas-pa #  bsgom-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / tshig 'di dag dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  'phags-pa'i-bden-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  bsgom-pa #  yongs-su-bstan-pa #  yin te /
taTA hi duHKam duHKataH AlaMbamAnasya tad viveka anvezaNAt duHKa alaMkanam viveka miSritam iti ucyate
# 'di-ltar #  sdug-bsngal #  la sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  dmigs-pa #  ni de-la # s dben ba tshol-ba # s sdug-bsngal #  la dmigs-pa #  ni dben-pa #  la gnas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tRzNA lakzaNam duHKa samudayam duHKa samudayataH AlaMbamAnasya tad virAga anvezaNAt tad AlaMbanam virAga niSritam
# srid-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni sdug-bsngal #  kun-'byung-ba #  ste / / sdug-bsngal #  kun-'byung-ba # r dmigs-pa #  ni de dang bral-ba #  tshol-ba # s de-la #  dmigs-pa #  ni 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  la gnas-pa # 'o /
duHKa niroDam duHKa niroDataH AlaMbamAnasya tad sAkzAtkaraNa anvezaNAt tad AlaMbanam niroDa niSritam
# sdug-bsngal #  'gog-pa #  la sdug-bsngal #  'gog-par #  dmigs-pa #  ni de mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # r 'dod-pa # s de-la #  dmigs-pa #  ni 'gog-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'o /
duHKa niroDa gAminI pratipad vyavasargaH iti ucyate tayA duHKa visarjanAt
# sdug-bsngal #  'gog-par #  'gro-ba # 'i lam ni des sdug-bsngal #  rnams spong-ba # 'i phyir rnam-par-spong-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tAm taTA alaMbamAnasya tad BAvanA anvezaNAt tad AlaMbanam vyavasarga pariNatam iti ucyate
# de-la #  de-ltar #  dmigs-pa #  ni bsgom-pa #  tshol-ba # s de-la #  dmigs-pa #  ni rnam-par-spong-ba # s yongs-su-bsgyur-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
Palam darSana heyAnAm kleSAnAm prahANam boDi aFgAnAm darSana mArga svaBAva tvAt
# 'bras-bu #  ni mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams spangs-pa #  ste / / byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  rnams kyi mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
mArga aFgAnAm AlaMbanam darSana mArgAt uttara kAlam sA eva yaTA dRzwAnAm satyAnAm yaTA BUta tA
# lam gyi yan-lag #  rnams kyi dmigs-pa #  ni de'i-'og-tu #  bden-pa #  ji-ltar #  mthong-ba #  rnams kyi yang-dag-pa-nyid #  ji-lta-ba #  de nyid do /
svaBAvaH samyak dRzwa yAdayaH azwO DarmAH
