tatra samyak dRzwiH paricCeda aFgam tayA yaTA anuBavam tattva avaDAraNAt
# de-la #  yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  ni yongs su gcod-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / des ji-ltar #  myong-ba # 'i de-kho-na #  nges-par-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samyak saMkalpaH para saMprApaNa aFgam tena yaTA aDigamam vyavasTApya vAc samutTApanAt
# yang-dag-pa'i-rtog-pa #  ni gzhan go-bar-byed-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / des ji-ltar #  rtog-pa #  rnam-pa # r bzhag nas ngag-kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
samyak vAc karma antAjIvAH para pratyaya aFgam tEH yaTAkramam aDigantuH parEdRzwa yAdi viSudDi niScayanAt
# yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang 'tsho-ba #  ni gzhan-yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / de-dag #  gi rtogs-pa #  dang lnga na-ba # 'i lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i go-rims-bzhin-du #  gzhan dag gis gtan-la-'bebs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra samyak vAcA aDigama anurUpa praSna vyAkaraNa sAMkaTya viniScayena asya darSana viSudDiH vijQAyate
# de-la #  yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  gis ni rtogs-pa #  dang mthun-par #  'dri-ba #  dang lung-ston-pa #  'bel-ba'i-gtam #  gtan-la-'bebs-pa # s de'i lta-ba #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r rnam-pa # r shes so /
samyak karma antena aBikrama pratikrama Adizu saMpanna cAritra tayA SIla viSudDiH samyak AjIvena yaTA anujQam DarmeNa cIvara Adi paryezaNAt AjIva viSudDiH iti
# yang-dag-pa # 'i lam gyi mthas ni 'gro-ba-dang-ldog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la spyod-pa #  phun su ma-tshogs-pa # s tshul-khrims #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r rnam-pa # r shes so / / yang-dag-pa'i-'tsho-ba # s ni ji-ltar #  gnang-ba #  bzhin-du #  chos-dang-mthun-pas #  gos la-sogs-pa #  tshol-ba # s yang-dag-pa'i-'tsho-ba #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r rnam-pa # r shes so /
samyak vyAyAmaH kleSa AvaraNa viSoDana aFgam tena aSeza saMyojana prahANAt
# yang-dag-pa # 'i rtsol bas ni / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-pa # r sbyor-ba # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / des kun-tu-sbyor-ba #  lhag-ma #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
samyak smRtiH upakleSa AvaraNa viSoDana aFgam tayA samyak SamaTa Adi nimitta asaMpramozeNa laya Adi upakleSa anavakASAt
# yang-dag-pa'i-dran-pa # s ni nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-sbyong-ba # 'i yan-lag #  ste / / des yang-dag-pa # 'i zhi-gnas #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  ma brjed-pa # s nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i skabs-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samyak samADiH vESezika guNa AvaraNa viSoDana aFgam tena aBijQA Adi guNa aBinirharaNAt
# yang-dag-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  ni yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  la sgrib-pa #  rnam-pa # r sbyong pa'i yan-lag #  ste / / des mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i yon-tan #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
BAvanA boDyaFga vat tat yaTA samyak dRzwim BAvayati viveka miSritAm iti vistaraH / tezAm ca padAnAm arTaH yaTA nirdizwam purastAt taTA anugantavyaH
# bsgom-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  bzhin te / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  dben-pa #  la gnas-pa #  bsgom-pa #  zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o /
pratipadAm Darma padAnAm ca pUrvavat arTa nirdeSaH veditavyaH duKA pratipada nAga mAlya rUpya miSritA yaTAkramam SamaTa vipaSya nAma anDAt / suKAH DyAna niSritAH yuga nadDa vAhi tvAt DanDa aBijQAH dvayoH api anayoH duHKa suKa niSrayayoH mRdu indriyANAm / kzipra aBijQA tayoH eva tIkzNa indriyANAm iti / SamaTaH navakAra citta sTitiH / tatra bAhya alaMbaneByaH pratisaMhRtyAH DyAtmam avikzepa ApAditaH cittasya upanibanDaH sTApanA / tasya cittasya evam Aditas upanibadDasya calasya OdArikasya tasmin= eva alaMbane saMtati yogena sUkzmIkaraNena ca aBisaMkzepaH saMsTApanA / tasya smRti saMpramozAt vahiH DA vikziptasya punar pratisaMharaNam avasTApanA / Aditas eva tasya cittasya bahis avisArAya upasTita smRtita upasTApanA / pUrvam eva vikzepa nimittezu rUpa Adizu AdIn avasaMjQAm aDipati kRtvA cittasya prasara AdAnam damanam / cetaH saMkzoBa karezu vitarka upakleSezezu AdIn avadarSanena prasara AdAnam Samanam / smRti saMpramozA dvi tarka Adi samudAcAre sati tad anaDivAsanA vyupaSamanam / aBisaMskAreNa niSCidra nirantara samADi pravAha avasTApanAH ekotIkaraNam / su aByasta tvAt anaBisaMskAreNa anABogena citta samADi pravAhasya avikzepeNa pravRttiH samADAnam iti / vipaSyanAH yaTA api tad DarmAn vicinoti iti evamAdiH / tatra carita viSoDanam AlaMbanam kOSalyAlaMbanam vA kleSa viSoDanam vA yAvat BAvikatayA vicinoti yaTAvat BAvitayA pravicinoti sa vikalpena manaskAreNa prajQA saha gatena nimittIkurvan parivitarkayati saMntIrayan parimImAMsAm Apadyate iti
# lam dang chos kyi gnas rnams kyi don ni snga-ma-bzhin-du #  bshad-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / zhi-gnas #  ni sems-gnas-pa #  rnam-pa #  dgu ste / / de-la #  phyi-rol #  gyi dmigs-pa #  rnams las phyir blan nas nang-du #  mi g-yeng bar gang dang-po #  nyid-du #  sems nye-bar-'dogs-pa #  ni 'jog-pa # 'o / / de-ltar #  sems g-yo-ba #  rags-pa #  thog-ma #  nyid-du #  nye-bar-brtags-pa #  de dmigs-pa #  de-nyid-la #  rgyun gyi tshul dang phra-ba # r byed-pa # s mngon-par-bsdus-pa #  ni rgyun-du #  'jog-pa # 'o / / brjed nas phyi-rol #  tu g-yengs par gyur-pa #  de-yang #  phyir bkug pa ste / / brlan te 'jog-pa # 'o / / sems phyi-rol #  tu mi-'phro-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir thog-ma #  nyid-du #  dran ba nye-bar-gnas-pa #  ni nye-bar-'jog-pa # 'o / / rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba'i rgyu gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la nyes-dmigs #  kyi 'du-shes #  kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  thog-ma #  nyid-du #  sems rab tu 'phror mi ster-ba #  ni dul-bar-byed-pa # 'o / / sems 'khrug-par-byed-pa #  nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # r byed-pa #  la nyes-dmigs-su-lta-ba # s 'phror mi ster-ba #  ni zhi-bar-byed-pa # 'o / / brjed nas rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  kun-tu-'byung-ba #  na de dang du mi len ba ni rnam-par-zhi-ba # r byed-pa # 'o / / mngon-par-'du-byed-pa # s skabs med cing bar-chad-med-pa # r ting-nge-'dzin #  rgyun-du #  brlan te 'jog-pa #  ni rtse gcig-tu #  byed-pa # 'o / / shin-tu #  goms-pa # 'i phyir mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  med cing lhun-gyis-grub-pa # r sems-kyi-ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi rgyun g-yeng ba med-pa # r 'byung-ba #  ni mnyam-par-'jog-pa # 'o / / lhag-mthong #  ni 'di-lta-ste # ; chos-rnams #  la rnam-par-'byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / de-la #  dpyod-pa #  rnam-par-sbyong-ba #  la dmigs-pa # 'am / / mkhas-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'am / / nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-par-sbyong-ba # 'ang rung ste / / ji-snyed-yod-pa # s rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'o / / ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yod-pa # s rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  shes-rab #  dang bcas-pa # s mtshan-ma # r byed-pa #  ni yongs su rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'o / / kun-tu-rtog-pa #  ni yongs su dpyod-par-byed-pa # 'o /
api Kalu SamaTa vipaSyanAm Agamya catvAraH mArgAH iti catvAraH mArga upadeSanAm aDikRtya
# yang zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  la brten-nas #  lam-bzhi # r 'gyur te zhes-bya-ba #  ni lam-bzhi #  bsten-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /
tatra praTamaH SamaTasya lABi tvAt aBinizIdan= eva cittam sTApayati yAvat samApatte vipaSyAnAyAH alABi tvAt tu samADim niSritya paScAt taTA anizaNNaH tAn DarmAn vicinoti yAvat parimImAMsAm Apadyate / dvitIyaH viparyayeNa veditavyaH
# de-la #  dang-po #  ni zhi-gnas #  thob-pa # 'i phyir 'dug bzhin-du #  sems 'jog-pa #  nas mnyam-par-'jog-pa # 'i bar dang lhag-mthong #  ma-thob-pa # 'i phyir ting-nge-'dzin #  de-la #  brten-nas #  phyis de-bzhin-du #  'dug ste / / chos de-dag #  la rnam-par-'byed-pa #  nas yongs su dpyod-par-byed-pa # 'i bar ngu'o; / / gnyis-pa #  ni de-la # s zlog-par-byed-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tRtIyA uBayasya alABi uBayatra yogam karoti
# gsum-pa #  ni gnyi-ga #  ma-thob-pa #  ste gnyi-ga #  la brtson par byed do /
kaTam kRtvA Sruta udgrahaNa muKena vivaSyanAyAm yogam karoti tad pUrvakam ca SamaTe
# ji-ltar #  zhe na thos-pa-'dzin-pa # 'i sgo nas lhag-mthong #  la brtson par byed do / / de sngon-du-'gro-ba # s zhi-gnas #  la brtson par byed do /
caturTaH uBayasya lABAt / ajQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriyam prayoga mArge nirveDa BAgIya saMgRhIte paQcadaSasu ca darSana mArga citta kzaNezu yat indriyam tat yaTA manu Endriyam paQca SradDA AdIni anAgamya Adi niSraya Bedena yaTAsaMBavam suKa sOmanasya dOrmanasya upekzA indriyANAm ca anyatamam
# bzhi-ba #  ni gnyi-ga #  thob-pa # 'o / / mi-shes-pa #  kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  ni sbyor-ba'i-lam #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # s bsdus-pa #  dang mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi sems-kyi-skad-cig #  bco lnga po dag la dbang-po #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / yid-kyi-dbang-po #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  lnga dang mi lcogs-pa #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gnas kyi bye-brag #  gis ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du bde-ba #  dang yid-mi-bde-ba #  dang btang-snyoms #  kyi dbang-po #  rnams las gang-yang-rung-ba # 'o /
dOrmanasya indriyam punar prayoga kAle nirveDa BAgIya pRzWena uttara vimokza spRhA saMgRhItam veditavyam
# yid-mi-bde-ba # 'i dbang-po #  ni sbyor-ba # 'i dus na nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i rjes la rnam-par-thar-pa #  mchog 'dod-pa # s bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tat etat saMBavataH daSaviDam indriyam anAjQAta pUrvasya tattvasya AjQAyE pravRtta tvAt anAjQAtam AjQAsyAmi indriyam iti ucyate
# de-dag #  ni srid-pa # s dbang-po #  rnam-pa-bcu #  ste / / de-kho-na #  sngon mi-shes-pa #  kun-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir zhugs-pa # s mi-shes-pa #  kun-shes-par-byed-pa # 'i dbang-po #  zhes-bya'o #  /
etat eva daSaviDam indriyam zoXaSAt darSanam arga citta kzaNAt yAvat vajra upamaH samADiH iti etasmin SEkzamA arge AjQa indriyam iti ucyate apUrva jQeya aBAvAt
# dbang-po #  rnam-pa-bcu-po #  'di dag nyid mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi sems-kyi-skad-cig #  bcu drug-pa #  nas rdo-rje #  lta-bu # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  ces bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  slob-pa'i-lam #  de-la #  kun-shes-pa'i-dbang-po #  zhes bya ste /
etat eva punar navaviDam indriyam dOrmanasya indriya varjam aSEkzamA arge AjQAtO= indriyam iti ucyate AjQA tA vinaH arhat indriyam iti kRtvA
# sngon ma-mthong-ba # 'i shes-bya #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yid-mi-bde-ba # 'i dbang-po #  ma-rtogs-pa # r dbang-po #  rnam-pa #  dgu po de-dag-nyid #  mi-slob-pa # 'i lam la kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa # 'i dbang-po #  zhes bya ste / / kun-shes-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  ni dgra-bcom-pa # 'i dbang-po #  yin pa'i phyir ro; /
BAvanA mArga aDikAreNa idam api vakzyate
# bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyi skabs su 'di yang brjod-pa # r bya ste /
UrDva BUmike mArge saMmuKIBAvena BAvyamAne asaMmuKIBUtAni api aDoBikAni kuSala mUlakAni BAvanAm gacCanti tezu viBu tva lABAt / viBu tvam punar uttapta saMmuKIBAvena taSitA veditavyA
# gong-ma # 'i sa pa'i lam la mngon-du-byed-pa #  bsgom-pa #  na sa-'og-ma # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba mngon-sum-du #  ma-gyur-pa #  rnams kyang bsgom-pa # r 'gyur te / / de-dag #  la dbang 'byor-ba #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / dbang 'byor-ba #  ni mchog-tu #  sbyangs-pa #  thob-pa #  ste / / mngon-sum-du-byed-pa #  ni dbang du rig-par-bya # 'o /
nizWA mArgaH sarva dOzWulyAnAm pratiprasrabDeH iti vistaraH / tatra sarva dOzWulyAni caturvitiH Bavanti
# mthar-phyin-pa # 'i lam ni gnas-ngan-len #  thams-cad #  rgyun-chad-pa #  zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  de-la #  gnas-ngan-len #  thams-cad #  ni nyi shu rtsa bzhi yin te /
tat yaTA sarvatragam aBilApa dOzWulyam yA cakzuH Adi sarva Darma nAma aBiniveSa vAsanA Alaya vijQAne saMnivizwAna Adi kAla anusRtAH yAsO= ucyate prapaQca vAsanA iti yatas cakzuH AdayaH DarmAH sanAma aBiniveSAH punar punar pravartante iti
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / mngon-par-brjod-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni kun-tu #  'gro-ba #  ni mig la-sogs-pa #  chos-thams-cad #  kyi ming la mngon bar zhen-pa # 'i bag-chags #  kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  la gnas-pa #  thog-ma-med-pa # 'i dus nas rjes-su-zhugs-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / de-la # s mig la-sogs-pa # 'i chos ming la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  rnams yang-dang-yang #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir te de ni spros-pa # 'i bag-chags #  zhes-bya'o #  /
vedita dOzWulyam sa AsravANAm vedanAnAm vAsanA / kleSa dOzWulyam kleSAnAm anuSayaH
# tshor-ba # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i tshor-ba #  rnams kyi bag-chags #  so / / nyon-mongs-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyi bag-la-nyal #  lo /
karma dOzWulyam sa AsravANAm karmaNAm vAsanA
# las-kyi-gnas #  ngan len ni zag-pa-dang-bcas-pa # 'i las rnams kyi bag-chags #  so /
vipAka dOzWulyam vipAkasya karmaNya tA
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i lus-las #  su mi-rung-ba #  nyid do /
kleSa AvaraNa dOzWulyam tIvra Ayata kleSa tA
# nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  mi bzad cing rgyun-ring-ba # 'o /
karma AvaraNa dOzWalyam mArga antarAyikA anantara Adi kakarma AvRta tA
# las-kyi-sgrib-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni lam gyi bar-chad-byed-pa #  mtshams-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las-kyi-sgrib-pa #  nyid do /
vipAka AvaraNa dOzWulyam satya aBisamaya viDura nAraka Adi Atma BAva pratilamBaH
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i sgrib-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len ni bden-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa #  sems-can #  dmyal-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i lus thob-pa # 'o /
nivaraNa dOzWulyam kuSala pakza prayoga antarAyika kAma Canda Adi aBiBUta tA
# sgrib-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len ni dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor-ba'i-bar-chad #  byed-pa #  'dod-pa-la-'dun-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s zil-gyis-gnon-pa #  nyid do /
vitarka dOzWulyam pravrajyABiH ati vibanDa kAma vitarka Adi aBiBUta tA
# rtog-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni rab-tu-'byung-ba #  la gags byed-pa #  'dod-pa #  la rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s zil byis gnon-pa #  nyid do /
AhAra dOzWulyam ati alpa bahu Bojana nena prayoga ayogya tA
# zas kyi gnas-ngan-len #  ni za ha-cang-nyung-ba #  dang mang-du-zos-pa # s sbyor-ba # 'i 'os sum gyur ba nyid do /
mETuna dOzWulyam dvaya dvaya samApatti kRtA kAya citta vyaTA
# 'khrig-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni gnyis kyis gnyis phrad-pa #  las gyur-pa #  dang lus dang sems la gnod-pa # 'o /
svapna dOzWulyam midDa kRtam ASraya jAXyam
# rmi-lam #  gyi gnas-ngan-len #  ni gnyid las gyur ba'i lus sems po nyid do /
vyADi dOzWulyam DAtu vEzamya kRta asvasTa tA
# nad kyi gnas-ngan-len #  ni khams-ma-snyoms-pa #  las gyur ba'i nyams rab tu mi-bde-ba #  nyid do /
jarA dOzWulyam BUta vipariNAma kRta aviDeya tA
# rga-ba # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni 'byung-bar-'gyur-ba #  las gyur ba'i dbang-med-pa #  nyid do /
maraNa dOzWulyam mriyamANasya sarva indriya Akula tA
# 'chi-ba # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni 'chi-ba #  na dbang-po #  thams-cad #  'khrug-pa # 'o /
pariSrama dOzWulyam atigamana Adi kRtaH aFgamardaH
# yongs-su-ngal-ba # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni ha-cang #  'gro-ba #  las gyur ba'i lus-dub-pa # 'o /
dRXa dOzWulyam yaTAsaMBavam eta deva aBilApa dOzWulya Adikam aparinirvANavatAm
# gnas-ngan-len #  bstan-pa #  ni mngon-par-brjod-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  la-sogs-pa #  'di dag dang ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar te / / yongs su mya-ngan #  las mi 'da' ba'i chos-can #  no /
OdArika maDya sUkzma dOzWulyAni yaTAkramam kAmarUpA rUpya avarANi veditavyAni
# gnas-ngan-len #  chen-po #  dang 'bring dang chung du ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o /
kleSa AvaraNa dOzWulyam SrAvaka pratyekabudDa boDi vipakzaH
# nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sgrib ba'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi byang-chub #  kyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  so /
samApattyA AvaraNa dOzWulyam nava anupUrva samApatti aBinirhAra vipakzaH
# snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sgrib-pa'i-gnas #  ngan len ni / / mthar gyi gnas ba'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  dgu mngon bar bsgrub-pa # 'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  so /
jQeya AvaraNa dOzWulyam sarvajQa tA vipakzaH / iti evam ezAm yaTAyogam sarva dOzWulyAnAm pratiprasra venizWA mArgaH
# shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  ni thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  kyi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  so / / de-ltar #  gnas-ngan-len #  'di dag thams-cad #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du rgyun bcad-pa #  ni mthar-phyin-pa # 'i lam ste /
yaTA uktam tasya cetaH vimukteH pAripUryA prajQA vimukteH pAripUryA kAya dOzWulyAnAm pratiprasrabDeH / smRtyA samanvAgama hetoH evam asya praTamam dvAram sudAntam Bavati su guptam su rakzitam su saMvRtam suBAzitam yat uta cakzuH vijQeyezu rUpezu evam yAvat manaH vijQeyezu Darmezu iti
# ji-skad-du #  sems rnam-par-grol-ba #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  dang shes-rab #  rnam-par-grol-ba #  yongs-su-rdzogs-nas #  lus-kyi-gnas-ngan-len #  rnams rgyun bcad de / / dran-pa-dang-ldan-pa # 'i rgyus 'di-ltar #  de'i sgo dang-po #  'di-lta-ste #  / / mig gis rnam-par-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i gzugs rnams la shin-tu #  dul-ba #  dang shin-tu #  spas pa dang shin-tu-bsrungs-pa #  dang shin-tu-bsdams-pa #  dang shin-tu-bsgoms-pa #  yin te / / yid kyis rnam-par-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi bar la zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o; /
vajra upamaH samADiH BAvanA mArgasya antyA prahANa mArga avasTA veditavyA
# rdo-rje #  lta-bu # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gyi mtha'i spong-ba # 'i lam gyi gnas-skabs #  su rig-par-bya # 'o /
sa ca samADiH nirantaraH tad pravAharaya lOkikena mArge Na antara AKaNXanAt
# ting-nge-'dzin #  de-yang #  bar-chad-med-pa #  ste / / de'i rkyen gyis 'jig-rten-pa'i-spyod-pa # s rab tu phan mi-phyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dRXaH sarva AvaraNEH acCidraNAt sarva AvaraNa BeditayA ca sAratvAt / eka rasaH iti nirvikalpa eka rasa tvAt
# brtan-pa #  ni sgrib-pa #  thams-cad-kyi # s mi phigs pa dang sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  ni phigs pas sra-ba # 'i phyir ro / / ro gcig pa ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  ro gcig pa'i phyir ro /
vyApI sarva jQeya sAmAnya taTa tAlaMbana tvAt
# khyab-pa #  ni shes-bya-thams-cad #  kyi spyi'i de-bzhin-nyid #  la dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
etad arTa pratibimbana arTa BagavatA uktam tat yaTA mahA SElaH parvataH aKaNXaH acCidraH aSuziraH ekaDanaH su saMvRtaH iti / nirantara ASraya parivRtti viDAna arka kzamArga lABinaH
# de'i don dang 'dra-bar #  bya-ba # 'i don-du #  bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis dper-na #  brag chen-po #  ma grum pa ser ka med-pa #  khong stong ma-yin-pa #  gcig-tu-bsdus-pa #  shin-tu #  mkhregs pa zhes gsungs so / / gnas-ma #  lus par gyur-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste /
citta ASraya parivRttiH Darma tA cittasya prakRti praBAsvarasya aSeza Agantu kopa kleSa apagama AdyA parivRttiH taTatA parivRttiH iti arTaH
# mi-slob-pa # 'i lam thob-pa # 'i sems kyi gnas gyur ba ni chos-nyid #  kyi sems rang-bzhin-gyis #  'od-gsal-ba #  glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  ma-lus-pa #  dang bral-ba # s gnas-gyur-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / de-bzhin-nyid #  du gyur zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
mArga ASraya parivRtiH pUrvam lOkikaH mArgaH aBisamaya kAle lokottara tvena parivRtaH SEkzaH ca ucyate sa avaSeza karaNIya tvAt
# lam gyi gnas-gyur-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  snga-ma #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i dus na 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  nyid-du #  gyur-pa #  ste / / bya-ba # 'i lhag-ma #  yod-pa # 'i phyir slob-pa #  zhes kyang bya'o /
yadA tu nirhata aSeza vipakzaH Bavati trEDAtuka vErAgyAt tadA asya mArga svaBAvasya ASrayasya paripUrNA parivRttiH vyavasTApyate
# gang-gi-tshe #  khams-gsum-pa #  la 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ma-lus-par #  gyur bar bsal-ba #  de'i tshe lam gyi ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi gnas-gyur-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
dOzWulya ASraya parivRttiH Alaya vijQAnasya sarva kleSa anuSaya apagamena parivRttiH veditavyA
# gnas-ngan-len #  gyi gnas-gyur-pa #  ni kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa #  nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  kyi bag-la-nyal #  gyi bag-chags #  dang bral-ba # r gyur bar rig-par-bya # 'o /
kzaye sati vizaye vA tasmin yat jQAnam kzaya jQAnam etat uktam Bavati
# zad-pa # r gyur nas shes-pa # 'am / / yul de-la #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni zad-pa-shes-pa #  ste /
niravaSezam prakzINe samudaye yat jQAnam tad avasTasya hetu niroDa alaMkanam vA kzaya jQAnam iti
# de ni 'di-skad-du #  kun nas 'byung-ba #  ma-lus-par #  spangs-nas #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dang de'i-gnas #  skabs na rgyu 'gog-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  ni zad-pa-shes-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
taTA anutpAde sati vizaye vA tasmin yat jQAnam anutpAda jQAnam AyatyAm sarvasya duHKasya atyantam anutpatti DarmatAyAm satyAm yat jQAnam anya satya alaMkbanam iti
# de-bzhin-du #  mi-skye-ba # r gyur nas shes-pa # 'am / / yul de-la #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni mi-skye-ba-shes-pa #  ste / / phyi-ma-la #  sdug-bsngal-thams-cad #  gtan-du #  mi-skye-ba'i-chos #  nyid-du #  gyur nas shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni bden-pa #  gzhan la dmigs-pa #  yang yin pa'o /
yat vA duHKa satyA anutpAda alaMkanam tat anutpAda jQAnam iti arTaH
# yang-na #  gang sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden ba la mi-skye-ba # r dmigs-pa #  de mi-skye-bar-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
daSA SEkzAH DarmAH aSEkzAn SIla AdIn paQca skanDAn aDikRtya
# mi-slob-pa # 'i chos bcu ni mi-slob-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste /

# de-la #  mi-slob-pa # 'i yang-dag-pa'i-ngag #  dang las-kyi-mtha' #  dang 'tsho-ba #  rnams ni mi-slob-pa # 'i tshul-khrims-kyi-phung-po # 'o / / yang-dag-pa'i-dran-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi phung-po # 'o /
samyak dRzwi saMkalpa vyAyAmAH prajQA skanDaH
# yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  dang rtog-pa #  dang rtsol ba rnams ni shes-rab #  kyi phung-po # 'o /
samyak vimuktiH vimuktiH skanDaH / samyak jQAnam vimuktiH jQAna darSana skanDaH iti / punar mArgasatyasya catvAraH AkArAH catvAri lakzaNAni
# yang-dag-pa # 'i rnam-par-grol-ba #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i phung-po # 'o / / yang-dag-pa # 'i shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i ye-shes-mthong-ba # 'i phung-po # 'o / / yang lam gyi bden-pa # 'i rnam-pa-bzhi #  dang mtshan-nyid-bzhi # 'o /
tatra tattva arTa mArgayati anA iti mArgaH / ayaTA BUtAnAm kleSAnAm pratipakza tvAt nyAyaH
# de-la #  'dis de-kho-na # 'i lam tshol-ba # s lam mo / / rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams kyi gnyen-por-gyur-pa #  sa rigs-pa # 'o /
tattva anavaboDa dozeNa anitya Adi viparyAsEH viparyastasya cittasya aviparyAse tattva avaboDe pratipAdanAt pratipad
# de-kho-na #  khong du-ma #  chud-pa # 'i nyes-pa # s mi-rtag-pa #  la rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r phyin-ci-log-pa #  rnams kyis phyin-ci-log #  tu gyur-pa # 'i sems phyin-ci-log #  med-pa #  de-kho-na #  khong du-ma #  chud-pa #  la 'jog-pa # s sgrub-pa # 'o /
nityaH Atyantike niHsaraNa pade yAnAt nEryANikaH iti
# nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i gnas rtag-pa #  brtan du-ba # r 'gro-ba # s nges-par #  'byin ba zhes-bya'o #  /
duHKa Adi satyezu anitya AdayaH zoXa SAkArAH lOkikAH lokottarAH ca santi
# sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bden-pa #  rnams la mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  drug ni 'jig-rten-pa #  yang yod 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  yang yod de /
tatra lOkikAH jQeye aprazwAH sAvaraNAH savikalpAH ca taTatAyAH aprativeDAt kleSa anuSayitvA adaBilApa muKena prapaQcanAt ca yaTAkramam
# de-la #  'jig-rten-pa #  rnams ni shes-bya #  la legs-par #  ma zhugs-pa #  dang sgrub-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  dang rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  ste / / de-bzhin-nyid #  ma-rtogs-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i bag-la-nyal #  yod-pa #  dang mngon-par-brjod-pa # 'i sgo nas spros-pa # 'i phyir te /
viparyayeNa loka uttarAH su pravizwAH nirAvaraNAH ca santaH nirvikalpa tayA lOkikeByaH viSizyante / kaTam punar ete avikalpayantaH jQeyezu pravizwAH Bavanti
# go-rims #  bzhin no / / bzlog-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  ste / / rgas-pa # r zhugs-pa #  dang sgrib-pa-med-pa # r gyur nas rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # s 'jig-rten-pa #  rnams las khyad-par #  du 'gyur ro / / de-dag #  rnam-pa # r mi rtog na ji-ltar #  shes-bya #  la legs-par-zhugs-pa # r gyur zhe na /
yasmAt etezu vartamAnaH anitya arTa paSyati sAkzAt anuBavati na tu anityam iti paSyati aBilApa prapaQca muKena iti
# 'di-ltar #  'di dag la gnas-pa #  ni mi-rtag-pa'i-don #  mthong zhing mngon du myong gi / / mi rtag go zhes mngon-par-brjod-pa #  dang spros-pa # 'i sgo nas mthong-ba #  ni ma yin no /
evam duHKa Adizu AkArezu yojayitavyam / Darma viniScayaH nAma tRtIyaH samuccayaH / Darma viniScaye DarmaH dvAdaSa aFgam vacaH gatam / tatra sUtram yat aBipreta arTa sUcana AkAreNa gadya BAzitam
# de-bzhin-du #  sdug-bsngal #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams la yang sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / bden-pa #  rnam-par-nges-pa # 'o / / chos rnam-par-nges-pa #  la chos ni gsung-rab-tu-gtogs-pa #  yan-lag-bcu-gnyis #  te / / de-la #  mdo'i-sde #  ni gang-bzhed-pa # 'i don smos-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  rkyang-ba # r gsungs-pa # 'o / / ci'i-phyir #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # s bzhed-pa # 'i don rnam-pa # r phye ste /
kim punar kAraNam taTAgataH tam aBipretam arTa vivRtya eva na deSayati iti Aha daSa anuSaMsAn saMpaSyan= taTAgataH sUcana AkAreNa Darmam deSayati
# ma gsungs she na / / smas pa / / phan yon bcu gzigs-nas #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  smos-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  chos ston te /
suKam vyavasTApayati dESikEH hi bahuDA vyavasTApya prApaNIyasya arTasya saMkzipya akRcCreNa vyavasTApanAt / suKam deSayati alpena mahataH arTa vistarasya pratyAyanAt tat yaTA sTApayati saMsTApayati iti evamAdi / SrotA api suKam udgRhNAti
# rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r sla-ba #  ni ston-pa # s go-ba # r bya-ba # 'i don rnam-pa #  mang-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  mdor bsdus te / / tshegs-chung-ngus #  rnam-par-'jog-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bshad sla-ba #  ni tshig nyung-ngu # s don chen-po #  rgyas-pa # r go-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir te / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'jog-pa #  dang rgyun-du #  'jog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / nyen-pa # s kyang gzung sla-ba # 'o /
Darma gOrava tayA kzipram saMBArAn paripUrayati BAva gamyaH ayam DarmaH iti avagamya jAta AsTasya tasmin Darme Adara muKena SradDA Adi saMBAra paripUraNAt
# chos la gus-pa # s myur-du #  tshogs yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa #  ni chos 'di dag bsgoms-pa # s shes-par-bya-ba #  yin par rtogs-nas #  gus-pa-skyes-pa #  chos de-la #  gces spras su bya-ba # 'i sgo nas dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshogs yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ASu Darma tAm prativiDyati taTA Adara prayogiNaH prajQAyAH tEkzNIBAvAt
# myur-du #  chos-nyid #  rtogs-par-'gyur-ba #  ni de-ltar #  gces spras su bya-ba #  sbyor-ba # 'i shes-rab #  rno-ba # r gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ratnezu avetya prasAdam pratilaBate deSanAyAH su vyavasTita BAva gamena dESika Adizu aBiprasAdya utpAdAt
# dkon-mchog #  rnams la shes-nas-dad-pa #  thob-pa #  ni bstan-pa #  la legs-par #  rnam-par-gnas-pa # r khong-du-chud-nas #  ston-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la dad-pa #  skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /

# mthong-ba # 'i chos la bde-bar-gnas-pa # 'i mchog la reg-pa #  ni dgongs-pa'i-don #  rtsol ba chen-po # s bsams nas rtogs-pa # s rab-tu-dga'-ba # 'i khyad-par-thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sAMkaTya viniScayena satAm cittam ArADayati gUXa arTa vivaraNAt atas eva paNXitaH paNXitaH iti saMKyAm gacCati yaSaH asya samantAt niScarati iti arTaH
# 'phel-ba # 'i gtam gyis gtan-la-'bebs-pa # s dam-pa #  rnams kyi sems-mgu-bar-byed-pa #  ni don zab-pa #  rnam-par-'byed-pa # s de'i-phyir #  mkhas-pa #  mkhas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i grangs su 'gro ste / / 'di'i snyan-pa #  kun-tu #  'byung zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

# gleng-gzhi'i-sde #  ni gang-zag #  'ga' zhig gi ched du gsungs-pa #  dang byung-ba-dang-bcas-pa # 'i bslab-pa #  bcas-pa #  gsungs-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / gzhi 'di dang skabs 'di zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o / / rtogs-pa-brjod-pa'i-sde #  ni dpe dang bcas-pa # r gsungs-pa #  ste / / des don gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir te / / mngon du gsal-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

# nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  the-tshom #  gyi gnyen-po # r ni mdo-sde'i-sde-snod #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / gdul bya rnams kyi som nyi byung-ba #  bcad-pa # 'i ched du mdo'i-sde #  dang dbyangs-kyis-bsnyad-pa'i-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  bshad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vinaya piwaka vyavasTAnam anta dvaya anuyoga upakleSa pratipakzeNa saMniDikAra pariBoga Adi pratikzepAt Sata sAhasraka vastra anujQAnAt ca / anta dvayam punar kAma suKa llika antaH Atma klema An ca
# nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  mtha'-gnyis #  dang ldan-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r 'dul-ba # 'i sde-snod #  / / rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / sog 'jog byed-pa # s yongs-su-spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  spong-ba #  dang brgya stong ri ba'i gos la-sogs-pa #  gnas ba'i phyir ro / / mtha'-gnyis #  ni 'dod-pa #  bsod snyoms kyi mtha' dang bdag dub-pa # 'i mtha'o /

# rang-gi #  lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # 'i nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r chos-mngon-pa # 'i sde-snod #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste / / der chos-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  rgya-cher #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar sUtra piwakam niSritya vineyAH SikzA traye vyutpadyante tatra tasya vistareNa udBAvita tvAt
# yang mdo-sde'i-sde-snod #  la brten-nas #  gdul bya rnams bslab-pa-gsum #  la byang-ba # r byed do / / de-la # s de rgyas-pa # r brjod-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# 'dul-ba #  la brten-nas #  lhag-pa'i-tshul-khrims #  dang lhag-pa'i-sems #  kyi bslab-pa #  bsgrub ste / / der so-sor-thar-pa # 'i sngom-pa # 'i bslab-pa'i-lam #  nye-bar #  bstan-pa #  la brten-pa #  la brten-nas #  tshul-khrims #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba #  dang de yongs-su-dag-pa # r 'gyur te / / 'gyod-pa-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  sems-mnyam-par-'jog-pa # 'i phyir ro /

punar sUtra piwakam niSritya granTa arTa vyutpattiH

# 'dus ba la brten-nas #  gnyi-ga #  mngon-sum-du #  byed do / / 'dul-ba # 'i sde-snod #  ni bslab-pa #  sgrub-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tatas Darma arTayoH sAkzAtkriyAyAH pada sTAnam iti ucyate ASraya arTena
# de'i-phyir #  chos-dang-don #  mngon-sum-du-bya-ba # 'i gnas yin-pas #  gzhi'i-gnas #  zhes-bya'o #  /
aBiDarmam niSritya parasparam sAMkaTya viniScaya kRtena Darma saMBogena sparSa vihAraH Bavati tatra bahu prakAram DarmANAm sva lakzaNa Adi Darma tAyAH vyutpAdanAt
# chos-mngon-pa #  la brten-nas #  phan tshun 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  gtan-la-'bebs-pa #  las gyur ba'i chos la rdzogs-pa # r longs-spyod-pa # s bde-ba-la-reg-pa # r gnas-pa # r 'gyur te / / der chos rnam-pa # r mang-po #  rnams kyi rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  la byang-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
etAni eva trINi piwakAni caturaSIti Darma skanDa sahasrANi Bavanti SrAvaka yAna aDikAreNa yAni sTavira Anandena udgRhItAni / kim punar ekasya Darma skanDasya parimANam
# nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'i skabs su gnas-brtan #  kun dga'-bo # s chos-kyi-phung-po #  brgyad khri bzhi stong gang dag gzung-ba #  rnams ni sde-snod #  gsum po 'di dag nyid yin no / / chos-kyi-phung-po #  gcig gi tshad ji tsam zhe na /
daSa Sata saMKyaH Darma skanDaH sahasra saMKyaH iti arTaH
# grangs brgya phrag bcu ni chos-kyi-phung-po #  ste / / grangs stong zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
yadi evam sahasra saMKyaH iti evam ki na ucyate
# gal-te #  de lta yin na grangs stong zhes de-skad #  du ci'i-phyir #  mi brjod ce na /
sAhasrikA eka skanDa vyavasTAne prayojana jQApana arTam / taTA hi eka Adi vRdDayA daSa saMKyA Sata saMKyA sahasra Adi saMKyAH / tad daSa Sata saMKyAH upanizadaH drazwavyAH / tat yaTA daSa SatAni sahasram Satam sahasrANAm Sata sahasram Satam Sata sahasrANAm kowiH iti evam sarva asUttarAsu saMKyAsu avaSyam anayoH daSa Sata saMKyayoH anyatara upanizad Bavati
# phung-po #  re-re #  la yang stong stong rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i dgongs-pa #  brtan-pa # 'i phyir te / / 'di-ltar #  gcig la-sogs-pa #  bskyed na grangs bcur 'gyur ro / / bcur bskyed na grangs bcur 'gyur ro / / grangs stong la-sogs-pa # 'i gzhi ni grangs brgya phrag bcu yin par blta'o / / 'di-lta-ste #  brgya phrag bcu ni stong ngo / / stong phrag brgya ni 'bum mo / / 'bum-phrag #  brgya ni bye-ba # 'o / / de-bzhin-du #  grangs gong-ma #  thams-cad-la #  yang brgya dang bcu po 'di gnyis las gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig gdon-mi-za-bar #  gzhir 'gyur te /
atas ete eva samasya daSa SatAni ekaH Darma skanDaH vyavasTApyate
# de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  bsdus na brgya phrag bcu po de-dag #  la chos-kyi-phung-po #  gcig rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
anayA ca gaNanayA caturaSIti Darma skanDa sahasrANi azwO kowyaH catvAriSat ca lakzAH Bavanti
# bgrad pa'i tshul 'dis na chos-kyi-phung-po #  brgyad khri bzhi stong gi tshig le 'ur byas-pa #  bye-ba #  phrag brgyad dang 'bum-phrag #  bzhi bcur 'gyur ro /
saH eza piwaka traya saMgRhItaH DarmaH kasya gocaraH
# bam po bdun pa / / sde-snod #  gsum gyis bsdus-pa # 'i chos 'di dag gang-gi #  spyod yul yin zhe na /
Sruta maya AdInAm citta cEtasikAnAm gocaraH AlaMbanam iti arTaH
# thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi spyod yul te / / dmigs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
etat saMgena sAlaMbana Adi lakzaNAnAm citta cEtasikAnAm Darmam AraBya alaMkbana Adikam vyavasTApyate
# de'i zhar la dmigs-pa-dang-bcas-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyi chos las brtsams te dmigs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
tatra Darme tezAm kim AlaMbanam
# de-la #  chos kyi nang nas de-dag #  gi dmigs-pa #  gang zhe na /
sUtra Adi nAma pada vyaQjana kAya saMgRhItA sUtra Adi deSanA iti arTaH
# mdo'i-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs kyis bsdus-pa # 'i mdo'i-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  bshad-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
AkAraH yAn skanDa AdIn arTa prakAra anAraBya sA deSanA tad AkArAH te citta cEtasikAH veditavyAH
# rnam-pa #  ni gang phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don gyi rnam-pa #  rnams las brtsams te bstan-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni rnam-pa #  rnams te / / de-dag #  ni sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o /
ASrayaH para vijQapti smRtiH vAsanA ca
# gnas ni gzhan-las #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  dang dran-pa #  dang-ba # g chags so /
tatra deSanA kAle para vijQaptiH ASrayaH yaH asO= ucyate paratas GozataH iti tatas uttara kAlam smRtiH ASrayaH yaTASrutam anusmRtya aByasanAt
# de-la #  bshad-pa # 'i dus na gzhan-las #  rnam-par-rig-pa #  gnas te / / de ni gzhan gyi sgra las-shes-pa #  'byung ngo / / de'i-'og-tu #  dran-pa #  gnas te ji-ltar #  thos-pa #  bzhin-du #  rjes-su-dran-pa # s goms-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatas uttarakAlam vAsanA SrayaH tad anusmRtim antareNa api paScAt aByAsa BAvanA balena pratiBAsanAt iti
# de'i-'og-tu #  bag-chags #  gnas te / / de'i rjes-su-dran-pa #  med kyang goms-pa # 'i bag-chags #  kyi dbang gis phyis snang-ba # r 'gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
saMprayogaH citta cEtasikAnAm anyonya sahAya BAvena sUtra Adi AlaMbane skanDa Adi pratisaMyukta arTa AkArEH saMpratipattiH / SUtuH tu eva Uharme AlaMbana praBedaH vyApya alaMkbana AdikaH caturviDaH
# mtshungs-par-ldan-pa #  ni sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams gcig gi grogs gcig yin pa'i tshul-gyis #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa #  dang rab tu ldan-pa'i-don #  gyi rnam-pa #  rnams kyi mdo-sde #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  yang-dag-par-rtogs-pa # 'o / / chos-la-dmigs-pa #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni khyab-pa'i-dmigs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi # 'o /
vyApya alaMbanam punar sa vikalpa pratibimba Adi Bedena catur biDam
# khyab-pa'i-dmigs-pa #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i gzugs-brnyan #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa-bzhi # 'o /
tatra aDimukti manaskAraH ekAnta lOkikaH yaH manaskAraH / tattvamanaskAraH lokottaraH tad pRzWa labDaH ca
# de-la #  mos-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni gang gcig-tu #  'jig-rten-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # 'o / / de-kho-na #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  dang de-kho-na # 'i rjes-las-thob-pa # 'o /
yAvat BAvika tayA DarmANAm etAvanti sarva Darma vastuni yat jQeya vyavasTAnam tat yaTA skanDa DAtu AyatanAni
# chos-rnams #  kyi ji-snyed-yod-pa #  ni chos-thams-cad #  kyi dngos-po #  'di dag tu zad do zhes gang zhes bya rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  rnams so /
yaTAvat BAvitayA eBiH prakArEH su jQeyam iti
# ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yod-pa #  ni rnam-pa # r 'di dag tu de shes-par-bya-ba #  ste /
tat yaTA satyamuKena tAni eva skanDa DAtu AyatanAni yaTAsaMBavam duHKa tojQeyAni yAvat mArgataH
# 'di-ltar #  bden-pa # 'i sgo nas phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  de-dag-nyid #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sdug-bsngal #  nyid-du #  shes-par-bya-ba #  nas lam gyi bar-du # 'o /
AkAra muKena ekEkam satyam caturBiH AkArEH jQeyam aviSezatas ca sarvANi taTatA AkAreNa
# rnam-pa # 'i sgo nas bden-pa #  re-re #  la yang rnam-pa-bzhi #  bzhis shes-pa # r bya'o / / bye-brag-med-par #  na thams-cad #  kyang de-bzhin-nyid #  kyis rnam-par-shes-pa # r bya'o /
Darma uddAna aDikAreNa vA anityataH sarva saMskArA jQeyA yAvat SAntataH nirvANam
# chos kyi sdom gyi skabs kyis na 'du-byed-thams-cad #  mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  du shes-par-bya-ba #  nas / / mya-ngan #  las 'das bzhi-ba #  nyid kyi bar-du # 'o /
vimokza aDikAreNa vA SUnyataH yAvat animittataH iti
# rnam-par-thar-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i skabs kyis na stong ba nyid nas mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'i bar-du # 'i /
kArya parinizpattiH ASraya parinizpattiH parinivRtta ASrayasya aviparIta alaMkbana saMpraKyAnAt
# dgos-pa #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni gnas-gyur-pa #  grub-pa #  ste / / gnas-gyur-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r snang-ba #  nyid do /
yaTAvat BAvitAyAH nirdaSe zoXa SaprakArAH uktAH trayaH ca vimokza AkArAH tezAm ca anyonya saMgrahaH / kaTa kRtvA
# ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yod-pa # r bstan-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  drug dang rnam-par-thar-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  bstan-pa #  de-dag #  ni gcig-gis-gcig #  sdud do / / ji lta zhe na /
zoXaSAnAm AkArANAm dvO SUnyatA AkArO SUnya AkAra anAtma AkAraH ca
# rnam-pa-bcu #  drug gi nang nas gnyis ni stong-pa-nyid #  kyi rnam-pa #  ste / / stong-pa'i-rnam-pa #  dang bdag-med-pa'i-rnam-pa # 'o / / drug ni smon-pa-med-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  ste /
zaXa praNihita AkArAH anitya AkArAH duHKa AkAraH hetu samudaya praBava pratyaya AkArAH ca tEH trEDAtuke aprapraNiDAnAt
# mi-rtag-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal-gyi-rnam-pa #  dang rgyu dang kun-'byung-ba #  dang rab-tu-skye-ba #  dang rkyen gyi rnam-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  gis khams-gsum-pa #  la smon-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
azwa avinimitta AkArAH SezAH niroDa mArgayoH nimittIkartum aSakya tvAt
# lhag-ma #  brgyad ni mtshan-ma-med-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  ste / / 'gog-pa #  dang lam la mtshan-ma # r byed mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
carita viSoDanam AlaMbanam rAga carita AdInAm aSuBa Adi tena utsada rAga Adi upaSamanAt
# spyod-pa #  rnam-par-sbyong-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'dod-chags #  la spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mi-sdug-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / des 'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa # 'i shas-che-ba #  nye-bar-zhi-ba # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
avidyA AdayaH DarmAH saMskAra AdIn DarmAn aBizyandayanti na hi ezAm nirhetukaH utpAdaH na api ISvara Adi vizama hetukaH iti yat jQAnam idam pratItyasamutpAda kOSalyam
# ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  ni 'du-byed #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  mngon du 'byin te / / 'di dag rgyu-med-pa #  las byung par ma yin zhing dbang-phyug #  la-sogs-pa #  mi-mthun-pa'i-rgyu #  las byung-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # r shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni / / rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba #  la mkhas-pa # 'o /
Darma mAtra hetuka tve api sati anurUpAt hetoH anurUpasya eva Palasya utpattiH tat yaTA su caritasya izwaH vipAkaH duScaritasya anizwaH iti evamAdi yat jQAnam idam sTAna asTAna kOSalyam veditavyam
# chos tsam gyi rgyu-las-byung-ba #  yin-du-zin #  kyang mthun-pa # 'i rgyu las mthun-pa # 'i 'bras-bu-nyid #  'byung ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  legs-par-spyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  sdug-pa #  dang nyes-par-spyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  mi-sdug-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  la mkhas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
kleSa viSoDanam AlaMbanam lOkikam Arga aDikAreNa aDas UrDva BUmInAm OdArika SAnta tA tena paryavasTAna vizkamBaNAt
# nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-par-sbyong-ba # 'i dmigs-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  gyi gnas-skabs #  su sa-'og-ma #  dang gong-ma #  rnams kyis rags-pa #  dang zhi-ba #  nyid des kun-nas-dkris-pa #  rnam-pa # r gnon-pa # 'i phyir ro /
lokottara mArga aDikAreNa samAsatas taTatA vyAsena catvAri Arya satyAni tena anuSaya samudGAtAt
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyi skabs su ni bsdu na de-bzhin-nyid #  do / / spros na 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa-bzhi #  ste / / des bag-la-nyal #  legs-par-bcom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sUtra Adi Darma vicArANAm saMbnaDena catasraH yuktayaH varNyante tABiH tad vicAraNAt / tatra apekzA yuktiH yA saMskArANAm utpattO pratyaya apekzA tat yaTA aFkurasya utpattO bIja udaka kzetrANi apekzyante vijQAnasya indriya arTa manaskArAH iti evamAdi
# mdo'i-sde #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos dpyad-pa #  dang 'brel-ba # s rig-pa #  bzhir brjod-pa # r bya ste / / de-dag #  gis de dpyad-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-la #  ltos-pa'i-rigs-pa #  ni gang 'du-byed-rnams #  'byung-ba #  na rkyen-la-ltos-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / myu-gu #  'byung-ba #  nas sa-bon #  dang dus dang chu dang; zhing rnams la ltos-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i dbang-po #  dang don dang yid-la-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
kArya kAraNa yuktiH tat yaTA cakzuH AdInAm cakzuH vijQAna Adi ASraya BAvaH rUpa AdInAm AlaMbana BAvaH cakzuH vijQAna AdInAm rUpa Adi prativijQApanam suvarNakAra AdInAm ca SilpinAm suvarNa Adi Gawanam iti evamAdi
# bya-ba-byed-pa # 'i rigs la ni 'di-lta-ste #  mig la-sogs-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-kyi-dngos-po # 'o / / gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni dmigs-pa'i-dngos-po # 'o / / mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  so-so # r rnam-par-rig-pa # r byed do / / gser-mgar #  la-sogs-pa # 'i lag bzo ba rnams ni gser la-sogs-pa #  byed ces bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
upapatti sADana yukti svaBAva viSeza saMgRhItasya sADyasya arTasya pratyakza Adi pramANa avirudDaH pratijQA Adi upadeSaH
# gtan-tshigs #  sgrub-pa # 'i rigs-pa #  ni sgrub-pa # 'i don ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  gyis bsdus-pa #  mngon-sum #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshad-ma #  dang mi-'gal-ba # r dam-bcas-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r bstan-pa # 'o /
Darma tA yuktiH tat yaTA agninA dAhaH udakena kledaH iti evamAdikA prasidDA DarmANAm Darma tA
# chos-nyid-kyi-rigs-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / mes ni tshig chus ni 'drul zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # r grags-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi chos-nyid #  de /
yaTA uktam cakzuH samRdDam SUnyam nityena yAvat AtmIyena / tat kasya hetoH / prakRtiH asya ezA iti
# ji-skad-du #  'byor ldan mig ni rtag-pa #  nas bdag-gi #  pa'i bar gyis stong ngo / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  / / 'di'i rang-bzhin #  ni 'di'o zhes gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
nAma paryezaNA nAma kAya AdInAm prajQapti sattvAt aparinizpannam ezAm sva lakzaNam iti yA vicAraNA
# ming kun-tu-tshol-ba #  ni ming-gi-tshogs #  la-sogs-pa #  btags-pa'i-yod-pa #  yin pa'i phyir 'di dag gi rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  med-pa # r dpyod-pa # 'o /
vastu paryAzaNA skanDa AdInAm taTA aparinizpattiH yaTA nAma kAya AdiBiH aBilapyantaH iti yA saMtIraNA parIkzaNa iti arTaH
# dngos-po #  kun-tu-tshol-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  ming-gi-tshogs #  la-sogs-pa #  brjod-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  med-pa # r gang rtog-pa #  ste / / yongs su rtog ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
svaBAva prajQapti paryAzaNAH yABiDAna aBiDeya saMbanDe svaBAva prajQapti mAtrasya vyavahAra nimitta tvena saMtIraNA / aBiDAna aBiDeya saMbanDaH / punar anyonya saMpratyaya nimitta tvam / taTA hi vyutpanna vyavahArasya aBiDAna mAtram SrutvA tad aBiDeye saMpratyaye utpadyate smRti muKena aBiDeyam vA punar upalaBya tad aBiDAne
# ngo-bo-nyid #  du 'dogs-pa #  kun-tu-tshol-ba #  ni brjod-pa #  dang brjod-par-bya-ba #  'brel-pa #  la ngo-bo-nyid #  du 'dogs-pa #  tsam gyi tha-snyad #  kyi rgyu nyid-du #  rtog-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la brjod-pa #  dang brjod-par-bya-ba #  'brel-ba #  ni rtogs-pa # 'i rgyu nyid do / / 'di-ltar #  tha-snyad #  la bya-ba #  ni brjod-pa #  tsam du thos-pa # s de'i brjod-par-bya-ba #  la dran-pa # 'i sgo nas rtogs-pa #  'byung ngo / / brjod-par-bya-ba #  dmigs na yang de brjod-pa #  la rtogs-pa #  'byung ste /
iti evaMviDe saMbanDe prasidDe cakzuH iti evamAdi sva lakzaNa prajQapti mAtram tad AKyAm AsapiNXa Adi vyavahArasya nimittam Bavati iti yA parIkzA iyam ucyate svaBAva prajQapti paryAzaNA
# rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # r 'brel-ba # r grags-pa #  la mig la-sogs-pa # 'i rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  du btags-pa #  tsam ni de brjod-pa #  sha sna gu la-sogs-pa # 'i tha-snyad #  kyi rgyur-gyur-pa # r gang kun-tu-rtog-pa #  de ni ngo-bo-nyid #  du 'dogs-pa #  kun-tu-tshol-ba #  zhes-bya'o #  /
viSeza prajQapti paryAzaNA yA taTA eva aBiDAna aBiDeya saMbanDe nitya anitya uttara anuttara rUpya nidarSana anidarSana tA Adi viSeza lakzaNa prajQapti mAtrasya vyavahAra nimitta tA saMtIraNA
# khyad-par #  du 'dogs-pa #  kun-tu-tshol-ba #  ni gang de-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa #  dang brjod-par-bya-ba #  'brel-ba #  rtag-pa #  dang mi-rtag-pa #  dang bla-na-yod-pa #  dang bla-na-med-pa #  dang gzugs-can #  dang gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  dang bstan-du-yod-pa #  dang bstan-du-med-pa #  khyad-par #  gyi mtshan-nyid #  du 'dogs-pa #  tsam gyi tha-snyad #  kyi rgyu nyid-du #  rtogs-pa # 'o /
catvAri yaTA BUta parijQAnAni yaTA aparyezitAni nAma Adi anupalabDi jQAnAni
# yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  gzhi ni ji-ltar #  kun du brtsal ba rnams kyis ming la-sogs-pa #  mi dmigs-pa # r shes-pa #  rnams so /
samADi prayuktasya yoga BUmiH paQcAkAra ADAra AdiH
# chos la ting-nge-'dzin #  bar brtson pa'i rnal-'byor #  gyi sa ni rnam-pa-lnga #  ste / / gzhi la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tatra ADAraH yAdRSam bAhuSrutyam SamaTa vipaSyanayoH pratizWA Bavati AlaMbana yogena tad ADAraH iti ucyate
# de-la #  gzhi ni mang-du-thos-pa #  ci-'dra-ba # r dmigs-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  gi gnas su 'gyur te / / de ni gzhi zhes-bya'o #  /
tat punar saMBRta saMBArasya satya aBisamayam aDikRtya udgRhItam yat sUtra Adikam Srutam
# de-yang #  tshogs-bsags-pa # 'i bden-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / gang mdo-sde #  la-sogs-pa #  thos-pa # s bzung-ba # 'o /
ADAnam tad AlaMbanaH yoni SomanaskAraH tena tasmin bAhu Srutye aviparIta arTa citta AkAreNa citta akaraNAt
# bskyed-pa #  ni de-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ste / / nges mang-du-thos-pa #  de-la #  phyi ci ma-log-pa # r don-sems-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  sems 'dzin-pa # 'o /
AdarSaH tad bAhu Sruti AlaMbanaH saha nimittena samADiH jQeya vastu saBAga pratibimba AkAraH iti arTaH tena
# me long lta-bu #  ni mang-du-thos-pa #  de-nyid-la #  dmigs-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  mtshan-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  ste / / shes-bya # 'o dngos-po #  dang mthun-pa #  gzugs-brnyan #  lta-bu #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
AdarSa tvam punar asya tena jQeya bimba parIkzaNAt veditavyam / AlokaH grAhya grAhaka anupalabDi jQAnam darSana mArga saMgRhItam pratyakza vRtti tvAt iti
# 'di'i mi long lta-bu #  nyid ni des shes-bya # 'i gzugs-brnyan #  la yongs-su-rtog-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / snang-ba #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa #  mi dmigs-pa # r shes-pa #  ste / / mngon-sum-du #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyis bsdus-pa # 'o /
kaTam ca punar boDisattvaH ekasyAm yOgaBUmO prayuktaH na upalamBam spRSati saMBRta puNya jQAna saMBAraH boDisattvaH kalpa asaMKyeya niryAtaH taTA aprativeDA anukUlam Srutam yoni Somanasikurvan samADim nizpAdayati
# ji-ltar #  na byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnal-'byor #  gyis 'di-la #  brtson pa mi dmigs-pa #  la reg ce na / / bsod nams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  bsags-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni bskal-pa-grangs-med-pa #  tshar phyin nas de-bzhin-nyid #  rtogs-pa #  dang mthun-pa'i-chos #  thos-pa #  tshul-bzhin #  yid la byed cing ting-nge-'dzin #  sgrub ste /
saH evam samAhite citte yat jQeya pratibimbam niSritya DyAyati tat tasmAt samAhitAt cittAt ananyat iti saMpaSyan= tasmin pratibimbe vizaya saMjQAm vyAvartya tad AkAram sva saMjQA mAtram avaDArayati
# de de-ltar #  mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sems-kyis #  shes-bya # 'i gzugs-brnyan #  gang-yin-pa #  la brten-nas #  bsam-gtan #  du byed do / / mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sems de-la # s de gzhan ma-yin-pa # r mthong-nas #  gzugs-brnyan #  de-la #  yul gyi 'du-shes #  bzlog-ste #  /
tadA ca asO sva citta mAtra avasTAnAt aDyAtma sTita cittaH Bavan sarvaTA grAhya BAvam prativedayate
# de'i rnam-pa #  rang-gi #  'du-shes #  tsam du 'dzin to / / de'i tshe rang-gi-sems #  tsam la gnas ba'i phyir sems nang-du #  gnas-par-gyur-pa # s gzung-ba #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  med-pa # r rab tu rtogs so /
tatas ca grAhya aBAvAt grAhakam api na parinizpannam iti tasya api aBAvam parivedayate
# de'i-'og-tu #  gzung-ba #  med-pa # s 'dzin-pa #  yang yongs su ma grub bo zhes de-yang #  med-pa # r rab tu rtogs so /
tatas pratyAtmam tad uBaya svaBAva upalamBa apagatam anupalamBam aDigacCati
# de'i-'og-tu #  so-so #  rang la de-gnyi-ga # 'i rang-bzhin #  du dmigs-pa #  dang bral nas dmigs-pa-med-pa # r khong du chud do /
etat eva ca aDikRtya uktam BagavatA pratibimbam manaH paSyan= iti vistaraH
# de nyid kyi dbang du mdzad nas bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mnyam gzhag-pa #  / / yid kyi gzugs-brnyan #  mthong-ba # s na / / zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs so /
ASrayaH ASraya parivRttiH dOzWulyA apagamAt pariSudDaH ASrayaH iti arTaH / sA ca iyam yoga BUmiH hetutaH PalataH ca nirdizwA veditavyA
# gnas ni gnas-gyur-pa #  ste / / gnas-ngan-len #  dang bral-ba # 'i phyir gnas yongs su dag zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / rnal-'byor #  gyi sa 'di ni rgyu-dang-'bras-bu # s bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
tatra ADAra AdiBiH caturBiH hetu nirdeSaH paScimena ekena Pala nirdeSaH iti
# de-la #  gzhi la-sogs-pa #  bzhis ni rgyu bstan to / / tha-ma #  gcig gis ni 'bras-bu #  bstan to /
yat uktam sTavira Anandena paQcaBiH Ayuzman SAriputra DarmEH samanvAgataH BikzuH laGu ca gRhNAti iti atra sUtre tEH eva paQcaBiH DarmEH laGu grahaNa AdIni catvAri yaTAyogam veditavyAni
# gnas-brtan #  kun dga'-bo # s tshe-dang-ldan-pa #  sh'a ri'i bu chos lnga dang ldan-pa # 'i dge slong myur-du #  'dzin to zhes gang smras-pa # 'i mdo de-la #  chos lnga po 'di dag gis myur-du #  'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhin-du #  ci-rigs-su #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
catvAri kaTam kRtvA / Darma kuSalaH laGu gRhNAti bAhu SrutyAt prAyeNa Binna pada vyaQjana tayA
# ji-ltar #  na chos la mkhas-pa # s myur-du #  'dzin zhe na / / mang-du-thos-pa # s tshig-dang-yi-ge #  phal-cher #  lcigs pa'i phyir ro /
arTa kuSalaH bahu gRhNAti aBiDarma Adi lakzaNa jQa tvAt skanDa DAtu Adi kaTA vastu aDikAreNa praBUta granTa saMkalanataH
# don la mkhas-pa # s mang-du #  'dzin te / / chos-mngon-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid-shes-pa # 'i phyir te; phung-po #  dang khams la-sogs-pa # 'i gtam gyi gzhi'i skabs su tshig le'u mang-du #  bzlums pa'i phyir ro /
vyaQjana kuSalaH nirukti kulaH ca sUdgRhItam gRhNAti sunirukta vyaQjana jQa tvAt AtmA iti janapada niruktim anaBiniviSya anuvyavahAra jQa tvAt ca granTa arTayoH aviparota grahaNataH
# yi-ge #  la mkhas-pa #  dang nges-pa'i-tshig #  la mkhas-pa # s ni tshig dang don ma nor-ba # r 'dzin-pa # s legs-par #  zin-pa # r 'dzin te / / nges-pa'i-tshig #  bzang-po # 'i yi-ge #  shes-pa #  dang; bdag go zhes yul-gyi-mi # 'i nges-pa'i-tshig #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  rjes su tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  shes-pa #  nyid kyi phyir ro /
pUrva anta apara anta anusaMDi kuSalaH udgRhItam na nASayati pUrvam udgahItAn DarmAt miSritya paScAt niHsartavyam iti budDa aBisaMDi jQa tvAt aDigamena tad sAra AdAnataH / Darma vihArI BikzuH Darma vihAri BikzuH iti Badanta ucyate iti atra sUtre BagavatA samastena Sruta cintA BAvanA vihAreNa Darma vihAraH Bavati na anyatara prayoga mAtreNa iti saMdarSitam
# sngon-gyi-mtha' #  dang phyi-ma'i-mtha' #  la dgongs-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  ni ril-gyis #  byed na chos la gnas-pa #  yin gyi / / sbyor-ba #  gang brten-nas #  phyis 'byung-ba # r bya-ba # r shes te / / dgongs-pa #  shes-pa # 'i phyir khong-du-chud-pa # s de'i snying-po #  len-pa # 'i phyir ro / / btsun pa chos la gnas-pa # 'i dge slong zhes-bya-ba # 'i do der ni bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis thos-pa-dang-bsam-pa #  dang bsgom-pa #  ni ril-gyis #  byed na chos la gnas-pa #  yin gyi /
tatra paryApti svADyAya deSanA bahulAH vitarkaNAH bahulAH ca iti anena kevalam Sruta cintA prayuktAH na BAvanA prayuktAH yoga AdiH iQcana AdataH na Darma vihAriNaH vyavasTApyante
# sbyor-ba #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  tsam gyis ni ma-yin-pa # r bstan to / / de-la #  kun-chub-par-byed-pa #  dang kha-ton #  du byed-pa #  dang bshad-pa #  mang-ba #  dang rtog-pa #  mang-ba #  de 'ba'-zhig #  ni thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  la zhugs-pa #  yin gyi / / bsgom-pa #  la zhugs-pa #  ma yin te / / rnal-'byor #  la-sogs-pa #  bor-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-phyir #  chos la gnas-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
yaH api kaScid Sruta cintAm anAgamya kevalam BAvanA prayuktaH syAt saH api na Darma vihArI vyavasTApyate
# gang-la #  la zhig gis thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  la ma brten-pa # r bsgom-pa #  'ba'-zhig #  la zhugs-pa #  de-yang #  chos la gnas-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
tatas eva tAvat Darma vihAriNam Bikzum AraBya iha tu BikzuH dDarmam paryApnoti sUtram geyam iti vistareNa uktvA paScAt Aha na riQcati yogam iti evamAdi yaTA vijQAyeta Srutam cintAm BAvanAm ca Agamya tad uBaya vihAreNa Darma vihArI iti / na riQcati yogam iti evamAdinA samADi prayoga asaMtuzwiByAm BAvanA mayam saMdarSitam / samADi prayogaH punar dviviDaH saMdarSitaH sAtatya satkRtya prayoga saMgRhItaH ca na riQcati yogam iti anena aviparIta prayoga saMgRhItaH ca na riQcati manaskAram iti anena
# de'i-phyir #  bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis chos la gnas-pa # 'i dge slong las brtsams te / / ci nas thos-pa-dang-bsam-pa #  dang bsgom-pa #  la brten-nas #  de-gnyi-ga #  la gnas-pa # s chos la gnas-pa #  yin par shes-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir 'di-la #  dge slong mdo'i-sde #  dang dbyangs-kyis-bsnyad-pa'i-sde # 'i chos kun chub bar byed-pa #  zhes rgya-cher #  bka' stsal nas de'i-'og-tu #  rnal-'byor #  mi 'dor ro zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs so / / rnal-'byor #  mi 'dor ro zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni / / ting-nge-'dzin #  la sbyor-ba #  dang chog-par-mi-'dzin-pa # s bsgom-pa #  las 'byung-ba #  bstan to / / ting-nge-'dzin #  la sbyor-ba #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / rgyun-du #  chud-pa #  dang gus-par-sbyor-ba # s bsdus-pa #  ni rnal-'byor #  mi-'dor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis bstan to / / ma-log-pa # r sbyor-ba # s bsdus-pa #  ni yid-la-byed-pa #  mi-'dor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis bstan to /
asaMtuzwiH na riQcati aDyAtma cetaH SamaTam iti anena saMdarSitA tad anAsvAdanAt uttara SamaTa prayogAt ca asya ariQcanam veditavyam
# chog-par-mi-'dzin-pa #  ni nang-du #  sems zhi-gnas #  su byed-pa #  mi-'dor-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  'dis bstan te de'i ro mi myang-ba #  dang gang-du #  zhi-gnas #  la sbyor-ba # s mi-'dor-ba # r blta'o /
kena kAraNena vEpulyam sUtra antare boDisattva pAramitA piwakam iti ucyate
# ci'i-phyir #  mdo-sde #  gzhan-las #  shin-tu #  rgyas-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i sde-snod #  ces bya zhe na /
tatra pAramitAnAm saMKyA nirdeSAt yAvat anyonya viniScayanAt ca
# der pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyi grangs bstan-pa #  nas gcig-la-gcig #  rnam-par-nges-pa # 'i bar-du #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra saMKyA dviviDA gaNanA saMKyA tanmAtra saMKyA ca
# de-la #  grangs ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / bgrangs ba'i grangs dang de tsam gyi grangs so /
zaz pAramitA iti gaNanA saMKyA
# pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug ces bya-ba #  ni bgrang-ba # 'i grangs so /
sarva AkArayoH yoDi sattva aByudaya niHSreyasa mArgayoH tisRBiH tisRBiH ca saMgrahAt zaXA iva pAramitA na BUyasyaH na alpa Asyasya iti iyam tanmAtra saMKyA
# byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-lam #  mngon-par-mtho-ba #  dang nges-par-legs-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  dang ldan-pa #  gnyis gsum gsum gyis bsdus-pa # 'i phyir pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug nyid de / / mi mang mi nyung-ba #  ni de tsam gyi grangs so /
triviDaH aByudayaH mahA Boga tA mahAtmatA mahA pakza tA ca
# mngon-par-mtho-ba #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / longs-spyod-chen-po #  nyid dang; bdag-nyid #  chen-po #  nyid dang phyogs chen-po #  nyid do /
tatra dAna pAramitAyAH mahA Boga tA Palam / SIla pAramitAyAH mahAtmatA Palam SIlena sugata Atma BAva saMpatti pratilamBAt
# de-la #  sbyin-pa # s longs-spyod-chen-po #  thob-pa # 'i phyir sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni longs-spyod-chen-po #  nyid do / / de-la #  tshul-khrims #  kyis bde-'gro # 'i lus-phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  'thob-pa # 'i phyir tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni bdag-nyid #  chen-po #  nyid do /
kzAnti pAramitAyAH mahA pakza tA Palam kzAntyA sarva jana aBigamana udyata apratilamBAt iti
# bzod-pa # s skye-bo #  thams-cad-kyi #  mngon du 'gro-bar-'gyur-ba #  thob-pa # 'i phyir bzod-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni phyogs chen-po #  nyid do /
triviDaH niHSreyasa mArgaH kleSam aBiBUya kuSala pakza prayoga upAyaH sattva paripAcana upAyaH budDa Darma samudAnayana upAyaH ca ezAm anyatareNa api vinA boDisattvasya niHSreyasa anupapatteH
# nges-par-legs-pa'i-lam #  yang rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor-ba # 'i thabs dang; sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r bya-ba # 'i thabs dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'i thabs te / / 'di dag las gang-yang-rung-ba #  zhig med na byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i nges-par-legs-pa #  mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tatra sattva paripAcana upAyaH DyAna pAramitA tad saMniSrayeNa aBijQABiH sattva paripAcanAt
# de-la #  sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r bya-ba # 'i thabs ni bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ste / / de-la #  brten-nas #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  rnams kyis sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar apratizWita nirvANa upAyataH zaXA iva pAramitAH
# yang mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i thabs su pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug nyid de /
boDisattvena hi nirvANa pratizWA viparyayeNa saMsAre aByudayaH parigrahItavyaH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la gnas-pa #  las bzlog-ste #  / / 'khor-ba #  na mngon bar mtho-ba #  yongs-su-gzung-ba # r bya'o /
saMsAra pratizWA viparyayeNa tasmin= asaMkleSa izwavyam
# 'khor-ba #  na gnas-pa #  las bzlog-ste #  / / der nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # r bya'o /
atas tisraH aByudaya lABa upAya astisraH tad asaMkleSa upAyAH yaTAyogam pUrva anusAreNa eva veditavyAH
# de'i-phyir #  gsum ni mngon-par-mtho-ba #  thob-pa # 'i thabs so / / gsum ni de na nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # 'i thabs te / / snga-ma # 'i tshul du go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
asaMkleSa upAye tu vIryeNa pratipakza BAvanA DyAnena kleSa vizkamBaNam prajQayA kleSa anuSaya samudGAtaH iti
# kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i thabs la brtson 'grus kyis ni gnyen-po #  bsgom mo / / bsam-gtan #  gyis ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa # r gnon to / / shes-rab #  kyis ni bag-la-nyal #  legs-par #  'joms so /
sarva anugraha tAm kleSa pratipakzatAm ca upAdAya iti aparaH paryAyaH
# sems-can #  rjes su 'dzin-pa #  dang nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-pa # 'i phyir-yang #  rnam-grangs #  gzhan te /
tatra dAnena boDisattvaH sattvAn upakaraNa upasaMhAra anugraheNa anugRhNAti
# de-la #  sbyin-pa # s ni byang chung sems dpa' sems-can #  rnams la yo-byad #  nye-bar-sgrub-pa # 'i phan-'dogs-pa # s rjes su 'dzin to /
SIlena viGAta utpaIXA viheWa akaraNena anugRhNAti yaTAkramam BogakAya citta upaGAta anupasaMhArAt
# tshul-khrims #  kyis ni phongs-pa #  dang gnod-pa #  dang rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  mi-byed-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  rjes su 'dzin te / / go-rims-bzhin-du #  logs spyod dang lus dang sems la gnod-pa #  mi sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kzAntyAH viGAta utpaIXA viheWa amarzaNena anugRhNAti pareByaH AtmanaH Boga Adi upaGAta sahanAt / ABiH tisRBiH anugRhNAti
# bzod-pa # s ni phongs-pa #  dang gnod-pa #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa # r rjes su 'dzin to / / gzhan dag gis bdag-gi #  longs-spyod #  la-sogs-pa #  la gnod-pa #  la mi-mjed-pa # 'i phyir te / / de gsum gyis rjes su 'dzin to /
vIryeNa AvizkamBita kleSaH api kuSala pakze prayujyate / DyAnena kleSam vizkamBayati
# brtson 'grus kyis ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa # r ma mnan yang dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor ro / / bsam-gtan #  gyis ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnam-pa # r gnon to /
prajQayA anuSayam samudGAtayati
# shes-rab #  kyis ni bag-la-nyal #  legs-par #  'joms par byed do /
imAH tisraH kleSa pratipakzAH veditavyA
# 'di gsum ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra pAramitA lakzaNam / boDisattvasya dAna pAramitA katamA
# de-la #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni gang zhe na /
yat boDisattvasya boDisattva Darma tAyAm vyavasTitasya boDi cittam niSritya karuNA puraHsareNa cetasA sarvA asti parityAge kAya vAc manaskarma / evam ca kRtvA dAna pAramitAyAH lakzaNam gotrataH praNiDAnataH ASayataH vastutas svaBAvataH ca nirdizwam veditavyam / tat yaTA boDisattva Darma tA gotram boDi cittam praNiDAnam karuNA puraHsaram cetaH ASayaH sarvAH tiparityAgaH vastu kAya vAc manaH karma svaBAvaH iti evam yAvat prajQApAramitA vistareNa veditavyAH / ayam tu viSezaH
# sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ni gang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i chos-nyid #  la gnas-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i byang-chub #  kyi sems la brten-nas #  snying-rje #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i sems-kyis #  bdog-pa #  thams-cad #  yongs-su-gtong-ba #  la lus dang dag dang yid-kyi-las #  te / / de-ltar #  byas-na #  sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  rigs dang; smon-lam #  dang bsam-pa #  dang dngos-po #  dang ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'di-lta-ste #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i chos-nyid #  ni rigs so / / byang-chub #  kyi sems ni smon-lam #  mo / / snying-rje #  sngon-du-gtong-ba # 'i sems ni bsam-pa # 'o / / bdog-pa #  thams-cad #  yongs-su-gtong-ba #  ni dngos-po # 'o / / lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar la yang rgya-cher #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'di ni bye-brag #  yin te /
SIla kzAnti vIrya pAramitAsu yaTAkramam sarva saMvara samAdAna anurayAyAm sarva apakAra duHKam arzaNa aDivAsanAyAm sarva kuSala Darma samudAnayana tAyAm yat kAya vAc manaskarma iti veditavyam
# tshul-khrims #  dang bzod-pa #  dang brtson 'grus kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la ni sdom-pa #  thams-cad #  yang-dag-par-len-pa #  dang; rjes-su-bsrung-ba #  dang gnod-par-byed-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa #  dang dang-du-len-pa #  dang dge-ba'i-chos #  thams-cad #  yang-dag-par-bsgrub-pa #  la lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  so zhes go-rims-bzhin-du #  brjod-pa # r bya'o /
DyAna pAramitAyAm sarva AkAra kAya vAc manaskarma viBu tve sarva AkArA cetasaH sTitiH iti
# bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la ni lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  kyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  dang dbang 'byor-ba #  la sems kyi gnas-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  dang ldan-pa # 'o /
prajQApAramitAyAm sarva AkAra kAya vAc manaskarma viBu tve yaH sarva AkAraH Darma pravicayaH iti vaktavyam
# shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la ni lus dang ngag dang yid-kyi-las #  kyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  dang dbang 'byor-pa #  la gang rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  chos rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'o zhes brjod-pa # r bya'o /
Sezam dAnava deva sarvam veditavyam
# lhag-ma #  thams-cad #  ni sbyin-pa #  bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
punar yat dAnam sarvajQa tAm AraBya sarvajQa tAyE saMvartate sarvajQa tAm parigRhNAti sarvajQa tA kRtyam ca karoti tad dAna pArimitA iti ucyate
# yang sbyin-pa #  ni rnam-pa-thams-cad #  mkhyen-pa #  nyid la brtsams pa dang thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  du 'gyur-ba #  dang thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  dang thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  kyi bya-ba-byed-pa #  ste /
etAni punar catvAri padAni yaTAkramam AramBataH vAsanAtaH kAyataH nisyandataH ca veditavyAni
# de ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / tshig bzhi-po #  de-dag #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  rtsom pa dang-ba # g chags dang sku dang rgyu-mthun-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra AramBataH sarvajQa tA mAraBya utpanna utpannasya tatra pariNAmanAt
# de-la #  rtsom pa ni thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  las brtsams te / / 'byung-ba #  dang byung-ba #  der yongs-su-bsngo-ba # 'i phyir ro /
tat eva punar dAnam saMtati vAsayate yatas AyatyAm sarvajQa tAyE saMvartate
# sbyin-pa #  de nyid rgyud la bag-chags #  su bsgos te / / de-la # s phi ma la thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  du 'gyur ro /
tat eva yadA paripUrNam Bavati tadA Darma kAya parinizpAdana yogena sarvajQa tAm parigRhNAti
# gang-gi-tshe #  de nyid yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r gyur-pa #  de'i tshe / / chos kyi sku yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  yongs su 'dzin to /
tatas uttara kAlam sAMBogikarga narmANika kAya nisyanda muKena sarvajQa tA kRtyam karoti / evam yAvat prajQApAramitA veditavyAH / anukramaH
# de'i-'og-tu #  longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa #  dang sprul pa'i skus rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i sgo nas thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  kyi bya-ba #  byed do / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  yang de-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / go-rims #  ni 'og ma 'og ma la brten-pa # 'i phyir te /
uttara uttara saMniSrayatAm upAdAya dAna pAramitayA ADyAtmika bAhya sarva vastu parityAga aByAsAt kAya jIvita nirapekzaH boDisattvaH mahAntam api Boga skanDam prahAya SIla samAdAnam karoti
# sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s ni nang dang phyi'i dngos-po-thams-cad #  yongs-su-gtong-ba # r goms-pa # s / / lus-dang-srog #  la mi-lta-ba # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  longs-spyod #  kyi phung-po #  chen-po #  yang spangs-nas #  tshul-khrims #  la yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa # r byed do /
SIla anurakzI Akruzwena mayA na pratyAkrozwavyam iti evamAdiBiH prakArEH kzamaH Bavati
# tshul-khrims #  rjes-su-bsrung-ba #  ni gshe yang bdag-gis #  slar gshe-ba # r mi bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis bzod-pa # r 'gyur ro /
kzamaH SIta AdInAm tat nidAnam prayoga asra sanAda ArabDa vIryA Bavati
# grang-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bzod-pa #  ni de'i gzhi las sbyor-ba #  mi-nyams-pa # s brtson 'grus brtsams pa yin no /
ArabDa vIryaH prayoga nizWA Pala aDigamAt aDyAnam saMpAdayati
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni sbyor-ba # 'i mtha'i 'bras-bu #  thob-pa # s bsam-gtan #  bsgrub bo /
saMpanna DyAnaH ca samAhita cittaH yaTA BUta jQAna alloka uttarAm prajQAm pratilaBate iti
# bsam-gtan #  phun sum tshogs te sems-mnyam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  shes-pa # s 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i shes-rab #  thob po / / yang gong-ma #  gong-ma #  ni gzhi-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar uttara uttara ADArataH SIlam dAnasya ADAraH evam yAvat prajQA DyAnasya
# tshul-khrims #  ni sbyin-pa # 'i gzhi yin no / / de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  ni bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i gzhi-yin-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
taTA hi SIlavataH dAnam viSudDam Bavati dAnena anugRhItasya SIlena paGAta akaraNataH
# 'di-ltar #  tshul-khrims-dang-ldan-pa #  ni sbyin-pa # s phan-btags-pa #  la tshul-khrims #  kyis gnod-pa # 'i byed-pa # 'i phyir sbyin-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r 'gyur ro /
evam asya pratigrAhakasya boDisattvena viheWa avirahita upakaraNa suKa upasaMhArAt SIla balena dAnapAramitA viSudDiH veditavyA
# de-ltar #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  len-pa #  po de-la #  rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  dang bral-ba # r yo-byad #  kyis bde-ba # r sbyor-ba # s tshul-khrims #  kyi stobs kyis sbyin-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
evam kzamiNaH SIla viSudDiH para apakArEH SikzA pada AKaNXanAt
# de-ltar #  bzod-pa-dang-ldan-pa #  ni gzhan-gnod-par-byed-pa #  dag gis bslab-pa'i-gzhi #  mi 'dral-ba # s tshul-khrims #  rnam-pa # r dag go /
ArabDa vIryasya kzAnti viSudDiH utsAha balena utpatya saMsAram aByupagatavataH akRcCreNa sattva vipratipatti duHKa sahanAt
# brtson 'grus brtsams pas spro-ba # 'i stobs kyi ched du 'khor-ba #  khas-blangs-pa #  ni sems-can #  log-pa # r sgrub-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  bde blag tu bzod-pa # s bzod-pa #  rnam-pa # r dag go /
DyAyinI vIrya viSudDiH saha suKena sOmanasyena sarva kuSala Darma prayogAt
# bsam-gtan-pa #  ni bde-ba #  dang bcas-pa #  dang yid bde pa dang bcas-pa # r dge-ba'i-chos #  thams-cad-la #  sbyor-ba # s brtson 'grus rnam-pa # r dag go /
prajQAvataH DyAna viSudDiH bahu prakArAn DarmAn vipaSyati aDyAtmam SamaTataH samADi aBivRdDeH na asti DyAnam aprajQasya iti gATAyAm vacanAt iti
# brtson 'grus brtsams pas shes-rab-dang-ldan-pa #  ni chos rnam-pa #  mang-po #  la rnam-pa # r bltas nas nang-du #  zhi-bar-byed-pa #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  rnam-par-'phel-ba # s bsam-gtan #  rnam-pa # r dag ste / / shes-rab #  med la bsam-gtan #  med / / ces tshig su bcad-pa #  las gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA OdArikaH ca aparaH anukramaH veditavyaH
# ji-ltar #  rags-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  yang go-rims-kyis #  yang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
sarva OdArikam hi dAnam atas praTamatas vyavasTApyate
# sbyin-pa #  ni thams-cad-kyi #  nang nas rags ste [*te] / / de'i-phyir #  sbyin-pa #  thog-mar #  rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
tad anantaram kzAnti AdiByaH SIlam OdArikam evam yAvat prajQAyAH DyAnam OdArikam
# de'i-'og-tu #  bzod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s tshul-khrims #  rags so / / de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  pas bsam-gtan #  rags-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
sarva sUkzmA tu prajQA atas sarva paScAt vyavasTApyate iti / nirvacanam
# shes-rab #  ni thams-cad-kyi #  nang na phra ste / / de'i-phyir #  thams-cad-kyi-tha-ma # r rnam-pa # r gzhag go /
kena kAraNena dAnam dAna pAramitA iti ucyate
# nges tshig ni ci'i-phyir #  sbyin-pa #  la sbyin-pa # 'i pha rol du phyin pa zhes bya zhe na /
mahat dAnam nirdozam nirmalam dAna pAramitA iti ucyate
# sbyin-pa #  chen-po #  dang skyon-med-pa #  dang dri-ma-med-pa #  ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
tatra mahat dAnam sarva prakAra ADyAtmika bAhya vastu dAnataH dIrGa kAla dAnataH ca / nirdozam vizama paryAzwayA Adi vivarjita tvAt nirmalam mAtsarya vipakza prahANAt / yaTA uktam dAna pAramitAm AraBya Arya akzaya mati nirdeSa sUtre nirmalam sa vAsana vipakza prahANAt / tat anayA triviDayA paramatayA dAna pAramitA iti aBidyotitam Bavati / triviDA parama tA svaBAva parama tA saha paricayena upAya para matA Pala parama tA ca
# de-la #  sbyin-pa #  chen-po #  ni nang dang phyi'i dngos-po # 'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  sbyin-pa #  dang yun-ring-du #  sbyin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / skyon-med-pa #  ni gnod-pa # s kun-tu-tshol-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ji-skad-du #  'phags-pa #  blo-gros #  mi-zad-pa # s bstan-pa # 'i mdo las sbyin-pa # 'i zad-pa #  las brtsams te bstan-pa #  / / btsun pa shar dva ti'i bu byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sbyin-pa #  yang mi-zad-pa #  ste / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  / / tshad-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / btsun pa sha ra dva ti'i bu byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi sbyin-pa #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba #  yang tshad-med-pa #  ste / / tshe dang spobs-pa #  dang bde-ba #  dang stobs dang kha-dog #  nye-bar #  brtan-pa # 'i phyir zas-'dod-pa #  rnams la zas-sbyin-pa # 'o / / nyon-mongs-pa # 'i sred-pa #  bsal-ba # 'i phyir btung-ba #  'dod-pa #  rnams la btung-ba #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / bde-ba #  dang 'byor-ba # 'i dngos-po-thams-cad #  bsdu-ba # 'i phyir / / bzhon-pa-'dod-pa #  rnams la bzhon-pa #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / ngo-tsha-shes-pa #  dang khrel-yod-pa #  dang mdog-gser #  gyi kha-dog #  yongs-su-sbyang-ba # 'i phyir gos-'dod-pa #  rnams la gos sbyin-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i lha'i sbyan yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir mar-me #  'dod-pa #  rnams la mar-me #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i lha'i snyan yongs-su-dag-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir sil snyan 'dod-pa #  rnams la sil snyan sbyin-pa # 'o / / tshul-khrims #  dang thos-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi dris byug-pa # 'i phyir spos dang byug-pa #  'dod-pa #  rnams la spos dang byug-pa #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / gzugs dang spobs-pa #  dang byang-chub-kyi-yan-lag #  gi me-tog #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir phreng-ba #  'dod-pa #  rnams la phreng-ba #  sbyin-pa # 'i / / lus kyi dri yid-du-'ong-ba #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / phye-ma #  'dod-pa #  rnams la phye-ma #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / skyes-bu-chen-po'i-mtshan #  ro bro ba'i mchog yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ro bro ba thams-cad #  'dod-pa #  la ro bro ba thas cad sbyin-pa # 'o / / sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi gnas dang skyabs dang gon dang dpung gnyen bya-ba # 'i phyir gnas-'dod-pa #  rnams la gnas-sbyin-pa # 'o / / sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  rab tu spangs-pa #  dang lha dang tshangs-pa'i-gnas-pa #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i gzims cha thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / mal-cha #  'dod-pa #  rnams la mal-cha #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i 'jig-rten #  gyi sa thams-cad-kyi #  byang-chub #  kyi snying rdo rdo-rje # 'i gdan thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir stan 'dod-pa #  rnams la stan sbyin-pa # 'o / / byang-chub #  kyi yo-byad #  thams-cad #  yongs-su-bskang-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir yo-byad #  'dod-pa #  rnams la yo-byad #  sbyin-pa # 'o / / mi rga mi-'chi-ba # 'i bdud rtsi'i bde-ba # s yongs-su-bskang-ba # 'i phyir na-ba #  dang sman 'dod-pa #  rnams la sman sbyin-pa # 'o / / rang dbang dang rang nyams dang rang-byung-gi-ye-shes #  yongs-su-bskang-ba # 'i phyir byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyis bran po dang bran-mo #  yongs-su-gtong-ba # 'i sbyin-pa # 'o zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  lta-bu # 'o / / dri-ma-med-pa #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro; / / dam-pa #  rnam-pa #  'di gsum gyis sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  zhes brjod-pa #  yin te / / dam-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni 'dris-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dam-pa #  dang thabs dam-pa #  dang 'bras-bu #  dam-pa # 'o /
paricayaH punar dIrGa kAla dAnataH veditavyaH
# 'dris-pa #  ni yun-ring-po-nas #  sbyin-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
evam yAvat prajQA pAramitA veditavyA
# shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  yang de-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
SIla AdInAm punar nirdoza tvam mA Atma samAropa varjita tva AdiBiH yaTAyogam tat akzayam atisUtrezu drazwavyam
# tshul-khrims #  la-sogs-pa # 'i skyon-med-pa #  ni bdag tu sgro-'dogs-pa #  rnam-par-spangs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i phyir te / / ci-rigs-su #  blo-gros #  mi-zad-pa # s bstan-pa #  las blta-bar-bya # 'o /
punar dvAdaSa viDena parama tvena yogAt pAramitA iti ucyate
# yang dam-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
dvAdaSa viDam punar parama tvam OdArya parama tvam sarva loka sampatti anarTi tvAt utkRzwa tvAt ca
# dam-pa #  rnam-pa-bcu #  gnyis la / / rgya-che-ba #  dam-pa #  ni 'jig-rten #  gyi phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  thams-cad #  mi-'dod-pa #  dang mchog-tu #  gyur ba'i phyir ro /
Ayata tva parama tvam tri kalpa asaMKyeya pariBAvanAt
# yun-ring-ba #  dam-pa #  ni bskal-ba #  grangs-med-pa #  gsum du yongs-su-bsgom-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aDikAra parama tvam sarva sattva arTa kriyA aDikAra pravRtta tvAt
# ched du bya-ba #  dam-pa #  ni sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi don-bya-ba # 'i ched kyi phyir ro /
akzaya tva param tvam mahA boDi pariNAmanayA atyantam aparyAdAnAt
# zad-mi-shes-pa #  dam-pa #  ni byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # s gtan-du #  yongs-su-gtugs-pa # r mi 'gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nErantarya parama tvam Atma para sama tA aDimokzAt sarva sattva dAna AdiBiH pAramitA paripUraNAt
# rgyun-mi-'chad-pa #  dam-pa #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  du mos-pa # 'i phyir sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
akRcCra tva param atvam anumodanA mAtreNa para dAna AdInAm pAramitA paripUraNAt
# chogs med-pa #  dam-pa #  ni gzhan gyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rjes-su-yi-rang-ba #  tsam gyis pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
viBu tva param tvam gagana gajaQja samADi AdiBiH dAna Adi paripUraNAt
# dbang 'byor-pa-dam-pa #  ni nam-mkha' #  mdzod kyi ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # s sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
parigraha parama tvam nirvikalpa jQAta parigRhIta tvAt / AramBa parama tvam aDimukti caryA BUmO= aDimAtrAyAm kzAntO / pratilamBa parama tvam praTamAyAm BUmO
# yongs-su-bzung-ba #  dam-pa #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis yongs-su-bzung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rtsom pa dam-pa #  ni mos-pas-spyod-pa'i-sa #  la bzod-pa-chen-po # r gyur-pa #  la'o / / thob-pa #  dam-pa #  ni sa dang-po #  la'o /
nisyanda parama tvam tad anyAsu azwAsu
# rgyu-mthun-pa #  dam-pa #  ni de-ma-yin-pa #  gzhan brgyad po dag la'o /
nizpatti param tvam daSamyAm BUmO tATAgatyAm ca boDisattva parinizpattyA budDa parinizpattyA ca iti
# 'grub-pa #  dam-pa #  ni sa bcu pa dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa'i-sa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  'grub-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas #  'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar paramEH IhitAH itAH ca iti pAramitAH budDa boDisattvEH cezwitAH gatAH ca iti arTaH
# yang dam-pa #  rnams kyis spyad-pa #  dang bgrod-pa # 'i phyir pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ste / / sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyis spyad-pa #  dang bgrod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
punar jQeya pAraMgatAH pAramitAH budDa tve pratizWitAH iti arTaH
# yang shes-bya # 'i pha rol tu son pas pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ste / / sangs-rgyas #  nyid la gnas zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
punar parAna AtmAnam ca paramAmi iti tArayantoti pAramitAH parAna AtmAnam ca duHKa arNavam atikrAmanti iti arTaH
# yang gzhan dang bdag mchog-tu #  gnod-pa #  las sgrol bar byed-pa # 'i phyir pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams te / / gzhan dang bdag sdug-bsngal #  gyi rgya-mtsho #  las 'da' bar byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
idam tAvat sADAraNam nirvacanam
# 'di ni re-zhig #  thun mong gi nges-pa'i-tshig #  go /
pratyekam punar dAyaka dAridra yApanaya tAddAnam dAha apanayanAt vA pratigrAhakAnAm
# so-so # 'i nges-pa'i-tshig #  ni sbyin-bdag #  gi dbul-ba #  sel-ba #  dang len-pa #  po rnams kyi gdung-ba #  sel-ba # 'i phyir sbyin-pa # 'o /
SAnta indriya AlamBanAt SuBa gati lIyanAt SEtya AlayAt ca SIlam yaTAkramam indriyezu gupta dvAra tA vAhanAt sugati gamana hetu BAvanAt avipratitisAra Adi AnupUrvyA yAvat nirvANa ASraya tvAt iti
# dbang-po #  zhi-ba #  thob-pa #  dang 'gro-ba #  bzang-po # r sbyor-ba #  dang bsil pa'i gnas yin-pas #  tshul-khrims #  te / / go-rims-bzhin-du #  dbang-po #  rnams kyi sgo sdom-par-byed-pa #  dang bde-'gror-'gro-ba # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa #  dang 'gyod-pa-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bar gyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro /
kroDa kzAra tiraskaraNAt kzati citta Agati raskaraNAt kzema AvizkaraNAt ca kzatinAm kzAntiH
# khro-ba # 'i tsha-ba #  sel-ba #  dang rma 'byin-pa # 'i sems 'ongs-pa #  sel-ba #  dang zhi-ba # r brjod-pa # 'i phyir bzod-pa # 'o /
kzati cittam punar yena apa kAriNAm pratyapakAraH kriyate tasya Agatasya anayA vilopanam tiraskaraNam veditavyam
# rma 'byin-pa # 'i sems zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-gis #  gnod-pa-byed-pa #  rnams la-la # n du gnod-pa-byed-pa #  ste / / de 'ongs-pa #  'dis 'bral-ba # r byed-pa #  ni sel-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
kzatam ezAm vEram vidyate iti kzatinaH tezAm aBaya prakASanam kzemasya AvizkaraNam veditavyam / vaDa vRdDa UhA yogAt voryam / tatra vaDAya iha AkuSala Darma vigamAya dvAByAm samyakprahANAByAm vRdDaye IhA kuSala Darma samudAgamAya dvAByAm samyakprahANAByAm ca / DAraNa yamana saMyamana vinayana nayanAt DyAnam / tatra DAraNAm AlaMbane cittasya yamanam vikzepataH saMyamanam cittasya vinayanam paryavasTAnAnAm vizkamBaNam nayanam viButvasya prApaNam veditavyam / para praNIta jQAnAt pratyAtma jQAnAt prakAra jQAnAt Sama prApti guNa prakarza jQAnAt ca prajQA / tatra para praNIta jQAnam paratas Goza anvayAH yoni SomanaskAra saMprayuktA prajQA pratyAtma jQAnam lokottarA prakAra jQAnam loka uttara pRzWa labDA Sama prAptaye jQAnam BAvanA mArge kleSa pratipakza BUtA guNa prakarzAya jQAnam vESezika guNa aBinirhArAya prajQA veditavyA / BAvanA paQcaviDA upaDi saMniSritA yAvat viBu tva saMniSritA / tatra upaDi saMniSritA catur AkArA
# rma 'byin-pa #  ni 'di dag la shar gnyer ba yod-pa # s rma 'byin-pa #  can te / / de-dag #  la mi-'jigs-pa #  sgrogs-pa #  ni bde-ba # r brjod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / sel-ba #  dang 'phel-bar-byed-pa #  dang ldan-pa # s brtson 'grus te / / de-la #  sel-ba # 'i phyir spyod-pa #  ni yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  gnyis kyis mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  dang bral-bar-byed-pa # 'o / / 'phel-ba # 'i phyir spyod-pa #  ni yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  gnyis kyis dge-ba'i-chos #  yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa # 'o / / 'dzin-pa #  dang sdom-pa #  dang 'dul-ba #  dang 'thob-pa # r byed-pa # s bsam-gtan #  te / / de-la #  'dzin-pa #  ni dmigs-pa #  la sems 'dzin-pa # 'o / / sdom-pa #  ni rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba las sems yang-dag-par-sdom-pa # 'o / / 'dul-ba #  ni kun-nas-dkris-pa #  rnams rnam-pa # r gnod-pa # 'o / / thob-par-byed-pa #  ni dbang 'byor-pa #  thob-par-byed-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / gzhan gyis smras-pa #  shes-pa #  dang so-so #  rang-gis #  shes-pa #  dang rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang rab-tu-zhi-ba #  thob-pa #  dang;
