/ / yon-tan #  mchog-tu #  phyin par shes-pa # s shes-rab #  ste / / de-la #  gzhan gyis smras-pa #  shes-pa #  ni gzhan gyi sgra'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa #  dang mtshungs-par-ldan-pa # 'i shes-rab #  bo / / so-so #  rang-gis #  shes-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i rjes las thob ba'o / / zhi-ba #  thob-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir shes-pa #  ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  la nyon-mongs-pa # 'i gnyen-por-gyur-pa # 'o / / yon-tan #  mchog-tu #  phyin par bya-ba # 'i phyir shes-pa #  ni yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i shes-rab #  tu rig-par-bya # 'o / / bsgom-pa #  ni rnam lnga ste / / phung-po #  la gnas-pa #  nas dbang 'byor-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o / / 'dir tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  / / phung-po # r brten-nas #  bsgom-pa #  ste / / yid la byed dang bsams-pa #  dang / / thabs dang dbang 'byor de-bzhin #  te / / de-dag #  thams-cad #  brjod-pa #  yin / / ji-skad-du #  / / rgyu dang smin dang smon-lam #  dang / / so-sor-brtags-pa # s phung-po # r dran / / zhes bshad-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / de-la #  phung-po #  la gnas-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  ste /
hetu saMniSritAH yaH gotra balena pAramitAsu pratipatti aByAsaH vipAka saMniSritAH yaH Atma BAva saMpad tibalena
# de-la #  rgyu la gnas-pa #  ni gang rigs kyi stobs kyis pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la nan-tan-gyis #  goms-par-byed-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-smin-pa #  la gnas-pa #  ni gang lus-phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i stobs kyis so /
prANi DAna saMniSritAH yaH pUrva praNiDAna balena
# smon-lam #  la gnas-pa #  ni gang sngon gyi smon-lam-gyi-stobs #  so /
pratisaMKyAna bala saMniSritAH yaH prajQA balena pAramitAsu pratipatti aByAsaH
# so-sor-brtags-pa'i-stobs #  la gnas-pa #  ni shes-rab #  kyi stobs kyis pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams la nan-tan-gyis #  goms-par-byed-pa # 'o /
manaskAra saMniSritA pAramitA BAvanA catur AkArA
# yid-la-byed-pa #  la gnas-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  ste /
aDimukti manaskAreNa sarva pAramitA pratisaMyukta sUtrAntam aDimucyamAnasya
# mos-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa # s bsgom-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  thams-cad #  dang ldan-pa # 'i mdo-sde #  la mos-pa #  bsgom-pa # 'o /
AsvAda nAmanaskAreNa labDAH pAramitAH AsvAdayataH guNa darSana yogena
# ro myang-ba # 'i yid-la-byed-pa # s bsgom-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  thob-pa #  rnams la phan yon mthong-ba # 'i tshul-gyis #  ro-myong-bar-byed-pa # 'o /
anumoda nAma naskAreNa sarva loka DAtuzu sarva sattvAnAm dAna Adikam anumodamAnasya
# rjes-su-yi-rang-ba #  yid-la-byed-pa # s bsgom-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  thams-cad-kyi #  sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rjes-su-yi-rang-ba # 'o /
aBinandana amanaskAreNa AtmanaH sattvAnAm ca anAgatam pAramitA viSezam aBinandamAnasya
# mngon bar dga'-ba #  yid-la-byed-pa # s bsgom-pa #  ni bdag dang sems-can #  rnams kyi ma-'ongs-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i khyad-par #  la mngon-par-dga'-ba # 'o /
ASaya saMniSritA pAramitA BAvanA zaXa AkArA atRptA ASayena vEpulya ASayena mudita ASayena upakara ASayena nirlepa ASayena kalyANa ASayena ca
# bsam-pa #  la gnas-pa #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  rnam drug ste / / mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  dang yangs-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  dang dga'-ba'i-bsam-pa #  dang phan-gdags-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  dang gos-pa #  med-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  dang dge-ba # 'i bsam-pa # 'o /
tatra boDisattvasya dAne atRpta ASayaH yat boDisattvasya ekakzaNe gaFgA nadI vAlikA samAn lokaDAtUn sapta ratna paripUrNAn pratipAdayataH gaFgA nadI vAlikA samAn= ca Atma BAvanA evam pratikzaNam gaFgA nadI vAlikA samAn kalpAn pratipAdayataH
# de-la #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sbyin-pa #  la mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  ni gang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  skad-cig-gcig #  la gang g'a'i klung gi bye-ma #  snyed kyi 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  rin-po-che-sna-bdun #  gyis yongs su bkang ba dang lus gang g'a'i klung gi bye-ma #  snyed sems-can #  gcig la sbyin-pa # r byed ce'o /
yaTA ca eka sattvasya evam yAvAn sattvaDAtuH anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO paripAcitavyaH / tam anena paryAyeNa pratipAdayet atRptaH eva boDisattvasya dAna ASaye iti
# de-bzhin-du #  skad-cig-re-re-la #  gang ga'i klung gi bye-ma #  snyed kyi bskal-pa # r sbyin-pa # r byed cing sems-can #  gcig la ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  sems-can-gyi-khams #  ji-snyed-pa #  bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  la yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed la rnam grang 'dis de-la #  sbyin yang mi-ngoms-pa #  nyid ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sbyin-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  ste /
yaH evaMrUpam ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya dAne atRpta ASayaH
# rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni sbyin-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i bsam-pa #  mi-ngoms-pa #  yin no /
na ca boDisattvaH evaMrUpAm dAna paraMparAm kzaNa mAtram api hApayati vicCinatti AboDi maNxana nizadanAt iti
# byang-chub-kyi-snying-po #  la 'dug gi bar-du #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # r sbyin-pa #  gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud-pa #  skad-cig #  tsam yang nyams-pa # r mi byed cing rgyun mi gcod de /
yaH evaMrUpe ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya dAne vipula ASayaH
# rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni sbyin-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i yangs-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o /
muditataraH ca boDisattvaH Bavati tAn sattvAn= taTA dAnena anugRhNan na ca te sattvAH tena dAnena anugRhyamANAH iti / yaH evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya dAne mudita ASayaH
# de-ltar #  sbyin-pa # s sems-can #  de-dag #  rjes su 'dzin-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni shin-tu #  dga'-ba #  yin gyi sbyin-pa #  des rjes su gzung-ba # 'i sems-can #  de-dag #  ni de lta ma yin te / / rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang yin ba de ni sbyin-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  dga'-ba'i-bsam-pa # 'o / / gang dag la de-ltar #  sbyin-pa # s phan-'dogs-pa # 'i sems-can #  de-dag #  ni bdag la shin-tu #  phan-'dogs-pa # r byang-chub-sems #  dpas mthong gi / / bdag-gis #  ni ma yin te /
upakaratarAn= ca boDisattvaH tAn sattvAn AtmanaH samanupaSyati yezAm taTA dAnena upakaroti na AtmAnam tezAm anuttara samyak saMboDi upastamBatAm uzAdAya iti
# de-dag #  ni bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  ston-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni sbyin-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i phan-'dogs-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni sems-can #  rnams la de-ltar #  sbyin-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i bsod nams yangs-pa #  mngon-pa # r 'du byas kyang len du phan-'dogs-pa # 'am / / rnam-par-smin-pa #  'dod-pa #  med de /
yaH evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya dAne upakara ASayaH / na ca boDisattvaH sattvezu taTA vipulam api dAna mayam puNyam aBisaMskRtya pratikAreNa vA arTI Bavati vipAkena vA iti / ye evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya dAnapAramitA BAvanAyAm nirlepa ASayaH / yat boDisattvaH taTA vipulasya api dAna skanDasya vipAkam sattvezu eva aBinandati na AtmanaH sarva sattva sADAraNam ca kRtvA anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO pariNAmayati iti / yaH evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya dAnapAramitA BAvanAyAm kalyANa ASayaH / tatra boDisattvasya SIla pAramitA BAvanAyAm yAvat prajQA pAramitA BAvanAya tRpta ASayaH yat boDisattvaH gaFgA nadI vAlikA samezu AtmaBAvezu gaFgA nadI vAlikA sama kalpa AyuH pramANezu sarva upakaraNa nirantara viGAtI tri sAhasra mahA sAhasre lokaDAtO= agni paripUrNe caturviDam IryApaTam kalpayan= ekam SIla pAramitAkzaNam yAvat prajQApAramitAkzaNam BAvayet etena paryAyeNa yAvat SIla skanDaH yAvatprajQA skanDaH yena anuttarAm samyaksaMboDim aBisaMbuDyate SIla skanDam yAvat prajQA skanDam BAvayet atRptaH evam boDisattvasya SIlam iti ABAvanAyAm ASayaH yAvat prajA pAramitA BAvanAyam
# rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i gos-pa #  med-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sbyin-pa # 'i phung-po #  yangs-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa #  de-lta-bu #  yang sems-can #  rnams kyi yin bar mngon-par-dga'-ba # r byed kyi / / bdag la ni ma yin te / / sems-can-thams-cad #  dang thun mong du byas-na # s bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  tu yongs su bsngo'o / / rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i dge-ba # 'i bsam-pa # 'o / / de-la #  tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa # 'i bar la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  ni / / gang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  lus gang gla'i klung gi bye-ma #  snyed du gyur cing tshe'i-tshad #  bskal-ba #  gang gla'i klung gi bye-ma #  snyed du gyur la rgyun-du #  yo-byad #  thams-cad-kyi # s phongs-pa # r gyur cing / / stong-gsum #  gyi stong-chen-po # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  mes rab tu gang-ba #  na spyod-la # m bzhi byed cing skad-cig-gcig #  la tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  nas / / skad-cig-gcig #  la shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom zhing rnam-grangs-'dis #  tshul-khrims-kyi-phung-po #  ji-snyed-pa #  dang shes-rab #  kyi bar gyi phung-po #  ji-snyed-pa #  gang-gis #  bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r 'tshang rgya ba'i tshul-khrims-kyi-phung-po #  nas shes-rab #  kyi bar gyi phung-po #  de bsgom yang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mi-ngoms-pa #  nyid ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  la mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  ste /
yaH evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya SIla pAramitA BAvanA AyAma tRpta ASayaH yAvat prajQApAramitAyAm BAvanAyAm
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i bsam-pa #  rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  la mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la mi-ngoms-pa # 'i bsam ba'o /
yat boDisattvaH tAm SIla pAramitA BAvanA paraMparAm yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanA paraMparamA boDimaNXa nizadanAt na BraMSayati na vicCinatti iti
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  byang-chub-kyi-snying-po #  la 'dug gi bar-du #  tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud-pa #  nas shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud-pa #  nyams-pa # r mi byed cing /
yaH evaMrUpaH ASAyaH ayam boDisattvasya SIla pAramitA BAvanAyAm yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanAyAm vipula ASayaH
# rgyun mi gcod-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas; shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  yangs-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o /
muditataraH ca boDisattvaH Bavati tayA SIla pAramitA BAvanayA yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanayA sattva ananugRhNan na tu eva te sattvAH anugRhyamANAH iti
# tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  des sems-can #  rjes su 'dzin-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni rab-tu-dga'-ba #  yin gyi / / rjes su bzung-ba # 'i sems-can #  de-dag #  ni de lta ma yin te / / rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni /
yaH evaMrUpa ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya SIla pAramitA BAvanAyAm yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanAyAm mudita ASayaH / upakaratarAn= ca sa boDisattvaH tAn sattvAn AtmanaH samanupaSyati yezAm taTA SIla pAramitA BAvanayA yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanayA upakarAti na AtmAnam tezAm anuttarAm samyaksaMboDi upastamBatAsu pAdAya iti
# tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i dga'-ba'i-bsam-pa # 'o / / tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa # s / / gang dag la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i sems-can #  de-dag #  ni bdag la shin-tu #  phan-'dogs-pa # r byang-chub-sems #  dpas mthong gi bdag-gis #  ni ma yin no / / de-dag #  ni bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  ston-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaH eva rUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya SIla pAramitA BAvanAyAm yAvat prajQApAramita aBAvanAyAm upakarASayaH
# rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  'di ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i phan-'dogs-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o /
na ca boDisattvaH taTA vipulam api SIla pAramitA mayam yAvat prajQApAramitAm ayam puNyam aBisaMskRtya tasya pratikAreNa vA arTI Bavati vipAkena vA iti
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni 'di-ltar #  tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  las byung-ba #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar las byung-ba # 'i bsod nams yangs-pa #  mngon-par-'dus-byas #  kyang / / de-la #  lan-du-phan-'dogs-pa # 'am rnam-par-smin-pa #  las 'dod-pa #  med de /
yaH evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya SIla pAramitAyAm yAvat prajQApAramitAyAm nirlepa ASayaH
# rnam-pa #  'di-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha rol tu phyin ba bsgom-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i gos-pa #  med-pa # 'i bsam-pa # 'o /
tatra yat boDisattvaH evam SIla pAramita aBAva nAmasya yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanA mayasya puNya skanDasya vipAkam sattvezu eva aBinandati na AtmanaH sarva sattva sADAraNam ca kRtvA anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO pariNAmayati iti
# de-la #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgoms-pa-las-byung-ba # 'i bsod nams kyi phung-po #  rnam-par-smin-pa #  de-lta-bu #  yang sems-can #  rnams kyi yin par mngon-par-dga'-ba # r byed kyi bdag la ni ma yin te / / sems-can-thams-cad #  dang thun mong du byas-na # s bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  tu yongs su bsngo'o /
yaH evaMrUpaH ASayaH ayam boDisattvasya SIla pAramitAyAm BAvanAyAm yAvat prajQApAramitA BAvanAyAm kalyANa ASayaH / upAya saMniSritA pAramitA BAvanA traya AkArA nirvikalpena jQAnena trimaNXala pariSudDi pratyavekzaNa tAm upAdAya
# rnam-pa #  de-lta-bu # 'i bsam-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  bsgom-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i dge-ba # 'i bsam-pa # 'o / / thabs la gnas te pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  gang zhe na / / rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i phyir rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis 'khor gsum yongs-su-dag-pa #  ste /
taTA hi saH upAyaH sarva manaskArANAm aBinizpattaye
# thabs de ni yid-la-byed-pa #  thams-cad #  mngon-par-'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
viBu tva saMniritA pAramitA BAvanA traya AkArA kAya viBu tvataH caryA viBu tvataH deSanA viBu tvaH ca
# dbang 'byor-ba #  la gnas te pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  bsgom-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / lus la dbang 'byor-pa #  dang spyod-pa #  la dbang 'byor-pa #  dang bshad ba la dbang 'byor-ba # 'o /
tatra kAya viBu tvam tATAgatO dvO kAyO drazwavyO svABAvikaH sAMBogikaH ca
# lus la dbang 'byor-pa #  ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i sku gnyis su blta-bar-bya #  ste / / rang-bzhin #  dang longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa # 'o /
tatra caryA viBu tvam nErmANikaH kAyaH drazwavyaH yena sarva AkArAm sarva sattvAnAm saha DArmika caryAm darSayati
# de-la #  spyod-pa #  la dbang 'byor-ba #  ni sprul pa'i skur blta-bar-bya #  ste / / des sems-can-thams-cad #  la spyod-pa #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  kun-tu #  ston to /
deSanA viBu tvam zaz pAramitA sarva AkAra deSanA AyAma vyAGAtataH
# bshad-pa #  la dbang 'byor-ba #  ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  bshad-pa #  la thogs-pa-med-pa # 'o /
praBedataH azwAdaSaBiH upastamBEH zaNNAm pAramitAnAm praBedaH veditavyaH
# rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni ston-pa #  bco brgyad kyis pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  drug rab-tu-dbye-ba # r blta-bar-bya # 'o /
azwAdaSa upastamBAH kAya upastamBaH citta upastamBaH kuSala upastamBaH sugati upastamBaH boDi upastamBaH karuNA upastamBaH sattva aparityAga upastamBaH hIna citta parityAga upastamBaH / anutpattika Darma kzAnti upastamBaH kuSala mUla prayoga upastamBaH kuSala mUla samudAgama upastamBaH kuSala mUla akzaya tA upastamBaH apariKeda upastamBaH sarva cintita arTa samRdDa yutamBaH gaNa parikarzaNa upastamBaH BUmi praveSa upastamBaH budDa Darma samudAnayana upastamBaH budDa kRtya anuzWAna upastamBaH ca
# rtog-pa #  bco brgyad ni lus rton-pa #  dang; sems rton-pa #  dang dge-ba #  rton-pa #  dang bde-'gro #  rton-pa #  dang byang-chub #  rton-pa #  dang snying-rje #  rton-pa #  dang sems-can #  yongs su mi gtong-pa #  rton-pa #  dang dman-pa # 'i sems yongs su dor-ba #  rton-pa #  dang mi-skye-ba'i-chos #  la bzod-pa #  rton-pa #  dang dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba la sbyor-ba #  rton-pa #  dang dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa #  rton-pa #  dang / / dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba mi-zad-pa #  rton-pa #  dang dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba la yongs-su-mi-skyo-ba #  rton-pa #  dang bsam-pa # 'i don-thams-cad #  'byor-ba #  rton-pa #  dang tshogs sdud-pa #  rton-pa #  dang sa la 'jug-pa #  rton-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa #  rton-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-mdzad-pa #  sgrub-pa #  rton-pa #  ste /
pratyekam dAna AdInAm trEviGyAt triBiH triBiH upastamBEH yaTAkramam saMgrahaH veditavyaH
# sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gsum du tha-dad-pa # s / / gsum gsum gyi go-rims-bzhin-du #  bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra triviDam dAnam aBaya dAnam Darma dAnam Amiza dAnam ca
# de-la #  sbyin-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni zang-zing-gi-sbyin-pa #  dang mi-'jigs-pa'i-sbyin-pa #  dang chos-kyi-sbyin-pa # 'o /
triviDam SIlam saMvara SIlam kuSala Darma saMgrAhakam SIlam sattva arTa kriyA SIlam ca
# tshul-khrims #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni sngom-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  dang dge-ba'i-chos-sdud-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  dang sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba # 'i tshul-khrims #  so /
triviDA kzAntiH apakAra marzaNa kzAntiH duHKa aDivAsanA kzAntiH Darma niDyAna kzAntiH ca
# bzod-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni / / gnod-pa-byed-pa #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  dang sdug-bsngal #  dang-du-len-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  dang chos la nges-par-sems-pa # 'i bzod-pa # 'o /
triviDam vIryam saMnAha vIryam prayoga vIryam sattva arTa kriyA vIryam ca
# brtson 'grus rnam-pa-gsum #  ni / / go-cha # 'i brtson 'grus dang sbyor-ba # 'i brtson 'grus dang sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba # 'i brtson 'grus so /
triviDam DyAnam dRzwa Darma suKa avihArAya DyAnam aBijQA nirhArAya DyAnam sattva arTa kriyAyE ca DyAnam
# bsam-gtan #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni mthong-ba # 'i chos la bde-bar-gnas-pa # r bya-ba # 'i bsam-gtan #  dang mngon-par-shes-pa #  mngon bar sgrub ba'i bsam-gtan #  dang sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba # 'i bsam-gtan #  no /
triviDA prajQA saMvRtya alaMbanA parama arTa alaMkanA sattva arTa AlambanA ca
# shes-rab #  rnam-pa-gsum #  ni kun-rdzob #  la dmigs-pa #  dang don-dam-pa #  la dmigs-pa #  dang sems-can-gyi-don #  la dmigs-pa # 'o /
tatra Amiza dAnam kAya upastamBaH anna pAna Adi upakaraNEH pratigrAhaka ASraya anugrahaNAt
# de-la #  zang-zing-gi-sbyin-pa #  ni lus rton-pa #  ste / / bza'-ba-dang-btung-ba #  la-la #  sogs-pa # 'i yo-byad #  rnams kyis len-pa # 'i lus la phan-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aBaya dAnam citta upastamBaH dOrmanasya viSeza apagamAya cetasaH ASvAsAya saMhArAt / iti evam anyat api yojyam
# mi-'jigs-pa'i-sbyin-pa #  ni sems rton-pa #  ste / / yid-mi-bde-ba # 'i bye-brag #  dang bral-bar-bya-ba # 'i phyir sems kyi dbugs-'byin-pa #  nye-bar-bsgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzhan la yang de-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
hIna cittam punar boDisattvasya saMsAra duHKa pariKeditayA SrAvaka pratyekabudDa cittam tad parityAga stamBaH duHKa aDivAsana kzAntiH veditavyA
# dman-pa # 'i sems ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  'khor-ba'i-sdug-bsngal #  gyis yongs su skyo-ba # s nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi sems te / / de yongs su 'dor-ba #  rton-pa #  ni sdug-bsngal #  dang-du-len-pa # 'i bzod-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
kuSala mUla akzaya tA sarva sattvezu kriyA arTa aDikAri tayA yAvat sAram nirupaDi Seze api nirvANa DAtO= aparityAgaH tad upastamBaH sattva arTa kriyA ayam vIryam veditavyam
# dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba mi-zad-pa #  ni sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi don-du-bya-ba #  lhag-par-byed-pa # s 'khor-ba #  ji-srid-pa #  dang phung-po #  lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings su yongs-su-mi-gtong-ba #  ste / / de rton-pa #  ni sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba # 'i brtson 'grus su rig-par-bya # 'o /
gaNa parikarzaNam karmam aDigamam niSritya vineyAnAm asamAhitasya cittasya samADAnAya samAhitasya vA cittasya vimokzAya avavAda anuSAsana uparadAnam tad upastamBaH sattva arTa kriyAyE DyAnam
# tshogs sdud-pa #  ni thob-pa #  la brten-nas #  'dus-pa #  rnams sems-mnyam-pa # r ma bzhag-pa #  mnyam-par-gzhag-pa # r bya-ba #  dang sems-mnyam-pa # r bzhag-pa #  rnam-par-thar-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir gdams pa dang rjes-su-bstan-pa #  rab-tu-sbyin-pa #  ste / / de rton-pa #  ni sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba # 'i bsam-gtan #  no /
BUmi praveSaH yayA deSanayA Darma aDimukti pUrvikayA saMBAra paripUrya apramuditAm BUmim praviSati tad upastamBaH saMvRti satya alaMkbanA prajQA / Sezam suyojya tvAt na yojitam
# sa la 'jug-pa #  ni chos la mos-pa #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i bshad-pa #  gang-gis #  tshogs yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byas-na # s / / rab-tu-dga'-ba # 'i sa la 'jug-pa #  ste / / de rton-pa #  ni kun-rdzob-kyi-bden-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'o / / lhag-ma #  ni legs-par-sbyor-ba # 'i phyir sbyar-ba # r ma byas so / / yang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ni sbyin-pa #  bdun te /
punar praBedaH sapta dAnAmi mUla dAnam gotra avasTasya boDisattvasya dAna pAramitA gotra mAtram niSritya dAnAt
# rtsa ba'i sbyin-pa #  ni rigs kyi gnas-skabs #  pa'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ste / / rigs tsam la brten-nas #  sbyin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
ADAna dAnam citta utpAda avasTasya praNiDAna samAdAnam niSritya dAnAt
# blangs-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  ni sems-bskyed-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  pa'i ste / / smon-lam #  yang-dag-par-blangs-pa #  la brten-nas #  sbyin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anugraha dAnam sva para arTa pratyavasTasya / anavagraha dAnam tattva arTa parIkzA avasTasya dAyaka Adi vikalpa aBiniveSa avagrAha aBAvAt
# rjes su 'dzin-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  ni bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  sgrub-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  pa'o / / 'dzin-pa-ngan-pa #  med-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  ni de-kho-na'i-don #  la yongs su rtogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  pa ste / / sbyin-bdag #  la-sogs-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i 'dzin-pa-ngan-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  med-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  ni mthu'i gnas-skabs #  pa ste /
nizparigraha dAnam praBAva avasTasya vinA vAhyena upakaraNa parigraheNa gagana gajaQja Adi samADiBiH AkASe pANim saMcArya yaTezwam ratna Adi varzaNAt / pratyarha dAnam paripAka avasTasya yaTA vineya anurUpam dAnAt
# phyi-rol #  gyi yo-byad #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  med-pa # r yang-na # m mkha' mdzod la-sogs-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  rnams kyis nam-mkha' #  la-la # g pa brkyang-na # s ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  rin-po-che #  la-sogs-pa # 'i char 'bebs-pa # 'o / / so-sor-rig-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  ni yongs-su-smin-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  pa'i ste / / sbyin-pa #  'dul-ba #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mthun-par #  sbyin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
mahAdAnam parama boDi avasTasya niruttara tvAt
# sbyin-pa #  chen-po #  ni byang-chub-mchog #  gi gnas-skabs #  pa ste / / bla-na-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
evam yAvat prajQA yaTAyogam veditavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyi bar-du #  ci-rigs-su #  sbyar-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
saMgrahaH dAnAdaBiH boDisattva BUmi saMgraha arTena tatra idam udAharaNa mAtram pAramita AdiBiH
# bsdus-pa #  ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s byang-chub-sems-dpa'i-sa #  bsdus-pa # 'i phyir te / / de-la #  pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyis rigs bsdus-pa #  'di ni dpe tsam mo /
gotra saMgrahaH dAna pAramitA Adi gotram liFgataH anugantavyam
# sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni rigs-kyi-rtags #  kyis bsdus-pa # r shes-pa # r bya'o /
citta utpAda saMgrahaH viSizwa citta utpAda saMgrahaNAt / dviviDaH hi citta utpAdaH aviSizwaH viSizwaH ca
# sems-bskyed-pa # s bsdus-pa #  ni khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i sems-bskyed-pa # s bsdus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sems-bskyed-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / khyad-par-can #  ma-yin-pa #  dang khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'o /
tatra aviSizwaH ahar vatAham anuttarAm samyaksaMboDim aBisaMbuDyeya iti
# de-la #  khyad-par-can #  ma-yin-pa #  ni kye-ma # 'o bdag bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  tu mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r 'tshang rgya bar shog shig snyam pa'o /
viSizwaH evam dAna pAramitAm paripUrayeyam yAvat prajQApAramitAm iti
# khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  de ni de-ltar #  sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r shog shig snyam pa nas / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
tat anena viSizwena citta utpAdena pAramitAnAm saMgrahaH veditavyaH tAsAm kAraNa BAvAt / sva para arTa saMgrahaH yat dAnena ESvarya parigRhaNa atyayam sva arTaH yat punar parAnupa karaNa upasaMhAreNa anugRhNAti ayam sva arTaH evam avaSizwABiH saMgrahaH veditavyaH
# khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i sems-bskyed-pa #  'dis ni pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / de-dag #  gi rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro / / bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  bsdus-pa #  las gang sbyin-pa # s phyug-po #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  'di ni bdag-gi-don #  to / / gang gzhan la yo-byad #  nye-bar-sgrub-pa # s rjes su 'dzin-pa #  'di ni gzhan-gyi-don #  to /
paramArTa saMgrahaH DarmaDAtum AraBya taTatAyAH dAna Adi sAmAnya lakzaNa tvAt
# lhag-ma #  rnams kyis bsdus-pa #  yang de-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / don-dam-pa # s bsdus-pa #  chos-kyi-dbyings #  las brtsams pa ni de-bzhin-nyid #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
jQAna saMBAram AraBya sarvajQa tA BAjana tA pAdanAt
# ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  las brtsams pa ni thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  kyi snod du sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jQAna parigraham AraBya sarvajQa tA parinizpAdanAt
# ye shes yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  las brtsams pa ni thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  yongs su sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jQAna anuparivartatAm AraBya paQcAnAm prajQApAramitA anuparivartanAt
# ye shes kyi rjes-su-'jug-pa #  las brtsams pa ni lnga po dag shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jQAna lakzaNam AraBya prajQApAramitAH samyak jQAna svaBAva tvAt
# ye shes kyi mtshan-nyid #  las brtsams pa ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir te /
iti evam taTatA samyak jQAna svaBAvataH paramArTaH dAna AdiBiH saMgRhItaH veditavyaH
# de-ltar-na #  de-bzhin-nyid #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i ye shes kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  don-dam-pa #  ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
etena udAharaNa mAtreNa SezaH saMgrahaH veditavyaH
# dpe brjod-pa #  'dis bsdus-pa #  la lhag-ma #  rnams brtag-pa # r bya'o /
vipakzaH dAna AdInAm yaTAkramam mAtsarya dOHSIlye kroDa kOSIdye vikzepa dOHprajQe
# mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  ni ser-sna #  dang 'chal-ba'i-tshul-khrims #  dang khro-ba #  dang le-lo #  dang rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba dang 'chal-ba'i-shes-rab #  ste sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
api Kalu yAvantaH kuSalAH DarmAH pAramitABiH saMgRhItAH tezAm yaH vipakzaH jQeya AvaraNam ca sa tAsAm vipakzaH veditavyaH / anuSaMsaH paQcaviDa Pala aDikAreNa aprameyaH veditavyaH / tat yaTA yaTAsva mAsAm vipakza prahANam visaMyoga Palam / dRzwe Darme sva para anugrahaNam puruzakAra Palam / AyatyAm uttarAt tara viSizwa ttaratama utpattiH nizyanda Palam / mahAboDiH aDipati Palam / mahA Boga tA sugati gamanam avaraBeda suKa sOmanasya bahulatA sattva ADipatyam avyAbADya Atma BAvatA maheSa AKya tA ca yaTAkramam dAna AdInAm vipAka Palam veditavyam / anyonya viniScayaH triviDaH prAyogikaH prABedikaH praBidya sAMdarSikaH ca / tatra prAyogikaH dAna prayoge sarvAsAm vRtti rUpalaByate
# yang pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams kyis bsdus-pa # 'i dge-ba'i-chos #  ji-snyed-pa #  de-dag #  gi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  gang-yin-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-yang #  de-dag #  gi mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  su rig-par-bya # 'o / / phan yon ni 'bras-bu #  rnam-pa-lnga # 'i gnas-skabs #  su dpag-tu-med-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / ji-ltar #  'di dag gi rang-gi #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  spong-ba #  bral-ba'i-'bras-bu #  dang mthong-ba # 'i chos la bdag-dang-gzhan #  rjes su 'dzin-pa #  skyes-bu #  byed-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang phyi-ma-la #  gong-nas-gong-du #  khyad-par-du-'phags-pa #  mchog dam-pa #  'byung-ba #  rgyu-mthun-pa'i-'bras-bu #  dang byang-chub-chen-po #  dbang-gi-'bras-bu #  dang longs-spyod-chen-po #  dang bde-'gror-'gro-ba #  dang khon-med-pa #  dang dbye-ba-med-pa #  dang bde-ba #  dang yid-bde-ba #  mang-ba #  dang sems-la-dbang #  ba dang lus la gnod-pa-med-pa #  dang dbang-che-bar-grags-pa #  ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / gcig-la-gcig #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / sbyor-ba-las-gyur-pa #  dang rab-tu-dbye-ba #  las gyur-pa #  dang rab tu phye-nas #  bstan-pa #  las gyur ba'o / / de-la #  sbyor-ba-las-gyur-pa #  ni sbyin-pa #  la sbyor-ba # r thams-cad #  'dus-pa # r dmigs te / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / nang dang phyi'i dngos-po #  yongs-su-gtong-ba # 'i sbyin-pa #  la sbyor-ba # 'o / / de-la #  gang yongs-su-btang-ba #  de ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o /
tat yaTA ADyAtmikam bAhyam vastu parityajanataH dAna prayogaH / tatra yaH parityAgaH sa dAna pAramitA
# de-la #  byams-pa'i-sems #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir gang gzhan la kun nas ma nar sems-pa #  dang gnod-pa #  dang rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  sdom-pa #  de ni tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o /
tatra eva yA mEtra cittasya paratra viGAta utpaIXA viheWa saMvaraNa tA sA SIla pAramitA / tatra eva yA uparoDa viGAta Keda marzaNa tA sA kzAnti pAramitA
# de-nyid-la #  gang nye-bar #  skor ba dang phongs-pa #  dang skyo-ba #  la ji-mi-snyam-pa #  de ni bzod-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o / / de-nyid-la #  gang phyir zhing sems spro-ba #  de ni brtson 'grus kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o /
tatra eva yA BUyas BUyas cittasya utsahanatA sA vIrya pAramitA
# de-nyid-la #  gang sems rtse gcig pa nyid de dge-ba #  las sems phyi-rol #  tu mi-'phro-ba #  de ni bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o /
tatra eva yA cittasya ekAgra tA kuSa lAt bahis avasaraNa tA sA DyAna pAramitA / tatra eva yA yaTAvat hetu Pala su gRhItatA dRzwi apara amarzaNa tA sA prajQApAramitA
# de-nyid-la #  rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  legs-par-bzung-ba #  dang lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  med-pa #  de ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o /
evam yAvat prajQApAramitAyAm yaTAyogam yojayitavyam uBaya dAnam sarvajQa jQAnam iti kRtvA / tatra prABedikaH svaBAva praBedena anukAra praBedena ca
# de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar la yang ci-rigs-su #  sbyar-ba # r bya ste / / mi-'jigs-pa'i-sbyin-pa #  ni thams-cad-du #  yang sbyin-pa #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / de-yang #  rab-tu-dbye-ba #  las gyur-pa #  ni ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  rab dbye-ba #  dang rjes su byed-pa # s rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang rjes-su-sbyor-ba # s rab-tu-dbye-ba #  dang skyed-pa # s rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'o /
tatra dAna AdInAm svaBAvaH yaTAkramam visargaH saMvaraH marzaNa aByutsAhaH citasTitiH pravicayaH ca / tatra dAna Adi prayogezu tad anya pAramitAnAm anuvRttiH pUrvavat
# de-la #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  ni rnam-pa # r gtong-ba #  dang sdom-pa #  dang ji-mi-snyam-pa #  dang mngon-par-spro-ba #  dang sems-gnas-pa #  dang rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa #  ste / / go-rims #  bzhin no / / de-la #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rjes su byed-pa #  ni sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  na / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  rnams rjes su 'jug ba ste snga-ma-bzhin #  no /
tatra dAna AdInAm upayogaH samAdApanA varNa vAdi tA su manojQa tA ca
# de-la #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rjes-su-sbyor-ba #  ni 'dzin-du-'jug-pa #  dang bsngags-pa-brjod-pa #  dang rab-tu-dga'-ba # 'o /
tatra dAna AdInAm ropaNA yA para saMtAne pratizWApanA
# de-la #  sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  skyed-pa #  ni gzhan-gyi-sems #  kyi rgyud la 'jog-pa # 'o /
tat atra dAna pAramitA Amiza dAnam tad anyAH paQca aBaya dAnam sarvAH sat Darma dAnam para saMtAne ropaNAt / tatra praBidya sAMdarSikaH eka avacAraka AdiBiH / tat yaTA yA dAna pAramitA SIla pAramitA api sA yA vA SIla pAramitA dAnapAramitA api sA paScAt pAdakaH yA yAvat SIla pAramitA dAna pAramitA api sA syAt dAna pAramitA na SIla pAramitA SIla pAramitayA asaMgRhItA yA dAna pAramitA
# de-la #  sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ni zang-zing-gi-sbyin-pa # 'o / / de-ma-yin-pa #  gzhan lnga ni mi-'jigs-pa'i-sbyin-pa # 'o / / thams-cad #  ni dam-pa'i-chos #  kyi sbyin-pa #  ste / / gzhan-gyi-sems #  kyi rgyud la skyes-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-la #  rab tu phye-nas #  bstan-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni gcig nas rtogs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'ang de yin nam / / tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'ang de yin nam zhe na /
evam yAvatya jQApAramitayA saMgRhItA dAna pAramitA paScAt pAdakEH yojayitavyA / yat dAnam sarvA sA pAramitA yA dAna pAramitA sarvam tat dAnam iti catuzkowikam
# tshig 'og ma dang sbyar-ba #  ste / / tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'ang de'o / / sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yin la / / tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  yang yod de / / tshul-khrims #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # s ma-zin-pa # 'i sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'o / / de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar-du #  sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  tshig 'og ma dang sbyor-ba #  rnams dang sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / sbyin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de thams-cad-sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yin nam; pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de thams-cad-sbyin-pa #  yin nam zhe na /
syAt dAnam na pAramitA yat na mahoboDi pariNAmitam / syAt pAramitAH na dAnam SIla AdayaH mahA boDi pariNAmitAH
# mu gsum du 'gyur te / / sbyin-pa #  yin la pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ni / / gang byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs su ma bsngos-pa # 'i sbyin-pa # 'o /
syAt dAnam ca pAramitA ca boDi pariNAmitAni dAna AdIni
# sbyin-pa # 'ang yin la pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'ang yin pa yod de; byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  rnams so /
syAt na dAnam na pAramitAH ukta vinirmuktAH DarmAH
# sbyin-pa #  yang ma yin la pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yang ma-yin-pa #  yod de / / sngar bshad-pa #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  so /
evam yAvat prajQApAramitAm AraBya catuzkowikam pratyekam yojayitavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar las brtsams te / / re-re #  la yang mu gsum gsum du sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
yaH dAnam samAcarati sarvaH asO dAna pAramitA anvayam puNyam prasavati iti catuzkowikam
# sbyin-pa #  la kun-tu-spyod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de thams-cad-sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i rgyu-las-byung-ba # 'i bsod nams skyed dam zhe na / / mu-bzhi # r 'gyur te /
praTamA kowiH mahA boDya pariNAmitam dAnam samAcarati
# mu dang-po #  ni byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs su ma bsngos-pa # 'i sbyin-pa #  spyod-pa # 'o /
dvitIyA kowiH dAna pAramitAm yAm samAdApana varNa BAzaNa sumanaH jQatABiH
# mu gnyis-pa #  ni sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  las yang-dag-par #  'dzin-du-'jug-pa #  dang bsngags-pa-brjod-pa #  dang yid-rab-tu-dga'-ba # 'o /
tRtIyA kowiH mahA boDi pariNAmitena dAnena
# mu gsum-pa #  ni byang-chub-chen-po # r yongs-su-bsngos-pa # 'i sbyin-pa # 'o /
caturTI kowiH etAn AkArAn sTApayitvA
# mu-bzhi #  pa ni rnam-pa #  'di dag ma-gtogs-pa # s so /
evam yAvat prajQApAramitAm AraBya pratyekam catuzkowikam yojayitavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa # 'i bar las brtsams te / / re-re #  la yang mu-bzhi #  bzhir sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
viSezataH vEpulye OdArya gAmBIrya deSanA tad Palasya sarvajQa tvasya parama udAra gamBIra tvAt Pala anurUpyeNa hetu nirdeSaH drazwavyaH
# shin-tu #  rgyas-pa #  la rgya-che-ba #  dang zab-pa # r yang bstan-pa #  ni de'i 'bras-bu #  thams-cad-mkhyen-pa-nyid #  mchog-tu-rgya-che-ba #  dang zab-pa # 'i phyir 'bras-bu #  dang mthun-par #  rgyu bsten-pa # r blta'o /
ekatyAnAm tad anaDimokze trAsaH boDisattva gotra vEkalyam prakRtyA hIna citta tayA gAmBIrya OdArya deSanAm na aDimoktum Saknuvanti / sati api tad gotra tve mahA boDim AraBya praNiDAna AdInAm kuSala mUla AdInAm anavararpaNAt sati api tad avaropaNe mahAyAna pratikzepaka sattva parigRhIta tvAt iti
# kha-cig #  de-la #  mi mos-pa #  dang skrag-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i rigs-dang-mi-ldan-pa #  dang rang-bzhin-gyis #  sems dman-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de'i rigs su gyur du zin-kyang #  byang-chub-chen-po #  las brtsams te / / smon-lam #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba ma-bskyed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba bskyed du zin-kyang #  theg-pa-chen-po #  spong-ba # 'i sems-can #  gyis yongs-su-zin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aDimucyamAnAnAm api ekatyAnAm aniryANam nIta arTa sUtram ananvizya svayam dRzwi parAmarza sTAyitayA yaTArutam arTa aBiniveSAtaH
# kha-cig #  mos kyang nges-par-'byung-ba # r mi-'gyur-ba #  ni nges-pa'i-don #  gyi mdo-sde #  ma brtsal te / / bdag-nyid #  lta-ba #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  la gnas-pa #  dang don la sgra ji bzhin-du #  mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i phyir te /
tat yaTA sarva Darma niHsvaBAva tA vacanAt sarva lakzaNena sarva BAva apavAdinaH
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / chos-thams-cad #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig gis mtshan-nyid #  thams-cad-kyi # s dngos-po-thams-cad #  la skur ba 'debs-pa # 'o /
evam anye api yaTA ruta arTa aBiniveSinaH mahA yAne na niryAnta udveditavyam nAnA aBiprAya BAzita tvAt mahAyAnasya iti
# de-bzhin-du #  gzhan la yang don la sgra ji bzhin-du #  mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni theg-pa-chen-po #  las nges-par #  mi-'byung-ba # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / theg-pa-chen-po #  la ni dgongs-pa #  sna-tshogs #  kyis gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
idam ca saMDAya uktam BagavatA mahA DarmAt arSe Darma paryAye boDisattvasya yaTA rutam ayoniSaH DarmAn vicinvataH azwAviMSatiH asat dRzwayaH utpadyante / azwAviMSatiH asat dRzwayaH katamAH
# 'di-la #  dgongs nas bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis chos kyi me long chen-po # 'i chos-kyi-rnam-grangs #  las gsungs-pa #  / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sgra ji bzhin-du #  tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # r chos-rnams #  rnam-par-'byed-pa #  la lta-ba-ngan-pa #  nyi shu rtsa brgyad 'byung ste / / lta-ba-ngan-pa #  nyi shu rtsa brgyad po dag gang zhe na /
nimitta dRzwiH yAvat aBimAna dRzwiH ca
# mtshan-ma # r lta-ba #  nas mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  gyi bar-du #  lta-ba # 'o /
tatra nisvaBAvAH sarva DarmAH anutpannAH iti evamAdikam mahAyAne rutam upalaBya tad aBisaMDya kuSalAH yaTArutam eva asya arTam aDimucyamAnAH aBAvaH eva ayam BagavatA deSitaH sarva DarmANAm anutpAdaH eva iti aBAva Adi nimittam aBiniviSante sA ezAm Bavati nimitta dRzwiH
# de-la #  theg-pa-chen-po #  la chos-thams-cad #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgrar dmigs shing thos-nas #  / / dgongs-pa #  de-la #  mi-mkhas-pa #  dag 'di'i don la sgra ji bzhin-du #  mos nas 'di ni dngos-po-med-pa-nyid #  du bstan to zhes chos-thams-cad #  ma-skyes-pa #  nyid-du #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # r mngon-par-zhen-pa #  ni de-dag #  gi mtshan-ma # r lta-ba #  yin no /
te evam aBAva Adi nimittam aBiniviSamAnAH trIn svaBAvAn avadante parikalpitam svaBAvam paratantram parinizpannam ca
# de-dag-nyid #  med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # r mngon-pa # r zhen nas kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'o /
tatra ayam parikalpitaH svaBAvaH yat rUpam iti vA yAvat nirvANAm iti vA aBilApa prajQapti mAtra Ba BUtaH niHSarIra arTaH yat bAlAH rUpa Adi lakzaNam samAropattaH parikalpayanti
# de-la #  'di ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de gang gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  brjod-pa # s brtags-pa #  tsam du zad nas yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  lus med-pa # 'i don gang-la #  byis-pa #  rnams kyis gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du sgro btags-nas #  yongs-su-rtog-pa # 'o /
tatra ayam paratantraH svaBAvAH yat tat eva aBUta parikalpa mAtram
# de-la #  'di ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo-bo-nyid #  de / / gang yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  kun-tu-rtog-pa #  tsam de nyid do /
tatra ayam parinizpannaH svaBAvaH yat sarva DarmANAm tattvam taTatA
# de-la #  'di ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de / / gang zhe na / / chos-thams-cad #  kyi de-kho-na #  de-bzhin-nyid #  do /
tad apavAda AkArAH tisraH dRzwayaH Bavanti prajQapti apavAda dRzwiH parikalpa apavAda dRzwiH tattva apavAda dRzwiH ca
# de-la #  skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  'dis lta-ba #  gsum du 'gyur te / / btags-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang kun du rtog-pa #  la skur ba 'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang de-kho-na #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba # 'o /
te evam sarvaTA sarva Darma anapavadamAnAH tasyAH apavAda dRzweH pratizWApana arTam kAMcid eva yuktim parigRhNanti ye api nIta arTAH sUtrAntAH niraBilApa DarmatA dyotakAH tAn api sarvAn sva dRzwayA anulomyena pariNAmayanti
# de-ltar #  de-dag #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  chos-thams-cad #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # s na / / skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  de gzhag-pa # 'i phyir rigs-pa #  'ga' zhig yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  dang nges-pa'i-don #  gyi mdo-sde #  gang dag brjod-du-med-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  ston-pa #  de-dag #  thams-cad #  kyang rang-gi #  lta-ba #  dang mthun-par #  yongs-su-grub-pa #  de-dag #  ni lta-ba #  gnyis su 'gyur te /
te eva dve dRzwaH BavataH parigraha dRzwiH pariNati dRzwiH ca
# yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang sgyur ba'i lta-ba # 'o / / de-dag #  yang lta-ba #  'di-'dra-ba # r 'gyur te /
te punar evaMdRzwayaH Bavanti yaH etAm IdRSIm dRzwim niSritya kuSalam akuSalam vA samAcarati sa niravadyaH eva Bavati nirdozaH sarvam eva asya tad kalyANa tAm yAti pUrva upacitAt ca AvaraNAt sa niHsara tA iti evam ezAm dve dRzwI anavadyatA dRzwiH niHsaraNa dRzwiH ca
# lta-ba #  'di-lta-bu #  la brten-nas #  dge-ba # 'am mi-dge-ba #  yang rung spyad na kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  med-pa #  dang skyon-med-pa # r 'gyur zhing de thams-cad #  dge-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  dang sngon bsags-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  las de 'byung-bar-'gyur-ba # r 'dzin-pa #  de-lta-bu #  de-dag #  gi lta-ba #  gnyis te / / kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  med-par-lta-ba #  dang nges-par-'byung-ba # r lta-ba # 'o /
te ca evam sva dRzwa avaBinivizwAH tat dRzwi viparyayeNa skanDa Adi Darma vyavasTApakam SrAvaka piwakam avajAnanti ye ca tAm apavAda dRzwim anaDimuktAH SrAvaka yAnIyAH tAn pradvizanti / te ete dve dRzwI BavataH avajQA dRzwiH prakopa dRzwiH ca / sva dRzwi anusAreNa ca ete yaTAvat SUnya tA nimitta apraNihitAni vyavasTApayamAnAH atallakzaNe tad lakzaNa saMjQinaH viparItam ezAm lakzaNam vyavasTApayanti evaMcittAH ca Bavanti yasyAm IdRSyAm DarmatAyAm avataranti avatarayanti vA sarve te aprameyam puNyam prasavanti iti evam ete dRzwI viparIta dRzwiH prasava dRzwiH ca
# de-dag #  lta-ba #  de-lta-bu #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa # s lta-ba #  de-las-bzlog-pa # 'i phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos rnam-par-'jog-pa #  nyan-thos-kyi-sde-snod #  khyad-du-gsod-pa #  dang gang dag skur ba 'debs-pa # r lta-ba #  de-la #  mi mos-pa #  nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  pa de-dag #  la rab tu sdang-ba # 'i lta-ba #  'di gnyis te / / dbang za-ba # 'i lta-ba #  dang rab-tu-'khrug-pa # 'i lta-ba # 'o / / rang-gi #  lta-ba # 'i tshul du na stong-pa-nyid #  dang mtshan-ma-med-pa #  dang smon-pa-med-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  yin no snyam nas / / de'i mtshan-nyid #  ma-yin-pa #  la de'i mtshan-nyid #  du 'du-shes #  pa ni de-dag #  gi mtshan-nyid #  phyin-ci-log #  tu rnam-pa # r 'jog cing 'di snyam-du #  yang sems te / / gang dag chos-nyid #  'di-lta-bu #  la 'jug-pa #  dang 'dzud-pa #  de-dag #  thams-cad #  bsod nams kyi phung-po #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  skyed do snyam pa la de-lta-bu # 'i lta-ba #  'di gnyis te / / phyin-ci-log #  tu lta-ba #  dang 'phel-ba # 'i lta-ba # 'o /
yadA punar te tAm dRzwim AraBya paraMranuyujyante tadA na kiMcid svayam icCanti aByupagantum Cala jAtiByAm ca parAn anuyuQjante
# gang-gi-tshe #  de-dag #  lta-ba #  de-la # s brtsams te gzhan dag gis dris-pa #  de'i tshe bdag ni ci-yang #  khas-len-pa # r mi 'dod kyi / / tshig dor dang ltag chod kyis gzhan la 'dri-ba # 'i lta-ba #  'di gnyis te /
te ete anaByupagama dRzwiH kusRti dRzwiH ca
# khas mi len-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang ngan g-yo'i lta-ba # 'o / / de-dag #  yang 'di-lta-bu # 'i nga-rgyal #  can du 'gyur ro /
te ca evam aBimAninaH Bavanti yaH evam pratipadyante te samyak budDAn BagavataH pUjayanti satkurvanti iti ezAm satkAra dRzwiH
# gang dag de-ltar #  sgrub-pa #  de-dag #  ni sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams la mchod-pa-byed-pa #  dang rim-gro-byed-pa # r 'dzin-pa #  de-dag #  gi lta-ba #  ni bkur-sti # 'i lta-ba # 'o /
aviparIta Darma tA kuSalEH ca tatA dRzweH vivecyamAnAH sUpa pannayA prasidDayA yuktayA pratyAyamAnA api tAm dRzwim na kaTaMcid parityajanti etat eva taTyam miTyA anyat iti ezA dRXa mUXa tA dRzwiH
# phyin-ci-log #  ma-yin-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  la mkhas-pa #  dag gis lta-ba #  de dang 'byed cing legs-par #  'thad-pa #  dang rab tu grags-pa # 'i rigs-pas #  yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa #  na yang lta-ba #  de ji-ltar #  yang yongs su mi 'dor te 'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni log-pa # 'o snyam pa de-dag #  ni rmongs-pa #  brtan-pa # 'i lta-ba # 'o /
etAsAm ca yaTAnirdizwAnAm dRzwInAm yat vAsanA dOzWulyam sA mUla dRzwiH / ete eva ca saptadaSa dRzwayaH doza udBAvanA muKena avaSizwABiH dRzwiBiH punar nidiSyante / tat yaTA dRzwa avadRzwa dRzwi nimitta dRzwiH iti ucyate aBAva Adi nimitta aBiniveSinaH eva sataH sarva nimitta anaBiniveSa sajQi tvAt
# lta-ba #  ji-skad-du #  bstan-pa #  de-dag #  gi bag-chags #  kyi gnas-ngan-len #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni rtsa ba'i lta-ba # 'o / / lta-ba #  bcu bdun po de-dag-nyid #  kyi skyon brjod-pa # 'i sgo nas yang bshad-par-bya #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / mtshan-ma # r lta-ba #  ni lta-ba #  la lta-ba #  ma-yin-pa # r lta-ba #  zhes bya ste / / med-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  nyid-du #  gyur kyang /
prajQapti apavAda dRzwiH parikalpa apavAda dRzwiH tattva apavAda dRzwiH ca prayoga nirAkaraNa dRzwiH sarva apavAdinaH vyAyAmaniH sAmarTya saMjQi tvAt
# mtshan-ma-thams-cad #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med do snyam pa'i 'du-shes-can #  du gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / brtags-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang kun du rtog-pa #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang de-kho-na #  la skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ni sbyor-ba #  sel-ba # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / thams-cad-la #  skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ni 'bad-pa #  mthu-med-pa # 'i 'du-shes-can #  du 'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
parigraha dRzwiH pariNati dRzwiH ca anEryANika dRzwiH anupAya prayuktasya tad PalAn avApteH
# yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang sgyur ba'i lta-ba #  ni nges-par-'byin-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / thabs-ma-yin-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  ni de'i 'bras-bu #  mi-'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anavadyata adRzwi niHsaraNa dRzwiH ca AvaraNa upacaya dRzwiH miTyA pratipadyamAnasya AvaraNa kzaya asaMBavAt
# kha-na-ma-tho-ba #  med-par-lta-ba #  dang nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i lta-ba #  ni sgrib-pa #  sogs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / log-pa # r sgrub-pa # 'i sgrub-pa #  zad mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
avajQA dRzwiH prakopa dRzwiH ca apuNya prasava dRzwiH sadDarma sabrahmacAri vipratipatti muKena mahAkzati samAsAdanAt anAt
# dbang za-ba # 'i lta-ba #  dang rab-tu-'khrug-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ni bsod nams ma-yin-pa #  'phel-ba # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / dam-pa'i-chos #  dang tshangs-pa #  mtshungs-pa # r spyod-pa #  la log-pa # r sgrub-pa # 'i sgo nas smas pa chen-po #  'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / phyin-ci-log #  tu lta-ba #  dang 'phel-ba # 'i lta-ba #  ni 'bras-bu-med-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ste /
viparIta dRzwiH prasava dRzwiH ca vEPalya dRzwiH asamyak Darma tA vyavasTApana grahaNa grAhaNEH viSezA naDi gamAt anaByupagama dRzwiH kusRti dRzwiH ca nigrAhya dRzwiH anyAyena vAdam kurvataH jaya asaMBavAt
# yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  rnam-par-'jog-pa #  'dzin-pa #  dang 'dzin-du-'jug-pa #  la khyad-par #  mi-'thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / khas mi len-pa # 'i lta-ba #  dang ngan g-yo'i lta-ba #  ni chad-pas-bcad-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / rigs-pa-ma-yin-pa # s rgol na rgyal mi srid-pa # 'i phyir ro /
satkAra dRzwiH aByAKyAna dRzwiH atada AKyAyini tat samArApaNAt
# bkur-sti # 'i lta-ba #  ni skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / de mi gsung-ba #  la de sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dRXa mUXa tA dRzwiH akaTya dRzwiH miTyA aBiniveSinA saha sAm kaTya pratizeDAn niraTaka tAm upAdAya
# rmongs-pa #  brtan-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ni bsnyad-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i lta-ba #  ste / / log-pa #  la mngon-par-zhen-pa #  dang 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  bya-ba #  bkag-pa # 'i phyir te /
mUla dRzwiH mahA dRzwiH tatas AyatyAm puzwatara sarva dRzwi gata pratApanAt
# don-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rtsa ba'i lta-ba #  ni lta-ba #  chen-po #  ste / / de-la # s phyi-ma-la #  lta-bar-gyur-pa #  thams-cad #  shin-tu #  brtas-pa #  rgyas-pa # r 'gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sarvAH etAH saptaviMSati dRzwayaH aBimAna dRzwiH aBUta aBimAna samutTita tvAt
# lta-ba #  nyi shu rtsa bdun po thams-cad #  ni mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  gyi lta-ba #  ste / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  gyis slong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atas eva anantaram tatra eva sUtre uktam iti imAH saptadaSa samAnAH daSa Bavanti daSa samAnAH saptadaSa Bavanti saptaviMSatiH samAnAH ekA Bavati ekA samAnA saptaviMSatiH Bavanti iti
# de'i-phyir #  mdo-sde #  de-nyid-la # s de'i-'og-tu #  'di dag gi bcu bdun yin yang bcur 'gyur ro / / bcu yin yang bcu bdun du 'gyur ro / / nyi shu rtsa bdun yin yang gcig-tu #  'gyur ro / / gcig yin yang nyi shu rtsa bdun du 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so / / bam po brgyad pa /
niHsvaBAvAH sarva DarmAH yasmAt svayam ezAm BAvaH na asti pratyayAn= tu apekzya BAvaH na pratiziDyate
# chos-thams-cad #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  'di dag ni bdag-nyid-kyis #  'byung-ba #  med kyi / / rkyen la ltos nas 'byung-ba #  bkag-pa #  ni ma yin no /
yena vA svaBAvena ete pUrvam aBUt na tena svena BAvena BUyas Sakyam eBiH Bavitum iti niHsvaBAvAH
# ngo-bo-nyid #  gang-du #  de-dag #  sngar byung-ba # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  der yang de-dag #  gis bskyed mi-nus-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o /
prApta aBrazwa lakzaNAnAm api pratyutpannAnAm sve BAve avasTAna aBAvAt niHsvaBAvAH
# thob la ma-nyams-pa #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba #  rnams kyang rang-gi #  ngo bo la mi-gnas-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o /
yAdRSaH vA adRzwa satyEH DarmANAm svaBAvaH lakzaNam aBilApa prapaQca vAsanAmuKena gRhyate tena bAla grAha anurUpeNa svaBAvena virahita tvAt niH svaBAvAH
# bden-pa #  ma-mthong-ba #  rnams kyis chos-rnams #  kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  de mtshan-nyid #  mngon-par-brjod-pa #  spros-pa # 'i bag-chags #  kyi sgo nas ji-ltar #  bzung-ba #  bzhin-du #  byis-pa # s bzung-ba #  dang mthun-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de dang bral-ba # 'i phyir ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o /
api Kalu sarva DarmAH ucyante trayaH svaBAvAH / tatra parikalpitasya sva lakzaNam eva na asti atas sva lakzaNa niHsvaBAva tayA niHsvaBAvaH
# yang chos-thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum ste / / de-la #  kun brtags kyi ngo-bo-nyid #  ni rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  kyis med-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  rang-gi-mtshan-nyid #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o /
paratantrasya svayam utpattiH na asti pratyaya apekzaNAt atas na asya svena BAvena BAvaH iti utpattiniH svaBAvatayA niHsvaBAvaH
# gzhan gyi dbang ni rkyen-la-ltos-pa # 'i phyir bdag-nyid-kyis #  'byung-ba-med-pa #  ste / / de'i-phyir #  rang-gis #  'byung-ba-med-pa # s na skye-ba #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o /
parinizpannaH viSudDi AlaMbana tvAt paratantra parikalpita lakzaNa aBAva svaBAva tvAt ca paramArTaH ca eza niHsvaBAvatA praBAvitaH ca iti paramArTa niHsvaBAvatayA niHsvaBAvaH / iti evam ca kRtvA niHsvaBAvAH sarva DarmAH drazwavyAH na tu sarvaTA lakzaNa aBAvam aDikRtya iti
# yongs-su-grub-pa #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i dmigs-pa #  yin pa dang gzhan gyi dbang dang kun rtags pa'i mtshan-nyid-med-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir te / / don-dam-pa #  yin la ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # s rab tu phe ba ste / / don-dam-pa #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # s ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o / / de-ltar #  chos-thams-cad #  la ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # r lta'i /
api Kalu mahA yAne taTAgatasya sarve aBiprAyAH saMkzepeNa catvAraH Bavanti
# rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  mtshan-nyid-med-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ni ma yin no / / yang theg-pa-chen-po #  la de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i dgongs-pa #  thams-cad #  ni mdor-na #  bzhir 'gyur te / / 'di-lta-ste #  /
tat yaTA samatA aBiprAyaH yat Aha aham eva tasmin samaye vipaSyI samyaksaMbudDaH aBUvam iti avaSizwa DarmakAya tvAt
# mnyam-pa-nyid #  la dgongs-pa #  ni nga nyid de'i tshe yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  rnam-pa # r gzigs su gyur to zhes gang gsungs-pa #  ste / / chos kyi sku la bye-brag-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kAla antara aBiprAyoyat Aha ye suKAvatyAm lokaDAtO praNiDAnam karizyanti te tatra upa patsyante iti vimala candra praBavasya ca nAmaDeya grahaNa mAtreNa niyataH Bavati anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO= iti kAla antareNa iti aBiprAyaH
# dus gzhan la dgongs-pa #  ni gang dag bde-ba #  can gyi 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  su smon-lam-'debs-pa #  ste / / de-dag #  der skye-bar-'gyur #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  dri med zla 'od kyi mtshan bzung-ba #  tsam gyis nges-par #  bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  'thob bo zhes gang gsungs-pa #  ste /
arTa antara aBiprAyaH yat Aha niHsvaBAvAH sarva DarmAH anutpannAH iti evamAdi ayaTArutArTatvAt
# dus-gzhan-na # 'o zhes dgongs-pa # 'o / / don gzhan la dgongs-pa #  ni chos-thams-cad #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa # 'o / / ma-skyes-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gang gsungs-pa #  ste /
pudgala ASaya aBiprAyaH yat tat eva kuSala mUlam kasyacid praSaMsanti kasyacid vigarha te alpa mAtra saMtuzwasya
# sgra ji bzhin ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang-zag #  gi bsam-pa #  la dgongs-pa #  ni gang-la #  la nas bsngags-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba de nyid cung-zad #  tsam gyis chog-par-'dzin-pa #  la-la-la #  smod do /
taTA rAga caritasya budDakzetra viBUti darSayati mAna caritasya kezAMcid eva budDAnAm aDikAm saMpattim varNayanti
# de-bzhin-du #  'dod-chags #  pa spyod-pa #  la ni sangs-rgyas-kyi-zhing #  gi rnam-pa # r 'byor-ba #  bsngags so / / nga-rgyal #  la spyod-pa #  ni sangs-rgyas #  kha-cig #  gis phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  lhag-pa # r bsngags so /
