punar sarve aBisaMBayaH aBisamasya catvAraH Bavantya vatAraNa aBisaMDya AdayaH
# yang ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  thams-cad #  ni mdor-na #  gzhug-pa #  la ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhir 'gyur ro /
tatra avatAraNa aBisaMDiH SrAvakezu drazwavyaH SAsanAH vatAraNa arTam anutrAsAya rUpa Adi astitva deSanAt
# de-la #  gzhug-pa #  la ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  rnams la blta-bar-bya #  ste / / bstan-pa #  la gzhug-pa # 'i don-du #  mi skag par bya-ba # 'i phyir gzugs la-sogs-pa #  yod-pa #  skad du bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
lakzaNa aBisaMDiH trizu parikalpita Adi svaBAvezu drazwavyaH niHsvaBAva anutpanna Adi sarva Darma deSanAt
# mtshan-nyid #  la ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  ni kun brtags la-sogs-pa #  ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum la blta ste / / chos-thams-cad #  ngo-bo-nyid-med-pa #  dang ma-skyes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratipakza aBisaMDiH dozANAm vinaye drazwavyaH yaTA azwa AvaraNa pratipakzata agra yAna saMBAzA
# gnyen-po #  la ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  ni nyes-pa #  rnams 'dul-ba # r blta ste / / dper-na #  sgrib-pa #  brgyad kyi gnyen-po # r theg-pa #  mchog yang-dag-par-bshad-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
azwa AvaraNAni budDa DarmO= ajQyate iti vistaraH / tad udAharaNAni ca yaTAyogam catur aBiprAryA nirdeSAni drazwavyAni
# sgrib-pa #  brgyad ni / / sangs-rgyas #  dang ni chos la brnyas-pa #  dang / / zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  ste / / de'i dper brjod-pa #  ni ci-rigs-su #  dgongs-pa #  gzhi bstan-pa # r blta'o /
pariNAmana aBisaMDiH aBiDAna gAmBIrye drazwavyaH yat Aha / asAre sAra matayaH viparyAse ca susTitAH / kleSena ca su saMklizwAH laBante boDim uttamAm / iti / atra ayam aBisaMDiH avikzepe yezAm sAra budDiH praDAna budDiH vikzepaH hi visAraH cetasaH viparyAse ca susTitAH iti nitya suKa Suci Atma viparyayeNa anitya Adike viparyAse ca susTitAH aparihANitaH kleSena ca su saMklizwAH iti dIrGa duzkara vyAyAma SrameNa atyarTa pariklizwAH
# bsgyur-ba #  la ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  ni brjod-pa #  zab-pa #  la blta-bar-bya #  ste / / ji-skad-du #  snyong po med la snying-po # r shes / / phyin-ci-log #  la shin-tu #  gnas / / nyon mongs kun nas rab nyin-mo # ngs / / byang-chub-dam-pa #  thob-pa # r 'gyur / / zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  ldem-po # r dgongs-pa #  ni 'di yin te / / rnam-pa # r mi g-yeng ba la gang dag snying-po # r blo 'byung-ba #  dang mchog-tu #  blo 'byung-ba # 'o / / rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba ni sems rnam-pa # r 'phro ba'o / / phyin-ci-log #  la shin-tu #  gnas zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / rtag-pa #  dang; bde-ba #  dang gtsang ba dang bdag las bzlog-pa #  ste / / mi-rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i phyin-ci-log #  la shin-tu-gnas-pa #  yongs-su-mi-nyams-pa # 'i phyir ro / / nyon mongs kun nas rab nyon mongs / / zhes-bya-ba #  ni yun-ring-por #  dka'-ba #  byed-pa # 'i rtsol bas shin-tu #  yongs su nyon-mongs-pa # r gyur-pa # 'o /
vEpulye Darma samADi kuSala boDisattva nirdeSaH SamaTa anuSaMsam vipaSyana anuSaMsam tad uBaya anuSaMsam ca aDikRtya veditavyaH
# shin-tu #  rgyas-pa #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  chos la ting-nge-'dzin #  du mkhas-pa # r bstan-pa #  ni zhi-gnas #  kyi phan yon dang lhag-mthong #  gi phan yon dang de-gnyi-ga # 'i phan yon gyi dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra SamaTa anuSaMsaH dviviDaH
# de-la #  zhi-gnas #  kyi phan yon ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te /
kzaNe kzaNe prakarza gAminyA prasrabDyA nirantaram ASraya sParaNAt pratikzaNam sarva dOzWulya ASraya drAvaNam aviSezeNa sarva deSanA Darme kara satA aDimokza samADAnAt viviDa skanDa Adi arTa AkAra saMjQA vigatAyAH sUtra Adi Darma ArAma rateH pratilamBaH ca / vipaSyana anuSaMsaH api dviviDaH
# skad-cig #  skad-cig #  la khyad-par-du-'gro-ba # 'i shin-tu-sbyangs-pa # s rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  lus la khyab-pa # 'i phyir skad-cig-re-re-la #  gnas-ngan-len #  gyi gnas-thams-cad #  'jig-par-byed-pa #  dang bstan-pa # 'i chos-thams-cad #  khyad-par-med-pa # s so gcig par mos te / / mnyam-par-'jog-pa # s phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i don gyi rnam-pa-tha-dad-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  dang bral-ba # s mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos kyi dga'-ba #  las dga'-ba #  thob-pa # 'o / / lhag-mthong #  gi phan yon yang rnam-pa-gnyis #  te /
yaTA pravicitta Darma nirantara asaMpramozAt pratismRti mAtra muKena aparicCinna AkAraH apramANaH sUtra Adi Darmezu prajQA avaBAsaH ASraya parivRtti pUrvarUpa BUtAnAm ca avikalpitAnAm anaBisaMskRtAnAm nimittAnAm samudAcAraH ca / tad uBaya anuSaMsaH Darma kAyasya jQeya AvaraNa prahANa ASraya parivRtti saMgRhItasya paripUraye daSamyAm BUmO parinizpattaye vA tATAgatyAm BUmO uttarAt uttaratara nizyanda vAsanA ADAna yogena hetu parigrahaH / tat etat paQcaviDAyAH BAvanAyAH Palam paQcaviDam nirvartate iti saMdarSitam / paQcaviDA BAvanA katamA / prasrabDi nimitta BAvanA saMBinna BAvanA nimitta BAvanena ABoga BAvanA parinirvRti nimitta BAvanA ca / kena kAraNena tulye Darma kAya nizyanda tve vEpulya DarmaH DUpa mAlya AdiBiH pUjyaH na taTA SrAvaka yAna DarmaH / vEpulya Darmasya sarva sattva hita suKa aDizWAna tAm upAdAya mahArTa tayA niruttarA prameya puNya prasava Ayatana tvAt
# ji-ltar #  rab tu rnam-pa # r phyir ba'i chos rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  mi-brjed-pa # s so-so # r dran-pa #  tsam gyi sgo nas mdo la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  la shes-rab-kyi-snang-ba # 'i rnam-pa #  yongs su ma chad-pa #  tshad-med-pa #  dang gnas-'gyur-ba # 'i snga rtags su gyur-pa #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  mngan-pa # r 'dus-ma-byas #  pa'i mtshan-ma #  rnams kun du 'byung-ba # 'o / / de-gnyi-ga # 'i phan yon ni chos kyi sku shes-bya # 'i sgrub-pa #  spangs-pa #  gnas-gyur-pa # s bsdus-pa # s sa bcu pa la yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba #  dang; de-bzhin-gshegs-pa'i-sa #  la yongs su bsgrub-pa # 'i phyir gong-ma #  bas kyang ches gong-ma # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bag-chags #  bskyed-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  rgyu yongs-su-'dzin-pa # r byed-pa # 'o / / chos kyi sku'i rgyu-mthun-pa # r 'dra-ba #  la ci'i-phyir #  shin-tu #  rgyas-pa # 'i chos la bdug-pa #  dang phye-ma #  la-sogs-pa # s mchod-pa # r 'os kyi / / nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'i chos la ni de lta ma yin zhe na / / shin-tu #  rgyas-pa # 'i chos ni sems-can-thams-cad #  la phan-pa-dang-bde-ba # 'i gzhir-gyur-pa # 'i phyir te /
prAptiviniScayaH nAma caturTaH samuccayaH / prApti viniScayaH aDigantR pudgala vyavasTAnataH aDigama vyavasTAnataH ca drazwavyaH
# don-che-ba # s bsod nams bla na med cing dpag-tu-med-pa #  skyed-pa # 'i gnas-su-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / thob-pa #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni thob-par-byed-pa # 'i gang-zag #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  dang mngon-par-rtogs-pa # r rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r lta-ba # 'o /
asati api pudgala dravye pudgala vyavasTAnam caturBiH kAraNEH
# gang-zag #  rdzas su med kyang rnam-pa-bzhi # s gang-zag #  rnam-pa # r gzhag ste /
tat yaTA suKa saMvyavahAra arTam rUpa AdInAm bahUnAm bahuDA aBinna lakzaNa saMjQAnAm ekayA sAmudAyikyA sattva prajQapti AkRcCreNa ehi yAhi iti evamAdi saMvyavaharaNAt
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / sla-ba # r tha-snyad #  gdags-pa # 'i phyir ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa # r mang-po #  mtshan-nyid #  dang ming tha-dad-pa #  mang-po #  rnams gcig-tu #  bsdus te / / sems-can #  zhes brtags-nas #  so zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  tshegs-med-pa #  nyid-du #  tha-snyad-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
loka anuvRtti arTam na hi loke Darma mAtra saMjQABiH sarvaH saMvyavahAraH nirUXaH kiMtarhi prAyeNa sattva saMjQayA
# 'jig-rten-pa #  dang mthun-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ni 'jig-rten #  na chos tsam gyi ming rnams kyi tha-snyad #  thams-cad #  ma grags kyi phal-cher #  sems-can #  gyi ming gis so /
tasmAt lokena saha saMvyavaharadBiH AryEH avaSyam saH anuvartitavyaH iti
# de-bas-na #  'phags-pa #  rnams kyis kyang gdon-mi-za-bar #  'jig-rten-dang-mthun-pa # 'i tha-snyad #  rnams kyis de dang mthun-par #  bya'o /
anutrAsa arTam pratItyasamutpAda Darma tAyAma kovidAH sahasA Aditas sarvaTA sattva aBAvam SrutvA uttrasyeyuH iti
# ji skrag-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir ni rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i chos-nyid #  la mi-mkhas-pa #  glo-bur-du #  thog-mar #  rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  sems-can-med-pa #  thos-pa #  na skrag-par-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /
AtmanaH parezAm ca dozavat tva guNavat tva udBAvana arTam ca itaraTAH hi sattva prajQaptim antareNa saMkleSa vyavadAna lakzaNa mAtra deSanAyAm satyAm amuzmin saMtAne amI dozAH prahINAH amI vA guNAH utpannAH iti na Sakyate vijQAtum iti
# bdag-dang-gzhan #  dag gi nyes-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  dang yon-tan-dang-ldan-pa #  brjod-pa # 'i phyir na gzhan-du #  sems-can #  du btags-pa #  med-pa # r kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  tsam bstan na che-ge-mo-zhig #  gi sems-kyi-rgyud #  la nyes-pa #  'di rnams spangs so / / yon-tan #  'di rnams skyes so zhes shes-pa # r mi-nus-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pudgala vyavasTAnam punar carita Adi praBedena saptaviDam
# gang-zag #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni spyod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis rnam-pa #  bdun te / / de-la #  'dod-chags #  la spyod-pa #  ni /
tatra rAga Adi caritaH tIvra Ayata rAgaH hIne api raQjanIye vastuni aDimAtra rAga utpAdAt utpannasya ca ciram anubanDAt / iti evam yAvat vitarka caritaH yaTAsvam vastuni yojayitavyaH / sama BAga caritaH prakRti sTaH saMkleSaH Otkawa yamAndya vivarjita samavasTe kleSaH iti arTaH yaTAvaH tu anurUpam kleSa samudAcArAt
# 'dod-chags #  kyi shas che zhing rgyun-ring-ba #  ste / / chags-par-'gyur-ba # 'i dngos-po #  ngan-pa #  la yang 'dod-chags #  cher 'byung-ba #  dang byung nas kyang yun-ring-du #  rjes su 'brel-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-par-rtog-pa #  la spyod-pa # 'i bar-du #  yang de-bzhin #  te / / rang-gi #  dngos-po #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / cha-mnyam-pa #  la spyod-pa #  ni / / nyon-mongs-pa #  rang-bzhin #  du gnas-pa #  ste / / nyon-mongs-pa #  shas-che-ba #  dang shas-chung-ba #  rnam-pa # r spangs-nas #  mnyam-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  ste / / dngos-po #  ji-lta-ba #  dang mthun-par #  nyon-mongs-pa #  kun du 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / nyon-mongs-pa #  chung du ni nyon-mongs-pa #  shin-tu #  srab-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  du gnas-pa #  ste; nyon-mongs-pa #  rang-bzhin #  du gnas-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa #  dag nas /
manda rajaskaH prakRti sTaH tanutara kleSaH prakRti sTeByaH ukta lakzaNeByaH tanutarAH kleSAH asya saH ayam prakRti sTaH utkawe api vastuni pUrva pratipakza aByAsa vaSena prakRtyAH mRdu kleSa samudAcArAt iti
# nyon-mongs-pa #  ches srab-pa #  yod-pa #  de ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  du gnas-pa # s srab-pa #  ste / / sngon gnyen-po #  chen-po #  goms-par-bya-ba # 'i dbang gis dngos-po #  shas-che-ba #  la yang rang-bzhin-gyis #  nyon-mongs-pa #  chung dus kun du 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
SrAvaka yAnikaH gotra indriya praNiDAna ASaya alaMkbana pratipatti Pala praBedEH nidizwaH veditavyaH
# nyan-thos #  rnams kyi theg-pa #  ni rigs dang dbang-po #  dang smon-lam #  dang bsam-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang sgrub-pa #  dang 'bras-bu # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i dbang gis bstan-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
prakRtyAH mRdu indriya tvam punar asya pratyekabudDa boDisattva indriyA pekzayA itaraTA hi Darma anusArya AdayaH tIkzNa indriyAH iti etat viruDyeta
# 'di'i dbang-po-rtul-po #  nyid ni rang-sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i dbang-po #  las ltos-pa # 'o / / gzhan-du #  ni chos kyi rjes-su-'brang-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dbang-po-rnon-po #  yin no zhes-bya-ba #  dang 'gal-ba # r 'gyur ro /
tatra anutpAdita pUrva nirveDa BAgIyaH aprApta pUrva PalaH ca Ka Xga vizANa kalpaH Bavati ekaH vihArI tad anyaH pratyeka jinaH varga cArI drazwavyaH
# de-la #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  sngon ma-bskyed-pa #  dang sngon 'bras-bu #  ma-thob-pa #  ni bse ru lta-bu # r gyur te gcig-pur-gnas-pa # 'o / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i rang rgyal-ba #  ni tshogs dang spyod-pa # 'o /
vyAkaraNam ca pratyalaBataH iti azwAByAm BUmO= anutpattikezu Darmezu kzAntim pratilaBate iti arTaH
# lung bstan-pa #  yang thob ces bya-ba #  ni sa brgyad pa la mi-skye-ba'i-chos #  la bzod-pa #  thob ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
asaMBRta saMBAra AdayaH mokza BAgIyAnAm ca mRdu maDya aDi mAtratayA nirveDa BAgIya utpAdanam satya aBisamayam ca pratiniyata aniyata tad janma kAlika tvAt yaTAkramam veditavyAH
# tshogs ma bsags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ni thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams dang nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  chung-ngu #  dang 'bring dang chen-po #  rnams kyi nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i phyogs dang bden-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  skyed-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  nges-pa #  dang ma-nges-pa #  dang tshe-rabs #  de nyid kyi dus dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra satya aDipateye Darme aDimukti prasAda lakzaNAni mokza BAgIyAni tatra eva Darma niDyAna kzAnti lakzaNAni nirveDa BAgIyAni SradDA praDAna tvAt prajQA praDAna tvAt ca yaTAkramam
# 'di-la #  bden-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'i chos la mos-pa #  dang dad-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams te / / de-nyid-la #  chos la nges-par-sems-pa # 'i bzod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyis nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  rnams ni dad-pa #  mchog yin pa dang shes-rab #  mchog yin pa'i phyir te / / go-rims #  bzhin no /
lOkikA graDarma prakRtyA eva kzaNikaH iti apravanDikaH iti arTaH
# 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  skad-cig-pa #  ste zhes-bya-ba #  ni rgyun ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
no tu vAsanA parihANitaH iti nirvANa aDikArikasya kuSala mUlasya utpAdita pUrvasya apunarutpAdya tvAt
# bag-chags #  yongs-su-nyams-pa # s yongs-su-nyams-pa #  ni ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  ni mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # r byed-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba sngar bskyed-pa # 'ang skyed mi-dgos-pa # 'i phyir ro /
mRdu mokza BAgI yam aDikRtya uktam BagavatA
# thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  chung-ngu # 'i dbang du mdzad nas bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis bka'-stsal-pa #  /
samyak dRzwiH aDimAtram lOkikI yasya vidyate
# 'jig-rten-pa #  yi yang dag lta / / chen-po #  su la yod gyur-pa #  /
api jAti sahasrANi na asO gacCati durgatim / iti
# de ni tshe-rabs #  stong du yang / / ngan-'gror-'gro-ba # r mi 'gyur ro /
api Kalu caturviDam mokza BAgIyam ADikArikam ADi mokzikam ADi kAmikam ABigAmikam ca
# zhe'o / / yang thar-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  bzhi ste / / skabs su gtogs-pa #  dang mos-pa #  las gyur-pa #  dang lhag-pa # r 'dod-pa #  las gyur-pa #  dang; thob-pa #  las gyur-pa # 'o /
kuSala Darma= Candam upAdAya yAvat mokza arTam kriyate tadA ADikArikam / tad pratisaMyukta deSana aDimokza sahagatam yat tat ADimokzikam
# dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la 'dun-pa #  nas nye-bar #  bzung-ste #  / / thar-pa # 'i cha mthun du bya-ba #  ji-snyed-pa #  de ni skabs su gtogs-pa # 'o / / de dang rab tu ldan-pa # 'i bstan-pa #  la mos-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni mos-pa #  las gyur-pa # 'o /
prIti prasAda sahagata mokza alaMkbana manaskAra bahulam yat tat ADikAmikam / nirveDa BAyIya utpAda niyatam tatra eva janmani yat tadA aBigAmikam / nirveDam AgIyam zaXviDam Anulomikam prAkarzikam prAtiveDikam anya pAriNAmikam eka janmikam eka Asanikam ca
# dga'-ba #  dang dad-pa-dang-ldan-pa #  thar-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'i yid-la-byed-pa #  mang-ba #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni lhag-pa # r 'dod-pa #  las gyur-pa # 'o / / tshe-'di-nyid-la #  nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  skyed-pa # r nges-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de ni thob-pa #  las gyur-pa # 'o / / nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  ni rnam-pa-drug #  ste / / rjes-su-mthun-pa #  dang khyad-par #  ba dang rab-tu-rtogs-pa #  dang gzhan-du #  yongs su sgyur ba dang skye-ba-gcig #  pa dang stan-gcig-pa # 'o /
tatra yat satya Alambana kAram Aditas mRdukam kuSala mUlam utpadyate tadA anulomikam
# de-la #  gang bden-pa-la-dmigs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba dang-po #  nyid-du #  chung du 'byung-ba #  de ni rjes-su-mthun-pa #  pa'o /
yat maDyam tat prAkarzikam tatas tat prakRzwatara tvAt / yat aDimAtram satya prativeDAya tatra eva janmani saMvartate tad prAtiveDikam
# gang 'bring du gyur-pa #  de ni khyad-par #  ba ste / / de-bas #  chos mchog-tu-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gang tshe-'di-nyid-la #  bden-pa #  rtogs-pa #  shas chen-por-gyur-pa #  de ni rab-tu-rtogs-pa #  pa'o /
tad punar yat aniyata gotrANAm boDi viSezAya pariNAmyate tat ca pratyekabudDAnAm anAcAryaka aBisaMboDAya janma antare pariNamati tad anya pAriNAmikam / yat tatra eva janmani satya prativeDAya saMvartate tadA eka janmikam
# de-yang #  gang ma-nges-pa # 'i rigs can rnams byang-chub #  khyad-par #  du gyur-pa # r yongs-su-bsgyur-ba #  dang gang yang rang-sangs-rgyas #  rnams tshe-rabs-gzhan #  la slob-dpon-med-par #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa # r yongs-su-bsgyur-ba #  de ni gzhan-du #  yongs su bsgyur-pa # 'o / / gang-gi-tshe #  de-nyid-la #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni tshe gcig pa'o /
yat tatra eva Asane tat ekAsanikam iti
# gang stan de-nyid-la #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  de ni stan-gcig-pa # 'o /
kAya sAkzI vimokza lABa nAgAmI azwO vimokzAn kAyena sAkzAtkRtvA upasaMpadya viharaNAt
# lus-kyis #  mngon-du-byed-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyir-mi-'ong-ba #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  brgyad thob-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-thar-pa #  brgyad po de-dag #  lus-kyis #  mngon-sum-du-byas-nas #  rdzogs-pa # r byas te gnas-pa # 'i phyir ro /
azwO vimokzAH rUpI rUpANi paSyati iti evamAdayaH paScAt nirdekzyante
# rnam-par-thar-pa #  brgyad ni gzugs-can #  gzugs rnams la lta-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / 'og nas 'chad do /
prajQA vimuktaH prajQA vipakza kleSa AvaraNa mAtra aSeza prahANAt
# shes-rab #  kyis rnam-par-grol-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni shes-rab #  kyis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  nyon-mongs-pa'i-sgrib-pa #  tsam ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
uBayatas BAga vimuktaH sarva kleSa samApatti AvaraNAByAm yaH vimuktaH
# gnyi-ga # 'i cha las rnam-par-grol-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i sgrib-pa #  thams-cad-la # s gang rnam-par-grol-ba # 'o /
srotApatti Pala pratipannakaH eka Asanikam nirveDa BAgIyam AraBya yAvat Adyam Palam na prApnoti
# rgyun-du-zhugs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  la 'jug-pa #  ni nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  stan-gcig-pa #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / dang-po # 'i 'bras-bu #  ma thob kyi bar-du # 'o /
kaH punar darSana mArga avasAne Adyam Palam prApnoti
# mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi tha-ma #  la dang-po # 'i 'bras-bu #  thob-pa #  gang zhe na /
yaH pradeSa vErAgyeNa api kAmeByaH avIta rAgaH samyaktvam niyAmam avakrAmati
# gang phyogs las 'dod-chags #  dang bral yang 'dod-pa #  dag las 'dod-chags #  dang ma bral zhing yang-dag-pa-nyid #  du nges-par #  'gyur-ba #  la 'jug-pa # 'o /
yaH tu pUrvam lOkikena mArgeNa kAma avacarAn BAvanA prahAtavyAn zaz prakArAn prahAya yatra yaH vIta rAgaH Bavan paScAt samyaktvam niyAmam avakrAmati sa zoXaSe citta kzaNe sakRdAgAmi eva Bavati
# gang sdar 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  gyis bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # 'i 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  rnam-pa-drug #  spangs-nas #  phal-cher #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # r gyur te / / phyis yang-dag-pa-nyid #  la nges-par #  'jug-pa #  de ni sems-kyi-skad-cig #  bcu drug-pa #  la-la # n cig phyir 'ong-ba #  nyid-du #  'gyur-ba # 'o /
nava api prakArAn prahAya kAma vIta rAgaH Bavan yaH niyAmam avakrAmati saH anAgAmI eva Bavati
# gang rnam-pa #  dgu char spangs-nas #  'dod-pa #  las 'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba # r 'gyur te / / nges-par-gyur-pa #  la 'jug-pa #  de ni phyir-mi-'ong-ba #  nyid-du #  'gyur-ba # 'o /
sarva darSana prahAtaya prahANe api trayANAm eva saMyojanAnAm prahANAt srotApanna vacanam ezAm mokza prApti bibanDana tvena prADAnyAt
# mthong-ba # s spang-pa # r bya-ba #  thams-cad #  spangs kyang kun du sbyor-ba #  gsum spangs-nas #  rgyun-du-zhugs-pa #  zhes brjod-pa #  ni / / 'di dag thar-pa #  thob-pa # 'i gegs su gyur-pa # s gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te /
taTA hi satkAya dRzwayA paQca upAdAna skanDa anAtmataH AtmIyataH ca aBiniveSya Alaya ArAmatayA duHKAt na uccalati
# 'di-ltar #  'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # s nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po dag la bdag dang bdag-gi # r mngon-pa # r zhen nas bdag la dga'-ba #  sdug-bsngal #  las mi 'phags so /
uccalitaH api kaTaMcid mokzam prati SIla vrata parAmarSena vicikitsayA ca asat mArga aBiniveSAt sat mArga saMSayanAt ca miTyA niryAti samyaktvam aniryAti
# ji snyed 'phags kyang thar-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang the-tshom #  gyi lam ngan-pa #  la mngon bar zhen-pa #  dang lam bzang-po #  la the-tshom-za-ba # 'i phyir / / log-pa # s nges-par #  'byung gi yang-dag-par #  nges-par #  mi 'byung ngo / / yang 'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba # s zhes-bya-ba #  la log-pa # r rtogs-pa #  ste /
punar satkAya dRzwayA jQeye vipratipadyate duHKa mAtre Atma AtmIya lakzaNa samAropaNAt / SIla vrata parAmarSena dRzwO tayA SudDi pratyayanAt / vicikitsayA pratipakze ratnatraya aniScayanAt iti
# sdug-bsngal #  tsam la bdag dang bdag-gi #  ba'i mtshan-nyid #  du sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa # s lta-ba #  la log-pa # r rtogs te / / des dag-pa # r yid-ches-pa # 'i phyir ro / / the-tshom #  gyis ni gnyen-po #  la log-pa # r rtogs te / / dkon-mchog-gsum #  la nges-par-mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sakRdAgAmi Pala pratipannakaH darSana mArgAt UrDvam kAmAvacarasya yAvat maDya maDyasya kleSa prakArasya prahANa mArge yaH pudgalaH
# lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  la 'jug-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi gong-du #  'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  'bring-po # 'i 'bring gi bar-du #  spong-ba # 'i lam la gnas-pa # 'i gang-zag #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
sakRdAgAmI maDya mRdoH kleSa prakArasya prahANa mArga parisamAptO yaH pudgalaH
# lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  'bring-po # 'i chung du spong-ba # 'i lam yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'i gang-zag #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
anAgAmi Pala pratipannakaH sakRdAgAmi PalAt UrDvam kAmAvacarANAm mRdu aDimAtra mRdu maDyayoH kleSa prakArayoH prahANa mArge yaH pudgalaH
# phyir-mi-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  la 'jug-pa #  ni / / lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i gong-du #  'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  chung du'i chen-po #  dang chung du'i 'bring-po #  spangs-pa # 'i lam la gnas-pa # 'i gang-zag #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
anAgAmI navamasya mRdu mRdoH kleSa prakArasya prahANAya mArga parisamAptO yaH pudgalaH
# phyir-mi-'ong-ba #  ni dgu pa nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  chung-ngu # 'i chung du spong-ba # 'i lam yongs-su-rdzogs-pa #  la gnas-pa # 'i gang-zag #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
sarva kAma avacara BAvanA prahAta vyaprahANe api paQcAnAm avaraBAgIyAnAm saMyojanAnAm prahANAt anAgAmi vacanam sUtre ezAm gati DAtu avara kAraNa tvena prADAnyAt / gatya varam punar naraka tiryak preta gatayaH
# 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  gang bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  thams-cad #  spangs kyang tha-ma # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  lnga spangs-pa # s phyir-mi-'ong-ba #  zhes mdo las 'byung-ba #  ni 'di dag 'gro-ba #  dang khams tha-ma # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa # s gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te / / 'gro-ba #  tha-ma #  ni sems-can #  dmyal-ba #  dang yid gas dang dud-'gro # 'o /
DAtu avaram kAmaDAtuH
# khams tha-ma #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  so /
tatra satkAya dRzwi SIla vrata parAmarSa vicikitsABiH gatya varAsam atikrAnta tvAt kAraNa tvam
# de-la #  'jig-tshogs-la-lta-ba #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  dang the-tshom #  rnams kyis ni 'gro-ba #  tha-ma #  las mi 'da' bas de'i rgyu nyid do /
kAma= Canda vyApAdAByAm DAtu avara asam atikramAt iti
# 'dod-pa-la-'dun-pa #  dang gnod-sems #  gnyis kyis ni khams tha-ma #  la mi 'da' bas de'i rgyu nyid do /
trEDAtuka sarva kleSa prahANe api paQcAnAm UrDva BAgIyAnAm prahANAt arhat vacanam UrDva upAdAna aparityAga kAraNa tvena prADAnyam
# khams-gsum-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-thams-cad #  spangs kyang gong-ma # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  lnga spangs-pa # s dgra-bcom-pa #  zhes brjod-pa #  ni gong-ma #  nye-bar-len-pa #  dang yongs-su-mi-gtong-ba # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa # s gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te /
tatra rUpa ArUpya rAgAByAm kAmaDAtO UrDva upAdAnam rUpa ArUpya DAtu upapattiH iti arTaH
# de-la #  gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa # 'i 'dod-chags #  gnyis kyis ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  nas gong-ma #  nye-bar #  len te / / gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  su skye zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go; /
OdDatyamAna avidyABiH UrDva aparityAgaH tRzNA mAna vicikitsA uttaraDyAyi tvena satra saMkleSAt iti
# rgod-pa #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang ma-rig-pa #  rnams kyis ni gong-ma #  yongs su mi gtong ste / / sred-pa #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang the-tshom #  gyi shas-che-ba # 'i bsam-gtan-pa #  nyid-du #  der kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kulam kulaH kulaH srotApannaH eva sakRdAgAmi Pala pratipannakaH devezu vA manuzyezu vA niyamena dvO BavO saMsRtya parinirvAti
# rigs nas rigs su skye-ba #  ni rgyun-du-zhugs-pa #  nyid de / / lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  la 'jug-pa #  lha'am mi rnams kyi nang-du #  nges-par #  srid-pa #  gnyis 'khor-ba # r byas-na # s yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # 'o /
ekavIcikaH sakRdAgAmi eva anAgAmi Pala pratipannakaH devezu eva ekam Bavam saMsRtyam parinirvAti
# bar-chad-gcig-pa #  ni lan-cig-phyir-'ong-ba #  nyid de / / phyir-mi-'ong-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  la 'jug-pa #  lha-nyid #  kyi nang-du #  srid-pa #  gcig 'khor-ba #  byas-na # s yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # 'o /
ekA vIciH antaram janma avakASaH asya saH ayam ekavIcikaH
# bar-chad-gcig-pa #  ni bar-skabs #  te skye-ba # 'i skabs-yod-pa #  de'i-phyir #  de ni bar-chad-gcig-pa # 'o /
antarA parinirvAyI yena kleSa AveDena upapatti deSam gatvA pratisandaDyAt tad parikzaye sati yena anuSaya mAtreNa maraNAt UrDva skanDAn aBinirvartayan tad avaSeze sati antarA aBavam aBinirvartya pUrva aByasta mArga saMmuKIBAvAt eva sa viSizwa anuSaya prahANe parinirvAti
# bar-ma-dor #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba #  ni nyon-mongs-pa # 'i shugs gang-gis #  skye-ba # 'i yul du song na nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba #  de zad nas bag-la-nyal #  tsam gang-gis #  shi-ba'i-'og-tu #  phung-po #  mngon-par-'grub-pa #  de'i lhag-ma #  lus pas bar de'i srid-pa #  mngon-pa # r 'grub ste / / sngon-goms-par-byas-pa # 'i lam mngon-du-gyur-pa # s bag-la-nyal #  lhag-ma #  spangs ste / / de nyid-du #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # 'o /
sa punar upapatti deSam pratyanud calita uccalita mAtra dUra ga BAva sTa tayA triviDaH veditavyaH sat puruza gati sUtra anusAreNa
# de-yang #  skye-ba # 'i yul las mi 'phags-pa #  dang 'phags-pa #  tsam dang ring-du-song-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  kyi rnam-pa-gsum #  ste / / skyes-bu-dam-pa # 'i 'gro-ba # 'i mdo'i tshul du rig-par-bya # 'o /
anaBisaMskAreNa yaH mArgam saMmuKIkRtya iti pUrvam su aByasta tvAt svarasa vAhitayA aprayatnena iti arTaH / viparyayAt aBisaMskAra parinirvAyI / UrDvasrotAH dviviDaH akanizWagaH Bava agragaH ca
# mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  med-pa # r lam-mngon-du-byas #  nas zhes-bya-ba #  ni sngon shin-tu #  goms-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir te / / bsgrim mi dgos zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  dang bcas-pa # s yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # 'o / / gong-du-'pho-ba #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / 'og min du 'gro-ba #  dang srid-pa # 'i rtse mor 'gro-ba # 'o /
tatra akanizWa gaH AsvAdana ababahula tayA utpanna utpanna mRdu Adi DyAna prakAra AsvAdanAt brahmakAyikAn AraBya nirantaram sarvezu sTAna antarezu sakRt sakRt upapadyamAnaH yAvat akanizWAn praviSya parinirvAti
# de-la #  'og min du 'gro-ba #  ni ro myang-ba #  mang-ba # s bsam-gtan #  gyi rnam-pa #  chung du la-sogs-pa #  skyes shing skyes-pa # 'i ro-myong-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir tshangs-ris #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  gnas gzhan thams-cad-du #  lan re-re #  skyes nas 'og min gyi bar-du #  zhugs te / / yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # 'o /
Bava agragaH caturTasya DyAnasya avyavakIrNa BAvi tvAt kevalam SudDa AvAsAn parihRtya taTA eva yAvat Bava agram gatvA parinirvAti
# srid-pa # 'i rtse mor 'gro-ba #  ni bsam-gtan-bzhi # n pa la spel mar ma bsgoms-pa # s gnas gtsang ma 'ba'-zhig #  bkol te / / de-bzhin-du #  srid-pa # 'i rtse mo'i bar-du #  song-nas #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # 'o /
vyavakIrNa BAvitasya caturTasya DyAnasya mRdu Adi paQca prakAra BAvita tvAt yaTAkramam paQcasu SudDa AvAsezu upapattiH veditavyA
# spel mar bsgom-pa #  ni bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  chung du la-sogs-pa #  lnga bsgoms-pa # s go-rims-bzhin-du #  gnas gtsang ma lnga po rnams su skye-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
cetayitvA acetayitvA iti svayam AtmAnam upakramamANaH anupakramamANaH vA iti arTaH
# gsod kyang rung mi gsod kyang rung zhes-bya-ba #  ni bdag-gis #  bdag-gi-srog #  gcod-pa # 'am / / mi gcod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
dRzwa Darma suKa vihArAt parihANam eti lOkikeByaH DyAneByaH iti arTaH / indriya uttApanam punar aDimAtra tA nayanam tIkzNa karaNam iti arTaH
# mthong-ba # 'i chos la bde-bar-gnas-pa #  las yongs-su-nyams-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / 'jig-rten-pa'i-bsam-gtan #  rnams las zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / dbang-po #  rnams sbyong-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni chen-po #  thob-par-byed-pa #  ste / / rno-ba # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
atas eva Akopya DarmAH BavyaH ca indriyANi uttApayitum iti na uktam prakRtyA tIkzNa indriya tvAt
# de'i-phyir #  mi-'khrugs-pa # 'i chos-can #  la dbang-po #  rnams yongs-su-sbyong-ba # 'i skal-ba-can #  zhes ma bshad de / / rang-bzhin-gyis #  dbang-po-rno-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kAmAvacara rUpa avacaraH eva boDisattvaH na ArUpya avaraH praBAva prAptasya sattva paripAcanAnA Ayatana tAm upAdAya tatra anupapattitaH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni 'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  dang gzugs-na-spyod-pa #  nyid yin gyi gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  ni ma yin te / / sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r bya-ba # 'i gnas-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir mthu'i khyad-par-thob-pa #  der mi skye'o /
ArUpya DAtu vyavakarzitena DyAnena iti paryudasta ArUpya upapattikena samADinA iti arTaH
# gzugs-med-pa'i-khams #  rnams par spangs-pa # 'i bsam-gtan #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs-med-pa # r skyes bor-ba # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  zhing bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
DyAna suKa viharati aparihINaH eva DyAneByaH DyAna vyAvartana kuSala tvAt / sattva paripAcana arTam kAmaDAtO= api boDisattvaH upapadyate iti veditavyam
# bsam-gtan #  gyi bden-pa # s gnas-pa #  ni yongs-su-ma-nyams-pa #  nyid de / / bsam-gtan #  las rnam-pa # r bzlog-pa #  la mkhas-pa # s sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni 'dod-pa'i-khams #  su yang skye-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sarvAm boDisattva caryAm iti tuzita Bavana vAc samupAdAya yAvat mAra parAjayam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i spyod-pa #  thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni dga'-ldan-gyi-gnas #  na gnas-pa #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / bdud las rgyal-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
budDacaryAm ca darSayati iti aBisaMboDim upAdAya yAvat mahA parinirvANam / aDimukti cArI boDisattva gotre vyavasTitaH Aditas mahA boDi prasTAnam upAdAya yAvat pramuditAm BUmim na praviSati pratyAtmam loka uttara aBigama aBAvAt
# sangs-rgyas #  kyi spyod-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  chen-po # 'i bar-du # 'o / / mos-pas-spyod-pa #  can gyi byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni rigs las gnas-pa #  thog-mar #  smon-lam #  chen-po #  btab-pa #  nas bzung nas rab-tu-dga'-ba # 'i sa la ma zhugs kyi bar-du #  ste /
aDyASaya cAraH daSasu BUmizu loka uttareNa aDigamena viSudDa ASaya tvAt
# so-so # r rang-gis #  'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  thob-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / lhag-pa'i-bsam-pa # s spyod-pa #  can ni sa bcu rnams su 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  thob-pa # s bsam-pa-dag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nimitta cArI zawsu BUmizu anicCataH api nimitta vyavakiraNAt
# mtshan-ma #  la spyod-pa #  can ni sa drug-po #  dag la mi-'dod-bzhin-du #  mtshan-ma #  dang 'dre-ba # 'i phyir ro /
animitta cArI saptamyAm yatnam kurvataH yAvat icCam nimitta asamudAcArAt
# mtshan-ma-med-pa # r spyod-pa #  can ni sa bdun po dag la bsgrims nas ji-srid #  'dod-pa # r mtshan-ma #  kun du mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
anaBisaMskAra cArI SezAsu BUmizu vEpAkika nirvikalpa jQAna pratilamBAt iti
# mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  med-pa # r spyod-pa #  can ni sa lhag-ma #  rnams su rnam-par-smin-pa #  las byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes rnams thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
sakRt nEryANikaH sakRt trEDAtuka avacarAn kleSAn prajahAti
# cig-car #  nges-par-'byin-pa #  ni khams-gsum-na-spyod-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  cig-car #  spong-ba # 'o /
prakAra SaH iti aDimAtra aDimAtrAn kAmarUpA rUpya avarAn BAvanA prahAtavyAn anuSayAn prajahAti evam yAvat mRdu mRdUn darSana prahAtavyAn na tu lOkika mArga vat BUmi prakAra Bedena pRTak pRTak iti arTaH
# rnam-pa # s zhes-bya-ba #  ni bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba # r 'dod-pa #  dang gzugs dang gzugs-med-pa #  na spyod-pa #  chen-po'i-chen-po #  cig-car #  spong-ba #  dang de-bzhin-du #  chung-ngu'i-chung-ngu # 'i bar-du #  ste / / mthong-ba # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  bzhin no / / 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  bzhin-du #  sa'i rnam-pa # 'i bye-brag #  gis so-so-ba #  ni ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tatra idam jQApakam yaToktam aMgulya grasUtre yat kiMcid rUpam yAvat vijQAnam atIta anAgata pratyutpannam iti vistareNa yAvat dUre yat vA antike tat sarvam EkaDyam asaMkzipya ekam BAgam karoti ekam piNXam ekam puQjam ekam rASim karoti ekam kRtvA atas pratisaMSikzate sarvam etat anityam sarvam duHKam iti vistaraH
# 'dir khungs ni sor-mo # 'i rtse mo'i mdo las gzugs gang-ci-yang #  rung ste zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba #  zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  nas / / rgyang-ring-po #  dang thag-nye-ba #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  de thams-cad #  gcig-tu #  bsdus te cha gcig-tu #  byed do / / gcig-tu #  bzlum mo / / gcig-tu #  sdom mo / / phung-po #  gcig-tu #  byed do / / cha gcig-tu #  byas shing phung-po #  gcig gi bar-du #  byas-na # s 'di-ltar #  yang-dag-par #  slob ste / / 'di thams-cad #  ni mi-rtag-pa #  / / 'di thams-cad #  ni sdug-bsngal-ba #  zhes rgya-cher #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
dvayoH eva Adi antayoH PalayoH prajQApyate
# de ni 'bras-bu #  dang-po # 'o / / tha-ma #  gnyis kho-na #  la gdags te /
tayoH trEDAtuka sarva darSana BAvanA prahAta vyASeza prahANa praBAvita tvAt yaTAkramam
# de gnyis ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa # s spong-ba # r bya-ba #  thams-cad #  ma-lus-pa #  spangs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir go-rims #  bzhin no /
maDyayoH tu na prajQApyate tayoH dRzwa satyasya kAma vacarANAm eva BAvanA prahAtavyAnAm sa avaSeza niravaSa prahANa praBAvita tvAt
# bar-ma #  dag la mi gdags te / / de-dag #  ni bden-pa-mthong-ba # 'i bsgom-pa # s spang-bar-bya-ba #  'dod-pa-na-spyod-pa #  nyid la lhag-ma #  dang bcas-pa #  dang lhag-ma #  med-pa # r spangs-pa # s rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sakRt nEryANikam ca aDikRtya viBaFga sUtre srotApanna anantaram arhat vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# cig-car #  nges-par-'byin-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i mdo las rgyun-du-zhugs-pa # 'i 'bras-bu # 'i 'og-tu #  dgra-bcom-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sa dRzwe Darme yadi AjQAm tArAgayati sarvatas niHSezam avIta rAga tvAt praNiDAna vaSena kAmaDAtO= upapadyate kzipra parinirvANa arTam / aBisamaya vyavasTAnam daSaviDam
# thams-cad-la #  ma-lus-par #  'dod-chags-dang-bral-ba #  ma-yin-pa # s de gal-te #  mthong-ba # 'i chos la kun-shes-pa #  thob-pa # r mi byed na myur-du #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'da'-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir smon-lam-gyi-dbang #  gis 'dod-pa'i-khams #  nyid-du #  skye'o / / mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni rnam-pa-bcu #  ste /
tatra Darma aBisamayaH satya aDipatyezu sUtra Adizu Darmezu paratas Gozam aDipatim kRtvA Di mAtrasya aDimukti prasAdasya paScima mokza BAgIya saMgRhItasya pratilamBaH
# de-la #  chos mngon bar rtogs-pa #  ni gzhan gyi sgra'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / bden-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  la thar-pa # 'i cha dang mthun ba tha-ma # s bsdus-pa # 'i mos-pa #  dang dad-pa #  chen-po #  thob-pa #  ste /
taTA hi tad aDimukti prasAda pratilamBAt tAni satyAni Darma aBisamayena aBisamitAni iti ucyante
# 'di-ltar #  de-la #  mos-pa #  dang dad-pa #  thob-pa # s bden-pa #  de-dag #  la chos-mngon-pa # r rtogs-pa # s mngon-par-rtogs-pa # r gyur zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
arTa aBisamayaH tezu eva Darmezu yoni SomanaskAram aDipati kRtvA aDimAtrAyAH satyezu Darma niDyAna kzAnte paScima nirveDa BAgIya saMgRhItAyAH pratilamBaH
# don mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni chos de-dag-nyid #  la gang tshul-bzhin-du #  yid-la-byed-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  bden-pa #  rnams la nges-par-'byed-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa #  tha-ma # s bsdus-pa # 'i chos nges-par-sems-pa # 'i bzod-pa-chen-po #  thob-pa # 'o /
sA punar Darma niDyAna kzAntiH triviDena yoni SomanaskAreNa praBAvitA aDimAtra mRdunA tad janma kAlezu Uzma gatezu aDimAtram aDyena mUrDvasu kzAntizu ca aDimAtra aDimAtreNa lOkikezu agra Darmezu iti / tattva aBisamayaH darSana mArgaH
# chos nges-par-sems-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  de-yang #  tshul-bzhin #  yid-la-byed-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyis rab-tu-phye-ba #  ste / / chen-po'i-chung-ngu # s ni tshe de'i dro-bar-gyur-pa #  rnams su'o / / chen-po'i-'bring-po # s ni rtse mo dang bzod-pa #  rnams su'o / / chen-po'i-chen-po # s ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i chos kyi mchog rnams su'o / / de-kho-na #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  ste /
tatra punar satya vyavasTApanAni aBisamaya antikAni saMvRti jQAnAni pratilamBataH lokottara jQAna ADipatyena tad abIpa UzaNAt na tu sammuKIkaroti zoXaSAnAm darSana mArga citta kzaNAnAm nirantara tvena lOkika citta anavakASAt / pRzWa aBisamayaH darSana mArgAt UrDva sarva BAva nAma argaH lOkikaH lokottaraH vA / ratna aBisamayaH samyaksaMbudDaH vata BagavAn su AKyAtaH asya Darma vinayaH supratipannaH SrAvaka saMGaH iti evam avetya niScitya Arya SrAvakasya budDa Adizu prasAdaH
# der ni bden-pa #  rnam-par-'jog-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'i mtha' las byung-ba #  kun-rdzob-shes-pa #  rnams thob ste / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes kyi dbang gis de'i sa-bon #  gsos pa'i phyir gyi mngon-sum-du-byed-pa #  ni ma yin te / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi sems-kyi-skad-cig #  bcu drug-po #  dag rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # s 'jig-rten-pa # 'i sems kyi skabs-med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rjes la mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  gyi gong-du #  'jig-rten-pa #  yang rung / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  yang rung ste / / bsgom-pa'i-lam #  thams-cad #  do / / dkon-mchog #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni / / kye-ma #  bcom-ldan-'das #  ni yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa # 'i sangs-rgyas #  rnams so / / de'i chos-'dul-ba #  ni legs-par-gsungs-pa # 'o / / nyan-thos-kyi-dge-'dun #  ni legs-par-zhugs-pa # 'o zhes de-ltar #  shes te / / nges nas sangs-rgyas #  la-sogs-pa #  la 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  dad-pa # 'o /
asamuda AcAra aBisamayaH yasya akaraNa saMvarasya ayaMkAnta SIla saMgRhItasya lABAt tad vipakza naraka Adi samudAcAram pratyevam niScayaH pravarttate kzoNAH me narakAH iti evamAdiH saH asamudAcAra aBisamayaH
# kun du mi-'byung-ba # r mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni mi-bya-ba # 'i sdom-pa #  'phags-pa #  dgyes-pa # 'i tshul-khrims #  kyis bsdus-pa #  thob-pa # s de'i mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  byed-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  kun du mi 'byung ste / / bdag-gi-sems #  can dmyal-ba #  zad do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / bdag-gi-sems #  can dmyal-ba #  zad do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste /
nizWA aBisamayaH sarva dOzWulyAnAm pratiprasrabDiH iti evamAdiH yaTA mArga satye nizWA mArgaH nirdizwaH iti evamAdiH yaTA
# de-ltar #  nges-par-'byung-ba #  de ni kun du mi-'byung-ba #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa # 'o / / mthar-thug-pa #  mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni gnas-ngan-len #  thams-cad #  shin-tu-sbyangs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ji-ltar #  lam gyi bden-pa #  las mthar-phyin-pa # 'i lam bstan-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
ete eva sapta aBisamayAH SrAvakANAm para toGozam Agamya pratilamBataH SrAvaka aBisamaye iti ucyate
# mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  bdun po de-dag #  ni nyan-thos #  rnams kyis gzhan gyi sga la brten-nas #  thob-pa # s nyan-thos #  kyi mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
paratas Gozam anAgamya pratilamBataH pratyekabudDaBi samayaH iti
# gzhan gyi sgra la ma brten-pa # r thob-pa # s rang-sangs-rgyas #  kyi mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
boDisattva aBisamaya ezu saptasu aBisamayezu boDisattvasya yA samudAgama kzAntiH SrAvaka pratyekabudDa vinaya upAya kOSalya arTam no tu sAkzAtkriyA sattva apekzayA hIna yAnA niryANAt / api Kalu tat praTamatas boDisattvasya BUmi praveSa aBisamayaH iti ucyate
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  dang rang-sangs-rgyas #  'dul-ba # 'i thabs-la-mkhas-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir / / mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  bdun po de-dag #  la byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i yang-dag-par-'grub-pa # 'i bzod-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste / / sems-can-la-lta-ba # s theg-pa #  chung dus-nges-pa # r mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir mngon-du-byed-pa #  ni ma yin no / / yang-thog #  ma nyid-du #  sa la 'jug-pa #  yang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
etam ca aBisamaya niSritya ucyate SrAvaka aBisamayAt boDisattva aBisamasya kaH prativiSezaH AlaMbana viSezataH vEpulyAlaMbana tvAt
# mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  de-la #  brten-nas #  nyan-thos #  kyi mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  las byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  khyad-par #  ci yod-pa #  brjod-pa # r bya ste / / dmigs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  na shin-tu #  rgyas-pa #  la dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
upastamBa viSezataH paripUrNa mahA kalpAsa Kyeya mahA puNya jQAna saMBAra paripUraNAt
# nye-bar-rtog-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni bskal-pa-chen-po #  grangs-med-pa # r bsod rnams dang ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
prativeDa viSezataH pudgala Darma nErAtmya aDipateya Darma prayoga veDataH loka uttareNa jQAnena tad uBaya prativeDAt aByupagama viSezataH sva Atma sama tayA sarva sattva aByupagamAt
# rab-tu-rtogs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni gang-zag #  dang chos-la-bdag-med-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # 'i chos la sbyor-ba # 'i 'phen-pa # s 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes kyis de-gnyi-ga #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / khas-len-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni bdag dang sems-can-thams-cad #  mnyam-pa-nyid #  du khas-len-pa # 'i phyir ro /
niryANa viSezataH daSaBiH BUmiBiH niryANAt
# nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i khyad-par #  ni sa bcu po dag gis nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
parigraha viSezataH avipratizWita nirvANa parigrahaNAt
# yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
pratizWA parivAra viSezataH budDa kzatra pariSIDanAt vineya jana upagrahaNAt ca
# gnas dang g-yog 'khor gyi khyad-par #  ni sangs-rgyas-kyi-zhing #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba #  dang gdul-ba # 'i skye-bo #  nye-bar #  sdud-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aBijanma viSezataH pitR vaMSa saMDAra kOrasa putra lakzaNa tvAt
# btsun par skye-ba # 'i khyad-par #  ni pha bzhin-du #  rang-gi-rigs #  yang-dag-par-'dzin-pa # 'i bu gtso bo'i mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
janma viSezataH parizad maNXalezu upapannaH
# skye-ba # 'i khyad-par #  ni 'khor-gyi-dkyil-'khor #  rnams su skye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
Pala viSezaH ca punar ASraya parivRtti viSezataH klizwa aklizwa sarva prakAra dOzWulya prahANAt sarva niruttara guNa ASraya tvena ASraya parivartanAt
# 'bras-bu # 'i khyad-par #  de-yang #  gnas-gyur-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni nyon-mongs-pa-can #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  ma-yin-pa # 'i gnas-ngan-len #  gyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  spangs-pa # 'i phyir yon-tan #  bla-na-med-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  gnas nyid-du #  gyur-pa # s gnas-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
guNa samRdDi viSezataH bala vaMSa AradyA veNika budDa Darma Adi aparimita guNa nizpatteH / paQcAkAra viSezataH viSudDi Adi viSezAt / tatra viSudDi viSezaH sa vAsana kleSa prahANAt
# yon-tan #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni stobs dang mi-'jigs-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  ma-'dres-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  dpag-tu-med-pa #  'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-pa-lnga # 'i khyad-par #  ni rnam-par-dag-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyi phyir te / / rnam-pa # r dag dang yongs dag dang / / lus-dang-longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa #  dang / / las kyi sangs-rgyas #  chos-rnams #  kyi / / khyad-par #  yongs-su-brjod-pa #  yin / / de-la #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
pariSudDi viSezaH budDakzetra pariSoDanAt
# yongs-su-dag-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni / / sangs-rgyas-kyi-zhing #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kAya viSezaH Darma kAya parinizpAdanAt
# lus-kyi-khyad-par #  ni chos kyi sku yongs su sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Boga viSezaH sadA boDisattveH saha parzad maNXalezu vicitra Darma saMBogAt
# longs-spyod #  kyi khyad-par #  ni rtag-tu #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams dang lhan-cig #  'khor-gyi-dkyil-'khor #  rnams su chos sna-tshogs #  brjod-pa # r longs-spyod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kam aviSezaH yaTArham nirmANeH samantAt ananta aparyantezu lokaDAtuzu budDa kRtya anuzWAnAt iti / kAyatraya viSezataH svaBAvika sAmBAgikanEH mANikAya parinizpatti lABAt
# las kyi khyad-par #  ni ci-rigs-par #  sprul pa rnams kyis kun du 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  mtha'-yas-mu-med-pa #  rnams su sangs-rgyas-kyi-mdzad-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sku gsum gyi khyad-par #  ni rang-bzhin #  dang longs-spyod #  rdzogs-pa #  dang sprul pa'i sku 'grub-pa #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nirvANa viSezataH nirupaDi Seze nirvANa DAtO sarva sattva hitAya sarva guNa samucCedAt
# mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni phung-po #  lhag-ma #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i dbyings su yang sems-can-thams-cad #  la phan-pa # r yon-tan-thams-cad #  rgyun mi gcod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
miSra upamiSra jQAna Sakti lABa viSezataH su viSudDa Darma DAtu eka rasa tayA tad ASritAsu sarva AkAra vara jQa tAsu pratyekam sarva budDAnAm sAmarTyAt
# 'dres shing nye-bar #  'dres-pa # 'i ye shes kyi nus-pa #  thob-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni chos-kyi-dbyings #  rnam-par-dag-pa # r ro gcig pa nyid dang de-la #  brten-pa #  rnams rnam-pa-thams-cad #  kyi mchog-shes-pa #  nyid rnams la sangs-rgyas-thams-cad #  so-so # r mthu-dang-ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
AvaraNa viSudDi viSezataH sarva kleSa jQeya AvaraNa prahANAt
# sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  rnam-par-dag-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  thams-cad #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
miSra upamiSra karma kriyA viSezataH ekEka sattva vinayanam prati sarva budDa ADipatyAt
# 'dres-pa #  dang nye-bar #  'dres-pa # 'i las-byed-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ni / / sems-can #  re-re #  'dul-ba # 'i phyir-yang #  sangs-rgyas-thams-cad #  kyi dbang gis byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aBisaMboDi nirvANa saMdarSana upAya viSezataH daSasu dikzu yaTAyogam sarva lokaDAtuzu yAvat apara antam punar punar budDa utpAda Adi saMdarSanena sarva vineya jana paripAcana vimucanAt / paQcAkAra paritrANa viSezataH ca veditavyaH upadrava Adi paritrANAt
# mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  ston-pa # 'i thabs kyi khyad-par #  ni phyogs-bcu # 'i 'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  thams-cad-du #  ci-rigs-par #  phyi-ma'i-mtha' # i bar-du #  yang-dang-yang #  sangs-rgyas-'byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ston-pa # s 'dul-ba #  thams-cad #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  dang rnam-par-thar-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yongs-su-skyob-pa #  rnam-pa-lnga # 'i khyad-par #  gyis kyang rig-par-bya # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnod-pa #  la sos pa las yongs-su-skyob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra upadrava paritrANam nagara praveSa AdiBiH ranDa AdInAm cakzuH Adi pratilamBAt
# de-la #  gnod-pa #  las yongs-su-skyob-pa #  ni grong-khyer #  du 'jug-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s long-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s mig la-sogs-pa #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro /
anupAya paritrANam lOkika samyak dRzwi pratilamBena sarva kudRzwi vivecanAt
# thabs-ma-yin-pa #  las yongs-su-skyob-pa #  ni 'jig-rten-pa # 'i yang-dag-pa'i-lta-ba #  thob-pa # s lta-ba-ngan-pa #  thams-cad #  dang bral-bar-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
apAya paritrANam darSana mArga utpAdanena durgati samatikramaNAt sat kAya paritrANam arhat tva sAkzAtkaraNena trEDAtukavi mokzANAt / yAna paritrANam boDisattvAnAm hIna yAna vid CandanAt iti
# ngan-song #  las yongs-su-skyob-pa #  ni mthong-ba'i-lam #  skyed-pa # s ngan-'gro #  las shin-tu #  bzlog-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'jig-tshogs #  las yongs-su-skyob-pa #  ni dgra-bcom-pa-nyid #  mngon-du-byed-pa # s khams-gsum-pa #  las rnam-par-thar-pa # r byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / theg-pa-dman-pa #  las yongs-su-skyob-pa #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams theg-pa-dman-pa #  las 'dun-pa-bzlog-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gnod-pa #  dag ni thams-cad #  dang / / thabs ma yin dang ngan-song #  dang / / thag-pa #  dman las skyob pas na / / de phyir mgon po dam-pa # 'o /
vESaMzika guNAH Arya SrAvakEH BAvanA mArge vA aBinirhriyante aSEkzamArge vA iti atas ezAm pRzWa nizWA aBisamayAByAm saMgrahaH veditavyaH
# yon-tan #  khyad-par-can #  rnams ni 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  rnams kyis bsgom-pa'i-lam #  dang mi-slob-pa # 'i lam la mngon-pa # r sgrub ste / / de'i-phyir #  'di dag rjes la mngon-par-rtogs-pa #  dang thar thug-pa # 'i mngon-par-rtogs-pa # s bsdus-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
te punar mEtrI AdayaH yaTA sUtra antarezu nirdizwAH SrAvaka yAne mahAyAne ca taTA eva veditavyAH / tezAm ca Aya samAsena paQcaBiH AkArEH yaTAyogam lakzaNa nirdeSaH veditavyaH niSrayataH AlaMbanataH AkArataH svaBAvataH sahAyataH ca eva / tatra tAvat mEtryA DyAnam niSrayaH sattvAH AlaMbanam suKena saMprayujyeran= iti AkAraH samADiH prajQA ca svaBAvaH SamaTa vipaSyanA saMgRhIta tvAt sarva guNAnAm citta cEtasikAH sahAyAH iti evam karuNA Adizu yaTAyogam yojayitavyam / upekzayA suKa Adizu sattvezu anunaya Adi aByupekzaNam aho vata saMkleSAt vimucyeran nitya yama AkAraH veditavyaH / sa ca hita ASaya vihAra iti ucyate / azwO vimokzAH / rUpI rUpANi paSyati ayam praTamaH vimokzaH iti vistaraH / tatra kaTam rUpI iti ucyate / sva AtmanyA rUpya samApatti saMniSrayeNa rUpa saMjQAyAH aBiBAvanAt rUpa saMjQA saMniveSanAt vA drazwavyAni rUpa saMjQA saMmuKI karaNAt iti arTaH
# byams-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mdo-sde #  gzhan dag las ji-skad-bstan-pa #  de-dag #  ni nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa #  dang theg-pa-chen-po # r yang de-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-dag #  kyang mdor-bsdus-na #  rnam-pa-lnga # s ci-rigs-su #  mtshan-nyid #  bshad-pa # r blta ste / / gnas dang dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  dang rang-bzhin #  dang grogs kyis so / / de-la #  byams-pa # 'i gnas ni bsam-gtan #  no / / dmigs-pa #  ni sems-can #  no / / rnam-pa #  ni bde-ba-dang-ldan-pa # r gyur cig snyam pa'o / / rang-bzhin #  ni ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  ste / / zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  gis bsdus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yon-tan-thams-cad #  kyi grogs ni sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams so / / snying-rje #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang de-bzhin-du #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / sems-can #  bde-ba # r gyur-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang rjes-su-chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  btang-snyoms #  su byed cing kye-ma #  nyon-mongs-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # r gyur cig snyam pa 'di ni btang-snyoms #  kyi rnam-par-rig-pa # r bya ste / / de-yang #  phan-pa'i-bsam-pa # s gnas-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / rnam-par-thar-pa #  brgyad ni gzugs-can #  gzugs rnams la lta-ba #  'di ni rnam-par-thar-pa #  dang-po # 'o zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o / / de-la #  ji-ltar #  na gzugs-can #  zhes bya zhe na / / gzugs-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la brten-nas #  bdag la gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  rnam-pa # r mi 'jog-pa # 'i phyir ram / / gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  'jog-pa # 'i phyir te / / lta-ba-po #  bdag la gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  mngon du byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / ji-ltar #  na gzugs rnams la lta-ba #  zhes bya zhe na /
kaTam rUpANi paSyati iti ucyate / suvarNa durvarNa AdIni rUpANi aDimucya darSanAt
# kha-dog #  mdzes-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gzugs rnams su mos nas lta-ba # 'i phyir ro /
kaTam vimokzaH iti ucyate
# ji-ltar #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  zhes bya zhe na /
vimucyate anena nirmANA AvaraNAt iti kRtvA
# 'dis sprul-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQA rUpya samApatti saMniSrayeNa drazwari sva Atmani rUpa saMjQA viBAvanAt rUpa saMjQA saMniveSanAt vAdrazwari nAma saMjQA saMmuKIkaraNAt iti arTaH / Sezam pUrvavat
# nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pa zhes-bya-ba #  ni gzugs-med-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  la brten-nas #  gzugs-kyi-'du-shes #  rnam-pa # r 'jig-pa # 'i phyir ram / / gzugs-med-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  'jog-pa # 'i phyir te / / lta-ba-po #  la ming du 'du-shes #  pa mngon du byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / lhag-ma #  ni snga-ma-bzhin #  no /
SuBam vimokzam kAyena sAkzAt kRtvA upasaMpadya viharata SuBa aSuBezu rUpezu anyonya apekzA saMjQAm anyonya anugama saMjQAm ca niSrityAni anyonya eka rasa saMjQA lABAt / taTA hi SuBAni rUpANi apekzya tad anyezu aSuBAni iti Bavati aSuBAni vA apekzya SuBAni iti na anapekzya eka jAtIyAnAm eva darSane SuBa aSuBa tA budDi aBAvAt
# sdug-pa # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  lus-kyis #  mngon-sum-du #  byas te / / rdzogs-pa # r byas-na # s gnas-pa #  ni sdug-pa #  dang mi-sdug-pa # 'i gzugs rnams la phan tshun ltos-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  dang phan tshun rjes-su-'brel-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  la brten-nas #  phan tshun ro gcig pa'i 'du-shes #  thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'di-ltar #  sdug-pa # 'i gzugs rnams la ltos nas de-las-gzhan-pa #  rnams la mi sdug go zhes-bya-ba # r 'gyur la mi-sdug-pa #  la ltos nas sdug ces bya-ba # r 'gyur gyi / / ma ltos-pa # r ni ma yin no / / rigs gcig pa rnams nyid mthong na sdug-pa #  dang mi-sdug-pa #  gnyis kyi blo mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
taTA hi SuBezu api aSuBa tA anugata aSuBezu api SuBa tA SuBa saMmatasya api tvac mAtrasya keSa Adi zawtriSada Suci dravya antara BAvAt iti evam anyonyam sarva rUpANi miSrayitvA SuBa tA eka rasa AkArayA saMjQayA vimucyate
# de-bzhin-du #  sdug-pa #  rnams la yang mi-sdug-pa-nyid #  rjes su 'brel to / / mi-sdug-pa #  rnams la yang sdug-pa-nyid #  rjes su 'brel to / / sdug-pa # r grags-pa #  yang brtags-pa #  tsam du zad de / / skra la-sogs-pa #  mi gtsang ba'i rdzas sum cu rtsa drug gi nang-du #  'dus-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-ltar #  gzugs thams-cad #  phan tshun bsres te sdug-pa-nyid #  du ro gcig pa'i rnam-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  kyis mos-pa # r byed do /
tasya evam rUpa Adi vimokza viBu tva lABinaH SuBa aSuBa nirmANa AvaraNam ca prahIyate tatra ca saMkleSa utpatti AvaraNam / kaH punar nirmANe saMkleSaH / SuBa rUpa nirmANe ABogaH aSuBa rUpa nirmANe prAtikUlyam iti
# de ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  gzugs la-sogs-pa # r mos-pa #  la dbang 'byor-pa #  thob-pa #  de sdug-pa #  dang mi-sdug-pa #  la sprul pa la sgrib-pa #  spong ste / / der ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  'byung-ba # 'i sgrib-pa #  spong ngo / / sprul pa la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  gang yin zhe na / / sdug-pa # 'i gzugs-sprul-pa #  la ni chags-pa # 'o / / mi-sdug-pa # 'i gzugs-sprul-pa #  la ni mi-mthun-pa # 'o /
AkASAnanti Ayatana AdIni catvAri Arya SrAvakasya yAni anASrava anukUlAni SudDAni tAni vimokzaka AKyAm laBante tad AsvAdana vimokzaNAt
# nam-mkha' #  mtha' yas skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa #  bzhi ni 'phags-pa #  nyan-thos #  kyi zag-pa-med-pa # 'i rjes-su-mthun-pa #  dag-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de-dag #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  thob ste / / de'i ro myang-ba #  las rnam-par-thar-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir ro /
ye te SAntAH vimokzAH atikramya rUpANi ArUpyAH tezu asaktiH pariSudDiH
# zhi-ba # 'i rnam-pa # r thar ba ni gzugs rnams las shin-tu #  'das nas gzugs-med-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  dag ste / / de-dag #  la mi-chags-pa #  ni yongs-su-dag-pa # 'o /
tasyAH AvaraNam ArUpya AsvAdanam iti
# de'i sgrib-pa #  ni gzugs-med-pa # 'i ro myang-ba # 'o /
saMjQA vedayita niroDasya niSrayaH na eva saMjQAnA saMjQAyatanam AlaMbanAkAra sahAyAH na santi citta cEtasikAnAm aBAvAt / svaBAvaH tasya citta cEtasikAnAm niroDaH
# 'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba #  'gog-pa # 'i gnas ni 'du-shes #  med 'du-shes #  med min skye-mched #  do / / sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams med-pa # 'i phyir dmigs-pa #  dang rnam-pa #  dang grogs ni med do / / de'i-rang-bzhin #  ni sems dang sems-las-byung-ba'i-chos #  rnams 'gog-pa # 'o / / de-yang #  thar-pa #  dang mthun-par-gnas-pa #  ste /
sa ca mokza anusadRSaH vihAraH lokottareNa mArgeNa parivRtya ASrayasya Arya SrAvakasya punar cita cEtasikAnAm api apravRtti avasTAyAH parama SAnta tvAt klizwa manaH asamAcArAt ca / ete ca azwO vimokzAH vihArAH iti ucyante eBiH AryANAm viharaNAt
# 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyis gnas-gyur-pa # 'i nyan-thos #  rnams kyi sems dang sems-las-byung-ba #  rnams kyang mi-'byung-ba # 'i gnas-skabs #  na / / mchog-tu #  zhi-ba #  dang nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi yid kyang kun du mi-'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / 'phags-pa #  rnams ni 'di dag gis gnas-pa # 'i phyir 'di dag ni 'phags-pa #  gnas-pa # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  brgyad ces bya'o /
tatra api bahu lamAByAm vimokzAByAm viharanti tRtIyena azwamena ca praDAna tvAt
# de-la #  'phags-pa #  dag ni gnas-pa #  gnyis kyis lan-mang-du #  gnas te / / gsum-pa #  dang brgyad pa ste / / mchog yin pa'i phyir ro /
atas eva ca anayoH kAyena sAkzAtkRtya upasaMpadya viharati iti vacanam na anyezu rUpya rUpi vimokza AvaraNa aSeza prahANa Adi aTa Akramam / tayoH saMpUrNa ASraya parivRtti sAkzAt karaNam upAdAya aparaH paryAyaH
# de'i-phyir #  de gnyis lus-kyis #  mngon-sum-du #  byas te / / rdzogs-pa # r byas-na # s gnas so zhes gsungs kyi gzhan rnams la ni ma yin te / / gzugs-can #  dang gzugs-med-pa # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  la sgrib-pa #  ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # 'i phyir go-rims #  bzhin no / / rnam-grangs #  gzhan-du-na #  de gnyis kyi gnas-gyur-pa #  rdzogs-pa #  mngon-du-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
azwO= aBiBvAya tanAni tatra aDyAtmam rUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati parIttAni suvarNa durvarNAni hIna praNI tAni tAni Kalu rUpANi aBiBUya jAnAti aBiBUya paSyati taTA ca saMjQI Bavati / idam praTamam aBiBvAya tanam
# zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  brgyad po de-la #  nang gzugs su 'du-shes #  pa'i phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs chung du kha-dog #  mdzes-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  dang ngan-pa-dang-bzang-po #  rnams la lta zhing gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  / / de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-ba #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  dang-po # 'o /
aDyAtmam rUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati aDimAtrANi suvarNa durvarNAni vistareNa yAvat tayA ca saMjQI Bavati
# nang gzugs su 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs chen-po #  kha-dog #  mdzes-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  dang ngan-pa-dang-bzang-po #  rnams la lta zhing gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zin gyis mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  /
idam dvitIyam aBiBvAya tanam / iti ete dve aBiBvAyatane rUpI rUpANi paSyati iti etasmAt vimokzAt aBinirhriyete
# de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-ba #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  gnyis-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  'di gnyis ni gzugs-can #  gzugs rnams la lta pa'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  de-la # s 'byung ngo /
aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati parIttAni vistareNa yAvat taTA asaMjQI ca Bavati / idam tRtIyam aBiBvAya tanam / aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati aDimAtrANi yaTA taTA asaMjQI ca Bavati / idam caturTam aBiBvAya tanam / iti ete dve aBiBvAyatane aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati iti eta smAt vimokzAt aBinirhriyete / evam kRtvA dvAByAm vimokzAByAm catvAri aBivAyatanAni veditavyAni
# nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs chung-ngu #  kha-dog #  mdzes-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  dang ngan-pa-dang-bzang-po #  rnams la lta zhing gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  / / de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-ba #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  gsum-pa # 'o / / nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs chen-po #  kha-dog #  mdzes-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  dang ngan-pa-dang-bzang-po #  rnams la lta zhing gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  / / de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par gyur-pa #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  bzhi-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  'di gnyis ni nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs rnams la lta zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  de-la # s 'byung ngo / / de-ltar-na #  zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  bzhi ni rnam-par-thar-pa #  gnyis kyis rig-par-bya # 'o / / nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs sngon-po #  / / kha-dog #  sngon-po #  / / sngon-po #  lta-bu # r ston-pa #  / / 'od sngon-po #  'byung-ba #  rnams la lta ste / / dper-na #  zar ma'i me-tog #  gam yul w'a r'a na s'ir byas-pa # 'i ras-phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  sngon-po #  / / kha-dog #  sngon-po #  /
aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati nIlAni nIla varNAni nIla nidarSanAni nIla nirBAsAni / tat yaTA umakApuzpam saMpannam vA vArANasIyakam vastram nIlam nIlavarNa nIlanidarSanam nIlanirBAsam evam eva aDyAtma marUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati nIlAni yAvat nIla nirBAsAni tAni Kalu rUpANi aBiBUya jAnAti aBiBUya paSyati taTA asaMjQI ca Bavati / idam paQcamam aBiBvAya tanam / aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati pItAni yAvat pIta nirBAsAni / tat yaTA karNikAra puzpam saMpannam vA vArANasIyakam vastram pItam pIta varNam iti vistaraH / idam zazWam aBiBvAya tanam / aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati lohitAni yAvat lohita nirBAsAni / tat yaTA banDujIvaka puzpam saMpannam vA vArANasIyam vastram lohitam lohita varNam iti vistaraH / idam saptamam aBiBvAya tanam
