 shes zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  / / de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-ba #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched-drug #  pa'o / / nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs dmar-po #  / / kha-dog #  dmar-po #  / / dmar-po #  lta-bu # r ston-pa #  / / 'od dmar-po #  'byung-ba #  rnams la lta ste / / dper-na #  ban du dzi ba ka'i me-tog #  gam / / yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras-phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dmar-po #  / / kha-dog #  dmar-po #  / / dmar-po #  lta-bu # r ston-pa #  / / 'od dmar-po #  'byung-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  / / nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs dmar-po #  kha-dog #  dmar-po #  / / dmar-po #  lta-bu # r ston-pa #  / / 'od dmar-po #  'byung-ba #  rnams la lta zhing / / gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  / / de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-pa #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  bdun pa'o / / nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs dkar-po #  / / kha-dog #  dkar-po #  / / dkar-po-lta-bu # r ston-pa #  / / 'od dkar-po #  'byung-ba #  rnams la lta ste / / dper-na #  skar ma pa wa sangs kyi mdog gam / / yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras-phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dkar-po #  / / kha-dog #  dkar-po #  / / dkar-po-lta-bu # r ston-pa #  /
aDyAtmam arUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati avadAtAni avadAta varNAni avadAta nidarSanAni avadAta nirBAsAni / tat yaTA uzasi tArakAyAH varNam saMpannam vA vArANasIyakam vastram avadAtam avadAta varNam avadAta nidarSanam avadAta nirBAsam evam eva aDyAtma marUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyatya vadAtAni avadAta varNAni avadAta nidarSanAni avadAta nirBAsAni tAni Kalu rUpANi aBiBUya jAnAti aBiBUya paSyati taTAsaMjQI ca Bavati
# 'od dkar-po #  'byung-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  / / nang gzugs-med-pa # r 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs dkar-po #  / / kha-dog #  dkar-po #  / / dkar-po-lta-bu # r ston-pa #  / / 'od dkar-po #  'byung-ba #  rnams la lta zhing gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  mthong-ste #  / / de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-pa #  'di ni zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  brgyad pa'o zhes-bya-ba #  'di bzhi ni sdug ba'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  lus-kyis #  mngon-sum-du #  byas te /
idam azwamam aBiBvAya tanam / etAni catvAri SuBam vimokzam kAyena sAkzAt kRtvA upasaMpadya viharati iti etasmAt vimokzAt aBinirhriyate
# rdzogs-pa # r byas-na # s gnas so zhes-bya-ba # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  de-la # s 'byung ngo /
tatra vimokzEH AlaMbanam aDimucyate parItta Adikam aBiBvAya tanEH tu aBiBavati tad antarDAna Adi aTa izwam vA karaNAt vaSa vartamAna tAm upAdAya
# de-la #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  rnams kyis ni dmigs-pa #  chung du la-sogs-pa #  la mos-pa # r byed do / / zil-gyis-gnon-pa #  rnams kyis ni dbang-byed-pa # 'i phyir zil gyis gnon te / / de'i nang-du #  'dus-pa # r byed-pa #  dang ji-ltar-'dod-pa #  bzhin-du #  byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra parIttAni rUpANi sattva saMKyAtAni alpa pramANa tvAt
# de-la #  gzugs chung du rnams ni sems-can #  du gtogs-pa #  ste / / chung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
aDimAtrANi asat saMKyAtAni gRha vimAna parvata AdIni mahA pramANa tvAt
# chen-po #  ni sems-can #  ma-yin-pa # r gtogs-pa #  ste / / khang-pa #  dang gzhal-med-khang #  dang ri la-sogs-pa #  rgya-che-ba # 'i phyir ro /
suvarNa durvarNAni SuBa aSuBa varNa saMgRhItAni
# kha-dog #  mdzes-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  ni kha-dog #  sdug-pa #  dang kha-dog #  mi-sdug-pa #  las bsdus-pa #  rnams so /
hIna praNItAni mAnuzyaka divyAni yaTAkramam / tAni Kalu rUpANi aBiBUya iti vaSe vartayitvA / jAnAti iti SamaTa mArgeNa / paSyati iti vipaSya nAma argeNa
# mi'i dang lha rnams ni bzang-po #  dang ngan-pa #  rnams te / / go-rims #  bzhin no / / gzugs de-dag #  zil-gyis-mnan-nas #  shes zhes-bya-ba #  ni dbang bsgyur-nas #  so zhes-bya-ba #  ni zhi-gnas-kyi-lam #  gyis so / / mthong zhes-bya-ba #  ni lhag-mthong #  gi lam gyis so /
taTA asaMjIjI ca Bavati iti aBiBUte nABi BUte vA tat niraBimAna saMjQitAm upAdAya
# de-lta-bu # r 'du-shes #  par 'gyur-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni zil gyis mnan tam / / zil gyis ma mnan kyang rung ste / / de-la #  mngon-pa'i-nga-rgyal #  med-pa # 'i 'du-shes-can #  gyi phyir ro /
nIlAni iti uddeSa padam
# sngon-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni bstan-pa'i-tshig #  go /
nIla varNAni sahajAm nIla tAm upAdAya
# kha-dog #  sngon-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni lhan-cig #  skyes ba'i sngo-ba #  nyid kyi phyir ro /
nIlanidarSanAni saMyoga nIla tAm upAdAya
# sngon-po #  lta-bu # r ston-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni sbyar-ba #  las gyur-pa # 'i sngo-ba #  nyid kyi phyir ro /
nIla nirBAsAni tad uBayoH praBA nirmokza BAsara tAm upAdAya
# 'od sngon-po #  'byung-ba #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni de-gnyi-ga #  las 'od-'byung #  ba rnams 'od-gsal-ba #  nyid kyi phyir ro /
yaTA nIlAni evam pIta lohita avadAtAni vistareNa veditavyAni
# sngon-po #  la ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  ser-po #  dang dmar-po #  dang dkar-po #  rnams la yang rgya-cher #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
dRzwAnta dvayam ca ekEkasmin sahaja sAMyogika varNa udBAvanatAm upAdAya
# dpe gnyis po re-re #  la yang lhan-cig-skyes-pa #  dang sbyar-ba #  las byung-ba # 'i kha-dog #  brjod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'di-lta-ste #  /
aparaH paryAyaH tad yaTA nIlam iti puzpa vastrayoH samAnam uddeSa padam / nIla varNam iti puzpam eva aDikRtya tasya sAMyogika nIla tva saMBavAt
# sngon-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni me-tog #  dang ras gnyi-ga #  la mtshungs-pa # r bstan-pa'i-tshig #  go / / kha-dog #  sngon-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni me-tog #  nyid kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / de lhan-cig-skyes-pa # 'i sngon-po #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / sngon-po #  lta-bu # r ston-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni ras kyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / de-la #  sbyor-ba-las-gyur-pa # 'i sngon-po #  nyid yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nIla nirBAsam iti ucyate puzpa vastre aDikRtya dvayoH api BAsvara tva saMBavAt
# 'od sngon-po #  'byung bzhes-bya-ba #  ni me-tog #  dang ras gnyi-ga # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  ste / / gnyi-ga #  la yang 'od-gsal-ba #  nyid yod-pa # 'i phyir ro /
iti evam kRtvA dRzwAnte api tat yaTA umaka apuzpam saMpannam vA vArANasIyakam vastram nIlam nIlavarNam iti evamAdi nirdeSaH upapannaH Bavati
# de-ltar #  byas-na #  dper-na #  zar ma'i me-tog #  dang yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras-phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  sngon-po #  kha-dog #  sngon-po #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i dpe yang 'thad-pa # r 'gyur ro /
evam pIta Adikam yojayitavyam / Sizwam yaTA aDimokzezu / kim Sizwam
# de-bzhin-du #  ser-po #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / lhag-ma #  ni rnam-par-thar-pa #  las byung-ba #  ji-lta-ba #  bzhin no zhes-bya-ba #  la lhag-ma #  gang zhe na /
aDyAtmam rUpa saMjQI bahirDA rUpANi paSyati iti evamAdi / tat punar yaTA rUpI rUpANi paSyati iti evamAdi nirdeSa anusAreNa drazwavyam
# nang gzugs su 'du-shes #  pas phyi-rol #  gyi gzugs rnams mthong-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / de ni gzugs-can #  gzugs rnams la lta-ba #  zhes ji-skad-bstan-pa # 'i tshul-bzhin-du #  blta-bar-bya # 'o /
evam aBiBvAya tanEH AlaMbanam vaSe vartayitvA kRtsna AyatanEH kRtsnam sParati samantAnantA paryantam vistArayati iti arTaH / tAni punar kRtsna AyatanAni daSa Bavanti
# ji-ltar #  zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  rnams kyis dmigs-pa #  la dbang bsgyur-nas #  zad-par-gyi-skye-mched #  rnams kyis zad-pa # r rgyas-pa # r byed de / / kun du mtha'-yas-pa #  khyab-pa # r byed ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / zad-par-gyi-skye-mched #  de-dag #  ni bcu yin te /
tat yaTA pRTivI kRtsnam ap kRtsnam tejaH kRtsnam vAyu kRtsnam pIta kRtsnam lohita kRt snama vat AtakRtsnam AkASa AnantyAyatana kRtsnam vijQAna AnantyAya Ayatana kRt snam ca
# zad-pa # r sa dang zad-pa # r chu dang zad-pa # r med dang zad-pa # r rlung dang zad-pa # r sngon-po #  dang zad-pa # r ser-po #  dang zad-pa # r dmar-po #  dang zad-pa # r dkar-po #  dang zad-pa # r nam-mkha' #  mtha' yas skye-mched #  dang zad-pa # r rnam shes mtha' yas skye-mched #  do /
kRtsna Ayatanezu pRTivI AdIni yadi na vyavasTApyeran tena ASraya mahABUtEH vinA tat upAdAya rUpam nIla Adikam sParitum na Sakyeta
# zad-par-gyi-skye-mched #  rnams la sa la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa # r mi gzhag na ni des-na #  gnas 'byung-ba-chen-po #  rnams la rgyur byas ba'i gzugs sngon-po #  la-sogs-pa #  des khyab-pa # r byed mi-nus-pa #  ste /
tasya ASrayasya rUpasya sParaNa samRdDim upAdAya ezAm kRtsnezu vyavasTAnam veditavyam
# de-bas-na #  gnas dang bcas ba'i gzugs la khyab-pa # r bya-ba #  'byor-pa #  nyid kyi phyir / / de-dag #  ni zad-pa # r la rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
Sezam yaTAsaMBavam vimokza vat AkASa AnantyAya Ayatana kRt snAdi
# lhag-ma #  ni rnam-par-thar-pa #  bzhin-du #  ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du sbyar-ba # r bya'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni zad-pa # r nam-mkha' #  mtha' yas skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tatra vimokzEH AramBaH aBiBvAya taneH prayogaH kRtsna AyatanEH parinizpattiH vimokzANAm veditavyAH
# de-la #  rnam-par-thar-pa #  rnams kyis ni rnam-par-thar-pa #  rnams rtsom mo / / zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  rnams kyis ni sbyor ro / / zad-par-gyi-skye-mched #  rnams kyis ni yongs-su-grub-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / bam po dgu pa /
araNA vihArI yezAm sattvAnAm ABAsam gantu kAmaH Bavati tezAm Atmani kleSa samudAcAram aDikRtya anAgata vRttAntam vihAra gataH eva praNiDijQAna balena avalokya taTA tad samIpam upasaMkrAmati na vA yaTA te tatra anunaya pratiDerzyAmAt saryAdikam kleSa upakleSa saraNam na utpAdayanti
# nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # r gnas-pa #  ni sems-can #  gang dag gi mig lam-du #  snang-ba # r 'dod-pa #  de-dag #  bdag la nyon-mongs-pa #  kun du mi-'byung-ba # 'i rnam-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  'dug bzhin-du #  bsams nas shes-pa # 'i dbang gis ma-'ongs-pa #  na 'byung-ba #  la lta ste / / de-ltar #  de'i drung-du #  'gro yang rung mi 'gro yang rung ci nas der de-dag #  la rjes-su-chags-pa #  dang khong-khro-ba #  dang phrag-dog-dang-ser-sna #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang 'thab rtsod mi skyed do /
atas idam ucyate araNA DyAnam niSritya kleSa utpatti anurakzO= iha rasa mRdDO= iti vistaraH
# de'i-phyir #  nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa #  ni bsam-gtan #  la brten-nas #  gzhan gyi nyon-mongs-pa #  'byung-ba #  rjes su srung-ba # r gnas-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba #  de-skad #  ces bya-ba # 'o /
praNiDi jQAnam tad lABI yat yat eva trEyaDvikAdika jQeya vRttAntam jQAtu kAmaH Bavati tatra tatra mAnasam praNiDAya idam jAnIyAm iti DyAnam samApadyate tatas vyutTitasya tat praNiDAnam samRDyati tat jQeyam jAnAti iti arTaH
# bsams nas zhes-bya-ba #  ni de thob-pa #  gal-te #  dus-gsum #  pa la-sogs-pa # 'i shes-bya # 'i rnam-pa #  de nyid shes-par-'dod-pa # r gyur na de-dang-der #  'di shes-par-'gyur-ba # r bya'o zhes bsams nas bsam-gtan #  la snyoms-pa # r 'jug cing de-la # s langs-nas #  de'i smon-pa #  'grub-pa # r 'gyur te / / shes-bya #  de ni shes so zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
Darma pratisaMvid paryAyezu tat yaTA vidyA AdIn AraBya ajQAnam adarSanam anaBisamayaH iti evamAdizu avyAGAta samRdDO yaH samADiH iti vistaraH
# chos so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  ni rnam-grangs #  su gtogs-pa #  rnams la 'di-lta-ste #  / / ma-rig-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la brtsams nas mi-shes-pa #  dang mi mthong-ba #  dang mngon-pa # r mi rtogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  la thogs-pa-med-pa # r yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o / / don so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  ni /
arTa pratisaMvid sva sAmAnya lakzaNe DarmANAm arTa antara Adi aBiprAye ca avyAGAta samRdDO= iti vistaraH
# chos-rnams #  kyi rang-dang-spyi'i-mtshan-nyid #  dang don gzhan la-sogs-pa #  la dgongs-pa #  la thogs-pa-med-pa # r yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes rgya-cher #  'byung-ba # 'o /
nirukti pratisaMvij janapada BAzAyAm iti prativizayam yaTAsvam anyonya saMjQA antara anuvyavahAre Darma nirvacane ca iti tat yaTA lujyate pralujyate tasmAt lokaH rUpyate tasmAt rUpaH iti evamAdike / pratiBAna pratisaMvidDarma praBedezu iti dravya santaH prajQapti santaH saMvRti santaH paramArTa santaH iti evamAdizu / RdDa yaBijQAH vicitra budDi vikuvita samRdDO= iti tat yaTA ekaH BUtvA bahuDA Bavati iti evamAdO
# nges-pa'i-tshig #  so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  la yul mi'i skad ces bya-ba #  ni yul so-so-ba # s ji-ltar #  rang-rang-gis #  gzhan dang gzhan ming gzhan gyi tha-snyad-'dogs-pa # 'o / / chos-kyi-nges-pa'i-tshig #  la zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'jig-pa #  dang rab tu 'jig-pa # s de'i-phyir #  'jig-rten #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang gzugs su rung-ba # s de'i-phyir #  gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / spobs-pa #  so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  ni rdzas-su-yod-pa # 'o / / btags-pa'i-yod-pa # 'o / / kun-rdzob #  tu yod-pa # 'o / / don-dam-pa # r yod-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  chos rab tu 'byed-pa # 'o / / rdzu-'phrul #  gyi mngon-par-shes-pa #  la rdzu-'phrul #  gyis rnam-par-'phrul-pa #  sna-tshogs #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  gcig-tu #  gyur nas mang-po # r gyur zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
vicitrANAm SabdAnAm anuSrava samRdDO= iti divya mAnuzyaka AdInAm
# sgra sna-tshogs #  nyan-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni lha-dang-mi # 'i la-sogs-pa # 'o /
para sattvezu citta carita praveSa samRdDO= iti sa rAga Adi citta pracAra yaTABUta jQAna samRdDO= iti arTaH
# sems-can-gzhan #  dag gi sems-can #  gyi spyod-pa #  la 'jug-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'dod-chags #  dang bcas-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems-kyi-rgyu-ba #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  shes-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
pUrva anta caryAyAH anusmaraNa samRdDO= iti atItam janma paraMparAm AraBya nAma jAti gotra Adi prakAra vRttAyAH iti arTaH
# sngon-gyi-mtha' # i spyod-pa #  rjes-su-dran-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'das-pa # 'i tshe-rabs #  gcig-nas-gcig-tu #  brgyud-pa #  las brtsams te / / ming dang rigs-dang-rus #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # 'i lo drung shes zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
cyuti utpAda aBijQAH divyena cakzuzA sattvAnAm cyavamAnAm upapadyamAnAnAm suvarNAnAm durvarNAnAm sugatim api gacCatAm durgatim api aparAntam AraBya cyuti upapAda saMdarSana samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# 'chi-'pho-dang-skye-ba #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  ni lha'i-mig #  gis sems-can #  'chi-'pho-ba #  dang skye-ba #  dang kha-dog-bzang-po #  dang kha-dog-ngan-pa #  dang bde-'gror-'gro-ba #  dang ngan-'gror-'gro-ba #  dang phyi-ma'i-mtha' #  las brtsams te / / 'chi-'pho-dang-skye-ba #  mthong-ba #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
Asrava kzaya jQAna samRdDO= iti yena upAyena AsravAH parikzoyante yaH ca ezAm parikzayaH tad jQAna nizpatti nimittam iti arTaH
# zag-pa-zad-pa #  shes-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-ba # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni thabs gang-gis #  zag-pa #  rnams yongs-su-zad-pa #  dang de-dag #  yongs-su-zad-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de shes-pa #  'grub-pa'i-rgyu #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
lakzaNa anuvyaQjanAni yat samADi prajQA ADipatyena budDAH BagavantaH dvAtriMSatA lakzaNEH aSItyA anuvyaQjanEH viBrAjamAnam rUpa kAyam saMdarSayanti vineyAnAm
# mtshan dang dpe byang bzang-po #  rnams ni gang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi dbang gis sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams skyes-bu-chen-po'i-mtshan #  sum cu rtsa gnyis dang dpe-byad-bzang-po #  brgyad cus rnam-pa # r mdzes-pa # 'i gzugs-kyi-sku # s 'dul-ba #  rnams la kun du ston to /
tad svaBAvAni tAni tezAm veditavyAni Darma kAya praBAvita tvAt budDAnAm BagavatAm iti
# de-dag #  gi de-dag #  ni de'i-rang-bzhin #  du rig-par-bya #  ste / / sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams ni chos kyi skus rab-tu-phye-ba # 'i phyir ro /
boDisattvAnAm tu taTA asaMdarSana samarTAnAm samADi prajQA svaBAvAni
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  de-ltar #  ston nus-pa #  rnams kyang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  kyi rang-bzhin #  no /
tat anyezAm parzad maNXalezu upapannAnAm tad samutTita vipAka svaBAvAni veditavyAni
# nga la gzhan-pa #  'khor-gyi-dkyil-'khor #  dag tu skyes-pa #  rnams ni de-la # s byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i rang-bzhin #  du rig-par-bya # 'o /
catasraH sarva kArAH pariSudDayaH budDAnAm BagavatAm mahA aBijQA prAptAnAm ca boDisattvAnAm
# sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  chen-po #  thob-pa #  rnams kyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  ni bzhi ste /
tatra yaTAkAmam ASrayasya upAdAna sTAna parityAgAnAm samRdDO= iti yatra icCati tatra upapatti grahaNataH tasyAm ca upapattO= AyuH saMskArAn aDizWAya yAvat icCam avasTAnataH yat ecCati tadA AyuH saMskAra utsarjanataH ca yaTAkramam
# de-la #  ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  gnas len ba dang bzhugs-pa #  dang yongs-su-gtong-ba #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni gang-du #  bzhed-pa #  der skye-ba #  'dzin-pa #  dang der skyes nas kyang tshe'i 'du-byed #  byin gyis brlabs te ji-srid #  bzhed-pa # r bzhugs-pa #  dang gang-gi-tshe #  bzhed-pa #  de'i dus na tshe de'i 'du-byed #  'der ba ste /
yaTAkAmam AlaMbanam aDikRtya nirmANa pariNAmana jQAnAnAm samRdDO= iti apUrva rUpa Adi nirmANataH pUrva utpannAnAm rUpa AdInAm suvarNa Adi tvena pariNAmataH sarva prakAra avagamanataH ca yaTAkramam / yaTAkAmam samADi muKa vaSa varti samRdDO= iti pratikzaNam yaTezwam aparimita samADi antara samApattaye
# go-rims #  bzhin no / / ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  dmigs-pa # 'i dbang du mdzad-pa # 'i sprul pa dang sgyur ba dang mkhyen-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa #  dang zhes-bya-ba #  ni sngon ma-byung-ba # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  sprul pa dang sngon byung-ba # 'i gzugs la-sogs-pa #  gser la-sogs-pa # r bsgyur-ba #  dang rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  thugs-su-chud-pa # 'i phyir de go-rims #  bzhin no / / ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  ting-nge-'dzin #  gyi sgo la dbang-sgyur-ba #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-ba # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni skad-cig-re-re-la #  ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  ting-nge-'dzin #  gzhan dpag-tu-med-pa #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTAkAmam DAraNI muKa saMDAraNa samRdDO= iti dvAcatvAriMSataH akzarANAm anyatama akzara manasikAre tad Adi sarva Darma paryAya aBilapana sAmarTya pratilamBAya iti arTaH
# ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  gzungs kyi sgo-kun #  du 'dzin-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  ni yi-ge #  bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis las yi-ge #  gang-yang-rung-ba #  yid-la-byed-pa #  na des thog-ma-kho-nar #  chos-kyi-rnam-grangs #  thams-cad #  brjod nus-pa #  thob-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
daSa balAni sTAna AsTAna jQAna balam karma sva jQAna balam DyAna vimokza samADi samApatti jQAna balam indriya para apara jQAna balam nAnA aDimukti jQAna balam nAnA DAtu jQAna balam sarvatra gAminI pratipad jQAna balam pUrva nivAsa anusmRti jQAna balam cyuti upapAda jQAna balam Asrava kzaya jQAna balam ca / tatra sTAna AsTAna jQAna balam DyAnam niSritya sarva prakAra hetu ahetu jQAna asaMgA pratihata saMmuKIBAve samADi AdayaH
# stobs ni bcu ste / / gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang las-bdag-gir-bya-ba #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang / / bsam-gtan #  dang rnam-par-thar-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang dbang-po #  mchog dang mchog-ma-yin-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang mos-pa-sna-tshogs #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang khams sna-tshogs #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang thams-cad-du-'gro-ba # 'i lam mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang sngon-gyi-gnas #  rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang shi 'pho-ba #  dang skye-ba #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  dang zag-pa-zad-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  so / / gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  ni bsam-gtan #  la brten-nas #  rgyu dang rgyu-ma #  yin pa rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  mkhyen-pa #  chags-pa #  med cing thogs-pa-med-pa #  mngon-du-gyur-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
evam karma sva jQAna bala Adizu sarva AkAra karma svaka tA jQAna asaMgA pratihata saMmuKIBAvaH iti yojayitavyam / catvAri vESAradyAni samyaksaMbudDasya vata me sataH ime te DarmAH anaBisaMbudDAH iti atra mAm kaScid SramaNaH vA devaH vA mAraH vA brahmA vA saha DarmeNa codayet vA smArayet vA nimittam api na samanupaSyAmya etat ca nimittam asamupaSyan kzema prAptaH ca vESAradya prAptaH ca udAram ArzaBam sTAnam prajAnAmi brahmacaryam pravartayAmi parizadi samyak siMhanAdam nadAmi / kzINa Asravasya vata me sataH ime AsravAH aparikzINAH iti / ye vA punar me SrAvakANAm antarAyikAH DarmAH AKyAtAH tAn pratizevamAnasya na alam antarAya tA iti yaH vA punar me SrAvakANAm niryANAya mArgaH AKyAtaH AryonEH yANikaH nErveDikaH sa vata na samyak niryAti tat karasya samyak duHKa kzayAya duHKasya anta kriyAyE iti atra mAm kaScid SramaNaH vA brAhmaNaH vA yAvat siMhanAdam nadAmi iti vistareNa ekasmin vaktavyam
# de-bzhin-du #  las-bdag-gir-bya-ba #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  la-sogs-pa #  la yang rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  de mkhyen-pa #  chags-pa #  med cing thogs-pa-med-pa #  mngon-du-gyur-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # r sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / mi-'jigs-pa #  ni bzhi ste / / nga mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r sangs-rgyas #  so zhes-bya-ba #  'di-la #  chos 'di dag mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r sangs ma rgyas so zhes dge-sbyong #  dang bra ma ze 'am / / lha 'am / / bdud dam / / tshangs-pa # 'am / / sus kyang chos-dang-mthun-pa # r nga la rgol-ba # 'am / / drod bar byed-pa # 'i mtshan-ma #  mi mthong-ste #  / / mtshan-ma #  de mi mthong-ba # s bde-ba #  thob mi-'jigs-pa #  thob bag-tsha-ba-med-pa #  thob-nas #  gnas so / / khyu-mchog #  gi gnas rgya-chen-po # r zhal gyis 'che'o / / tshangs-pa'i-'khor-lo #  bskor ro / / 'khor-gyi-nang-du #  seng-ge # 'i sgra yang-dag-par #  sgrog go / / nga zag-pa #  zad do zhes-bya-ba #  la zag ba 'di dag yongs-su-ma-zad #  do / / zhes-bya-ba #  dang ngas nyan-thos #  rnams la bar-du-gcod-pa'i-chos #  gang dag bstan-pa #  de-dag #  bsten kyang-ba # r du gcad-pa # r mi 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  dang yang ngas nyan-thos #  rnams la nges bar 'byung-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir / / 'phags-pa #  nges-par-'byin-pa #  des-pa # r 'byung pa'i lam gang bshad-pa #  de nges-par-'byung-ba #  ma yin no zhe'am / / de byed-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  yang-dag-par #  zad-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  dang sdug-bsngal #  gyi tha-ma #  byed-pa # r mi 'gyur ro zhes 'di-la #  dge-sbyong #  ngam sus kyang nga la zhes-bya-ba #  nas seng-ge # 'i sgra yang-dag-par #  sgrog ces bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  rgya-cher #  re-re #  la yang brjod-pa # r bya'o /
tAni etAni vESAradyAni sva arTam para arTam ca AraBya veditavyAni
# mi-'jigs-pa-bzhi #  po 'di dag ni rang-gi-don #  dang gzhan-gyi-don #  las brtsam par rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra dviviDaH sva arTaH jQAna viSezaH prahANa viSezaH ca
# de-la #  rang-gi-don #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / ye shes kyi khyad-par #  dang spangs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  ro /
dviviDaH para arTaH vipakza Darma vivarjanam pratipakza Darma nizevaNam ca
# gzhan-gyi-don #  yang rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / mi-mthun-pa # 'i chos yongs-su-spang-ba #  dang gnyen-po # 'i chos la brten-pa # 'o /
tatra aBisaMboDi vESAradyam jQAna Atmakam sva arTam eva AraBya sarva AkAram mayA sa praBeda paryantam jQeyam aBisaMbudDam iti etasyAH pratijQAyAH samyak niranuyojya tvena sarvasmin loke pratizWApana samRdDO yaH samADiH iti pUrvavat
# de-la #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa #  la mi-'jigs-pa #  ni ye shes kyi bdag-nyid #  de rang-gi-don #  la brtsams nas rnam-pa-thams-cad-du #  ngas rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtha' dang bcas-pa # r shes-par-bya-ba #  mngon-pa # r sangs-rgyas #  so zhes zhal-gyis-'che-ba #  ste / / yang-dag-par #  rgol-ba #  med-pa # r 'jig-rten-thams-cad #  du 'jog-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  gang-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  snga-ma-bzhin #  no /
evam SezANi api vESAradyAni yojayitavyAni / sarva AkArAH punar AsravAH sa vAsanAH kleSAH drazwavyAH
# mi-'jigs-pa #  lhag-ma #  rnams kyang de-bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / zag-pa # 'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams su rig-par-bya # 'o /
sarva AkArAH antarAyikAH DarmAH sarve sAMkleSikAH vipakza DarmAH drazwavyAH
# bar-du-gcod-pa'i-chos #  rnam-pa-thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi chos kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  thams-cad-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
sarva AkAraH nEryANikaH mArgaH prayoga mArgam AraBya yAvat nizWA mArgaH drazwavyaH / trINi AveNikAni smRti upasTAnAni / iha SAstA SrAvakANAm Darmam deSayati anukampakaH kAruNikaH arTa kAmaH hita ezI karuNAyamAnaH idam vaH BikzavaH hitAya idam suKAya idam hita suKAya iti / tasya te SrAvakAH SuSrUzante Srotram avadaDati AjQA cittam upasTApayanti pratipadyante Darmasya anuDarmam / tatra taTAgatasya na nAndI Bavati na sOmanasyam na cetasaH utplAvita tvam upekzakaH tatra taTAgataH viharati smRtaH saMprajAnan / idam praTama AveNikam smRti upasTAnam / yat AryaH sevate yat AryaH sevamAnaH arhati gaNam anuSAsitum
# nges-par-'byin-pa'i-lam #  gyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  ces bya-ba #  ni sbyor-ba #  nas-bzung-ste #  / / mthar-phyin-pa # 'i lam gyi bar-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  gsum ni 'di-la #  ston-pa #  thugs brtse ba can thugs rje dang ldan-pa #  / / don bzhed-pa #  / / phan-pa # r bzhed-pa #  / / thugs rje can nyan-thos #  rnams la dge slong dag 'di ni phan-pa # r 'gyur-ba # 'o / / 'di ni bde-bar-'gyur-ba # 'o / / 'di ni phan-pa-dang-bde-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'o zhes chos-ston-pa #  'di-la #  nyan-thos #  de-dag #  gus-par #  nyan-pa #  dang rna-ba #  gtod-pa #  dang kun-shes-pa # 'i sems nye-bar-'jog-pa #  dang chos kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-pa #  de-la #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  dgyes-pa # r mi 'gyur / / yid-bde-ba # r mi 'gyur / / thugs dga'-ba #  ya ya por mi 'gyur gyi btang-snyoms-can #  du de-bzhin #  gshes-pa #  de-la #  gnas te / / dran-pa #  dang shes-bzhin #  dang ldan-pa #  'di ni ma-'dres-pa # 'i dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  dang-po #  ste / / gang 'phags-pa #  bsten-na # s kyang 'khor la rjes-su-bstan-pa # r 'os-pa # 'o /
punar aparam SAstA SrAvakANAm Darmam deSayati yAvat idam hita suKAya / tasya te SrAvakAH na SuSrUzante yAvat na pratipadyante Darmasya anuDarmam
# gzhan-yang #  ston-pa #  'di ni phan-pa-dang-bde-ba # r 'gyur-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  chos-ston-pa #  de-la #  nyon thos de-dag #  gus-par #  mi nyan-pa #  nas / / chos kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  mi sgrub ba'i bar de-la #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  kun-nas-mnar-sems #  su mi 'gyur /
tatra taTAgatasya na AGAtaH Bavati na akza antiH na apratyayaH na cetasaH anaBirAt DiH upekzakaH tatra iti vistaraH / idam dvitIyam
# mi-bzod-pa # r mi 'gyur / / thugs mi ches par mi 'gyur / / thugs mi-mnyes-pa # r mi 'gyur gyi btang-snyoms-can #  du de-la #  zhes-bya-ba #  rgya-cher #  sbyar te 'di ni gnyis-pa # 'o /
tRtIye ayam viSezaH asya eke SrAvakAH SuSrUzante yAvat pratipadyante Darmasya anuDarma meke na SuSrUzante yAvat na pratipadyante Darmasya anuDarmam / tatra taTAgatasya na nAndaH Bavati yAvat cetasaH nABiH AdiH iti
# gsum-pa # 'i bye-brag #  ni 'di yin te / / de-la #  nyan-thos #  kha-cig #  gus-par #  nyan-pa #  nas chos kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  sgrub-par-byed-pa #  dang kha-cig #  gus-par #  mi nyan-pa #  nas chos kyi rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  mi sgrub-pa # 'i bar de-la #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # r dgyes-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba #  nas thugs mi mnyen-pa # r mi-'gyur-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
etAni trINi smRti upasTAnAni SAstuH gaNa parikarzaNe yaTAkramam sarva AkAra anunaya pratiGata duBaya saMkleSa vAsanAyAH asamudAcAra samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  gsum po 'di dag ni ston-pa # 'i tshogs-yongs-su-sdud-pa #  la go-rims-bzhin-du #  rjes-su-chags-pa #  dang khong-khro-ba #  dang de-gnyi-ga # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang-ba # g chags kyi rnam-pa-thams-cad #  kun du mi-'byung-ba #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
trINi ArakzANi / pariSudDa kAya samudAcAraH taTAgataH / na asti taTAgatasya apariSudDa kAya samudAcAra tA yAm taTAgataH praticCAdayitavyAm manyeta kaccit me pare vijAnIyuH iti / evam vAc manaH samudAcArate veditavye
# bsrung-ba #  med ba gsum ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i sku'i phrin-las #  kyi spyod-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  ste / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  sku'i phrin-las #  yongs su ma-dag-pa #  med de / / bdag la gzhan gyis shes su 'ong ngo zhes bcab par dgongs-pa #  med-pa #  dang de-bzhin-du #  gsung dang thugs kyi phrin-las #  la yang rig-par-bya # 'o / / de-dag #  gi tha-snyad #  gdags su med-pa # r dogs-pa #  mi mda' ba'i phyir /
eBiH nirvaktavya tayA nirASaFka tvAt svayam SAstu vineya jana parikarzaNam AraBya yaTezwam nigRhya prasajya avavAda anuSAsanI prayogaH samRdDayati iti veditavyam
# ston-pa #  nyid kyis gdul-ba # 'i skye-bo #  sdug-pa #  las brtsams te / / ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  tshar bcad de spa bkod nas gdams pa dang rjes-su-bstan-pa #  la sbyor-ba #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
asaMmoza Darma tA sarva vineya kAryam AraBya yaTAvat kRtasya BAzitasya ca aBilapana samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# bsnyel ba med-pa # 'i chos-nyid #  ni gdul-ba # 'i bya-ba #  thams-cad-la # s brtsams te / / ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  mdzad-pa #  dang gsungs-pa # 'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  mngon-par-brjod-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
vAsanA samudGAtaH sarvajQasya sataH kleSa jQeya AvaraNa Seza sUcakAnAm kAya vAc cezwitAnAm asamudAcAra samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# bag-chags #  yang-dag-par-bcom-pa #  ni thams-cad-mkhyen-pa # r gyur nas nyon-mongs-pa #  dang shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa # 'i lhag-ma #  yod-pa #  ston-pa # 'i sku dang gsung gi g-yo-ba #  kun du mi-'byung-ba #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
mahA karuNA trEDAtuka avacarezu sarva sattvezu nirantara sarva prakAra duHKa alaMkana karuNA vihAra samRdDO samADi AdayaH / azwAdaSa AveNikAH budDa DarmAH tat yaTA na asti taTAgatasya sKalitam na asti ravitam na asti muzitA smRtiH na asti asamAhitam cittam na asti nAnA tva saMjQAH na asti pratisaMKyAya upekzAH na asti Canda parihAriH na asti vIrya parihANiH na asti samADi parihANiH na asti prajQA arihANiH na asti vimukti parihANiH sarvam taTAgatasya kAya karma jQAna pUrva gamam jQAna anuparivarti sarvam vAkkarma jQAna pUrva pUrva gamam jQAna anupavarti atIte aDva nyasaFgam apratihatam jQAnam anAgate aDvani asaFgam apratihatam jQAnam pratyutpanne aDva nyasaFgam apratihatam jQAnam iti jQAnam iti vijQAnam iti jQAnam iti / ezAm punar vyavasTAnam tat yaTA arhan BikzuH kzINa AsravaH grAmam piNXAya caran= ekadA caNXena hastinA sa arGa samAgacCati / yaTA caNXena hastinA evam caNXa nASvena caNXayA gavA caNXena kukkureNa / gahanam vA kaNwaka bAwam vA mRdnAti / alagardam vA padAByAm samAkrAmati / tad rUpam vA AgAram praviSati yatra enam mAtR grAmaH ayoga vihitena upanimantrayati / araNye vA punar amArgam hitvA kumArgeNa gacCati / corEH vA taskarEH vA sArDam samAgacCati siMhEH vyAGrEH vA apara vRkEH vA iti evaMBAgIyam sKalitam arhataH taTAgatasya sarveNa sarva na asti / punar ayam arhan= eka dAraNye pravaNe anvAhiNXat mArgAt apanaSya SUnya AgAram praviSya Sabdam udIrayati Gozam anuSrAvayati mahArutam ravati / vAsanA dozam vAgamya klizwam mahA hAsam hasati danta vidarSakam saMcagDitam upadarSanati / iti evaMBAgIyam arhataH ravitam taTAgatasya sarveNa sarvam na asti / na asti taTAgatasya muzitA smRtiH aklizwa cira kRta cira BAzita anusmaraNa tAm uzA AdAya / punar aparam arhan samApannaH samAhitaH Bavati vyutTitaH asamAhitaH / taTAgatasya tu sarva avasTam na asti asamAhitam cittam / punar aparam arhan= ekAntena upaDA ca pratikramaNa saMjQI Bavati nirupaDike ca nirvANe SAnta saMjQI / taTAgatasya upaDO nirvANe ca nAnAtva saMjQA na asti parama upekzA vihAritAm upAdAya / punar aparam arhan= apratisaMKyAya sattva arTa kriyAm aDyupekzate / taTAgatasya tu iyam evaMBAgIyA pratisaMKyAya upekzA na asti

 mi-rigs-pa #  skyes-pa # s bos-pa # 'i khyim de-lta-bu # r 'jug-pa #  dang dgon-pa # r lam nor nas lam-log-pa # r 'gro-ba #  dang chom-rkun #  rnams dang rkun-po #  rnams dang seng-ge #  dang stag dang spyang ki dang lhan-cig #  'gro-ba #  dang de-lta-bu #  dang mthun-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dgra-bcom-pa # 'i 'khrul-pa #  de ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  thams-cad-kyi-thams-cad #  du mi mnga'o / / gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  res-'ga' #  dgon-pa #  na nags khrod chen-po # r rgyu-ba #  na lam nor te / / grong stong du phyin nas sgra-'byin #  pa dang sgra sgrogs-pa #  dang ku-co #  cher 'don-pa #  dang-ba # g chags kyi nyes-pa #  la brten-nas #  nyon-mongs-pa-can #  gyi gad mo rta-gad #  so snang-ba # r dgod-pa #  dang 'phya-ba #  nye-bar #  ston-pa #  dang de-lta-bu #  dang mthun-pa #  dgra-bcom-pa # 'i ca-co #  de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  thams-cad-kyi-thams-cad #  du mi-mnga'-ba # 'o / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  bsnyel ba med de nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # r yun-ring-po-nas #  mdzad-pa #  dang gsungs-pa #  rjes-su-dran-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  ni snyoms-pa # r zhugs nas mnyam-par-bzhag-pa # r 'gyur gyi langs-nas #  mnyam-par-bzhag-pa #  ni ma yin no / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  ni gnas-skabs-thams-cad #  du sems-mnyam-pa # r ma bzhag-pa #  med do / / gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  ni phung-po #  la shin-tu #  mi-mthun-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  su lta zhing phung-po #  med-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la zhi-ba # 'i 'du-shes #  su 'gyur ro / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  ni phung-po #  dang mya-ngan-las-'das-pa #  la tha-dad-pa # 'i 'du-shes #  mi mda'o / / gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  ni so-so # r ma-brtags-pa # r sems-can-gyi-don #  yal-ba # r 'dor ro / / de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  ni de-lta-bu #  dang mthun-pa #  so-so # r ma-brtags-pa # 'i btang-snyoms #  mi mda'o /
punar aparam arhan jQeya AvaraNa viSudDim AraBya aprApta parihANyA Candena api parihIyate vIrye NApi smRtyA samADinA prajQayA vimuktyA vimukti jQAna darSanena api parihIyate
# gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  ni shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  las brtsams te / / 'dun-pa #  las kyang ma-thob-pa # 'i yongs-su-nyams-pa # s yongs su nyams so / / brtson 'grus dang dran ba dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang shes-rab #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba #  las kyang yongs su nyams so /
iti iyam sapta AkArA parihANiH taTAgatasya na asti
# de-bzhin-gshegs-pa-la #  ni yongs-su-nyams-pa #  rnam-pa #  'di drug med do /
punar aparam arhan= ekadA kuSale kAya karmaNi pravartate ekadA vyAkRte
# gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  ni res-'ga' #  lus-kyi-las #  dge-ba #  la 'jug / / res-'ga' #  lung-du-ma-bstan-pa #  la 'jug go /
yaTA kAya karmaNi evam vAc karmaNi manaskarmaNi ca
# lus-kyi-las #  ji-lta-ba # r dag gi las dang yid-kyi-las #  kyang de-bzhin #  no /
taTAgatasya trayANAm api karmaNAm jQAna pUrva gama tvAt jQAna anuparivarti tvAt ca na asti avyAkRtam karma tatra jQAna samutTApana tAm upAdAya jQAna pUrva gamam / jQAna sahacaratAm upAdAya jQAna anuparivarti
# de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i phrin-las #  gsum po ni ye shes sngon-du-'gro-ba #  dang ye shes kyi rjes-su-'brang-ba # 'i phyir lung-du-ma-bstan-pa # 'i las med do / / de-la #  ye shes kun-nas-slong-ba # 'i phyir ye shes sngon-du-'gro-ba # 'o / / ye shes dang lhan-cig #  rgyu-ba # 'i phyir ye shes kyi rjes-su-'brang-ba # 'o /
punar aparam arhan trEyaDvikam jQeya vastu na ca ABoga mAtrAt pratipadyate yena asya saktam jQAna darSanam Bavati
# gzhan-yang #  dgra-bcom-pa #  ni rtsol btsam gyis dus-gsum #  gyi shes-bya'i-dngos-po #  rtogs-pa # r mi 'gyur te / / des-na #  de'i ye-shes-mthong-ba #  chags-pa # r 'gyur ro /
na ca sarvam pratipadyate yena asya pratihatam jQAna darSanam Bavati
# thams-cad #  rtogs-pa # r yang mi 'gyur te / / des-na #  de'i ye-shes-mthong-ba #  thogs-pa # r 'gyur ro /
taTAgataH trEyaDvikama ABoga mAtrAt sarvam vastu pratipadyate / tasmAt ete azwAdaSa AveNikAH budDa DarmAH iti ucyante
# de-bzhin-gshegs-pa #  ni rtsol ba tsam gyis dus-gsum #  gyi shes-bya'i-dngos-po #  thams-cad #  rtogs te / / de-lta-bas-na #  de-dag #  ni sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  ma-'dres-pa #  bco brgyad ces bya'o /
tatra ezAm AdyAH zaw asADAraNa kAya vAc manaH karma pariSudDi samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# de-la #  'di dag las dang-po #  drug ni sku dang gsungs dang thugs kyi phrin-las #  thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tatra na asti sKalitam iti ayam kAya karma pariSudDim AraBya
# de-la #  'khrul-pa #  med ces bya-ba #  'di ni sku'i phrin-las #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  las brtsams pa'o /
na asti ravitam iti ayam vAc karma para SudDim AraBya
# ca-co #  med ces bya-ba #  'di ni gsung gi phrin-las #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  las brtsams pa'o /
tatra na asti muzita smRtiH na asti asamAnitam cittam na asti nAnA tva saMjQA na asti apratisaMKyAya upekzya etat catuzwayam manaH karma pariSudDim aDikRtya veditavyam
# bsnyel ba med-pa #  dang tha-dad-pa # 'i 'du-shes-med-pa #  dang sems-mnyam-pa # r ma bzhag-pa #  med-pa #  dang so-so # r ma-brtags-pa # 'i btang-snyoms #  med ces bya-ba #  'di bzhis ni thugs kyi phrin-las #  yongs-su-dag-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
na asti Canda parihAriH yAvat na asti vimukti jQAna darSana parihANiH iti sa ASrayANAm sa PalAnAm taTAgata indriyANAm aprApti aparihANi samRdDO samADi AdayaH / tatra ASrayaH CandaH / Palam vimuktiH vimukti jQAna darSanam ca
# 'dun-pa #  nyams-pa #  med ces bya-ba #  nas / / rnam-par-grol-ba #  nyams-pa #  med ces bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  drug ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i dbang-po #  gnas-dang-bcas-pa #  dang 'bras-bu-dang-bcas-pa #  rnams ma-thob-pa # 'i yongs-su-nyams-pa #  med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / de-la #  gnas ni 'dun-pa # 'o / / 'bras-bu #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # 'o /
indriyANi vIrya AdIni veditavyAni
# dbang-po #  ni brtson 'grus la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
sarvam kAya karma vAc karma manaskarma jQAna pUrva gamam jQAna anuvarti iti ete trayaH asADAraNa karma cAra samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# lus-kyi-las #  dang dag gi las dang yid-kyi-las #  thams-cad #  ye shes sngon-du #  'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes-su-'brang-ba #  zhes bya-pa #  'di gsum ni thun-mong-ma-yin-pa # 'i phrin-las-mdzad-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
atIte aDvani asaFgam apratihatam jQAnam yAvat pratyutpanne aDvani iti ete trayaH asADAraNa jQAna vihAra samRdDO samADi AdayaH
# 'das-pa'i-dus #  la ma chags ma thogs-pa # 'i ye shes zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / da-ltar-byung-ba # 'i dus la zhes-bya-ba #  'di gsum ni ye shes la gnas-pa #  thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i ting-nge-'dzin #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
skanDa DAtu Ayatanezu sarva AkAra jQa tA samRdDO= iti skanDa AdInAm svaBAva viSeza lakzaNa praBeda paryanta jQAna nizpattO= iti arTaH
# phung-po #  dang khams dang skye-mched #  rnams la rnam-pa-thams-cad #  mkhyen-pa #  nyid yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  dang khyad-par #  gyi mtshan-nyid #  dang rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mthar-thug-pa #  mkhyen-pa #  grub ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
tezAm punar aBinirhAraH niSrayataH aBinirhAraka pudgalataH aBinirhAra upAyataH ca paridIpitaH
# de-dag #  ni mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i gnas dang mngon-par-sgrub-pa #  po gang-zag #  dang mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i thabs kyis yongs su bstan to /
aBinirhAra upAyaH punar yaTA vyavasTAnam manaskAra bahulIkAra tA yaTAdeSanam samAhitasya cittasya punar punar tatra DAraNam iti arTaH
# mngon-par-sgrub-pa # 'i thabs ni ji-ltar #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  bzhin-du #  lan-mang-du #  yid-la-byed-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA pramANAni aBinirhartu kAmaH maMtrI saha gatena cittena avEreNa asatnena iti evamAdikAm deSanAm DyAna saMniSrayeNa BAvayan manasikurvan bahulIkaroti evam aBijQA AdIn aBi nirhartu kAmaH ekaH BUtvA bahuDA Bavati iti evamAdikam vyavasTAnam manasikurvan bahulIkaroti iti yojayitavyam
# ji-ltar #  bstan-pa #  bzhin-du #  sems-mnyam-pa # r gzhag nas yang-dang-yang #  de-la #  'jog ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / 'di-lta-ste #  tshad-med-pa #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa # r 'dod-pa #  byams-pa-dang-ldan-pa # 'i sems kho-na #  med-pa #  'gran-zla-med-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s bstan ba bsam-gtan #  la brten-nas #  bsams-pa # s yid-la-byed-pa # s mang-du #  byed do / / de-bzhin-du #  mngon-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa # r 'dod-pa # s gcig-tu #  gyur nas mang-po # r 'gyur zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa # s mang-du #  byed do zhes sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
te ete apramANa AdayaH guNAH dvi prakArAH
# tshad-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yon-tan #  'di dag ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  te /
sva kAritra pratyupasTAnAH ca yEH AryaH yaTAyogam vipakza prahANa Adikam karma karoti vEhArikAH ca yEH parama praSAnta nirvikalpa jQAna saMgRhItEH anAlambana apramANa AdiBiH dRzwe Darme suKam viharati
# rang-gi #  bya-ba #  la nye-bar-gnas-pa #  ni gang dag gis 'phags-pa #  ci-rigs-su #  mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  spong-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las-byed-pa # 'o / / gnas-pa #  las gyur-pa #  ni mchog-tu #  zhi-ba #  rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes kyis bsdus-pa #  dmigs-pa-med-pa # 'i tshad-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gang dag gis mthong-ba # 'i chos la bde-bar-gnas-pa # 'o /
tatra apramANA eva pakzam prajahAti iti yaTAkramam vyApAdam vihiMsAm aratim anunaya pratiGO ca
# de-la #  tshad-med-pa #  rnams kyis mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  spong ngo zhes-bya-ba #  ni gnod-sems #  dang rnam-par-'tshe-ba #  dang mi-dga'-ba #  dang rjes-su-chags-pa #  dang khong-khro-ba #  dang go-rims #  bzhin no /
etAni ca catvAri apramANAni anukampA iti ucyate eBiH sattva arTam pratyanuguNam pravartanAt
# tshad-med-pa-bzhi #  po 'di dag ni snying brtse ba zhes bya ste / / 'di dag gis sems-can-gyi-don #  gyi rjes-su-mthun-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
atas tEH viharamANaH sarva sattvezu anukampA vihAritayA puNya saMBAram paripUrayati
# de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  gi gnas na sems-can-thams-cad #  la thugs brtse bar gnas-pa # s bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r mdzad do /
atas eva sattva paripAke ca na pariKidyate sarva sattva anukampitvena sva Atma nirapekza tvAt
# de nyid kyi phyir sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r mdzad-pa #  la yongs su mi skyo ste / / sems-can-thams-cad #  la thugs brtse bas bdag la mi-lta-ba # 'i phyir ro /
vimokzezu dvAByAm vimokzAByAm nirmANa karma aBinirharati
# rnam-par-thar-pa #  rnams las gnyis kyis ni sprul pa'i lam mngon-pa # r sgrub bo /
tRtIyena SuBe nirmANe na saMkliSyate
# gsum-pa # s ni dge-ba #  sprul pa la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
catuBiH Arya vimokzEH SAntezu mokzezu na sajjate
# gzugs-med-pa # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  bzhi ni zhi-ba # 'i rnam-par-thar-pa #  rnams la mi chags so /
praScimena parama praSAntena Arya vihAreNa viharati
# tha-ma # s ni 'phags-pa'i-gnas-pa #  mchog-tu #  rab-tu-zhi-ba # 'i gnas-pa # s nas te /
taTA taTA aDimokza arTaH ca vimokzaH veditavyaH
# de-la #  de-ltar #  mos-pa # 'i don ni rnam-par-thar-pa # 'i don-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
aBiBvAya tana AdInAm karma pUrvavat tad nirdeSa anusAreNa eva yojayitavyam / araNAyAH Adeya vacanaH Bavati para citta anurakzaNa praDAna tayA yaTA anurUpam vacanAt / praNiDi jQAnena bahu mataH ca Bavati lokasya sarvam jAnAti iti gOravita tvAt
# zil-gyis-gnon-pa # 'i skye-mched #  la-sogs-pa # 'i las kyang snga-ma-bzhin-du #  de bstan-pa # 'i tshul du sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # s ni gzhan-gyi-sems #  rjes-su-bsrung-ba #  gces su byed-pa # s ji-ltar-mthun-pa #  bzhin-du #  smra-ba # 'i phyir gzung-ba # 'i tshig tu 'gyur ro / / bsams nas shes-pa # s ni thams-cad #  shes so zhes gus-par #  bya-ba # 'i phyir 'jig-rten #  na mang-po # s bkur-ba # r 'gyur ro /
pratisaMvidBiH deSanayA sattva cittAni saMtozayati bahu vicitrEH prakArEH saMSaya= CedanAt
# so-so #  yang-dag-par #  rig-pa #  rnams kyis ni rnam-pa-sna-tshogs #  mang-po # s the-tshom #  gcod-pa # 'i phyir bshad-pa # s sems-can-rnams-kyi-sems #  tshim par mdzad do /
RdDi divya Srotra para citta jQAna pUrvenivA sacyuti upapadA Asrava kzaya aBijQABiH yaTAkramam kAya karma AdinA SAsane Avarjayati
# rdzu-'phrul #  dang lha'i-rna-ba #  dang gzhan-gyi-sems #  shes-pa #  dang sngon-gyi-gnas #  dang 'chi-'pho-ba #  dang skye-ba #  dang zag-pa-zad-pa # 'i mngon-par-shes-pa #  rnams kyis ni go-rims-bzhin-du #  lus-kyi-las #  la-sogs-pa # s bstan-pa #  la 'dun-pa # r mdzad do /
divya Srotra aBijQayA sarva ruta prakAra aByupapattitaH vAc karmaNA Avarjanam veditavyam
# lha'i-rna-ba # 'i mngon-par-shes-pa # s ni sgra'i rnam-pa-thams-cad #  rtogs-nas #  ngag-gi-las #  kyis 'dun-pa # r mdzad-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
ASraya pariSudDayA yaTAkAmam ASrayasya upAdAna sTAna parityAgAt aDikRtya saMcintya Bava upapatti parigrahaNa AdIni trINi veditavyAni
# gnas-yongs-su-dag-pa # s ni ji-ltar-bzhed-pa #  bzhin-du #  gnas len-pa #  dang bzhugs-pa #  dang yongs-su-gtong-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  srid-pa # r skye-ba #  yongs-su-'dzin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  gsum du rig-par-bya # 'o /
AlaMbana pariSudDayA Darma vaSa vartI Bavati citta pariSudDayA samADi vaSa vartI jQAna pariSudDyA sat Darmam DArayati
# dmigs-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa # s ni chos la dbang sgyur ro / / sems-yongs-su-dag-pa # s ni ting-nge-'dzin-la-dbang #  sgyur ro / / ye shes yongs-su-dag-pa # s ni dam-pa'i-chos #  yang-dag-par #  'dzin to /
balezu dvAByAm balAByAm aByudaya mArga deSayati SezEH niHSreyasa mArgame tAvat ca budDAnAm BagavatAm karaNIyam
# stobs rnams kyi nang nas stobs gnyis kyis ni mngon bar mtho-ba # 'i lam ston to / / lhag-ma #  rnams kyis ni nges-par-legs-pa'i-lam #  ston te / / sangs-rgyas #  bcom-ldan-'das #  rnams kyi mdzad-pa #  ni 'di dag go /
tatra sTAna AsTAna jQAna balena Bagavat nirhetukaH aByudayaH prakRti ISvara Adi hetukaH vA iti evam ahetu vizama hetuvAdam pratikzipati
# de-la #  bcom-ldan-'das #  kyis gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni mngon-par-mtho-ba #  rgyu-med-pa #  las byung-ba #  dang rang-bzhin #  dang dbang-phyug #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu las byung ngo zhes rgyu-med-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa #  rgyur smra-ba #  de spong ngo /
karma svaka tA jQAna balena svayam akRtam api karma AgacCati iti evam akRta aByAgama vAdam pratikzipati yatas samyak aviparItam sugati mArga deSayati
# las-bdag-gir-bya-ba #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni las bdag-gis #  ma byas kyang las 'ong ngo zhes ma-byas-pa #  dang phrad-pa # r smra-ba #  de spong ngo / / 'di-ltar #  yang-dag-par #  ma nor-ba # r bde-'gro # 'i lam ston to /
DyAna vimokza samADi samApatti jQAna balena sattvAnAm citta caritAni cetaH pracarAn anupraviSati
# bsam-gtan #  dang rnam-par-thar-pa #  dang ting-nge-'dzin #  dang snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni sems-can #  gyi sems kyi spyod-pa #  rnams te; sems-kyi-rgyu-ba #  rnams rjes su rtogs so /
indriya parApara jQAna balena deSanA BAjana tAm SradDA indriya paripAkam anupraviSati
# dbang-po #  mchog dang mchog-ma-yin-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni bshad-pa # 'i snod dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i dbang-po #  yongs-su-smin-pa #  rjes su rtogs so /
nAnA aDimukti jQAna balena ASayam hIna praNIta aDimuktika tAm anupraviSati
# mos-pa-sna-tshogs #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni bsam-pa #  ste / / ngan-pa-dang-bzang-po #  la mos-pa #  rjes su rtogs so /
nAnA DAtu jQAna balena anuSaya samudGAtana Sakya kleSa tAm anupraviSati
# khams sna-tshogs #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni bag-la-nyal #  skyed nus-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  rjes su rtogs so /
sarvatra gAminI pratipad jQAna balena alaMkabanam SrAvaka yAnam mahA yAnam vA deSanA Darma saMgRhIta Darmam anupraviSati
# thams-cad-du-'gro-ba # 'i lam mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni dmigs-pa #  nyan-thos-kyi-theg-pa # 'am / / theg-pa-chen-po #  bstan-pa # 'i chos-kyis #  bsdus-pa #  rjes su rtogs so; /
pUrvena vAsa anusmRti jQAna balena saMBAram pUrva janma samudAya gatam Arya mArga hetum anupraviSati / cyuti upapAda jQAna balena Bavya tA mAyatyAm anupraviSati
# sngon-gyi-gnas #  rjes-su-dran-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni tshe-rabs #  snga-ma #  dag na tshogs yang-dag-par-sgrub-pa #  'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyi rgyu rjes su rtogs so / / 'chi-'pho-dang-skye-ba #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni phyi-ma-la #  'os su 'gyur-ba #  rjes su rtogs so /
Asrava kzaya jQAna balena niHsaraNam ca sarvasmAt trEDAtukAt anupraviSati yatas yaTAvat mokza mArga deSayati
# zag-pa-zad-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyis ni 'jig-rten-thams-cad #  nas nges-par-'byung-ba #  rjes su rtogs te / / gang-la # s ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  thar-pa # 'i lam ston to /
bala tvam punar ezAm eBiH skanDa kleSa deva putra maraNa mAra nigrahaNa viSezAt
# stobs nyid ni 'di dag gi phung-po #  dang nyon-mongs-pa #  dang lha'i-bu #  dang 'chi bdag-gi #  bdud tshar-gcod-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyi phyir ro /
viSezaH punar jQeya AvaraNa prahANe api anantarAya kRta tvAt sTAna asTAne yAvat Asrava kzayaH iti sarvatra praSnam pRzwasya praSna vyAkaraNa vyAGAtAt ca
# khyad-par #  ni shes-bya'i-sgrib-pa #  spangs-nas #  bar-chad #  mi-byed-pa #  dang gnas dang gnas-ma-yin-pa #  nas zag-pa-zad-pa #  mkhyen-pa'i-stobs #  kyi bar thams-cad-du #  dri-ba #  dris na dri-ba #  lung-ston-pa #  la thogs-pa-med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vESAradyEH parizadi samyak AtmanaH SAstR tvam Atma para hita pratipanna tvam vyavasTApayati
# mi-'jigs-pa #  rnams kyis ni 'khor-gyi-nang-du #  bdag ston-pa #  yang-dag-pa #  bdag-dang-gzhan #  la phan-pa # r zhugs-pa #  nyid-du #  yang-dag-par #  'jog-pa # 'o /
ca udakAn= ca aBisaMboDO yAvat mArge tIrTyAn saha DarmeNa nigRhNAti
# mngon-pa # r rdzogs-par-byang-chub-pa #  nas lam gyi bar la rgol-ba # 'i mu-stegs-can #  rnams chos-dang-mthun-pas #  tshar gcod do /
smRti upasTAnEH asaMklizwaH gaNam parikarzati SUSrUzamANa Adizu anuyAdi saMkleSa aBAvAt
# dran-pa #  nye-bar-gzhag-pa #  rnams kyis ni gus-par #  nyan-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la rjes-su-chags-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  can ma-yin-pa # s tshogs yongs su sdud do /
arakzyEH nirantaram gaNam avadati samanuSAsti sva doza AvirBAvanA SaMkayA anurakzya aBAvAt
# bsrung-ba #  med-pa #  rnams kyis ni rang-gi #  nyes-pa #  brjod du dogs nas bsrung-ba #  med-pa # 'i phyir rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  tshogs la 'doms so /
asaMmoza Darma tayA budDa kRtyam na hApayati upasTite sattva arTa kRtye pramAdena kzaNam api alaMGanAt
# bsnyel ba med-pa # 'i chos-nyid-kyis #  ni sems-can-gyi-don #  bya-ba #  nye-bar-gnas-pa #  la skad-cig #  tsam yang-ba # g med-pa # s 'gal-ba # r mi mdzad-pa # 'i phyir sangs-rgyas-kyi-mdzad-pa #  mi 'dor ro /
vAsanA samudGAtena niHkleSaH kleSa pratirUpAm cezwAm na darSayati yaTArhan BikzuH sKalita Adikam darSayati
# bag-chags #  legs-par-bcom-pa # s ni de-ltar #  dgra-bcom-pa #  las 'khrul-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  ston-pa #  lta-bu #  ma yin te / / nyon-mongs-pa-med-pa # s / / nyon-mongs-pa #  lta-bu # 'i spyod-pa #  mi ston to /
mahA karuNayA zawkRtvA rAtriMdivasena lokam vyavalokayati kaH hIyate kaH parihIyate iti evamAdiBiH prakArEH pratyavekzaNAt
# thugs-rje-chen-po # s ni su nyams-pa # r 'gyur su 'phel-ba # r 'gyur zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis so-sor-rtog-pa # 'i phyir nyin-mtshan #  lan drug du 'jig-rten #  rnam-pa # r gzigs so /
AveNikAnAm budDa DarmANAm karma asADAraNa kAya vAc manaH karma pariSudDi samRdDO= iti evamAdi lakzaNa nirdeSa aDikAreNa yojanavyam / sarvakArajQa tayA sarva sattvAnAm sarva saMSayAn Cinatti sarvatra avyAhata jQAna tvAt / Darma netrIm ca dIrGa kAlam avasTApayati tatra tatra vineya saMSaya= Cedana arTa deSitAnAm Darma paryAyANAm saMgIti kArEH anukrameNa saMjQApanAt
# sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  ma-'dres-pa #  rnams ni sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi phrin-las #  thun-mong-ma-yin-pa #  yongs-su-dag-pa #  yang-dag-par #  'byor-pa # 'i zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  bstan-pa # 'i skabs bzhin-du #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o / / rnam-pa #  thams mkhyen-pa #  nyid kyis ni thams-cad-du #  ye shes thogs-pa-med-pa # s sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi the-tshom #  gcod do / / the-tshom #  bcad-pa # 'i phyir de-dang-der #  bstan-pa # 'i chos-kyi-rnam-grangs #  rnams yang-dag-par-bsdus-pa # 'i rim-gyis #  yang-dag-par #  bsdus nas chos-kyi-tshul #  yang yun-ring-du #  'jog go /
Darma netrIm nisritya aparipakAH sattvAH paripacyante paripakvAH ca vimucyante
# chos-kyi-tshul #  de-la #  brten-nas #  sems-can #  yongs-su-ma-smin-pa #  rnams ni yongs-su-smin-pa # r mdzad / / yongs-su-smin-pa #  rnams ni rnam-par-grol-ba # r mdzad do /
viSizwa mArga lABe hIna mArga vihAniH tat yaTA Pala saMgRhIta mArga lABe pratipannaka mArgaH vihInaH iti ucyate punar asaMmuKIkaraNAt
# khyad-par-du-'phags-pa # 'i lam thob-nas #  lam dman-pa #  'dor-ba #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / 'bras-bu # s bsdus-pa # 'i lam thob-pa # r gyur na 'jug-pa'i-lam #  rnam-pa # r 'dor zhes bya ste / / yang mngon du mi-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro; /
sakala prahANam ca sAkzAtkaroti Pala prApti kAle tu tad vipakza jAtIya kleSa pratipakza dOzWulya aSeza prahANAt ASraya parivRtti viSeza lABataH samavasarga vihAnyA vijahAti iti antyantA samudAcAram vijahAti iti arTaH
# bsdoms te spong-ba #  yang mngon-sum-du #  byed do zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'bras-bu #  thob-pa # 'i dus te / / de'i mi-mthun-pa # 'i rigs kyi nyon-mongs-pa'i-phyogs #  kyi gnas-ngan-len #  ma-lus-par-spangs-pa # s gnas-gyur-pa # 'i khyad-par-thob-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rgyun yang-dag-par #  gcod-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'dor-ba # s rnam-pa # r spong zhes-bya-ba #  ni gtan-du #  kun du mi-spyod-pa # s rnam-pa # r 'dor zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
naH tu boDisattvaH taTA vijahAti sarva sattva parinirvANa aBiprAya pUrvaka tvAt tad mArgasya
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni de-ltar #  rnam bar spong-ba #  ma yin te / / de'i lam ni sems-can-thams-cad #  yongs su mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # 'i bsam-pa #  sngon-du #  btang-ba # 'i phyir ro /
atas eva boDisattvAH akzaya kuSala mUlAH akzaya guNAH iti ucyante tat yaTA kzam iti sUtre akzaya tA nirdizwA iti
# de'i-phyir #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams ni dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba mi-zad-pa #  dang yon-tan #  mi-zad-pa #  zhes bya ste / / 'di-ltar #  blo-gros #  mi-zad-pa # s bstan-pa # 'i mdo las mi-zad-pa #  bstan-pa #  rnams yin no /
SASvataH loke aSASvataH iti evamAdizu praSnezu avyAkRtavaH tu vyavasTAnam anarTa upasaMhita tvena ayoni SatvAt / tezAm tezAm praSnAnAm kIdRSaH punar praSnaH arTa upasaMhitaH
# 'jig-rten #  rtag-pa # 'o mi-rtag-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'dri-ba #  la lung mi ston-pa # 'i dngos-po #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  ni don-dang-mi-ldan-pa # s tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'dri-ba #  de-dag #  gi 'dri-ba # 'i don-dang-ldan-pa #  ji-lta-bu #  zhe na /
tat yaTA catvAri Arya satyAni AraBya yaH praSnaH
# 'di-lta-ste #  'phags-pa'i-bden-pa-bzhi #  las brtsams nas gang 'dri-ba #  ste /
taTA hi sa hetu Pala saMkleSa vyavadAna cintA antarBUtaH iti
# 'di-ltar #  de rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  dang kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i sems-pa # 'i nang-du #  gtogs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
boDisattvasya nyAm avakrAntO= api SrotA Apanna tva avyavasTAnam apratizWita mArga pratilamBAt pratiSrotaH pratipatti aparinizpanna tAm upAdAya
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i skyon-med-pa #  la zhugs kyang rgyun-du-zhugs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # r rnam-pa # r mi gzhag-pa #  ni mi-gnas-pa # 'i lam thob-pa # s rgyun la 'jug-pa #  yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
jQeyam zaXviDam BrAntiH yAvat aBra anti nizyandaH ca
# shes-bya #  ni rnam-pa-drug #  ste / / 'khrul-ba #  nas ma 'khrul-pa # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /
tatra BrAntiH grAhya grAhaka aBiniveSaH
# de-la #  'khrul-pa #  ni gzung-ba-dang-'dzin-pa # r mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'o /
BrAnti ASrayaH yasmin= Arya jQAH nagocare saMskAra nimitta mAtre aBUta parikalpa Atmake sati bAlAnAm saH aBiniveSaH pravartate
# 'khrul-pa # 'i gnas ni 'phags-pa # 'i ye shes kyi spyod yul 'du-byed #  kyi rgyu tsam yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # r kun du rtog-pa # 'i bdag-nyid #  du gyur ba gang-la #  byis-pa #  rnams gang mngon-par-zhen-pa # s 'jug go /

# 'khrul-pa #  yang yin la ma 'khrul-ba #  yang yin pa ni 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes dang mthun-pa #  thos-pa-las-byung-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams te / / shes-bya #  ba rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes dang mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aBrAntiH nirvikalpa jQAnam
# ma 'khrul-pa #  ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ye shes so /
aBrAnti nizyandaH Arya mArga pRzWa labDAH kuSalAH DarmAH / upAya kOSalyam punar caturviDam / sattva paripAka kOSalyam catvAri saMgraha vastUni tEH saMgRhya kuSalezu Darmezu niyojanAt / budDa Darma paripUraNa kOSalyam prajQApAramitA dAna pAramitAm yAvat sarva AkAra vara jQa tAm paripUrayitu kAmena boDisattvena mahAsattvena asyAm eva prajQApAramitAyAm Sikzitavyam iti vacanAt
# ma 'khrul-pa # 'i rgyu-mthun-pa #  ni 'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyi rjes la thob-pa # 'i dge-ba'i-chos #  rnams so / / thabs-la-mkhas-pa #  ni rnam-pa-bzhi #  ste / / sems-can #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r bya-ba #  la mkhas-pa #  ni bsdu-ba'i-dngos-po-bzhi #  ste / / de-dag #  gis bsdus nas dge-ba #  rnams la 'dzud-pa # 'i phyir ro / / sangs-rgyas-kyi-chos #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r bya-ba #  la mkhas-pa #  ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  ste / / sbyin-pa # 'i pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  nas / / rnam-pa-thams-cad #  mkhyen-pa #  nyid kyi bar-du #  yongs-su-rdzogs-pa # r byed-par-'dod-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sems-dpa'-che # n pos shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  'di nyid la bslab-pa # r bya'o zhes gsungs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kzipra aBijQa tA kOSalyam zawkRtvA rAtri divasam pApa pratideSanA puNya anumodanA budDa aDyezaNA kuSala mUla pariNAmanA ca yaTAkramam Arya mEtreya paripRcCAyAm
# mngon-par-shes-pa #  myur-ba #  la mkhas-pa # s ni nyid mtshan lan drug tu sdig-pa #  bshags pa dang bsod nams la rjes-su-yi-rang-ba #  dang; sangs-rgyas #  la gsol-ba-btab-pa #  dang dge-ba # 'i rtsa ba yongs-su-bsngo-ba #  ste / / 'phags-pa #  byams-pa # s zhus-pa #  las ji-skad #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
DarmAn upacCeda kOSalyam ca apratizWita nirvANa tayA punar panara anuparatam atyantam ca samantAt lokaDAtuzu yaTAvineyam budDa boDisattva caryA saMdarSanAt iti / aBUta parikalpaH daSaviDaH / tatra mUla vikalpaH Alaya vijQAnam sarva vikalpAnAm bIja BUta tvAt
# lam rgyun-mi-'chad-pa # 'i mkhas-pa #  ni mi-gnas-pa # 'i mya-ngan-las-'das-pa # s phyir zhing rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  gtan-du #  'jig-rten-gyi-khams #  kun du 'dul pa ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  sangs-rgyas #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i spyod-pa #  kun du ston-pa # 'i phyir ro / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i kun du rtog-pa #  ni rnam-pa-bcu #  ste / / rtsa ba'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni kun-gzhi # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  ste / / rnam-par-rtog-pa #  thams-cad-kyi #  sa-bon-du-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nimitta vikalpaH deha pratizWA Boga pratiBAsA vijQaptayaH grAhya nimitta BUta tvAt
# mtshan-ma # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni lus dang gnas dang longs-spyod #  kyi rnam-par-rig-pa #  ste / / gzung-ba #  dang mtshan-ma # r gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tAH punar yaTAkramam rUpi indriya BAjana loka rUpa Adi vizaya lakzaNAH drazwavyAH
# de-dag #  ni dbang-po-gzugs-can #  dang snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  dang gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i yul gyi mtshan-nyid #  dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  blta-bar-bya # 'o /
nimitta pratiBAsasya vikalpaH zaX vijQAnakAyAH manaH ca yaTA ukta grAhya nimitta AkAra tvAt
# mtshan-ma # r snang-ba # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i tshogs drug dang yid de gzung-ba # 'i mtshan-ma #  ji-skad-du #  bshad-pa # 'i rnam-par-gyur-pa # 'i phyir ro /
nimitta vikAra vikalpaH yaTA ukta deha Adi nimittasya anyaTA tvena utpAdaH
# mtshan-ma # r gyur-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni ji-skad #  bshad-pa # 'i lus la sogs ba'i mtshan-ma # 'i rnam-pa #  gzhan-du #  bskyed-pa # 'o /
nimitta pratiBAsa vikAra vikalpaH yaTA uktasya cakzarvi jQAna Adi nimitta pratiBAsasya suKa Adi avasTA antareNa utpAdaH
# mtshan-ma # r snang-ba # r 'gyur-ba'i-rnam-pa # r rtog-pa #  ni mig gi rnam-par-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mtshan-ma # r snang-ba #  ji-skad-du #  bstan-pa #  dag bde-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i gnas-skabs #  gzhan-du #  bskyed-pa # 'o /
para upanItaH vikalpaH deSanA saMgRhIta nAma pada vyaQjana kAya lakzaNaH
# gzhan gyis bstan-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni bstan-pa # r bsdus-pa # 'i ming dang tshig-dang-yi-ge # 'i tshogs kyi mtshan-nyid #  do /
sa punar dviviDaH durAKyAta Darma vinaya AtmakaH sva AKyA Darma vinaya AtmakaH ca
# de-la #  yang rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / nyes-par-bshad-pa # 'i chos-kyi-tshul #  gyi bdag-nyid #  dang legs-par #  bshad-pa # 'i chos-kyi-tshul #  gyi bdag-nyid #  do /
atas tad aDipateyam anaskAra saMgRhItO yaTAkramam yoni Soka vikalpaH ayoni aSOvikalpaH ca veditavyaH
# de'i-phyir #  de'i dbang-du-byas-pa #  yid-la-byed-pa # s bsdus-pa #  tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang tshul-bzhin #  gyi rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
aBiniveSa vikalpaH ayoni SovikalpA dvAzazwi dRzwi gata saMgRhItaH yaH vikalpaH / vikzepa vikalpaH yoniSas vikalpAt aBAva Adi grAha lakzaNaH yaH vikalpaH
# mngon-par-zhen-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  las lta-ba # r song-ba #  drug cu rtsa gnyis su bsdus-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o / / rnam-pa # r g-yeng ba'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ni tshul-bzhin #  dang tshul-bzhin #  gyi rnam-par-rtog-pa #  las dngos-po-med-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  'dzin-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kyi rnam-par-rtog-pa #  gang-yin-pa # 'o /
sa punar daSaviDaH aBAva vikalpaH yAvat yaTArTa nAma vikalpaH ca
# de-yang #  rnam-pa-bcu #  ste / / dngos-po-med-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  nas don ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  ming du rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o /

# rnam-par-rtog-pa #  'di bcu ni shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  las thog-mar #  bstan-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya #  ste /
yaTA uktam iha SAriputra boDisattvaH boDisattvaH eva san boDisattvam na samanupaSyati
# ji-skad-du #  sh'a ri'i bu 'di-la #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  nyid yod-bzhin-du #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong /
boDisattva nAma na samanupaSyati / prajQApAramitAm na samanupaSyati / boDim na samanupaSyati / carati iti na samanupaSyati / na carati iti na samanupaSyati / taTA hi nAma svaBAvena SUnyam na SUnyatayA rUpam svaBAvena SUnyam na SUnyatayA yAvat vijQAnam svaBAvena SUnyam na SUnyatayA / tat kasya hetoH
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i ming yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong / / shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong / / byang-chub #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong / / spyod ces bya-ba # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong / / mi spyod ces bya-ba # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong-ste #  / / 'di-ltar #  ming ni ming gi ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  stong ste / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyis ni stong-pa #  ma yin no / / gzugs ni ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  stong ste / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyis ni stong-pa #  ma yin no / / rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  ni stong ste / / stong-pa-nyid #  kyis ni stong-pa #  ma yin no / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  /
yAH rUpasya SUnyatA na tat rUpam na api anyatra rUpAt SanyatA rUpam eva SUnyatAH SUnyatA eva rUpam evam yAvat vijQAnam / tat kasya hetoH
# gzugs kyi stong-pa-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de gzugs ma yin no / / stong-pa-nyid #  las gzugs gzhan ma yin no / / gzugs nyid stong-pa-nyid #  do / / stong-pa-nyid #  gzugs so / / de-bzhin-du #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  /
nAma mAtram idam yat uta boDisattvanAma iti boDisattvaH iti prajQApAramitA iti boDiH iti rUpam iti yAvat vijQAnam iti
# 'di-lta-ste #  / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i ming zhes-bya-ba #  dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  dang byang-chub #  ces bya-ba #  dang gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  nas rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar 'di ni ming tsam ste /
svaBAvasya hi na utpAdaH na niroDaH na saMkleSaH na vyavadAnam

prajQApAramitAyAm caran boDisattvaH utpAdam api na samanupaSyati yAvat vayavadAnam api na samanupaSyati / tat kasya hetoH
# shes-rab #  kyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la spyod-pa # 'i byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni skye-ba #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong-ba #  nas / / rnam-par-byang-ba # 'i bar-du #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong ngo / / de-ci'i-phyir-zhe-na #  /
kRtrimam nAma prati te DarmAH kalpitAH Agantukena nAmnA anuvyavahriyante / yaTA yaTA anuvyava hriyante taTA taTA aBiniviSanti
# ming bcos-ma #  la chos de-dag #  so-sor-brtags-nas #  / / glo-bur-gyi-ming #  gis rjes su tha-snyad-'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ji-lta-ji-lta # r rjes su tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  de-lta-de-ltar #  mngon-pa # r zhen to /
tAni boDisattvaH sarva nAmAni na samanupaSyati asamanupaSyan= aBiniviSate
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni ming thams-cad #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong ngo / / yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong-ba # s mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med do /
tatra aBAva vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha boDisattvaH boDisattvaH eva sanniti evamAdi sat Sabdasya BAva arTa tvAt
# de-la #  dngos-po-med-pa #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  nyid-du #  yod do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs te / / yod-pa # 'i sgra ni dngos-po # 'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
