# dngos-po # r rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong-ba #  nas / / mi spyod do zhes-bya-ba # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong ngo zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  gsungs te / / gang-zag #  dang chos kyi dngos-po #  bkag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
samAropa vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha taTA hi nAma svaBAvena SUnyam iti aBUta parikalpasya svaBAva pratizeDAt
# sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r 'di-ltar #  ming ni ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  stong ngo zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / yang-dag-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'i kun du brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  bkag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
apavAda vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha na SUnyatayA iti tasmin= Amni tena parikalpitena parikalpita svaBAvena virahita tAyAH sarvadA astitvAt / ekatva vikalpa prati pakzENa Aha yA rUpasya SUnya tA na tat rUpam yAvat vijQAnam iti BAva antara tvAt
# skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r stong-pa-nyid #  kyis ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / ming de kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  de dang bral-ba-nyid #  du thams-cad-du #  yod-pa # 'i phyir ro / / gcig pa nyid-du #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r gzugs kyi stong-pa-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de gzugs ma yin no zhes-bya-ba #  nas rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i stong-pa-nyid #  gang-yin-pa #  de rnam-par-shes-pa #  ma yin no zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  gsungs te /
rUpa AdayaH hi parikalpitaH svaBAvaH SUnyatA parinizpannaH iti / pRTakatva vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha na api anyatra rUpAt SUnyatAyAH rUpam yAvat SanyatA eva vijQAnam iti parikalpita svaBAvasyA lakzaNa tvAt tat vyatirekeNa tat BAs vAsaMBavataH
# ngo-bo-nyid #  gzhan ma-yin-pa # 'i phyir gzugs la-sogs-pa #  ni kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  do / / stong-pa-nyid #  ni yongs-su-grub-pa # 'o / / tha-dad-pa #  nyid-du #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r stong-pa-nyid #  las gzugs gzhan-pa #  yang ma yin no / / gzugs nyid stong-pa-nyid #  do / / stong-pa-nyid #  gzugs so zhes-bya-ba #  nas rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du #  gsungs te / / kun-brtags-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  yin-pas #  /
svaBAva vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha nAma mAtram idam yat uta rUpam iti yAvat vijQAnam iti aBilApa vyatirekeNa aBilApya svaBAva aBAvAt
# de-la # s ma-gtogs-par #  de med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / ngo-bo-nyid #  du rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r 'di-lta-ste #  / / gzugs zhes-bya-ba #  nas rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar 'di ni ming tsam mo zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te / / brjod-pa #  las ma-gtogs-par #  brjod-pa'i-ngo-bo-nyid #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
viSeza vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha svaBAvasya na utpAdaH yAvat vayavadAnam api na samanupaSyati iti utpAda Adi viSeza lakzaNa pratizeDAt
# khyad-par #  du rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  mi skye zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / rnam-par-byang-ba #  yang yang-dag-par #  rjes su ma mthong ngo zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  gsungs te / / skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i khyad-par #  gyi mtshan-nyid #  bkag-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA nAma arTa vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha kRtrimam nAma prati te DarmAH kalpitAH Agantukena nAmnA vyavahriyante iti evamAdi Adi te
# ming ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  don-du #  rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r ming bcos-ma #  la chos de-dag #  so-sor-brtags-nas #  glo-bur-gyi-ming #  gis rjes su tha-snyad-'dogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs so /
yaTArTa nAma vikalpa pratipakzeNa Aha tAni boDisattvaH sarva nAmAni na samanu paSyan= aBiniviSate iti yaTArTam nAmnA adarSana aBiniveSAt / nirvikalpanAt triDA saMtuzwi nirvikalpana AdiBiH
# don ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  ming du rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i gnyen-po # r byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i ming de-dag #  thams-cad #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su mi mthong do / / yang-dag-par #  rjes su ma-mthong-ba # s mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med do zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs te; don ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  ming du mi mthong na mngon-par-zhen-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ni rnam-pa-gsum #  ste /
tatra pRTagjanAH yadi anitya tA AdikAm kAMcid eva Darma tAm AraBya citta paryavasAnam nItvA labDa paritozAH Bavanti evam etat iti niScinvantaH sA tezAm saMtuzwi nirvikalpa tA iti ucyate tatra sarva tarka AKya vikalpa uparateH
# chog-par-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / de-la #  so-so'i-skye-bo #  rnams ni gang mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  chos-nyid #  'ga' zhig las brtsams nas sems-pa #  mthar khrid de / / 'di ni de-bzhin #  no zhes nges-par #  'byed cing yongs su tshim pa thob-par-byed-pa # r 'gyur te / / de-dag #  gi de ni chog-par-'dzin-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  nyid ces bya ste / / de-la #  mi-rtog-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni rnam-par-rtog-pa #  thams-cad #  rgyun bcad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
SrAvakAH skanDezu nitya Adi viparyAsa pratipakzeNa yaTAvat rUpa Adikam DarmaDAtum parIkzamANAH lokottareNa jQAnena nErAtmyam prativiDyanti atas sA tezAm aviparyAsa nirvikalpa tA iti ucyate / boDisattvAH tat api rUpa Adi Darma mAtram prapaQcaH iti viditvA sarva Darma nimittAni viBAvayantaH parama SAntena lokottareNa jQAnena sarvatragAm taTatAm prativiDyanti atas sA tezAm nizprapaQca nirvikalpata iti ucyate / kaTam punar asO nizprapaQca nirvikalpa tA iti ucyate
# nyan-thos #  rnams ni phung-po #  rnams la rtag-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  phyin-ci-log #  gi gnyen-po # r ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  gzugs la-sogs-pa #  la chos tsam du yongs su brtags-pa # s 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i shes-pa # s bdag-med-pa # r rtogs te / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  gi ni de phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ces bya'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  chos tsam de-yang #  spros-pa # r rig-nas #  chos-thams-cad #  kyi mtshan-ma #  rnam-pa # r bshig ste / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i ye shes mchog-tu #  zhi-ba # s de-bzhin-nyid #  thams-cad-du-'gro-ba #  rtogs te / / de'i-phyir #  de-dag #  gi de ni spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ces bya'o / / ji-ltar #  na de spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  zhes bya zhe na gal-te #  yid-la-byed-pa #  med-pa # s de-skad #  bya-ba #  ni /
yadi amanaskArataH tena supta matta AdInAm nirvikalpa tA prasaFgaH tezAm Darma nimitta amana skArAt
# des-na #  gnyid-kyis-log-pa #  dang ra ro pha la-sogs-pa #  yang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur te / / de-dag #  la chos-kyi-mtshan-ma #  yid-la-byed-pa #  med-pa # 'i phyir ro /
aTa samatikramataH tena dvitIya DyAnAt praBRti sarvatra nirvikalpa tA prApnoti vitarka vicAra vikalpAnAm samatikramAt tatas ca vikalpasya SarIram hi citta cEttAH trEDAtukAH iti asya viroDaH
# ji ste yang-dag-par-'das-pa # s de-skad #  bya na ni des-na #  bsam-gtan-gnyis-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  thams-cad #  kyang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur te / / rtog-pa-dang-dpyod-pa # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  rnams las yang-dag-par-'das-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-phyir #  na rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i lus ni khams-gsum-pa # 'i sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni 'di dang 'gal lo / / ji ste rnam-par-zhi-ba # s de-skad #  bya na ni /
aTa vyupaSamataH tena saMjQA vedita niroDa samApattiH nivikalpa tA prApnoti tatra citta cEtavikalpa vyupaSamAt tatas ca jQAna aBAvaH prasajyate / aTa svaBAvataH tena rUpam nirvikalpatA prApnoti tasya avikalpa svaBAva tvAt
# des-na #  'du-shes-dang-tshor-ba #  'gog-pa # 'i snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  yang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur te / / der sems dang sems-las-byung-ba # 'i rnam-par-rtog-pa #  rnam-par-zhi-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de'i-phyir #  shes-pa #  med-pa # r 'gyur ro / / ji ste ngo-bo-nyid-kyis #  de-skad #  bya na ni / / des-na #  gzugs kyang rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur te / / de rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'i ngo-bo-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro / / ji ste dmigs-pa #  la mngon bar 'du-byed #  pa med-pa # s de-skad #  bya na ni /
aTa alaMbane aBisaMskAraH tena sa vikalpatA eva nirvikalpa tA prApnoti nirvikalpam etat iti etasya aBisaMskArasya nimitta vikalpa lakzaNa tvAt
# des rnam-par-rtog-pa #  dang bcas-pa #  nyid rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  'gyur te / / 'di ni rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa # 'o zhes mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  'di ni mtshan-ma #  la rnam-par-rtog-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  yin pa'i phyir ro /
tasmAt nEBiH prakArEH nirvikalpa tA drazwavyA / api tu AlaMbane anaBisaMskAra tA adrazwavyA / kaTam kRtvA
# de-lta-bas-na #  rnam-pa #  de-dag #  gis rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid-du #  mi blta ste / / 'on-kyang #  dmigs-pa #  la mngon-par-'du-byed-pa #  med-pa #  nyid-du #  blta'o /
yadA hi asya boDisattvasya Anulomikam avavAdam Agamya prakRtyA sarva Darma nimittAni aparinizpannAni iti vicArayataH tad vicAraNa aByAsa bala ADAnAt pratyAtmam anaBisaMskAreNa eva yaTAvat nizpaQcaDAtO sarva Darma taTatAyAm cittam samADIyate sA asO= ucyate nizprapaQca nirvikalpata iti
# ji-ltar #  zhe na gang-gi-tshe #  byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rjes-su-mthun-pa #  nyid kyi gdams pa la brten-nas #  / / chos-thams-cad #  kyi mtshan-ma #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  yongs-su-ma-grub-pa # r rnam-par-rtog-pa #  ste / / rnam-par-rtog-pa #  de-la #  goms-pa'i-stobs #  bskyed-pa # s so-so #  rang-gis #  mngon bar 'du-byed #  pa med-pa #  nyid kyis ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i chos-kyi-dbyings #  chos-thams-cad #  kyi de-bzhin-nyid #  la sems-mnyam-pa # r 'jog ste /
prakRtyA tIkzNa indriyaH boDisattvaH iti uktam prAk kaTam tena kAlena kAlam indriyANi uta apayitavyAni iti ucyate
# de ni de'i spros-pa #  med-pa # 'i rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  nyid ces bya'o / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  ni rang-bzhin-gyis #  dbang-po-rnon-po #  zhes sngar bshad na / / de ji-ltar #  dus-dus-su #  dbang-po #  rnams sbyang-ba # r bya zhe na /
sva jAtIyAnAm mRdu Adi trEviDyAt uttara uttara aBinirhArataH tat uttApanam veditavyam
# rang-gi-rigs #  kyi dbang-po-rtul-po #  la-sogs-pa #  rnam-pa-gsum #  gyis gong-nas-gong-du #  mngon-pa # r bsgrubs-pa # s de sbyar-ba # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
anyaTA tIkzNa indriya gotrANAm indriyANAm ekaviDye sati boDisattvAnAm indriya kRtaH viSezaH na eva upalaByate
# gzhan-du-na #  dbang-po-rnon-po # 'i rigs rnams kyi dbang-po #  rnams rnam-pa #  gcig-tu #  gyur na ni / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyi dbang-po # r gyur-pa # 'i khyad-par #  mi dmigs-pa # r 'gyur na /
sa ca upalaByate iti / sAMkaTya viniScayaH nAma paQcamaH samuccayaH
# de-yang #  dmigs-pa #  de'i-phyir #  ji-skad #  bshad-pa #  de grub bo / / bo ma po bcu pa ste tha-ma # 'o /
saptaviDa sAMkaTya viniScaye arTa viniScayaH svaBAva arTa AdIn zaXarTAn AraBya veditavyaH
# 'bel-ba'i-gtam #  gyi rnam-par-nges-pa #  bdun la don rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi don la-sogs-pa #  don drug las brtsams par rig-par-bya # 'o /
tatra / svaBAvaH trayaH svaBAvAH parikalpitaH paratantraH parinizpannaH ca / hetu arTaH trayaH hetavaH
# de-la #  ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi don ni ngo-bo-nyid #  gsum ste / / kun-brtags-pa #  dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs-su-grub-pa # 'o / / rgyu'i don ni rgyu gsum ste / / skye-ba'i-rgyu #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
utpatti hetuH taTA hetu samanantara alaMkbana aDipati pratyayAH tatas sarva saMskRta nirvartanAt
# rgyu dang de-ma-thag-pa #  dang dmigs-pa #  dang bdag-po'i-rkyen #  rnams te / / de-la #  'dus byas thams-cad #  grub-pa # 'i phyir ro / / 'byung-ba # 'i rgyu ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
pravRtti hetuH tad yaTA vidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH yAvat samudayaH niroDaH ca Bavati iti etayA AnupUrvyA saMkleSa vyavadAna pravRtteH tat yaTA vidleSa vyavadAna pravRtteH
# ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas kun-'byung-ba # r 'gyur-ba #  dang 'gag-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar 'dis mthar-gyis #  kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro /
sidDi hetuH pratyakza upalamBa anupalamBa samAKyAna saMgRhItaH tena sADyasya apratItasya arTasya sADanAt
# 'grub-pa'i-rgyu #  ni mngon-sum-du #  dmigs-pa #  dang mi dmigs-pa #  mtshungs-pa #  sro bsnyad-pa # s bsdus-pa # s te / / des bsgrub-pa # r ma grags-pa # 'i don sgrub-pa # 'i phyir ro /
Pala arTaH paQca PalAni
# 'bras-bu # 'i don ni 'bras-bu #  lnga ste /
vipAka Palam tat yaTA Alaya vijQAnam
# rnam-par-smin-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / kun-gzhi #  rnam-par-shes-pa # 'o /
nizpanda Palam tat yaTA pUrva utpannAnAm kuSala AdInAm DarmANAm tad sAntAnikAH uttara kuSala AdayaH DarmAH
# rgyu-mthun-pa'i-'bras-bu #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sdar skyes-pa # 'i dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi de'i rgyu-las-byung-ba #  dge-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  chos phyi-ma #  rnams so /
aDipati Palam tat yaTA sarva sattva sADAraNam karma ADipatyena BAjana lokaH
# bdag-po'i-'bras-bu #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / sems-can-thams-cad #  kyi thun mong gi las kyi dbang gis snod-kyi-'jig-rten #  no /
puruzakAra Palam tat yaTA sasya AdayaH visaMyoga Palam tat yaTA Arya mArgeNa anuSaya samudGAtaH
# skyes-bu #  byed-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / lo-tog #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / bral-ba'i-'bras-bu #  ni 'phags-pa'i-lam #  gyi bag-la-nyal #  legs-par-bcom-pa # 'o /
karma arTaH pUrvavat drazwavyaH tat yaTA karma saMkleSa nirdeSe / yoga arTaH paQca yogAH sAmUhikaH yogaH tat yaTA gRha kAzWa izwaka AdInAm
# las kyi don ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / las kyi kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  bstan-pa # 'o / / ldan-pa'i-don #  ni rnam-pa-lnga #  ste / / mang-po #  las gyur-pa # 'i ldan-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / khang-pa # 'i shing dang pha gu la-sogs-pa # 'o /
AnubanDikaH yogaH tat yaTA anuSaya Adi hetuH taTA hi tasmin satya samudAcaradBiH api kleSa AdiBiH yuktaH iti ucyate / sa ambanDikaH yogaH tat yaTA sva janmanAm parasparam / AvasTikaH yogaH tat yaTA anugraha AdyAH saMtAna vyavasTAH taTA hi tAsu vartamAnaH suKena yuktaH yAvat duHKa asuKena yuktaH iti ucyate
# rjes su 'ching-ba #  las gyur-pa # 'i ldan-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / bag-la-nyal-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyu ste / / 'di-ltar #  de yod-na #  kun du mi spyod kyang nyon-mongs-pa #  sogs-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'brel-pa # r gyur-pa # 'i ldan-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / rang-gi #  skye-bo #  rnams phan tshun 'brel-pa # 'o / / gnas-skabs #  las gyur-pa # 'i ldan-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  / / phan-'dogs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems-kyi-rgyud #  kyi gnas-skabs #  te; / / 'di-ltar #  de'i 'phral du bde-ba-dang-ldan-pa #  nas / / sdug-bsngal #  yang ma yin bde-ba #  yang ma-yin-pa # 'i bar-du #  ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  / / 'gyur-ba #  las gyur-pa # 'i ldan-pa #  ni 'di-lta-ste #  /
vEkArikaH yogaH Agantu kopa kleSa Adika saMmuKIBAvaH taTA hi tasmin sati rAga AdiBiH SradDA AdiBiH ca yuktaH iti ucyate
# glo-bur #  gyi nye-ba'i-nyon-mongs-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  mngon-du-gyur-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / de yod-na #  'dod-chags #  la-sogs-pa #  dang dad-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
vRtti arTaH paQca vRttayaH / lakzaNa vRttiH saMskRtasya trINi lakzaNAni utpAda AdIni tEH prakArEH vartanAt / avasTAna vRtti rAtreyasya ADAre vyavasTAnam / viparyAsa vRttiH sAMkleSikAnAm DarmANAm ayaTABUtam vartanAt / aviparyAsa vRttiH vyavadAnikAnAm DarmANAm
# 'jug-pa'i-don #  ni 'jug-pa #  lnga ste / / mtshan-nyid #  la 'jug-pa #  ni skye-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  'dus-byas-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  gsum ste / / de-dag #  gi rnam-pa # r 'byung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / rten la 'jug-pa #  ni rten la gnas-par-bya-ba #  gnas-pa #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  sa la sems-can #  rnams so / / phyin-ci-log #  gi 'jug-pa #  ni kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  te / / yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba #  bzhin ma-yin-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro / / phyin-ci-log #  ma-yin-pa # 'i 'jug-pa #  ni 'phags-pa'i-lam #  ste / / de phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro / / rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i 'jug-pa #  ni chos-rnams #  kyi rnam-pa-tha-dad-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  ste /
praBeda vRttiH sarva saMskArANAm atIta anAgata pratyutpanna ADyAtmika bAhya Adi prakArEH vartanAt
# 'di-ltar #  'du-byed-thams-cad #  'das-pa #  dang ma-'ongs-pa #  dang da-ltar-byung-ba #  dang nang dang phyi la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa # r 'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vyAKyA viniScayaH yena sUtrAntAnAm arTam nirdiSati
# rnam-pa # r bshad-pa #  rnam-pa # r des-pa #  ni gang-gis #  mdo-sde #  rnams kyi don ston-pa #  ste /
sa punar parijQeya vastu AdInAm zazNAm arTAnAm pratisUtram yaTAsaMBavam pratipAdanAt
# de-yang #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  la-sogs-pa #  don drug-po #  dag mdo-sde #  so-so # r ji-ltar #  mthun mthun du ston-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra parijQeyam vastu skanDa Adi
# de-la #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  ni phung-po #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
parijQeyaH arTaH anitya tA Adi
# yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i don ni mi-rtag-pa-nyid #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
parijQA upanizad SIla indriya gupta dvAra tA Adi
# yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i rgyu ni tshul-khrims #  dang dbang-po # 'i sgo bsdams-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
parijQAH boDi pakzyAH DarmAH
# yongs-su-shes-pa #  ni byang-chub-kyi-phyogs #  kyi chos-rnams #  so /
parijQA Palam vimuktiH / tat pravedanA vimukti jQAna darSanam iti / api Kalu caturdaSa muKAni vyAKyAyAH
# yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # 'o / / de rab-tu-shes-pa #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i ye-shes-mthong-ba # 'o / / yang rnam-pa # r bshad-pa # 'i sgo bcu bzhi ste /
vyAKyA saMgraha muKam yatra sUtrasya utpatti prayojanam padArTaH anusanDiH aBiprAyaH ca udya parihAraH ca varNyate / vastu saMgraha muKam yatra sUtra muKam SikzA Arya satyavaH tu Adizu pratipAdyate
# rnam-pa # r bshad-pa #  bsdu-ba # 'i sgo ni gang na mdo-sde #  'byung-ba # 'i dgos-pa #  dang tshig gi don dang mtshams sbyar-ba #  dang dgongs-pa #  dang brgal-ba #  dang lan brjod-pa # 'o / / dngos-po #  bsdu-ba # 'i sgo ni gang na mdo-sde #  bslab-pa #  dang 'phags-pa'i-bden-pa #  dang dngos-po #  la-sogs-pa # r ston-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / sdig-pa #  thams-cad #  mi bya ste / / dge-ba #  phun-sum-tshogs-pa # r bya / / rang-gi-sems #  ni yongs su 'dul /
tat yaTA sarva pApasya akaraNam iti gATA tisraH SikzAm aDikRtya iti evamAdi
# 'di ni sangs-rgyas #  bstan-pa # 'o / / zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  bslab-pa-gsum #  gyi dbang-du-byas-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
aFga upAFga muKam yatra ekena padena uddeSaH SezEH nirdeSaH iti pradarSyate
# yan-lag #  dang nye-ba # 'i yan-lag #  gi sgo ni gang-du #  tshig gcig gis bstan-pa #  la lhag-ma #  rnams kyis bshad do zhes rab tu ston-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA dvAdaSa kzaraNa saMnipAta deSanAyAm Atma sampad para sampad iti anayoH dvayoH yaTAkramam paQcaBiH paQcaBiH uttarEH padEH nideSaH iti / uttara uttara nirhAra muKam yatra uttarasya uttarasya aBinirharaNa ASraya tvAt ete DarmAH evam deSitAH iti pradarSyate / tat yaTA paQca indriyANi / taTA hi SraddaDAnaH vIryam AraBate ArabDa vIryasya smRtiH upatizWate upasTita smRteH citam samADIyate samAhita cittaH yaTABUtam prajAnAti iti / pratikzepa muKam yatra idam AraBya idam pratikzipyate iti pradarSyate / tat yaTA vA asya Opamya sUtre Asrava kzayam AraBya catvAraH pudgalAH pratikzipyante
# dper-na #  dal 'byor phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  bcu gnyis bstan-pa #  las bdag phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  dang gzhan phun-sum-tshogs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshig 'di gnyis go-rims-bzhin-du #  tshig 'og ma lnga lngas bshad-pa #  lta-bu #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  mi-nyid #  dang yul-dbus-su-skyes-pa #  dang dbang-po #  rnams ma-tshang-ba-med-pa #  dang las-kyi-mtha' #  smin-pa # r ma-gyur-pa #  dag gnas-su-gyur-pa #  la dad-pa #  dang sangs-rgyas-rnams-'byung-ba #  dang dam-pa'i-chos-ston-pa #  dang bstan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  gnas-pa #  dang gnas-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  kyi rjes-su-'jug-pa #  dang gzhan la snying brtse ba'o / / gong-nas-gong-du #  mngon-pa # r bsgrub-pa # 'i sgo ni gong-du #  'og ma ni gong-ma #  la mngon bar bsgrub-pa # 'i gnas yin pa'i phyir chos de-dag #  ni de-ltar #  bstan to zhes ston-pa # 'o / / dper-na #  dbang-po-lnga #  po rnams te 'di-ltar #  dang na brtson 'grus brtsom mo / / brtson 'grus brtsams na dran-pa #  nye-bar #  gnas so / / dran ba nye-bar #  gnas na sems-mnyam-pa # r 'jog go / / sems-mnyam-pa # r bzhag na yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu shes so zhes-bya'o #  / / spong-ba # 'i sgo ni 'di-las #  brtsams nas 'di spong-ba # r ston-pa #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  /
itas bAhyakaH ihaDArmikaH Sruta cintA mAtra saMtuzwaH BAvanAyAm paritasyamAnaH aparipUrNa saMBAraH ca / jAnataH ca aham BikzavaH paSyataH ca AsravANAm kzayam vadAmi iti evamAdinA sUtra KaNXena AdyaH pudgalaH pratikziptaH
# ste'u yu lta-bu # 'i mdo las zag-pa-zad-pa #  las brtsams nas 'di-las #  phyi-rol-pa #  dang chos 'di ba thos-pa #  dang sems-pa #  tsam gyis chog-par-'dzin-pa #  dang bsgom-pa # s yongs su yi chad-pa #  dang tshogs yongs-su-ma-rdzogs-pa # 'o / / dge slong dag nga ni shes-bzhin #  mthong bzhin-du #  zag-pa #  rnams zad-pa # r smra'o zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mdo'i-tshig #  gi dum-bu # s dang-po # 'i gang-zag #  spangs so /
BAvanA yogam anuyuktasya iti evamAdinA dvitIyaH
# sgom-pa # r sbyor-ba #  la brtson pa zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni gnyis-pa #  spangs so /
vAsyA Opamya dRzwAntena tRtIyaH / nOdRzwAntena caturTaH iti
# ste yu'i dpes ni gsum-pa #  spangs so / / gru'i dpas ni bzhi-pa #  spangs so /
akzara paNima muKam yatra anyasmin= arTe prasidDAni akzarANi anyasmin pariNAmyante / tat yaTASradDaH ca akRtajQaH ca iti gATAyAm
# yi-ge #  yongs su sgyur ba'i sgo ni gang-du #  don gzhan la rab tu grub-pa # 'i yi-ge #  rnams gzhan-du #  yongs-su-bsgyur-ba #  ste / / dper-na #  mi gang ma dad byas mig za / / zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  lta-bu # 'o /
nASa anASamuKam tatra praNAhaH apraNASaH tad uBaya upAyaH tad uBaya praBedaH ca pradarSyate
# chud-za-ba #  dang chud-mi-za-ba # 'i sgo ni gang-du #  rab tu chud-za-ba #  dang rab tu chud-mi-za-ba #  dang de-gnyi-ga # 'i thabs dang de-gnyi-ga # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba #  ston-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA sujAta sUtre praNASaH bAhya ADyAtmika upaDi avasAnam
# dper-na #  legs-par #  skyes kyi mdo las rab tu chud-za-ba #  ni phyi dang nang gi rdzas la lhag-par-chags-pa # 'o /
tatra bAhyaH upaDiH gRha kalatra Adi lakzaNaH ADyAtmikaH paQca upAdAna skanDa lakzaNaH
# de-la #  phyi'i rdzas ni khyim-dang-chung-ma #  la-sogs-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  do / / nang gi rdzas ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga'i mtshan-nyid #  do /
apraNASaH tad uBaya aDyavasAna vigamaH
# rab tu chud-mi-za-ba #  ni de-gnyi-ga # l lhag-par-chags-pa #  dang bral-ba # 'o /
praNASa upAyaH apravrajanam pravrajitasya ca asra vakzayam prati pramAdaH
# rab tu chud-za-ba # 'i thabs ni rab tu mi-'byung-ba #  dang rab tu byung nas kyang zag-pa-zad-pa # r bya-ba #  la bag mi-byed-pa # 'o /
viparyayAt aprakASa upAyaH drazwavyaH
# de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni chud-mi-za-ba # 'i thabs su blta-bar-bya # 'o /
tatra uBayatas vatA ayam sujAtaH kula putraH SoBate yat ca keSa SmaSrUNi avahArya yAvat pravrajitaH yat ca AsravANAm kzayAt yAvat prajAnAm iti anena aprakASa tad upAya apadeSena tad viparIta lakzaNa praNASa tad upAyO sUcitO BavataH
# de-la #  kye-ma #  rigs-kyi-bu #  legs-par #  skyes 'di ni gnyis kyis mdzes te / / gang skra dang kha sphu bregs nas rab-tu-byung-ba # 'i bar dang gang-zag #  pa zad nas rab tu shes so zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar 'dis chud-mi-za-ba #  dang de'i thabs nye-bar #  bstan-pa # s de-las-bzlog-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  chud-za-ba #  dang de'i thabs bstan-pa # r 'gyur ro /
apraNASa praBedaH gATA anugItena darSitaH SoBate vata BikzuH ayam upaSAntaH nirASravaH iti / tat evam pravrajanam Asrava kzayaH ca paridIpitaH / sa punar Asrava kzayaH / vIta rAgaH visaMyuktaH hi anupAdAya nirvRtaH / DArayati antyam deham jitvA mArasya vAhinIm
# chud-mi-za-ba # r rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa'i-dbyangs #  kyis rab-tu-bstan-pa #  / / dge slong 'di ni mdzes-pa #  ste / / nye-bar #  zhi zhing zag-pa #  zad / / ces bya-ba # 'o / / de-ltar #  rab-tu-byung-ba #  dang zag-pa-zad-pa #  yongs su bstan to / / zag-pa-zad-pa #  de-yang #  / / 'dod-chags #  bral zhing bral-ba #  ste / / nyer len med-pa # s mya-ngan #  'das / / bdud-kyi-sde #  ni pham byas-na # s / / lus kyi tha-ma #  'dzin-pa #  yin /
iti anena lOkika mArga vErAgyataH lokottareNa mArgeNa avaraBAgIya saMyojana prahANataH UrDva BAgIya saMyojana prahANataH ADyAtmika upaDi prahANataH ca paridIpitaH
# zhes-bya-ba #  ste / / 'dis ni 'jig-rten-pa'i-lam #  la 'dod-chags-dang-bral-na # s 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam gyis tha-ma # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  spangs-pa #  dang gong-ma # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i kun du sbyor-ba #  yang spangs-pa #  dang nang gi rdzas yongs su spangs-pa # r yang bstan-pa # 'o /
hetu Pala kzaya aDikArAt ca ayam nirdeSaH drazwavyaH
# rgyu-dang-'bras-bu #  zad-pa # 'i skabs yin-pas #  kyang 'di ba stan par blta'o /
etad viparyayeNa praNASa praBedaH sUcitaH drazwavyaH iti
# 'di-las-bzlog-pa #  ni rab tu chud-za-ba # 'i bar-du #  dbye-ba #  bsnyad-pa # r blta-bar-bya # 'o /
pudgala vyavasTAna muKam yatra iyataH pudgalAn aDikRtya idam BAzitam iti pradarSyate
# gang-zag #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sgo ni gang-du #  gang-zag #  'di snyed kyi dbang-du-byas-nas #  'di gsungs so zhes-bya-ba # r ston-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA Odaka upame sUtre dviviDO pudgalO tri catur praBedAn aDikRtya BAzitam pRTagjanam dRzwa satyam ca
# dper-na #  chu las gyur-pa #  lta-bu # 'i mdo las byung-ba #  lta-bu #  ste / / de ni gang-zag #  gnyis dang gsum dang bzhir rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i dbang du mdzad nas gsungs te / / so-so'i-skye-bo #  dang bden-pa-mthong-ba # 'o /
pRTagjanaH tri BedaH aSuklaH alpa SuklaH bahu SuklaH ca / dRzwa satyaH catuHpraBedaH catvAraH pratipannakAH catvAraH Pala sTAH trayaH SekzAH ekaH aSEzaH
# so-so'i-skye-bo #  ni gsum du rab tu phye-nas #  bsnyad-pa # r blta-bar-bya #  ste / / dkar-po #  ma-yin-pa #  dang cung-zad #  dkar-ba #  dang cher dkar-ba # 'o / / bden-pa-mthong-ba #  ni bzhir rab tu dbye ste / / 'bras-bu-la-gnas-pa #  bzhi ste / / gsum ni slob-pa # 'o / / gcig ni mi-slob-pa # 'o /
praBeda vyavasTAna muKam yatra catuzkowika diBiH praSnEH arTaH varNyate
# rab-tu-dbye-ba #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa # 'i sgo ni gang-du #  mu-bzhi #  la-sogs-pa #  dri-ba #  rnams kyi don brjod-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA anitya sUtre yaH sat idam samanupaSyati sarvaH asO rUpam samanupaSyati yaH vA rUpam samanupaSyati sarvaH sa sat idam samanupaSyati iti catuzkowikaH kaH
# dper ni mi-rtag-pa # 'i mdo las gang-gis #  'di legs-par #  mthong-ba #  des gzugs thams-cad #  mthong ngam / / gang-gis #  gzugs thams-cad #  mthong-ba #  des thams-cad #  legs-par #  mthong ngam zhes-bya-ba #  mu-bzhi # 'o /
praTamA kowiH vedanA ArdIH caturaH skanDAn nitya Suci suKa Atma viparyAsEH asamAropya parijQeya prahAtavyAn= ca samanupaSyataH
# mu dang-po #  ni tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  phung-po #  bzhi la rtag-pa #  dang gtsang ba dang bde-ba #  dang bdag tu phyin-ci-log #  tu sgro ma btags-pa # r yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dang spang-bar-bya-ba #  yang-dag-par #  rjes su blta-ba # 'o /
dvitIyA kowI rUpam nitya Suci suKa Atma viparyAsEH samAropya aparijQyA prahAtavyam ca samanupaSyataH
# mu gnyis-pa #  ni gzugs la rtag-pa #  dang gtsang ba dang bde-ba #  dang bdag tu phyin-ci-log #  tu sgro btags-nas #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba-ma-yin-pa #  dang yongs-su-spang-ba # r bya-ba-ma-yin-pa # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su blta-ba # 'o /
tRtIyA kowI rUpam nitya Suci suKa Atma viparyAsEH asamAropya parijQeya prahAtavyAn= ca samanupaSyataH caturTI kowiH vedanA AdIn= caturaH skanDAn nitya Suci suKa Atma viparyAsEH samAropya aparijQeya aprahAtavyam ca samanupaSyataH
# mu gsum-pa #  ni gzugs la rtag-pa #  dang gtsang ba dang bde-ba #  dang bdag tu phyin-ci-log #  tu sgro ma btags-pa # r yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba #  dang yongs-su-spang-ba # r bya-ba #  yang-dag-par #  rdzes su blta-ba # 'o / / mu-bzhi #  pa ni tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  phung-po #  bzhi la rtag-pa #  dang gtsang ba dang bde-ba #  dang bdag tu phyin-ci-log #  tu sgro btags-nas #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba-ma-yin-pa #  dang spang-bar-bya-ba #  ma-yin-pa # r yang-dag-par #  rjes su blta-ba # 'o /
yaTA rUpe catuzkowikaH evam vedanA AdO sarvatra vistareNa drazwavyam
# gzugs la mu-bzhi #  ji-lta-ba #  de-bzhin-du #  tshor-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  thams-cad-la #  yang rgya-cher-sbyar-bar-bya # 'o /
yAvat yasya kRtam karaNIyam sarvaH sa na aparam asmAt Bavam prajAnAti yAvat na aparam asmAt Bavam prajAnAti sarvasya tasya kRtam karaNIyam
# gang bya-ba-byas-pa #  de thams-cad #  'di-las #  srid-pa #  gzhan mi shes so zhes-bya-ba #  yin nam / / gang 'di-las #  srid-pa #  gzhan mi-shes-pa #  de thams-cad #  bya-ba-byas-pa #  yin nam zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
Aha catuzkowikam
# smras-pa #  / / mu-bzhi #  ste /
praTamA kowiH yAvat jIvam su carita cAriNaH pRTagjanasya
# mu dang-po #  ni ji-srid-'tsho'i-bar-du #  legs-par-spyad-pa #  spyod-pa # 'i so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i'o /
dvitIya ucCeda dRzwa yAdInAm
# gnyis-pa #  ni chad-pa # r lta-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'o /
tRtIyA aSEkzasya
# gsum-pa #  ni mi-slob-pa # 'i'o /
caturTI tAn AkArAn sTApayitvA
# bzhi-pa #  ni rnam-pa #  de-dag #  ma-gtogs-pa # 'i'o zhes 'byung-ba #  lta-bu # 'o /
naya muKam yatra zaXBiH nayEH arTaH varNyate tattva arTa nayena prAptinayena deSanA nayena anna dvaya vivarjana Anayena acintya nayena aBiprAyanayena ca / ezAm ca zaNNAm nayAnAm pUrvakAH trayaH nayAH uttarEH triBiH nayEH yaTAkramam anugantavyAH
# tshul gyi sgo ni gang-du #  tshul drug gi sa-bon #  brjod-pa #  ste / / de-kho-na'i-don #  gyi tshul dang 'thob-pa # 'i tshul dang bshad-pa # 'i tshul dang mtha'-gnyis #  spangs-pa # 'i tshul dang bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa # 'i tshul dang dgongs-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  so / / tshul drug-po #  'di dag las tshul gong-ma #  gsum ni tshul 'og ma gsum gyis go-rims-bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya #  ste /
tat yaTA svAdana sUtre asti BikzavaH rUpe AsvAdaH iti evamAdinA apavAda antam samAropa antam ca varjayitvA tattva arTanayaH aBidyotitaH / asti AsvAdaH AdInavaH niHsaraNam iti anena apavAdAntaH varjitaH rUpe yAvat vijQAnaH iti anena samAropAntaH skanDa mAtre saMkleSaH vyavadAnam ca anAtmani iti pradarSayatA yAvat ca aham BikzavaH yAvat anuttarAm samyaksaMboDim aBisaMbudDaH asmi iti aDyajQA sizam iti anena prAptinaH acintya nayena paridIpitaH pratyAtma vedanIya aDigama sUcanAt / sarvam eva idam sUtram deSanA nayaH / sa ca aBiprAyeNa anugantavyaH
# dper-na #  ro myang-ba # 'i mdo las dge slong dag gzugs la ro-myong-ba #  yod do zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s ni skur-pa-'debs-pa # 'i mtha' dang sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i mtha' spangs-nas #  de-kho-na'i-don #  gyi tshul ston to / / ro myang-ba #  dang nyes-dmigs #  dang nges-par-'byung-ba #  yod do zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni skur ba 'debs-pa # 'i mtha' spangs so / / gzugs nas rnam-par-shes-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar 'dis ni sgro-'dogs-pa # 'i mtha' spangs-te #  / / phung-po #  tsam la kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # 'am / / rnam-par-byang-ba # r zad kyi bdag ni med do zhes rab tu bstan to / / dge slong dag ngas ji tsam tu bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  kyi bar-du #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r sangs-rgyas #  so zhes-bya-ba # r nang-du #  'du-shes #  so zhes-bya-ba #  'dis ni 'thob-pa # 'i tshul bsam-gyis-mi-khyab-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  yongs su bstan te / / so-so #  rang-gis #  rig-par-bya-ba #  thob-pa # r ston-pa # 'i phyir ro / / mdo 'di thams-cad #  ni bshad-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  so / / de-yang #  dgongs-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  khong-du-chud-pa # r bya ste /
sa parijQeyam vastu parijQeyam arTam parijQAm parijQA Palam tad pravedanAm ca aBipretya idam sUtram BAzitam iti
# yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  dang yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i don dang yongs-su-shes-pa #  dang yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i 'bras-bu #  dang de rab-tu-shes-pa #  la dgongs nas mdo de-dag #  bshad do /
tatra parijQeyam vastu rUpa Adikam
# de-la #  yongs-su-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i dngos-po #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'o /
parijQeyaH arTaH AsvAda AdikaH tena prakAreNa tasya rUpa Adikasya vastunaH parijQAnAt
# yongs su shes bar bya-ba # 'i don ni ro myang-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  ste / / rnam-pa #  des gzugs la-sogs-pa # 'i dngos-po #  de yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i phyir ro /
parijQA ezAm paQcAnAm upAdAna skanDAnAm evam tri parivartena yaTA BUta parijQAnam
# yongs-su-shes-pa #  ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lnga po dag nga ltar gsum du bsgyur-ba # s yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rtogs-pa # 'i shes-pa # 'o /
parijQA Palam asmAt sa devakAt lokAt yAvat sa deva mAnuzAyAH prajQAyAH vimuktiH yAvat vipramuktiH
# yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i 'bras-bu #  ni lha dang bcas-pa # 'i 'jig-rten-'di #  las zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / lha-dang-mi #  dang bcas-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar las grol ba nas rnam-pa # r rab tu grol zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du # 'o /
tad pravedana anuttarAm samyaksaMboDim aBisaMbudDaH asmi iti aDyajQAsizam iti
# de rab-tu-shes-pa #  ni bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r sangs-rgyas #  par nang-du #  shes so zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
parijQa Adi muKam yatra tattva lakzaNam Aramya parijQA lakzaNena prahANa lakzaNena sAkzAtkriyA lakzaNena ezAm eva tattva lakzaNa AdInAm prakAra Beda lakzaNena ASraya ASrita saMvanDa lakzaNena parijQa AdInAm AntarAyika Darma lakzaNena Amulomika Darma lakzaNena aparijQA Adizu ca AdIn avAnuSaMsA lakzaNena ca arTaH nirdiSyate
# yongs-su-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sgo ni gang-du #  de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  las brtsams nas yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang spong-ba # 'i mtshan nyad dang mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang bsgom-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang de-kho-na # 'i mchan nyid la-sogs-pa #  'di dag gi rnam-pa # 'i rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang; gnas dang gnas-pa # r 'brel-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang yongs-su-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa'i-chos #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  dang rjes-su-mthun-pa'i-chos #  kyi mtshan-nyid #  dang yongs-su-ma-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dang yongs-su-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la nyes-dmigs #  dang phan yon gyi mtshan-nyid #  kyis don ston-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA atra eva AsvAdana sUtre
# dper-na #  ro myang-ba # 'i mdo de-nyid-la # s 'byung-ba #  /
tatra tattva lakzaNam upAdAna skanDa saMgRhIta duHKa satyam / parijQA lakzaNam tasya eva AsvAda AdinA yaTABUtam parijQAnam / prahANa lakzaNam sAkzAtkriyA lakzaNam ca sarvasmAt lokAt vimuktiH AvaraNa prahANe na ASraya parivRtti sAkzAtkaraNAt BAvanA lakzaNam viparyAsa apagatena cetasA bahula vihAraH
# de-la #  de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  ni nye-bar-len-pa # 'i phung-po #  lngas bsdus-pa #  sdug-bsngal #  gyi bden-pa # 'o / / yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni ro myang-ba #  la-sogs-pa # s de nyid yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu shes so; ;spang-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni 'jig-rten-thams-cad #  las rnam-par-grol-ba #  ste / / sgrib-pa-spong-ba #  dang gnas-gyur-pa #  mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro / / bsgom-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni phyin-ci-log #  dang bral-ba # 'i sems-kyis #  len mang-du-gnas-pa # 'o /
prakAra Beda lakzaNam tattva lakzaNasya paQcaDA BedaH rUpam yAvat vijQAnam iti / parijQA lakzaNasya triDA BedaH AsvAdam ca AsvAdayataH yAvat niHsaraNam ca niHsarataH yaTABUtam prajAnAti
# rnam-pa # r rab-tu-dbye-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  rnam-pa-lnga # 'i dbye-ba #  ste / / gzugs nas rnam-par-shes-pa # 'i bar-du # 'o / / yongs-su-shes-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rnam-pa # r gsum du rab tu dbye ste / / ro myang-ba #  la ro myang-ba #  dang nyes-dmigs #  la nyes-dmigs #  dang nges-par-'byung-ba # 'i bar la nges-par-'byung-ba # r yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rab tu shes so /
prahANa lakzaNasya sAkzAtkriyA lakzaNasya dviDA BedaH kleSa vimuktiH duHKa vimuktiH ca
# spong-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  dang mngon-sum-du-byed-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  su dbye ste / / nyon-mongs-pa #  las rnam-par-grol-ba #  dang sdug-bsngal #  las rnam-par-grol-ba # 'o /
tatra sa devakAt loka AdyAt sevadeva mAnuzAyAH prajAyAH vimuktiH kleSeByaH vimokzAdataH eva tad viSezaNa arTam Aha niHsRtaH iti / tat yaTA hi anyatra sUtre niHsaraNam katamat BayaH
# de-la #  lha dang bcas-pa # 'i 'jig-rten #  zhes-bya-ba #  nas / / lha-dang-mi # r bcas-pa # 'i skye-dgu # 'i bar las grol ba ni nyon-mongs-pa #  rnams las rnam-par-thar-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-bas-na #  de bye-brag-tu-bya-ba # 'i phyir nges-par-'byung-ba #  zhes gsungs te / / 'di-ltar #  mdo gzhan-las #  nges-par-'byung-ba #  gang zhe na /
Canda rAga vinayaH Canda rAga prahANam Canda rAga samatikramaH iti uktam
# gang 'dir 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  'dul-ba #  dang 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  spang-ba #  dang 'dun-pa-dang-'dod-chags #  las yang-dag-par #  'da' ba'o zhes gsungs so /
evam anAgata duHKa aBinirvartaka kleSa saMyoge sati duHKAt api vipramuktaH Bavati iti viSezaNa arTam Aha visaMyuktaH vipramuktaH iti
# de-ltar #  ma-'ongs-pa # 'i sdug-bsngal #  mngon bar 'grub-par-byed-pa # 'i nyon-mongs-pa #  dang bral na sdug-bsngal #  las kyang rnam-par-grol-ba # r 'gyur ro zhes bye-brag-tu-bya-ba # 'i phyir bral-ba #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba #  zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs so /
BAvanA lakzaNasya dviDA BedaH darSana mArgaH BAvanA mArgaH ca
# bsgom-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni rnam-pa-gnyis #  su rab tu dbye ste / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  dang bsgom-pa'i-lam #  mo /
tatra viparyAsa apagatena cetasA iti darSana mArgam darSayati bahulam vyahArzam iti anena BAvanA mArgam
# de-la #  phyin-ci-log #  dang bral-ba # 'i sems-kyis #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / mthong-ba'i-lam #  ston to / / len mang-du-gnas-pa # r 'gyur ro zhes-bya-ba #  'di ni bsgom-pa'i-lam #  ston to /
ASraya ASrita saMbanDa lakzaNam tad valakzaNa AdInAm uttarottarANAm ASraya tva sUcanAt
# gnas dang gnas-pa # r 'brel-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni / / de-kho-na'i-mtshan-nyid #  la-sogs-pa #  'og ma gong-ma # 'i gnas yin par ston-pa # 'i phyir ro /
parijQa AdInAm AntarAyika lakzaNam evam tri parivartena yaTABUtam aparijQAnam
# yongs-su-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i bar-du-gcod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni de-ltar #  gsum du bsgyur-ba #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rnam-pa # r mi-shes-pa # 'o /
anulomika lakzaNam yaTA vyavasTAnam ezAm eva rUpa AdInAm AsvAdAt itas vicAraNA
# rjes-su-mthun-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  ni gzugs la-sogs-pa #  'di dag ji-ltar #  gnas-pa #  bzhin-du #  nyes-dmigs #  la-sogs-pa # r rnam-par-dpyod-pa # 'o /
aparijQAna AdIn avalakzaNa vimuktiH yAvat anuttarAyAH samyaksaMboDeH asaMboDaH
# yongs su mi-shes-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la nyes-dmigs-kyi-mtshan-nyid #  ni mi grol ba nas bla-na-med-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rdzogs-pa'i-byang-chub #  mngon-pa # r rdzogs-pa # r 'tshang mi rgya pa'i bar-du # 'o /
viparyayAt anuSaMsa lakzaNam veditavyam iti / bala abala muKam yatra ekena padena anucyamAnena ayam arTaH na gamitaH syAt iti pratyekam sarvezAm padAnAm sAmarTya pradarSyate
# de-las-bzlog-pa #  ni phan yon gyi mchan nyid-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o / / stobs dang stobs ma-yin-pa # 'i sgo ni gang-du #  tshig gcig ma brjod na don 'di go-ba # r mi-'gyur-ba # s tshig so-so #  thams-cad-kyi # s nus-pa #  ston-pa #  ste /
tat yaTA pratItya utpAda sUtre asmin sati idam Bavati asya utpAdAt idam utpadyate yat uta avidyA pratyayAH saMskArAH iti evamAdi ezAm ca padAnAm pratyekam sAmarTya pUrvavat veditavya yaTA pratItyasamutpAdasya lakzaNa nirdeSe
# dper-na #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i mdo las 'di yod-pa # s 'di 'byung / / 'di skyes-pa # 'i phyir 'di skye-ba #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  ma-rig-pa # 'i rkyen gyis 'du-byed-rnams #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / tshig 'di dag gi so-so # 'i nus-pa #  ni ji-ltar #  gang-du #  rten cing 'brel-ba # r 'byung-ba # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du bshad-pa #  bzhin-du #  rig-par-bya # 'o /
pratyAhAra muKam yatra sUtrasya ekam padam gRhItvA vistareNa arTaH pratinirdiSyate / tat yaTA zaXBiH DarmEH samanvAgataH BikzuH himavantam api parvata rAjam muKa vAyunA cAlayet kaH punar vAdaH sa vAsanAyAH avidyAyAH / katamEH zaXBiH / iha BikzavaH BikzuH cittasya utpAda kuSalaH Bavati iha BikzuH viviktam kAmEH yAvat caturTa DyAnam upasaMpadya viharati
# bzlas te brjod-pa # 'i sgo ni gang-du #  mdo'i-tshig #  gcig bzung-ba # s rgya-cher #  don-yang-dag-pa # r ston-pa #  ste / / dper-na #  chos drug dang ldan-pa # 'i dge slong ni kha'i dbugs kyis ri'i-rgyal-po #  gangs-ri #  yang 'thor na ro lta-bu # 'i ma-rig-pa #  lta-smos #  kyang ci dgos / / drug gang zhe na / / 'di-la #  dge slong dag 'di-la #  dge slong sems-bskyed-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin pa nas / / thabs-la-mkhas-pa #  yin no zhes-bya-ba # 'i bar-du #  gsungs-pa #  lta-bu # 'o / / mdo 'di-las #  ji-ltar #  na dge slong sems-bskyed-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin zhe na / / 'di-la #  dge slong ni 'dod-pa #  dag las dben-pa #  nas bsam-gtan-bzhi-pa # 'i bar-du #  rdzogs-pa # r byas-na # s gnas te /
evam hi BikzuH cittasya utpAda kuSalaH Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  dge slong sems-bskyed-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin no /
kaTam ca BikzuH cittasya sTiti kuSalaH Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na dge slong sems-gnas-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin zhe na /
iha BikzuH Asevana anvayAt hAna BAgIyam DyAnam tat sTiti BAgIyam karoti
# 'di-la #  dge slong ni kun du bsten-pa # 'i rgyu'i bar gyis gang nyams-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i bsam-gtan #  de gnas-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # r byed de /
evam BikzuH sTiti kuSalaH Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  dge slong de sems-gnas-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin no /
kaTam ca BikzuH vyutTAna kuSalaH Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na dge slong de sems ldang-bar-byed-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin zhe na /
iha BikzuH Asevana anvayAt sTiti BAgIyam DyAnam tad viSeza BAgIyam karoti
# 'di-la #  dge slong ni kun du bsten-pa # 'i rgyus gnas-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # 'i bsam-gtan #  de khyad-par #  du gyur-pa # 'i cha-dang-mthun-pa # r byed de /
evam hi BikzuH vyutTAna kuSalaH Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  dge slong ldang-bar-byed-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin no /
kaTam ca BikzuH Aya kuSalaH Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na dge slong 'phel-bar-byed-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  yin zhe na /
iha BikzuH anutpannAnAm kuSalAnAm DarmANAm iti vistareNa dve samyak prahANe
# 'di-la #  dge slong ni dge-ba'i-chos #  ma-skyes-pa #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  yang-dag-par #  spang-ba #  nyid rgya-cher #  bya ste /
evam hi BikzuH Aya kuSalaH Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  dge slong 'phel-ba #  la mkhas-pa #  yin no /
kaTam ca BikzuH apAya kuSalaH Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na de slong 'bri-ba #  la mkhas-pa #  yin zhe na /
iha hi BikzuH utpannAnAm pApakAH nAma kuSalAnAm iti vistareNa dve samyak prahANe
# sdig-pa #  mi-dge-ba'i-chos #  skyes-pa #  rnams zhes-bya-ba #  yang-dag-par-spong-ba #  gnyis kyis rgya-cher #  bya ste /
evam hi BikzuH apAya kuSalaH Bavati
# de-ltar-na #  dge slong 'bri-ba #  la mkhas-pa #  yin no /
kaTam hi BikzuH upAya kuSalaH Bavati
# ji-ltar #  na dge slong thabs-la-mkhas-pa #  yin zhe na /
iha hi BikzuH Canda samADi praDAna saMskAra sama anvAgata mRdDi pAdam BAvayati iti vistareNa catvAraH RdDi pAdAH
# 'di-la #  dge slong ni 'dun-pa'i-ting-nge-'dzin #  spong-ba'i-'du-byed #  dang ldan-pa # 'i rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  bsgom mo zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  rdzu-'phrul-gyi-rkang-pa #  bzhi rgya-cher #  sbyar te /
evam hi BikzuH upAya kuSalaH Bavati iti
# de-ltar-na #  dge slong thabs-la-mkhas-pa #  yin no zhes 'byung ngo /
aBinirhAra muKam yatra pratipadam catuzka AdiBiH nirdiSyate
# mngon-par-sgrub-pa'i-sgo #  ni gang-du #  tshig re-re #  la yang mu-bzhi #  la-sogs-pa #  ston-pa #  ste /
tezu api catuzka Adizu ekEkam padam aparEH catuzka AdiBiH aparyantaH hi nirhAraH veditavyaH
# mu-bzhi #  pa la-sogs-pa #  la de-dag #  gi tshig re-re #  la yang gzhan bzhi la-sogs-pa # s thug-pa #  med-pa # r mngon bar bsgrub-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / dper-na #  sangs-rgyas #  rtsom pa'i mdo las /
tat yaTA budDa Akzepa sUtre catvAraH ime boDisattvAnAm boDi pariSoDakAH DarmAH SUnyatA BAvanA sarva sattvezu apratihata citta tA boDisattvAnAm nityam hita upasaMharaNa tA nirAmizeNa cittena Darma dAna saMprakASana tA ca iti
# bzhi-po #  'di dag ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  sems-dpa'-che # n po rnams kyi byang-chub #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # r byed-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  te / / stong-pa-nyid #  sgom-pa #  dang sems-can-thams-cad #  la zhe-'gras-pa #  med-pa # 'i sems dang byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la rtag-tu #  phan-pa #  nye-bar-sgrub-pa # 'i sems dang zang-zing-med-pa'i-sems #  kyis chos-kyi-sbyin-pa #  yang-dag-par #  rab tu ston-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  bzhi ni bdag-dang-gzhan-gyi-don #  las brtsams te /
catuzkaH sva arTa parama arTa ca AraBya boDi pariSoDanAya catur pakza pratipakzeNa veditavyaH / catvAraH vipakzAH samApatti AsvAdanA vyApAdaH mAnaH tRzNA ca lABa satkAre / aparaH paryAyaH praTamena DarmeNa kleSa prahANa pratipakzaH
# byang-chub #  yongs-su-sbyong-ba # 'i phyir mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  bzhi'i gnyen-po # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / mi-mthun-pa'i-phyogs #  bzhi ni snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i ro myang-ba #  dang gnod-sems #  dang nga-rgyal #  dang rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la sred-pa # 'o / / rnams grangs gzhan-du-na #  chos dang-po # s ni nyon-mongs-pa-spong-ba # 'i gnyen-po #  bstan to /
SezEH hIna yAna parivarjanA paridIpitAH triBiH kAraNEH boDi cittena sarva sattva upAdAnataH avatIrNa paripAcanataH anavatIrNa avatAraNataH ca eva
# lhag-ma #  rnams kyis ni rgyu gsum gyis theg-pa-dman-pa #  yongs-su-spang-ba # r bsten te / / byang-chub #  kyi sems-kyis #  sems-can-thams-cad #  nye-bar #  'dzin-pa #  dang zhugs-pa #  yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  dang ma zhugs-pa #  'jug-par-byed-pa # s so /
aparaH paryAyaH praTamena jQAna saMBAraH triBiH puNya saMBAraH paridIpitaH upAdAna paripAcana avatAraNEH pratyekam puNya viSeza prasavanataH
# rnam-grangs #  gzhan-du-na #  dang-po # s ni ye-shes-kyi-tshogs #  yongs su bstan to / / gsum gyis ni bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su bstan te / / nye-bar #  'dzin-pa #  dang yongs-su-smin-pa # r byed-pa #  dang 'jug-pa #  rnam-pa #  re-re # s kyang bsod nams kyi khyad-par #  skyed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
punar dvAByAm kAraNAByAm ASayataH ca mEtra citta tayA pratipattitaH ca aDigama Agama upadeSAByAm
# yang rgyu gnyis kyis rig-par-bya #  ste / / bsam-pa # s ni byams-pa'i-sems #  su'o / / bsgrub bas ni thob-pa #  dang lung nye-bar #  ston-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
caturBiH DarmEH samanvAgatAH boDisattvAH SUnyatAm BAvayanti aDyAtmam citta avikaMpana tayA aDimukti pravicaya bala ADAnatayA sarva DarmANAm yaTA Atmya prativeDataH sarva AvaraNa vimokzataH ca
# chos bzhi dang ldan na byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  stong-pa-nyid #  bsgom ste / / nang-du #  sems su rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang mos-pa #  la rab tu rnam-par-'byed-pa # 'i stobs-skyed-pa #  dang chos-thams-cad #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  rtogs-par-byed-pa #  dang sgrib-pa #  thams-cad-la # s rnam-par-thar-pa #  ste /
yat ASritya yaTA ca BAvayanti tat etena paridIpitam
# 'di dag gis ni gang-la #  brten-nas #  ji-ltar #  bsgom-pa #  de yongs su bsten to /
kim ASritya / DyAna pAramitAm
# gang-la #  brten-nas #  she na / / bsam-gtan #  gyi pha-rol-tu-phyin-pa #  la'o /
kaTam BAvayanti
# ji-ltar #  bsgom zhe na /
pRTagjana mArgeNa Sruta cintA bala ADAnataH SEkza mArgeNa SEkza mArgeNa ca
# so-so'i-skye-bo # 'i lam gyis thos-pa-dang-bsam-pa # 'i stobs-skyed-pa #  dang slob-pa'i-lam #  dang mi-slob-pa # 'i lam gyis so /
caturBiH DarmEH samanvAgatAH boDisattvAH sarva sattvezu apratihata cittAH Bavanti mEtrI BAvanayA pratipatyavikopanatayA nimitta avikalpanatayA Keda sahizNu tayA ca / atra api yat ASritya yaTA ca apratihata cittAH Bavanti tat paridIpitam Bavati
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  chos bzhi dang ldan na / / sems-can-thams-cad #  la zhe 'gras ba med-pa # 'i sems dang ldan-pa #  yin te / / byams-pa-bsgom-pa #  dang sgrub-pa #  rnam-par-mi-'khrugs-pa #  dang mtshan-ma #  la rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang skyo-ba #  bzod-pa # 'o / / 'dir yang gang-la #  brten-nas #  ji-ltar #  zhe-'gras-pa #  med-pa # 'i sems dang ldan-pa #  yin pa de yongs su bstan to /
kim ASritya
# gang-la #  brten-nas #  she na /
pOrvajanmikIm mEtrI BAvanAm
# tshe-rabs #  snga-ma # 'i byams-pa #  bsgoms-pa #  las so /
kaTam apratihata cittAH Bavanti
# ji-ltar #  zhe-'gras-pa #  med-pa # 'i sems dang ldan-pa #  yin zhe na /
miTyA pratipatti sTitezu sva cita avikopanataH apakArizu apakAra nimitta avikalpanataH para hita arTam vyAyAma apariKedataH ca
# log-pa # r sgrub-pa #  la gnas-pa #  rnams la sems rnam-par-mi-'khrugs-pa #  dang gnod-par-byed-pa #  rnams la gnod-par-byed-pa # 'i mtshan-ma # r rnam-par-mi-rtog-pa #  dang gzhan-la-phan-pa # 'i don-du #  rtsol ba la yongs-su-mi-skyo-ba # 'o /
caturBiH DarmEH samanvAgatAH boDisattvAH boDisattvAnAm nityam hitam upasaMharanti AtmanaH paritulanatayA samyak avavAda pravartanatayA sOraBya suKa saMvAsana tayA pUjA lABa satkAra paricarya upasaMharaNa tayA ca / atra api yat ASritya yaTA ca upasaMharati tat paridIpitam
# byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  chos bzhi dang ldan na byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams la rtag-tu #  phan-pa #  nye-bar-bsgrub-pa #  yin te / / bdag yongs su 'jal-ba #  dang yang-dag-pa # 'i gdams pa la 'jug-pa #  dang des shing 'grogs-na-bde-ba #  dang mchod-pa #  dang rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  dang bsnyen-bkur-bya-ba #  nye-bar-sgrub-pa # 'o / / 'dir yang gang-la #  brten-nas #  ji-ltar #  nye-bar #  ba sgrub-pa #  de yongs su bsten to /
kim ASritya / nihata mAna tAm / kaTam upasaMharati
# gang-la #  brten-nas #  she na / / nga-rgyal #  bcag pa la'o / / ji-ltar #  nye-bar #  bsgrub ce na /
yaTA uktam triBiH prakArEH hIna sama SizwAnAm boDisattvAnAm yaTAkramam

caturBiH DarmEH samanvAgatAH boDisattvAH nirAmizeNa cittena Darma dAnam saMprakASayanti antarAya suKa prativeDa tayA mohala yAna nayana kOSalya tayA nATa kara Darma ArAma tayA ca

# rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  bar-du-gcod-pa # r byed-pa #  nyid-du #  legs-par #  rtogs-pa #  la'o / / ji-ltar #  yang-dag-par #  rab tu ston ce na /
saMdarSanataH mUXAnAm samAdApanataH samuttejanataH ca pramAda saFga anAtma pariBavena vA lInAnAm saMpraharzaNataH samyak pratipannAnAm prakRtyA eva ca Darma ArAma tayA

tatra / eka avacArakaH nAma praSnaH yena ekam Darmam pariSizwEH saha pratyekam praSnayitvA tam apahAya dvitIyam tena anyEH ca saha praSnayati evam ekEkasya eva sarvAn praSnayati

# de-ltar #  re-re-nas #  gsal-ba # 'i tshul-gyis #  skye-mched #  thams-cad #  phan tshun du sbyar-ba # r bya'o /
pUrva pAdakam dvayoH DarmayoH kaTaMcid eva Darmam AraBya parasparam pRzwayoH pUrva Darmam aDizWAya yat vaya akriyate / tat yaTA yat jQAnam jQeyam api tat yat vA jQeyam jQAnam api tat iti / pUrva pAdakam yat tAvat jQAnam jQeyam api tat iti / syAt jQeyam na jQAnam tad anye DarmAH iti
# tshig gong-ma #  dang sbyor-ba #  gnyis gnyis po ni chos 'ga' zhig la brtsams nas phan tshun dris na chos gong-ma #  la brten-nas #  gang lung-ston-pa #  ste / / dper-na #  shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de shes-bya #  yang de'am / / shes-bya #  gang-yin-pa #  shes-pa #  yang de 'am zhes-bya-ba # 'i ni tshig gong-ma #  dang sbyor-ba #  ste / / shes-pa #  gang-yin-pa #  de shes-bya #  yang de yin no / / shes-bya #  yin la shes-pa #  ma-yin-pa # 'ang yod de / / de-las-gzhan-pa # 'i chos-rnams #  so /

# tshig rab-tu-dbye-ba #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni gnyis-pa #  dang gsum-pa #  dang bzhi-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  mngon-par-sgrub-pa'i-sgo #  nas chos-ston-pa #  la mtha' yas so /
anABoga ABoga mAtra sarva arTa sidDi viniScayaH taTAgatam jQAnam vinA pUrva ABogena sarvezu arTezu ABoga sahakAlam asaMgA pratihata jQAna darSana pravRtteH
# lhun-gyis-grub-pa #  dang rtsol ba tsam gyi don-thams-cad-'grub-pa #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni de-bzhin-gshegs-pa # 'i ye shes te / / sngon gyi rtsol ba med-pa # r yang don-thams-cad #  la rtsol ba'i mdo las chags-pa-med-pa #  dang thogs-pa-med-pa # 'i ye shes kyi mthong-ba #  'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vAda viniScayaH vAda vAda aDikaraNa Adizu kOSalyam / tatra sarvam vacanam vAdaH / prakAraSas loke vAdaH pravAdaH / virudDayoH vAdaH vivAdaH
# smra-ba #  rnam-par-nges-pa #  ni smra-ba #  dang smra-ba # 'i zhal ce ba la-sogs-pa #  la mkhas-pa #  ste / / de-la #  smra-ba #  ni tshig thams-cad #  do / / rmad khyer-ba # r smra-ba #  ni 'jig-rten #  na rnam-pa # r smra-ba # 'o / / rtsod par smra-ba #  ni mi-mthun-par-smra-ba # 'o /
apavAdaH garhitaH vAdaH / anukUlaH vAdaH anuvAdaH sAMkaTya viniScayaH / avagamAya vAdaH avavAdaH / vAda aDikaraNam atra vAdaH kriyate iti kRtvA
# tshig ngan-pa # r smra-ba #  ni smad-pa # r smra-ba # 'o / / mthun-par #  smra-ba #  ni rjes-su-mthun-pa # r smra-ba # 'o / / gdams par smra-ba #  ni khong-du-chud-pa # r bya-ba # 'i phyir smra-ba # 'o / / smra-ba # 'i zhal ce ba ni gang-du #  smra-ba # r bya-ba #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  / / rgyal-po'i-pho-brang #  ni gang na rgyal-po #  nyid bzhugs-pa # 'o /

# tshad-ma # r rung-ba # 'i zla grogs ni gang dag gi tshig smra-ba #  dang phyir-rgol-ba #  gnyi-ga # s mi gcod-pa # 'o /

# dge-sbyong #  dang bram-ze #  chos-dang-don #  la mkhas-pa #  rnams ni gang dag bstan-bcos #  de-dang-de-dag #  gi tshig dang don la blo byang-ba # 'o / / smra-ba # 'i gzhi ni gang-la #  brten-nas #  smra-ba # r bya-ba #  ste / / 'di-lta-ste #  sgrub-pa #  dang grub-pa # 'o / / de-la #  ngo-bo-nyid #  sgrub-pa #  ni bdag-gi #  ngo-bo-nyid #  dang chos-kyi-ngo-bo-nyid #  de yod de zhe'am /
tatra svaBAvaH sADyaH Atma svaBAvaH Darma svaBAvaH ca na asti iti vA asti iti vA / viSezaH sADyaH Atma viSezaH Darma viSezaH ca sarva gataH na sarva gataH nitya anityaH rUpya rUpI iti evamAdiBiH prakArEH
# med do zhes-bya-ba # 'o / / khyad-par #  sgrub-pa #  ni bdag-gi #  khyad-par #  dang chos kyi khyad-par #  te / / thams-cad-du #  song-ba # 'am / / thams-cad-du #  song-ba #  ma-yin-pa # 'am / / rtag-pa # 'am mi-rtag-pa # 'i gzugs-can #  nam gzugs-can-ma-yin-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  su'o /
pratijQA sADyasya sva rucita arTasya para saMprApaNa vijQApanA / sADya grahaNam yadi na kriyeta sidDasya api sva pakzasya parezAm deSanA pratijQA prasajyeta / sva rucita arTa grahaNam na kriyeta para pakzasya api sADyasya vacanam pratijQA prasajyeta / para grahaNam na kriyeta ekAkinaH api tad vacanam pratijQA prasajyeta / saMprApaNa grahaNam na kriyeta kAyena api tad arTa aBinayanam pratijQA prasajyeta / vijQApana agrahaNam na kriyA iti avijQAte api tad arTe SrotRBiH pratijQA prasajyeta
# dam-bca'-ba #  ni bdag 'dod-pa #  sgrub-pa # 'i don gzhan la go-ba # r ston-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  la / / gal-te #  sgrub-pa #  ma smos na bdag-gi #  phyogs grub zin-pa #  yang gzhan dag la bstan-pa # r dam-bca'-ba # r 'gyur ro / / bdag 'dod-pa # 'i don ma smos na ni gzhan gyi phyogs bsgrub-pa # 'i tshig kyang dam-bca'-ba # r 'gyur ro / / gzhan ma smos na ni gcig-pu #  yang tshig de dam-bca'-ba # r 'gyur ro / / gal-te #  go-ba # r ma smos na ni lus kyi don de brda spyod-pa #  yang dam-bca'-ba # r 'gyur ro / / gal-te #  ston-pa #  ma smos na ni nyan-pa #  rnams kyis don de ma shes na yang dam-bca'-ba # r 'gyur ro /

# ji-ltar #  bstan-pa #  bzhin-du #  rnam-par-gzhag-pa #  la nyes-pa #  'di dag thams-cad-med-pa # r 'gyur te / / de-lta-bas-na #  'di rnam-par-gzhag-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

# 'di-ltar #  mngon-sum-du #  dmigs-pa #  dang ma dmigs-pa #  zhes bstan-pa #  'dis sgrub-pa #  de-nyid-la #  ma grags-pa # 'i don la yid-ches-pa #  skye-ba #  ste / / des-na #  de bsnyad-pa # 'i rgyur-gyur-pa # 'i phyir gtan-tshigs #  zhes-bya'o #  /

# mngon-sum-du #  dmigs-pa #  dang ma dmigs-pa #  ni ngo-bo-nyid #  kyi tshul dang rtags kyi dbang-du-byas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /

# dpe ni mtha' mthong-ba #  dang mtha' ma-mthong-ba #  mtshungs-pa # r sbyar zhing bsnyad-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni grags-pa # 'i cha dang ma grags-pa # 'i cha rtogs-par-bya-ba # 'i phyir / / bsnyad ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
upanayaH Sizwa tad jAtIya tad Darma upagamAya naya tva samAKyAnam / yaTA sADyaH arTaH triBiH avayavEH sADitaH taTA SizwAnAm api tad jAtIyAnAm sADyAnAm sADita arTa Darma upagamAya naya tvena samAKyAnam yuktyA atideSaH upanayaH
# nye-bar-sbyor-ba #  ni de'i rigs kyi chos lhag-ma #  de-dang-'dra-ba #  la de'i chos sbyar-ba # 'i phyir tshul-gyis #  mthun-par #  bsnyad-pa # 'o zhes-bya-ba #  ni ji-ltar #  bsgrub-pa # 'i don yan-lag #  gsum gyis bsgrubs-pa #  de-bzhin-du #  / / lhag-ma #  de-dang-'dra-ba #  sgrub-pa #  grub-pa #  rnams la yang sgrub-pa # 'i don-gyis #  chos sbyar-ba # 'i phyir ro / / tshul-gyis #  mthun-par #  bsnyad cing rigs-pa #  'dra-bar #  ston-pa #  ni nye-bar #  sbyar-ba # r bya'o /

# phung-po #  la bdag tu 'dogs-pa #  la nyes-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  dmigs-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni gtan tshig te / / bdag de-la #  'dogs na phung-po # 'i mtshan-nyid #  du'am / / phung-po #  rnams la'am / / phung-po #  rnams las gzhan-pa # 'am / / phung-po #  med-pa #  zhig tu gdags grang na /

# 'das-pa #  de yod-pa # 'i mtshan-nyid #  kho-nar #  'dogs-pa #  na de-ltar #  gyi mtshan-nyid #  du'am / / da-ltar-byung-ba # 'am / / de-ltar #  byung ngam sa gzhan-du # 'am / / da-ltar-byung-ba #  la mi ltos-pa #  zhig tu gdags grang na /

# smra-ba #  chad-pas-bcad-pa #  ni gang-gis #  smra-ba #  chad-pa # s bcad ces bya-ba #  ste / / de-yang #  gtam rjes bcad-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'o / / de-la #  gtam rjes bcad-pa #  la ni bdag-gi #  ni ma legs so /
tatra kaTA tyAgaH asADu mama sADu tava iti evamAdiBiH prakArEH sva para vAda doza guNa aByupagamaH / kaTA sAdaH anyena anya pratisaraNa AdiBiH vikzepaH iti arTaH / yaTA uktam sUtre AyuzmAn= cundikaH tIrTikEH saha vAdam kurvan= avajAnitvA pratijAnAti pratijAnitvA avajAnAti iti / kaTA dozaH AkulA divacanam / tatra Akulam yat aDikAram utsRjya vicitra kaTA pratAnanam / saMrabDam yat kopa udDavam drava udDavam / agamakam yat DarmataH arTataH ca parzad vAdiByAm agRhItam / amitam yat aDikam punar ukta arTam jQAta arTam ca / anarTam anarTa yuktam tat paQcAkAram drazwavyam / nirarTakam apArTakam yukti Binnam sADyasamam jAti= Cala upasaMhitam arTa anupalabDitaH asaMbadDa arTataH anEkAntikataH sADanasya api sADyataH ayoniSaH asaBya sarva vAda anugamataH ca
# khyod kyi ni legs-so-zhes-bya-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rnam-pa #  rnams kyis rang dang gzhan gyi smra-ba # 'i skyon dang yon-tan #  khas-blang-ba # 'o / / gtam 'phro lus pa ni gzhan nas gzhan-du #  brgyud-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s bskal-ba # 'o / / gtam gyi nyes-pa #  ni cal col la-sogs-pa # 'i tshig go / / de-la #  cal col ni gang skabs bor-te #  / / gtam-sna-tshogs #  rgyas-par-byed-pa # 'o / / 'khrugs-pa #  ni gang khros-pa # s g-yeng ba dang dga'-ba # s g-yeng ba'o / / brda phrad du mi-rung-ba #  ni gang chos-dang-don #  'khor dang phyir-rgol-ba #  rnams kyis ma-zin-pa # 'o / / ran-pa-ma-yin-pa #  ni gang tshig lhag-ma #  dang zlos-pa #  dang nyungs pa'o / / don-dang-ldan-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ni de rnam-pa-lnga # r ba lta-ba # r bya ste / / don-med-pa #  dang don dang bral-ba #  dang rigs-pa #  dang bral-ba #  dang sgrub-pa # r mtshungs-pa #  dang ltag chod dang ldan-pa #  ste / / don mi dmigs-pa # 'i phyir ri / / don dang ma-'brel-ba # 'i phyir ro / / ma-nges-pa # 'i phyir ro / / grub-pa #  yang bsgrub dgos-pa # 'i phyir ro / / tshul-bzhin-ma-yin-pa #  dang tshogs-pa # r 'byung-ba #  ma-yin-pa #  dang smra-ba #  thams-cad #  dang ldan-pa # 'i phyir ro /
akAla yukta vacanam yat pUrvakam vaktavyaMpaH ca AdaBihitam paScAt vaktavyam pUrvam aBihitam
# dus-tshigs #  ma-yin-pa # r smra-ba #  ni gang sngar smra-ba # r bya-ba #  de phyis smra-ba #  dang phyis smra-ba # r bya-ba #  de sngar smra-ba # r bya'o /
asTiram yat pratijQAya avajQAtam avajQAya pratijQAtam ati tvaramANayA vAcA hi tUrNa parAmRzwaH
# mi-rtag-pa #  ni gang dam bcas nas smod-pa #  dang smad nas yang dam-'cha'-ba #  dang myur ches pas ha-cang #  rtab rtab por gyur te mi-gsal-ba # 'o /
apradIpta vacanam yat Canda lakzaNa samatikrAntam apratyanuBAzya uttara vihittam saMskRtena AraBya prAkRtena avasitam prAkRtena AraBya saMskRtena paryavasitam ca
# tshig mi-gsal-ba #  ni gang sgra'i mtshan-nyid #  dang 'gal-ba #  dang phyir ma bzlas par len smras-pa #  dang legs-par-sbyar-ba #  las brtsams te / / tha-ma # l bas mthar phyung-ba #  dang tha-mal-pa #  las brtsams te legs-par-sbyar-ba # s mthar phyung-ba # 'o /
aprabadDam yat antara aDizWita vicCinnam vAc pratiBAnam iti / vAda niHsaraNam yena vAdAt niHsarati akaraNena vA guNa dozO vicArya vAdasya nigraha sTAnAnAm AsAdanAt karaNena vA nirvahanAt iti
# tshig rgyun-chags-pa #  ma-yin-pa #  ni / / gang-ba # r skabs su tshig dang spobs-pa #  thogs-pa #  dang rgyun-chad-pa # 'o / / smra-ba #  las byung-ba #  ni gang-gis #  smras-pa #  las byung-ba #  ste / / smra-ba # 'i yon-tan #  dang nyes-pa #  brtags-nas #  mi-byed-pa # s 'byung-ba #  ni chad-pa'i-gnas #  su mi-'gyur-ba # 'i phyir ro /

vAde bahu karAH DarmAH ye vAde avaSyam upayujyante

# 'di-ltar #  gzhan gyi gzhung lugs la mkhas-pa #  ni smra-ba #  la gces spras byed-pa # 'i chos te / / des gtam gyi gzhi-thams-cad #  du smra-ba # r byed do / / lhag-ma #  rnams ni go sla bsam bshad do /
kuSala pakza prayuktena iti uktvA pratipatti sArakeNa iti vacanam ASaya viSudDi jQAnana arTam na lABa satkAra Adi nimittam Sruta Adi kuSala pakze prayuktena iti arTaH
# dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la brtson pa zhes-bya-ba #  gsungs nas nan-tan #  snying-po # r byed-pa #  zhes bka'-stsal-pa #  ni bsam-pa #  rnam-par-dag-pa #  bstan-pa # 'i phyir te / / rnyed-pa-dang-bkur-sti #  la-sogs-pa # 'i rgyur thos-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la brtson pa ma yin zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

# sems-can-bsdus-pa #  ni nyan-thos #  la-sogs-pa #  las bye-brag-tu-bya-ba # 'i phyir te / / gzhan-la-phan-pa # r sgrub-pa #  lhur len ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

# gang dag dang lhan-cig-tu #  rtsod pas smra-ba # r bya-ba # 'i phyir / / smra-ba #  de-dag #  kun-shes-pa # r bya-ba # 'i bsam-pa # s phyir smra-ba #  ma yin gyi skyon gdags-pa # 'i bsam-pa # s so /

# gzu bo gang dag gi mdun-du #  de smra-ba # r bya-ba # 'i tshogs de-dag #  kyang rung-ba #  ma yin zhing bya-ba-ma-yin-pa # 'am / / mngon bar zhen-pa #  can dag go /
sarvaH api ca vAdA prAyeNa zaXBiH dozEH yuktaH Bavati
# smra-ba # r bya-ba #  thams-cad #  kyang phal-cher #  nyes-pa #  drug dang ldan-pa #  yin te /
taTA hi vAdam kurvANaH kadAcid ati raBasena asat pakzam api parigRhya aBiniveSena Cala jAti nigraha sTAnAni api prayukte / vacana paryavasAnam anigamayya api akAlena vaktum AraBate / samyak api uktAm prativAdinaH kaTAm apapAtayati paMsayati iti arTaH
# 'di-ltar #  smra-bar-byed-pa #  na yang res-'ga' #  byung-rgyal #  du phyogs ngan-pa #  yang yongs-su-bzung-nas #  mngon bar zhen-pa #  dang tshig dor dang ltag chod dang chad-pa'i-gnas #  rnams la yang sbyor-ba #  dang tshig mjug-tu #  phyin phyin du mi sdong par dus-ma-yin-pa # r smra-ba # r rtsom pa dang phyir-rgol-ba # s legs-par #  smras kyang khyad du gsod de smod ces bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /

# tshig-brlang-po #  yang smra-ba #  ste / / des phyir-rgol-ba #  la-sogs-pa # 'i sems-'khrugs-pa # r byed-pa #  dang bdag kyang de-dag #  la sems-'khrugs-pa #  zhes-bya-ba # 'i nyes-pa #  'di drug dang ldan-pa #  yin no /
upaSAntasya ca durlaBaH vAdaH
# nye-bar-zhi-ba #  ni smra-ba #  dkon no /

# nye-bar-ma-zhi-ba #  la ni gang-gis #  gzhan dad-pa #  thob-par-'gyur-ba #  dang rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i gnas dang ldan-pa #  dang rang-gi-sems #  mnyam-par-'jog-pa # r 'gyur-ba #  dang gzhan-gyi-sems #  bsrung-ba #  dang rang-gi-sems #  bsrung-ba #  gnyi-ga #  dkon no /
prAyeNa vAde kaTam aham jayeyam pare parAjIyeran= iti evam cittam samudAcarati
# smra-ba #  phal-cher #  ni ji-ltar #  na bdag rgyal-ba # r 'gyur zhing pha rol pham par 'gyur snyam pa'i sems de kun du 'byung ngo /

# de yod-na #  yongs su gdung pa'i sdug-bsngal #  gyis kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa # r 'gyur ro / / de yod-na #  bde-ba-la-gnas-pa # r mi 'gyur ro /
tatas nirantara kuSala pakza prayoga asAmarTyAt tatas viSeza aDigamam pratyaprApti parihANiH iti
# de'i-phyir #  rgyun mi chad-pa # r dge-ba'i-phyogs #  la sbyor-ba # r mi nus so / / de'i-phyir #  khyad-par-thob-pa # r bya-ba #  la ma-thob-pa # s yongs-su-nyams-pa # r 'gyur ro /
mAtaram pitaram hatvA iti asyAm gATAyAm loke yat atyarTam avadyam pAtakam tat aBiDAyIni akzarANi etAni viSudDO pariNAmitAni
# pha dang ma ni bsad byas shing / / zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  'di ni 'jig-rten #  na gang shin-tu #  kha na ma thob sdig tor rtsi ba da brjod-pa # 'i yi-ge #  rnams rnam-par-dag-pa # r yongs-su-bsgyur-ba # 'o /
kim ca loke atyarTam avadyam saMmatam / guru jana GAtaH mahA jana GAtaH ca
# 'jig-rten #  na shin-tu #  kha-na-ma-tho-ba # r grags-pa #  ni skye-bo #  bla-ma #  bsad-pa #  dang skye-bo #  chen-po #  bsad-pa # 'o /
sa punar guru janaH dviviDaH pratiniyataH loka sADAraNaH ca

# de-la #  so-sor-nges-pa # 'i skye-bo #  bla-ma #  ni pha dang ma'o / / skyong-bar-byed-pa #  ni rgyal-po # 'o / / sbyin-gnas #  ni bram-ze #  gtsang sbra can rnams te /
tat ezAm sarvezAm GAtaH guru jana GAtaH iti ucyate
# de-dag #  ni shin-tu #  dag-pa # r grags-pa # 'i phyir ro / / de-dag #  thams-cad #  bsad na ni skye-bo #  bla-ma #  bsad-pa #  zhes-bya'o #  /
mahA jana GAtaH rAzwrasya sa anucarasya GAtaH
# skye-bo #  chen-po #  bsad-pa #  ni yul-'khor #  'khor dang bcas bcom nas zhes-bya-ba # 'o /
anucarAH punar gavASva mahiza uzwra AdayaH veditavyAH / kaTam punar etAni akzarANi viSudDO pariNAmyante
# 'khor ni ba-lang #  dang rta dang rnga mo dang ma he la-sogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o / / ji-ltar #  yi-ge #  'di dag dag-pa # r yongs su bsgyur zhen /
mAtra Adi GAta vacanasya tRzNA Adi prahANa pariNAmanAt yaTAkramam tRzNAm karma Bavam sa upAdAnam vijQAnam dRzwi SIla vrata parAmarSa dvayam zaXa Ayatanam ca sa gocaram aDikRtya mAtra AdayaH drazwavyAH tat sADarmyAt
# ma la-sogs-pa #  bsad-pa # 'i tshig ni sred-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  spong-ba # r yongs-su-bsgyur-ba # 'i phyir te / / go-rims-bzhin-du #  sred-pa #  dang las kyi sred-pa #  dang nye-bar-len-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  dang lta-ba #  dang tshul-khrims-dang-brtul-zhugs #  mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  gnyis dang skye-mched-drug #  spyod yul dang bcas-pa # 'i dbang-du-byas-nas #  / / ma la-sogs-pa # r blta-bar-bya #  ste /
tatra tRzNA nirvRtti hetuH / karmaBavaH utpatti hetuH
# de-dang-'dra-ba # 'i phyir ro / / de-la #  sred-pa #  ni mngon-par-grub-pa # 'i rgyu'o / / las-kyi-srid #  pa ni skye-ba'i-rgyu #  ste /
sa ca BAvanA bIja AGAna yogena pitR BUtaH drazwavyaH
# de ni bsgom-pa # 'i bag-chags #  skyed-pa # 'i tshul-gyis #  pha lta-bu # r blta-bar-bya # 'o /
AByAm hetuByAm sa upAdAnam vijQAnam pravartate / tasya evam pravartamAnasya sati api mokza aBilAze mokza prApti viGna karO= anupAya agra SudDi pratyAyakO parAmarSO
# rgyu 'di gnyis las ni nye-bar-len-pa #  dang bcas-pa # 'i rnam-par-shes-pa #  'byung ngo / / de de-ltar #  byung na thar-pa #  'dod du zin-kyang #  mchog-tu #  dag-pa # r yid-ches-pa # r byed-pa # 'i mchog-tu-'dzin-pa #  gnyis thar-pa #  thob-pa #  la gegs byed do /
Srotriya sADarmyam anayoH etat eva veditavyam yat uta agra SudDayaBiniveSaH / tasya eva punar vijQAnasya ASraya alaMkbana BAvena zaXa Ayatanam sagocaram veditavyam iti
# 'di gnyis gtsang sbra can dang 'dra-ba #  ni 'di-lta-bu # r rig-par-bya #  ste / / 'di-ltar #  mchog dang 'dag-pa # r mngon bar zhen-pa # 'o / / rnam-par-shes-pa #  de'i-gnas #  dang dmigs-pa'i-dngos-po # s skye-mched-drug #  spyod yul dang bcas-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
aSrAdDaH ca akRtajQaH ca iti asyAm gATAyAm hIna arTa aBiDAyIni akzarANi uttama arTe paridIpitAni / hInaH loke caturviDaH manaH karma hInaH kAya karma hInaH vAc karma hInaH upaBoga hInaH ca / manaH karma hInaH punar dviviDaH kuSala pravRtti vElomyena ca aSradDaH para loka Adi asaMtyayena dAna Adizu aprayogAt
# yid mi ches dang byas mi gzo / / zhes-bya-ba # 'i tshigs-su-bcad-pa #  'di ni / / don ngan-pa #  brjod-pa # 'i yi-ge #  rnams mchog gi don-du #  yongs-su-bsgyur-ba # 'o / / 'jig-rten #  na ngan-pa #  rnam-pa-bzhi #  ste / / yid-kyi-las #  ngan-pa #  dang lus-kyi-las #  ngan-pa #  dang ngag-gi-las #  ngan-pa #  dang longs-spyod #  ngan-pa # 'o / / yid-kyi-las #  ngan-pa #  yang rnam-pa-gnyis #  te / / dge-ba-la-'jug-pa #  dang mi-mthun-pa # s yid-mi-ches-pa #  ste / / 'jig-rten-pa #  rol la-sogs-pa #  la yid-mi-ches-pa # s / / sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  la mi sbyor-ba # 'i phyir ro /
akuSala pravRttyA AnukUlyena ca akRtajQaH yatra upakAra anapekzitvena mAtR vaDa Adi duScarite nirmaryAt tvAt / kAya karma hInaH cOraH saMDi= CedakaH atyarTam garhita jIvita tvAt
# mi-dge-ba #  la 'jug-pa #  dang mthun-pa # s byas-pa-mi-gzo-ba #  ste / / sngon phan-btags-pa #  la mi-lta-ba # r ma-gsod-pa #  la-sogs-pa # s nyes-par-spyod-pa #  la yang mi 'dogs-pa # 'i phyir ro / / lus-kyi-las #  ngan-pa #  ni khyim 'bigs-pa # 'i rkun-po #  ste / / 'tsho-ba #  shin-tu #  smad-pa # 'i phyir ro /
vAc karma hInaH mRzAvAda Adi praDAnaH tad rUpasya saBA Adizu praveSa aBAvAt / upaBoga hI naH SvA kA kaH pretaH vA iti evamAdikaH Cardita BakzaNAt iti
# ngag-gi-las #  ngan-pa #  ni brdzun-du-smra-ba #  la-sogs-pa #  lhur-len-pa #  ste / / de-lta-bu #  dang ldan-pa #  ni tshogs-pa #  la-sogs-pa # 'i nang-du #  'jug tu mi-rung-ba # 'i phyir ro / / longs-spyod #  ngan-pa #  ni / / khyi dang bya-rog #  dang yi nga gas la-sogs-pa #  ste /
kaTam punar etAni akzarANi uttama arTe pariNAmyante

aSrAdDa Adi vacanAnAm arhati pariNAmanAt

# de-la #  yid-mi-ches-pa #  ni rnam-par-grol-ba # 'i ye-shes-mthong-ba #  dang ldan-pa # s rang-gi #  yid-ches-pa # 'i phyir ro /
akRtajQaH asaMskRta nirmANa jQAnAt

saMDi= CettA punarBava pratisaMDi hetu kleSa prahANAt
# khyim 'bigs-par-byed-pa #  ni yang-srid-pa # r nying-mtshams-sbyor-ba # 'i rgyu nyon-mongs-pa-spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
hata avakASaH AyatyAm sarva gatizu duHKAna BinirvartanAt
# go-skabs #  bcom zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / phyi-ma-la #  'gro pa thams-cad-du #  sdug-bsngal #  mngon-par-mi-'grub-pa # 'i phyir ro /

# 'di'i lus ni byang-chub-sems-dpa' # i ting-nge-'dzin #  la brten-nas #  mthong-ba #  dang bsgom-pa'i-lam #  gnyis kyis byang-chub-chen-po #  la reg-pa # 'o /
mAtsarya Darma tAm anuvRMhayati iti sa vAsana mAtsarya anuSaya prahANena tat taTatA ASraya parivRtti sAkzAtkaraNAt
# ser-sna # 'i chos-nyid #  'phel-bar-byed-pa #  ni bag-chags-dang-bcas-pa # 'i sems ser-sna # 'i bag-la-nyal #  spangs-pa # s de'i de-bzhin-nyid #  gnas-gyur-pa #  mngon-du-byed-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dAnena ca pariKidyate dIrGa kAlam dAna nimittam parama duzkara Srama aByupagamAt
# sbyin-pa # s yongs su skyo-ba #  ni yun-ring-por #  sbyin-pa # 'i rgyu mchog-tu #  bya-dka'-ba # s ngal-ba # r bya-ba #  khas-blangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
yAcanakam ca dvezwi svayam grAha aBirucita tayA yAcanaka prAtikUlyAt
# slong-ba #  la tshig-pa #  za-ba #  ni rang-gis #  len-pa # r 'dod-pa # s slong-ba #  dang mi-mthun-pa # 'i phyir ro /
na kiMcid kadAcid dadAti sarvasya vastunaH sarvadA dAnAt
# res-'ga' #  ni ci-yang #  sbyin-pa # r mi-byed-pa #  ni dngos-po-thams-cad #  rtag-tu #  sbyin-pa # 'i phyir ro /
dUre ca Bavati dAnasya AsAdya dAna Adi parivarjanAt
# sbyin-pa #  las ring du gyur-pa #  ni nye-ba #  la sbyin-pa #  la-sogs-pa #  yongs su spangs-pa # 'i phyir ro /
tatra parameNa brahmacaryeNa samanvAgataH iti lokottareNa mArgeNa iti arTaH
# tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  dang ldan-pa #  zhes-bya-ba #  ni / / 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam dang ldan zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go /
na anyatra mETunAt mETunasya niHsaraNam paryezate iti tasya eva yaTA BUta parijQAnena tad prahANAt
# 'khrig-pa #  las gzhan-du #  'khrig-pa # s nges-par-'byung-ba #  mi 'tshol-ba #  ni de nyid yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yongs su shes-nas #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
yaTA BUta parijQAnam punar asya taTatA apratibeDAt veditavyam
# de-la #  yang-dag-pa #  ji-lta-ba-bzhin-du #  yongs-su-shes-pa #  ni / / de'i de-bzhin-nyid #  rab-tu-rtogs-pa # r rig-par-bya # 'o /
mETuna prahANena upekzakaH Bavati abrahmacarya prahANa upekzaNAt
# 'khrig-pa #  spong-ba #  la g-yeng ba ni mi-tshangs-par-spyod-pa #  spong-ba # 'i thabs la rtog-pa # 'i phyir ro /
utpannam ca mETuna rAgam aDivAsayati kAma rAgasya aDyAtmam utpannasya bahis pravAsanAt
# 'khrig-pa'i-'dod-chags #  skyes-pa #  dang-du-len-pa #  ni / / 'dod-pa-la-'dod-chags #  nang-du #  skyes-pa #  phyi-rol-du #  spong-ba # 'i phyir ro /
mETuna pratipakzeNa ca DarmeNa uttrasyati tad pratipakzeNa mArgeNa sarva sattva uttaraNAya vyavasyati iti kRtvA
# 'khrig-pa # 'i gnyen-po # 'i chos-kyis #  skrag-pa #  ni de'i gnyen-po # 'i chos-kyis #  sems-can-thams-cad #  bsgral ba'i don-du #  rtsol ba'i phyir ro / / rgyun-mi-'chad-par #  gnyis-kyis-gnyis-sbyor-ba #  ni /
aBIkzNam ca dvaya dvayam samApadyate saMkleSa vyavada na dvayena Pala hetu Bedena catur satya Atmakena SamaTa vipaSyanAt vayena / punar punar lOkika lokottara mArga dvayam samApadyate iti kRtvA
# zhi-gnas-dang-lhag-mthong #  ba gnyis kyis 'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa #  gnyis la snyoms-par-'jug-pa #  ste / / kun-nas-nyon-mongs-pa #  dang rnam-par-byang-ba #  gnyis kyis 'bras-bu #  dang rgyu'i bye-brag #  gis bden-pa #  bzhi'i bdag-nyid #  du gyur-pa # 'i don-du #  'jig-rten-pa #  dang 'jig-rten-las-'das-pa # 'i lam-gnyis #  la snyoms-par-'jug-pa # 'i phyir ro /
kim upAdAya idam SAstram aBiDarma samuccayaH iti nAma laBate
# bstan-bcos #  'di ci'i-phyir #  chos-mngon-pa # r kun las btus pa zhes-bya-ba # r ming btags she na /
nirukti nyAyena / sametya uccayatAm upAdAya tattvam aBisametya aDigamya boDisattvaMH saMkalanAt iti arTaH / samantAt uccayatAm upAdAya aBiDarma sUtrataH sarva cintA sTAna saMgrahAt iti arTaH / samyak uccayatvAya Ayatana tAm ca upAdAya iti aviparItena upAyena yAvat budDa tva prApaNAt iti arTaH / iti aBiDarma samuccaye BAzyataH sAMkaTyaviniScayaH nAma paQcamaH samuccayaH samAptaH
# nges-pa'i-tshig #  gi tshul-gyis #  rtogs-nas #  bsdus-pa # 'i phyir te / / byang-chub-sems-dpa' #  rnams kyis de-kho-na #  nyid mngon-pa # r rtogs shing khong-du-chud-nas #  mdor bsdus zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / kun las btus pa'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni chos-mngon-pa # 'i mdo rnams las te / / bsam-pa # 'i gnas-thams-cad #  bsdus-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / yang-dag-par #  mtho-ba # 'i gnas yin pa'i phyir zhes-bya-ba #  ni phyin-ci-ma-log-pa # 'i thabs kyis sangs-rgyas #  nyid kyi bar-du #  thob-par-byed-pa # 'i phyir zhes-bya-ba # 'i tha-tshig #  go / / chos-mngon-pa #  kun las btus pa'i bshad-pa #  / / slob-dpon #  chen-po #  rgyal-ba'i-sras #  kyis mdzad-pa #  rdzogs so /
